उपदेशे गुरुःकुर्यात्तस्मात्तन्मन्त्रशोधनं ॥  
  
तत्प्रकारं प्रवक्ष्यामि शृण्वं तु सकरासुराः ।  
गुरुः सिद्धासने संस्थोगुदमेढ्रान्तरं दृधं ॥  
  
वामेन पार्ष्णि नापीड्य तस्योपरि तु विन्यसेत् ।  
पादं तु दक्षिणं गुल्फं ग्रन्थ्योरन्योन्यमर्द्दनं ॥  
  
यथा स्यात् तत्प्रकर्तव्यं ततो दषिणपार्ष्णिना ।  
लिङ्गमूलं विनिष्पीड्यस्थिरकाय उपाविशेत् ॥   
  
प्। २१ब्)  
  
गुदमाकुञ्च्यपवनसपानाख्यं तदा गुरुः ।  
उत्थापयेत् ततः प्राणामधु सम्यङ्निरोधयेत् ॥  
  
अपानः प्राणयोः कुर्यात् सङ्घट्टं चैक दृङ्मना ।  
मूलाधारेचित् स्वरूपः कुण्डल्यां परमात्मनि ॥  
  
जातदोषं स्वस्य मन्त्रं चिन्तयेत् तत्र सद्गुरुः ।  
तस्य मन्त्रस्याक्षराणि क्रमादेकैकशस्तुतः ॥  
  
सुषुम्णाया तु मार्गेण मूलाधारे प्रवेशयेत् ।  
स्वाधिष्ठाने ततश्चक्रे मणिपूरेह्यनाहते ॥  
  
विशुद्ध आज्ञा चक्रे च भित्वा भित्वा प्रवेशयेत् ।  
एवं नीत्वा ब्रह्मरन्ध्रं तत्रन्यात् सोममण्डलात् ॥  
  
निर्गता मृतसंसिक्तमन्त्राणां सु विभावयेत् ।  
पुनः सुषुम्णा मार्गेण आज्ञा चक्रे च तारयेत् ॥  
  
विशुद्धे नाहते चापि मणिपूरे च चक्रके ।  
स्वाधिष्ठाने ततो भेदान्मूलाधारं प्रवेशयेत् ॥  
  
ततस्तन्मन्त्रमृष्यादिन्यासः पूर्वं जपेन्मनुं ।  
उक्तशापाद्विनिर्मुक्तं पश्चादुपदिशेच्चतं ॥  
  
अल्पपुण्यतया पापाधिक्यात् पापः कलौयुगे ।  
आशीर्वादफलं स्तोकं पूर्णपापादिजं फलं ॥  
  
वाचिकानां तु शापानां नाशाद्यर्थ मथोच्यते ॥  
  
अथ मन्त्राणां जननादि संस्काराः ॥  
  
श्रीपर्ण्यो वा चन्दनस्य पीठे चूतादिकस्य वा ।  
कस्तूरी कुङ्कुमाब्जैश्च विलिखेत् पाञ्चभौतिकं ॥  
  
चक्रमावाहयेत् तत्र मातृकाख्यां सरस्वतीं ।  
यथोक्तविधिना पूजां कृत्वा चाष्ठोत्तरशतं ॥  
  
जपित्वा मातृकां तस्या मध्यात् स्वाभीष्टमन्त्रकं ।  
स्वरव्यञ्जन विन्दुश्च सर्गयोगाक्षराणी च ॥  
  
पृथक् पृथगथोद्वृत्य चैकीकृत्य गुरूक्तितः ।  
गृहीतं जमयेत् मन्त्रं प्रोक्तं सञ्जननं त्विदं ॥  
  
आद्यन्तं प्रणवं कृत्वा प्रणवां तरितां जपेत् ।  
अष्टोत्तरशतं मन्त्रं वर्णानेतत्तु जीवनं ॥  
  
रोचना कुङ्कुमाभ्यां च भुजपत्रे लिखेन्मनुं ।  
प्रत्यक्षरं शतं वारं ताडयेच्चन्दनाम्भसा ॥  
  
समुच्चरन् वायुबीजमेतत्ताडनमुच्यते ।  
कुण्ठिताः शावराः मन्त्राः ताडिताः सिद्धिकारकाः ॥  
  
पूर्वोक्तपीठे संलिख्य तन्मन्त्राक्षर सङ्ख्यया ।  
आदायकरवीरस्य पुष्पाण्पथ समुच्चरन् ॥  
  
प्रत्यक्षरं च तैः पुष्पैः शतवारं हुनेदिति ।  
उच्चरन् वह्निबीजं च वोधनं त्वेतदुच्यते ॥  
  
प्राग्वत् पीठे च तैर्द्रव्यैः पद्ममष्टदलं लिखेत् ।  
तत्कर्णिकायां मालत्या लिखेत् कलिकयैकया ॥  
  
प्। २२अ)  
  
एकैकार्णं तु मन्त्रस्य तन्मन्त्राक्षर सङ्ख्यया ।  
अश्वत्थ पल्लवं गृह्यतमेवं मन्त्रमुच्चरन् ॥  
  
अभिषिञ्चाम्यमुं मन्त्रं नम इत्यभिषेचयेत् ।  
नानासुगन्धितो येन पल्लवैः केन चाक्षरं ॥  
  
एकमष्टोत्तरशतमभिषेकस्त्वयं स्मृतः ।  
अभिषेको मन्त्रशुद्धिं कुर्यान्नृणां यथा जलं ॥  
  
ज्योतिर्मन्त्रश्चिन्तनीयामूलाधारेग्निमण्डले ।  
संस्कर्तव्यं मनुं तस्य उर्ध्वमेवं विभावयेत् ॥  
  
आणवाष्यः साहजिकः आगन्तुः कार्मणः स्मृतः ।  
योगाख्यामायिकः प्रोक्तः स्वमन्त्रे तु मलत्रयं ॥  
  
ज्योतिर्मन्त्रेण निर्दग्धमेकमेक विचिन्तयेत् ।  
एवं तु विमलो जातः स्वमन्त्र इति चिन्तयेत् ॥  
  
ज्योतिर्मन्त्रस्तु वेदादि हौ&मितिद्यक्षरो मतः ।  
विमलीकरणं त्वे तत्प्रयोगां तेपि कारयेत् ॥  
  
प्राग्वत् पीठे कुङ्कुमादि द्रव्यैर्मन्त्रं विलेखयेत् ।  
ताम्रादिपात्रं कर्पूर वा सितेन जलेन च ॥  
  
शुद्धेनापूर्यलिखितमन्त्रेणाष्टोत्तरंशतं ।  
अभिमन्त्र्यजलं तेन मन्त्रेण कुशबिन्दुभिः ॥  
  
प्रत्यक्षरं प्रोक्षयेत् तदे तदाप्यायनं मतं ।  
पुरश्चर्या क्लेशितानां समावर्तनवत्विदं ॥  
  
कस्तूर्याद्यैस्ताम्रपात्रमध्ये मन्त्रं विलेखयेत् ।  
पात्रान्तरे च कर्पूरादिकवासित सज्जलं ॥  
  
गृहीत्वा चार्घ्यपात्रेण पठमन्त्रमिमं मनुं ।  
तर्पयामि नम्ॐ तेन तर्पयेदिति तर्पणं ॥  
  
ॐ ह्रीं श्री& पूर्वकं मन्त्रं जपेदष्टोत्तरं शतं ।  
जपेदेतद्दीपने स्यात् सर्वमन्त्रेष्वपीष्यते ॥  
  
जप्यमानस्य मन्त्रस्य गोपनं त्वप्रकाशनं ।  
संस्कारा दशसम्प्रोक्ता सर्वतन्त्रेषु गोपिता ॥  
  
एवमेकादश प्रोक्तः संस्कारा अथ पञ्च च ।  
प्रतिमन्त्रं वक्ष्यमाणो जपहोमश्च तर्पणं ॥  
  
मार्जनं भोजनं चापि द्विजानामिति षोडशः ।  
प्रोक्ताः मन्त्रस्य संस्काराः देवशापादि मोचकाः ॥  
  
दीक्षाकालं प्रवक्ष्यामि तच्छृणुष्व वरानने ॥  
  
इति श्रीतन्त्रचिन्तामणौमन्त्राणां जागरणादि षोडशसंस्कारनिर्णयन्नाम   
पञ्चम प्रकाशः ॥ ५ ॥  
अथ मासफलं ॥  
  
ईश्वरोवाच ॥  
  
चैत्रे दुःखाय दीक्षास्याद् वैशाखे रत्नसञ्चयः ।  
मरणं भवति ज्येष्टे चाषाढे वन्धुनाशनं ॥  
  
समृद्धिः श्रावणेनूनं भवेद् भाद्रपदक्षयः ।  
प्रजानाशोऽथाश्विने तु भवेच्चा शुभमेव च ॥  
  
ज्ञानं स्यात् कार्तिके सौख्यमार्गश्रीर्ष भवेत्किल ।  
पौषे ज्ञानक्षयोमाद्येभवे मेधा विवर्द्धनं ॥  
  
प्। २२ब्)  
  
फाल्गुणे सर्वसिद्धिः स्यात् मलमासं विवर्जयेत् ।  
निषिद्धमासे तु तत् तद्विशेषो शृणु भेदत्तः ॥  
  
षष्टी भाद्रपदेमासि तथाश्विन चतुर्दशी ।  
कार्तिकी नवमी शुक्लामार्गो शुक्लातृतीयका ॥  
  
पौषे च नवमी शुक्लामाघे शुक्ला चतुर्थिका ।  
फाल्गुणे नवमी शुक्ला चैत्रे काम त्रयोदशी ॥  
  
वैशाखे चाक्षया चैव ज्येष्ठे दशहरातिथिः ।  
आषाढे पञ्चमी शुक्लाश्रावणे शुक्लपञ्चमी ॥  
  
एतानि देवपर्वाणि तीर्थकोटि फलं लभेत् ।  
निन्दितेष्वपि कालेषु दीक्षोक्ता पर्वणी शुभा ॥  
  
अथ पक्षफलं ॥  
  
भुक्तिमुक्तिप्रदः शुक्लकृष्ण मोक्षप्रदः स्मृतः ।  
वामाचारवतां शुक्लो न सत्कृष्णौपि मध्यमः ॥  
  
तिथेः फलं बुद्धिनाशः क्रमाद् ज्ञेयः सुसिद्धये ।  
अगौरीमान्त्रिकात्रष्टा विगणेशाश्च दुःखिता ॥  
  
सिद्ध्यन्ति मन्त्राः सर्वेपि न सिद्ध्यन्ति कदाचन ।  
समृद्धिर्द्रुतसिद्धिश्च मूर्खता दुःखनाशनं ॥  
  
जडतारिक्तनाशश्च सर्वपूर्णं भवेत् फलं ।  
शुक्लाश्रेष्ठा नैव कृष्णा शुभाशुभ नराहरेः ॥  
  
सिद्धिः स्यात् सर्वमन्त्राणामशैवानां महाभयं ।  
सिद्धिर्हातु विशेषेण पुत्रहानिः पितृनृते ॥  
  
अमावास्या सोमवारे भौमवारे चतुर्दशी ।  
सप्तमी रविवारेण सूर्यपर्वशतैः समा ॥  
  
अथ वारफलं ॥  
  
रविवारे भवेद्वित्तं सोमशान्ति भवेत्किल ।  
आयुरङ्गारकेहन्ति तत्र दीक्षां विवर्जयेत् ॥  
  
बुधः सौन्दर्यमाप्नोति ज्ञानस्यान्न बृहस्पतौ ।  
शुक्रे सौभाग्यमाप्नोति च शो * * * * * * (?  
  
atha nakṣatraphalaṃ ||  
  
kramāddīkṣāphalaṃbhānāṃ samatā ca yathā vipat |  
manastāpaḥ priyāsaukhyaṃ saukhyaṃ maṃtrasya siddhayaḥ ||  
  
siddhiśca krūramaṃtrāṇāṃ śaktimaṃtrasya siddhayaḥ |  
sarve maṃtrāḥ prasiddhyaṃti sarpamaṃtrasya siddhayaḥ ||  
  
nidhanaṃ rājadaṇḍaśca vaśitvaṃ sarvasiddhayaḥ |  
rudradaivatasaṃsiddhiḥ śīghraṃ siddhiḥ śubhāmati ||  
  
devamaitrī sarvehāniḥ kalahaśca mahābhayaṃ |  
saṃpadrogojapātsiddhiḥ kṣobhaḥ saṃtāpa īśatā ||  
  
sarvasiddhiphalaṃbhānāṃ kramāddakṣatha vāmake |  
caturaste tvadhaḥpāto dagdhāliṃgitadhūmite ||  
  
p. 23a)  
  
adhomukhe śubhebhe ca caṃdraśuddhau viśeṣataḥ |  
kṛṣṇe tārābalaṃ kuryāṃt svanāmādi viciṃtanaṃ ||  
  
atha yogaphalaṃ ||  
  
yogāśca prītirāyuṣmānsaubhāgyaḥ śobhanaḥ śubhaḥ |  
śukarmā ca dhṛtirvṛddhirdhruvaḥ siddhiśca harṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
varīyā&śca śivaḥ siddho brahmā iṃdraśca ṣoḍaśaḥ |  
viṣkaṃbhādika yogānāṃ nāmatulyaṃ phalaṃ bhavet ||  
  
ānaṃdādika yogānāṃ sarvatrā vikalaṃ phalaṃ |  
śubhāni karaṇānyāhurdīkṣāyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
atha karaṇaphalaṃ ||  
  
vavavālagataittilaścavaṇijastadanaṃtaraṃ |  
karaṇānyetāni śubhānyeva sarvataṃtreṣu bhāvinī ||  
  
śakunyādī niviṣṭiṃ ca viśeṣeṇa vivarjayet |  
viṣṭiṃ vihāya karaṇevare siddhirdrutaṃ bhavet ||  
  
sarvasiddhirviṣṭipucchesthire tu sthiratā bhavet ||  
  
atha lagnaphalaṃ ||  
  
atha lagnaphalaṃ devādhanaṃdhānyaṃ samṛddhayaḥ |  
mṛtyurvātha bhaveddhāniḥ paśupatya vināśanaṃ ||  
  
rājyaṃ vā devatā siddhirhānirmedhā vināśanaṃ |  
ratnādi lakṣmīlābhaśca dhanaṃdhānyaṃ ca siddhayaḥ ||  
  
pūrṇasiddhiḥ pratāpaśca hānirvijñānanāśanaṃ |  
putraprāptirmaṃtrasiddhiḥ paśavorvipulaṃ dhanam ||  
  
sadāduḥkhaṃ tathā hānirvāmitāṃ mithunaḥ śubhaḥ |  
vāgināṃ yavanānāṃ ca viruddhaṃ vahudhā śubhaṃ ||  
  
atha kālaphalaṃ ||  
  
dharmataḥ prātakālaḥ syāt saṃgame rājyadāyakaḥ |  
madhyāhne sarvasiddhiḥ syāt sāyāhne madhyamo bhavet ||  
  
rajanī maṃtradāne tu niṣiddhā deśikottamaiḥ |  
caraḥ sarvovivarjaḥ syāt sthirarāśiṣu saukhyadā ||  
  
sthiralagnaṃ viṣṇumaṃtre śivamaṃtre caraṃ śubhaṃ |  
dviḥ svabhāvagataṃ lagnaṃ śaktimaṃtre praśasyate ||  
  
tṛtīyaikādaśaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ daśamasthaḥ śubhaḥ śaśī |  
janmacaṃdraḥ śubhaḥ proktā janmanakṣatra varjitaḥ ||  
  
śuklapakṣe dvitīyastu paṃcamo navamastathā |  
gocare ye grahāḥ śuddhāstairyuktopi śubhaḥ śaśī ||  
  
śubhamadhyasthito vāpi caṃdramā śubhado bhavet |  
paṃcāṃga śuddhedivase svādaye caṃdrasūryayoḥ ||  
  
guru śukrodaye caiva śasyate maṃtrasaṃskriyā |  
śukrosto yadi vā vṛddho gurvādibhyo bhavedyadi ||  
  
meṣavṛścika siṃheṣu tadā doṣo na vidyate |  
asvādhyāya bhūmikaṃpe saṃdhyāgarje ca bhairava ||  
  
ulkāpāte ca divase tatra dīkṣāṃ vivarjayet |  
śikṣati janmanakṣatre saṃkrāṃtau viṣuve'yane ||  
  
p. 23b)  
  
anyeṣu puṇyayogeṣu grahaṇe caṃdrasūryayoḥ |  
paṃcaparvayugādyāsuvyatīpātādi vāsare ||  
  
atra dīkṣā śubhā proktā nātra kāryā vicāraṇā |  
yanmāsatithivārādiśodhanaṃ proktameva hi ||  
  
maṃtradīkṣā paraṃ tatra vijñeyaṃ sādhakottamaiḥ |  
vidyādīkṣāparaṃ naiva tithimāsādi śodhanaṃ ||  
  
yadaivecchā tadā dīkṣā gurorājñānusārataḥ |  
pausukṣavau pratyathana kālādi niyamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
  
niṃdyānitāni sarvāṇi praśastāni vimuktaye ||  
  
śaśidivākarayorgrahaṇe janmani śiṣyasya makarasaṃkrāṃtau ||  
  
karuṇāsamaye ca gurornakṣatrādīpyate tena dīkṣāyāṃ ||  
  
saṃtīrtherkavidhugrāse tattudāmana parvaṇoḥ |  
maṃtradīkṣāṃ prakurvāṇo māsarkṣādīnna śodhayet ||  
  
ravisaṃkramaṇe caiva sūryasya grahaṇe tathā |  
tatra lagnādikaṃ kiṃcinna vicārya kadācana ||  
  
mahāṣṭamyāṃ viśeṣeṇa dhanakāmārthasiddhaye ||  
  
sūryagrahaṇakāle tu nānyadanveṣitaṃ bhavet |  
sūryagrahaṇakālena sāmānyo nāsti kaścana ||  
  
tatra yadyatkṛtaṃ sarvemanaṃta phaladaṃ bhavet |  
na māsatithi vārādi śodhanaṃ sūryaparvaṇi ||  
  
dadātīṣṭaṃ gṛhīyattattasmin kāle gurornṛṣu |  
siddhirbhavati maṃtrasya vināyāse navai tataḥ ||  
  
kartavyaṃ sarvayatnena maṃtrasiddhimabhīpsubhiḥ |  
caṃdragraha sahasreṇa sūryagraha samo bhavet ||  
  
tato lakṣaguṇaṃ proktaṃ grahaṇaṃ nijavāsare |  
tatra sūryagrahaḥ śasto na tu caṃdragrahaḥ kvacit ||  
  
caṃdragrahe tu dāridryaṃ śaure sarvasamṛddhaye |  
sūryagrahaḥ śivaḥ proktaḥ caṃdrākhyaḥ śaktireva ca ||  
  
sūryagrahe śaktidīkṣā paśudīkṣā na kārayet |  
caṃdragrahe viṣṇudīkṣā paṃcarātraṃ na kārayet ||  
  
caṃdrasūryagrahe dīkṣā sarvadīkṣā śubhāmatā |  
caṃdragrahe śaktidīkṣā sarvadīkṣottamottamā ||  
  
navāratithiṛkṣādinamāsaniyamastathā |  
na yogakaraṇaṃ nāpi na vicāraṃ samācaret ||  
  
devī bodhaṃ samārabhya yāvatsyā navamī tithiḥ |  
kṛtā tāsu budhairdīkṣā sarvābhiṣṭa phalapradā ||  
  
bodhane naiva durgāyāḥ kālākālaṃ na kārayet |  
aśokākhyāṣṭāmī yatra rāmākhyo navamī tathā ||  
  
yugādyāyāṃ janmadine vivāhadivase tathā |  
viṣuvā'yanayordvaṃdve naiva kiṃcid vicārayet ||  
  
p. 24a)  
  
ayane viṣuve caiva yugādyāsu tathaiva ca |  
grahaṇe ca mahātīrthena kālasyā vicāraṇaṃ ||  
  
tulasīnikaṭe vilvamūledhātrītale tathā |  
anādidevasānnidhye mahākṣetre gavāṃ gṛhe ||  
  
devī pūjādine vāpi nāsti kālasya nirṇayaḥ |  
tithiṃ vinā vidīkṣāyā viśiṣṭāvasaraṃ śṛṇu ||  
  
durlabhe sadgurūṇāṃ tu sakṛtsaṃga upasthite |  
tadanujñā yadā labdhvā sa dīkṣā savaro mahān ||  
  
grāme vā yadi vāraṇye kṣetre vā divase niśi |  
gurāvaśruta dṛṣṭe ca siddhakṣetre suśobhanaṃ ||  
  
āgaccheti gururdaivād yadā dīkṣā tadā bhavet |  
yadaivecchā tadā dīkṣā gurorājñānurūpataḥ ||  
  
na tithirna vrataṃ homā na snānaṃ japaḥ kriyā |  
dīkṣāyā kāraṇaṃ kiṃtu svecchā vāpte tu sadgurau ||  
  
śiṣyānāhūyaguruṇā kṛpayā yadi dīyate |  
tadā lagnādikaṃ kiṃcinna vicāryaṃ kathaṃcana ||  
  
sarvevārāḥ grahāḥ sarve nakṣatrāṇi ca rāśayaḥ |  
yasminnahani saṃtuṣṭā guruḥ sarvasukhāvahaḥ ||  
  
puṇyatīrthe kurukṣetre devā pīṭhe catuṣṭaye |  
prayāge śrīgiraukāśyāṃ kālākālaṃ na śodhayet ||  
  
dvayoḥ parāge harivāsare ca arddhodaye caiva mahodaye ca |  
dīkṣā praśastā kathitā śivena siṃhastha doṣo na hi manyate ca ||  
  
gayāyāṃ bhāskarakṣetre vireje caṃdraparvate |  
catvare ca mataṃge ca tathā kanyāśrameṣu ca ||  
  
na gṛhṇīyāt tato dīkṣāṃ tīrtheṣve teṣu pārvatī |  
iti te kathitaṃ devī dīkṣākālaṃ sureśvarī ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau dīkṣākālanirṇayenāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ prakāśaḥ || 6 ||  
śrīdevyuvāca |  
  
vāmamārge kathaṃ dīkṣā dakṣiṇe ca kathaṃ bhavet |  
kiṃ tatrāvaśyakaṃ keṣāṃmitime nirṇayaṃ vada ||  
  
īśvara uvāca |  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi sarvataṃtreṣu gopitaṃ |  
dīkṣāvidhiṃ paṃcavidhaṃ tadrājñāmuttamottamaṃ ||  
  
uttamaṃ mahādāḍhyānāṃ sāmānyānā tu madhyamam |  
brāhmaṇānāmalpamuktaṃ yatīnāmapi cālyakaṃ ||  
  
tasmādādau pravakṣyāmi tubhyaṃ yaccottamottamaṃ |  
yasmin jñāte cottamādi bhedānāṃ viṣayo bhavet ||  
  
tatra vakṣyāmi dīkṣāṃgaṃ vāstu yāgapuraḥ saraṃ |  
tatra bhūmīparīkṣyeta vāstujñāna viśāradaḥ ||  
  
p. 24b)  
  
tatra prathamato bhūmiparīkṣā |  
  
plavasthānaṃ ca gaṃbhīraṃ dīrghatoyāśayaṃsaraḥ |  
agniśālāgni hotṛṇāṃ puṇyasthānaṃ pariśrutaṃ ||  
  
dvijānāṃ sa vratānāṃ vā āśrayaḥ svāśramotha vā |  
dīkṣāyāmatiśastāni sthānānyetāni pārvatī ||  
  
mahānadīnāṃtīrāṇi gaṃgāsāgarasaṃgame |  
praśastāni ca tīrthāṇi kṣetrāṇi cāśramāṇyapi ||  
  
araṇyāni ca sarvāṇi parvatāḥ sakalā api |  
sanirjuropyupagirirdevatāyatanānyapi ||  
  
atha niṣiddhāni |  
  
na ca dīkṣāṃ prakurvīta nikuṃje gahane vane |  
dvisīmnice mahāraṇye mātsaryamṛgasevite ||  
  
sphuṭitā ca saśalyā ca valmīka rohiṇī tathā |  
dūrataḥ parivarjyābhūḥ karturāyurddhanāpahā ||  
  
sphuṭitāmaraṇaṃ kuryādduṣarādhanavāśinī |  
saśalyā kleśadā nityaṃ viṣamā śatruvarddhinī ||  
  
īśakoṇa pravāsā ca kartuḥ śrīdāsuniścitaṃ |  
pūrvaplavāvṛddhikarī varadā bhūttarahlavā ||  
  
dakṣiṇaplavayā bhūmi nityaṃ mṛtyubhayapradā |  
gṛhakṣayakarī sā ca bhūmiryā nairṛtaplavā ||  
  
dhanahānikarī pṛthvīkīrtitā varuṇaplavā |   
vātaplavā tathā bhūmirnityamudvegakāriṇī ||  
  
prathame bhūpradeśe ca parīkṣāṃ kārayedbudhaḥ |  
brāhmaṇībhūḥ kuśopetā kṣatriyāsyāccharākulā ||  
  
kuśakāśākulā vaiśyā śudrāḥ sarvatṛṇākulā |  
kuṃdeṃdugopahemālivarṇāyā brāhmaṇāditaḥ ||  
  
brāhmī sarvārthasiddhaḥ syāt kṣatriyā rājyadā tathā |  
dhanadhānyakarī vaiśyā śūdrā tu niṃditānune ||  
  
mṛttikā gaṃdhamāghrāya śubhāśubha nirūpiṇaṃ |  
nānāgaṃdhān mahāśokāmāṃsagaṃdhāndhaneśvaraḥ ||  
  
kaṭugaṃdhā bhavedrogī viṣṭāgaṃdhā ca niṣphalā |  
maṃdyagaṃdhānnirogīsyā durgaṃdhī bhayamādṛśet ||  
  
siddhirnagaṃdhasaṃbhūte sudhā ca vaṇijāyatā |  
kṣāragaṃdho tathā nāśopāni gaṃdhā śubhāvahā ||  
  
punaḥ svādaṃ vadivyāmi śubhāśubhagataṃ tu va |  
āmlāvighnī tathā bhūmiḥ kaṣāyā hi nirogitāṃ ||  
  
lavaṇena mahānāśotiktenāpi nijo ripuḥ |  
viśeṣaḥ svādamāsādya maṃtrī tasyāni rūpyate ||  
  
bhūme parigrahaṃ kuryādyā vadāyatanaṃ bhavet |  
śalyādi śodhanaṃ kuryāttuṣāṃgārādi dūrayet ||  
  
śarkalā yatra vidyaṃte kleśo bhavati mānavaḥ |  
aṃgāreṇa tathā rogā lohanāyāsa jāyate ||  
  
p. 25a)  
  
dagdhādinā ca kāṣṭena rājabhītiḥ prajāyate |  
tṛṇena jāyate śokaḥ iṣṭakeṇā sthirī bhavet ||  
  
vetaśāvaṃdha vairvyāptaṃ vaṃśena maraṇaṃ bhavet |  
viṣṭayā vaṃdhanaṃ prāptaṃ śūnyabhāṇḍena śunyatā ||  
  
carmaṇā kalahaṃ vidyāt karpaṭe dhananāśanaṃ |  
asthināṃ ca bhavenmṛtyumasthinā jñāyate bhuvi ||  
  
mṛttikā snigdhapatraṃ ca yaḥ sa bhāgabhavennaraḥ |  
vālukā yatra vidyaṃte tatra vidyā mahāsukhī ||  
  
pāṣāṇaṃ ca mahābhāgī sphāṭikā niḥśriyo bhavet |  
maṇināroganāśaśca hiraṇyairddhanavānbhavet ||  
  
viśeṣajaṃ tu savare pravakṣyehaṃ śubhāśubhaṃ |  
urageṇāsthirābhūmirmaṇḍūkena dhanāgame ||  
  
pippalīkā bhavecchokā mukhakairdhānyavardhayet |  
chuchuṃdarī mahānāśo kaumyeṇa dhanavān bhavet ||  
  
śalabhairogitāṃ yāṃti pataṃgeṇa mahābhayaṃ |  
hidiṃgikā mahātrāsovicchikaṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ||  
  
gṛhagodhau mahāsiddhiḥ kṛkalādbhayanāśane |  
evamādīni jaṃtūnāṃ śubhena śubhadā bhavet ||  
  
aśubhenāśubhaṃ vidyā jaṃtūnāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |  
bhūmistu khananāchodhyā sveṣṭakuṇḍādi karmaṇi ||  
  
khanyamāne jalaṃ yāvacchalya doṣo vinaśyati |  
dūre yatra sthiraṃ vāriḥ khanituṃ naiva śakyate ||  
  
paṃcahastaṃ ca kātavyaṃ śalyadoṣopaśāṃtaye |  
asthikīṭāṃgāramalādikahīnaṃ śubhāvahaṃ ||  
  
anyathātaṃ mṛdaṃ tyaktvā pūrayeccha bhayāmṛdā |  
grāmād vahisthayā tatra viprādyaiḥ svasvavarṇayā ||  
  
śalyoddhāraṃ tataḥ kṛtvā pūrayet su samaṃ yathā |  
etadakaraṇe maṃtrī na kiṃcit phalamāpnuyāt ||  
  
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ śalyoddhāra kramo mayā |  
evaṃ viśodhyatāṃ bhūmiṃ kāryādvāstu prapūjanaṃ ||  
  
smārtā ca tāṃtrikī cetidvividhāsannigadyate |  
carasthira prabhede ca dvidhā vāstuḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
gṛhaprāsāda kūpānāṃ maṇḍapasya jalasya ca |  
apareṣvapi kāryeṣu yoga homādikeṣu ca ||  
  
tūtane vigrahe kāryon yathā mahadupadravā ||  
  
atha vāstu puruṣotpattiḥ ||  
  
vāstunāmāpurā kaścida surobhūn mahābalaḥ |  
trailokyaṃ nirjitaṃ tena tripaṃcāśacca devatāḥ ||  
  
yeraṇe saṃmukhe jātāstena teti nipīḍitāḥ |  
punaḥ punarjitā yuddhe sa evāsit prajāpatiḥ ||  
  
divyavarṣa sahasrāṃte devāḥ śaraṇamāgatāḥ |  
viṣṇormamāti pārvatyā deveṃdreṇāpitacchrutaṃ ||  
  
p. 25b)  
  
yoddhukāmaḥ sobhyadhāvantāradena pracoditaḥ |  
kṛtaṃ yuddhaṃ tena sārddha mallābhirvarṣapaṃcakaṃ ||  
  
tato daityo madotsikto viṣṇumāyā vimohitaḥ |  
uvāca vacanaṃ tuṣṭo vrīyatāṃ vrīyatāmiti ||  
  
nendreṇa na kubereṇa mamatoṣakaraṃkṛtaṃ |  
sasainyenāpitadyuddhaṃ tvayā tu jaṭilena hi ||  
  
kṛtaṃ viṣṇusahāyena pārvatyarddhīgadhāriṇā |  
tenāhaṃ tuṣṭi māpannastrailokya parameśvaraḥ ||  
  
adeyaṃ nāsti me kiṃcidyāvayaṃ tu trayopi ca |  
ityākarṇya vacastasya śivayorbhrūḥ pracoditaḥ ||  
  
hariḥ prāhamahādhanyadaityendratvatsamostikaḥ |  
satyaṃ trivākyaṃ kuruṣu tadā vācyo ca romayā ||  
  
śivenāpi ca pārvatyā eka evā paro na hi |  
triṣu vā ca tadā daityastadā viṣṇurvyatijñipat ||  
  
yathāte tvaritaṃ mṛtyuḥ sa upāyaḥ pradarśyatāṃ |   
viṣṇoḥ chalamiti jñātvā daityeṃdraḥ samabhāṣataḥ ||  
  
avaśyameva gaṃtavyaṃ sa vaiḥ kālamukhehare |  
tathāpi svapratijñārthaṃ yogacchati sa jīvati ||  
  
paraṃ tvekonamevaṃ śayaiścamat sevanaṃ kṛtaṃ |  
tasya mārgaṃ darśayitvā deho yaṃti papātyatāṃ ||  
  
kāle tasmiṃśca bhodevā vāgravā cāśarīriṇī |  
daityeṃdra kurumāśokaṃ bhūmerjanmatavā bhavet ||  
  
tatraiva tvaṃ layaṃ yā hitvattoṣārthaṃ varaṃ śṛṇu |  
ye varṇāḥ svasya bhogārthaṃ kariṣyaṃti navaṃ gṛhaṃ ||  
  
tatra tvadutsavamṛte nānāduḥkhairupahutāḥ |  
kālakarṇyādikā dāsyo vināyaka mukhāścate ||  
  
sevakāpīḍayiṣyaṃti ityājñāpa rāmeśvarī |  
ityākarṇyavayaḥ sopi gataṃ kṛtvā mahītale ||  
  
praviveśa tato devairmat pāṣāṇaiḥ prapūritaṃ |  
ye naye nirjitā devāḥ punarudgamasaṃkayā ||  
  
tasyorddhaṃ tu tripaṃcāśannivāsaṃ ca kurudyatāḥ |  
mūrddhavyagni samādiṣṭo mukhe cāpaḥ samāśritaḥ ||  
  
pṛthvīdharorvyamā caiva talasthānamadhisthitau |  
vakṣasthale cāpa vatsuḥ pūjanīyaḥ sadābudhaiḥ ||  
  
netrayorditimajjanyauthotrerditi jayaṃtakau |  
sarpeṃdrauskaṃdhasaṃsthaut pūjanīyau prayatnataḥ ||  
  
satyarogādayastadvadvāhya paṃca ca paṃca ca |  
rudreśvarājayakṣmā ca vāmahaste samasthitaḥ ||  
  
sāvitraḥ savitā tadvaddhaste dakṣiṇamāstitau |  
vivasthānatha mitraśca jaṭharesaṃ vyavasthitau ||  
  
p. 26a)  
  
pūṣā ca pāpayakṣmā ca hastayormaṇibaṃdhake |  
tathaivā suraśeṣau ca vāmapārśve samāsthitau ||  
  
pārśve tu dakṣiṇe tadvadvitathaḥ sagṛhakṣataḥ |  
uccāryamā vubhau jñeyau jāṃghvo gaṃdharva puṣpakau ||  
  
jaṃghayorbhṛṃga sugrīvausphiddhasthau dauvārikau mṛgaḥ |  
jayaśakau tathā meḍhrapādayoḥ pitarastathā ||  
  
madhyena ca pado brahmā hṛdaye sa tu pūjyate |  
tasmāda vaśyaṃte pūgṛhavā sa mukhecchayā ||  
  
śṛṇvaṃ tu tadvidhiṃ devā vāmadakṣiṇamārgataḥ |  
bhadrabhūmi praśodhyaṃte daśadaṇḍa samālikhet ||  
  
adhodhautiryakādau ca tenekāśihikoṣṭakaṃ |  
vāstu maṇḍalakaṃ kāryamaṣṭahastaṃ tu nāparaṃ ||  
  
ekāśīti padaṃ cakraṃ vaidikastatra devatāḥ |  
madhyakoṣṭeṣu nava sutvādau brahmāṇamarcayet ||  
  
apavatsaṃ tadīśāne prāgaryannaṃ trikoṣṭake |  
āgneya savitāraṃ ca vivasvaṃta mayāktiṣu ||  
  
indraṃ nairṛtya digbhāge mitraṃ paścimagaṃ triṣu |  
vāyavye rājayakṣmāṇaṃ sumeruṃ cottaratraye ||  
  
vaidakoṣṭheṣu vaiśyanyāmīśakoṇācca devatāḥ |  
śikhīparyaṇa śrāpaścaditiḥ proktoṣṭhayordvayoḥ ||  
  
kramādete paṃcadevāḥ jñātavyāḥ savyamārgataḥ |  
jayaṃtendroḥ sūryasatyabhṛṃgā āgneyakoṇake ||  
  
aṃtarīkṣaṃ tathā vātaḥ pūṣā sāvitra eva ca |  
catuṣka īśato devāstato dakṣiṇa paṃcake ||  
  
yugme kramā ca vitatho bṛhatkṣatayamo yathā |  
gaṃdharvo bhṛṃgarājaśca nair-ṛtīstha catuṣkake ||  
  
īśānato jayanṛpau pitṛdau vārikau tathā |  
tataḥ paścādvike paṃcamugrīva puṣpadaṃtakaḥ ||  
  
varuṇā suraśeṣāśca vāyavye īśatastva hi |  
rudraśca pāpayakṣmāśca rogaścottara paṃcasu ||  
  
saravyau bhallāṭa somau ca bhujaścāditistathā |  
devā ete paṃcacatvāriṃśadarvāśca bhaktitaḥ ||  
  
uktānamiti devānāṃ padānyāpūryapaṃcabhiḥ |  
madhye padānāṃ navakaṃ mārjayitvā prapūrayet ||  
  
sitena rajasā bhūyastaddikṣu catasṛṣvapi |  
ṣaṭkaṃ saṃsājya rajasā raktena paripūrayet ||  
  
śiṣṭhāni ca padānyatra yathāsthānaṃ prakalpayet |  
vicitrāṇi tato madhye brahmāṇaṃ saṃprapūrayet ||  
  
rathobhistadyatho tebhyaḥ pāyasānnairvaliṃ haret |  
pāyasairmadhuraiḥ sarvān saṃyajenmadhurānvitaiḥ ||  
  
tattaddravyaivāmatimān pūjayeddoṣaśāṃtaye |  
pāṣāṇe pratimāyāṃvā vāstopateḥ pratijāni ||  
  
iti vaidika maṃtreṇa tasyā vāhana pūjanaṃ |  
nāmamaṃtreṇa cānyeṣāṃ pūjāṃ kṛtvā prapūrayet ||  
  
atha tāṃtrika mārge tu catuḥ ṣaṣṭipade tathā |  
koṇayoḥ sūtrayugalaṃ madhye brahmāṇa nirccayet ||  
  
p. 26b)  
  
catuḥkoṣṭheṣu tatpūrvādyāsu koṣṭha dvikedvithike |  
āryakaṃ ca vivasvaṃtaṃ mitramanyaṃ mahīdharaṃ ||  
  
sāvitraḥ savitāśakra induttidrudratarjayau |  
ayāyavatsakauceti śaivyāḥ koṇārddhakoṣṭayoḥ ||  
  
sarvaṃ grahaścāryamāṇaṃ bhaṃjakaṃ pilipicchakaṃ |  
carakiṃ ca vidārīṃ ca pūtanā pūrvato dvayoḥ ||  
  
īśānaścārthaparjanyojayaṃtaḥ śakrabhāskarau |  
saṃvyovṛṣoṃtarīkṣaśca pūrvāśākoṣṭagāstathā ||  
  
agniḥ pūṣā ca vitathoyamotha gṛharakṣakaḥ |  
gaṃdharvo bhṛṃgarājaśca mṛgodakṣiṇadiggatāḥ ||  
  
nair-ṛtiśca tathā dauvārikaḥ sugrīvakastathā |  
varuṇaḥ puṣpadaṃtaścāsuraḥ sopākhyarogakau ||  
  
paścādathottare vāyurnāgo mukhyastataḥ paraṃ |  
somabhallāḍhārgalākhyā aditirditiruttare ||  
  
brahmasthānaṃ raktavarṇairdiśaḥ pītairvidiksitaiḥ |  
tato diśastu haritairvidiśaḥ kṛṣṇavarṇakaiḥ ||  
  
aruṇaḥ paridhiḥ kāryaḥ suṃdaraṃ maṇḍalaṃ bhavet |  
uktānāṃ sarvadevānāṃ svarūpaṃ ca nigadyate ||  
  
akṣamālāṃ varaṃ dakṣe vāme daṇḍa kamaṇḍalu |  
dadhānamaṣṭa nayanaṃ yajenmadhyembujāsanaṃ ||  
  
sarve caturbhujādevā vāstudehe vyavasthitāḥ ||  
  
atha vāstu dhyānaṃ |  
  
ākuṃcitakaraṃ vāstumuttānamasurākṛtiṃ |  
smaren pūjāsu kudryādiniveśetva dharānanaṃ ||  
  
jānunī kūrparāśakte diśivāta hutāśayoḥ |  
yaidryāpādapraḍhau raudryāṃ śirosya hṛdayāṃjaliḥ ||  
  
kṛtāṃjalipuṭā ūrddhve khaḍgakheṭakapātayaḥ |  
brahmāṇaṃ sannirīkṣyeta tadvaktrābhimukhāścate ||  
  
svasvasthāna sthitāścaiva sādhāraṇamudāhṛtaṃ |  
marīciḥ śvetavarṇaḥ syādvivasvā ekavarṇakaḥ ||  
  
śātakuṃbhenibhomitraḥ kṛṣṇavarṇastu bhūdharaḥ |  
savittīnīlavarṇābhaḥ sāvitro dhūmavigrahaḥ ||  
  
iṃdraścāruṇa varṇābhaḥ śuklaścendra jayastathā |  
rudraḥ pravāla sadṛśaḥ pīto rudrajayastathā ||  
  
āpo gokṣīradhavalaḥ āpavatsojavādyutiḥ |  
īśānaḥ kṣīradhavalaḥ parjanyāṃ janasannibhaḥ ||  
  
jayaṃto janasaṃkāśo maheṃdraścāmaladyutiḥ |  
ādityo raktavarṇaḥ syāt satyakaścitravarṇakaḥ ||  
  
vṛṣo vaṃdhūka puṣpābhaḥ kuṃdābhaścāṃtarīkṣakaḥ |  
udyaddinakarābhogniḥ pūṣālaktāktasannibhaḥ ||  
  
p. 27a)  
  
vitathaśceṃdra cāpābho vidyudvarṇo gṛhakṣataḥ |  
yamaścāṃ jana saṃkāśo gaṃdharvaḥ padmarāgavat ||   
  
bhṛṃgarājastu bhṛṃmābhomṛgojīmūtasannibhaḥ |  
nir-ṛtiḥ pāvakākṣaścapīto dauvārikasmṛtaḥ ||  
  
sugrīva nīlakaṇṭhābhaścaṃdrābhaḥ puṣpadaṃtakaḥ |  
varuṇaḥ sphaṭikābhaśca bhṛṃgābhaścāvaromaromataḥ ||  
  
śeṣāścotpala saṃkāśo rogaścaiveṃdra nīlavat |  
vāyuḥ kṛṣṇātravarṇaḥ syurnnāgaḥ śaṃkhendusannibhaḥ ||  
  
mukhyā mauktikasaṃkāśo bhallāṭa śvetapadmavat |  
somaḥ sphaṭika saṃkāśo'rgaloraktotyalaghutiḥ ||  
  
diti kuṃdeṃdu dhavalā kapilā aditiḥ smṛtāḥ |  
carakī śaṃkhasadṛśī vidārī pāvakādyutiḥ ||  
  
pūtanā hima saṃkośo meghābhāpilapicchakī |  
khaḍgaṃ ca pāśapātraṃ ca churikāṃ kartakāṃ tathā ||  
  
dadhānā bhīmarūpāstārākṣasya parikīrtitāḥ |  
sitāraktaśca pītaśca kṛṣṇaḥ skaṃdādikā grahāḥ ||  
  
vajraṃ śaktiṃ ca khaḍgaṃ ca pāśaṃ ca vikṛtānatā |  
dadhānābhīṣaṇāḥ proktā grahāḥ skaṃdādi kāścate ||  
  
homādikaṃ tathā kuryāt svaiḥ svaiścāhutimādadet |  
vrīhimuṅgayavaiḥ kṣaudraḥ ghṛtadugdhaplutaiḥ kramāt ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ cāṣṭottara viṃśatimeva vā |  
pratyekaṃ tairhuneddravyairmaṃtraistadvacca pāyasaiḥ ||  
  
valiṃ ca teṣāṃ kurvīta pāyasairvyaṃjanātvitaiḥ |  
sasitairdugdhakadalīphalāpupādisaṃyutaiḥ ||  
  
valivadāya yet pūrvaṃ pūjayet sādhakastataḥ |  
annādibhiśca saṃyuktaṃ māṣabhaktyādi maṇḍitaṃ ||  
  
gṛhāṇemaṃ baliṃ brahman vāstudoṣaṃ praṇāśayaḥ |  
gaṃdhādi śarkarāpūpapāyaso parisaṃyutaṃ ||  
  
āryakākhya gṛhāṇemaṃ sarvadoṣaṃ praṇāśaya |  
caṃdanādyarcitanāthaḥ karpūrā gurumaṇḍite ||  
  
vivasvadvai gṛhāṇemaṃ sarvadoṣaṃ praṇāśaya |  
saguḍaṃpāyasaṃ nātha puṣpādi susamanvitaṃ ||  
  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyaṃ mitraśāṃtiṃ prayacchame |  
māṣodanaṃ samāṃse ca gaṃdhādikṣīra saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
gṛhāṇemaṃ mahībhṛtvaṃ sarvadoṣa praṇāśaya |  
evaṃ madhye tu saṃpūjya īśānādi valiṃ haret ||  
  
puṣpādi kuśakanīyaṃ śarkarā guru vā sitaṃ |  
sāvitra vai gṛhāṇemaṃ śāṃtimāśuprayacchame ||  
  
p. 27b)  
  
piṣṭakaṃ saguḍaṃ nāthaṃ raktagaṃdhādi śobhitaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ sūrya vighnamāśu praṇāśayaḥ ||  
  
śītamatraṃ tathā puṣpaṃ kuṃkumādi samanvitaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ baliṃ hṛdyaṃ śakradeva namostute ||  
  
odanaṃ ghṛtasaṃyuktaṃ vastragaṃdhādi maṃḍitaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ baliṃ hṛdyamiṃdra jananamostute ||  
  
pakvāpakvamidaṃ māṃsaṃ vastrapuṣpādi saṃyutaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyarudradeva namomyahaṃ ||  
  
samāṃ saghṛta saṃpakvagaṃdhapuṣpādi saṃyutaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ rudrajayasvasti namostute ||  
  
kṣīrakhaṇḍa samāyuktaṃ puṣpādibhiralaṃkṛtaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyamāpaśāṃtiṃ prayacchame ||  
  
dadhidaṃguḍasaṃmiśraṃgaṃdhādibhiḥ susaṃyutaṃ |  
gṛhāṇe valiṃ vatsa vighnametvaṃ pranāśaya ||  
  
saghṛtaṃ māṣabhaktaṃ ca raktagaṃdhādi saṃyutaṃ |  
baliṃ gṛhāṇa sarvatvaṃ rakṣavighnaṃ vināśayaḥ ||  
  
māsaṃ puṣpādi saṃyuktaṃ māsabhaktopasaṃyutaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ skaṃdarakṣavighnaṃ vināśaya ||  
  
svamāṃsaṃ piṣṭakairyuktaṃ pakvamāṃsodakānvitaṃ |  
aryaman vai gṛhāṇemaṃ sarvavighnaṃ vināśaya ||  
  
raktamaṃsodanaṃ matsyagaṃdha dhūpasamanvitaṃ |  
jaṃbhakatvaṃ gṛhāṇemaṃ rakṣavighnaṃ vināśaya ||  
  
chāgakarṇānvitaṃ māṃsaṃ vastragaṃdhādi saṃyutaṃ |  
pilipiccha gṛhāṇemaṃ rakṣavighnaṃ vināśaya ||  
  
ghṛtena sādhitaṃ māṃsaṃ vastragaṃdhādi saṃyutaṃ |  
carakitvaṃ gṛhāṇemaṃ rakṣavighnaṃ vināśaya ||  
  
raktapuṣpaṃ samāsaṃ vai raktavastrādi saṃyutaṃ |  
vidāri vai gṛhāṇemaṃ rakṣavipraṃ vināśaya ||  
  
pittaraktāsthitaṃ yuktaṃ raktagaṃdhādimaṃḍitaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ pūtanatvaṃ rakṣavighnaṃ vināśaya ||  
  
saghṛtaṃ cākṣataṃ puṣpavastra gaṃdhādyalaṃ kṛtaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ tvīśa vāstudoṣapahārakaḥ ||  
  
utpalaṃ pāyasairyuktaṃ vastrādika samanvitaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyaṃ devarāja namostute ||  
  
paṃcahastaṃ supītaṃ ca dhvajaṃ saṃkādimaṇḍitaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyaṃtiṣṇusuta namostute ||  
  
odanaṃ ghṛtasaṃpūrṇaṃ paṃca ** (?) di maṇḍitaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyaṃ devarāja namostute ||  
  
raktapuṣpayutaṃ bhaktaṃ raktagaṃdhādibhiryutaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyaṃ megharāja namostute ||  
  
vitānaṃ dhūmravarṇābhaṃ gaṃdhādi suśobhitaṃ |  
raktayuktaṃ gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ satya namostute ||  
  
p. 28a)  
  
idaṃ tu māṃsa bhaktaṃ vai vastragaṃdhādi pūjitaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ vṛṣa valiṃ vāstudoṣaṃ vināśaya ||  
  
idaṃ śārdūla māṃsaṃ tu naivedyādi susaṃyutaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyaṃ vyomaśāṃtiṃ prayachame ||  
  
suvarṇaṃ piṣṭakaṃ cātha vastragaṃdhādibhiryutaṃ |  
ghṛtānvitaṃ gṛhāṇemaṃ saptajihvanamostute ||  
  
kṣīraṃ lājā samāyuktaṃ gaṃdhapuṣpādi saṃyutaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyaṃ pūṣadeva namostute ||  
  
māṃsaudanaṃ gaṃdhamālyayutaṃ vastrādibhūṣitaṃ |  
vitathena valiṃ gṛhna vāstudoṣaṃ vināśaya ||  
  
matsyamāṃ sa yutaṃ bhaktaṃ gaṃdhapuṣpādyalaṃkṛtaṃ |  
yamarāja gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ śāṃtiṃ prayacchame ||  
  
pakvamāṃsaudana navanītaṃ vastrādi maṇḍitaṃ |  
prītikaraṃ gṛhāṇemaṃ gṛhana rakṣa namostute ||  
  
nānāgaṃdha samāyuktaṃ raktadhūpādibhiryutaṃ |  
valiṃ gṛhāṇa gaṃdharva sarvadoṣaṃ pranāśaya ||  
  
imāṃ tu sākunīṃ jihvāṃ māṣabhakto paristhitaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ bhṛṃgarājaṃ valiṃ śāṃtiṃ prayacchame ||  
  
evaṃ tilaghṛtoyetaṃ gaṃdhapuṣpādibhiryutaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyaṃ mṛgadev anamostute ||  
  
śarkarāmaṇḍitaṃ khaṇḍaṃ vastragaṃdhādyalaṃkṛtaṃ |  
prītovaliṃ gṛhāṇemaṃ rakṣarāja namostute ||  
  
caṃdanā gurukākhaṇḍa vastragaṃdhādibhiryutaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyaṃ dauvārikaṃ namostute ||  
  
idaṃ tu pāyasaṃ nātha gaṃdhapuṣpādi miśritaṃ |  
sugrīva vai gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ śāṃtiṃ prayacchame ||  
  
yavāgvalaṃ kṛtaṃ dugdhaṃ bhaktoparisamarpitaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyaṃ jaladeva namostute ||  
  
māṣabhaktaṃ kuśasthaṃ ca ghṛtagaṃdhādi saṃyutaṃ |  
puṣpadaṃta gṛhāṇemaṃ vāstudoṣaṃ pranāśaya ||  
  
madhunā sādhitaṃ piṣṭaṃ gaṃdhādyai rūpaśobhitaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ roga sarvadoṣa praṇāśaya ||  
  
sa ghṛtaṃ maṇḍakaṃ vedamaṃtrādyairupaśobhitaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyaṃ mṛgavāhanamostute ||  
  
idaṃ tu kṛśarānnaṃ me dugdhagaṃdhādi sādhitaṃ |  
pātāleśa gṛhāṇemaṃ vighnamāśu praṇāśaya ||  
  
nārikelādikaṃ bhaktaṃ pītavastrādi saṃyutaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ mukhya vāstudoṣaṃ praṇāśaya ||  
  
dadhigaṃdhādibhiryuktaṃ pītapuṣpasamanvitaṃ |  
valiṃ pragṛhyatāṃ somaḥ sarvadoṣaṃ praṇāśaya ||  
  
odanaṃ ghṛta saṃmiśraṃ gaṃdhapuṣpa samanvitaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyaṃ bhallāṭakanamostute ||  
  
p. 28b)  
  
māṣānnaṃ tu ghṛtāttyaktuṃ gaṃdhapuṣpādimaṇḍitaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyamargalākhya namostute ||  
  
pālikāṃ madhusaṃmiśrāṃ vastragaṃdhādi saṃyutaṃ |  
gṛhāṇemaṃ valiṃ hṛdyaṃ devamātarnamostute ||  
  
kṣīrakhaṇḍa samāyuktaṃ nānāpūjāpaśobhitaṃ |  
daityamātargṛhāṇemaṃ sarvadoṣaṃ praṇāśaya ||  
  
svargapātāla martyeṣu ye devāvāstu devatāḥ |  
gṛhnaṃtvimaṃ baliṃ hṛdyaṃ tuṣṭāyāṃ tu svamaṃdira ||  
  
mātaro būtavetālāye cānye valikāṃkṣiṇaḥ |  
viṣṇoḥ pariṣadāye ca tepi gṛhnaṃtvimaṃ baliṃ ||  
  
pitṛbhyaḥ kṣetrapālebhyo valiṃ datvā prakāmataḥ |  
abhāvādukta mārgasya kuśapuṣpādibhiryajet ||  
  
vāstuśeṣa kriyā bhūtaḥ sarvarakṣā vibhūtikṛt |  
bhūtaprīti pradaścāsmindiśā balirudīryate ||  
  
dikpāla pariṣat sarvabhūtānuddiśyanāmabhiḥ |  
pūjā visarjanāṃtāyatsa vijñeyo diśāṃ valiḥ ||  
  
dadhyaṃvu rajanī yutvā jāsaktuṃ tileṃdhasā |  
dravyeṇa vitaredikṣu valiṃ dikku sa yorgataḥ ||  
  
surāṇāṃ tejasāṃ caiva pretānāṃ rākṣasāmapi |  
devyā jālānāṃ prāṇānāṃ nakṣatrāṇāṃ ca tatpunaḥ ||  
  
vidyānāmadhipānāṃ ca tānyathoktān valiṃ haret |  
sa vāhana pada proktā parivārāya śaktaye ||  
  
tatpārṣadebhyaśca tataḥ sarvebhya iti saṃyutaṃ |  
bhūtebhyaśca kramādbhūyaḥ prācyāṃdiśi kṣipedvaliṃ ||  
  
dviṣatpiśācavetālarakṣorakṣārthināmiha |  
deśāṃvali viśeṣeṇa sarvasaṃpat samṛddhidāṃ ||  
  
devī devaviśeṣāṇi karme kṛtvā su maṃtriṇā |  
mahāvali pradānena prasṛte desamaṇḍale ||  
  
kuchālaṃ cāstramaṃtreṇa pūjayet parameśvarī |  
khanitaḥ puruṣāyāpi dāpayed dakṣiṇādibhiḥ ||  
  
hīnāṃgavarjanīya ca avatyāṃ caiva varjayet |  
tatkṣaṇānmṛttikāṃ bhūmivasudhoddṛtya pūjayet ||  
  
dvibhujepītta dehastu jagadhārikaṃ jāsamaḥ |  
viśvakarmāgadāsauyājñānamudrākṣa sūtrabhṛt ||  
  
viśvakarma jagadvyāpi saṃsāra sṛṣṭikārakaḥ |  
atra kudālahastatvaṃ viśvakarmā namostute ||  
  
ekāśīkoṣṭha nirbheda cāstau viśvātmakarmakaḥ |  
kuddāra gṛhatāṃ maṃtrakhananaṃ kuru sāṃprataṃ ||  
  
bhadramuhūrtamāśritya khanyate vāstu koṣṭake |  
svarṇakuddāra rūpatvaṃ bhūmikhanana karmaṇi ||  
  
viśvakarmāyudhaṃ nityaṃ namostu vāstumūrtaye |  
kuddārairdāpayittopi kīṭakoṭi śatairapi ||  
  
p. 29a)  
  
kṣamyato pṛthivī devī viṣṇusthāpana hetave |  
śubhāśubhāni vāstūnāṃ krameṇaiva vadāmyahaṃ ||  
  
kakṣāṃtare ca nityaṃ ca sarvatra bhadramādṛśe |  
śīrṣe caiva bhavenmṛtyuḥ vakṣaṃ ca duḥkhabhāgināṃ ||  
  
haste caurabhayaṃ vidyāt urayā paśunāśanaṃ |  
jñānau videśagamanaṃ pādābhyāṃ ca nirarthakaṃ ||  
  
vāmadakṣiṇa nityevaṃ vāstukṣetamudīrita |  
nipuṇaṃ kārayenmaṃtrī kalyāṇaṃ pauṣṇatāṃ kṛtaṃ ||  
  
samāhita samo bhūtvā khanite vāstukakṣate ||  
  
atha visarjanamaṃtraḥ ||  
  
tato visarjayeddevī devān vāstu prapūjitān |  
yāṃ tu devagaṇāḥ sarve pūjāmādāya pārthivīṃ ||  
  
iṣṭakāma prasiddhyarthaṃ punarāgamanāya ca |  
ityetat kathitaṃ devī vāstuyāgasya rakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
sarvapāpaharaṃ caiva sarvakāma prapūrakaṃ |  
evāsuraṃ ca vāstūnāṃ prakāreṇāga vāstukaṃ ||  
  
ekāśīti pade koṣṭamīśanair-ṛtyamaṇḍalaṃ |  
īśeśirastathā pucchaṃ maṇḍalākāra vāstu sa ||  
  
koṣṭhe ca devatā pūjyaṃ madhye brahmā prapūjayet |  
bhādrapadādi sarvasyāmāsi māsi trayaṃ trayaṃ ||  
  
digānāmiśamādini ca rataṃ ca vidhīyate |  
kanyādi saṃkramaṃ jñātvā digānāṃ ca kramoragāḥ ||  
  
tulāmithunapūrvādirāśvinī kārtike tathā |  
evaṃ krameṇa saṃyātā mārgaśīrṣaṃ ca pauṣakaṃ ||  
  
māghamāsāṃtakaṃ cakre dhanūrmakarakuṃbhakaṃ |  
mīnameṣa vṛṣau caiva phālguṇaṃ caitrameva ca ||  
  
vaiśākhāṃta kramaṃ jñātvā paścimādiṣu vā kramaṃ |  
mithune karkaṭaḥ siṃhau jyeṣṭhāṣāḍhāṃ ca śrāvaṇaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ kramaṃ prabudhyaṃ tanāgānāṃ vāstu saṃkramaṃ |  
prayaṃtrayopi māsāni catuṣṭaya diśākrama ||  
  
svapitaṃ vāma pārśvaṃte dvibhujaṃ navabhiḥ phaṇā |  
ekāśikoṣṭha cāṃgāni vyāpakaṃ nāgavāstu sa ||  
  
khanitaṃ grīva vāmāgre nipuṇaṃ kārayetsudhīḥ |  
evaṃ nāgasya vāstūni jalakārya viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
athavā nirmite gehe vāstu pūjāṃ samārabhet |  
nair-ṛtyakoṇe gehesyahesya caturasrākṛtiṃ śubhāṃ ||  
  
kṛtvā samatalāṃ bhūmiṃ vitastyuccāṃ ca vedikāṃ |  
vistārāyāmato hastamātrāṃ tatra likhedbudhaḥ ||  
  
ekāśīti pade koṣṭhe lekhayecchuchabhumiṣu |  
svaiḥ svaiḥ maṃtrastu vāstvādān pūjayet pūrvavat sudhīḥ ||  
  
evaṃ siṃhagate bhānau pūrṇāyāṃ prativatsaraṃ |  
svagehe vāstu pūjāṃ yo maṇḍapeṣu samācaret ||  
  
p. 29b)  
  
navālamaraṇaṃ vyādhi bhūtapretādikāni ca |  
na sarpapīḍāmanyonya kalahādya śubhāni ca ||  
  
putrapautra dhanārogya paśudāsī samṛddhibhāk |  
arogī vijayīkhyātaściraṃ jīvati tadgṛhe ||  
  
rājaveśmasu sarvatra tathā ca mahiṣī gṛhe |  
sacivāmātyasenānībhavaneṣu pure tathā ||  
  
vidadhyāt prativarṣeaṃ tu prokta siddhyai tu deśikaḥ |  
na ceduktānyathā rūpaphalaiḥ kleśo niśaṃ bhavet ||  
  
bhairava kṣetrapālānāṃ yoginīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ |  
vāmācārairvaliḥ kāryā mahiṣairvāpi kukkuṭaiḥ ||  
  
ārādhitāstu vāmena jāyaṃteti vubhukṣitāḥ |  
devatā valimicchaṃti taddhīnaṃ haṃti sādhakaṃ ||  
  
madyamāṃsa pramattāste proktanena pracoditāḥ |  
kadācicchubhamicchaṃti tasmāt sadbhinna vāmataḥ ||  
  
kriyatebhyarcanaṃ tāsāṃ ghātastu nikaṭe yataḥ |  
śubhaṃ bhavati vā no vādyathā śāstre tathājane ||  
  
yāvanna madyamāṃsāsījanastāvada valolupaḥ |  
bhukte tasmin tanmanāḥ syāt kvajapaḥ kvacaṃ devatāḥ ||  
  
madyamāṃsādikatyāgāttasyāvāti niṣevaṇāt |  
dṛśyate tulyarūpoyaḥ sa siddhonyastu pātakī ||  
  
evaṃ parīkṣya kartavyā siddhānāmapi saṃgatiḥ |  
tatsaṃsargī paṃcamoyamanya saṃgena gaṇyate ||  
  
kālarūpeṇa kalanāgītā gītāgāthāvidheḥ puraḥ |  
mayyadhairyādvṛṣo naśyettṛṣṇayādvau vinaśyataḥ ||  
  
dhāturvādāṃ trayaṃ naśyet sarvanāśastu vāmataḥ |  
iti saṃciṃtya bhodevāḥ svadharmaḥ śreyase bhavet ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau vāstuyāganirṇayo nāma saptamaḥ prakāśaḥ || 7 ||  
  
vāstu śāṃtiṃ vidhāyaivaṃ sadasadjñāna hetave |  
tataḥ samīkṛtāyāṃ tu bhūmaudivasā dhanaṃ caret ||  
  
sūtrakarkaṭakīlāni gṛhītvā ca niśāṃtare |  
ādyaṃtaraṃ ca saṃyuktānalikā dhruvavedhiyā ||  
  
yāmyottarāsā tanmadhye keṃdrāvṛttaṃ samālikhet |  
rekhāṃ tato vṛttamadhye te makarkāṭakena tu ||  
  
dhanuḥ kuryāttataścāyaṃ tataḥ kuryāddhanuḥ punaḥ |  
evaṃ cāpāni ṣaṭ tatra padmaṃ bhavati ṣaḍdalaṃ ||  
  
saumye yāmya trayaṃ kṛtvā datvānāṃ madhyadeśataḥ |  
dīrghārekhākṛtā sā tu bhavet pūrvā parābhidhā ||  
  
yāmya paścimayoḥ saumya pūrvayoruparisthayoḥ |  
cāpayorarddhagaṃ sūtramīśānīrākṣasī bhavet ||  
  
p. 30a)  
  
anyayoścā payorevamāgneyo vāyavī bhavet |  
vidiktaṃ sthāni sūtrāṇi samānyeva hi vṛttataḥ ||  
  
yatheṣṭaṃ vahirānīyanikhanet tatra kīlakān |  
vaddhaṃ caturṇāṃ kīlānāṃ mastake dṛḍhasūtrakaṃ ||  
  
samakarṇaṃdigaṃkaṃ tacchuddaṃ syāccaturasrakaṃ |  
gaṇeśaṃ pūjayitvādau puṇyāhaṃ vācayet sudhīḥ ||  
  
tataḥ paṃcavinānaiśca maṃḍapaṃ racayecchubhaṃ |  
maṇḍapaṃ kuladīkṣāyāṃ kuryādviṃśati hastakaṃ ||  
  
madyamāṃsapuraṃdhrīṇāṃ samāveśo yathā bhavet |  
maṃḍapoṣṭā daśakalaḥ siddhāṃte vāmamārgake ||  
  
alpatvāt tatra kuṇḍānāṃ madhikepi sa paṃcake |  
vaidikya vahusāmāgryāṃ navakuṃḍe tu ṣoḍaśaḥ ||  
  
kuṃḍālpatāyāṃ sāmagryāmalpayācendrahastakaḥ |  
dakṣiṇe vahu sāmagryāṃ sūryahastaṃ tu maṃḍapaḥ ||  
  
alpāyāṃ daśahastaḥ syānnavahastaḥ sadāviśāṃ |  
śūdrāṇāṃ saptahastaḥ syācchaṃkarāṇāṃ tu paṃca ca ||  
  
proktaṃ mānaṃ maṃḍapānāṃ sarvataṃtreṣu gopitaṃ |  
proktā nānāvidhā hastāstannirṇayamatha śṛṇu ||  
  
yasmindeśe ca kāle ca sapmutpanno yathā yavā |  
teṣāmaṣṭādarārṇāsyādaṃgulaṃ tu dvijanmanāṃ ||  
  
samodaraistu śūdrāṇāṃ saṃkarādau tathā rasaiḥ |  
avaidikasya viprāderetatsaṃkhyākaśālibhiḥ ||  
  
yatra kartā svayaṃ tatra māname tadanyatonyathā |  
ācarya dakṣiṇakare madhyamāṃguli madhyamaṃ ||  
  
parvaṇāraṃtaraṃ dīrghaṃ mātrāṃgulamudāhṛtaṃ |  
ucchrāya pratimāyāśca prāsāde * ? stu nirmitiḥ ||  
  
vedikāpīṭha śivikārathādye tatpramāṇataḥ |  
vināṃguṣṭhena śeṣābhirmuṣṭiraṃgulibhiḥ kṛtaḥ ||  
  
caturdhā vibhajedekobhāgo muṣṭāṃgulaṃ tu tat |  
homāṃgāni śruvādīni kuṇḍasthaṇḍila vedikāḥ ||  
  
yajñopavītamauṃjāḍhyaṃ kuryān muṣṭyaṃgulena tu |  
yaṃ kaṃ citpauruṣāyāmaṃ vibhajya daśadhā punaḥ ||  
  
evaṃ dvādaśabhāgaṃ tu kṛtvā teṣṭe kamaṇḍaluṃ |  
dehalabdhāṃgulaṃ nāmajānīyāttasya tatpunaḥ ||  
  
ebhiścaturviṃśatibhirhastaḥ syādaṃgulaiḥ punaḥ |  
anena pratimāṃgāni satapunmānmeva ca ||  
  
narāṇāṃ cāpi nārīṇāṃ kuryādgopyaṃ prakāśitaṃ |  
caturdaśakaraṃ koṭi home saṃpatti saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
anyathā dvādaśakaraṃ rakṣahome tu diktaraṃ |  
maṇḍapaṃ navadhā kṛtvā madhyabhāgasyavedikā ||  
  
p. 30b)  
  
staṃbhāstuvedikākoṇe maṃḍapādhau sthitā vahiḥ |  
paṃcamāṃ sanyasedbhūmaupuṣṭatāsāṃśa sūtrataḥ ||  
  
mastake kalaśākāraṃ taddśāṃśena kārayet |  
svāyāmoccābhavedvedī navakoṣṭhotthasaṃdhiṣu ||  
  
maṃḍapasya tṛtīyāṃśaṃ dīrghānstaṃbhān suvinyaset |  
dvādaśaivaṃ tu paṃcāśo bhūmau kūṭaṃ dadyāṃśataḥ ||  
  
madhyastaṃbhasthitaṃ kūṭaṃ mṛdaṃ yābhaṃ prakalpayet |  
vāhyastaṃbhorddhato deyā valayodvādaśairbahiḥ ||  
  
dakṣadīkṣāvidhau padmanibhaṃ kūṭaṃ tu kārayet |  
tridhāraṃ vāmadīkṣāyāṃ śaṃkhābhaṃ vaiṣṇavemakhe ||  
  
caturasrā catuḥ koṇāvedī sarvaphalapradā |  
taḍāgādi pratiṣṭhāyāṃ padminī patrasannibhā ||  
  
rājñāṃ syāt sarvato bhadrā caturbhadrābhiṣecane |  
vivādve śrīdharādevī viṃśatyastra samanvitā ||  
  
vāmamārgeṇa dīkṣāyāṃ guptādyastrā tu vedikā |  
staṃbhānāmupūristhāpyānya vraṇāni ṛjūni ca ||  
  
ekajātīni kāṣṭhāni vidyāstaṃbhagalenyaset |  
nārikeladalairvaśaḥkaṭairācchādayet punaḥ ||  
  
huṃhā māruta vṛṣṭyādi bhavanaḥ syādyathā tathā ||  
  
pūrvoktasaṃsādhita dikṣu kuryādvārāṇi catvāri tu maṇḍapasya |  
paṃcāṃśamānā khalu dehalīsyādvi procchite tatra kapādvaśākhe ||  
  
vāmamārgedvāramidaṃ dakṣiṇe śreṣṭhamaṇḍape |  
kuryāddohalikāṃ ramyāṃ sāṣṭhāṃgulakaradvayaṃ ||  
  
  
vitastyāconnavaśikhaṃ dvārastho bhayapārśvayoḥ |  
sthāpayet phalakaudvau tu śreṣṭhamadhye kaniṣṭhake ||  
  
maṃḍapetau dīrghatayā kramāt sārddhakaradvayaṃ |  
sapāda dvitayaṃ yugmahasta paṃcāṃśakaṃ bhuvi ||  
  
nikhanedagnimīḍeti gāyatryā pārśvayordvayoḥ |  
tatsajātīyakāṣṭena tāvadvistāragarbhakaṃ ||  
  
caturasraṃ tu viṣamaṃ dvayorūpani kīlayet |  
darbhamālā ca vadhnīyāt pūrvadvāre vidhisvayaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ tu dakṣiṇadvāre tadvāreplakṣakoṣṭhajaṃ |  
iṣetvetinyasenmālāṃ vaṃdhayet pūrvakastathā ||  
  
auduṃvaramayaṃ kuryāt paścimadvāratastvidaṃ |  
agnenyā yā hi maṃtreṇa plekṣajaṃ vaidikemakhe ||  
  
prāgvadevaṃ prakurvīta vaṭavṛkṣamayaṃ tathā |  
śannodevīti maṃtreṇa saumyadigdvārato nyaset ||  
  
teṣāmuparitiryaksthaḥ kāṣṭhānāṃ madhyato vilaṃ |  
kṛtvā toraṇa jātīya koṣṭhe caracayechuddhaṃ ||  
  
p. 31a)  
  
śreṣṭha madhye jaghanyeṣu śaivayāge triśūlakaṃ |  
viśveśagoṃgulaṃ dīrghaṃ taccaturthośa vistṛtaṃ ||  
  
vaiṣṇave dvādaśāṃśe nā śaṃkhacakragadāṃvujaṃ |  
prāgādi kramayogena nyaset sauropi vaiṣṇavaḥ ||  
  
ṛjuvai madhyamaṃ śṛṃgaṃ kiṃcidvaktraṃ tu pārśvayoḥ |  
evaṃ śūlo gaṇapatiḥ śivādyāḥ śivavatmatāḥ ||  
  
tatastu maṃḍapaḥ syāgre bhūmbūrddhvaṃ daśahastakaṃ |  
bhūmau karadvayaṃ vaṃśaḥ svacchavastrā ca guṃṭhitaḥ ||  
  
vistṛtaścaika hastena dīrghaḥ paṃcakarairddhvajaḥ |  
maṃtradevaṃ likhet tatra sāyudhaṃ ca savāhanaṃ ||  
  
ghaṃṭācāmarasaṃyuktaṃ devatāvarṇavarṇakaṃ |  
sthāpayitvā dhvajaṃ paścād daśadikṣu prakalpayet ||  
  
digīśānāṃ patākāśca dhvajasyārddha pramāṇataḥ |  
vedokta tattanmaṃtreṇa tattadvarṇāśca taddiśi ||  
  
trātāramiṃdramiti ca pītavarṇāharediśi |  
āgneyyā piṃgalātvanno agnervaruṇa maṃtrataḥ ||  
  
sugaṃdhapaṃthā manunā kṛṣṇavarṇātvayā smṛtā |  
asutvaṃtepi manunā nair-ṛtyāṃ dhūmravarṇikā ||  
  
tatvāyāti brahmaṇeti vāruṇyāṃsita varṇikā |  
ānomiyudbhiriti ca vāyavyāṃ haritā bhavet ||  
  
vayaḥ somavrata iti saumyāyāṃ caṃdravarṇikā |  
tamīśānamitīśānyāmativiśvetāpatākikā ||  
  
īśāna pūrvayormadhye śeṣaraktapatākinaṃ |  
toyanair-ṛtya madhye tu vidhiṃ raktapatākinaṃ ||  
  
vāmamārge vedamaṃtro vajrapāta samaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
brahmaṇānāṃ vāmamārgo narakāyaiva jāyate ||  
  
maṃtrābhāvenāma maṃtrān praṇavādyāṃchataṃtakān |  
pathe dakṣiṇamārge tu vāme praṇava varjitān ||  
  
maṇḍapo parivadhnīyādatiśvetaṃ vitānakaṃ |  
alaṃkuryāt puṣpamālādibhirenaṃ tu veṣṭayet ||  
  
āmrāśvattha dalotpannāyuktayā dīrghamālayā |  
staṃbhādukulasaṃveṣṭya madhye kuryācca vedikāṃ ||  
  
iṣṭikābhira pakvābhirhastavistṛti piṇḍakāṃ |  
maṇḍapāyāma rudrāṃśa * * * ? pteṣu rāmakaiḥ ||  
  
aśaiḥ samunnatāṃ vāpi mānamasya vilokya ca |  
sāmagryādessamāveśo yathā syāditi maṇḍapaḥ ||  
  
ayutāhuti homastu vidheyaḥ sthaṇḍilopari |  
ekahastamitaṃ kuṇḍaṃ daśarakṣāvadhi smṛtaṃ ||  
  
lakṣāṇāṃ daśarenaikaṃ hastahastaṃ vivarddhayet |  
daśahastaṃ koṭihomevaidikānāmitīritaṃ ||  
  
p. 31b)  
  
madyamāṃsādi homastu kuṇḍa eva vidhīyate |  
paṃcāśat pramite home prakoṣṭakṛta muṣṭikaṃ ||  
  
kuṇḍasyamānaṃ bhavati śateratni samaṃ bhavet |  
sahasraṃ hastamātre syāt dvihastamayutemataṃ ||  
  
caturhastamitaṃ lakṣe ṣaḍdalaṃ daśalakṣake |  
koṭi homecāṣṭahastaṃ kuṇḍaṃ vāmairvidhīyate ||  
  
ekakuṇḍavidhāne tu caturasraṃ vidhīyate |  
brāhmaṇānāṃ viśeṣeṇa staṃbhane cāpi pūrvataṃ ||  
  
navavidhāne tu vahnibhāge bhagākṛtiḥ |  
bhogārthaṃ cāpi putrārthaṃ vāsinā caturasravat ||  
  
arddhacaṃdranibhaṃvānya vaiśyānāṃ sarvakarmaṇi |  
anyeṣāṃ māraṇe proktaṃ catuḥkuṇḍe tatheṣyati ||  
  
trikoṇakuṇḍaṃ nair-ṛtyaṃ ripughātakaraṃ smṛtaṃ |  
vidveṣakārayāṃ caitachūdrāṇāṃ ca viśiṣyate ||  
  
vṛttaṃ mukhyaṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ śāṃti karmaṇi |  
paścimāyāṃ tu tatkāryaṃ vauddhārīṇāṃ ca siddhidaṃ ||  
  
ṣaṭkoṇa muccāṭayati chedeṣu ca viśiṣyate |  
vāyavyāṃ kārayet tacca saṃkarāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
udīcyāṃ pauṣṭike padmaṃ vṛṣṭidaṃ tuṣṭidaṃ tathā |  
sarvaprayogeṣṭhanayā paraprītikaraṃ mataṃ ||  
  
aṣṭakoṇaṃ muktikaramaiśānyāṃta vidhīyate |  
kārāgṛhāt tathā rogyācciṃtāde mokṣamāpnuyāt ||  
  
aṣṭakuṇḍavidhāne tu kramoyaṃ navakuṇḍake |  
navamaṃ caturasraṃ syāt pūrveśā na digaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
vidhāne paṃca kuṃḍānāmīśāne paṃca saṃbhavet |  
samakuṇḍavidhāne tu na khāto vedike vahi ||  
  
anyadeka paṃcakoṇamabhicāra vināśanaṃ |  
tathānyat saptakoṇaṃ ca kuṃḍabhūta nirkṛtane ||  
  
athādau caturasrasya kuṃḍasya vidhirucyate |  
nābhi yoni samāyuktaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ kuṇḍaṃ trimekhalaṃ ||  
  
dvimekhalaṃ tu śūdrāṇā śaṃkarāṇāṃ tu mekhalaṃ |  
yāvat kuṇḍasya vistāraḥ khananaṃ tāvadeva hi ||  
  
yāvat kuṃḍamiheṣṭasyāttāvaddiktādhanekṛte |  
caturasraṃ samaṃ kuryāt sumakarṇaṃ ca śilpacet ||  
  
ekahastasyayaḥ karṇobhujāste tu karadvayaṃ |  
dvihastasya tu karṇasyā trihastabhujasaṃmiti ||  
  
caturhastādike pyevaṃ kaṃṭhaḥ sarvatra bhūsamaṃ |  
jinabhāga samāstasya vahiḥ kāryāstu mekhalā ||  
  
dvādaśāṃgu vistārādyot sedhāccaturaṃgulā |  
tadurddhamaparādīrghāḥ ṣṭāṃgulātāca dṛccatā ||  
  
p. 32a)  
  
caturbhiraṃgulairdīrghātāvaduccātadūrddhataḥ |  
dairghyāt sūryāṃgulāṃ yonistryaṃśonā vistareṇa tu ||  
  
ekāṃgulocchritāsātu praviṣṭābhyaṃtare tathā |  
kuṃbhadvaya samādyuktā cāśvatthadalavanmatā ||  
  
aṃguṣṭha mekhalā yuktā madhye vāhyadhṛtiḥ kṣamā |  
yonyāstu paścimebhāge mekhalā tritayā vahi ||  
  
caturasraṃ bhavet pīṭhaṃ kuṇḍaṣaṣṭāṃśa vistṛtaṃ |  
tāvaddīrghaṃ tathoccaṃ ca tālaṃ tanmadhyato nayet ||  
  
yoni madhyetha tadvṛttaṃ kuṇḍaṣaṣṭhāṃśamānataḥ |  
prāgagnicānya kuṇḍānā proktāyo nirudaṅmukhī ||  
  
śeṣāḥ pūrvamukhāyoni kuṇḍeyoniṃ ca varjayet |  
kuṇḍamadhyestha keṃdrā tu kuryāt karkaṭakena tu ||  
  
prasāritenavyāsārka bhāgatulyena tatparaṃ |  
ṣaṣṭhāṃśena tu vṛttaṃ syāt pūrvavṛttaṃ tu karṇikā ||  
  
karṇikāgre vāhya vṛttābhyaṃtareṣṭa dalāni tu |  
evaṃ ṣaḍaṃgulorccaḥ syānnābhirvedākhamīritaṃ ||  
  
iṣṭasya caturasrasya jināṃśo bhaga ucyate |  
sapādaiḥ paṃcabhirbhāgairmadhye sūtraṃ vivardhayet ||  
  
prācyāmatha prakuryācca caturthā caturasrakaṃ |  
madhyato bhrāmayet kakāṭakaṃ paścimasaṃsthayoḥ ||  
  
arddhacāpākṛtiṃ rudraṃ vahirdiśyostadagrataḥ |  
cihnāṃtaṃ pātayet sūtraṃ hayorapi tadā bhavet ||  
  
aśvatthadalasaṃkāśaṃ yonikuṇḍa mudaṅmukhaṃ |  
prāṅmānāścātra kartavyā yonirūpāḥ sumekhalāḥ ||  
  
caturasrīkṛtaṃ kṣetraṃ daśadhāpi bhajedvudhaḥ |  
ekamekaṃ tvajedeśamadha ūrddhve ca taṃtravit ||  
  
jyāsūtraṃ pātayedagretanmānāddhāmayet tataḥ |  
arddhacaṃdranibhaṃ kuṇḍaṃ ramaṇīyamidaṃ bhavet ||  
  
atra tadyāmya pṛṣṭasyādekaṃ tanmāraṇāya ca |  
saumyapṛṣṭaṃ tatonyatra yoniḥ paścimadignatā ||  
  
agraṃ prāktibhuje kāryaṃ laṃvāstulyā trayopi ca |  
sāṃtaraṃ sarvataṃtreṣu proktapatra niraṃtaraṃ ||  
  
ekahaste tu hastādyā bhujo bhūddvādaśābdayaḥ |  
dvihastadvautrayaṃ paṃcatrihastedyarka bhūmayaḥ ||  
  
caturhastatrayaṃ caṃdraḥ paṃcahaste triśeṣarāḥ |  
ṣaḍasredryabdarānāścanagebhyākṛtisāgarā ||  
  
aṣṭahastekṛtā gakṣmādeva viśvāgnaṃyogavi |  
vedāti dhṛti yugmāni daśahastabhujā ime ||  
  
vyāsārddhaṃ caturasrasya svasyāṣṭādaśabhāgayuk |  
tāvat karkāṭakādvṛttaṃvṛttakuṇḍamihocyate ||  
  
p. 32b)  
  
racayeccaturasrasyavyāsārddhe nṛpabhāgayuk |  
tāvat karkaṭake nāpi kuryādvṛttaṃ manoharaṃ ||  
  
tena karkaṭamānena cihnaṣaṭkaṃ ca pūrvavat |  
kṛtvā tatra bhujāndatvā kuṇḍamevaṃ ṣaḍasravat ||  
  
iṣṭasya caturasrasya caturviṃśāṃka kalpanāṃ |  
kṛtvā tanmadhyataḥ sūryabhogakarkāṭakena ca ||  
  
vṛttaṃ kuryāt punaḥ sārddhaṃ tithibhāgairdvitīyakaṃ |  
digvidikcāṃtarāle ca sūtrāṇyaṣṭau prapātayet ||  
  
tatoṃtarvṛttarekhāyā īśaḥ sūtrāgrasūtrakaḥ |  
rekhāṃ nayedvāhyavṛtte pūrvasūtrasya mūrddhani ||  
  
tato dakṣiṇarekhāyāmaṃtarvṛttasya mūrddhani |  
tāmānayeddalaṃ tasyādevamaṣṭadalāni ca ||  
  
aṃśavyā sārddhakenāpi yadvṛttaṃ sā tu karṇikā |  
tataḥ ṣaḍaṃgavyā sārddhavṛttena tatkeśarāṇi ca ||  
  
vyāsa ṣaṣṭhāṃ samānocca karṇikākeśarāṇi ca |  
gurūkta yuktyā nikhanedyathā padmākṛtirbhavet ||  
  
padmākṛtiṃ prakurvīta kaṇṭhamekhalayā saha |  
kāryaṃ tathācārukābhiścaturasra samaṃ yathā ||  
  
atheṣṭa caturasrasya vyāsaḥ svadvādaśāṃśayuk |  
tenaiva bhrāmayedvṛttaṃ cihnānyatradigaṣṭake ||  
  
kramānnyasettaduparibhujāndadyāt samāniti |  
aṣṭāsraṃ jāyate kuṇḍatadvatkaṇṭhaścamekhalā ||  
  
iṣṭasya caturasrasya vyāsārddhasvanagāṃśayuk |  
tadvyāsārddhena tat tasyāt tatra cihnāni paṃca tu ||  
  
samabhāgena deyāni teṣu sūtrāṇi dāpayet |  
jyārūpāṇi dhanurlopā kuṇḍaṃ paṃcāsrakaṃ bhavet ||  
  
iṣṭasya caturasrasya vyāsārddhaṃ paṃcamāṃśayuk |  
bhrāmayettenaṣṭattaṃtu saptādānāṃkanātu tat ||  
  
khyātānyetāni kuṇḍāni tāṃtrike smārtakarmaṇi |  
anādhikānyakaṇṭhāni viyonīti śrutīrite ||  
  
ācārya kuṇḍaṃ navamaṃ caturasraṃ tu vedike |  
aṣṭāśaktau tu catvāri dikṣu kuṇḍāni tāṃtrike ||  
  
tadaśaktāvekameva caturasraṃ prakalpayet |  
śaktyā upāsane vāmapāthyaikaṃ yoni kuṇḍakaṃ ||  
  
amekadoṣadaṃ kuṇḍaṃ mānaṃ nyūnādhikaṃ yadi |  
tasmāt samyakparīkṣyedaṃ kartavyaṃ śubhamicchatā ||  
  
khātādhike bhavedrogī hīne dhenudhanakṣayaḥ |  
cakrakuṇḍe tu saṃtāpo maraṇacchinnamekhale ||  
  
mekhalārahite śokopyadhikevitta saṃkṣayaḥ |  
bhāryā vināśakaṃ kuṇḍaṃ proktayonyā vinā kṛtaṃ ||   
  
p. 33a)  
  
apatyadhvasanaṃ proktaṃ kuṇḍaṃ yatkaṇṭhavarjitaṃ |  
śṛṃgārarahitaṃ yacca kuṇḍaṃ jarjaramekhalaṃ ||  
  
yajamāna vināśāya proccāṭaḥ sphaṭike bhavet |  
sūcādhikesu hṛdveṣaḥ sūtrahīne daridratā ||  
  
anāle jaṭhare rogaḥ chidre kuḍetva vācyatāṃ |  
yathokta kuṇḍepyutpātādevaṃ jāte phalaṃtvidaṃ ||  
  
ṣaṭvāṇāddhirvahni netramitāḥ syuḥ paṃcamekhalā |  
dharmabhede jātibhede vācārya yajamānayoḥ ||  
  
ṣaṣṭīśenāṣṭamāṃśena mekhalā dvitayaṃ mataṃ |  
kaulike vāmamārge ca vauddhejaine ca śāvare ||  
  
kuṇḍānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ sruksruvā lakṣaṇaṃ tataḥ |  
prakalpayet sruvaṃ yoge vakṣyamāṇena vartmanā ||  
  
kālaskareṇāmalakī parā śakhadirairapi |  
suvarṇarūpya tāmrairvā ayobhirapi kārayet ||  
  
sruksruvautaijasaugrāhyau na kāsyāgra salīsakau |  
yajñadārumayo vāpi tāṃtrikau śilpi saṃmatau ||  
  
parṇe vā brahma vṛkṣāderacchidre madhya ucchrite |  
dhīparṇī siṃsapākṣīraśākhiṣvekatasaṃ guruḥ ||  
  
gṛhītvā vibhajeddhastamātrāṃ śaṭtriṃśatāpunaḥ |  
viṃśatyaṃśairbhaveddaṇḍo vaidikairaṣṭa * * * ?  ||  
  
ekāṃśenamitaḥ kaṃṭhaḥ saptabhāgamukhaṃ mataṃ |  
vedī tryaṃśena vistāraḥ kaṃṭhasya parikīrtitaḥ ||  
  
atra kaṃṭhaḥ samānaḥ syānmukhe mārge prakalpayet |  
kaniṣṭhāṃgulamānena sarpiṣo nirgamāya ca ||  
  
vedī madhye vidhātavyo bhāgenaikenakarṇikā |  
vidadhīstavahīstasyā ekāṃśenābhito'vaṭaṃ ||  
  
tasya khyātaṃ tribhirbhāgairvṛttamarddhāśato vahiḥ |  
aṃśenaikena parito dalāni parikalpayet ||  
  
mekhalā mukhavedyāḥ syānnebhiraddhāśamānataḥ |  
daṇḍamūlāgrayoḥ kuṃbhau guṇavedauṃgulaiḥ kramāt ||  
  
daṇḍīyugaṃ yamāṃśaiḥ syāddaṇḍasyānāha īritaḥ |  
ṣaḍbhiraṃśaiḥ pṛṣṭhabhāgo vedyākūrmākṛtirbhavet ||  
  
haṃsasya hastino vāpi potriṇo vā likhenmanuṃ |  
mukhasya pṛṣṭhabhāge tu saṃproktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ sucaḥ ||  
  
sauvarṇa sruksruvausyātā saumyakarmaṇi sarvataḥ |  
bhavetāmāyasāvetau staṃbhanādiṣu karmasu ||  
  
tadalābhepalāśasya parṇābhyāṃ hūyate haviḥ |  
palāśapatre niśchidre ruciresruksruvau matau ||  
  
p. 33b)  
  
vidadhyādvāśvattha patre saṃkṣipte homakarmaṇi ||  
  
atha sruvalakṣaṇaṃ |  
  
srucaścaturviṃśatibhirbhāgairāracayet sruvaṃ |  
dvāviṃśatyā daṇḍamānamaṃśairetasya kīrtitaṃ ||  
  
caturbhiraṃśaisanāhakarṣāhyagrāhitacchiraḥ |  
aṃśadvayenanikhaṃ netyaṃke mṛgapadākṛtiḥ ||  
  
daṇḍamūlāgrayorgaṇḍī bhavet kaṃkaṇabhuṣitāḥ |  
sruvasyavidhirākhyātaḥ śāstresminmaṃtrasaṃjñake ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau paśupakuṇḍādinirṇayo nāmāṣṭaḥ prakāśaḥ || 8 ||  
athāṃkurārpaṇaṃ ||  
  
pratiṣṭāyāṃ ca dīkṣāyāṃ snāpane cotsave tathā |  
saṃprokṣaṇe ca śāṃtyarthaṃ vivāhe mauṃjivaṃdhane ||  
  
sarvamaṃgalakāryeṣu kārayeda kurārpaṇaṃ |  
pratiṣṭādi ca sātpūrvaṃ navame saptame dine ||  
  
paṃcame vā tṛtīye vā sadyo vācāṃkurārpaṇaṃ |  
puṇyāha ghoṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā brāhmaṇaiḥ sahadeśikaḥ ||  
  
bījāropaṇa karmedaṃ kartavyaṃ sarvakāmadaṃ |  
maṃḍapottara digbhāgeśālāṃ pūrvāparāyatāṃ ||  
  
taṃ maṇḍemaṇḍapaṃ kuryādakṣāḥ prāgvaruṇāyataṃ |  
vāmyodīcyāṃ yataṃ vāmadīkṣāyāṃ saṃprasaśyate ||  
  
gomayenopaliptāyāṃ bhūmau dakṣetha vāmake |  
sa tailataṇḍule naiva sa taila vijayādravaiḥ ||  
  
tatra rekhāḥ paṃcakaradīrghā kāryāstu paṃca ca |  
vitastyaṃtaritā rudrarekhā kāryāstathāyatā ||  
  
catvāriṃśat koṣṭhakāḥ syuścaturviṃśati koṣṭhakaiḥ |  
brāhmaṇaistatravīthīsyāt purayed raktacūrṇakaiḥ ||  
  
paścāt koṣṭha catuṣkaṃ ca brahmasthānaṃ tadīritaṃ |  
āpneya koṣṭhamārabhya īśānnāṃtaṃ prapūrayet ||  
  
pītaraktaśvetakṛṣṇarajñobhiḥ sṛṣṭimārgataḥ |  
koṣṭhadvayaṃ tathā vīthī raktenaiva prapūrayet ||  
  
viṣṇusthānaṃ tadagre tu jñeyaṃ koṣṭha catuṣṭayaṃ |  
prāgvadrajobhirāpūryatadagrepi ca vīthikā ||  
  
proktaṃ koṣṭha catuṣkayaddudrasthānaṃ tadīritaṃ |  
tatpūryaṃ pūrvavadraṃgairāraktaiḥ sarvarekhikāḥ ||  
  
vistāronnati dairghyeṇa hastamātrāstuṃ pālikā |  
kāryāḍamarukākārāścatasro viṣṇudaivatāḥ ||  
  
dūrvāmra pallavāśvatthadalopetāśca veṣṭitā |  
sūtreṇa viṣṇuḥ sthānasya catuḥkoṣṭhe niveśayet ||  
  
vairavya paṃcamukhyastāḥ kāṣṭajā ṣoḍaśāṃgulaiḥ |  
āyāmocchrāya dairghyākhyairyuktā paśyānniveśayet ||  
  
brahmasthāne pallavāṃdi sūtraiḥ prāgvacca yojitāaḥ |  
pātrāṇi trividhānyāhuskurārpyaṇa karmaṇi ||  
  
pālikāḥ paṃcamukhyaśca śarāvāṃśca catuḥ kramāt |  
proktāḥ syusarvatatvajñairharirbrahmaśivātmikā ||  
  
p. 34a)  
  
eṣāmucchrāyadratneyaḥ ṣoḍaśā dvādaśāṣṭabhiḥ |  
aṃgulaiḥ kramaśastāni śubhānyāveṣṭyataṃtunā ||  
  
prakṣālya deśikasteṣu padeṣvāhitaśāliṣu |  
sugaṃdhidārbhapuṣpeṣu paścimādi niveśayet ||  
  
pālikā cakravistāraḥ ṣoḍaśāṃgula mucyate |  
bhavetkaṃṭhavilaṃ cāsyāt tadaṣṭyaṃgula vistṛtaṃ ||  
  
padepīṭhasya vistāraṃ ṣaḍaṃgulamudāhṛtaṃ |  
caturaṃgula utsedhastatsaṃdhiśvāṃgulaṃ bhavet ||  
  
tatsaṃdhestu bhavennābhaṃ padepīṭhārddhameva ca |  
bhavet paṃcamukhī caiva ghaṭikā sarvakāmada ||  
  
caturaṃgula vistārāṇyāhurvaktrāṇi paṃcavai |  
catvāri ca caturdikṣu ūrddhvamekaṃ yathā vidhiḥ ||  
  
ghaṭikāyāma vistāro dvādaśāṃgula mucyate |  
ācāryāḥ kathayatyeke ṣoḍaśāṃgula mucyate ||  
  
ācāryāḥ kathayaṃtyeke ṣoḍaśāṃgulameva ca |  
dvādaśāṃgula vistāraṃ śarāvasya mukhaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
caturaṃgula vistāra madhastānmūlamucyate |  
sa bhave kanakaṃ rūpyatāmraṃ tomārtikānyapi ||  
  
śaivāḥ śatāvāścatvāro teṣu pātrāṇi vinyaset |  
vahnyādīśānaparyaṃtaṃ catuṣkeṣu pṛthak pṛthak ||  
  
prokteṣu teṣu pātreṣu brahmaviṣṇuśivān yajet |  
saṃpūjayeccharāveṣu rudracaṃdanapuṣpakaiḥ ||  
  
pālikāmuttathā viṣṇuṃ brahmāṇaṃ ghaṭikāsu ca |  
mṛdvālukākarīṣaiścoddhvataḥ pātrāṇi pūrayet ||  
  
brahmādibhiśca kuddālaṃ pūjayitvā dināṃtare |  
gītanṛtya samāyuktaṃ gajavāji samanvitaṃ ||  
  
gurvādayorathāruḍhāgajāruḍhāstathā pare |  
gatvā tīraṃ taḍāgasya nadyā puṣpaṃ vanasya vā ||  
  
tatra śuddhaṃ bhuvobhāgaṃ darbhaiḥ saṃsṛjya vāstrataḥ |  
abhyukṣyacārdyatoyena tattanmaṃtramanusmaran ||  
  
hṛdā bhūmiṃ samāvāhya gaṃdhapuṣpaiḥ samarccayet |  
kuddālī maṃtramaṃtreṇa khalvā bhūmimatho mṛdaṃ ||  
  
gṛhītvā vāmadevena pūrayet kāṃsyapātrake |  
hṛdāmṛdaṃ ca saṃmṛjya vastreṇācchādya dhārayet ||  
  
puraṃ vā nilayaṃ vāpi sarvamaṃgala niḥsvanaiḥ |  
guruḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā maṃḍapatvānayet tataḥ ||  
  
etatkarma divākāle kuryādrātrau na buddhimān |  
tataḥ svarṇādike pātre daśabījāni vāpayet ||  
  
va& vījaṃ prajapenmaṃtrī dugdhena kṣālayet tataḥ ||  
tāni priyaṃ guhyāmākatilaśarṣapaśālayaḥ ||  
  
muṅjāḍhakī suriṣyā vā khalyomāṣāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |  
mūlamaṃtrābhijaptāni paṃcaghoṣapuraḥsaraṃ ||  
  
p. 34b)  
  
āśīrvāgbhirdvijātīnāṃ maṃgalācārapūrvakaṃ |  
nirvapatteṣutrāḥ treṣu deśikoyatamānasaḥ ||  
  
bījaṃ mukhyena mūlena prāṅmukho vā gudaṅmukhaḥ |  
vāpayet sarvavījāni pālikādiṣṭha tu kramāt ||  
  
bījānāmadhipaḥ somastasmādrātrau tu nirvapet |  
bījebhyo daivatebhyaśca sa rātrau kāṃtimān yataḥ ||  
  
tasmādgurustu bījāni niśāyāmeva vāpayet |  
skaṃdaṃ priyaṃgau niṣyāca vāyumagniṃ kulutthake ||  
  
āḍhakyāṃ nir-ṛtiḥ somaḥ muṅgevaiva svataṃtile |  
prajāpatiṃśāli bījetvanaṃtaṃ sarṣayercayet ||  
  
iṃdraṃ śyāme tu māṣe ca varuṇaṃ tu nagātmaje |  
somajaṃ pūjayennityamadhi vā sa dināvadhi ||  
  
adhivāsadine prāpte somamudvāsayedguruḥ |  
tryaṃvakāya ca śarvāya śaṃkarāya śivāya ca ||  
  
sarvaloka pradhānāya śāśvatāya namo namaḥ |  
vikīryānena maṃtreṇa haridrā cūrṇamiśritaṃ ||  
  
toyaṃ pravarṣayetteṣu siṃcettoyairdinaṃ pratiṃ |  
haridrābhiḥ samatyajya vastrairācchādyadeśikaḥ ||  
  
valiṃ trividha pātrāṇāṃ dikṣu pūrvāditaḥ kṣipet |  
praṇavādyairna mātaiśca rātraurātrīśa nāmabhiḥ ||  
  
bhūtāni pitaro yakṣānāgābrahmāśivohariḥ |  
gurupadiṣṭamārgeṇa samyak pātra trayāgataḥ ||  
  
navāhaṃ tu baliṃ dadyāttattaduddiśyadaivataṃ |  
saṃdhyayorubhayorarddharātrau cāpi valiṃ haret ||  
  
śālyodanaṃ tilālājāsaktavaḥ prathamedine |  
haridrā cūrṇasaṃyukto bhūtebhyoyaṃ valirmataḥ ||  
  
evaṃ dvitīyadivase pitṛbhyastilataṃḍulaiḥ |  
tṛtīyasaktavolājā yakṣebhyo dadhi saṃyutāḥ ||  
  
nāgebhyaḥ saktu vasturye nārikelajalaplutāḥ |  
dadyāt puṣpākṣata valiṃ paṃcame brahmaṇemudā ||  
  
ṣaṣṭe śivāya cāpūyayuktaṃ bhaktaṃ praśasyate |  
guḍaudanaṃ saptamehni viṣṇave vinivedayet ||  
  
viṣṇorevāṣṭamadibhedaddhyodanavaliḥ smṛtaḥ |  
kṛśarānnaṃ tu navame viṣṇoreva praśasyate ||  
  
vāmamārge caturdikṣu maṃtrastasya valiṃ caret |  
brahmasthāne tu vetālomeṣastasya valinsurā ||  
  
viṣṇusthāne bhairavīsyādajastasyā valirmataḥ |  
bhairavastu śivasthāne māhiṣaṃ valimicchati ||  
  
p. 35a)  
  
gauḍī mādhvī ca yaiṣṭī ca surāstatra kramānmatāḥ |  
madyamāṃsaṃ madyayuktaṃ bhūtebhyo valiriṣyate ||  
  
pitṛbhyaḥ sāsavapalaṃ yakṣebhyaḥ kukkuṭomadhu |  
bhekoduruvalirnāge vāmamārge valisvayaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ gateṣu navasu divaseṣu vilokayet |  
prarūḍhāṇyaṃ kurāṇyanyona vīkṣeta kadācana ||  
  
ācārya eva praviśettacchiṣyovātadājñayā |  
yajñamānābhivṛddhyarthamaṃkurāṇi parīkṣayet ||  
  
samyak tasyodgamojātaḥ kiṃnaṣṭaṃ madhyamaṃ ca kiṃ |  
samyagatyudgame siddhiḥ kuṃthite vighnamāpnuyāt ||  
  
kīṭabhuktenyaphalaṃ rutite sarvanāśanaṃ |  
dhūmravarṇānya pūrṇāni tathā tīryaggatāni ca ||  
  
śyāmalāni ca kubjāni varjayeda śubhāni ca |  
avṛṣṭiṃ kurute kṛṣṇaṃ dhūmrābhaṃ kalahaṃ tathā ||   
  
apūrṇajananāśaṃ ca durbhikṣaṃ śyāmalākulaṃ |  
tīryagjāte bhavedvyādhiḥ kubje śatrubhayaṃ bhavet ||  
  
aśubhevāṃ kulejāte śāṃtihomaṃ samācaret |  
mūlamaṃtreṇa juhuyādgurumūrtidharaiḥ saha ||  
  
aghorāstreṇa cāstreṇa śataṃ vātha sahasrakaṃ |  
samyak pūrvaṃ prarūḍhāṇi komalāni sitāni ca ||  
  
siddhiḥ priyaṃgubhirjñeyā śyāmākaiḥ strīsukhaṃ bhavet |  
tilaiḥ pūjyajanollāsaiḥ sarṣapairnābhicārakaḥ ||   
  
śālībhiḥ sarvamānyatvaṃ mudgedeva kṛpā bhavet |  
catuḥpādāstadāḍhakyāṃniṣyā vā kṣetramaṃdire ||  
  
khalvaiḥ satkarmasiddhiśca māśaiḥ śāṃtirarerbhavet |  
sarvaiḥ samudgatairvāmai siddhiḥ pātastvatonyathā ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau aṃkurārpaṇanirṇayonāma navamaḥ prakāśaḥ || 9 ||  
  
atha dīkṣāvidhiṃ vakṣye matrīṇāṃ hitakāmyayā |  
vinā tayā na labhyeta sarvamaṃtraphalaṃ yataḥ ||  
  
caturvidhā samuddiṣṭā kriyāvatyādibhedataḥ |  
kriyāvatī varṇamayī kalātmāveṣamaryapi ||  
  
tatra kriyāvatī dīkṣā vahusvānna nigadyate |  
dīkṣādānāt pūrvadine prātaḥ kṛtyaṃ nivartya ca ||  
  
samalaṃ kṛtyadehaṃ svaṃsvagṛhepūjanaṃ caret |  
gaṇeśasya vidhānena puṇyāhaṃ vācayet tataḥ ||  
  
nāṃdīmukhaṃttarpayitvā paṃcavādyapuraḥsaraṃ |  
yathoktakṛtasaṃbhārogacchedguru gṛhaṃ prati ||  
  
ācārya ṛtvigvaraṇasaṃbhāro * ? daśāmataḥ |  
śrīparṇī vṛkṣapīṭhāmi hastamānānimānataḥ ||  
  
p. 35b)  
  
aṣṭāṃgula samucchrāya sahitāni samāni ca |  
saptaviṃśati darbhāṇāṃ ceṇegre graṃthabhūṣitāḥ ||  
  
viṣṭarāḥ sarvayajñeṣu lakṣaṇaṃ parikīrtitaṃ |  
sukhoṣṇodaka saṃbhūtāḥ pādyārthe tāmragaḍḍukāḥ ||  
  
śaṃkhā arghyapradānāya gaṃdhapuṣpajalānvitāḥ |  
sutāmrasyakamaṇḍalvāḥ ācamyodakapūritāḥ ||  
  
tairyutā madhupakvārthaṃ kāṃsyā dadhyādi pūritāḥ |  
mahadarghyāṇi vastrāṇi mudrikādyaṃ subhūṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
mayūrapatra chatrāṇicoṣṇīṣāṇi samāharet |  
pādukācāharet tatra carmābharaṇabhuṣitāḥ ||  
  
kṛtvai tat phalamāpnoti mahāyajñārhaṇopamaṃ |  
anyebhyo madhuparkasya viprebhyaḥ pūjanaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
bhaktyā tadviguṇaṃ dadyādācāryāya subhaktimān |  
anyairdvijaiḥ samaṃ yatra deśikasya prapūjanaṃ ||  
  
tasmin yajñephalaṃ svalpamanāvṛṣṭau yathākṣiteḥ |  
evaṃ gurugṛhaṃgatvā praṇamya gurupādukāṃ ||  
  
datvā varaṇasāmagrīṃ saṃkalpya vṛṇuyādguruṃ |  
uccāryāmukamaṃtrasya grahaṇāyadvijottamaḥ ||  
  
gurutveneti saṃbhāṣyatvāmahaṃ ca tatovṛṇe |  
ityuktvā vṛṇuyācchiṣyo vṛtosmīti tato guruḥ ||  
  
yathocitaṃ guroḥ karmakuruṣveti vadecchiśuḥ |  
karavāṇīti coccārya gurorevāhvayātataḥ ||  
  
brāhmaṇān vṛṇuyādaṣṭau vedavedāṃgapāragān |  
taddevatopāsakāṃśca ṛtvitkenātha vā yadā ||  
  
catvāri kuṇḍani tadā catvāro ṛtvijaḥ smṛtāḥ |  
tataḥ śiṣyeṇa sahito yāyādyāga gṛhaguruḥ ||  
  
upaviśya ca tadvāre parīkṣāmārabhet tataḥ |  
guruḥ svayaṃ daṃtakāṣṭhaṃ kṣīravṛkṣādi saṃbhavaṃ ||  
  
athavā cūtavṛkṣasya dvādaśāṃgulamānataḥ |  
śiṣyāya mūlasaṃjaptaṃ pradadyāddaṃtadhāvanaṃ ||  
  
daṃtān viśodhya purataḥ sthaṇḍile hastamātrake |  
caturasre tyājayeta parīkṣeta tato guruḥ ||  
  
tadagraṃ yaddiśāsaṃsthaṃ tatredaṃ pūrvataḥ phalaṃ |  
bhūtirhṛdayasaṃtāpo vaṃdhunāśastathāmṛtiḥ ||  
  
śokaśca vyagratā saukhyaṃ jñānalābhaḥ kramāt phalaṃ |  
amaṃgalasthānapāte prāyaścittaḥ samācaret ||  
  
aṣṭādhikaṃ sahasraṃ vā śataviṃśatireva vā |  
astrasaṃpuṭitenaiṣāṃ nāmnā svāhanvitena ca ||  
  
doṣājahijahītyevaṃ padaṃ nāmāvasānugaṃ |  
kevalājyena juhuyādduḥsvapneyyevameva hi ||  
  
p. 36a)  
  
daṃtakāṣṭhaṃ punardeyaṃ punarduṣṭe caturguṇaṃ |  
tṛtīyamapi duṣṭaṃ cenna grāhyā sā tu devatā ||  
  
vāmamārge sakṛdapi guruśiṣyau vināśayet ||  
  
atha svapnaparīkṣāmāha |  
  
tataḥ svapnaparīkṣyāṃ ca kuryāt tadvidhirucyate |  
vedikānāṃ dakṣiṇānāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca vāmināṃ ||  
  
yajjāgrato devamudaitidaivamātṛbhyamaṃtrān japatastriretān |  
divaikabhugdakṣiṇapārśvaśāyīsvapnaṃ parīkṣeta yathopadeśaṃ ||  
  
svapnamānavamāśritya svāpacet pūrvamastakaṃ |  
gṛhasthān darbhaśayyāyāṃ pūrvaśīrṣāstra rakṣitān ||  
  
hṛdā sadbhasmaśayyāyāṃ yatān dakṣiṇamastakān |  
devasya dakṣiṇebhāge śiṣyaṃtamadhivāsayet ||  
  
ahatāstaraṇāstīrṇe sadarbhaḥ śayane śuciḥ |  
maṃtrite ca śivaṃ dhyāyan prāk sirasko niśiḥsvapet ||  
  
śikhāvaddhasya sūtrasya śivayātacchikhāṃguruḥ |  
āveṣṭyāhatavastreṇa tamācchādya ca varmaṇā ||  
  
rekhā trayaṃ ca parito bhasmanā tilasarṣapaiḥ |  
kṛtvāstra japtaistadvāhyedigīśānāṃ valiṃ haret ||  
  
gurupādārcanaṃ kṛtvā upavāsī jiteṃdriyaḥ |  
darbhaśayyāṃgato rātrau dṛṣṭvā svapnaṃ nivedayet ||  
  
bhagavan devadeveśa śūlabhṛdvṛṣavāhanaḥ |  
iṣṭāniṣṭhe samācakṣu svapnemūptasya sāṃprataṃ ||  
  
niśāṃte paśyati svapnaṃ śubhaṃ vā yadi vā śubhaṃ |  
oṃhṛtsakalalokāya viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave ||  
  
viśvāya viśvarūpāya svapnādhipataye namaḥ |  
svapnamānavamaṃtroyamupavāsī jiteṃdriyaḥ ||  
  
darbhaśayyāgato rātrau svapnaṃ paśyedyathā tathaṃ |  
bhuktvāśayītaśayane suśuddhe vasudhātale ||  
  
ardharātre samutthāya pādaśau ca vihāya ca |  
ācamya devaṃ saṃsmṛtya saṃpūjya ca sa paṃcakaiḥ ||  
  
śivadaivatayoraikyaṃ bhāvayan prajapedidaṃ |  
namojāyatrinetrāya piṃgalāya mahātmane ||  
  
vāmāya viśvarūpāya svapnādhipataye namaḥ |  
svapne kathayame nityaṃ sarvakāryamaśeṣataḥ ||  
  
svapnastu prathameyāme saṃvatsara phalaṃ bhavet |  
ṣaḍbhirmāsairdviyāmotthastribhirmāsaistriyāmakaḥ ||  
  
caturthe māsamātreṇa prātaḥkāle tu satvaraṃ |  
ciṃtārugjālpadīrghaṃ yat tatphalaṃ naiva vidyate ||  
  
vātādhikyādbhavet svapnaḥ sāhasoḍḍīnapūrvakaṃ |  
pitrāttejogni pītādiraktaṃ krodhādikaṃ tathā ||  
  
p. 36b)  
  
adhyāśayetādiśita śayanādyaṃ valāṃsitaḥ |  
vāte prātastvaṃgamardaḥ pittāddāhastu netrayoḥ ||  
  
kaphāt prasevate nityaṃ dvaṃ dvaṃ dvaṃ dvaṃ na kiṃ triṣu |  
siddhaṃ vā svaguruṃ devaṃ prasannā vā kumārikāṃ ||  
  
gaṃgāṃgāṃ bhāratīṃ bhānuṃ liṃginaṃ liṃgamaiśvaraṃ |  
vāraṃ chatraṃ rathaṃ dīpaṃ prāsādā kamalaṃ nadīṃ ||  
  
kuṃjaraṃ vṛṣaṃbhaṃ mālyaṃ samudraṃ phalitaṃ drumaṃ |  
parvataṃ projjvaladvahniṃ mamamāsaṃ surāsavaṃ ||  
  
grahādbhānividhaṃ sūryaṃ ratnānyā bharaṇāni ca |  
siṃhāsanaṃ vimānaṃ ca dhvajaṃ rājyābhiṣecanaṃ ||  
  
śvetacaṃdanavastrāṇi śālayaḥ kuṃkumaṃ madhu |  
lājāsiddhārthakaṃ nāryo navabhāṇḍaṃ ca pāyasaṃ ||  
  
aśvaṃ phalāni siddhānnaṃ dadhivāra vilāsinīṃ |  
dugdhaṃ vādyāni cāṣaṃ ca mayūraṃ na kulaṃ mṛdaṃ ||  
  
vaddhameka paśuṃ puṣpaṃ sadvākyaṃ cekṣu maṃjanaṃ |  
pūrṇakuṃbhaṃ darpaṇaṃ ca mīnavājyaṃ ca rocanā ||  
  
śaṃvarodanahīnaṃ ca śastrāṇi ca patākikāḥ |  
bhāradvāja nṛpālau ca vedaśabdaṃ ca gāyanaṃ ||  
  
kaśāmāṃgalyagītāni cāṃkuśaṃ yaddhṛdaḥ priyaṃ |  
svapne dṛṣṭvāni caitāni sādhakaḥ siddhimāpnuyāt ||  
  
vyādhyārddhyarttanāsti duḥkhaṃ sāmānyasukhamāpnuyāt |  
yadākarma sukāmyeṣu striyaṃ svapneṣu paśyati ||  
  
kāmayaṃtī nadī siṃdhustaraṇaṃ bhramaṇaṃ cakhe |  
bhāskarodayanaścaiva grahaṇaṃ caṃdrasūryayoḥ ||  
  
harmyaṃ prāsādanāmāśca vṛṣaśailāgnirohaṇaṃ |  
bhojanaṃ dadhibhaktasyāt pakvamāṃsaṃ ca bhakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
kṛmiviṣṭānulepaśca rudhireṇābhiṣecanaṃ |  
tāṃbūlabhakṣaṇaṃ madyapānaṃ dadhyasi caṃdanaṃ ||  
  
pracaṇḍaḥ kiraṇaḥ svacchaḥ kāryasiddhestu lakṣaṇaṃ |  
kṛṣṇāṃ varadharā nārī kṛṣṇagaṃdhānulepanāṃ ||  
  
avagūhatiyaṃ svapnesārātristasya paścimā |  
evaṃ tu raktayā vyādhiḥ śokoruṇaḥ samānayā ||  
  
bhinnayā kalahā hatyāpītayā kīrayāni yat |  
śvetāṃvaradharā nārīśvetamālyānupanā ||  
  
avagūhatiyaṃ svapne tasya śrīsarvatomukhī |  
āsane śayaneyāne salile vāhane gṛhe ||  
  
jvalamāne viṃbudhyeta tasya śrīsarvatomukhī |  
sitoragasyadaṃśaścejjāyate dakṣiṇekare ||  
  
daśāhobhirbhavellābho rogīrogād vimucyate |  
nigaḍairvāhupāśena vadhyate vā suto bhavet ||  
  
pratiṣṭāvarddhate tasya dugdhapānāddhanātyayaḥ |  
surāṃraktaṃ piban vidyāṃ labhed viprodhanaṃ paraḥ ||  
  
p. 37a)  
  
dadhi dṛṣṭvā bhavet prītirgodhūmaiśca dhanāgamaḥ |  
siddhāviṣṭāgataṃ vidyāṃllābhaḥ siddhārthakaistathā ||  
  
dadhilābhā bhavedartho ghṛtalābhāddhruvaṃjayaḥ |  
ghṛtāsanāddhanakleśojayastu dadhibhakṣaṇe ||  
  
liṃgādyabhyarcanaṃ dṛṣṭvā vyavahāre jayo bhavet |  
yastu madhye taḍāgādebhuṃjīta ghṛtapāyasaṃ ||  
  
niṣkaṃpaṃ puṣkaraṃ patretaṃ vidyāt pṛthivīpatiṃ |  
devatāliṃginogāvaḥ pitaro brāhmaṇo nṛpāḥ ||  
  
yaṃ vadati naraṃ svapne tat tathaiva bhaviṣyati |  
astraiḥ saṃveṣṭayedyastu grāmaṃ vā nagaraṃ tathā ||  
  
grāme maṇḍalarājyaṃ syānnagare pārthivo bhavet |  
caṃdratārārkagrasanaṃ parimārgaṇameva ca ||  
  
bhūmyaṃ vudhīnāṃ grasanaṃ śatrūṇāṃ ca vadhakriyā |  
jayo vivāhadyūteṣu śatrūṇāṃ ca tathā jayaḥ ||  
  
vaḍavā mahiṣī siṃhīgohastinyādvidohanaṃ |  
prasādo guru vipreṣṭha devasiddhādikācchubhaḥ ||  
  
snānaṃ rājyābhiṣekaśca svaśiracchedanamṛtiḥ |  
tīrthodakānāṃ taraṇaṃ tathā viṣa *?  laṃghanaṃ ||  
  
gohasti vaḍavāsūtirvahnirābhastathaiva ca |  
parastryā liṃganaṃ tasyālābha rodanameva ca ||  
  
viṣṭālepaḥ kuṃdajātīvakulakṣeśa darśanaṃ |  
raṇadvidyudvimarddeṣu jayonigaḍavaṃdhanaṃ ||  
  
paśumartyamṛgāṇāṃ ca labdhiradhyasanaṃ tathā |  
śikhilābhaḥ śvetavastre puṣpacaṃdanedhāraṇaṃ ||  
  
maṇitāla suvarṇādi pātre bhojanakaṃ yadā |  
paśyet tadā sādhakasya jñeyā siddhirūpa sthitā ||  
  
kāryārttanāṃ kāryasiddhi ṛṇārtānāṃ dhanāgamaḥ |  
vaṃdhyā varmatuṣāgnyāhi lavaṇāṃgāramiṃdhanaṃ ||  
  
viṭklīconmattatailānijaṭilārivasauṣadhaṃ |  
rogābhṛśaṃ ca sanyāsī rugnābhyaktau kṣudhāturaḥ ||  
  
vimuktakeśaḥ parito tvagāsṛk śaraṭaḥ kṣutaṃ |  
mārjārayuddhaṃ kārpāsogarbhiṇī varajasvalā ||  
  
guḍastakraṃ ca kāṣāyī paṃkaraṇḍā kaligṛhe |  
vastādikasya svavalalulāpasavalaṃ tathā ||  
  
aṃdhaḥ kubjo durvacano vadhiraḥ khaṃjakukṣakau |  
vamanaṃ ca ghaṭoriktorajakīmalināṃvarā ||  
  
etairdṛṣṭairnakāryaṃ syādrotī mṛtyumavāpnuyāt |  
aśokaṃ karavīraṃ ca pālāśaṃ vāpi puṣpitaṃ ||  
  
svapnepi salilaṃ dṛṣṭvā naraśokamayāpnuyāt |  
rūpāṃtare praveśaśca dakṣiṇāśāgatistathā ||  
  
p. 37b)  
  
paṃkenimajjanaṃ snānaṃ putrabhāryā vināśadaṃ |  
gohasti dvijaviprādivarjye kṛṣṇena śobhanaṃ ||   
  
raktagaṃdhāṃvaraḥ sranvī kṛṣṇā vā dakṣiṇāmakhaḥ |  
kharoṣṭramahiṣārūḍhastrimāsaṃ na sajīvati ||  
  
śvabhre vā patate gehe dvāraṃ vāsyavidhīyate |  
navottiṣṭhatiyastasmāttadaṃtaṃ tasya jīvitaṃ ||  
  
cāṃtaṃ mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca saṃtānaṃ jananaṃ cyutiḥ |  
śukraṃ ca paśyedyaḥ svapne tasyāyurdaśamāsikaṃ ||  
  
tāḍyate vikṛtaiḥ kṛṣṇaiḥ puruṣairudyatāyudhaiḥ |  
pāṣāṇaistāḍyate cāpi tasya mṛtyurnna saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
mahiṣoṣṭhu kharārūḍhastairābhyaktaśca muṇḍitaḥ |  
dakṣiṇāśāṃ prasthitoyaḥ yasya mṛtyurnnasaṃśayaḥ ||  
  
paśyet prāsādapatanaṃ gṛhasya śaśisūryayoḥ |  
parvatānāṃ ca vṛkṣāṇāmadhikārāṣyutirbhavet ||  
  
hāniścaiva svagātrāṇāṃ vyādhinābhibhavastathā |  
gṛhasaṃmārjanaṃ lepo gomayena mṛdāpi vā ||  
  
tīrthānadīṃ samāyātastīrenyadvasanaṃ dhṛtaṃ |  
rogīrogādvimucyeta hāniḥ svasthasya jāyate ||  
  
puṃnāmāno mṛgakhagāḥ potakīsūkarīralā |  
piṃgalāchuchukāpallīvāmāṃ kokilā śivā ||  
  
strīnāmāno mṛgakhagāḥ śrīkaṇṭhāyābharoruruḥ |  
chikaro pipalobhāsaḥ dakṣe kākarkṣa kukkurāḥ ||  
  
dṛṣṭāścedrogiṇo roganāśaḥ sādhakasiddhayaḥ |  
śvasthasya codyamāllābho digvyatyāsānnaśobhanaṃ ||  
  
atha duḥkhaśca śāṃtiḥ |  
  
trirātraupoṣito bhūtvā haviṣyāsī purohitaḥ |  
sakṣīrāṇāṃ ghṛtāktānāṃ samidhānāṃ śataṃ dahet ||  
  
pālāśānāṃ tu gāyatryā śūdraḥ snātvā haviṣyabhuk |  
dīpaṃ dadyād vipragṛhe viṣṇorgehe śivālaye ||  
  
evaṃ dṛṣṭvā śubhaṃ svapnaṃ gṛhnīyān manumanyathā |  
gṛhīte hānirevasyādvānyaṃ devaṃ viciṃtayet ||  
  
atha svapnanivedanaṃ |  
  
śiṣyastu śucirācāṃte puṣpahasto gurūttamaṃ |  
praṇamya śirasā hṛṣṭhastasmai svapnaṃ nivedayet ||  
  
svapnevākṣi samakṣāmvā āścaryasatiharṣadaṃ |  
akasmādya divā paśyantākhyātavyaṃ gurorvinā ||  
  
svapnānnidrā phalaghnīsyāt svapno vācyo macānyathā |  
evaṃ vicārya sa tato guruḥ pujāṃ samācaret ||  
  
vidhāyā ca manaṃ tatra sāmānyārghye vidhāya ca |  
arghyodakena saṃprokṣya dvārapūjāṃ samācaret ||  
  
p. 38a)  
  
tataśca deśiko vighnāndivyārālokanena ca |  
aṃtarīkṣagatānastrodakairutsādayet kramāt ||  
  
pārthivān pārṣṇighātaistu tribhirutsārya yatnataḥ |  
aṃgaṃ saṃkocya kiṃcittu śākhāṃ vāma gatāṃ spṛśan ||  
  
utsāritānāṃ viprānāṃ dadanvanvada tu dakṣiṇo |  
brahmāṇaṃ cāstvadhīśaṃ ca nair-ṛtyāṃdiśi pūjayet ||  
  
carghyāṃvunā ca gavyena yātasthānesu siṃcite |  
vīkṣaṇādyaistataḥ śuddhiṃ caturdvārāṃ samācaret ||  
  
saṃvīkṣya mūlamanunāhyastreṇa prokṣayettataḥ |  
kuryāttāḍanamaṃtreṇa kavacenā vasevayet ||  
  
śrīkhaṃḍāguru caṃdraiśca dhūpitestreṇasaṃkadhā |  
yavāṃścaṃdanasiddhyarthadūrvābhasmākṣatān kuśān ||  
  
salājānvikirenmaṃtrī pratyuhaghnā hi maṇḍape |  
mārjayedastramaṃtreṇatān maṃtrīdarbhamuṣṭinā ||  
  
āsanāya tu varddhanya īśānesvāpayeccatān |  
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvātha viprāṃnsaṃtoṣya yatnataḥ ||  
  
vedikāyāṃ likhet paścāt sarvato bhadramaṇḍalaṃ |  
atha tat saṃpravakṣyāmi kuryāt tāṃtrikakarmaṇi ||  
  
nṛpavarga samākāryā koṣṭhakāścaturasrake |  
madhye ṣaḍvarga koṣṭhāni mārjayet tatra saṃlikhet ||  
  
āyāma dvādaśāṃśaṃ ca vahistyaktvātha madhyataḥ |  
tato vṛttatrayaṃ madhye samaṃ kuryād yathāvidhi ||  
  
karṇikāmadhyavṛttena dvitīyena tu keśarān |  
aṃtarvṛttena patrāṇi patrāṃgaṃ tyaktabhāgataḥ ||  
  
kiṃjalkāgreṣu saṃsthāpyā pārśvatastvarddhacaṃdrakāḥ |  
tadagre tu tribhiḥ koṣṭhaiḥ pādān koṇeṣu vinyaset ||  
  
śeṣāṇi pīṭhagātrāṇi parataḥ paṃkti yugmakaṃ |  
vīthīṃ kuryānmārjayitvā caturdikṣu ca madhyataḥ ||  
  
kramādvābhyāṃ caturbhiśca koṣṭhairdvāra catuṣṭaye |  
koṣṭhatrayena caikena pratyekaṃ dvārapārśvayoḥ ||  
  
śobhābhavaṃtyataḥ koṣṭhairekatastribhireva ca |  
upaśobhāstataḥ koṣṭhaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ koṇāni kalpayet ||  
  
śuklaṃ taḍulacūrṇaṃ syādutsadhāyāmatastathā |  
aṃgulena samākāryāḥ sīmārekhā dalāni ca ||  
  
pīṭhagātrāṇi ca dvāracatuṣkaṃte prapūrayet |  
avipre pūraṇīyāni rakte naiva dalānyapi ||  
  
kusuṃbhacūrṇamāraktaṃ pūraṇīyāstu tena tu |  
dvāraśobhāḥ pīṭhapādāḥ sarvavarṇairviniścayāt ||  
  
pītaṃ haridrā cūrṇaṃ syāt pīṭhagarbhaṃ ca karṇikāṃ |  
upaśobhāśca viprāṇyaḥ pīṭhagarbhaṃ ca kṛṣṇataḥ ||  
  
vilvapatrasya cūrṇotthoharitastena pūrayet |  
saṃdhīṃśca kalpavallīṃśca pītaraktena keśarān ||  
  
vīthī catuṣka madhye tu kalpavallī prapūrayet |  
patramūla phalākāra maṇḍitā hṛdayaṃgamāḥ ||  
  
p. 38b)  
  
nānāvarṇa rajobhistrāṃ jayet kuśalī guruḥ |  
kṛṣṇavarṇena konāni vahirekhā trayaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
śuklāruṇākhya kṛṣṇaistu rajobhirbhūṣayet kramāt |  
sarvataṃtreṣṭidaṃ proktaṃ sarvato bhadramaṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
vakṣyetha devayonīnāṃ sarvatobhadramaṇḍalaṃ |  
mārgetha dakṣiṇe tatra koṣṭhākāra vivargakāḥ ||  
  
prāgvadeva tu tanmadhye padmaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśatā śubhaṃ |  
ekapaṃktyā bhavet pīṭhaṃ dvāraṃ śobhā ca pūrvataḥ ||  
  
ṣaḍbhiḥ koṣṭhaistu koṇāni raṃjitavyaṃ ca pūrvavat |  
pīṭhapādāḥ paridhayaḥ padmādyaṃ pūrvavanmataṃ ||  
  
vāmamārge maṇḍalaṃ syāt koṣṭairapūkavalgitaiḥ |  
caturbhiḥ paṃkajaṃ madhye tadvāhye vīthikā tu vā ||  
  
kalpavallī samāyuktā padmaṃ pūrva vadeva hi |  
dikcatuṣke tu padmāni caturbhiḥ koṣṭhakaiścaret ||  
  
vidiśāsu caturbhiḥ syuścatuṣṭāveda saṃkhyakāḥ |  
catuṣ.ka padmavīthānāṃ madhye svastikasannibhaṃ ||  
  
jāyate taccatuḥkoṣṭhe vidiśo su caturṣvapi |  
rajobhiḥ śuklahāridra raktanīlaiḥ prapūrayet ||  
  
svastikā nīlaraktāśca pūrvavat parikalpayet |  
uditaṃ maṃḍalaṃ hyetat navapadmaṃ suśobhanaṃ ||  
  
vedyā uparivadhnīyāt phalapuṣpopaśobhitaṃ |  
vedikāyāmāsane sa prāṅmukhaḥ saṃviśedatha ||  
  
vaddhapadmāsato maunī ṛjukāyo jiteṃdriyaḥ |  
deśikeṃdrastu saṃsthāpya pūjopakaraṇāni tu ||  
  
dakṣiṇe vāmabhāge tu sthāpayet kalaśaṃ śubhaṃ |  
sugaṃdhijala saṃpūrṇahasta prakṣālanāya ca ||  
  
paścāt pātraṃ nidhāyātha dīpān prajvālayecchubhān |  
vyajanaṃ mukulaṃ chatraṃ cāmaraṃ dikṣu maṃtravit ||  
  
saṃskuryāttāni sarvāṇi vakṣyamāṇa vidhānataḥ |  
karaśuddhiṃ vidhāyātha kuryāttālatrayaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
śaramaṃtreṇa digvaṃdhaṃ kuryānmaṃtrī samāhitaḥ |  
mahastu tata utpannaṃ rakṣayettaṃ hi sarvataḥ ||  
  
bhūtaśuddhiṃ tataḥ kṛtvā prāṇasthāpanamācaret |  
nyāsādikaṃ tataḥ kuryāddeśikoyatamānasaḥ ||  
  
ṛṣiṃ vinyaset tato mūrddhni chaṃdho vaktragataṃ nyaset |  
devatāṃ hṛdayenyasya mūlamaṃtrasya deśikaḥ ||  
  
ṣaḍaṃgaṃ vinyasenmaṃtrī paṃcāṃgaṃ ca yathāvidhi |  
asya maṃtrasya paṃcāṃgaṃ netraṃ tasya vidhīyate ||  
  
p. 39a)  
  
aṃgairvihīnasya manoraṃgaṃ te naiva kalpayet |  
tattattaṃtroktamārgeṇanyāsānanyān samācaret ||  
  
śarīresvasyamaṃtrajño yogapīṭhaṃ prakalpayet |  
dehātmake tataḥ pīṭhe dhyāyen maṃtrasya devatām ||  
  
darśayitvā tato mudrāḥ sthāpayedarghyamuttamaṃ |  
jalena pūritāṃ dakṣe prokṣaṇī sthāpayet tataḥ ||  
  
taṃtrātmamalyaṃ śaṃkhāṃṣu tata uttarato nyaset |  
pādyamācamanīyaṃ ca madhuparkaṃ ca maṃtravit ||  
  
tato mūlāṃvunā maṃtrī prokṣaṇyadbhiḥ samāhitā |  
svātmānaṃ maṇḍalaṃ cānyat pūjopakaraṇādikaṃ ||  
  
prokṣayed gaṃdhapuṣpādyairddeśesvedeśikottamaḥ |  
yogapīṭhaṃ samabhyarcyanyāsamārgeṇa maṃtravit ||  
  
pīṭhāṃtaṃ ca tatastatra pūjayediṣṭadevatāṃ |  
devatātmātataḥ paṃcakuryācca sumanoṃtalīn ||  
  
śīrṣa hṛdi tathādhāre varaṇe sarvagātrake |  
pūjayecca nivedyena rahitaiścaṃdanādibhiḥ ||  
  
sarvopacāraistaṃvesthaṃ gurvādiṣṭena vartmanā |  
samāpayedidaṃ sarvaṃ prokṣaṇyadbhiḥ samācaret ||  
  
pāṇīyaṃ prokṣaṇī saṃsthaṃ tyaktvā saṃpūryavpūrvavat |  
upacāraiścaṃdanādyairmaṇḍalaṃ pūjayed guruḥ ||  
  
pūjayet karṇikāṃ pūrvaṃ śālibhistaṃḍulaistataḥ |  
darbhānyaseduparyeṣāṃ sākṣataṃ kūrcakaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
chinnamūlā kuśādīrghāḥ saptaviṃśati saṃkhyakāḥ |  
brahmagraṃthisthitāstvagradeśe kūrca ihocyate ||  
  
yajedādhāra śaktyādīn pīṭhamaṃtrāvasānakaṃ |  
svarṇādi racitaṃ tatra kalaśaṃ chidravarjitaṃ ||  
  
dvādaśāṃgula haimaṃ ca raupyaṃ ṣoḍaśameva ca |  
mārtikaṃ tāmrakuṃbhaṃ ca ṣaṭtriṃśadaṃgulaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
vittaśāṭhyaṃ na kurvīta kṛte niḥphalamāpnuyāt |  
triguṇātmakasūtreṇa veṣṭitaṃ sarvato vahiḥ ||  
  
caṃdanāguru karpūrairmadhye samyaktadhūpitaṃ |  
dhruvaṃ japanvidhānena sthāpayed deśikottamaḥ ||  
  
navaratnāni nikṣipya kuṃbhe kūrcamathopari |  
pūrvācaṃdana saṃyuktaṃ vinyasedakṣatānvitaṃ ||  
  
puṣpaṃ nīlaṃ ca vaiḍūrya vidrumaṃ mauktikaṃ tathā |  
tato marakaṭaṃ vajraṃ gomedhaṃ padmarāgakaṃ ||  
  
proktāni navaratnāni deśikaiḥ taṃtravikramaiḥ |  
kṣādyaṃtaṃ kramato maṃtraṃ mātṛkā manasā japan ||  
  
mūlamaṃtraṃ japennaṃte ciṃtayennaikyamātmanaḥ |  
ghaṭasya pīṭhābhedaṃ ca ciṃtayet sādhakottamaḥ ||  
  
p. 39b)  
  
paṃcāśadauṣadhīkkāthaiḥ pūrayet tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
ekena sahitāstāśca varṇauṣadhyaścatā imāḥ ||  
  
caṃdanaṃ cāpi raktākhyaṃ caṃdanaṃ cā gurustathā |  
kapūrośīrakuṣṭāni vālakaṃ cāpi keśaraṃ ||  
  
kaḥkolakaṃjāti phalaṃ jaṭāmāṃsīmurātathā |  
graṃthikaṃ rocanājātī putraṃ pippala vilvayoḥ ||  
  
pṛśnaparśī citrakaṃ ca lavaṃgakabhṛśaṃ tathā |  
kaḥkolaṃ cāpi guṃjāsyādudusvarakakāśmarī ||  
  
padmakāṣṭhaṃ śaṃkhapuṣpī mayūrasya śikhā tathā |  
plakṣogni maṃthaśca tathā muhuparśī kuśāḥ punaḥ ||  
  
pāṣāṇabhedakaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ śaṃkhapuṣpī ca rohiṇaṃ |  
śyonāko vṛhatī caiva pāṭalā mukhakarṇikā ||  
  
tulasī śikharī iṃdravallī bhṛṃgābhidho nṛpaḥ |  
tato parājitā tālamūlī cāpi kṛtāṃjali ||  
  
dūrvā śrīdevikanyākhyābhāratho bhadramustakaṃ |  
lavaṃgarahitāścaitā paṃcāśat saṃkhyakā iti ||  
  
dugdhaṃ vṛkṣatvayā kvāthairbrahmabhūrukvṛgudbhavaiḥ |  
gaṃdhapaṃkaprasthanādi vā sitairvāśubhairjalaiḥ ||  
  
kvāthāditoyairāpūryaśaṃkhaṃ tasminviloḍayet |  
gaṃdhāṣṭakaṃ tasya tasya devasyātha vinikṣipet ||  
  
gaṃdhāṣṭakasya saṃyogāt sāmarthyāddeśikasya ca |  
saśaktikajjalaṃ kuṃbhe bhavedevaṃ vidurbudhāḥ ||  
  
ādau kṛśānu saṃvaṃdhī kalādaśakamarcayet |  
dhūmārciruṣmājvalinījvālinī visphuraṃgiṇī ||  
  
suśrīḥ surūpā kapilāhavyakavyavahedraye |  
kalā ṣoḍaśakaṃ sauraṃ pūjayet tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
tāpinī tāpinī dhūmrā marīcirjvālinī ruciḥ |  
suṣumṇā bhogadā viśvāvodhinīdhāriṇīkṣamā ||  
  
kalāḥ ṣoḍaśakaṃ cāṃdraṃ yajet paścād gurūttamaḥ |  
amṛtāmānadā pūṣā puṣṭituṣṭiratirdhṛtiḥ ||  
  
śaśinī caṃdrikā kāṃtirjyotsnāśrīprītiraṃgadā |  
pūrṇāpūrṇāmṛtākāṃtidāyinyaḥ svasyajāḥ kalā ||  
  
bhedāhi bhedasaṃjātāḥ kalāḥ paṃcāśadinduyuk |  
sannidhāyya pratiṣṭhāpyābhyarcayet kramaśastutāḥ ||  
  
nivṛttiḥ pratiṣṭhā vidyāśāṃtiṛddhiścadīpikāḥ |  
recikā mocikāpārā sūkṣmāsūkṣmāmṛtā tathā ||  
  
jñānadāpyāyanīcānyāpinī vyomarūpakā |  
anaṃtā sṛṣṭi ṛddhīkāsmṛtirmedhā ca kāṃtikā ||  
  
lakṣmīrdyutiḥ sthirāsthitiḥ siddhirjarā ca pālinī |  
kṣāṃtīścaryauratiḥ kāmāvaradāhlādinī tathā ||  
  
p. 40a)  
  
prītidīrghī tīkṣṇaraudrībhayā nidrāvataṃdrikā |  
kṣukrodhinī kriyotkārī mṛtyuḥ pītāśvetāruṇā ||  
  
asitā ca tathānaṃtā madhye madhye prapūjayet |  
ha oṃ saḥ śuci ṣaḍiti prati viṣṇustaveti ca ||  
  
triyaṃvakaṃ ca gāyatrī viṣṇuryoniṃ tathaiva ca |  
tārasya paṃcabhedotthakalānāṃ pūjane sudhī ||  
  
kalādaśakamāvāhya sṛṣṭyādyaṃ sannidhāpya ca |  
haṃsaḥ śuciṣaḍitpādyāṃ ṛcaṃ saṃjapya pūjayet ||  
  
prāṇasaṃsthāpanaṃ kṛtvā kalānāṃ pūjayeccatāḥ |  
evaṃ jarādyāstīkṣṇādyāḥ pītādyāśca vidhānavit ||  
  
nivṛttyādyāścāpi yajedukta yuktyā vicakṣaṇaḥ |  
akārokārakau proktau makāro viṃdunāmakau ||  
  
śaktiḥ śāṃtohyamīsaptadhruvabhedāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |  
aṃtimaudvāvimaubhedaupṛthageva samīritau ||  
  
tataḥ aśvatthapanastha cūtānāṃ pallavāmṛḍaṃ |  
vadhayediṃdravāruṇyālatayāsyedyanasya tu ||  
  
kalpavṛkṣadhiyātaṃ ca bhāvayet kalaśopari |  
pātraṃ taṃḍula saṃpūrṇaṃ nārikela phalānvitaṃ ||  
  
kalpavṛkṣaphalaṃ hyetatsthāpayedanayādhiyā |  
paṭṭavastrayuge nāpi ghaṭaṃ saṃveṣṭayet tataḥ ||  
  
etat pradhānakuṃbhasya sthāpanaṃ parikīrtitaṃ |  
atha pūrvādikāṣṭhāsu toraṇānāṃ samipataḥ ||  
  
yathecchayā maṃḍalāni kuryādvāṣṭadalāni ca |  
tadūrddhaṃśālipuṃjaṃ tu pratidvāraṃ samācaret ||  
  
dadūrddha pūrṇakalaśaṃ tatra ceṣṭāt prapūjayet |  
prāgdhruvaṃdharāṃ dakṣe paścādvākyatimuttare ||  
  
vighneśamatha cāgneyādiṣu kuṃbhān suvinyaset |  
amṛtaṃ durjayaṃ siddhārthakaṃ maṃgalamarcayet ||  
  
punaḥ pūrvādikāṣṭāsu kramādiṃndrādikānyajet |  
lokapālānmaṇḍaleṣu kuṃbhopari ca tadvacā ||  
  
airāvataṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ vāmanaṃ kumudāṃjadau |  
puṣpadaṃtaḥ sārvabhaumaḥ supratīkaṃ tadagrataḥ ||  
  
tato guruḥ svavedyāṃ tu gatvā svasyāsane viśet |  
saṃciṃtya mūlamaṃtreṇa mūrtiṃ tasmin guruttamaḥ ||  
  
tasyāṃ mūrtau mamāvāhya pūjayediṣṭa devatāṃ |  
smṛtvā mūlamanuṃ maṃtrī samyaṅnādī yathā tataḥ ||  
  
nirgamayya ca caitanyaṃ nāsikāgra vinirgataṃ |  
aṃjalau mātṛkā padmemahaḥ puṣpānvite guruḥ ||  
  
p. 40b)  
  
mastakāṃtaṃ samutthāpya tasyāmāvāhayet tataḥ |  
saṃsthāpanaṃ sannidhānaṃ sannirodhaṃ tataścaret ||  
  
saṃmukhīkaraṇaṃ cāpi sakalī karaṇaṃ tataḥ |  
tato vaguṃṭhanaṃ kāryamamṛtīkaraṇaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
paramīkaraṇaṃ kuryāt kramataḥ svasvamudrayā |  
kramādvidadhyācca tata upacārāt prakalpayet ||  
  
āsanāni prasūnāṃtānupacārān prakalpayet |  
tattanmaṃtravidhāneṣu proktāṃgāvaraṇānyapi ||  
  
sarvāṃta lokapālānāṃ tadastrāṇāṃ ca pūjanaṃ |  
vidhāya pūjāmevaṃ hi dhūpadīpanivedyakaiḥ ||  
  
kṛte nivedya ca tato maṇḍalaṃ paritaḥ kramāt |  
pravālāṃkura pātrāṇi sthāpanīyāni maṃtraṇā ||  
  
vedikāyā dakṣabhāge kṛtvā sthaṇḍilamuttamaṃ |  
saṃsthāpya vahni saṃskṛtya vaiśvadevaṃ samārabhet ||  
  
yathāvidhi tatastatra gaṃdhādyairdevatāṃ yajet |  
tatra praṇava pūrvābhirhutvāvyāhṛtibhiḥ purā ||  
  
juhuyān mūlamaṃtreṇa pāyasena ghṛtena ca |  
paṃcaviṃśatibhiḥ paścāddhṛtvāvyāhṛtibhiḥ punaḥ ||  
  
saṃpūjyatāṃ caṃdanādyaiḥ pīṭhamūrtau niyojayet |  
agniṃ visṛjya śiṣṭhena pāyasena valiṃ haret ||  
  
pārṣadebhyaścandanādi puṣpākṣata samanvitaṃ |  
tata utthāpya naivedyaṃ tatsthalaṃ śodhayet sudhīḥ ||  
  
punaryajeccopacāraiḥ paṃcabhirdarśayet tataḥ |  
tarpaṇaṃ vyajanaṃ chatraṃ cāmaraṃmukhavāsakaṃ ||  
  
sahasram ca japenmaṃtrī mūlamaṃtra samāhitaḥ |  
devatāyai nivedyāthataṃjapaṃ saṃpade tataḥ ||  
  
īśānadiśiyaḥ pūrve isthāpito vikirotra ca |  
suvarṇavastra saṃyuktaṃ karatyaṃ jalapūritaṃ ||  
  
nyasedatra yajedastra devatāṃ ghorarūpiṇīṃ |  
paścimāsyāṃ kheṭgakheṭadhāriṇīṃ siṃhasaṃsthitāṃ ||  
  
tiṣṭhansaṃpūjya ca tato gṛhītvātaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ |  
bhramedaṃ tastu dakṣeti lokeśānāmitīrayan ||  
  
nālamuktairnodakena devājñā śrāvaryastataḥ |  
svasthānesthāpayettaṃtu puṇyaṃtreṇa tatorcayet ||
