upaviśya tu bhūyostu gaṃdhādyairmaṃtravittamaḥ |  
proktakuṇḍeṣu vidhivad vahne saṃsthāpanaṃ caret ||  
  
athāgni saṃskāraḥ |  
  
munayaḥ ucuḥ |  
  
agniḥ kva kva ca devāśca hūyategnau surān kathaṃ |  
tamprāpnuvaṃtite devābhinnākasmādvadasvanaḥ ||  
  
īśvara uvāca |  
  
na svarge na ca tīrtheṣu nauṣadhīṣu nabheṣu ca |  
ṛṣayordevatāḥ saṃti maṃtrāsravaṃ hi devatāḥ ||  
  
p. 41a)  
  
sādhakānāṃ phalaṃ dātuṃ tattadrūpaṃ dhṛtaṃ suraiḥ |  
mukhyasvarūpaṃ teṣāṃ tu maṃtrā eva na cetarat ||  
  
tanmaṃtrairyadrutaṃ vahnau kiṃ taddahati pāvakaḥ |  
grahaścinoti tacchreyo yathānāḍyonnajaṃ rasaṃ ||  
  
nirdoṣā tu yathā nāḍī vahedannarasaṃ laghu |  
devayogyo grahastacchredyāṃśaṃ vahate sure ||  
  
sūryabhātiṣubheṣṭharkanādryāśreyobhivarddhate |  
poṣayen vaidikānmaṃtrā nitarān haṃti cāmavat ||  
  
tatastribheṣu saumyasya nāḍībuddhivilāsakṛt |  
tasmāttriṣusitasyāpi vāmināmati puṣṭidā ||  
  
tatastriṣuśane sarve nāśayenmaṃtra saṃcayan |  
caṃdrasya sarvamaṃtrāṇāṃ puṣṭikartṛ tatastriṣu ||  
  
tataḥ satriṣvāranāḍīparenyatra vināśakṛt |  
tasmāt triṣurgurornāḍī satvaraṃ maṃtrasiddhidā ||  
  
rāhunāḍī triṣu tato na satpaiśācaketare |  
triṣṭhataḥ ketunāḍī tu sadbhūte devamaṃtrahṛt ||  
  
tithivāsarasaṃyogāt kṛtaśeṣādṣutāśanaḥ |  
khasthekaukutale netre pratyakṣegnau svarūpake ||  
  
mārayet sādhakaṃ khasthoharate bhūtale dhanaṃ |  
pratyakṣogniḥ phalaṃ datte śubhameva svarūpagaḥ ||  
  
nityanaimittike durgāhomādau na vicārayet |  
vahne tu sthāpanaṃ kuryādvaidikaḥ kalpamārgataḥ ||  
  
tāṃtrikaḥ kuṇḍasaṃskārānaṣṭādaśa samācaret |  
mūlamaṃtreṇa saṃpaśyet prokṣayedastra maṃtrataḥ ||  
  
kuśaiḥ saṃtāḍayet kuṇḍaṃ astramaṃtraṃ paṭhan tridhā |  
tataḥ kavacamaṃtreṇa kuṇḍasyā bhakṣaṇaṃmataṃ ||  
  
astramaṃtreṇa khananaṃ kuṇḍasyāṃgulamānataḥ |  
aṃguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ tāṃmṛdaṃ maṃtreṇa coddharet ||  
  
punaḥ śuddhamṛdātaṃ ca pūrayeddhṛdayāṇunā |  
samīkuryāt tatostreṇa secayet kavacena ca ||  
  
kāṣṭhādinākuṭṭayettanmaṃtreṇasyād yathādṛḍhaṃ |  
kuśaiḥ saṃmārjayet kuṇḍaṃ tataśca kavacāṇunā ||  
  
vilepanaṃ gomayābhiḥ kavace naiva kārayet |  
kavacenāgni sūryendu kalāḥ kuṇḍe viciṃtayet ||  
  
trisūtrīkṛta sūtreṇa veṣṭayet pratimekhalaṃ |  
trivāraṃ varmamaṃtreṇa kuṇḍapūjāṃ tataścaret ||  
  
tāraścāmukakuṇḍāya āsanaṃ tena so iti |  
eṣorghya ityādyūhaiśca sakalaṃ pūjanaṃ caret ||  
  
nābheśca mekhalānāṃ ca kuryādevaṃ prapūjanaṃ |  
saṃciṃtayet tatostreṇa tat kuṇḍaṃ vajravadṛṭaṃ ||  
  
p. 41b)  
  
vahnerjvālānilāsāya hṛnmaṃtreṇa kuśaistataḥ |  
kuṇḍasya tu caturdikṣu kuryānmārga catuṣṭayaṃ ||  
  
acchinnāgaiḥ kuśairvastramaṃtritaiḥ kuṇḍabhittiṣu |  
bhūtapretādidṛṣṭīnāma śucīnāṃ samācaret ||  
  
uccāṭanamime proktāḥ saṃskārā dhṛti saṃmitā |  
bhavedanena vidhinā kuṇḍasyāpyakṣa cāṭavaṃ ||  
  
vāmahome tu saṃskārā ādyāścatvāra eva hi |  
trisrastihyolikhedrekhāḥ prāśudagrācchadādhunā ||  
  
smṛtāśca prāṅmukhāgrāṇāṃ devāvillīśaṃ vāsavāḥ |  
udaṅmukhāgrarekhāṇāṃ brahmasūryaidavaḥ kramāt ||  
  
vilikhedarbhakāṇḍena vāmamārgestu maṃtrataḥ |  
trikoṇo pariṣaṭkoṇaṃ trikoṇaṃ citayasya tu ||  
  
viṣṇvīśa vāsavādīmāṃṣaṇḍāṃ tatra tu pūjanaṃ |  
vāmamārgetviṣṭa devāstrikoṇe pūjanaṃ bhavet ||  
  
saṃprekṣya praṇavenā yogapīṭhaṃ samarcayet |  
tadvidhiḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi maṇḍūkaṃ ciṃtayettale ||  
  
kālāgni rudraṃ tasyorddhaṃ śaktiyuktaṃ viciṃtayet |  
tadūrddhaṃ ciṃtayet kūrma tasya pṛṣṭhe vasuṃdharāṃ ||  
  
śvetadīpaṃ tatra ciṃtyaṃ sudhāsiṃdhu suveṣṭitaṃ |  
maṃdārān pārijātāṃśca saṃtānān haricaṃdanān ||  
  
kalpavṛkṣāṃśca tatraiva ciṃtayet pūjayedapi |  
etādṛśa gṛhe ciṃtyaṃ rasya maṇimayaṃ gṛhaṃ ||  
  
svarṇapīṭhaṃ tu tanmadhye tasya pādānviciṃtayet |  
puruṣārthāṃstu dharmādīn dharmajñānaṃ virāgatāṃ ||  
  
aiśvaryamiti cāṃgāni pīṭhasyoktāni tatra tu |  
madhyenaṃtaṃ tatra padmamānaṃdamayakaṃdakaṃ ||  
  
saṃchinnālaṃ tasya coktā vikāramayakeśarāḥ |  
prakṛtyātmaka pātrāṇi paṃcāśadvarṇakarṇikā ||  
  
sūryasyeṃdoḥ pāvakasya maṇḍala tritayaṃ tataḥ |  
tataḥ pūrvādikāṣṭhāsu satvaṃ rajastamastataḥ ||  
  
aṃtarātmā punaścātmā paramātmā tataḥ paraṃ |  
māyātatvaṃ ca jñānātmākatvātatvaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ ||  
  
vidyātatvaṃ paraṃ tatvaṃ yogapīṭhamitīritaṃ |  
svāgrādi prāgdakṣiṇena tatpadmakeśare prabhuḥ ||  
  
madhyāṃtaṃ pūjayedetājayāṃ ca vijayāṃ tathā |  
ajitākhyāṃ cāparājitāṃ nityāṃ ca vilāsinīṃ ||  
  
dogdhīmadyorāṃ ca tathā maṃgalāmatha tatra tu |  
hrī& sarvaśakti kamalāsanāya nama uccarat ||  
  
datvā puṣpāṃjaliṃ kuṇḍe pūjayed bhuvaneśvarīṃ |  
āvāhanādi paramīkaraṇāṃtaṃ ca pūjayet ||  
  
p. 42a)  
  
kāmonmattaṃ śivaṃ tatra devīmṛtumaṃtī tathā |  
gāṇeśa śaivaśāketeṣu dhyāyet saṃpūjayediti ||  
  
vaiṣṇe ca tathā śaure lakṣmīmṛtumatīṃ smaret |  
nārāyaṇasya saṃyogājjātamagniṃ viciṃtayet ||  
  
araṇyātmaṇito vipragehā vahniṃ kumārikāṃ |  
suvāsināsadvastrākṛtaśaucā samāharet ||  
  
pātrāṃtareṇa pihite tāmrapātrādike śubhe |  
agnipraṇayanaṃ kuryāccharāve vātha nūtane ||  
  
dadyādaṃtreṇa pātregniṃ kavacena pidhāya ca |  
jīrṇeśarāve kāpāle bhinnapātre tatholmuke ||  
  
nāgni praṇayanaṃ kuryād vyādhi hānibhayāpahaṃ |  
kravyādāṃśaṃ ca nairṛtye tyajedastreṇa vahnitaḥ ||  
  
devāṃśaṃ mūlamaṃtreṇa sthāpayedagrataḥ sudhīḥ |  
paścāttamagniṃ saṃskāraiḥ saṃkuryādvīkṣaṇādibhiḥ ||  
  
pradīpakalikākāraṃ teja āvāhayettataḥ |  
aikyaṃ jāṭharavaiṃdavyaṃ vahnibhyāṃ pārthivasya ca ||  
  
smṛtvāgni bījakenātha caitanyaṃ yojayedratha |  
oṃkāreṇābhimaṃtryātha dhenumudrā mṛtīkṛtaṃ ||  
  
saṃrakṣa ca śareṇātha kvacenāvaguṇṭhayet |  
tataḥ saṃpūjya kuṇḍasyadrāmapatiḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ ||  
  
praśavena tataḥ svasya saṃmukhaṃ sviṣakuṃḍake |  
devyāyonau tatra jānuspṛṣṭa bhūmau ca deśikaḥ ||  
  
śivavījamiti dhyātvā niḥkṣipedāśuśukṣaṇiṃ |  
devadevyorācamanaṃ maithunītadhiyācaret ||  
  
citpiṃgala hanahana pacapaca dahadaha |  
sarvajñā jñāpayasvā hātārādi jinavarṇakaḥ ||  
  
amuṃ manuṃ prabhāṣyaiva kṛśānuṃ jvālayet tataḥ |  
maṇivaṃdhau samau kṛtvā karau tu prasṛtāṃgulī ||  
  
madhyame tilite kṛtvā tanmadhyāṃguṣṭakau kṣipet |  
iyaṃ sā paramāmudrā jvālanī homakarmaṇi ||  
  
agniṃ prajvalite vaṃde jātavedaṃ hutāśanaṃ |  
suvarṇavarṇamanalaṃ samiddhaṃ sarvatomukhaṃ ||  
  
anena jvalite maṃtreṇopatiṣṭheddhutāṃśanaṃ |  
mukha naiva dhamedagniṃ mukhā devohyajāyata ||  
  
prādeśamātrāṃ samidhaṃ mulāgradyutasaṃplutāṃ |  
tūṣṇīṃ vahnau samutkṣipyajikāyā devatā nyaset ||  
  
vinyasedātmano dehe maṃtrī jihvādavirbhujaḥ |  
liṃgapāyu śirovaktraghrāṇa netreṣu sarvataḥ ||  
  
vahnirāghrīśa saṃyuktāḥ sādiyāṃtāḥ saviṃdavaḥ |  
varṇāmaṃtrāḥ samuddiṣṭā jihvānāṃ saptadeśikaḥ ||  
  
p. 42b)  
  
kuśaiḥ palāśādiparṇai vā sa pavitreṇa kenacit |  
tataḥ pravinyasejjihvādehe maṃtrī vibhāvasoḥ ||  
  
saliṃgagudamurddhāsya nāsā netreṣu cakramāt |  
sa sarvāṃgeṣu jihvāstā vakṣyaṃte trividhātmikā ||  
  
hiraṇyāgagaṇāraktā kṛṣṇā caiva tu suprabhā |  
vahu ūpā cātiraktā jihvāḥ saptetisyatvikāḥ ||  
  
padmarāgā suvarṇānyā tṛtīyā bhadralohitā |  
lohitānaṃtaraṃ śvetādhūminī ca karālikā ||  
  
rajasyo rasa vā vahnervihitā kāmyakarmasu |  
viśvamūrtisphuliṃginyau dhūmravarṇa manojavā ||  
  
lohitānyā karālākhyā kālītāmasya īritā |  
etāḥ saptaniyuktaṃte krūrakarma sumaṃtribhiḥ ||  
  
svasvanāma samābhāḥ syurjihvākalyāṇaretasaḥ |  
amartyapitṛgaṃdharvayakṣanāgapiśācakāḥ ||  
  
rākṣasāḥ saptajihvānāmīritā adhidevatā |  
jihvāsu tridaśādīnāṃtattatkārya samāptaye ||  
  
juhuyādvāṃchitāṃ siddhiṃ dadyustā devatāmatā |  
analerāghiṃvaṃdvaṃtāḥ sā diyāṃ tākṣarānvitāḥ ||  
  
maṃtrī pravinyased bhūyā vahneraṃgāni vai kramāt |  
sahasrārciḥ svasti pūrṇa uttiṣṭha puruṣastathā ||  
  
dhūmavyāpī saptajihvo havyavāhā tṛtīyakaḥ |  
aśvodarajavaiśvānarākhyakaumāra tejasaḥ ||  
  
viśvamukho devamukho mūrtayoṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ |  
pradakṣiṇa krameṇaiva saṃsiṃcya ca tato jalaiḥ ||  
  
mekhalo parisaṃśuddhaiḥ punardarbha catuṣṭayaiḥ |  
prāgagrairudagraiśca hitvā pūrvāṃ paristaret ||  
  
ekumekhalake kuṇḍe mekhalādhaḥ paristaret |  
dvimekhale dvitīyāyāṃ madhyamāyāṃ trimekhale ||  
  
sthaṇḍile sikatānāṃ tu vāstubhūmau paristaret |  
nālamekhalayormadhye paridhi sthāpanāya ca ||  
  
raṃdhraṃ kuryāttathā vidvānmadhyamāmekhalopari |  
palāśakāśmarī vilvavikaṃkaṭa samudbhavān ||  
  
ekavṛkṣodbhavānārdrān paridhītvāhu mātrakān |  
prāṇānāyamya vidhivat paristīrthakuśāṃtaraiḥ ||  
  
svagṛhokta vidhānena vāyudeśācca pūrvataḥ |  
sruksruvau ca praṇītāṃ ca prokṣaṇīpātra yugmakam ||  
  
ādyasthālīṃ ca paridhīnidhyā ca kuśamuṣṭayaḥ |  
adhomukhāni pātrāṇi homadravyaṃ valiṃ tathā ||  
  
p. 43a)  
  
gaṃdhapuṣpākṣatādīni sarvānyāsādayedatha |  
tānyabhyukṣya pavitreṇa cottānāni vidhāya ca ||  
  
prokṣaṇī pātrayugalaṃ paripūrya śubhāṃvunā |  
datvā kṣatānpavitraṃ ca tadūtyūyanidhāyayet ||  
  
diśyuttarasyāṃ tatpātraṃ praṇītāṃ pūryate budhaiḥ |  
tataḥ kiṃcit praṇītāṃvu prokṣaṇyādhāya tajjalaiḥ ||  
  
yajñasādhanasaṃbhāraṃ prokṣayen mūlamaṃtrataḥ |  
vṛṇuyād brāhmaṇaṃ śāṃtaṃ devatāṃ maṃtradīkṣitaṃ ||  
  
kuṇḍasya dakṣiṇebhāge veśayettaṃ kuśāsane |  
amukāmukagotrohamamukāmukagotriṇaṃ ||  
  
dīkṣāṃga bhūtahomesmin brahmāṇaṃ tvāṃ vṛṇo iti |  
vastrālaṃkārādikena kṛtvātaṃ paripūrayet ||  
  
kuryāt kuśavaddhuṃ cāpi labhyate brāhmaṇo na cet |  
kuṇḍamadhye tu ṣaṭkoṇagarbhitaṃ svarṇakarṇitaṃ ||  
  
nānākeśara saṃyuktaṃ caturdvāra samāvṛtaṃ |  
ciṃtayedaṣṭadalakaṃ caturasra trayāvṛtaṃ ||  
  
pūjāpīṭhaṃ tu tadvahnestatra maṇḍūka kādikān |  
jñānātmāṃtaṃ yogapīṭhaṃ saṃpūjyāṣṭa daleṣu tu ||  
  
prāgdakṣiṇena madhyāṃtaṃ pītāṃ śvetāṃ tathāruṇāṃ |  
kṛṣṇāṃ dhūmrāṃ ca pūjayedvisphuliṃginīṃ ||  
  
rucirāṃ jvālinīṃ ceti sarvaṃ pīṭhaṃ prapūjayet |  
sarvaśaktiḥ komalāsanāya dṛdvādaśākṣaraḥ ||  
  
samastapīṭhapūjāyāṃ vahnermaṃtra udāhṛtā |  
tato hutāśanaṃ dhyāyedvarasvastika śaktibhiḥ ||  
  
abhayena ca saṃyuktairbhujaiḥ samyagvirājitaṃ |  
siṃdūravarṇaṃ padmasthaṃ svarṇālaṃkārabhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
trinetraṃ ca jaṭāmaulimaruṇāsragitāṃvaraṃ |  
dhyātvaivaṃ manunānena pūjayedupacārakaiḥ ||  
  
vaiśvānaro jātavedo ihāvaha lohitākṣa |  
sarvakarmāṇi sādhaye svāhāṃtaḥ praṇavādikaḥ ||  
  
saptaviṃśatyakṣaroyaṃ maṃtraḥ syādvahni pūjanaṃ |  
tataḥ ṣaṭkoṇa madhye ca jihvā dhyānaṃ ca pūjanaṃ ||  
  
jihvā jvālārucaḥ sarvāvarābhayakarostathā |  
aiśyāṃ hiraṇyā svarṇābhāṃ śāṃtipauṣṭika siddhidā ||  
  
vaiḍūrya varṇā kanakā prācyāṃ staṃbhana kāryakṛt |  
vidveṣe tadvaṇādityanibhāraktāgni koṇagā ||  
  
p. 43b)  
  
kṛṣṇāṃjana ca paprakhyā naiṛtyāṃmāraṇakṣamāḥ |  
suprabhā padmarāgā bhāvāruṇyāṃ dhanadāyakā ||  
  
atiraktā jayābhāsoccāṭe vāyurdiśāgatā |  
vahurūpā tu ṣaṭkoṇa madhye ṣaḍvarṇa saṃyutā ||  
  
anekakārya saṃsiddhi nāśakartrī ca sāmatā |  
yathā kāryaṃ tathā jihvā dṛśyate cet svadiggatā ||  
  
jvālā rūpā tadā siddhiviparye tu viparyayaḥ |  
agnīśāsura vāyavyā devāgre cāpi dikṣu ca ||  
  
pūjayecca ṣaḍaṃgāni patre vyāvṛtti devatāḥ |  
iṃdrādīnsāyudhānyaścāt saṃpūjyāgniṃ punaryajet ||  
  
tataścādhomukhau kṛtvā sruksruvau tu pratāpayet |  
kuśāgraistu tayoragraṃ madhyaṃ madhyaiśca mārjayet ||  
  
mūlaṃ mūlaistridhā caiva mārjayitvā pratāpayet |  
dhṛtvātau vāmahastena prokṣayet prokṣaṇī jalaiḥ ||  
  
dakṣiṇeṇa karāgreṇa punaḥ saṃtāpayeccatau |  
kuśānkṣiptā tato vahnau svadakṣatau kuśāstare ||  
  
saṃsthāpya sruksruvau paścādghṛta saṃskāramācaret |  
samādāya ghṛtasthālī maṃtramaṃtreṇa secayet ||  
  
ghṛtaṃ tatra samāpūrya vīkṣaṇādi susaṃskṛtaṃ |  
vāyavye vāhyatāṃgāvot kṛtvā teṣu hṛdānyaset ||  
  
tāpanaṃ tu samuddiṣṭaṃ kuśadvayamataḥ kṣipet |  
ājye prajvalitaṃ vahnau vinyasetadghṛtānvitaṃ ||  
  
pavitrīkaraṇaṃ darbhadvayena jvalito hṛdā |  
varmaṇājyaṃ ca nīrājya vahnau darbhadvayaṃ kṣipet ||  
  
abhidyotanametatsyādudyotanamathocyate |  
kuśaṃ prajvalitaṃ cākṣye darśayattaddhṛdā kṣipet ||  
  
vahnābuddhāsya ca ghṛtamaṃgārānagniṣu kṣipet |  
ayaḥ saṃspṛśya maṃtrajñaḥ kuryādutplavanaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
astre maṃtraṃ japaṃ maṃtrāṃkuśau prādeśamātrakau |  
aṃguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ ca gṛhītvā ghṛtamutplavet ||  
  
tato dṛḍhaṃ kuśābhyāṃ tu svābhimukhyena saṃplavet |  
ghṛtaṃ tatsyāt saṃplavanaṃ ṣaṭsaṃskārā itīritāḥ ||  
  
uttamaṃ goghṛtaṃ proktaṃ madhyamaṃ mahiṣī bhavaṃ |  
adhamaṃ chāgalī jātaṃ niṣiddhaṃ tveḍakādijaṃ ||  
  
krītaṃ yadāpaṇe cājyaṃ svāducedgavyavattu tat |  
kuśadvayaṃ ghṛtenyasya tataḥ prādeśa saṃmitaṃ ||  
  
sa graṃthikatvāhvāgnaudvau śuklakṛṣṇau viciṃtayet |  
pakṣau vāma iḍāṃ dakṣe piṃgalāṃ madhyatastataḥ ||  
  
p. 44a)  
  
suṣumṇāṃ saṃsmarenmaṃtrī tato homaṃ samācaret |  
dakṣabhāgātsruveṇākṣyaṃ pragṛhnīṃyā hṛdādhunā ||  
  
dakṣenetre hutāśasyāgneye svāheti homayet |  
gṛhītvājyaṃ vāmabhāgā hṛdā vāmegni locane ||  
  
hunet somāya svāheti tyāgaḥ sarvatra saṃmataḥ |  
hṛnmaṃtreṇa gṛhītvājyaṃ madhyato madhyalocane ||  
  
hunettasyāgni somābhyāṃ svāheti ca tṛtīyakāṃ |  
dakṣabhāgāt punastyājyaṃ hṛnmaṃtreṇa samāharet ||  
  
agnivaktre'gnayesviṣṭe kṛte svāheti homayet |  
satārābhirvyāhṛtibhirājyena juhuyāt punaḥ ||  
  
juhuyādagnimaṃtreṇa trivāraṃ deśikottamaḥ |  
garbhādhānādikā vahneḥ samudvāhāvasānikāḥ ||  
  
śubhe karmaṇi kartavyā ājyāhutyaṣṭakaiḥ kriyā |  
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuccārya karmanāma samuccaret ||  
  
saṃpādayāmi svāheti sarvakarma svayaṃvidhiḥ |  
garbhādhānaḥ puṃsavanaṃ sīmaṃtonnayanaṃ caret ||  
  
jātaṃ vāgīśvarī garbhāt prāgvayeddhyo hutāśanaṃ |  
jātakarmaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā nālachedaṃ samācaret ||  
  
sūtakaṃ sādhayitvātha kuryānnāma yathāvidhiḥ |  
tṛptaye yasya pade tatsyāgnistannāmapūrvakaḥ ||  
  
cauropanayanaṃ vahnermahānāmnī vrataṃ tathā |  
mahāvrataṃ copaniṣaddhataṃ godānameva ca ||  
  
samāvartanamudvāhaḥ śākte vāgbhava pūrvakāḥ |  
tataśca vahneḥ pitarau devadevyādikau tathā ||  
  
pūjayitvā visṛjyātha mūlāgreṣu ghṛtaplutāḥ |  
samidho niḥkṣipetyaṃ ca vahnāvatha ca pūrvavat ||  
  
sa bījarasa nānāmnācaike kāmāhutiṃ hunet |  
tataścāṃgāni juhuyād vahnermūrtyaṣṭakaṃ tathā ||  
  
indrāgni lokapālāṃśca āyudhāni tataḥ paraṃ |  
maṃtreṇākāra pūrveṇa svāhāṃtena vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
svāhā vasāne juhuyāddhyāyan maṃtradevatāṃ |  
caturvāraṃ sruveṇājyaṃ gṛhītvāsuci niḥkṣipet ||  
  
tenaiva tāṃ vidhāyāgnau hunettiṣṭan guruḥ svayaṃ |  
vauṣaḍaṃte vahnestu manunāsaṃ yade tat ||  
  
jihvāyāṃ madhyasaṃsthāyāṃ maṃtrī jvālāvalītaroḥ |  
tārādyairdaśabhirbhedaiḥ pūrvapūrva samanvitaiḥ ||  
  
p. 44b)  
  
manunā gāṇapatyena hunetpūrvaṃ daśāhutī |  
juhuyācca caturvāraṃ samaste naiva tena su ||  
  
saṃpūjya devatāpīṭhaṃ vahnau samyaktato guruḥ |  
agnirūpadharāṃ tatra pūjayediṣṭa devatām ||  
  
ājyena sadhyamanunā paṃcaviṃśati saṃkhyakaṃ |  
hunenmaṃtrī cāgnimukhevaktraikīkaraṇaṃ tvidaṃ ||  
  
ātmāgni devatānāṃ ciṃtayennaikyamātmavit |  
ekādaśātha mūlena hunedājyena vā hutiḥ ||  
  
rātrīsaṃdhyā name taddi proktaṃ deśikamuttamaiḥ |  
aṃgaprabhṛtyāmṛttīmāmekai kāmāhutiṃ hunet ||  
  
pūrvādi dikṣu kuṃḍeṣu sarveṣvapi yathāvidhiḥ |  
evaṃ vahniṃ susaṃskṛtya caruṃ gopayasā pacet ||  
  
na caitāmrādike pātre kṣāriteva śarādhunā |  
mūlādhunābhimaṃtryātha taṇḍulānśālisaṃbhavān ||  
  
tithi prasṛtimānena śarāṇuṃ prajapan kṣipet |  
prakṣālitena pātreṇa yāvadvaktraṃ pidhāya ca ||  
  
hra& maṃtreṇa tato mūla manunā deśikottamaḥ |  
pacedguruḥ prāṅmukhastasvinnetamabhidhārayet ||  
  
mūlena śruvasaṃsthena ghṛtenāthāvatārayet |  
haṃ maṃtreṇāstra saṃjapte kuśastīrṇe vibhajyatāṃ ||  
  
tridhāsvekaṃ devatāyai paraṃ vahnau nivedayet |  
śiṣṭaṃ śiṣyeṇasahito gururbhuṃjīta maṃtravit ||  
  
prādeśamātraṃ dvirjaptaṃ yathoktaṃ daṃtadhāvanaṃ |  
śiṣyāya dadyāt saradātviśodhyakṣālitaṃ tyajet ||  
  
ācāṃta maṃtraṃ ca yathā vidhitaṃ śikhāyāṃ vaṃdhaiḥ murakṣitamamuṃ   
pravidhāya maṃtrī |  
vedyāṃśayītakuśasaṃstaraṇeraṇanyāṃ śiṣyeṇa sārddhaṃ mamunā gadito   
dhivāsaḥ ||  
  
atha dīkṣādinakṛtyaṃ |  
  
samutthāyoṣasi punaḥ snānasaṃdhyādikaṃ caret |  
guruḥśiṣyo ṛtvijaśca gacchedyāga gṛhaṃ prati ||  
  
sarve te svasva kuṇḍeṣu juhuyuḥ saghṛtaistilaiḥ |  
punaḥ sādhyena manunā jyeṣṭhottara sahasrakaṃ ||  
  
apradīptena hotavyaṃ madhyamenāpyaniṃdhite |  
pradīpte lelihānegnau hotavyaṃ karmasiddhaye ||  
  
aṃdho budhaḥ sadhūme tu juhuyādyo hutāśane |  
yajamāno bhavedaṃdhaḥ saputra iti ca śrutiḥ ||  
  
yonarviṣijuhotyagnauvyaṃgāriṇi ca mānavaḥ |  
maṃdāgnirāmayāvī ca daridraścopa jāyate ||  
  
agneḥ karṇe homatovyādhi vādhānetreṃdhatvaṃ nāsikāyāmathāvidhiḥ |  
dravyachedomastakesyānmukhāṃtarhomaṃ kuryāt tena nityaṃ vipaścit ||  
  
p. 45a)  
  
yatra kāṣṭhaṃ tatra śrotre yatra dhūmastu nāsike |  
yatrālyajvalanaṃ netre yatra bhasma tu tacchiraḥ ||  
  
yatraiva jvalito vahnistatra jihvā prakīrtitāḥ |  
vaiśvānaraṃ sthitaṃ dhyāyet siddhomeṣu deśikaḥ ||  
  
śayānamājya homeṣu nivarṇaśeṣa vastuṣu |  
svarṇasiṃdūravālārka kuṃkumakṣaudrasannibhaṃ ||  
  
savarṇareva sauvarṇaḥ śobhanaḥ parikīrtitaḥ |  
bherīvāridahastīṃdradhvanirvahneḥ śubhāvahaḥ ||  
  
nāgaḥ caṃpakapunnāgapāṭalā yūthikānibhaḥ |  
padmeṃdīvarakalhāraḥ sarpirguggulusannibhaḥ ||  
  
pāvakasya śubhogaṃdho ityuktastava vedibhiḥ |  
pradakṣiṇāstyaktakaṃpāśchatrābhāḥ śikhinaḥ śikhāḥ ||  
  
śubhadā yajamānasya rājyasyāpi viśeṣataḥ |  
kuṃdendudhavalodhūmo vahneḥ proktaḥ śubhāvahaḥ ||  
  
kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇagate varṇo yajamānaṃ vināśayet |  
śvetorājyaṃ nihaṃtyābhuvāya saḥ svarasannibhaḥ ||  
  
svaraḥ svara samovahne dhvaniḥ sarvavināśakṛt |  
pūtigaṃdho hutabhujorhyetu duḥkhaprado bhavet ||  
  
chinnavṛttāśikhā kuryān mṛtyuṃ dhanaparikṣayaṃ |  
śukapakṣanibho dhūmaḥ pārāvata samaprabhaḥ ||  
  
hāniṃ tu ragajātīnāṃ gavāṃ ca kurute'cirāt |  
evaṃvidheṣu doṣeṣu prāyaścittāya deśikaḥ ||  
  
mūlenājyena juhuyān paṃcaviṃśatimāhutiḥ |  
śiṣyaṃ snātaṃ paṃcagavyaṃ pāyayen maṃtravittamaḥ ||  
  
kuṇḍasyābhyā samānīya divyadṛṣṭyāvyalokayet |  
hṛtpuṇḍarīkā caitanyaṃ tasyātmani niyojayet ||  
  
ācāryastatra cādhvānaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ śodhayet kramāt |  
śodhanaṃ nāmatatvānāṃ kāraṇaikatva ciṃtanaṃ ||  
  
varṇādīnāṃ kalānāṃ ca tāsāṃ cidaikya ciṃtanaṃ |  
gururvahiḥ praviharet saṃskṛteṣūkta vartmanā ||  
  
sarvartvijaścaṃdanādyaiḥ saṃpūjyā prokta devatāṃ |  
sarvāvaraṇa saṃyuktau mūlena juhuyustataḥ ||  
  
paṃcaviṃśatidhā sarpiḥ saṃyutena payoṃdhasā |  
sruveṇākṣaṃ samityāṇyāsruvā śeṣaṃ kareṇa tu ||  
  
tatrā divyena hotavyaṃ tīrthe vāhyena vā tathā |  
dadyādvaliṃgaṃdhapuṣpadhūpapūrvakamādarāt ||  
  
nakṣatrāṇāṃ savārāṇāṃ rāśīnāṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak |  
devatābhyaḥ padaṃ proktā divānaktaṃ vadet tathā ||  
  
p. 45b)  
  
cāribhyaścātha sarvebhyo bhūtebhyaśca namo vadet |  
hunenmahāvyāhṛtibhisvato deśikasattamaḥ ||  
  
aṃgaprabhṛtyā vṛttīnāṃ hunedbhūyo ghṛtena vai |  
brahmārpaṇākhya maṃtreṇa sarvakarmachidesudhīḥ ||  
  
juhuyādāhutīraṣṭau kevalājyena maṃtravit |  
hutvā pūrṇāhutī maṃtrī srutvā mūlāṇunmatataḥ ||  
  
agnisaṃprārthyāgni sāṃgamaṃtreṇaikāhutiṃhunet |  
sarpiṣāsru ca māpūrya puṣpaṃ coparyadhomukhaṃ ||  
  
sruguparisruvaṃ datvā puṣpaṃ tatra prapātayet |  
savyottara karābhyāṃ ca saṃpuṭābhyāṃ ca śeṣavat ||  
  
saṃgṛhyotthāya saṃlagnau nābhautiryaṅnidhāya ca |  
pūrṇādarvītimaṃtreṇa mūlena vasu saṃyutaḥ ||  
  
dadyāt pūrṇāhutīstisraḥ sarvakāma prapūraṇīḥ |  
śrotriyasye tadduddiṣṭamanyaḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ caret ||  
  
mūlena vauṣaḍaṃtena svāhāṃtena tu vāmagaḥ |  
homaṃ tu māṃsamadyābhyāṃ tīrthājyābhyāṃ ca pūrṇatāṃ ||  
  
kuryāt svāhāṃta mūlena phalājyena tu vaidikaḥ |  
dakṣapādaṃ puraskṛtya dakṣaḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ caret ||  
  
śaktihome vāmapādaṃ vāmamārgī ca sarvataḥ |  
punaḥ saṃtyajya gaṃdhādyairmūlamaṃtreṇa maṃtravit ||   
  
kuṇḍādudvāsya vācāryo devatāṃ kalaśe nyaset |  
sāṃgāṃ śāvaraṇaṃ tatra pūjayecca yathāvidhiḥ ||  
  
saptavyāhatyagni jihvāṃgamūrtīnāmathaikikāṃ |  
dugdhena pariṣiṃcyāgniṃ prārthayīta tato guruḥ ||  
  
bhobho vahne mahāśakte sarvakāmapradāyaka |  
karmāṃtarepi saṃprāpte sānnidhyaṃ kurusādaraṃ ||  
  
iti maṃtreṇa saṃprārthya vahnimudvāsayedapi |  
tato brahmāṇamudvāsya brāhmaṇāya pradāpayet ||  
  
dvāviṃśatyalamātreyaṃ nirmitaṃ tāmrapātrakaṃ |  
taṇḍulaistat samāpūrya sahiraṇyaṃ sadakṣiṇaṃ ||  
  
dadyād viprāyatattuṣṭyai pūrṇapātramitīritaṃ |  
tataḥ parisarānagnau paridhīn prakṣipennatu ||  
  
nityanaimittikenāstu kṣipeddeśika sattamaḥ |  
vastreṇa netramaṃtreṇa śiṣyanetre nivadhyate ||  
  
kuṇḍāhaste samādāya nayanmaṇḍalasannidhau |  
sumanobhiḥ prapūryāsya aṃjalī kṣepayerdyade ||  
  
mūlamaṃtroccārapūrvaṃ devatāprītayeguruḥ |  
netravaṃdhamayāsyopaveśayet kuśasaṃstare ||  
  
p. 46a)  
  
tataśca pāṭhayan śiṣyaṃ maṃtramenaṃ gurūttamaḥ |  
ajñānatimirāṃdhasya jñānāṃjana śalākayā ||  
  
cakṣurunmīlitaṃ yena tasmai śrīguravenamaḥ |  
aṃtaḥ pūjāvidhānena saṃharejjanaṣeccataṃ ||  
  
śiṣyotha tasya maṃtrasya nyāsāṃ deho parinyaset |  
paṃcopacārairabhyarcyakalastheṣṭadevatāṃ ||  
  
yathokta vartmanā tatra sakalīkṛtyamācaret |  
athopaveśayecchiṣyaṃ bhūṣitaṃ maṇḍalāṃtare ||  
  
kuṃbhāsyastha suradruṃścamūrddhanyasya śiśorguruḥ |  
atha paṃcaninādaiśca viprāṇāṃ ca vanaiḥ saha ||  
  
susthitaṃ niyatātmānaṃ siṃcet kalaśapuṣpakaiḥ |  
yena prakāreṇa purāyojitaśca sudhāmayaiḥ ||  
  
toyairakṣarasaṃyuktairghaṭasthenaivartmanā |  
atha śiṣyaṃ cābhiṣiṃcedāśusaṃpadavāptaye ||  
  
gṛhītvābhyarcitaṃ pūrvaṃ karakaṃ hyastrarūpiṇaṃ |  
tattoyairabhiṣiṃcettaṃ rakṣāyai deśikottamaḥ ||  
  
janena śiṣṭena śiśuṃ gururā vāmayettataḥ |  
taddevasvarūpeṇa vidadhyāt sakalīkṛtiṃ ||  
  
vāsasī vimale ramye paridhāyājñayā guroḥ |  
ācamya nikaṭe tasya samyaktasya manuṃ triśaḥ ||  
  
dakṣakarṇevadedvidvānviprāyodakapūrvakaṃ |  
anyebhyastu vade devameva maṃtraṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
dakṣakarṇe triśovidyāmekoccāreṇacoccaret |  
eṣuvidhirdvijātīnāṃ strīśūdrāṇāṃ ca vāmataḥ ||  
  
svayaṃ jyotirmayīṃ vidyāṃ gacchaṃtīṃ bhāvayedguruḥ |  
agatāṃ bhāvayecchiṣyo na sosmīti viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ śiṣyaḥ prajapedguruṇoditaṃ |  
aṣṭāviṃśativāraṃ vāhyaṣṭa kṛtvothavā japet ||  
  
gurudevātma maṃtrāṇāmaikyaṃ śiṣyo vibhāvayan |  
praṇāmaṃ gurave kuryāt sādhako bhaktimānmuhuḥ ||  
  
sāṣṭāṃgaścātha paṃcāṃgaṃ pūjākarmasusaṃyataḥ |  
hastābhyāṃ caraṇābhyāṃ ca jānubhyāṃ vakṣasā tathā ||  
  
mūrddhyā dṛṣṭyā tathā vācā cittenāṣṭhāṃga īritaḥ |  
hastajānu śirovākya * * * * * (?) īritaṃ ||  
  
alaṃkārāṃśca vāsāṃsidadyādṛtvigmya ādarāt ||  
  
īśvarāvarṇa vudhyānu dvijāsīṃbhiśca naṃdanaḥ |  
pradadyādgurave śiṣyaḥ svadhanārthaṃ tadarddhakaṃ ||  
  
daśāṃśaṃ vā pradadyācca vittaśāthya vivarjitaḥ |  
gobhūhiraṇya vipinagṛhakṣetrādikaṃ tathā ||  
  
p. 46b)  
  
akleśādanna vastrādi dadyādvittānusārataḥ |  
prākārāṃtaramālaṃvya guruṃ yatnene toṣayet ||  
  
tadadhīnamanānityaṃ tacciṃtana parāyaṇaḥ |  
tasyādābja rajobhūṣo bhavet sādhakasattamaḥ ||  
  
tato nānāvidhairbhakṣyairlehyacoṣyaistathā pare |  
brāhmaṇān bhojayet samyak pradadyādbhūri dakṣiṇāṃ ||  
  
evaṃ kriyāmayī dīkṣā saṃpadātrī nirūpitā |  
rājñāṃ dhanāhya vaiśyānāṃ viprāṇāṃ vyavasāyināṃ ||  
  
atha vīrāṇāṃ viśeṣaḥ ||  
  
kuladravyaiḥ samabhyarcya kulacakraṃ vidhānataḥ |  
śiṣyāya darśayet samyagdīkṣerya kaulikīmatā ||  
  
ṛṣyādi * ? sattāmenāṃ likhitvā bhūmimadhyagāṃ |  
puṣpādinā samabhyarcya śiṣyāyātha pradarśayet ||  
  
yadi śiṣye mahāprītistadākarṇe vadedguruḥ |  
tatopyatitarāṃ śiṣyo guruścedbhaktibhājanaṃ ||  
  
tadāgaṃḍūṣa pūrvāhi dadyādenāṃ gurūttamaḥ |  
nirvikalpopi śiṣyastadgṛhnīyāddhṛṣṭhamānasaḥ ||  
  
tadabhāvena siddhiḥ syāddevatāśāpamāpnuyā |  
siddhidravyaṃ mukhepūrya paṃcavyomāmṛtānvitaṃ ||  
  
abhiṣiṃcet priyaṃ śiṣyaṃ gaṃḍūṣākhyoyamīritaḥ |  
ayaṃ dīkṣākramaḥ prokto bhogayuksiddhimicchatāṃ ||  
  
atha kulastrīṇāṃ viśeṣaḥ |  
  
vīrakāṃtāṃ samānīya suśīlāṃ suyaśasvinī |  
kulabhaktaguruṃ prāpya dīkṣayet kuladīkṣayā ||  
  
pārānaṃdarasāghūrṇalocanāṃ kulajāṃ satīṃ |  
tāṃbūla pūgapūrṇāsyāṃ guruvākyarataḥ mukhī ||  
  
nijaputrīvadācāryastadbhālapaṭṭake likhet |  
śakticakraṃ tridhāvṛtya likhet kāmakalāṃ tataḥ ||  
  
tanmadhye deyamaṃtreṇa darbhitaṃ māmalāṃchanaṃ |  
tatra devīṃ samāvāhya dhṛtvā tatra prapūjya ca ||  
  
tatastatputrikākarṇe ṛṣiśchaṃdaḥ samanvitaṃ |  
mūlamaṃtraṃ tridhāvṛtya kathayed vāmakarṇakaḥ ||  
  
adyaḥ prabhṛti putrītvaṃ kuladīkṣārcaneratā |  
yathopadiśyavidhinā sāmarasyaṃ samānayet ||  
  
ityanujñāṃ gurorlajjādaṇḍavat praṇamedbhuviṃ |  
trāhinātha kulācāra padminī padmanāyakaḥ ||  
  
tvatpādāṃbhoruhacchāyāṃ mūrddhni dehi yaśodhana |  
gurave dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāttāṃbūlāruṇalocanaḥ ||  
  
svakulaṃ paramīkṛtya yathoddiṣṭaṃ samarcayet |  
aṃgāvaraṇa pūjādauyadina kramate kulaṃ ||  
  
p. 47a)  
  
tadā mūrddhni guruṃ dhyātvā kulāmṛtarasena tu |  
tarpayitvā kulaṃ dhyātvā japenmaṃtraṃ nirākulaṃ ||  
  
atha varṇamayīdīkṣā |  
  
atha varṇamayīṃ dīkṣāṃ śṛṇvaṃ tu jñānadāyinīṃ |  
puṃprakṛtvātmakatvaṃ ca varṇānāṃ samudīritaṃ ||  
  
tādṛskaṃ ca śarīrasya proktamevāstideśikaiḥ |  
tatastanau śiśornyasye darśāndeśikasattamaḥ ||  
  
saṃharedvaiparītyena varṇān tatsthāna saṃsthitān |  
deśikeṃdraḥ svasāmarthyādājñayā devatātmanaḥ ||  
  
devatātmā bhavecchiṣyastadā saṃlīna tatvakaḥ |  
tatastu śiṣya caitanyaṃ paramātma niyojayet ||  
  
tānarṇāṃstata utpādya nyasecchiṣya śarīrake |  
tasmiṃśca sṛṣṭi kramatastaccaitanyaṃ punarnyaset ||  
  
bhavecchiṣ.yo devatātmā nityānaṃdātmakaḥ śivaḥ |  
jñānadārṇamayīdīkṣā kathitāḥ sarvasiddhidā ||  
  
atha vakṣye kalāṃ dīkṣāṃ maṇimādyaṣṭasiddhidāṃ |  
veda paṃcakalāṃ dīkṣādakṣeṣṭa trikalāmatā ||  
  
kupaṃcāśat kalā vāme siddhamaṃtra gurostu sā |  
grāhyādrutaṃ siddhakartrī viparīte viparyayaḥ ||  
  
kalā nivṛtti pramukhā bhūtānāṃ paṃcaceritāḥ |  
śiṣyakāye bhūtamaye vedhayettā kramātsudhīḥ ||  
  
pādādi jānuparyaṃtaṃ nivṛttiḥ saṃsthitāḥ kalāḥ |  
jānvoḥ sakāśādānābhiḥ pratiṣṭhākhyāḥ kalāsthitāḥ ||  
  
nābhitaḥ kaṇṭhaparyaṃtaṃ vidyākhyā saṃsthitāḥ kalāḥ |  
kaṇṭhatohyālalāṭāṃtaṃ śāṃtyākhyā saṃsthitāḥ kalāṃ ||  
  
bhālācchirāvadhiḥ proktā śāṃtyatītākalāḥ tathā |  
saṃhṛtiḥ kramato vidvān vedhayet sthānatonyataḥ ||  
  
sthāne svīyājñayā caiva dīkṣā paṃcakalāḥ smṛtāḥ |  
aṣṭatriṃśatkalādīkṣāyuktiṃ śṛṇvaṃ tu devatāḥ ||  
  
krameṇakādikāvarṇāpatra dvādaśa saṃsthitāḥ |  
vilomābhādikā yatra tatra sthāna dvaye kalā ||  
  
bhāvanīyāstu sūryasya ṣoḍaśāsuvidhostathā |  
yakārādisthale vahnerbhāvanīyāḥ kalādaśaḥ ||  
  
tato varṇa kalānāṃ tu varṇasthānārccamaṃ hṛtiḥ |  
punaścajanayecchiṣyaṃ kalādīkṣāvidhiḥ svayaṃ ||  
  
atha vedhamayīdīkṣā |  
  
kaulike vāmamārge ca vedadīkṣā phalapradā |  
anyāstāda dakṣiṇemārge'nyathādbhūpatito bhavet ||  
  
p. 47b)  
  
dīkṣāṃ vedhamayīṃ vakṣyeyāṃ lajjā tyajate janaḥ |  
tatkālameva saṃsāraṃ jīvanmuktobhijāyate ||  
  
mūlādhāre tu śiṣyasya dhyāyet kaṃjaṃ caturdalaṃ |  
tasyāmadhye trikoṇe tu tanmadhye cāpi kuṇḍalīṃ ||  
  
trirāvartamayīṃ devīṃ vidyutpuṃjasvarūpiṇīṃ |  
māhādevamayīṃ sākṣāddhānamātra śarīriṇāṃ ||  
  
aṇoraṇīyasīṃ devīṃ cakraṣaṅka prabhedinīṃ |  
suṣumṇā vartmanādivyāṃ yāṃtiṃ śivagṛhaṃ prati ||  
  
sāṃtavādidalasthārṇāt padmasthāne samāharet |  
ṣaḍdale kamale taṃtulāṃta vādyarṇayugdale ||  
  
svādhisthāne guruḥ samyagyojayitvā tu vedhayet |  
tadarṇānānayedviṣṇauviṣṇuṃtaṃ nābhipaṃkaje ||  
  
phāṃtaḍādyarṇasaṃyukte digdale vedhayet svayaṃ |  
varṇān tān yojayedrudrerudraṃtaṃ hṛtsaroruhe ||  
  
kāṃtaṭhādyarṇa patrābjairvedhayedīśvare svayaṃ |  
varṇān tānāharedasmin kaṃthapadmevataṃ tathā ||  
  
kalādalamaye padme svarān saṃyojya yatnataḥ |  
sadāśivetha saṃyojyatānstadbhrūmadhyapadmake ||  
  
dvidalehakṣa saṃyukte vedhayitvātha deśikaḥ |  
śaktyā sa daivamātmānaṃ nayet paraśivāvadhi ||  
  
deśikājñāvaśācchiṣyodagdhā jñānastadākṣitau |  
patedavāptavijñānaḥ sarvajño jāyate tataḥ ||  
  
sadāśivaḥ svayaṃbhūyāt satyameva na saṃśayaḥ |  
iyaṃ jñānapradā proktā dīkṣāvedhātmikā śubhā ||  
  
atha sparśamayīdīkṣā |  
  
guruḥ svasyaṃ guruṃ dhyāyet svahastai śivarūpiṇaṃ |  
mūlavidyāṃ ṣaḍaṃgaṃ ca mātṛkādi manuṃ japan ||  
  
śiṣyasya mastake datvā kṛpayā dakṣiṇaṃ karaṃ |  
paścādupadiśet proktā sparśadīkṣāti siddhidā ||  
  
sadāśiveti cidrūpe guruścittaṃ nidhāpayet |  
maṃtrānsamastāntajjātān dhyāyaṃtsvayaṃ tadātmakaṃ ||  
  
jāto gurośca kṛpayā kevalohaṃ sadāśivaḥ |  
iti dhyāyannupadiśedvāgdīkṣātkiyamīritā ||  
  
nimīlya nayane dhyātvā paramātmani devatāṃ |  
taddarśanānaṃda pūrṇanetrābhyāṃ vīkṣayed guruḥ ||  
  
śiṣyaṃ prasannacittaḥ san paścādupadiśoditi |  
maṃtrasiddhasya siddhyaisyādṛgdīkṣephalaṃpradā ||  
  
gurorā lokamātreṇa bhāṣaṇāt sparśanādapi |  
sadyaḥ saṃjāyate jñānaṃ sādīkṣā śāṃbhavī smṛtā ||  
  
bhuktimukti prasiddhyarthaṃ parikṣya vidhivadguruḥ |  
paścādupadiśenmaṃtramanyathāniḥ phalaṃ labhet ||  
  
p. 48a)  
  
atha upadeśo yathā |  
  
mahādīkṣā tathā dīkṣā upadeśastataḥ paraṃ |  
yuge kṛtādau kartavyā upadeśaḥ kalauyuge ||  
  
caṃdrasūryagrahetīrthe siddhakṣetre śivālaye |  
maṃtramātra prakathanamupadeśaḥ sa ucyate ||  
  
atha kaulikopadeśaḥ |  
  
nyāsajālaṃ vidhāyādau śaṃkhapātrādi sthāpanaṃ |  
kṛtvā devīṃ samabhyarcya makārapaṃcakaiḥ plutaḥ ||  
  
kāraṇaṃ tanmukhe datvā paścādvidyāṃ samuccaret |  
kathitoyaṃ maheśāni upadeśastu kaulikaḥ ||  
  
anyāyena ca yodadyādgṛhnātyanyāyataścayaḥ |  
dadato gṛhnato vāpi kulaśāpo bhaviṣyati ||  
  
guruśiṣyāvubhau mohoda parīkṣya parasparaṃ |  
aśāstrīyopadeśaṃ tu yo gṛhnāti dadāti ca ||  
  
bhuṃjītetāvubhau ghorānnarakānekaviṃśatiḥ |  
asaṃskṛtyopadeśaṃ tu yaḥ karoti vimūḍhadhīḥ ||  
  
vinaśyaṃti ca tanmaṃtrāḥ saikateśālivījavat |  
anarhamaṃtravijñānaṃ tiṣṭhati kadācana ||  
  
tasmāt parīkṣya vaktavya manyathā niḥphalaṃ bhavet |  
sacchiṣyāyāni bhaktāya tadjñānamupadiśyate ||  
  
tatprāpnoti vratī nityaṃ gokṣīrā tu yathā ghṛtaṃ |  
dhanecchā bhayalobhādyairayogyaṃ yadi dīkṣayet ||  
  
devatāśāpamāpnoti kṛtaṃ ca vikṛtaṃ bhavet |  
atha svapnalabdha maṃtropāsanama kramamāha ||  
  
svapnamaṃtrā mahādevi tridhā vai pariniṣṭitā |  
pātāle bhuvirāṭ cakraṃ svargatāṃḍava cakrakaṃ ||  
  
svarge cakradvayaṃ devī tripurākhyaṃ dvitīyakaṃ |  
ādau virāṭ tato devi śivatāṃḍavameva ca ||  
  
tṛtīyaṃ tripurākhyaṃ tu svapnamaṃtrāstridhā sthitā |  
tatraiva suhṛdaṃto ye te virāṭ cakragocarāḥ ||  
  
astrāṃtāstu maheśāni śivatāṃḍava gocarāḥ |  
tripurā cakramadhyasthāḥ vahnijāyāṃti kāmatāḥ ||  
  
ete maṃtrāstvautsukena bhuvi svapnena gocarāḥ |  
svapnamārgeṇa deveśi upadiṣṭāḥ śivena tu ||  
  
teṣāṃ tu lakṣaṇaṃ devi śṛṇu yatnena sāṃprataṃ |  
pātāla cakraṃ maṃtrāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ śṛṇu sāṃprataṃ ||  
  
aṃjanaṃ guṭikāguptiścājñā siddhistathaiva ca |  
śivatāṃḍava cakrasya lakṣaṇaṃ śṛṇu pārvatī ||  
  
khaḍgavetāla siddhiśca parakāya pradeśanaṃ |  
carācara gatitvaṃ vahyaṇimādyaṣṭakaṃ tathā ||  
  
p. 48b)  
  
tripurā cakra maṃtrāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ śṛṇu pārvatī |  
manorathasya cākleśa tripurācakramaṃḍale ||  
  
ṣaṣṭhisiddhīśvaro bhūtvā bhuvisvarge ca bhūtale |  
tatra kiṃ vā prakartavyaṃ kiṃ tatra maṇḍalaṃ bhavet ||  
  
ṛṣiśchaṃdādikaṃ dhyānaṃ pīṭhaṃ nyāsādikaṃ śiva |  
yatra noktaṃ mahādeva tatra tat tatkathaṃ bhavet ||  
  
svapnalabdhasya maṃtrasya ṛṣiḥ śiva itīritaḥ |  
gāyatrī chaṃdaścidrūpā devatā parikīrtitā ||  
  
kādibījaṃ svarāḥ śaktiravyaktaṃ kīlakaṃ mataṃ |  
pīṭhaṃ tu mātṛkāpīṭhaṃ dhyānādi mātṛkoktavat ||  
  
mūlamaṃtrā ṣaḍāvṛttyā ṣaḍaṃganyā samācaret |  
svapnalabdhe mahādevī dakṣamūrtiḥ paraṃparā ||  
  
pūjayed dakṣiṇāmūrtiṃ gurutvena maheśvarī |  
tadguruśca bhavedviṣṇustadguruścaturānanaḥ ||  
  
tadguruḥ śaṃkaraḥ prokta evaṃ gurukramomataḥ |  
jātasūtaka doṣasya vāraṇaṃkenavāṃ bhavet ||  
  
tanmevada mahādeva likhedaṣṭadalaṃ śubhaṃ |  
tanmadhye kalaśaṃ sthāpyaṃ tatra vai vaiparītyakaṃ ||  
  
vaṭapatre kuṃkumena likhitvā maṃtrameva tu |  
kalaśaṃ purataḥ sthāpya guroḥ prāṇānniveśayet ||  
  
guroḥ sakāśād grahaṇājjāta sūtakavāraṇaṃ |  
vinā puraskriyāṃ devi maṃtromṛta itīritaḥ ||  
  
tasmāt kuryāt puraścaryāṃ mṛtasūtakaśāṃtaye |  
yo maṃtraścetanāyuktaḥ sumaṃtraḥ siddhidāyakaḥ ||  
  
caitanyaṃ tu puraścaryā caitanyaṃ gurumeva ca |  
yaṃtracaitanyakaṃ devi maṃtracaitanyakaṃ tathā ||  
  
gurucaitanyakaṃ caiva caitanyaṃ tṛtaye namaḥ |  
caitanyatrayahīnoyaḥ samaṃtraḥ siddhido na hi ||  
  
puraścaryādyanukte tu diksahasraṃ japaṃ caret |  
dvāviṃśākṣaraparyaṃtaṃ diksahasraṃ prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
taduttaraṃ mahādevī gajāṃtaka sahasrakaṃ |  
svapnalabdhe maheśāni tryaṃgātpuratkriyāmatā ||  
  
japahomau brāhmaṇānāṃ bhojanaṃ tritayaṃ mataṃ |  
atha svapnādilabdha ripumaṃtrasyā vivekyādi guroraniṣṭaphaladudevatāyāśca   
krameṇa parityāgarucyate ||  
  
śrīdevyuvāca |  
  
bhagavandeva deveśa guruṇā jñāninā yadā |  
lobhena maṃtrā dattaścettena duḥkhamavāpyate ||  
  
tadā kiṃ devakartavyaṃ saukhyaṃ yenopajāyate |  
ihaloke paritrāpi yena saṃlabhyate sukhaṃ ||  
  
p. 49a)  
  
īśvara uvāca ||  
  
prāyaḥ kaliyuge devi guravo lobha saṃyutāḥ |  
śiṣyā sukhepsavastena na tayorlabhyate kvacit ||  
  
prāyo maṃtragrahastena duḥkhāyaivopajāyate |  
tadarthaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi sarvataṃtreṣu gopitaṃ ||  
  
vikṣiptatā maṃtradoṣe gurudoṣakadarthatā |  
ādhirvyādhirdevadoṣe tasmāttaṃ parivarjayet ||  
  
maṃtratyāgavidhiṃ vakṣye yena saṃjāyate mukhaṃ |  
vidvānsaṃbrāhmaṇaṃ jñātvā taṃtreṣu pariniṣṭitaṃ ||  
  
prātastasya gṛhe gatvā svīyaṃ duḥkhaṃ nivedayet |  
tatastena prakartavyo maṃtratyāgavidhiḥ paraḥ ||  
  
śuciḥ samāhito bhūtvā prārabhet pravaredine |  
aśeṣaduḥkhanāśāyadeśikaḥ pravaraṃ vidhiṃ ||  
  
tatrādauramya bhavane kuṃbhaṃ dīkṣāvidhiḥ kramāt |  
maṇḍape sthāpayedvidvān pūrayettajjalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ||  
  
viloma maṃtrapāṭhena tatrāvāhyeṣṭha devatāṃ |  
sakalīkṛtya saṃpūjyā varaṇāni prapūjayet ||  
  
evaṃ sāvaraṇāmiṣṭvāmaṃtrī maṃtrasya devatāṃ |  
hunedvilomamaṃtreṇa goghṛtena sahasrakaṃ ||  
  
aṣṭānvitaṃ śataṃ cāpi tataḥ satarpayet prabhuṃ |  
brahmārpaṇena manunā devatābhyo valiṃ tataḥ ||  
  
yavānnaiścāpi dugdhānnairdigvidikṣvadha ūrddhvataḥ |  
āyāhīndrasurādhīśaḥ śatamanyo śacīpate ||  
  
namastubhyaṃ gṛhāṇe saṃpuṣpadhūpādikaṃ valiṃ |  
āyāhi tejasānātha havyavāhavalaprada ||  
  
gṛhāṇa puṣpadīpādi valimenaṃ prayojitaṃ |  
pretanāthatva māyāhi bhinnāṃ janasamadyute ||  
  
valiṃ dalaṃ gṛhītvemaṃ suprīto varatobhava |  
namaste rakṣasāṃ nātha nir-ṛte tvamihāgataḥ ||  
  
gṛhāṇa valipūjādi mayā bhaktyā niveditaṃ |  
paripaścima dikpāla jalanātha namostute ||  
  
bhaktyā niveditāṃ pūjāṃ gṛhītvā sukhamāpnuhi |  
prabhaṃjana prāṇapatetvamehi saparicchada ||  
  
mayā prayuktaṃ vidhivad gṛhāṇa valimādarāt |  
kuberatārakādhīśāvagacchaitāṃ surottamau ||  
  
puṣpadhūpādibhiḥ prītau ca bhavetāṃ varadau mama |  
īśatvameveṃ hi bhagavan sarvavidyāśrayaprabho ||  
  
pūjitaḥ puṣpadhūpādyaiḥ prīto bhavavibhūtaye |  
āyāhi sarvalokānāṃ nātha brahman samarccanaṃ ||  
  
p. 49b)  
  
gṛhāṇa sarvavighnānmenirvartaya namostute |  
āgaccha varadāvyakta viṣṇorviśvasyanāyaka ||  
  
pūjitaḥ paramābhaktyā bhavattvaṃ sukhado mama |  
tataḥ saparivārāṃśca pūjayen maṃtra devatāṃ ||  
  
maṃtreṇa viparītena puṣpadhūpopacārakaiḥ |  
tatastu prārthayed vidvān pūjitāṃ maṃtradevatāṃ ||  
  
ānukulyādyanālokhyamayātaralabuddhinā |  
upātto duḥkhado maṃtra taddoṣaṃ vinivartaya ||  
  
pāpaṃ pratihataṃmestubhūyācchreyaḥ sanātanaṃ |  
tanotu mamakalyāṇaṃ pāvanī bhaktireva ca ||  
  
iti saṃprārthya maṃtreṇa maṃtrayaṃtra vilomataḥ |  
likhitvāmala karpūraścaṃdanena samarcayet ||  
  
kalaśopari saṃsthāpya bhaktyā paramaṃyāṃ yutaḥ |  
tadyaṃtraṃ svasya śirasi vadhyāsmāyā ghaṭodakaiḥ ||  
  
maṃtrapūtaiḥ punaścātyaṃ kuṃbhatoyaiḥ prapūrayet |  
tanmadhye maṃtramaṃtraṃ ca niḥkṣipyātha prapūrayet ||  
  
taṃ kuṃbhaṃ nimnagānīre śuddhevānya jalāśaye |  
visṛjedatha vipraśca yathāśaktyā pratoṣayet ||   
  
itthaṃ kṛtavidhānasya durlabhasya manorujaḥ |  
vinaśyaṃti na saṃdehaḥ kramāccittaḥ prasannatā ||  
  
jāyatetī ca saṃpanno varddhate tat kulaṃ kramāt |  
evamuktā manutyāgo gurustyāgastathonyate ||  
  
maṃtroyaddevatāyāḥ syāttithau tasyā bhavedvratī |  
gurutyāgasya saṃkalpaṃ kuryātta doṣapūrvakaṃ ||  
  
gurvaṃtaraṃ ca saṃciṃtyanaraṃ vā devameva vā |  
rāśikūṭena saṃśuddhaṃ devatāṣṭaka madhyataḥ ||  
  
kuryādekaṃ guruṃ tatra pūrvā bhāve paraṃparaṃ |  
ādau tu dakṣiṇāmūrtiḥ sūryaścaṃdro hutāśanaḥ ||  
  
maṃtrāvaraṇadevatva jñātidevaḥ kuleśvaraḥ |  
deśadeva ime tvaṣṭyai naro vā lakṣaṇānvitaḥ ||  
  
guroryugmaṃ pūjayitvā nāsannata guruṃ dvayaṃ |  
devatāmnāya saṃproktaṃ dravyaṃ tannāmato yajet ||  
  
triparṇasya palāśasya prāgramuṣṭiṣu dakṣiṇe |  
prādeśa pramitānāṃ ca kuśānāmūrddhvavartmani ||  
  
toyaṃ pūrṇaṃ ghaṭaṃ prācyāṃ dugdhapūrṇāṃ ca paścime |  
uttare tu surāpūrṇamāprāyadravyamīritaṃ ||  
  
prāgguroścāpi caitanyaṃ praviṣṭaṃ nūtane gurau |  
iti saṃciṃtya maṃtrastu tasmāllabdho viciṃtayet ||  
  
p. 50a)  
  
aṣṭottara sahasraṃ ca manuṃ japtvā samāpayet |  
maṃtrasya varṇasaṃkhyākāndevatā prītikārakaiḥ ||  
  
dravyaistu bhojayedviprān devatārādhanakṣamān |  
tadabhāve vaidikāṃśca maṃtrā vedamayāyataḥ ||  
  
tadāmnāya pravṛttān vā tadabhāve tu bhojayet |  
evaṃtyāgoguroruktaḥ sarvataṃtreṣu gopitaḥ ||  
  
asiddhoyaḥ svayaṃ śiṣyaṃ kathaṃ saṃtārayiṣyati |  
devatyāgaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvataṃtreṣu gopitaṃ ||  
  
kṛta nityakriyaḥ pūjāṃ devatāyāṃ samācaret |  
saṃkalpaṃ ca tataḥ kuryāddhenu tyāgādi pūrvakaṃ ||  
  
parokṣaṃ vā samakṣaṃ vā guroḥ saṃprārthayetsuraṃ ||  
  
trailokyanāthajagadīśamaheśvarastvaṃ   
brahmāṇḍakoṭijaṭharādbhutaśāṃtyaciṃtya |  
yastvaṃ mayālpamatinādvibhujādidehī dhyāto parādhaṃ śatakaṃ   
mamatatkṣamasva ||  
  
tvaṃ sūryacaṃdradahaneśagaṇeśaviṣṇurbrahmeṃdraśaktinarayāganagasvarūpa |  
dhyāto sivālyaviṣayeparipūjitositanmeparādhaśatakaṃ bhagavan kṣamasva ||  
  
vedopi naiva munayo na ca bhāratītvāṃ jānāti maṃdamatinā svaguruktarītyā |  
dhyātastvamevamaparādhakṛtāmayedaṃ duḥkhaṃ   
pralabdhamadhunāśaraṇāgatoṣaṃ ||  
  
dhyānaṃ karomi manasā na ca tehyanaṃta maṃtrākṣarātmakamidaṃ   
paribhāvayāmi |  
rūpaṃ tvadīyamiti yatpravadaṃti vedāḥ siddhirjayānna ca vahiḥ kṛtapūjanādyaiḥ   
||   
  
evaṃ saṃprārthya deveśaṃ praṇameddaṇḍavat punaḥ |  
maṃtrapūtyādikaṃ sarvaṃ gurave tatsamarpayet ||  
  
tadabhāve pūjakāṃtadbhaktāya pradāpayet |  
kuryājjapaṃ dviguṇitaṃ sarvatrāpi ca taddhitān ||  
  
prāgvacca bhojayedviprān gurvādīṃścāpitoṣayet |  
evaṃ tu devatā tyāgo mayātubhyaṃ niveditaṃ ||  
  
dīkṣāṃtaraṃ maheśāni pratyahaṃ prajapanmanuṃ |  
prāṇāṃtepi na vaityājyastyāgācchāpamavāpnuyāt ||  
  
japaṃ pūjā tato jāpyaṃ kuryād yatnena nityaśaḥ |  
pūjāṃte prajapen maṃtraṃ na maṃtraṃ kevalaṃ japet ||  
  
pūrṇābhibhiṣekahīnasya pūjāpaṃcopacārikāḥ ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau dīkṣāvidhinirṇaye nāma daśamaḥ prakāśaḥ || 10 ||  
atha pūrṇābhiṣekadīkṣāmāha ||  
  
p. 50b)  
  
pūrṇābhiṣekadīkṣā tu caṃdrasūryagrahe bhavet |  
suṃdarī tāriṇī kālī kramāddīkṣā trigāminī ||  
  
kramāt pūrṇe maheśāni kramāchaṃbhurbhaviṣyati |  
caṃdrāgni pakṣa ṣoḍhākhya parānirvāṇa tatparā ||  
  
ṣaṭsāṃbhavaṃ tato devi cakrasaṃbhedanena ca |  
svacakradeha vijñānaṃ parakāya praveśanaṃ ||  
  
etadjñānādbhavenmedhā dīkṣā proktā mayā tava |  
hādrāviḍaṃ nigaditaṃ śṛṇukādau maheśvarī ||  
  
cakrāgni rasarājñī ca mahārājñī tataḥ śive |  
mahākāmakalākālī guhyakālī tataḥ śive ||  
  
guhyakālī dvidhā proktā sakalā niṣkalā kramāt |  
daśavaktrā tu sakalā proktā vā sṛṣṭikā kalā ||  
  
ugrāsaumyā mahākrūrā tridhā sāpi prakīrtitā |  
niḥkalāguhyaśaṃśaṃtā kālībhedena kīrtitā ||  
  
kevaleyaṃ bhavenmedhāhuyī sāmrājyarūpiṇī |  
caṃdrāgni vedapaṃcārṇā tathā nīlā krameṇa ca ||  
  
haṃsatārā mahānīlā tadaṃte cīna śāṃbhavī |  
kevalā tu bhavenmedhā siddhiṛddhi kriyādvidhā ||  
  
tritayā divyasāmrājyamedhā dīkṣā prakīrtitā |  
devarūpā divyarūpā maṃtrarūpā mahābalā ||  
  
sarvarūpā sarvapūrvā mahat sāmrājyamedhayā |  
siddhiṛddhikrameṇaiva bhedavāhulyamīritaṃ ||  
  
vidyārājyābhidhādīkṣā chinnamastāvidhau smṛtā |  
caṃdravahni rasoraktaśyāmā ca ṣoḍaśī tathā ||  
  
paraṣoḍhā saptadaśī tadajātā parā bhavet |  
dīpinīmālinī kullākramādvidyādirājyadā ||  
  
vagalāyā maheśāni sāmrājya parameṣṭhatā |  
caṃdraveda sūkṣmamerurmaṃtrahīnaṃ śivāṃtaraṃ ||  
  
hṛdayaṃ ca śatārṇāṃ ca paṃcārṇaṃ kullukā tathā |  
gāyatrī kramayogena sāmrājya parameṣṭhyaṃ dhṛk ||  
  
etatpaṃcaka saṃyuktaḥ sarvasāmrājya buddhi dhṛk |  
śrīdivya sarvasāmrājyadīkṣā sarvottarā bhavet ||  
  
tatopi dīkṣā deveśi nāsti brahmāṇḍa golake |  
daśavidyā prabhedāśca mahāvidyā prabhedajāḥ ||  
  
siddhividyā prabhedāśca mahāmaṃtrāstathaiva ca |  
tadaṃga maṃtrādeveśi śāvaraṃ deśaśāvaraṃ ||  
  
kālaśāvarakaṃ devi tathaiva siddhaśāvaraṃ |  
tridhādarśana maṃtrāśca tathāmnāya kramodbhavāḥ ||  
  
kādihādikahatvena ūrddhvāmnāyāt kalau śive |  
tathāyatanamaṃtrāśca yatkiṃcinmaṃtrajālakaṃ ||  
  
sarvādhikāro deveśi etaddīkṣāvidhau bhavet |  
etaddīkṣā samāyuktaḥ sākṣācchrī kālikāsvayaṃ ||  
  
p. 51a)  
  
praharākṣu krameṇaiva daśavidyā svarūpadhṛk |  
kāmakalābhidhāvidyāḥ sa bhedā vṛttidevatāḥ ||  
  
aṃgamaṃtrāstathānyepi tasyacāstragatāḥ sadā |  
kramadīkṣā maheśāni paṃcavidyāḥ subhedataḥ ||  
  
tadaṃgamaṃtrā gāyatrī kullukā paṃcakaṃ śive |  
anyavidyāvidhau proktaṃ rahasyāti rahasyakaṃ ||  
  
kramadīkṣāṃ vinā devi yojayet sādhakodhamaḥ |  
sadaridro mahāpāpī sutahārī prajāyate ||  
  
śrīvidyāyāṃ kālikāyāṃ tārāyāṃ parameśvarī |  
kramadīkṣāṃ vinā devi yojayet sādhakodhamaḥ ||  
  
sa daridrī mahāghorī lakṣmī hīnastu niṃditaḥ |  
aṃdhaḥ kāṇakubjapaṃguḥṣaṇḍhastu kuṣṭayuk * * (?) ||  
  
sarvarogayuto bhūyādādhi ciṃtā samākulaḥ |  
sutahārī ca strīhārī kanyā rājyavināśakaḥ ||  
  
athavā vātulo bhūyonmaṃtraḥ kṣobhamavāpnuyāt |  
devatāśāpamāpnoti dāridryaṃ tadgṛhe sadā ||  
  
viśeṣāddevadeveśi strīhārī vikalaḥ sadā |  
kramadīkṣā samāyukto rājā bhavati niścitaṃ ||  
  
mahāvibhava saṃyuktaḥ sarvasiddhiḥ samanvitaḥ |  
vijayo vinayaḥ sādhuḥ siddhaśca siddhidaḥ śubhaḥ ||  
  
prahṛṣṭātmā sarvavettāḥ trikālajñaḥ kaviḥ mukhīṃ |  
koṭi siddhīśvaraḥ śūraḥ suṃdaraḥ kāmamohanaḥ ||  
  
ānaṃdātmā parātmā ca parājita guṇottaraḥ |  
rājarājeśvaraḥ sākṣāt mahākālasamaḥ kalau ||  
  
etadvidyopāsakasya dāridryaṃ dīnatā kvacit |  
guruhīnā kramātyāgāt saṃpradāya viyogataḥ ||  
  
dāridryaṃ prathamaṃ bhūyānnātrakāryāvicāraṇā |  
ciṃtāmaṇi gṛhaṃ yatra yatra ratnasya maṃditaṃ ||  
  
navaratnātmasopānaḥ sarvaiśvaryopasaṃgṛhaṃ |  
kalpavṛkṣavanaṃ yatra pārijātavanaṃ tathā ||  
  
sparśamāṇastu prākāro dāridryaṃ tatra kutra vai |  
tasmāt kamavihīnasya dāridryaṃ tu pade pade ||  
  
kramayuktaṃ guruṃ prāpya kramaṃ saṃprārthayetsudhīḥ |  
anyathā gurumauḍhyena dāridratvamavāpnuyāt ||  
  
alpāyurvābhaveddevinātrakāryā vicāraṇā |  
vidherlipiṃ tu saṃmārjya tasyāḥ prakṣīṇato vrajet ||  
  
evaṃ gurūrdīkṣāṃ kuryāt pūrṇābhiṣecanaṃ |  
vinā yenābhiṣekeṇasādhakaḥ pūrṇavodhatāṃ ||  
  
ācāryatvaṃ navāpnoti sadgatiṃ ca samīhitāṃ |  
tasmādguruḥ priyaṃ śiṣyaṃ vodhayitvābhiṣecayet ||  
  
p. 51b)  
  
vināpūrṇābhiṣekeṇa paśurūpaḥ śivopi ca |  
vināpūrṇābhiṣekeṇa kālīṃ tārāṃ ca yojayet ||  
  
tasya kriyāṃ hariṣyāmi vātulo jāyate naraḥ |  
vināpūrṇābhiṣekeṇa gurudharmeṇa pārvatī ||  
  
na japo na tathā homo na pūjā pūrṇa kvacit |  
pūrṇābhiṣekahīnastu kauliko mriyaṃte yadi ||  
  
piśācatvamavāpnoti yāvadāhūta saṃplavaṃ |  
pūrṇābhiṣeko deveśi daśavidyāvidhau smṛtaḥ ||  
  
pūrvoktamaṇḍape sthitvā gurudhyāna parāyaṇaḥ |  
aṃkurāropaṇaṃ vāstuyāgaṃ kuryātyarehani ||  
  
kuṇḍaṃ nirmāya yatnena yathā vihitamādarāt |  
homaṃ kṛtvā guru kulaṃ mānyaṃ pūjya yathādarāt ||  
  
vedikāyāmiṣṭadevaṃ gurustṛtayamādarāt |  
vastrālaṃkaraṇaiḥ pūjyā guruśaktaya eva ca ||  
  
yathā divyaugha caraṇaṃ siddhaugha caraṇaṃ śive |  
mānavaughaṃ maheśāni svagurūṇāṃ catuṣkakaṃ ||  
  
abhiṣeka kriyābhijñastadvartanapuraḥ saraṃ |  
snānadvayaṃ yathoktena kṛtvā yatnena pārvatī ||  
  
paṃcapallavayogena durvā vilvaphalaistathā |  
vaidikaistāṃtrikairmaṃtraiḥ ṣecayecchiṣyamādarāt ||  
  
ayameva maheśāni pūrṇadīkṣākramaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
anyatsarvaṃ maheśāni dīkṣāpaṭalagocaraṃ ||  
  
viracya vipulaṃ cakraṃ maṇḍapeti manoharaṃ |  
khārītoyabhṛtaṃ kuṃbhaṃ sthāpayeccakra madhyataḥ ||  
  
anyeṣu kalaśān ratnavastra hemasamanvita |  
daleṣu vidhivat sthāpya tatrāvāhyaṣṭadevatāṃ ||  
  
abhyarcya madhyacāṃteṣu sāṃgāvaraṇadevatā |  
spṛśaṃ ca madhyakalaśamācāryaḥ prapaṭhediti ||  
  
sāṃgāṃśca caturo vedāntatastena jalena tu |  
abhyasiṃcedguruḥ śiṣyamiti pūrṇābhiṣecanaṃ ||  
  
vedebhyaḥ sarvataṃtrāṃśca taṃtrebhyo manavastathā |  
yatojātāstataḥ śiṣyaḥ sarvamaṃtraikabhājanaṃ ||  
  
bhavedācāryanāmā ca kuryānnāmāṃtaraṃ guruḥ |  
etādṛśasyayo dīkṣā gṛhnīyāt sa tu siddhibhāk ||  
  
sarvamaṃtrapradāneṣu samarthaḥ sa tu jāyate |  
sarvedevāvaśāstasya vedapaṃthā tu sātvikaḥ ||  
  
eṣa eva vidhistaṃtramārgesyāddakṣiṇābhidhe |  
viśeṣastatratoyānitīrthānāmāharetsudhī ||  
  
p. 52a)  
  
gaṃgāyā yamunāyāśca sarasvatyā mahodadheḥ |  
siṃdhugodāvarīrevākāverībhyaḥ pṛthūdakāt ||  
  
mahendrajāyāḥ sarayūcarmaṇvatyāśca puṣkarāt |  
mahānadyā vedikāyā kṣiprāvetravatījalaṃ ||  
  
kurukṣetrasya gaṃḍakyāḥ pūrṇāyāmānasasya ca |  
ghaṭedatvā japenmaṃtrānnānātaṃtra gatānapi ||  
  
abhiṣekastu taistoyai siddhāste manavosya tu |  
prayogārthaṃ tathānyasya dānārthamathavāmake ||  
  
madhye tīrthaghaṭaṃ sthāpyaśeṣāstoya ghaṭāmatāḥ |  
ye ye āvāhitā devā guruṇā tu surāghaṭe ||  
  
te te kurvaṃti sānnidhyaṃ maṃtrarūpāścatanmukhe |  
svayaṃ siddhyati vāgasya mūrddhānaṃ naiva nāmayet ||  
  
yadarthaṃ nāmito mūrdhā tasya mṛtyurnasaṃśayaḥ |  
vāmamārge gururyasya īdṛksiddho yadā bhavet ||  
  
śiṣyaśca nirahaṃkāraḥ sadā daivata tatparaḥ |  
devatārthaṃ yasyanāditrayaṃ bhoge mano na ca ||  
  
sa eva siddho vāmesyādanyonirayabhājanaṃ |  
daridro duḥkhito mūrkha ihaloke paratra ca ||  
  
kriyā dīkṣāvidhiṃ kuryādyathā śaktyā gurūktitaḥ |  
sajīvamīnayuktena surayā pūritena ca ||  
  
paṃcāmṛtaiḥ susaṃpūrṇaṃ śaṃkhena kalaśena vā |  
abhiṣekaṃ tataḥ kuryāt kulavṛkṣottha pallavaiḥ ||  
  
ayaṃ pūrṇābhiṣekotra kulamārge prakīrtitāḥ |  
abhiṣiṃcedguruḥ śiṣyaṃ nāmāsmai pradiśetsvayaṃ ||  
  
ānaṃdanātha śabdādaudvyakṣaraṃ caturakṣaraṃ |  
niyojyaivāmukosīti gururādautamādvayet ||  
  
yathā nārīpiturgotrāt paturgotraṃ samāśrayet |  
tathāśaktyupadeśena kaulogotrāṃtare vrajet ||  
  
athocyate maheśāni kaulānāṃ gotramuttamaṃ |  
durlabhaṃ sarvataṃtreṣu śāṃbhavaṃ tatprakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
upapātakalakṣāṇi mahāpātaka koṭayaḥ |  
kṣaṇāddahaṃtidīkṣeyaṃ vidhinā guruṇā kṛtā ||  
  
raseṃdreṇa yathāviddhamayaḥ sauvarṇatāṃ vrajet |  
dīkṣāviddhastathāhyātmā śivatvaṃ labhate dhruvaṃ ||  
  
gataṃ śūdrasya śudratvaṃ gatā viprasya vipratā |  
dīkṣā saṃskāra saṃpanne jātibhedo na vidyate ||  
  
dārvaśmalohamṛdulajātiliṃgaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ |  
yathocyate mahādevastathā varṇāstu dīkṣitāḥ ||  
  
p. 52b)  
  
pūrṇābhiṣekaṃ kṛtvā tu yatra kutra mṛtopi cet |  
sa eva devīrūpaḥ syāt sa devodhanyatāmiyāt ||  
  
pūrṇābhiṣekayuktasya yatkiṃcidamṛtaṃ bhavet |  
tasya kriyā ca saphalā devatā suprasīdati ||  
  
pūrṇābhiṣekayukto hi maṃtrāndṛṣṭvā japecchive |  
tatkṣaṇāt siddhimāpnotinā ca kāryā vicāraṇā ||  
  
guruṃ vināpi deveśitvabhiṣekītvayaṃ japet |  
taṃ sabhedaṃ sādhayitvā siddhiṃdātu mathārhati ||  
  
kaulāvadhutamārgeṣu tīrthayātrāṃ na ca vrajet |  
tīrthāsanaṃ ca saṃnyāsaṃ vratadhāraṇameva ca ||  
  
upavāsaṃ muṇḍanaṃ ca sarvathā parivarjayet |  
pūrṇābhiṣeka śirasaṃ tena tatra na muṃḍanaṃ ||  
  
pūrṇābhiṣeka saṃyuktaścāṇḍālopi bhavedyadi |  
sa brahmarṣirmaheśāni nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ||  
  
pūrṇābhiṣeka hīnoya ṛṣivarjyopi pārvatī |  
sa brāhmaṇādhamaḥ proktastvabhiṣekī dvijottamaḥ ||  
  
pūrṇābhiṣekī deveśi yasmindeśe virājite |  
saṃdeśo dhanyatāṃyāti samaṃtāt koṭiyojanaṃ ||  
  
navyādhirna ca vai mṛtyurna śatrūṇāṃ bhayaṃ kvacit |  
pūrṇarūpaḥ śivaḥ proktaḥ śiva eva na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
kovādehīkasya dehaḥ sukhaṃduḥkhaṃ ca kasya ca |  
kojātaḥ komṛto devi sarvaṃ brahmasvarūpakaṃ ||  
  
yasminkāle bhaveddevi maṃtradevasya vismṛtaḥ |  
tadevamaraṇaṃ proktaṃ maraṇaṃ maraṇaṃ na hi ||  
  
pūrṇābhiṣeka yuktānāmadhikāro hi sarvataḥ |  
pūrṇābhiṣekaḥ saṃyuktastyajedetadvayaṃ śive ||  
  
ahaṃtā mamatā tyāgaḥ prathamaṃ buddhilakṣaṇaṃ |  
ahamiti maheśāni prathamodhyā sa īritaḥ ||  
  
mameti ca maheśāni dvitīyodhyā sa īritaḥ |  
ahaṃtā mamatā hīnaḥ pūrṇadīkṣāyuto bhavet ||  
  
kullukāyā japenāpi pūrṇadīkṣāphalaṃ labhet |  
vidyānāṃ kulapūjyatvāt kullukā tena kīrtitāḥ ||  
  
vidyāsaṃbaṃdhi doṣāṇāṃ bhakṣayitrīyataḥ śive |  
vikhyātā kullukā tena sarvadoṣa harā parā ||  
  
kullukājaya yuktānāṃ vidyāsiddhirbhaveddhruvaṃ |  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau pūrṇābhiṣekanirṇayo nāmaikādaśamaḥ prakāśaḥ || 11   
||  
p. 53a)  
  
atha gurubhaktiḥ ||  
  
kulāgamastvayaṃ mārgo guruṇā saṃpradarśitaḥ |  
samyagācaritaścetsyābhuktimuktyoṣprasādhanaṃ ||  
  
vipropiguṇayuktopi na bhaktaścennaśasyate |  
mlecchāpi guṇahīnopi bhaktimān śiṣya ucyate ||  
  
gurubhaktivihīnasya tayorvidyā vrataṃ kulaṃ |  
vyarthaṃ sarvaṃ śavasyeva nānālaṃkārabhūṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
nārāyaṇe mahādeve mātāpitrośca rājani |  
yathābhaktirbhaveddevi tathā kāryāṇije gurau ||  
  
ekagrāmasthitaḥ śiṣyastrisaṃdhyaṃ praṇamedguruṃ |  
ekaḥ krośasthitaścāpi guruṃ pratidinaṃ namet ||  
  
arddhayojanagaḥ śiṣyaḥ praṇamet paṃcaparvasu |  
ekayojanamārabhyayojana dvādaśāvadhi ||  
  
tat tadyojana saṃkhyātairmārgegatvā namedguruṃ |  
dūradeśaḥ sthitaḥ śiṣyo bhaktyā tat sannidhiṃ gataḥ ||  
  
tat tadyojana saṃkhyātaṃ māseṣu praṇamedguruṃ |  
atidūrasthitaḥ śiṣyo yadecchāsyāt tadā vrajet ||  
  
riktahastastunopeyādrājānaṃ devatāṃ guruṃ |  
phalapuṣpāṃvarādīni yathā śaktyā samarcayet ||  
  
gurvagreṇa tapaḥ kuryānna snāyādātma śuddhaye |  
na laṃghayed gurorājñāmuttaraṃ na vadettathā ||  
  
apriyaṃ ca tathā kāle kāmakrodhau viśeṣataḥ |  
nāpracchannamukhodrūyāguroragre kadācana ||  
  
advaitaṃ devapūjāṃ ca guroragre parityajet |  
pādukāyogapaṭṭādi gurucihnāni sādaraṃ ||  
  
na laṃghayet spṛśennaiva tatsamakṣaṃ na dhārayet |  
paryyaṃkaśayanaṃ tadvattathāpāda prasarpaṇaṃ ||  
  
aṃgaṃ bhaṃgaṃ ca līlāṃ ca na kuryād gurusannidhau |  
chāyāṃ na laṃghayet tasya gacchenna purato guroḥ ||  
  
na kurvīta guroragre prabhāvaṃ śiṣyasaṃgrahaṃ |  
ahaṃkāraṃ na kūrvīta nollakṣaṇaṃ dhārayed vapuḥ ||  
  
jātāmāyā yadi braṃśe śapathaṃ gurusaṃjñitaṃ |  
na kuryācchivasaṃjñaṃ vā pramādena kriyeta cet ||  
  
tadarthaṃ nirvahedyatnādaṃte pūjājapājapāhutī |  
anirvāhetu kāryasya yadarthaṃ śapathaḥ kṛtaḥ ||  
  
prāyaścittaṃ manoḥ kuryānmūlākhyasya sahasrakaṃ |  
na niyogaṃ gurordadyādyuṣmadānābhibhāṣayet ||  
  
śrīnāthadevasvāmīti vodhane bhāṣaṇe vadet |  
ṛṇadānaṃ tathā dānaṃ vastūnāṃ krayavikrayaṃ ||  
  
na kuryādgurubhissārddhaṃ śiṣyobhūṣṇuḥ kadācana |  
guroḥ saṃnihitedyastu pūjayedanyamamvike ||  
  
p. 53b)  
  
sayāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ pūjā sā viphalā bhavet |  
yasmin dravye gurorasti spṛhānānu bhavecca tat ||  
  
avaśyaṃ yadi vāṃchāsyādanu bhūyāt tadājñayā |  
atyalpaṃ hi gurordravyemaddattaṃ svīkarotiyaḥ ||  
  
tiraścāṃ yonimāpannaḥ kravyādairbhakṣyatetriye |  
gurudravyālāṣī ca gurustrīgamanotsukaḥ ||  
  
patitaḥ syānna saṃdehaḥ prāyaścittannavidyate |  
guruḥsthānaṃ saṃpradāyaṃ taddharmaṃ yonicārayet ||  
  
gurubhiḥ sa vahiḥ kāryodaṃḍyovadhyaśca pātakī |  
pādukāmāsanaṃ vastraṃ vāhanaṃ chatracāmaraiḥ ||  
  
dṛṣṭvā gurornamaskuryānnatadbhogāya kalpayet |  
uktānukteṣu kāryeṣu nopekṣāṃ kārayet priye ||  
  
sadasadya gururvrūyāttat kāryamaviśaṃkayā |  
brahmahatyāśataṃ kṛtvā gurvājñāṃ paripālayet ||  
  
nigrahenugrahe vāpi guruḥ sarvasyakāraṇaṃ |  
nirgataṃ yadgurorvakrāt tatsarvaṃ śāstramucyate ||  
  
ājñābhaṃgorthaharaṇaṃ gurora priyavartanaṃ |  
gurudrohamidaṃ prodgaryaḥ kuryāt sa tu pātakī ||  
  
na viśedāsanedevi devatā gurusannidhau |  
jātividyādhanāḍhyo vā dūradṛṣṭvā guruṃ mudā ||  
  
abhimāno na kartavyo jāti * ? vidhanādibhiḥ |  
tatpāpaṃ samavāpnoti gurvagre nṛtabhāṣaṇāt ||  
  
gobrāhmaṇavadhaṃ kṛtvā na tatpāpamavāpnuyāt |  
daṇḍapraṇāṃaṃ kṛtvaikaṃ triḥpradakṣiṇamācaret ||  
  
gurustadguruyoge tu vaṃdeta praguruṃ priye |  
tato namedguruṃ sopi gurvagre tannivārayet ||  
  
praguroḥ sannidhau śiṣyaḥ svaguruṃ manamānayet |  
guruktaṃ paruṣaṃ vākye māśiṣaṃ cintayeddhṛdi ||  
  
tena saṃtāḍito vāpi prasādamiti saṃsmaret |  
bhogyayogyāni vastuni gurave sarvamarpayet ||  
  
taccheṣamiti saṃciṃtya grāhyaṃ tasyājñayāmudā |  
ekākṣarapradātāraṃ yo guruṃtvavamanyate ||  
  
saśca yoniṃ śataṃ gatvā cāṇḍālatvamavāpnuyāt |  
guraumanuṣyabuddhiṃ ca maṃtrevākṣarasemuniṃ ||  
  
pratimāyāṃ śilāṃ buddhiṃ kurvāṇo narake vrajet |  
guruśaktiśca tatputro tajyeṣṭhaśca guruḥ samaḥ ||  
  
ātmavaccakanīyāṃ saḥ putravat paripālakāḥ ||  
  
atha dakṣiṇācāramāha |  
  
śrīdevyuvāca |  
  
asmin ghore kaliyuge svalpa siddhyatidarpitāḥ |  
bhaviṣyaṃjanāsteṣāṃ sthirasiddhiḥ kathaṃ bhavet ||  
  
agrevaṃśādivṛddhiśca vaṃśedevakṛpā tathā |  
mokṣaḥ kathaṃ sādhakasya tathāvada kṛpānidhe ||  
  
p. 54a)  
  
īśvara uvāca |  
  
ahaṃkāra parityāgāt kāmyakarmavivarjatān |  
svadharmāccaraṇāt sarvaṃ manāyāsena jāyate ||  
  
etat kartumaśaktaścenniṣiddhaṃ tu parityajet |  
vihitaṃ karmakurvīta siddhiḥ syāt putrapautrikī ||  
  
tatrādau kathayiṣyāmi niṣiddhaṃ viddhinā saha |  
devasthāne gurusthāne śmaśāne ca catuṣpathe ||   
  
pādukāsanaviṇmūtramaithunāni vivarjayet |  
dhanyago gurudevāgni kośapustaka saṃmukhaṃ ||  
  
naiva prasātayelpādau na caitāni vilaṃghayet |  
ālasya madanaṃ mohaśāpapaiśūnya vigrahān ||  
  
asūyāmātsasaṃmānaṃ paraniṃdāṃ ca varjayet |  
liṃginaṃ vratinaṃ vipraṃ vedavedāṃga saṃhitāḥ ||  
  
purāṇāgaśāstrāṇi kalpāṃścāpi na dūṣayet |  
yugaṃ kuśalamaśmānaṃdāmabuhrīmulūkhalaṃ ||  
  
sūryaṃ saṃmārjanaṃ daṇḍaṃ dhvajaṃ vai tūryamāyudhaṃ |  
kalaśaṃ cāmaraṃ chatraṃ darpaṇaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ tathā ||  
  
bhogabhogyāni cānyāniyāgra dravyāṇi yāni ca |  
mahāsthāneṣu vastūniyāni vā devatālaye ||  
  
divyoktāni padārthāni bhūtā viṣṭāniyāni vai |  
laṃghayejjānu naitāni na caitāni yadā spṛśet ||  
  
yā goṣṭīlokavidviṣṭāyā vatsvairavisarpiṇī |  
parahiṃsātmikāyā ca na tāmavataret kvacit ||  
  
pratigrahaṃ na gṛhnīyādātma bhogavidhitsayā |  
devatātithi pūjārthaṃ yatnatoppūrjayeddhanaṃ ||  
  
vibhītakakaraṃjārkāsnuhīcchāyāṃ na laṃghayet |  
staṃbhadīpamanuṣyāṇāmanyeṣāṃ prāṇināṃ tathā ||  
  
nakhāgrakeśanirddhūtasnānavastra paṭhodakaṃ |  
etat sparśaṃ tyajeddūraṃ kharaśvājalajastathā ||  
  
liṃgasthānaṃ ca nirmālyaṃ nādhyānnaiva ca laṃghayet |  
nadyāṃ pravāhayet sarvaṃ dadyādvā śivadīkṣite ||  
  
lokodvegakarīyā ca yā ca marma nikṛṃtinī |  
sthityudvegakarīyā ca tāṃgiraṃ naiva bhāṣayet ||  
  
ramyamapyujjvalamapi manasopi samīpsitaṃ |  
lokavidveṣaṇaṃ veṣaṃ na gṛhnīyāt kadācana ||  
  
taṃtroktān samayācārānaihi kāmuṣṃikocitān |  
ācarannādaracchiddhiṃ dīkṣitaḥ sodhigacchati ||  
  
sāmānyasiddhaurakṣārthaṃ pareṣāṃ na kadācana |  
prayoktavyaḥ svasya maṃtro mahāpadyapi sādhakaiḥ ||  
  
p. 54b)  
  
yatra yatra parīvādo mātsaryācchrūyate guroḥ |  
tatra tatra na vastravyaṃ pramādāt saṃsmareddhariṃ ||  
  
viṣṇoḥ śivasya śāstrasya vedasyārka gaṇeśayoḥ |  
bhavānyā vā yatra niṃdā tasmiṃnsthāne vasetana ||  
  
karmaṇā manasā vācā na hiṃset paradārakān |  
sa dīkṣite namokāryaḥ śāpānugrahakarmaṇi ||  
  
na tena maṃtro vaktavyo mudrā vā samayā api |  
siddhamaṃtrasya kartavyaṃ trividhaṃ parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ tatrādau nitya mucyate |  
devaguruṃ gurusthānaṃ kṣetraṃ kṣetrādhi devatāḥ ||  
  
siddhān siddhādhivāsāṃśca śrīpūrvaṃ samudīrayet |  
dhārayedārjavaṃ satyaṃ sauśīlyaṃ samatāṃ ghṛtiḥ ||  
  
śāṃtirdayāmavasthāṃ ca divyāṃ śaktiṃ ca sarvadā |  
gamanāgamanaṃ kuryāt praṇamya gurupāduke ||  
  
paścāt pādena nirgaccht praṇamya ca gurorgṛhāt |  
malamūkādirahitaḥ keśaśmaśruviluṃvanāt ||  
  
somasūryāṃtarasthaṃ ca gavāśvatthādi madhyagāṃ |  
bhāvayeddevatāṃ viṣṇuṃ guruvipra śarīriṇāṃ ||  
  
maṃtraguptiśca kartavyā satataṃ maṃtrasiddhaye |  
gurornāma na gṛhnīyādvadeśavaśyaketviti ||  
  
oṃ śrīpūrvaṃ gurornāmadevanāma taduttaraṃ |  
pādaśabda sametoyaṃ na ta mūrddhvāṃjalīyutaḥ ||  
  
jasaṃtaṃ ca dadennāmatithyarṇaṃ ca hareryama |  
ayaṃ ca dakṣiṇācāraḥ kathitaḥ parameśvarī ||  
  
atha kulācāramāha |  
  
atha vakṣye kulācāramārge śāstrārthanirṇayaṃ |  
kaulikānāṃ kule jāto jyeṣṭho yadi na dīkṣitaḥ ||  
  
kaniṣṭho dīkṣitaścet syāt sakuryāt kulapūjanaṃ |  
pūjāṃte śeṣamādāya jyeṣṭhaṃ natvā nivedayet ||  
  
tasyocchiṣṭaṃ tu gṛhnīyāt kaniṣṭa iti nirṇayaḥ |  
pūjā madhye guraujyeṣṭhe pūjye vāpi samāgate ||  
  
na svāvrūyāt sthitiṃ śeṣaṃ mācaret tadanujñayā |  
nityārcanaṃ divākuryādrātrau naimittikārcanaṃ ||  
  
kāmyārcanaṃ proktakāle vahavo yatrasaṃgatāḥ |  
natvā svasvaguruṃ tatra svasvamārgeṇa tarpayet ||  
  
vināśanaṃ vinā snāna gaṃdhapuṣpākṣatānvinā |  
vinā madyaṃ vinā māṃsaṃ kulapūjāṃ na kārayet ||  
  
na kuryāt pralayaṃ bhuktvā vinā maṃtre pūjanaṃ |  
śaktyā vinā tathā pānamekahastena nārcayet ||  
  
śrīcakramekonokuryādekapātre ca nārcayet |  
napi vedekahastena cakreniṣṭīvanaṃ na ca ||  
  
p. 55a)   
  
praṇamya praviśeccakraṃ vinirgacchet praṇamya ca |  
śrīcakraṃ nāsane tiṣṭennā ca vīrāsane kvacit ||  
  
śrīcakradarśanaṃ nṝṇāṃ netrayoḥ pāpanāśanaṃ |  
tannāsti cedvraṇī dvaṃdvaṃ kaulikasyākṣi yugmakaṃ ||  
  
anācārāt sadācārāṃścakrasthān śaktitaulikān |  
śivagaurīdhiyāsarvān bhāvayennāvamānayet ||  
  
kulācāryagṛhaṃ gatvā bhaktyā pāpaviśuddhaye |  
yācayedamṛtaṃ vānnaṃ tadabhāve jalaṃ pibet ||  
  
kulācāryeṇa vecchaktyādattaṃ pātraṃ tu bhaktitaḥ |  
namaskṛtya pragṛhnīyādanyathā narakaṃ vrajet ||  
  
uṣṇīṣī kaṃcukī nagno muktakeśaśca uktavān |  
asnātonāti bhaktaśca vivādī ca parāṅmukhaḥ ||  
  
nedaṃ yasya kule jātaṃ yaśca saṃskāramādvijaḥ |  
vedādhyāyī kuladravyasevanānnirddhano bhavet ||  
  
yogāmṛtasya niṣṭīvānmadyabhāṇḍa paribhramāt |  
ūrddhvanālenapānācca devatāśāpa māpnuyāt ||  
  
ekāsane niviṣṭāye bhuṃjānāścaikabhājane |  
ekapātre pivaṃto yetaṃ yāṃti narakaṃ sadā ||  
  
ye sevaṃte kuladravye mekagrāmasthite gurau |  
tat kulejñe ca tatputre svahyeṣṭha kuladeśike ||  
  
vinānujñāṃ sa pāpātmā rauravaṃ nirayaṃ vrajet |  
paṭhanaṃ dharmaśāstrasyahya kulastrī niṣevanaṃ ||  
  
śrautakarmasyācaraṇaṃ śrotriyāṇāṃ ca saṃgatiḥ |  
kāmārthāyuryaśolobhojñānasaukhyādināśakaṃ ||  
  
ripuṇāpi na kartavyo vāgvādaścakra madhyataḥ |  
pitṛmātṛsamaṃ paśyettenoktaṃ puruṣaṃ mahet ||  
  
śrīguruṃ kulaśāstrāṇi pūjyasthānāni yāni ca |  
bhaktyā śrīpūrvakaṃ vidvān praṇamya parikīrtayet ||  
  
pāraṃparyāgamāmnāya maṃtra cārādikaṃ tathā |  
sarvaṃ guru kulālladhvaṃ saphalaṃ syānnavānyathā ||  
  
śrīśāstraṃ pūjayennityaṃ paśugehena niḥkṣipet ||  
  
svadāravanniṣeveta kulaśāstrāṇi sarvaṇi varjayet paradāravat ||  
  
saṃskārārthaṃ chinnabhinnā vyastavarṇāṃśca vaidikāṃn |  
maṃtrān paṭhen saṃpradāyāttaiḥ syādatravyavasthitiḥ ||  
  
dharmaśāstraviruddhoya ācāraḥ sa tu kaulikaḥ |  
cakreṇākārayedetā daivāt prāptāḥ prapūjayet ||  
  
gamanaṃ naiva kurvīta kṛtvā nirayamāpnuyāt |  
mātaraṃ gurupatnīṃ ca bhaginīṃ bhaginīsutāṃ ||  
  
bhrātṛjāyāṃ vīrabhāryāṃ kumārīṃ vratadhāriṇīṃ |  
vyaṃgāṃgīṃ vikṛtāṃgīṃ cakṣudhāṃ prītāṃ samāhṛtāṃ ||  
  
p. 55b)  
  
srūyāṃ sakṛtkāmagatāṃ vṛddhāṃ naivāmanoharāṃ |  
manoharāṃ yauvanasthāṃ suveṣāṃ cāruhāsinīṃ ||  
  
raktāṃta nayanāṃ śyāmāṃ pūjayet kaulikāṃgaṇāṃ |  
akasmācca na seveta balena kulayoginīṃ ||  
  
cakramadhye svyaṃ kṣudhāṃ vāstvataḥ prārthinīṃ bhavet |  
āmaṃ māṃsaṃ surākuṃbhaṃ mattebhaṃ siddhadarśanaṃ ||  
  
sahakāramaśokaṃ ca krīḍāṃ lubdhāṃ kumārikāṃ |  
ekavṛkṣaṃ śmaśānaṃ ca samūhaṃ yoṣitāmapi ||  
  
nārīṃ ca raktavasanāṃ dṛṣṭvā vaṃdeta bhaktitaḥ |  
guruśaktisuto jyeṣṭhaḥ kaniṣṭhaḥ kuladeśikān ||  
  
kuladarśana śāstrāṇi kuladravyāṇi kauikān |  
prerakāt sūcakāṃścāpi vācakān darśakāṃstathā ||   
  
śikṣakān vodhakān yogiyoginī siddhapūrūṣān |  
kanyāḥ kumārikānagnā unmattānapi yoṣitaḥ ||   
  
naniṃdenna jugupsetanahasennā ca mānayet |  
nāpriyaṃ nānṛtaṃ brūyāt kasyāpi * ? kuyoginaḥ ||  
  
kurūpe sati kṛṣṇeti na niṃde kulayoṣitaṃ |  
parikṣayennabhaktānāṃ vīrāṇāṃ ca kṛtā kṛte ||  
  
na paśyet patitāṃ nagnāmunmattā prakaṭastanīṃ |  
na divāsevayennārīṃ tadyoniṃ na nirīkṣayet ||  
  
striyaṃśatāparādhāṃ vā puṣpeṇāpi na tāḍayet |  
doṣāṃ na gaṇayet strīṇāṃ guṇāneva prakāśayet ||  
  
tiṣṭhaṃti kulayoginyaḥ kulavṛkṣeṣu sarvadā |  
tatpatreṣu na bhoktavyamarkapatre viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
na svayet kulavṛkṣādho na copadravamācaret |  
dṛṣṭvā bhaktyā namaskuryācchedayenna kadācana ||  
  
śleṣyāṃtakakaraṃjākṣaniṃvāśvattha kadaṃvakāḥ |  
vilvovaṭoḍuṃvarau ca viṃcāveti daśasmṛtāḥ ||  
  
prāyaścittaṃ bhṛgoḥ pātaḥ saṃnyāsaṃ vratadhāraṇaṃ |  
tīrthayātrādigamanaṃ kaule paṃcavivarjayet ||  
  
aṃhaḥ kaulaṃ vahiḥ śaivaṃ janamadhye tu vaiṣṇavaṃ |  
kaulaṃ tu gopayeddevi nārikela phalāṃvuvat ||  
  
guruṃ prakāśayeddhīmān maṃtraṃ yatnena gopayet |  
aprakāśaḥ prakāśābhyāṃ kṣīyate saṃpadāyuṣaṃ ||  
  
sarvācāra paribhraṣṭaḥ kulācāraṃ samāśrayet |  
kulācāra paribhraṣṭo rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet ||  
  
vāmācāraṃ tu kathayeda kulīnāma sadguruḥ |  
ācārāt patitaḥ śiṣye pātakī sagururbhavet ||  
  
p. 56a)  
  
sarvabhūtahiteraktaḥ samayācārapālakaḥ |  
anityakarma saṃtyāgī nityānuṣṭāna tatparaḥ ||  
  
parasyāṃ devatāyāṃ tu sarvakarmanivedakaḥ |  
anyamaṃtrārcanaḥ śraddhāmanyamaṃtrasyapūjanaṃ ||  
  
kulastrī vīraniṃdāṃ ca taddravyasyāpahāraṇaṃ |  
strīmayaṃ ca jagatsarvaṃ svayaṃtāvattathā bhavet ||  
  
peyaṃ carvaṃ tathā coṣyaṃ bhakṣyaṃ lehyaṃ gṛhaṃ sukhaṃ |  
sarvaṃ ca yuvatīrūpaṃ bhāvayedyatamānasaḥ ||  
  
striyodevāstriyaḥ prāṇāḥ striya eva hi bhūṣaṇaṃ |  
strīsaṃgiṇā sadābhāvyamanyathā svastriyāmapi ||  
  
taddhastāvucitaṃ puṣpaṃ taddhasta gṛhitaṃ jalaṃ |  
taddhastaracitaṃ bhojyaṃ devatābhyo nivedayet ||  
  
kulajāṃ yuvatīṃ vīkṣya namaskuryāt samāhitaḥ |  
yadi bhāgyavaśenaiva kuladṛṣṭistu jāyate ||  
  
tadaiva mānasīṃ pūjāṃ tadā tāsāṃ prakalpayet |  
vālāṃ vā yauvanonmattāṃ vṛddhāṃ vā suṃdarīṃ tathā ||  
  
kutsitvāṃ vā mahāduṣṭāṃ namaskṛtya vibhāvayet |  
tāsāṃ prahāraṃ niṃdāṃ ca kauṭilyamapriyaṃ tathā ||  
  
sarvathā na ca kartavyamanya siddhi * ? rodhakṛt |  
gocarmasthaṃ yathākṣīraṃ na peyaṃ syādvijottamaiḥ ||  
  
tathā paśumukhāddharmo na śrotavyastu kaulikaiḥ |  
asaṃskāraṃ pibeddravyaṃ valotkāreṇa maithunaṃ ||  
  
svahastena paśuṃ hatvā rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet |  
vīrahatyā vṛthāpānaṃ vīradravyāpahāraṇaṃ ||  
  
vīrastrīgamanaṃ caiva tatsaṃyogastu paṃcamaḥ |  
mahāpātakamityuktaṃ kaulikānāṃ kulāgame ||  
  
śṛṇu putrarahasyaṃ me samayācāra saṃbhavaṃ |  
yena hīnā na siddhyaṃti janmakoṭi sahasraśaḥ ||  
  
manavaḥ kulaśāstrāṇāṃ kulacaryānuyāyināṃ |  
udāracittaḥ sarvatra vaiṣṇavācāra tatparaḥ ||  
  
paraniṃdā sahiḥṣṇuḥ syāddupakārarataḥ sadā |  
parvate vipine vāpi nirjane śūnyamaṃḍape ||  
  
catuṣpathe jale śūnye yadi daivādgatirbhavet |  
kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvā manuṃjatvā natvā gacchedyathā mukhaṃ ||  
  
gṛddhaṃ vīkṣya mahākālīṃ namaskuryādalakṣitaḥ |  
kṣemaṃkarīṃ tathā vīkṣyajaṃvukīṃ yamadūtikāṃ ||  
  
kuraṃgaṃśyenaṃbhūkākau kṛṣṇamārjārameva ca |  
kṛśodarī mahācaṇḍe muktakeśī valipriye ||  
  
kulācāra prasannāsyenamaste śaṃkarapriye |  
śmaśānasthaṃ śavaṃ dṛṣṭvā pradakṣiṇa manuṃsmaran ||  
  
praṇamyānena maṃtreṇamaṃtrī sukhamavāpnuyāt |  
ghoradaṃṣṭrekarālāsyekiṭiśabda praṇādivi ||  
  
p. 56b)  
  
ghoraghoraravāsphāla namaste citivāsini |  
raktavastraṃ tathā puṣpaṃ rājānaṃ rājaputrakaṃ ||  
  
hastyaścarathaśastrāṇi phalakān vīrapuruṣān |  
mahiṣaṃ kulanāthaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā mahiṣamarddinī ||  
  
praṇamya jayadurgāṃ vāsa ca vighnairnalipyate |  
jayadevī jagaddhātrī tripure ca tridaivate ||  
  
bhaktebhyo varade devi mahiṣaghnī namostute |  
madyabhāṃḍaṃ samālokya matsyaṃ māṃsaṃ varastriyaṃ ||  
  
dṛṣṭvā ca bhairavīṃ devī praṇamya vivṛṣenmanuṃ |  
ghoravighnavināśāya kulācāra samṛddhaye ||  
  
namāmi varade devī muṇḍamālā vibhūṣite |  
raktadhārā samākīrṇe varadetvānnamāmyahaṃ ||  
  
sarvavighnaharedevi namaste varavallabhe |  
eteṣāṃ darśane naiva yadi daivānna kurvate ||  
  
śaktimaṃtraṃ puraskṛtya tasya siddhirnnajāyate |  
vedaśāstrapurāṇāni spaṣṭā veśyāṃganā iva ||  
  
eyaṃ tu śāṃbhavī vidyāṃ guptā kulavadhūriva |  
suguptāṃ kaulikācāra manu gṛhnaṃti devatāṃ ||  
  
vāṃchā siddhiṃ prayacchaṃti nāśayaṃti prakāśanāt |  
kulapuṣpaṃ kuladravyaṃ kulapūjāṃ kulaṃ japaṃ ||   
  
guruṃ kulapatiṃ cāpi kulamālī kulākulaṃ |  
kulacakraṃ kuladhyānaṃ sarvathā na prakāśayet ||  
  
prakāśāt siddhihāniḥ syāt prakāśādvaṃdhanādikaṃ |  
prakāśādvalahāniḥ syāt prakāśāddevahiṃsanaṃ ||  
  
prakāśān mṛtyulābhaḥ syānna prakāśyaṃ kadācana |  
pūjākālena maheśāni yadikopyatra gacchati ||  
  
darśayedvaiṣṇavīṃ mudrāṃ viṣṇunyāsaṃstathāstavaṃ |  
kadācidaṃgahāniḥsyānna ca vyaktaḥ kadācana ||  
  
paraṃ pūjā na kartavyā na ca vyaktiḥ kadācana |  
aṃtaḥ śāktā vahiḥ śaivāḥ sabhāryā vaiṣṇavāmatāḥ ||  
  
nānārūpadharāvīrāvicaraṃti mahītale |  
dakṣiṇākhyaṃ kulācāraṃ kathitaṃ tava suvrate ||  
  
na kasmaicit pravaktavyaṃ yadīcchet priyamātmanaḥ |  
atha vāmakulamārgādhikāritā vivekamāha ||  
  
vakṣyetha prakaṭaṃ dharmaṃ kaulikānāṃ ca vāmanī |  
ihaloke paratrāpiyaṃ kṛtvā sukhamāpnuyāt ||  
  
brāhmaṇyaṃ svasya viprastu samyajñātvā samāviśet |  
vāmamārgetha vā kaule tatrāpi ca na laṃghayet ||  
  
p. 57a)  
  
svasvavarṇā samācāraṃ na kuryāt tatpratigrahaṃ |  
parastrī dhananiṃdā ca vedaśāstrādi niṃdanaṃ ||  
  
anigrahaṃ cendriyāṇāṃ vacanaṃ guruviprayoḥ |  
saṃgaḥ sarvātmanātyājyoguptastiṣṭedguruṃ vinā ||  
  
satsaṃgaśca vivekaśca niścalaṃ nayanadvayaṃ |  
yasya nāsti naraḥ soṃdhaḥ kathaṃ vāme sukhaṃ labhet ||  
  
saṃsārikaḥ sukhaṃ proktaṃ vrahmajñosmītivādinaṃ |  
karmabhaṃgo bhayabhraṣṭaṃtaṃ tyajedetyajaṃ yathā ||  
  
madyaṃmāṃsaṃ surāpānaṃ matsyāḥ strīṇāṃdhavāstathā |  
anekā yatra jāyaṃte tatra vāmo gatipradaḥ ||  
  
sthitvā tu dakṣiṇemārge guptaṃ bhuṃktye palādikaṃ |  
sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate kṛmiṃ ||  
  
vinā valiṃ palāṃ bhuṃktye vinā pūjāṃ surāṃ pibet |  
dūtīyajñaṃ vinā gacchet striyaṃ vāmyapi nārakī ||  
  
avudhvā samayācāraṃ kuladharmaṃ caredyadi |  
sa guruścaiva śiṣyaśca yoginīnāṃ bhavetyaśuḥ ||  
  
vāmamārgamajānāti mūḍhātmāmokṣamicchati |  
pārāvāramapāraṃ sa vāhubhyāṃ tartumicchati ||  
  
sarvakarmavihīnāye varṇāśrama vivarjitāḥ |  
kaule vā vāmamārgaṃ te bhuktimukteścabhājanaṃ ||  
  
niṃdaṃ tu vāṃdhavāḥ sarvetyajaṃ tu strī sutādayaḥ |  
janāhasaṃtumāṃ dṛṣṭvā rājānodaṇḍadyaṃ tu vā ||  
  
rogadāridrya duḥkhādyaiḥ pīḍitopyaniśaṃ tvahaṃ |  
lakṣmīstiṣṭatu vā yātu na muṃcāmiparthatvidaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ yasya dṛḍhā bhaktiḥ sa vāme siddhimāpnuyāt |  
nārthalābhānna ca krodhānnaḍheṣānna ca matsarān ||  
  
na kāmānna bhayādvāpimārgaṃ prāptaṃ parityajet |  
pratyahaṃ nārcayeddevīṃ mārgesmin vighnamāpnuyāt ||  
  
gurukāruṇya saṃpūto dehanirddhūtakalpaṣaḥ |  
kulapūjārato yastu soyaṃ kaulo navetaraḥ ||  
  
parokṣeko na jānīte kasya kiṃ ca bhaviṣyati |  
yadvai pratyakṣaphaladaṃ tadevottamadarśanaṃ ||  
  
gurūpadeśa nihitā mahāṃtā iti kecana |  
mohayaṃti janān kecit svayaṃ pūrvaṃ vimohitāḥ ||  
  
peyaṃ madyaṃ laṃ khādyaṃ samālokya priyāmukhaṃ |  
ityevā caraṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ paramāḥ pravadaṃti ca ||  
  
madyapānena manujo yadi siddhiṃ labheta cet |  
madyapānaratāḥ sarve saṃsiddhāna bhavetyume ||  
  
māṃsabhakṣaṇamātreṇa yadi puṇyāgatirbhavet |  
kravyādānāṃ tadā mokṣo māṃsādanyannabhuṃjate ||  
  
strīsaṃbhogena bhodevī yadi mokṣobhi jāyate |  
tadā sarvepi muktāḥ syuḥkasyajanma bhaviṣyati ||  
  
kṛpāṇadhārāgamanādvyāghrakarṇāvalaṃvanāt |  
bhujaṃgadhāraṇānnūnamaśakyaṃ kulavartmanaḥ ||  
  
p. 57b)  
  
vṛthāpānaṃ tu deveśi surāpānamihocyate |  
tanmahāpātakaṃ jñeyaṃ vedādiṣu nirūpitaṃ ||  
  
anāṃghre ca mavālokyamanāścādyamapeyakaṃ |  
madyaṃ māṃsaṃ paśūnāṃ tu kaulikānāṃ mahat phalaṃ ||  
  
amedhyāni dvijātīnāṃ madyānyekādaśaiva hi |  
dvādaśāṃ tu surāmadyaṃ sarveṣāmuttamaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
tasmād brāhmaṇa rājanyau vaiśyaśca na surāṃ pibet |  
surādarśanamātreṇa kuryāt sūryāvalokanaṃ ||  
  
tasya saṃsargamātreṇa prāṇāyāma trayaṃ caret |  
ājānubhyāṃ bhavet snānaṃ nābhyāmupavasedahaḥ ||  
  
uddhanoce strirātraṃ tu madyasya sparśane vidhiḥ |  
surāpāne kāmakṛte jvalaṃtītāṃ prave * * (?) t ||  
  
mukhe tayā vinirddagdhetacchuddhiṃ samavāpnuyāt |  
avidhānena yohanyādātmārthe prāṇinaḥ priye ||  
  
nivasennarakeghore dināni paśuromabhiḥ |  
samitāni durācārastiryagyoniṣu jāyate ||  
  
vidhivadgāṃdvijaṃ vāpi hatyāpāpairnalipyate ||  
  
sarvebhyaḥ kaulikaḥ śreṣṭhastūrdhvāmnāyī ca vāgamaḥ |  
adhikārī bhaktiyuktoyaścamadguru sevakaḥ ||  
  
sa eva kauliko vaṃdya itaremadyapānatāḥ |  
smaraṇaṃ kīrtanaṃ tasya darśanaṃ vaṃdanaṃ tathā ||  
  
saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ ca kurute rājasūyādhikaṃ phalaṃ |  
sa yatra vasate devāstatra śrīvijayo bhavet ||  
  
dṛṣṭve dṛśaṃ ca praṇamedanyairvarjyaḥ sadūrataḥ ||  
  
pūrvāmnāyaḥ sṛṣṭirūpaḥ sthitirūpaṃ tu dakṣiṇaḥ |  
saṃhāraḥ paścimāmnāya uttarenugraho bhavet ||  
  
maṃtrayogaṃ viduḥ pūrvaṃ bhaktiyogaṃ tu dakṣiṇaṃ |  
paścimaṃ karmayogaṃ tu jñānayogaṃ tathottaraṃ ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau dakṣiṇādyācāranirṇayo nāma dvādaśaḥ prakāśaḥ ||   
12 ||  
  
atha śyāmādi pratyekavidyāyāṃ viśiṣya maṃtrasiddhyaikakāraṇaṃ mahānīlādi   
kramamāha ||   
  
devyuvāca |  
  
deveśaśrotumicchāmi rahasyāti rahasyakaṃ |  
daśavidyādikādevaṃ daśavaidyekramāḥ prabhoḥ ||  
  
puraivakathitā svāmintaṃ kramaṃ vada saṃprati ||  
  
śiva uvāca ||  
  
rahasyāti rahasyaṃ ca kathyate tava bhaktitaḥ |  
mahānīla krameṇaiva kālikā siddhidāyinī ||  
  
mahānīlakramo devī dvividhā parikīrtitaḥ |  
sakalo niṣkalaścetitaṃ kramaṃ śṛṇu pārvatī ||  
  
p. 58a)   
  
khaḍgahastaśiranyasta sarvadā muktakuṃtalaḥ |  
sadāmāṃsāsavollāsa vijayāghūrṇalocanaḥ ||  
  
siṃdūratilakaṃ bhālepāṇau tu madirārasaṃ |  
na karoti naro yastu sa kathaṃ mama pūjakaḥ ||  
  
rātrau paryaṭanaṃ caiva rātrau śakteḥ prapūjanaṃ |  
na karoti naro yastu sa kathaṃ mamapūjakaḥ ||  
  
yoni cuṃvanakaṃ karmaśakterāliṃganaṃ tathā |  
na karoti naro yastu sakathaṃ mama pūjakaḥ ||  
  
tāṃbūlaṃ yonicakraṃ ca muṇḍamālā śavāśanaṃ |  
siṃdūraṃ khaḍgakaṃ caiva saṃvidā savayorasaṃ ||  
  
etāṃvihāyayaḥ kaścit kālīṃ sādhitumudyataḥ |  
ihakṣobhamavāpnoti paratra narakaṃ vrajet ||  
  
komurvudayugairdevi na hi siddhyatitāriṇī |  
siṃdūraviṃdubhūyugme svayaṃbhū munipatrakaṃ ||  
  
raktacaṃdanajaṃ vāpi tripuṇḍraṃ ca tatopari |  
kurvandalekajjalasya viṃdurdeyo maheśvari ||  
  
mahānīla kramedevi tilakaḥ parikīrtitaḥ |  
śmaśānaśāyī māṃsāsī saṃvidā naṃdamānasaḥ ||  
  
striyaṃ paśyan pṛśan gacchan sarvakālaṃ japaṃ caret |  
veśyārataḥ śmaśānastho mṛducūḍaka saṃyutaḥ ||  
  
daṃtākṣamālayādevi rājadaṃtena meruṇā |  
mālāṃ kṛtvā japeddevi sadā tāṃbūlacarvakaḥ ||  
  
kapālapātrasaṃpūjā vīrasādhana tatparaḥ |  
kapālamālābharaṇo rāmācuṃvana tatparaḥ ||  
  
śaktyānaṃdo netrayugaṃ mukhehālāṃ gṛhāṃgaṇe |  
veśyā vālākare mālāśaktilolābhagāṃvuje ||  
  
yonisaṃ cuṃvanaṃ kṛtvā sarvakālaṃ japaṃ kare |  
śaktyudbhavāna saṃkāryaḥ sarvametaccarācaraṃ ||  
  
avicārī prahṛṣṭātmāstrībhakto vijiteṃdriyaḥ |  
īdṛgvidho naro devī mahānīla kramomataḥ ||  
  
rājadaṃtamayī mālādviradoṣṭrāśca saṃbhavāḥ |  
asaktānāṃ niṣkalaḥ syāttaṃ kramaṃ śṛṇu pārvatī ||  
  
pītayādugdhakaṃ pītvā saccidānaṃdamānasaḥ |  
sphāṭikīmālikāṃ kṛtvā vihāre japamācaret ||  
  
dikkāla niyamonāstisthityādi niyamo na ca |  
na japekāla niyamo mahāmaṃtrasya sādhane ||  
  
yasmin maṃtre sadācārastatra dharmastu tādṛśaḥ |  
bhrāṃtistatra na kartavyā svargo vā mokṣa eva ca ||  
  
mṛdukomalakaṃ devi cūḍakaṃ vātha cūḍakaṃ |  
śarvavīrāsanaṃ kṛtvā yonitogāsanaṃ ca vā ||  
  
p. 58b)  
  
kāmarūpāsanaṃ devī muratāsanameva ca |  
siṃdūrāsanakaṃ devī parvatāsanameva ca ||  
  
sarovarāsanaṃ ceti tilapuṣpe cakhaṃ jayaṃ |  
caṃdraviṃvaṃ sarpiṇī ca cuṃvanāsanameva ca ||  
  
prayāgāsanakaṃ devī mahāprayāgāsanaṃ tathā |  
sparśakhaṭvāsaneceti yoni cuṃvanamāsanaṃ ||  
  
niṣkāsparśāsanaṃ devī vāyuḥ sparśāsanaṃ ca vā |  
āśreyāsanakaṃ devī tathā muṇḍāsanaṃ tathā ||  
  
śrīmuṇḍamurataṃ vāpi śrīvīramurataṃ ca vā |  
paṃcavīrāsanaṃ devī mureṃdrādi diśāḥ kramāt ||  
  
śrīdevyuvāca |  
  
deveśa śrotumicchāmi mahācīna kramaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
śiva uvāca |  
  
mahācīnakramaṃ devī kathyate sāṃprataṃ mayā |  
mahācīna krameṇaiva tārāśīghra phalapradā ||  
  
brahmacīno divyacīno vīracīnastṛtīyakaḥ |  
mahācīnonikalaścacīnaḥ paṃcāvidhomataḥ ||  
  
mahācīnaḥ kramāddevī dvividhaḥ parikīrtitaḥ |  
sakalo niṣkalaśceti sakalovauddhagocaraḥ ||  
  
niṣkalo brāhmaṇānāṃ ca dvitīyaṃ śṛṇu pārvatī |  
navadvayaṃ tribhuvane sārātsārataraṃ paraṃ ||  
  
mahācīna kramodevī dvividhaiva prakīrtitaḥ |  
tatraiva devadeveśi traiguṇyādbhedabhājanaṃ ||  
  
snānādimānasaṃ śaucaṃ mānasaḥ pravarojapaḥ |  
pūjanaṃ mānasaṃ divyaṃ mānasaṃ tarpaṇādikaṃ ||  
  
mānaso niyamo prokto mānasaṃdaṃtadhāvanaṃ |  
sarva eva śubhaḥ kālānāśubho vidyate kvacit ||  
  
na viśeṣo divārātrau na saṃdhyāyāṃ mahāniśi |  
vastrā īmānasaṃ śaucaṃ dehasparśādivāriṇāṃ ||  
  
śuddhiṃ na kārayedatra nirvikalpaṃ manaścaret |  
nātraśuddherapekṣāsti navāmedhyādidūṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
ya evaṃ ciṃtayen maṃtraṃ sarvakāmaḥ samṛddhidaṃ |  
gadyapadyamayīvāṇī sabhāyāṃ tasya jāyate ||  
  
tasya darśanamātreṇavādino niḥprabhāmatāḥ |  
rājānopi ca dāsatvaṃ bhajaṃti kiṃ pare janāḥ ||  
  
sarvadā pūjayeddevīmasnāta kṛta bhojanaṃ |  
mahāniśya śucau deśe valiṃmaṃtreṇa dāpayet ||  
  
strīdveṣo naiva kartavyo viśeṣāt pūjanaṃ striyaḥ |  
japasthāne mahāśaṃkhaṃ niveśyorddhe japaṃ caret ||  
  
striyaṃ gacchan pṛśan paśyan yatra kutrāpya cūḍake |  
bhuktvā tāṃvūlamanyāṃśca bhakṣa dravyānyathārucīn ||  
  
p. 59a)  
  
māṃsaṃ matsyaṃ dadhikṣaudraṃ saṃvidāsavadyorasaṃ |  
bhuktvānyaśeṣabhakṣyāṇi bhuktvā bhakṣyaṃ carejjapam ||  
  
dikkālaniyamonāsti sthityādi niyamo na ca |  
na japekāla niyamo nārcādiṣu valiṣvapi ||  
  
svecchā niyama uktotra mahāmaṃtrasya sādhane |  
vallāsanaṃghohadehasparśasparśādivāriṇaḥ ||  
  
tailaṃ saṃlāpya deveśi tāṃvūlaṃ bhakṣayan sadā |  
nānāvarāṇi saṃdhāryyadehaṃ vastreṇa mārjayet ||  
  
evaṃ snānaṃ careddevi sarvadā tadgatāśayaḥ |  
mahācīna kramodevī viprasnānamidaṃ bhavet ||  
  
śuddhiṃ na cārcayedatra nirvikalpaṃ manaścaret |  
sugaṃdhiścetalauhityakusumairaktacaṃdanaiḥ ||  
  
vilvairmaruvakādyaiśca tulasīvarjitaiḥ śubhaiḥ |  
varjayed vilvapatraṃ ca manuṃ yatnena varjayet ||  
  
keśān saṃvarddhayeddevī sarvadā tailabhūṣitaḥ |  
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ viśeṣadivasaṃ sadā ||  
  
nādharmo vidyate subhrū kiṃtu dharmo mahān bhavet |  
svecchā niyama uktotra pravareddhṛṣṭamānasaḥ ||  
  
kṛtārthaṃ manyamānastu saṃtuṣṭo niyamānasaḥ |  
harernāmanagṛhnīṃyānna spṛśet tulasīdalaṃ ||  
  
nānya ciṃtā prakartavyo siddhirdivasamātrataḥ |  
anyathā naiva siddhiḥ syāt prajapairapi koṭibhiḥ ||  
  
puraścaraṇa lakṣaiśca homādīnāṃ ca koṭibhiḥ |  
brāhmībhūte mahācāre nirvikalpaḥ priyestivai ||  
  
bhrūyugme kuṃḍale devi siṃdūraṃ tatdanaṃtaraṃ |  
kucaṃdanaṃ tripuṇḍraṃ ca paṃkajaṃ vāsakeśaraṃ ||  
  
muṇḍamālāgaledhāryā kapālapāṇi saṃgataḥ |  
ityācāraparonityaṃ mahācīna kramo bhavet ||  
  
sarvadānaṃda hṛdyaḥ sarvadābhakta sevakaḥ |  
karṇanetrāṃtarasthoyaḥ mahāśaṃkhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
paṃcāśanmaṇibhirmālāgonalebhāsthi saṃbhavā |  
mālākuryān maheśāni cāṣṭasiddhīśvaro bhavet ||  
  
saivatārā maheśāni nātrakāryā vicāraṇā |  
śivaśaṃkaraviśveśaviśvatārakaśāśvataḥ ||  
  
vedahīnā vaidyadharmāstānkathaṃ brāhmaṇaścaret ||  
  
śiva uvāca ||  
  
sādhudevī mahāprājñe priye sādhaka supriye |  
tadbhāvanāśramāyatrastadbhāvamādaret priye ||  
  
yathā śrāddhavidhau devimāṃsaṃ mukhyaṃ prakīrtitaṃ |  
kalua tacca niṣiddhaṃ syādbrāhmaṇānāṃ maheśvarī ||  
  
p. 59b)  
  
ātmārthaṃ vā parārthaṃ vā paśūn hatvā paśurbhavet |  
yāvaṃti tasya romāṇitāvadyonimavāpnuyāt ||  
  
tathā tadbhāvanāyāṃ tu na ca doṣosti pārvatī |  
sa karastu mayā proktā niṣkalaṃ śṛṇu pārvatī ||  
  
maṇivaṃdhādadhapāṇiṃ pādāṃgulyādadhaḥ śive |  
mukhaṃ prakṣālayeddevī cīnasthānamidaṃ bhavet ||  
  
jānubhyāmavanīṃ dhṛtvā bhūmau mastaka mānayet ||  
cīnamārge namaskārakīrtitastu mayā tava ||  
  
pūrvakramasya deveśi kramaḥ pratinidhirmayā |  
snānadānādikaṃ kṛtvā tathā pūjādikaṃ priye ||  
  
tathā snānaṃ name deho na ca pāmanāstivai |  
kiṃ snānaṃ kasyacit snānamasnātaḥ kṛtabhojanaḥ ||  
  
sarvameva hṛdaṃbhojemayi sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ ||  
mayijñātā maṃtrasiddhirmamadevāvarapradā ||  
  
tejorūpaṃ jagatsarvaṃ tāriṇī tatsvarūpadhṛk |  
tattejasīsvasyadehaṃ saṃbhāvyajapamācaret ||  
  
bhāvanā ca śamāpanno bhavedyogī mahākaviḥ |  
guḍārdrakarasenaiva surā tu brāhmaṇasya ca ||  
  
tadabhāve jalaṃ devi saṃbhāvya pūjanaṃ caret |  
tabhāva hṛdayāsannaḥ sadā tadrajamānasaḥ ||  
  
dvaṃdvabhāvaṃ parityajya sarvasiddhīśvaro bhavet |  
brahmā caiva vaśiṣṭaśca tathānye ca ṛṣīśvarāḥ ||  
  
niṣkalaḥ kramamārgeṇa bhajaṃti satataṃ śive |  
tārābhaktā maheśāni brahmaṇā parikīrtitāḥ ||  
  
brahmavidyā mahāvidyā sarvatra durlabhākalau |  
rahasyāti rahasyaṃ ca goptavyaṃ paśusaṃkaṭe ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
chinnamastāvidhau devakramaṃme vrūhi satvaraṃ ||  
  
śiva uvāca ||  
  
divyacīna krameṇaiva chinnamastā varapradā |  
kramadvayaṃ maheśāni pūrvamekaṃ prakāśitaṃ ||  
  
etasyāstilakodevi bhrūmadhye cakracaṃdanaṃ |  
tadaṃte rocanāpatre tripuṇḍraṃ divyavarṇakaiḥ ||  
  
śmaśānabhasmaviṃdustu tanmadhye dāpayet priye |  
mukhe mukhaṃ pradatvā tu sarvakālaṃ japecchive ||  
  
yonicakraṃ samālocya yatkiṃcit kurute naraḥ |  
tattadakṣayamāpnotichinnāvidyā prasādataḥ ||  
  
kālītārā chinnamastā tathā ṣaṭśāṃbhavī śive |  
dikkālaniyamo nāsti sthityādi niyamo na hi ||  
  
pātāle kuhare durge parvate taṭinī taṭe |  
aṃtarīkṣe tathā bhūmau sarvatra japamācaret ||  
  
p. 60a)  
  
viśeṣaḥ kathitā devīśakti tatvasya pāvanaṃ ||  
  
devyuvāca |  
  
gaṃdharvākhyaṃ kramaṃ deva kathayasvamayi prabho ||  
  
śiva uvāca |  
  
gaṃdharvākhya krameṇaiva suṃdarī bhuvidurlabhā |  
gaṃdharvākhya kramaṃ devi kathyate śṛṇu sāṃprataṃ ||  
  
bhrūmadhye kuṃkumaṃ devi tadaṃte malayāguru |  
aṣṭagaṃdha tripuṇḍrasya madhye kastūrikānvitaṃ ||  
  
sugaṃdhaśvetalauhitya puṣpaiḥ saṃbhūṣito naraḥ |  
svastikāṃkita dehastho ratnaprākārasaṃyutaḥ ||  
  
aṣṭagaṃdhasya dhūmena nānāsaugaṃdhyabhūṣitaḥ |  
raktamālyāṃvaradharo muktāhāropaśobhitaḥ ||  
  
pūrṇābhiṣeka śirasi tena tatra na muṃḍanaṃ |  
keśān saṃvarddhayeddevi saugaṃdhya tailabhūṣitaḥ ||  
  
nānāsaugaṃdhya bhojyaiśca rājayogyai maheśvariḥ |  
āyāni saṃgataḥ pūtāḥ kiṃ punarvahnitāpitāḥ ||  
  
sadā coṣṇodakaiḥ snāyāt tadabhāve yathodakaṃ |  
gṛhaṃ citraistu saṃcitredarpaṇodarasannibhaṃ ||  
  
vitāna dvajabhūṣāḍhyaṃ ghaṃṭhānādopaśopaśobhitaṃ |  
paṃcavāditra saṃyuktaṃ nānāghoṣa samanvitaṃ ||  
  
ataḥ sūkṣmāṃ varairyuktaḥ svarṇapātrādi raṃjibhiḥ |  
graiveyavalayāṃgulyabhūṣaṇaiḥ bhūṣitaḥ sadā ||  
  
nānāmadhurabhojyaiśca dugdhapākairanekakaiḥ |  
nānābhogenasaṃyukto gaṃdharvākhyaḥ kramo bhavet ||  
  
iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ bhairavākhyaṃ śṛṇu kramaṃ |  
svapuṣpaiḥ kramayogena bhairavī bhuvi durlabhā ||  
  
svapuṣpākhyaḥ kramodevi kathyate śṛṇu sāṃprataṃ |  
taruṇī suṃdarī ramyāṃ tāruṇyāmṛtavigrahāṃ ||  
  
sadāratausābhilāṣāṃ maithunodyatamānasaṃ |  
maṃtrayaṃtra samāyuktāṃ samāyuktāṃ maheśvarī ||  
  
nagnāṃtāṃ ca vihāyādau svayaṃ nagno japaṃ caret |  
parasparālokanaṃ ca kartavyaṃ ca parasparaṃ ||  
  
avikārāṃ yadā devī sādhanārhonacānyathā |  
vikāre bhāvanāne ca sādhako naśyati kṣaṇāt ||  
  
tat kuṃḍaṃ ca maheśāni kṣaṇādvikarṣitaṃ bhavet |  
tathāpi svasya dehasya vikāraṃ na hi kārayet ||  
  
sāpi ceddevadeveśi savikārī yathā bhavet |  
puṣpiṇī manunādevi palātpuṣpaṃ samānayet ||  
  
drāviṇī manunādevi valādṛṣṭyāḍanaṃ nayet |  
ubhayaṃ caiva saṃgṛhya jayaṃ kuryān maheśvarī ||  
  
śaktiśca sādhako devi daṃpatī durlabhau smṛtau |  
vagalā suṃdarī tārākālādyāsvapi yatnataḥ ||  
  
p. 60b)  
  
kramoyaṃ yogyatāṃ samyak nātrakāryā vicāraṇā |  
kalidoṣāvaśāddevīnāyaṃ yogobhaviṣyati ||  
  
tasmāt pāśavavetkalpevālāśastādhunā śive |  
vālāyāmubhavācārodakṣiṇomukhya eva hi ||  
  
śīghraṃ ca siddhikāmaścedgavākṣāyogamabhyaset |  
yatra strīṇāṃ samūhosti nadī na daśamudrake ||  
  
yatra snānaṃ na kurvaṃti gavākṣaṃ tatra kārayet |  
tāmālokya prayatnena japaṃ kuryānniraṃtaraṃ ||  
  
sarvāḥ saṃvīkṣyayeddevī svarṇaratnādibhiḥ priye |  
iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ tilakaṃ śṛṇu pārvatī ||  
  
vāmahastatale yaṃtraṃ vilikhyā yatnataḥ śive |  
avaśiṣṭena tilakaṃ kārayet parameśvarī ||  
  
bhāle kastūrikā viṃduṃ muniputraṃ sucaṃdanaṃ |  
tanmadhye śvetaviṃduṃ ca keśādi pūrvavad bhavet ||  
  
daśavidyāvidhau devi keśavarddhanamīritaṃ ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
deveśa śrotumicchāmi kamalā kramanirṇayaṃ ||  
  
śiva uvāca ||  
  
bhrūyugmedyu śṛṇaṃ devī siṃdūraṃ tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
sveta tripuṇḍraṃ deveśi tanmadhye keśaraṃ śive ||  
  
snātaḥ śuklāṃvaradharaḥ śuklamālyānulepanaḥ |  
śuklabhūṣaṇabhūṣāḍhyaḥ strisaṃdhyaṃ snānamācaret ||  
  
haviṣyāsī bhūmiśāyī madhurānna priyo naraḥ |  
bhṛguvāsaraparyaṃtaṃ dvitīyaṃ bhṛguvāsaraṃ ||  
  
dinavṛddhi krameṇaiva kumārīṃ pūjayetsadā |  
dvitīya bhṛgubhārabhya hrāsayeddinavṛddhitaḥ ||  
  
pratyahaṃ pūjayeddevi nānāvāditra niścanaiḥ |  
dinaṣoḍaśaparyaṃtaṃ pratyahaṃ tu samācaret ||  
  
punastadvimamārabhyataddināṃtaṃ maheśvarī |  
pūjayet prayato nityaṃ devatābhāva tatparaḥ ||  
  
pradakṣiṇā prakartavyā kalābhāva krameṇa ca |  
dīpāstatra pradātavyā kalāvṛddhiḥ krameṇa ca ||  
  
brāhmaṇān bhojayennityaṃ kalābhāvakrameṇa ca |  
ityācāraparaḥ śrīmān viṣṇurūponaro bhavet ||  
  
rājacihnāni sarvāṇi prayataḥ pūjayet sadā |  
sarvasāmrājyā lakṣmyāstu nātho bhūyānna saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
dhanadātasya dehasthā rājā ca kiṃkaro bhavet ||  
  
devyuvāca ||
