deveśa śrotumicchāmi brahmamārga kramaṃ śiva ||  
  
śiva uvāca ||  
  
veśyāyāḥ kajjalaṃ deyaṃ siṃdūreṇa tripuṇḍrakaṃ |  
haridrā bhrūyugedeyāśvetapatraṃ samācaret ||  
  
p. 61a)  
  
raktaviṃduṃ ca tanmadhye sarvadā tadgatodbhavet |  
bhojane śayane rātrau maithunaṃ sarvadā bhavet ||  
  
ucchiṣṭahaste deveśi ucchiṣṭe na valiṃ haret |  
śaktyucchiṣṭaṃ parocchiṣṭaṃ bhojanaṃ sārvakālikāṃ ||  
  
jape kuryān maheśāni rātrāveva japaṃ caret |  
tāmbūlaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā tāṃbūlī caiva mohayet ||  
  
tāṃbūlabhakṣīṃ māṃsāsī bhuktvācārcāṃ ca kārayet |  
gṛhaṃ pralipya yatnena mārjanyā mārjanaṃ caret ||  
  
prajaped yatnato devi nānyathā siddhyati dhruvaṃ |  
ucchiṣṭa haste deveśi svadehaṃ procchyate sadā ||  
  
ucchiṣṭahastaḥ prajaped brahmamārgaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |  
brahmamārgaḥ kramodevi gatitastu mayā tava ||  
  
anena kramayogena siddhamārgaḥ kramo bhavet |  
siddhavidyā prabhāvāsyāt pratyakṣā varadāyinī ||  
  
sureṃdropi ca dāsaḥ syānmanuṣyāṇāṃ ca kākathā |  
rahasyaṃ kathitaṃ bhadre goanīyaṃ svayonivat ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
vada śrībhuvaneśānyāḥ kramaṃ paramadurlabhaṃ ||  
  
śiva uvāca ||  
  
divyabhāva krameṇaiva bhuvanā śīghrasiddhidā |  
hakāro śivarūpitvā ukāraḥ pāpanāśakaḥ ||  
  
ikāraḥ kāmarūpatvāt māyā tena prakīrtitāḥ |  
brahmāṇḍa me taddeveśi māyayā veṣṭitaṃ bhavet ||  
  
yasyāṃ māyā vinā devi ma ca kiṃcit prabhāsate |  
yadbhāsarahitaṃ kiṃcinna ca kiṃcit prabhāsate ||  
  
yadbhāvarahitaṃ kiṃcinna ca tadbhāsate kvacit |  
yadbhāsāsahitaṃ devi jagade tat prabhāsate ||  
  
yāṃ vinā tu maheśāni jagadyatra samaṃ bhavet |  
evaṃ krameṇa deveśi sadā tadgatamānasaḥ ||  
  
trailokyavijayī bhūyānnātrakāryāvicāraṇā |  
etasyā tilakaṃ devi kathyate yatnataḥ śṛṇu ||  
  
śvetacaṃdanaviṃdustu bhrūmadhye tu pralāpayet |  
gaṃdhasāraṃ tadaṃte syāttripuṇḍraṃ divyavarṇataḥ ||  
  
raktākṣatāśca tanmadhye tena siddīśvaro bhavet ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
deveśa śrotumicchāmi dhūmāvatyāḥ kramaṃ śive ||  
  
śiva uvāca ||  
  
dhūmāvatyāḥ kramodevi kathyate śṛṇu pārvatī |  
bhrūmadhye kajjalaṃ devi bhasmaviṃdustadaṃtare ||  
  
tripuṇḍraṃ ca lalāṭe syācchavabhasmatadaṃtare |  
kṛṣṇavastrāṃ varadharo kṛṣṇagaṃdha vibhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
gaṃdhapuṣpeṇa saṃyuktaḥ śmaśānāsanasaṃgataḥ |  
dhūmavarṇaṃ jagatsarvaṃ maṃtrī dhūmamayaṃ bhavet ||  
  
kākapicchaṃ vāsanaṃ syāt kṛṣṇa dravyaṃ pradhārayet |  
brahmacārī mitāhārī nirvikalpo jiteṃdriyaḥ ||  
  
satyavādī hṛdācāro bhūśāyīkuśaviṣṭharaḥ |  
snānaṃ viṣavaṇaṃ kuryāduccāṭana parāyaṇaḥ ||  
  
p. 61b)  
  
svacittaṃ kākavatkṛtya jagaduccāṭaye dhruvaṃ |  
ityācāra paro bhūyāddhūma kramagato bhavet ||  
  
kākakramastugadito kimanyacchrotumicchasi ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
deveśa śrotumicchāmi vagalā kramanirṇayam |  
saubhāgyārca krameṇaiva vagalā śīghradarśinī ||  
  
pītāṃvaradharo maṃtrī pītabhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ |  
pītamālyāṃ varadharopītāgehe samāsthitaḥ ||  
  
pītapūjāparaḥ proktaḥ pītānnapītamānavaḥ |  
pītadravyopabhogī ca pītāsana samanvitaḥ ||  
  
pītahomī pītapuṣpī pītaśaktiḥ samanvitaḥ |  
rocanā bhrūvimaṃ dadyān kuṃkumaṃ munipatrakaṃ ||  
  
haridrayā tripuṇḍraṃ ca tanmadhye khādiraṃ śive |  
haricaṃdanadhūpena dhūpitaḥ parameśvarī ||  
  
śaktau sarvaṃ tu saṃpādya kramamārgarato bhavet |  
sṛṣṭisthityaṃta saṃhāraḥ pūjā ca trividhākalau ||  
  
kerale sṛṣṭipūjāsyādgarbhekaulāgama kramāt |  
arcanaṃ gauḍadeśe tu sthitimārgaṃ kumārakā ||  
  
guptakaulāgamodevi gauḍadeśārcanevidhiḥ |  
kāmarūpāgamaṃ devi saṃhāraḥ kramapūjanaṃ ||  
  
gauḍāgameva cāṃcalya sāṃkhyāyana munistathā |  
uktā vāmāgamaścaiva sthitya cā śṛṇuputraka ||  
  
sarvāṃgasuṃdarīṃ ramyāṃ sarvāvayava śobhitaṃ |  
navoḍhāṃ puṣpiṇīṃ caiva prārthayedviprakanyakāṃ ||  
  
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ kumārakāṃ |  
atha vā bhaumavāre vā niśāyāṃ bhṛguvāsare ||  
  
suvāsitena tailena kuryādanyajanaṃ tathā |  
bhūlikātaulpamānīya āstīryodamukhe tadā ||  
  
tasyopari samāstīrya śamaṃtairjāti campakaiḥ |  
karpūraṃ caiva kastūrīmiśritaṃ caṃdanaṃ tathā ||  
  
sarvāṃga lepanaṃ kuryāllakṣmīsūktena buddhimān |  
paryaṃkoparitāṃ kanyāṃ caṃdanena vilepitāṃ ||  
  
dhruvādyairiti maṃtreṇa kanyāṃ dakṣiṇato mukhīṃ |  
unmūkhī śamanaṃ kuryācchrīsūktena kumārakaḥ ||  
  
tasyāḥ pādau prasāryātha guptenārccanamācaret |  
nyastvā ṣoḍhā dvayaṃ caiva vagalā paṃcakaṃ nyaset ||  
  
kanyāṃ caiva nyaseddevaṃ tattadaṃgāni saṃsmaret |  
janaṃ japapuraṃ caiva mārjayen mūlavidyayā ||  
  
p. 62a)  
  
gaṃdhadvāreti maṃtreṇa kuryāt kastūri lepanaṃ |  
mūlamaṃtreṇa vai tatra puṣpamālāṃ samarpayet ||  
  
nivedayed dravyaśuddhiṃ tatraiva japamācaret |  
prayogasiddhidaṃ puṃsāṃ maṃtrasiddhikaraṃ paraṃ ||  
  
etatkramaṃ vinā devi prayogo na bhavet kvacit |  
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena siddhyarthī deva bhūtale ||  
  
saubhāgyākhya kramaṃ devī vinā siddhiṃ na koṭibhiḥ |  
abhimānāṣṭakaṃ tyaktvā tyaktvā vaidūṣaṇaṃ trayaṃ ||  
  
tyaktvā paṃceṃdriyā śaktiṃ saubhāgya kramamācaret |  
sukhaduḥkhe same kṛtvā lābhālābhau jayājayau ||  
  
śītoṣṇa samatāṃ kṛtvā saubhāgya kramamācaret |  
ṣoḍhādvayaṃ ca na jñātvāyaḥ karotyarcanaṃ bhuvi ||  
  
patitaḥ sa bhaveddevi rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet |  
vāhyāṃtarayordevi prabhedajñānayorvinā ||  
  
pītakramo na kartavyo devatāśāpamāpnuyāt |  
saṃkalpaṃ ceti kalkena tyaktvā vijñānamānasaḥ ||  
  
pītaḥ kramaṃ tataḥ kuryānno cedbhraṣṭo bhaveddhruvaṃ |  
jiteṃdriya sukhaṃ kṛtvā kuryāt pītakramaṃ śive ||  
  
sukhārthaṃ kurute yosau devatāśāpamāpnuyāt |  
svasyā deśavidhiṃ caiva vā jñātvā parimeśvarī ||  
  
yaḥ karotyarcanaṃ devi sa vipraḥ patito bhavet |  
yastu kanyāmanaḥ kṣobhaṃ karoti yajane śive ||  
  
bhrāṃtacitto bhavet sadyo vācaspatiri vā paraḥ |  
notpādayedvadennaiva manaścaiva śarīrayoḥ ||  
  
vedanāṃjana yadyastu sa naraḥ parito bhavet |  
sapatnīṃ mātṛpatnīṃ vā gurubhāryāmathāpi vā ||  
  
arcayedbhuvanopetāṃ sāṃkhyāya na samarpitāṃ |  
dīkṣāyutāṃ ca rajakīṃ kulālagṛhakanyakāṃ ||  
  
puliṃda kanyakāṃ vāpi golakuṃḍāmṛtamādarāt |  
arcayed ṛṣipatniṃ ca pūrvokta lakṣaṇairyutāṃ ||  
  
arcaṇaṃ vidhimārgeṇa pūjādūrvā samomatāṃ |  
sarvalakṣaṇa saṃyukto puṣpiṇīmarcayecchive ||  
  
mataṃga muninoktaṃ ca sadyaḥ siddhikaraṃ tvidaṃ |  
siddhakramoyaṃ deveśi nāsti siddhirguruṃ vinā ||  
  
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena gurvājñā paripālakaḥ |  
siddho bhavati deveśi nātrakāryā vicāraṇā ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
mahārāja kramaṃ deva kathayasva mama prabho ||  
  
p. 62b)  
  
śiva uvāca |  
  
mahārāja kramo devi kathyate śṛṇu sāṃprataṃ |  
nānāvicitra sopāna maṇḍite citramaṃdape ||  
  
saudhoṣṭālaka saṃśobhidhitā na dhvajaśobhite |  
nājopavaṃ na saṃyukte haṃsamāyūraśobhite ||  
  
nānāvicitraramye ca gajavāji virājite |  
sarvatobhadra saṃyukte nānābharaṇabhūṣite ||  
  
dhūpāmoda samāyukte citradīpena laṃkṛte |  
ratnasiṃhāsane ramye ratnābharaṇabhūṣite ||  
  
jātīcaṃpakapunnāgaketakīgaṃdhaśobhite |  
karpūrā gurukastūrī rocanā kuṃkumairyutaḥ ||  
  
jaṭāmāṃsyādi saugaṃdhyalepanaiḥ paribhūṣitaḥ |  
ghaṃṭhāninādasaṃyuktaḥ sarvadā śuddhamānasaḥ ||  
  
ānaṃdamagna hṛdayodivyavastrairalaṃkṛtaḥ |  
divyamālyāṃ varadharo divyabhūṣairalaṃkṛtaḥ ||  
  
tāṃbūlapūrṇavadanodevendra itrarājitaḥ |  
vedapātrairmṛtyapātrairbhogapātrairnināditaḥ ||  
  
nṛtyagītaiśca vādinnaścaturviṃśativācakaiḥ |  
saṃgītarāgatālaiśca dhvanibhiścanināditaḥ ||  
  
nānādeśopabhāṣābhirgadyaipadyairalaṃkṛtaḥ |  
nānāvicitrabhūṣābhirbhāṣitaḥ sādhakottamaḥ ||  
  
samastarājavarṣāṇī mohanādrānnanāyikā |  
śrīmahārājamātaṃgī sarvadevapramohinī ||  
  
tasyāstu tilakaṃ devi kathyate śṛṇu pārvati |  
kuce dvaṃdvaṃ ca bhrūmadhye gurusārāstadaṃtare ||  
  
kastūrikā tripuṇḍraṃ ca tanmadhye keśaraṃ śive |  
mahārāja kramo devi kathitastu mayā tava ||  
  
atha vā devadeveśi svayaṃgāṇa paro bhavet ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau mahānīlādikramanirṇayo nāma trayodaśaḥ prakāśaḥ ||   
13 ||  
atha vīrapaśubhāvānnigadyaṃte ||  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
vīrabhāvo mahādeva kathyate śṛṇu bhairava |  
nirdvaṃdvamānaso bhūtvā hṛdā kāmakalā tanuḥ ||  
  
niśā su pūjā pravarāhe tu vyuktā sadaiva hi |  
nijaṃ kulaṃ samādhāya svayaṃ bhairava rūpadhṛk ||  
  
kulaṃ ca bhairavī yūyaṃ tadgātrenyāsavistaraṃ |  
prasūna tūlikāmadhyeṃ puṣpakara saṃyute ||  
  
nānāgaṃdha samākīrṇe kuladravyeṇa yaṃtrake |  
likhitvā pūjayecchaktaughanasthāpanapūrvakaṃ ||  
  
svavāmabhāge ṣaṭkoṇaṃ tanmadhye brahmaraṃdhrakaṃ |  
likhitvā tatrakuṃbhaṃ vai sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tathā ||  
  
tāmraṃ bhūmimayaṃ vāpi mahāloha vivarjitaṃ |  
sthāpayet kalaśādhāraṃ kuṃbhaṃ sugaṃdhivāsitaṃ ||  
  
hetu dravyaṃ brāhmaṇādibhedataḥ saṃprapūrayet |  
tatra yaṃtraṃ vilikhyādau yadyat kulasamudbhavaṃ ||  
  
p. 63a)  
  
dhyātvaiṣṭadevatāṃ tatra japedaṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ |  
dhenuyoniṃ pradarśyātha amṛtaṃ tadviciṃtayet ||  
  
dṛṣṭvā mṛtamupāttaṃ vai nṛtyaṃti yoginīgaṇāḥ |  
nṛtyaṃti bhairavāḥ sarve nṛtyaṃti mātaropi ca ||  
  
indrādayaḥ surāḥ sarve nṛtyaṃti madhulolupāḥ |  
brahmaviṣṇumaheśādyāṃ nṛtyaṃti harṣatatparāḥ ||  
  
arghabhāṇḍaṃ tridhā kṛtvā gurave caikabhāgakaṃ |  
ekaṃ kulāyaṃ vai datvā ekena devatarpaṇaṃ ||  
  
pītvā kularasaṃ nānāvastrālaṃkārabhūṣitaḥ |  
sākṣādyadi gururnasyāttadātoye visarjayet ||  
  
ānaṃdarūpavān bhūtvā pūjayet parameśvarī |  
tat tatkalpavidhānena tattadyatnena pūjayet ||  
  
visarjanaṃ vidhāyātha svakule yojayettataḥ |  
tadviṃvara sa pānena amṛtaṃ bhujyate ||  
  
taccakorarasāsvāde saṃmado mama jāyate |  
tatphalagrahaṇādeva meru śṛṃgāvarohaṇaṃ ||  
  
latāliṃgena mātreṇa sudhādhauta kalevaraḥ |  
mūlayoge kṛte tatra japedaṣṭa sahasrakaṃ ||  
  
yatra jāpe ca home ca yatra saṃkhyā na coditā |  
tatreyaṃgaṇanāproktā aṣṭottara sahasrakaṃ ||  
  
jalapūtaṃ havirdravyaṃ gṛhītvā tarpayettataḥ |  
vidhāya tarpaṇaṃ deva pradakṣiṇa manu vrajet ||  
  
stutvā praṇamya kalpokta sravena toṣayet tataḥ |  
tasmāt kulaṃ samāyogya kṛtvā yatnena saṃjapet ||  
  
kule sākṣādyatastatvaṃ svayaṃ tiṣṭhati tatvataḥ |  
sadyaṃ māṃsaṃ tathā matsyaṃ mudrāmaithunameva ca ||  
  
ebhireva kṛtāḥ pūjā kulācāra prakīrtitaḥ |  
tena tat kulaśāstrajñaiḥ pūjanīyā prayatnataḥ ||  
  
kulaṃ kulaṃ cāṣṇakulaṃ niścalaṃ saśyavartate |  
sa dhanyaḥ sa ca vijñānī kularūpaḥ sa eva tu ||  
  
yatra tatra kujevāre śmaśānegamane kṛte |  
pūjāphalaṃ bhavet tatra saptavā sarasaṃmitaṃ ||  
  
caturdaśyāgate tatra pakṣa pūjāphalaṃ bhavet |  
na gacchennārya tatsthāne paśureva na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
nāstyasmādadhikaṃ deva iti ciṃtāparāyaṇaḥ |  
madena dravyabhoktā tu bhavet kulaparāyaṇaḥ ||  
  
sādhakekṣo bhayāpanne mamakṣobhaḥ prajāyate |  
tasmādyatnīdvīravarobhavet bhāgayutaḥ sukhī ||  
  
bhogena mokṣamāpnoti bhogena kulaṃ sādhanaṃ |  
vinā hetukamāsādya kṣobhayukto maheśvaraḥ ||  
  
na pūjāṃ mamasaṃparkaṃ na dhyānamanuciṃtanaṃ |  
tasmād bhuktvā ca pitvā ca pūjayet parameśvara ||  
  
p. 63b)  
  
prakramacyutadoṣostināparaṃ doṣabhūṣaṇaṃ |  
yadyadvadati vidrāviyat karoti yadarcati ||  
  
tat sarvaṃ kularūpaṃ tu dhyātvā ca viharet sudhīḥ |  
ekākī nirjanedeśe śmaśāne parvatevane ||  
  
śūnyagehe nadītīre niḥsaṃgo viharenmudā |  
vīrāṇāṃ japakālastu sarvakālaḥ praśasyate ||  
  
sarvadeśe sarvapīṭhe kartavyaṃ ca na saṃśayaḥ |  
vīrasādhanakāryaṃ ca kartavyaṃ vīrapūruṣaiḥ ||  
  
divyairapi ca kartavyaṃ paśubhirna ca pāmaraiḥ |  
varaṃ pāmara kāryaṃ ca mayaśoriti niścitaṃ ||  
  
yadyannasatpurā proktaṃ saṃketaṃ maṃtrasādhane |  
aṃjanaṃ guṭikādiṃ ca kuryādvīro mahābalaḥ ||  
  
divyevīrenabhedosti yadbhedaṃ tattu kathyate |  
śāṃto vinīto madhuraḥ kalālāvaṇya saṃyutaḥ ||  
  
divyaṃ tu devavatprāyo vīraścoddhatamānasaḥ |  
vibhūti bhūṣaṇairvāpi caṃdanairvāpilepitaḥ ||  
  
ākāragopano vā pityakto vā kulabhairava |  
raktacaṃdanadigdho vā vaiṣṇavaścāpyavaiṣṇavaḥ ||  
  
apamāne ca pūjāyāṃ hṛṣṭapuṣṭaḥ sadā bhavet |  
devaniṃdā paro vāpi tattatpūjāparopi vā ||  
  
pūjāratastadrahitaḥ kulākulamatosthitaḥ |  
nijabhāva samāyukto devavadviharetkṣitau ||  
  
svakulāṃ puraścaryā rātrau kuryānna cānyathā |  
vedahīnodvijedeva yathā na śrutijā kathā ||  
  
viṣṇubhaktiṃ vinādevabhaktirne prabhavedyathā |  
śāktajñānaṃ vināmuktiryathāhāsyāya kalpate ||  
  
guruṃ vinā yathā taṃtre nādhikāraḥ kathaṃcana |  
patihīnā yathā nārī sarvakarma vivarjitā ||  
  
kulaṃ vinādevavidhīṃ kadāpi mamasādhane |  
nādhikārīti kauleya tasmādbhāva paro bhava ||  
  
avinītaṃ kulaṃ yasya sa kathaṃ mamapūjakaḥ |  
tasmādyatnāttathākāryaṃ yathāsyādvinayānvitaṃ ||  
  
bhāvābhāvātkuleśāstrenādhikāraḥ kathaṃcana |  
tena bhāvaviśuddhastu sādhakaḥ kauliko bhavet ||  
  
paśubhāvaṃ pravakṣyāmi "ṣṛṇuvatsa samāhitaḥ |  
yathāvidhi paśurvidyāṃ gṛhītvā bhāvatatparaḥ ||  
  
prathamaṃ pūrvasevārthaṃ yatnataḥ śuddhimācaret |  
namatsya bhojanaṃ kuryānnastriyaṃ manasāsmaran ||  
  
na paradravya lobhīsyānnabhogeṣāṃ na saṃbhajet |  
siṃdhutīre parvate ca kānane vā surālaye ||  
  
vilvamūle vivikte ca puṇyekṣetre ca śobhane |  
na śūdradarśanaṃ kuryāt koṭilyaṃ yatnatastyajet ||  
  
p. 64a)  
  
devatā śubhavarṇāstu dhyātavyā susamāhitaiḥ |  
trisaṃdhyaṃ devapūjā tu trisaṃdhyaṃ japamācaret ||  
  
rātrau maṃtraṃ ca mālāṃ ca na spṛśecca kadācana |  
na maṃtramuccaredbhuktvā maunīsyāt sarvakarmasu ||  
  
parvakālestriyaṃ naiva gacchet sādhakasattamaḥ |  
puṣpaṃgaṃdhaṃjalaṃ caiva svayamānīya pūjayet ||  
  
maithunaṃ tatkathālāpaṃ tadgoṣṭhiṃ parivarjayet |  
ṛtukālaṃ vinā cāpi gacchenna striyamādarāt ||   
  
purāṇaśravaṇe śraddhā vedavedārtha tatparaḥ |  
na rātrau bhojayed vidvān tāṃbūlaṃ parameśvara ||  
  
guruṇā yadyadādiṣṭaṃ tatsarvaṃ yatnataścaret |  
svajātakusumaṃ caiva hetu dravyaṃ ca bhairavaṃ ||  
  
spṛṣṭvārothā samāghrāya paṃcagavyena śuddhyati |  
raktavastraṃ na gṛhṇīyāddevībhaktiparāyaṇaḥ ||  
  
viṣṇutaṃtreṣu kalpāni tadanuṣṭhānameva ca |  
kāryaṃ vīrakathālāpaṃ na kuryādvīravaṃdanaṃ ||  
  
nityaśrāddhaṃ mayā śrāddhaṃ saṃdhyāvaṃdanameva ca |  
tīrthasnānaṃ pīṭhadeśagamanaṃ dharmatatparaḥ ||  
  
paśustu trividhaḥ proktaḥ krameṇa śṛṇu bhairava |  
adīkṣitaḥ kriyāhīno maṃtra taṃtra vivarjitaḥ ||  
  
mahāpaśuritikhyātaḥ sarvatoyaṃ vigarhitaḥ |  
dīkṣito niṃdako yastu dvitīyaḥ saprakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
ekākīyā na nirataḥ paśurityabhidhīyate |  
asyādhikāraḥ pūjāyā na gurutve kadācana ||  
  
pūrvasyanādhikārosti pūjādeśa gatāgatau |  
pūrvastu sarvakaulerhi vahiḥ kāryaḥ svadeśataḥ ||  
  
pūrvadarśanamātreṇa kuladarśanamācaret |  
brahmahatyādikaṃ pāpaṃ varaṃ satyaṃ na ca prabho ||  
  
pūrvadarśanamevātra satyaṃ satyaṃ vadāmyahaṃ |  
mamātmā sāpi deveśi vibhūrityapi sa prabho ||   
  
tathāpi tatra me śaṃkā jāyate tat padepade |  
varaṃ kula parityājyaṃ varaṃ svakulahiṃsanaṃ ||  
  
varaṃ svakulahānistu varaṃ svakulakuṭṭanaṃ |  
kāyena manasā vācā varaṃ svakulapātanaṃ ||  
  
na kūrvīta paśoḥ saṃgaṃ svamārgaṃ kṣayakāraṇāt |  
kulaśāstre dvayaṃ pāpaṃ gariṣṭhaṃ kulanāśanaṃ ||   
  
svakule mahatī niṃdā parayogāt kuleśvara |  
tasmādapi mahāpāpaṃ paśusaṃgāt prajāyate ||  
  
p. 64b)  
  
sarvathā tatra bhāvaudvaunaprakāśyo kuleśvara |  
sabhāvaścavibhāvaśca paśudveṣāt prajāyate ||  
  
daivācca jāyate vīrovīrāddaiva prajāyate |  
daive vīrena saṃdehaḥ sāmyamityabhidhīyate ||  
  
bhāvastu mānasodharmaḥ śābdaḥ sahikathaṃ bhavet |  
tasmādbhāvo na vaktavyo diṅmātraṃ samudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
yathekṣu rasamādhuryaṃ rasanairjñāyate prabho |  
tathā bhāvavibhāvastu manasā paribhāvyate ||  
  
śṛṇu yatnena deveśi rahasyāti rahasyakaṃ |  
vinā madyenamāṃsena puṃścalīsevanaṃ vinā ||  
  
na maṃtraḥ siddhamāpnoti caṃdrasaura kramārcitaṃ |  
alināpūritaṃ pātraṃ vanitāpūritaṃ mukhaṃ ||  
  
aliṃ valiṃvarāṃ rāmāṃ kinnasiddhyati bhūtale |  
satyametadvināyoṣitsaṃgaṃ maṃtraṃ na siddhyati ||  
  
saṃga eva hi kārtavyo maithunaṃ na kadācana |  
pūjanīyā sadāyoṣāmadbhāvakṛta niścayā ||  
  
tasmāttu maithunaṃ devakartavyaṃ mama sādhakaiḥ |  
ahaṃ tu jagatāṃ dhātrī jananījanmakāriṇī ||  
  
madbhāvapratiyaṃtrāyāṃ sāhameva suniścitaṃ |  
kartavyaṃ maithunaṃ naiva tasyā manavikāraṇaṃ ||  
  
mohādvā guruvodhyādvyā yadā tat kurute sudhīḥ |  
vīro vāpyathavā divya avudhyā narakaṃ vrajet ||  
  
gurupatnīṃ dvijapatnīṃ pitṛpatnīṃ prapūjayet |  
maithune narakaṃ yāvattāvat koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet ||  
  
ahaṃ ca roṣasaṃpanno nāśayāmitamīśvara |  
niraṃtaraṃ rogapīḍā jāyate tasya pāpinaḥ ||  
   
kadācit karmasaṃtāpaḥ kadācit karṇapīḍamaṃ |  
kadācidapivān yasyāt kadācinnavicarcikā ||  
  
anālokyaṃ ca vādhiryaṃ khaṃjatā kubjatā tathā |  
anyepi vividhā rogāḥ kuṣṭyādyāḥ prabhavaṃtihi ||  
  
cakṣunāśocchrutichedo nāśācchedastathaiva ca |  
pādacchedaḥ karacheda śirachedopi jāyate ||  
  
paśupīḍā rājapīḍā vahnipīḍā ca jāyate |  
kulaṃ tasyātra doṣeṇa mrīyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
ete te kathitā doṣāyoṣinmaithuna saṃbhavā |  
adhikāravihīnānāmadhikārayutaiścaret ||  
  
śiva uvāca |  
  
mahānmamaivasaṃdeho varddhate jagadīśvarī |  
mamānugrahato devi madvaktuṃ ca tvamarhati ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
ahameva paraṃ dhyānamahameva parāśrutiḥ |  
mattaḥ parataraṃ viśvaṃ na kiṃcidavalokyate ||  
  
p. 65a)  
  
ahameva jagatsarvaṃ jagadevāhamīśvara |  
madbhāvabhāvitānārī bhaveddetādṛśī śiva ||  
  
evaṃ jñāna viśiṣṭaḥ syādadhikārī bhavecchiva |  
brahmādika maheśo vā sarvadeva sadyo hi saḥ ||  
  
jāyamānasya vālasya mātṛyoniḥ svaliṃgayoḥ |  
saṃgharkeṇa vikāro hi na tayorjāyate kvacit ||  
  
sādhakasya tathā yasya matiḥ syādadhikāriṇī |  
sodhikārī bhavennityaṃ yāgādau sahayoṣitāṃ ||  
  
madbhāva pratipannāyāṃ matsvarūpāhameva sā |  
vikāraṃ na hi yoṣāyāṃ tasyāmarpita eva hi ||  
  
evaṃ yasya sthirābuddhiḥ svādhikārī na saṃśayaḥ |  
sādhakasya svadehe syāt yatsvarūpeṣṭadevatā ||  
  
tadvarṇasamatejobhiḥ pūrṇaṃ tu vanamaṇḍalaṃ |  
bhāvanābhisthirīkṛtya devatā dhyānatanmayaḥ ||  
  
yathāsvarūpavarṇādi ciṃtayedyatamānasaḥ |  
evaṃ jñāne samutpanne svacchadaṃ viharet pumān ||  
  
evaṃ yasya mamonāsti tasya pratinidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |  
kumāryāmeva kartavyaṃ na kṣaratyāṃ kadācana ||  
  
kumārī bhojanādeva kumārī bhojanādapi |  
kumārī ciṃtanādeva trailokyavijayī bhavet ||  
  
śṛṇu devi varārohe rahasya mahadadbhutaṃ |  
vinā pūjāṃ striyoyonausaṃgamet sādhakottamaḥ ||  
  
saptajanmadaridraḥ syānnarakekoṭikalpasaḥ |  
brahmahatyā surāpānastena gurvaṃ gaṇāgamaḥ ||  
  
evaṃ nānākṛto doṣo jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ |  
vīro vāpyathavā divyo na vuddhyā narakam vrajet ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau bhāvanirṇayo nāmāścaturddaśaḥ prakāśaḥ || 14 ||  
  
athādau satvādi guṇabhedāt nityādi vibhedamāha ||  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
dhanināṃ madhyamānāṃ ca daridrāṇāṃ gṛhīsināṃ |  
paradeśa sthitānāṃ ca kārāgehādivāsināṃ ||  
  
kāryādau vyāvṛtānāṃ ca yuktānāṃ sūtakādibhiḥ |  
kāryāṃge ca svabhāve cā vāmakānāṃ kṛpānidhe ||  
  
ṣaḍāmnāya rahasye na kathaṃ nityakriyā bhavet |  
lokalajjāvatāṃ vā dinacaryāṃ vada prabho ||  
  
śrīśiva uvāca |  
  
mahākālena yatproktaṃ yanmahāmāyayāśrutaṃ |  
rahasyātirahasyaṃ tat sarvataṃtreṣugopitaṃ ||  
  
p. 65b)  
  
āmnāyānāṃ rahasyaṃ tadāhnikaṃ procyate mayā |  
śṛṇvaṃ tu sarvebho devāḥ sādhakānāṃ prasiddhidaṃ ||  
  
tatra nityaṃ tridhā proktaṃ guṇatraya vibhedataḥ |  
adhikāravihīnaṃ cenmānasaṃjñānapūrvakaṃ ||  
  
svasthacittenayatinākṛtaṃ tacchuddhamucyate |  
tādṛśaṃ cedgṛhasthena nirdravyeṇātha vā kṛtiṃ ||  
  
ruglena pathikenāpi karāgṛhagatena vā |  
bhaktito cāpi tanmiśraṃ vāhyapūjādhikārataḥ ||  
  
śītādibhītyāvāvittaḥ saṃkṣayādalpakāryataḥ |  
stryāderniyogādgalitaṃ gṛhīṇomānasaṃmataṃ ||  
  
vāhyapūjādikaṃ yacca ekāṃte niyamena ca |  
bhaktyā kṛtaṃ gṛhasthena tacchuddhaṃ rājasaṃmataṃ ||  
  
pūjārthaṃ yadyā ca yitva śraddhābhaktividhāya vā |  
lokabhītyā devabhītyā yattadrājasamiśritaṃ ||   
  
pratāraṇārthaṃ lokānāṃ yācitaṃ devanāmataḥ |  
dravyaṃ kṛtaṃ tadduddeśagalitaṃ tat tu rājasaṃ ||  
  
vāmamārgaṃ samāśrityakaulaṃ dharmaṃ vicārya ca |  
anyadharmasya cādveṣāt kṛtaṃ śuddha tu tāmasaṃ ||  
  
kṛtaṃ yatkāmataḥ karma caihnikaṃ pāralaukikaṃ |  
vāmamārgaṃ samāśritya miśritaṃ tattunāmasaṃ ||  
  
jihvālobhena yatsvādyaṃ pānaṃ yat kāmatorataṃ |  
athavā māraṇādyarthaṃ galitaṃ tattutāmasaṃ ||  
  
śuddhasatvena mokṣaḥ syāt svargaḥ syānmiśrasatvataḥ |  
siddhirgalita satvāsyā daihikī ca manuṣyatā ||  
  
svargaḥ syādrājasācchuddhātkāmaḥ syānmiśrarājasāt |  
galigādrājasāttiryagyonāvavi sukhaṃ bhavet ||  
  
sātvikā tāmasāddevayonitvaṃ prāpnuyānnaraḥ |  
miśratāmasatoduḥkhīnārakī vāddhytāmasāt ||  
  
karmapaṃcavidhaṃ proktaṃ paṃcadhā muktidāyakaṃ |  
prasarpaṇamupādānamījyādhyāyastathādyutiḥ ||  
  
saṃmārjano palepādi saṃskāro devamaṃdire |  
bhavārjanaṃ sarpaṇaṃ syāddevasālokyakārakaṃ ||   
  
pūjāsādhanasāmagryāmelanaṃ bhaktasevanaṃ |  
tatprītiḥ syādupādānaṃ devatārūpadāyakaṃ ||  
  
pīṭhapūjanapūrvaṃ yat ṣoḍaśādyupacārakaiḥ |  
sa yogo liṃgadehasyanāśakaḥ kālayogakṛt ||  
  
atha prātaḥ kṛtyaḥ yathā ||  
  
brāhmyānmuhūrtādvakṣyāmi sādhakasya hitaṃ paraṃ |  
kālikāyā maheśāni śayyāyāṃ guruciṃtanaṃ ||  
  
suṃdaryāstu maheśāni rātrivāsaṃ parityajet |  
chinnāyādevaṃ deveśi saṃyogī bhūyasaṃsmaret ||  
  
p. 66a)  
  
tārāyāṃ devadeveśi śaktyā sahaguruṃ smaret |  
guruṃ smṛtvā kuṇḍalinīṃ samyagyogena yojayet ||  
  
sādhakaḥ prātarutthāya kulavṛkṣaṃ praṇamya ca |  
mūlādi brahmaraṃdhrāṃtaṃ kulaṃ dhyātvā guruṃ smaret ||  
  
tataḥ samastake ciṃtyaṃ sahasradalapadmakaṃ |  
karpūrābhaṃ smerettatra śrīguruṃ nijarūpiṇaṃ ||  
  
iti śrīgurorvidyamānatveśāṃtatvenyaset ||  
  
suprasannaṃ lasadbhūṣāmaṇḍitaṃ śvetacaṃdanaṃ |  
varābhaya jñānamudrā pustakairvyāvṛtai karaiḥ ||  
  
yuktaṃ śvetāṃvaraṃ śāṃtaṃ śvetapuṣpavibhūṣitaṃ |  
vāmāṃkagatayaḥ śaktyā liṃgitaṃ raṇavarṇayā ||  
  
raktavastrābharaṇa vā raktacaṃdanamālyayā |  
vāme līlākamalayāliṃgityā dakṣiṇena ca ||  
  
dhyāyedaṃ tanmukhaṃ śāṃtaṃ śrīguraṃ śivarūpiṇaṃ |  
tatpāda padmayugalaṃ srutapīyūṣadhārayā ||  
  
abhiṣiktaṃ svasya dehamevaṃ śiṣyo viciṃtayet |  
arcayed gaṃdhapuṣpādyairvādyasthairmānasaistu vā ||  
  
śrīgurormānasayajanamāha |  
  
laṃ haṃ yaṃ raṃ vamuccārya tattadbhūtātmanaḥ padāt |  
samarpayāmi saṃprocya namoṃtomānasārcane ||  
  
śaṃvaiśaktyātmane procya tāṃbūlaṃ caiva pūrvavat |  
kaniṣṭhā tarjanī madhyānāmāścāṃguṣṭhayogataḥ ||  
  
sarvāsīyojanānmudrā kramāt paṃcavidhāsmṛtā |  
aimuktā yoginaṃ mudrāṃ dairśayettāṃvurārpaṇe ||  
  
nāmabhistasya saṃketaḥ saṃsiddhairgurukīrtakaiḥ |  
praṇamyatthaṃ hṛnmanunā bhāvayettallayaṃ hṛdi ||  
  
atha strīgurutve viśeṣadhyānamāha ||  
  
aruṇāmaruṇākalpāṃ karuṇāpūrṇalocanā |  
varābhayakarāśāṃtāṃ smarāmi mama gauravī ||  
  
nijanātha kareśaśvannija vāmakalevarāṃ |  
sa padmakarayāśaśvallīlāṃdolitalocanāṃ ||  
  
atha vīrāṇāṃ viśeṣo yathā ||  
  
mahācīna guruṃ dhyātvā svaguruṃ saṃsmarettataḥ |  
paṃcopacāraiḥ saṃpūjya vīradravya krameṇa tu ||  
  
atha kulagurumāha ||  
  
prahlādānaṃdanāthākhyaṃ sanakānaṃdameva ca |  
kumārānaṃdanāthaṃ ca vaśiṣṭānaṃdanāthakaṃ ||  
  
krodhānaṃdaṃ sukhānaṃdaṃ dhyānānaṃdaṃ tataḥ paraṃ |   
vodhānaṃda sukānaṃdī dhyāyet kulamukhopari ||  
  
atha mahārasarasollāsahṛdayāghūrṇalocanāḥ ||  
  
p. 66b)  
  
kulāliṃga na saṃbhinnāścūrṇitāśeṣatāmasāḥ |  
kulaśiṣyaiḥ parivṛtāḥ pūrṇāṃtaḥ karaṇodyatāḥ ||  
  
varābhayayutāḥ sarve kulataṃtrārthavādinaḥ ||  
  
atha śrīgurordhyānam ||  
  
nīlāṃvaraṃ nīlavilepayuktaṃ śaṃkhādibhūṣitatanuṃ muditaṃ trinetram ||   
vāmāṃgapīṭhasthitanīlaśaktirvadāmivīraṃ karuṇānidhānaṃ ||  
  
vīraṃ dhyātvā mahādevī vīramālāṃ japedbudhaḥ |  
aṣṭottara sahasraṃ ca vāmahaste samarpayet ||  
  
atha gurupādukāmāha ||  
  
athavā vāgbhavaṃ māyāṃ lakṣmībījaṃ samuddharet |  
hasakhaphreṃ tathā naṃdabhairavākhyaṃ sahakhaphreṃ ||  
  
gurunāma tathā tathāśaktirnāma śrīpādukāṃ smaret ||  
  
daśadhā saptadhā vāpi tridhā vā prajapetsudhīḥ |  
japaṃ samarpayet paścāt śrīgurordakṣiṇekare ||  
  
akhaṇḍamaṇḍalākāraṃ vyāptaṃ yena carācaraṃ |  
tatpadaṃ darśitaṃ yena tasmai śrīguravenamaḥ ||  
  
ajñānatimirāṃdhasya jñānāṃjanaśalākayā |  
cakṣurunmīlitaṃ yena tasmai śrīguravenamaḥ ||  
  
tatastu mūlādhārādi brahmaraṃdhrāṃtamudyate |  
ādhāraskaṃdamityāhurgudameḍhrasyamadhyagaḥ ||  
  
mṛdvāsane samāsīnaḥ sarvaciṃtā vivarjitaḥ |  
caturasraṃ caturyaṃtraṃ vasāṃtaṃ svarṇavarṇakaṃ ||  
  
trikoṇavṛtta tanmadhye icchājñāna kriyātmakaṃ |  
sūryakoṭi pratīkāśāṃ caṃdrakoṭiḥ ṣuśītalāṃ ||  
  
sārddha trivalayākārāṃ sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitāṃ |  
madhye svayaṃbhuliṃgaṃ tu koṭisūryaḥ samaprabhaṃ ||  
  
tadūrddhve kāmavījaṃ tu kalayā iṃdunāyakaṃ |  
tadūrddhve tu śikhākārāṃ kuṇḍaliṃ brahmavigrahāṃ ||  
  
tejodaṇḍaṃ suṣumṇāṃtaḥ sahasraravisannibhaṃ |  
tadātmakaṃ mūlamaṃtraṃ dhyātvā tattejasāvṛtaṃ ||  
  
svaśarīraṃ viciṃtyeti prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ caret |  
mūlamaṃtreṇa maṃtrasya ṛṣyādinyā samācaret ||  
  
aṃganyā saṃvidhāyātha hṛdidevaṃ viciṃtayet |  
mānasairupacāraiśca pūjayitvā manuṃ japet ||  
  
yathāśaktyātha devāyataṃ japaṃ ca samarpayet ||  
  
atha śyāmāyā viśeṣamāha ||  
  
dhyātvā hṛdamvuje kālīṃ dhyānoktāṃ pūjayettataḥ |  
mānasairupacāraiśca pūjayitvā manuṃ japet ||  
  
p. 67a)  
  
gaṃdhādibhiśca gāyatrīmaṣṭāviṃśati saṃkhyakāṃ |  
prajapeddaśasaṃkhyāṃ vā śrūyatāṃtāṃ ca bhairavī ||  
  
kāmo'lākṣinādāṃto dakṣiṇāṃgeyutātataḥ |  
vidmahe kūrcavījaṃ ca cāmuṇḍau ṅeṃyutā tataḥ ||  
  
dhīmahīti vadettannaḥ kālī pracodayāt tataḥ |  
gāyatryeṣāmayā proktā sarvataṃtreṣu gopitā ||  
  
yāṃ vinā sa kalāvidyā na siddhyaṃti kadācana ||  
  
atha japāvidhirucyate ||  
  
vīrahaṃsamayāvidyā saṃkalpaṃ kārayedbudhaḥ |  
haṃsākhyā sādhanaṃ vakṣye maṃtrāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā ||  
  
yasya vijñānamātreṇa sarvajño bhuvijāyate |  
haṃsātmikāṃ bhagavatīṃ jīvo jayati sarvadā ||  
  
asyāḥ smaraṇamātreṇa jīvanmukto bhavennaraḥ |  
asya haṃsasya deveśi nigamāgamapakṣakau ||  
  
agnisomau tathā vāpi pakṣau tāraḥ śiro bhavet |  
viṃdu trayaṃ śikhā netre mukhe nāda pratiṣṭhitaḥ ||  
  
śivaśaktipadadvaṃdvaṃ kālāgnī yārśvayugmakaṃ |  
ayaṃ paramahaṃsastu sarvavyāpī prakāśavān ||  
  
hakāreṇa vahiryāti sakāreṇa viśet punaḥ |  
sayāḥ saṃvodhamātreṇa jīvanmukto bhavennaraḥ ||  
  
prāṇāyāma prabhāvena jīvanmuktastu jāyate |  
ṛṣirhaṃso'vyaktapūrvāgāyatrī cheda ucyate ||  
  
devatā paramādistuhaṃsohaṃ bījamucyate |  
saśaktiḥ kīlakaṃ sohaṃ praṇavastatvameva hi ||  
  
udāttasvara ityevaṃ manorasya prakīrtitaḥ |  
mokṣā'rthe viniyogaḥ syādevaṃ kuryāt sadānaraḥ ||  
  
sūryātmanevahṛddevisomātmane śirastathā |  
niraṃjanaṃ śikhājyotirnirābhāsā tathā priye ||  
  
avyaktaṃ netrayornyasya anaṃtostraphaḍaṃ yajet |  
evaṃ nyāsavidhiṃ kṛtvā gaṇeśādau samarpayet ||  
  
ṣaṣṭiśvāsairbhavet prāṇaḥ ṣaṭprāṇānāḍikāmatā |  
ṣaṣṭhināḍyāhyahorātraṃ japasaṃkhyā japamanoḥ ||  
  
ekaviṃśati sāhasraṃ ṣaṭśatādikameva ca |  
prajapet pratyahaṃ jīvo brahmānaṃdamayīṃ parāṃ ||  
  
utpattirjapa āraṃbhomṛtirasya nivedanaṃ |  
vinā japena satataṃ jape bhavati sarvadā ||  
  
evaṃ japastu vijñāto gaṇeśādau nivedayet |  
ṣaṭśatāni gaṇeśasya ṣaṭsahasraṃ prajāyate ||  
  
ṣaṭsahasraṃ gadāpāṇeḥ ṣaṭsahasraṃ pinākinaḥ |  
sahasraṃ ātmane caiva sahasraṃ paramātmane ||  
  
p. 67b)  
  
sahasraṃ purave caiva saṃkalpoyaṃ yathā vidhi |  
raktavarṇe gaṇeśaṃ ca mūlādhāre caturddale ||  
  
vādiveda samāyukte ṣaṭśataṃ ca samarpayet |  
svādhiṣṭhānaṃ vidrumābhaṃ ṣaṭkoṇaṃ vādi ṣaṭkakaṃ ||  
  
sāvitryā ca samāyukte brahmaṇe ca samarpayet |  
vidyuṃtpuṃjaprabhābhaṃ ca dalaṃbhādi daśākṣaraṃ ||  
  
lakṣmīnārāyaṇau vaṃde ṣaṭsahasraṃ nivedayet |  
mahānīla prabhe caivakādi dvādaśapatrake ||  
  
umāmaheśvarau vaṃde ṣaṭsahasraṃ nivedayet |  
viśuddhe dhūmravarṇe ca kalāpātre svarānvite ||  
  
prāṇaśaktyātmakau vaṃde sahasraṃ ca samarpayet |  
ājñāyāṃ vidyudābhāyāṃ śubhau dakṣau niyojīte ||  
  
paramātmani parāśaktau sahasraṃ samarpayet |  
stutvā praṇamya devājñāṃ ślokairebhiśca prārthayet ||  
  
śivādikasthalebhāvamūhaṃ sveṣṭasya vācayet ||  
  
trailokya caitanyamayādi daivaśrīśaṃkaratvaccaraṇājñayaiva |  
prātaḥ samutthāya tava priyārthaṃ saṃsārayātrā manuvartayiṣye ||  
  
saṃsārayātrā manuvartamānaṃ tvadājñayā śaṃkaradevadeva |  
sparddhāti ca skārakalipramādābhayānimāṃmābhibhavaṃ tu nātha ||  
  
iti saṃprārthya deveśamājñāmādāya tasya tu |  
prārthayitvādharāṃ śvāsayuktaṃ pādaṃ nidhāpayet ||  
  
samudramekhale devi parvatastanamaṇḍale |  
viṣṇupatnī namastubhyaṃ pādasparśaṃ kṣamasvame ||  
  
prātaḥkṛtyama kṛtvā tu yo devīṃ bhaktitorcayet |  
pūjā ca viphalā tasya śaucahīnā yathā kriyā ||  
  
atha śaucavidhiḥ ||  
  
tato gṛhādvahiryāmyāṃ nair-ṛtīṃ vā diśaṃ vrajet |  
pade padesmaredastraṃ dūreyāyāddvijālayāt ||  
  
atītyavāṇamātrāṃ tu bhuvaṃ grāmādvilokya ca |  
noṣaṇena śmaśāne ca tripathe vā catuṣpathe ||  
  
gokule rājamārge vā vane copavane tathā |  
devatā yatane varjyaṃ goradhyāyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
varcco mūtrādikaṃ varjyaṃ yasmādvai kṛttikāsutaṃ |  
daśahastaṃ parityājya mūtraṃ kuryājjalāśayāt ||  
  
catvāriṃśat purīṣe tu tīrthe nadyāṃ caturguṇaṃ |  
karṇe kṛtvā pavitraṃ ca viṇmūtraṃ kārayet tadā ||  
  
ubhe mūtrapūrīṣe ca divākuryādudaṅmukhaḥ |  
rātrau ca dakṣiṇe kuryādube saṃdhye yathā divā ||  
  
chāyāyāmaṃdhakāre vā rātrā vahani vādvijāḥ |  
yathā samanmukhaḥ kuryāt prāṇavādhabhayeṣu ca ||  
  
p. 68a)  
  
uttiṣṭhaṃ vṛṣayodevāgaṃdharvāyakṣarākṣasāḥ |  
paritastyajyatāṃ sthānaṃ viṇmūtrotsarjanāyame ||  
  
anena manunāloṣṭha tṛṇairudvāsya devatāḥ |  
kuryān malacyutiṃ tatra vā sasākaṃ praveṣṭya ca ||  
  
piṃḍāloko na kartavyastathākāśa nīrīkṣaṇaṃ |  
samyak vā vaśyakaṃ kṛtvā vāyuṃ kāṣṭhenamṛjya ca ||  
  
loṣṭena vātha vāmṛjyanāśmanāmṛjyate gudaṃ |  
punaḥ śaucaṃ prakartavyaṃ mṛdāmalakamātrayā ||  
  
dvitīyā ca tṛtīyāyātadarddhārdvā prakīrtitāḥ |  
śucideśāttu saṃgrāhyāḥ śarkarāśmādi varjitāḥ ||  
  
vipre gaurāmṛdaḥ proktāḥ kṣatreraktāstathoditāḥ |  
vaiśyasya haritāḥ proktāḥ kṛṣṇā strīśūdrayostathā ||  
  
yasmindeśe tu yattoyaṃ yādṛkīmṛttikā bhavet |  
saiva tatra praśastāsyāttayāśaucaṃ vidhīyate ||  
  
ekaliṃge gude saptadaśa vāmakare tathā |  
ubhayoḥ saptadātavyāstisroṃ'ghryoścāpi mṛttikāḥ ||  
  
mūtrotsarge vāmahasteliṃge paṃcaiva mṛttikā |  
trikāradvitaye caikāpādayorathavā caret ||  
  
gaṃdhalepa kṣayakaraṃ manoglāniharaṃ paraṃ |  
kuryādvādaśa gaṃḍūṣāt pūrīṣotsarjanottaraṃ ||  
  
mūtratyāge tu catura ācamya tristaraḥ paraṃ |  
etacchauvaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ dviguṇa brahmacāriṇāṃ ||  
  
triguṇaṃ vāṇaprasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ ca caturguṇaṃ |  
divāśaucasya rātryarddhaṃ svasya śaucasya sarvadā ||  
  
tadarddhaṃ rujimārgasthastrī śūdrāṇāṃ tadarddhakaṃ |  
śaucaṃ kṛtvā tato mṛdbhistṛbhirjapyairviśodhayet ||  
  
śaucakarma vihīnasya sakalā niṣphalāḥ kriyā ||  
  
atha daṃtadhāvanavidhiḥ ||  
  
tataḥ samāhareddaṃtadhāvanaṃ vihitaidhasāṃ |  
te cāpāmārgavadarīnirguṇḍī vilvavāsakāḥ ||  
  
aśokacaṃpakaḥ plakṣaparṇajaṃvudhavaśruvaḥ |  
arkanyagrodhakhadirakaraṃjakakubhādikaṃ ||  
  
śīrṣeśauryaṃ vaṭe dīptiḥ kadaṃve vijayīraṇe |  
plakṣe sarvārthasiddhiḥ syādvadaryāṃ madhurasvaraḥ ||  
  
khadiremukhasaugaṃdhyaṃ vailvena vipulaṃ dhanaṃ |  
apāmārge dhṛtirmedhā prajñākāṃtiryaśastathā ||  
  
āyuḥ śīlaṃ tathā lakṣmīḥ saubhāgyaṃ copajāyate |  
arkeṇahanyate rogānarthalābhāśca jāyate ||   
  
audumbare vāgviśuddhiścaṃpakasyādṛṭa śrutiḥ |  
jātī vakulamaṃdāraiḥ svapnaṃ tasya na paśyati ||  
  
p. 68b)  
  
sarvakaṃṭakinaḥ puṇyāḥ kṣīriṇastu yaśaḥsvina |  
anyeṣāṃ vṛkṣajātīnāṃ na bhakṣeddaṃtadhāvanaṃ ||  
  
palāśavakulaṃkāśaṃ bhakṣayedyastu sāsapaṃ |  
tāvadbhavati cāṇḍāloyāvadgāvaṃ na paśyati ||  
  
sphāṭikaṃ vā tiriktaṃ ca hīnaṃ catvagvivarjitaṃ |  
arddhadagdhaṃ pathibhraṣṭaṃ śmaśānasthaṃ tathaiva ca ||  
  
ucchicchaviṣṭā sūtradilagnaṃ yatnāt parityajet |  
kanīnyagra samasthaulya praguṇaṃ dvādaśāṃgulaṃ ||  
  
dvādaśāṃgula viprāṇāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ navāṃgulaṃ |  
aṣṭāṃgulaṃ ca vaiśyānāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ ca ṣaḍaṃgulaṃ ||  
  
caturaṃgulamānaṃ tu nārīṇāṃ vidhirucyate |  
cūrṇitāgraṃ tvacāyuktaṃ gṛhṇīyān manunānunā ||  
  
āyurvalaṃ yaśovarccaḥ prajāpaśuvastūni ca |  
brahmaprajñāṃ ca medhāṃ ca tanno dehi vanaspate ||  
  
prāṅmukhodaṅmukho bhūtvā upaviśya sukhāsane |  
bhakṣayen mukhaśuddhyarthaṃ yathoktaṃ taṃtadhāvanaṃ ||  
  
klīmuktvā kāmadevāya sarvajanapriyāya ca |  
namoṃtastithi varṇoyaṃ maṃtrodaṃtaviśodhane ||  
  
prakṣālpaṃ daṃtakāṣṭaṃ ca śuddhadeśe purastyajet |  
vaktraṃ mūlānunānityaṃ kṣālayet siddhihetave ||  
  
pratipaddaśe ṣaṣṭhīṣu navamyarkadinaṃ tathā |  
caṃdrasūryoparāge ca na kuryāddaṃtadhāvanaṃ ||  
  
abhāvedaṃtakāṣṭasya niṣiddhāyāṃ tithau tathā |   
apāṃ dvādaśa gaṃḍūṣaiḥ kurvīta mukhaśodhanaṃ ||  
  
atha pūjāhomakarmasiddhayesnānamucyate ||  
  
snānapūrvāḥ kriyāḥ sarvāḥ snānaṃ ca daivate bhavet |  
prātaḥkāle ca madhyāhne sāyāhne stotrapāṭhake ||  
  
yadā yadā manoglānistadaiva snānamācaret |  
vidyoccāraṃ tu yaḥ yakuryādasnātaḥ kṛtabhojanaḥ ||  
  
tasya vidyā bhavennaṣṭā rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet |  
aśuciḥ sanmaheśāni vidyoccāraṃ tu yaścaret ||  
  
tasya nāśo bhaveddevi vidyādagdhāṃ bhaveddhruvam |  
snānakālācca saṃproktāḥ snānabhedā chṛṇu priye ||  
  
snānaṃ paṃcavidhaṃ proktaṃ yena devīmayo bhavet |  
vāruṇe nābhasaṃ caiva tṛtīyaṃ bhasmajaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
caturthaṃ taijasaṃ devī paṃcamaṃ daivataṃ bhavet |  
brahmāviṣṇuśca rudraśca īśvaraśca sadāśivaḥ ||  
  
p. 69a)  
  
ete paṃcamahāsatvāḥ paṃcasnāne vyavasthitāḥ |  
parāvaṃtadatītāva tatparā tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
citpadātadatītāva paṃcamī parikīrtitāḥ |  
vāruṇaṃ dvividhaṃ proktaṃ vaidikaṃ tāṃtrikaṃ tathā ||  
  
svaśākhokta vidhānena vaidikaṃ snānamīritaṃ |  
svasvakalpoktavidhinā tāṃtrikaṃ snānamācaret ||  
  
śaṃkunāstrābhi japtena śucisthānāttumṛttikāṃ |  
gṛhītvāstreṇa saṃsiṃcyayā yājjalaniketanaṃ ||  
  
tatrādau jalakūlaṃ tu kṣālayedastravāriṇā |  
mṛdaṃ kṛtvā dvidhā tatra ekabhāgopagaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
nidhāyagomayaṃ darbhāṃstilāṃścāpyabhimaṃtritān |  
mṛttikāgomayābhyāṃ ca kardyataṃ snānamācaret ||  
  
vahiruddhṛtatoyenamalaḥ snānaṃ tataḥ paraṃ |  
vidhāya vaidikaṃ snānaṃ tadaṃgaṃtarpaṇaṃ tathā ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmite vatsaḥ snānaṃ kulamukhāvahaṃ |  
kṛṣṇāraktāharirnīlā vividhā mamamūrtayaḥ ||  
  
tatastāṃtrikasnānasya vidhirastreṇamṛttikāṃ |  
samādāyāstramaṃtreṇa maṃtrayitvā tṛṇādikaṃ ||  
  
śikhāmaṃtreṇāpahṛtya trirmūlenābhi maṃtrayet |  
mūrddhādi pādaparyaṃtaṃ vilipya praṇayejjalaṃ ||  
  
ādhāraḥ sarvabhūtasya viṣṇoratulatejasaḥ |  
tadrūpāśca tato jātāstā āpaḥ praṇamāmyahaṃ ||  
  
saṃmukhīṃkaraṇaṃ mudrāṃ vadhvā prāṇaṃ niruṃdhya ca |  
nimajya tūṣṇī mutthāya nābhimātre jalesthitaḥ ||   
  
ācāṃtaḥ kuladravyeṇa sadarbhaḥ kulapuṣpakaṃ |  
kulapātraḥ sa darbhaṃ ca sa tilaṃ sa jalaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
trividhaṃ kuladarbho hi coditaḥ kālaśaṃtunā |  
kathyate tatra deveśi gopanīyā kuleśvarī ||  
  
kulacakroparigatāḥ kuladarbhāḥ mukheṣṭadā |  
trayodarbhāḥ samuddiṣṭāḥ suvarṇaiḥ rajataiḥ kuśaiḥ ||  
  
tatra śākte dvayaṃ cānyamanyeṣāṃ tu trayo matāḥ |  
suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ caiva japapūjādi karmasu ||  
  
karṣārddhakarṣamātraṃ vā pavitrāya prakalpayet |  
kuśakāryakaraṃ proktaṃ na tu vanyakuśāḥ kuśāḥ ||  
  
tarjanyā rajataṃ dhāryaṃ svarṇaṃ dhāryamanāmayā |  
eṣa eva kuśaḥ proktoradarbhovarasaṃbhavaḥ ||  
  
p. 69b)  
  
kūrcāṇāṃ paṃcakaṃ likhyaparitovartamekhalāṃ |  
śūlaṃ kapālamālikhya brahmakūrcaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
etasyādhāraṇādevavāṃchā kāryamavāpnuyāt |  
tridhādarbhaḥ prakathitaḥ kālikādarbhavartmani ||  
  
gopanīyamidaṃ bhadre sārāt sārataraṃ mahat |  
kapālaṃ ca tathā khaḍgaṃ strīvījāni ca paṃca ca ||  
  
anāmāyāmidaṃ dhāryaṃ svarṇavarṇaṃ śubhāvahaṃ |  
kūrcādyakālikātārā saptatārādyameva ca ||  
  
sarvavījādyarūpaṃ ca kuladarbhaṃ ca dhārayet |  
vidyāśrīkīrtijananaṃ śāṃtidaṃ sarvasiddhidaṃ ||  
  
savasauṃdaryadaṃ bhadre vījāsiddhiḥ pradarśakaṃ |  
gṛhītvā kuladevasya prītaye snānamācaret ||  
  
tāṃtrikaṃsnāna saṃkalpaṃ māsollekhādipūrvakaṃ |  
kṛtasaṃkalpa evāsau kulacakraṃ jale nyaset ||  
  
kṛtvātha mūlamaṃtreṇa prāṇāyāma trayaṃ caret |  
vinyasya ca ṣaḍaṃgāni kalpayet tirthamagrataḥ ||  
  
caturasre hastamātretajjale parikalpite |  
brahmāṇḍodaratīrthāṇikaraiḥ spṛṣṭāniterave ||  
  
tena satyena deveśa tīrthaṃ dehi divākara |  
iti sūryaṃ prārthayitvā kromityaṃkuśamudrayā ||  
  
aṃkuśamudrā yathā ||  
  
dakṣamuṣṭiṃvidhāyātha tarjanyaṃ kuśarūpiṇī |  
aṃkuśākhyā mahāmudrā trailokyākarṣaṇa kṣamā ||  
  
mitvārkamaṇḍalaṃ tasyāttīrthānyā vāhayediha |  
gaṃge ca yamune caiva godāvarī sarasvatī ||  
  
narmadesiṃdhukāverī jale'sminsannidhiṃ kuru |  
eva muktvā tu tīrthāni tasmin toye niyojayet ||  
  
mūlamaṃtreṇātha tīrthaḥ śaktistatra samāhvayet |  
arkasya maṇḍalaṃ dhyātvā tanmaṃtreṇa ca pūjayet ||  
  
sarvānaṃdamayīmaśeṣaduritarddhvaṃ sāmṛgāṃka prabhāṃ   
tryakṣāmūrddhvakaradvayenadadhaṃtīpāśaṃ sṛṇī vā mataḥ ||  
aṃtaścāmṛtapūrṇahemakalaśaṃ muktākṣamālāṃvarāṃ   
gaṃgāsiṃdhusaridvarādisahitāṃ śrītīrthaśaktiṃ bhaje ||  
  
hrā& hrī& hrū& hrai& hrau& hraḥ ||  
  
iti sarvānaṃdamayeparaṃ ||  
  
tīrthaśakti tathā hiliyugaṃ vahnigehini |  
ekaviṃśākṣaraḥ proktastīrthaśaktermahāmanuḥ ||  
  
p. 70a)  
  
tajjalaṃgāṃgamaṃtreṇa maṃtrayedaṣṭavārakaṃ |  
tāro namo bhagavati bhūyādaṃ vetatoṃvike ||  
  
aṃvālike mahāmālinyehyehi bhagavatpatha |  
aśeṣatīrthālavālemāyā śrīvījamuccaret ||  
  
śivajaṭādhirūḍhe ca gaṃgegaṃgāmbike dviṭhaḥ |  
gaṃgāvidyeyamākhyātā tripaṃcāśadbhirakṣaraiḥ ||  
  
vāme tu gaṃgāmaṃtradhyānayorviśeṣaḥ |  
tāro namo bhagavati vāgbhavaṃ ca hilidvayaṃ ||  
  
hilidvayaṃ paṃcagaṃge māṃ pāvayadvitayaṃ vadet |  
svāhāṃtastārakāvarṇo manuḥ pāpapraṇāśanaḥ ||  
  
dhyānaṃ ||  
  
raktāṃvarāṃ raktavarṇāṃ śūlakuṃbhavarābhayān |  
karaiḥ saṃdadhatīsmegraṃ kacchapasthāṃ surādibhiḥ ||  
  
tadrūpābhiḥ sapāyasya nāśāyamunisevitaṃ |  
bhuvaneśyā samāloḍyāmṛtīkṛtya sudhāṇunā ||  
  
kavacenāvaguṇṭhyātha saṃrakṣāstreṇa maṃtravit |  
mūlena devatāṃ tatra sāṃgāṃ sāvaraṇāṃ tathā ||  
  
samāvāṣka jaledhyātvā tatpādadvayanirgataṃ |  
dhyātvā tīrthaṃ smaran mūlamaṃtrī snāyājjalairbhṛśaḥ ||  
  
hṛdidevaṃ smaret paścāt siṃcettu kuṃ kuṃbhamudrayā ||  
  
kuṃbhamudrāyathā ||  
  
dakṣāṃguṣṭhe parāṃguṣṭhe kṣiptvā hastadvayena tu |  
sāvakāśā caika muṣṭirmudreyaṃ kuṃbhasaṃjñitā ||  
  
tribhiḥ ślokairmūlamaṃtratāravaṃvījapūrvakaiḥ |  
simṛkṣo nikhilaṃ viśvaṃ muhuḥ śukraṃ prajāyate ||  
  
mātaraḥ sarvabhūtānāmāpodevyaḥ punaṃtumāṃ |  
alakṣmīmalarūpāyā sarvabhūteṣu saṃsthitāḥ ||  
  
kṣālayaṃ tu nijaḥ sparśādāyo devyaḥ punaṃ tu māṃ |  
yanmekeśeṣu daurbhāgyaṃ sīmaṃteyaccamūrddhani ||  
  
lalāṭe karṇayorakṣṇorāpastaṃghnaṃtuvo namaḥ |  
tataḥ svāhāṃta mūlena trirā ca manamācaret ||  
  
tridhā devaṃ ca saṃtarpya toyamadhyāttato vrajet |  
dhautaṃ vastrayugaṃ dhṛtvā prakṣālyānu karau tathā ||   
  
mṛdābhistatra ācāmedeṣa snānavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |  
maṃtrasnānaṃ prakartavyaṃ śītayordeśa kālayoḥ ||  
  
toyābhāve gate durge kārya svāsthye ca vārddhake |  
toyābhāve ca yat kāryaṃ durge kāle ca śītataḥ ||  
  
gamane kṣipra siddhyarthaṃ gurukāryeṣva taṃdritaḥ |  
prāptāpadyatha viprendra niśābhāge tathā mune ||  
  
prakṣālyapādā vācamya proddhṛtena tu vāriṇā |  
sthānaṃ daśadiśaḥ prāgvat saṃśodhyopaviśet tataḥ ||  
  
p. 70b)   
  
jalaṃ hastatalenyasya kramānprāsāṃstataścaret |  
mātṛkādīṃstathā mūlemaṃtranyāsā na śeṣataḥ ||  
  
nyāsāṃ te saṃspṛśettoyaṃ maṃtrasnānamidaṃ varaṃ |  
devalādudakasnānāt saṃskāra parivarjitāt ||  
  
prabhāsādiṣu tīrtheṣu yatphalaṃ snātakasya tu |  
jñeyaṃ daśaguṇaṃ tasmānmaṃtrasnānasya niścayāt ||  
  
atha mānasasnānaṃ ||  
  
manasā mūlamaṃtreṇa prāṇāyāmapurassaraṃ |  
kūrvīta mānasaṃ snānaṃ dṛṣṭatīrtheṣu bhāvanāt ||  
  
atha taijasasnānaṃ ||  
  
taijasaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yena siddhyaṃti siddhayaḥ |  
gurudaivatamaṃtrāṇāmaikyaṃ saṃbhāvayeddhiyā ||  
  
gurutejo maṃtratejo devatāyāstathaiva ca |  
ekīkṛtyā tricaitanyaṃtanmūrtiṃ parikalpayet ||  
  
hṛdaye devatāsthānaṃ kaṇṭhe caiva manurmataḥ |  
sahasrāre gururproktāstri caitanyaṃ vibhāvayet ||  
  
tāṃ mūrtiṃ svasyadehe tu yathāsvā vayavottamāṃ |  
saṃbhāvayenmaheśāni daivataddarśanaṃpradaṃ ||  
  
taijasaṃgaditaṃ devidaivataṃ śṛṇu pārvati ||  
  
atha daivataṃsnānaṃ ||  
  
mūlādhāraṃ samārabhya virātaṃ parameśvarī |  
devatāṃ bhāvayeddevi svamukhe tanmukhaṃ śive ||  
  
tasyāḥ sarvāṃśakaṃ devi svadehesthānayogataḥ |  
dvāradeśa maheśāni gaṃgā ca yamunā tathā ||  
  
svadehe bhāvitāyāṃ tu gaṃgayā kiṃ phalaṃ bhavet ||  
  
iḍānāmanāḍīsthitā vāmabhāge tannordakṣiṇe piṃgalānāmanāḍī |  
tayoḥ pṛṣṭhavaṃśaṃ samāśritya madhye suṣumṇā sthitā brahmaraṃdhraṃ tu   
yāvat ||  
  
iḍā gaṃgeti vikhyātā suṣumṇā yamunā nadī |  
sarasvatī piṃgalā syāt prayāgaṃ dehamadhyagaṃ ||  
  
dehajñānaṃ vinā devī vāhyasnānena kiṃ phalaṃ |  
gurupaṃktiṃ sahasrāre aṃgāni bhrūvibhāvayet ||  
  
kaṇṭhamūlāṃtakaṃ devi sarvāvaraṇadevatāḥ |  
bhāvayed yatnato devī daivatasnānamīritaṃ ||  
  
anena snānayogena kiṃ tadyannakaresthitaṃ |  
snānapūrvāḥ kriyāḥ sarvāḥ śuddhāṃ siddhiṃ prayāṃti ca ||  
  
tasmāt snānaṃ purākuryāddeṣvekaṃ dehaśaktitaḥ |  
tatastu tilakaṃ kuryādvarṇajaṃ daivatasya ca ||  
  
brāhmaṇasyorddhvapuṇḍraṃ syāt kṣatriyasya tripuṇḍrakaṃ |  
arddhacaṃdraṃ tu vaiśyasya śūdrāṇāṃ vartulā kṛtiṃ ||  
  
p. 71a)  
  
ūrddhvapuṇḍraṃ mṛdā kuryāt tripuṇḍraṃ cāpi bhasmanā |  
keśareṇa ca kastūryā śeṣaṃ śītaṃ yathā ruci ||  
  
vaiṣṇavasyorddhvapuṇḍraṃ syāt tripuṇḍraṃ śivasevinaḥ |  
arddhacaṃdrogaṇeśasya devībhaktasya vartulaṃ ||  
  
nārāyaṇa paro yastu caṃdanasya triśūlakaṃ |  
bhāle vibhūtivat kuryādbrahmaviṣṇuśivātmakaṃ ||  
  
bhasmanā corddhvapuṇḍraṃ tu tiryak puṇḍraṃ tathā mṛdā |  
ūrddhvapuṇḍreti puṇḍraṃ syāt norddhvapuṇḍraṃ tripuṇḍrake ||  
  
brahmahatyā samaṃ proktaṃ munibhirvedapāragaiḥ |  
rudrapiṇḍasamudbhūtādvijāmohasamanvitaḥ ||  
  
pitaraṃ tannajānaṃtitedhiveśyāsutā iva |  
tripuṇḍraṃ brāhmaṇo vidvān manasāpi na laṃghayet ||  
  
śrutvā vidhīyate yastu satyāgīyājakī bhavet |  
vedasyādhyayane śūdronādhikārī yathā bhavet ||  
  
tripuṇḍraṃ na vipronādhikārī śivārccane |  
vibhūtidhāraṇaṃ kāryaṃ vaidikaṃ tāṃtrikaṃ tathā ||  
  
kapilāyā sa kṛcchastraṃ gṛhītaṃ gaganeya tat |  
na klinnaṃ nāpi kaṭhinaṃ na durgaṃdhi na coṣitaṃ ||  
  
uparyadhaḥ parityajya gṛhṇīyāt patitaṃ yadi |  
piṇḍīkṛtya śivāgnau ca tatkṣipen mūlamaṃtrataḥ ||  
  
apakvamatipakvaṃ ca saṃtyājyaṃ vāsitaṃsitaṃ |  
ādāya vāsasāloḍya bhasmādhāre viniḥkṣipet ||  
  
bhasmasaṃgrahaṇaṃ kuryāddevenudvāsite sati |  
udvāsane kṛte yasyāccaṇḍabhasma prajāyate ||  
  
bhasmaviddhiparaṃ devi satyaloka sukhāhvayaṃ |  
bhasmanā sarvapāśānāṃ pāpānāṃ ca sureśvarī ||  
  
bhasmetikīrtitaṃ tena munibhistatvavedibhiḥ |  
tatpunardvividhaṃ viddhimukhyaṃ gauṇaṃ tathaiva ca ||  
  
mukhaṃ proktaṃ paraṃbrahma gauṇamāgneya mucyate |  
bhasmaṃ tadevamārabhya mukhaṃ tadaparaṃ vudhaḥ ||  
  
āgneya gauṇamajñānadhvaṃsakaṃ jñānasādhanaṃ |  
gauṇaṃ nānāvidhaṃ viddhi śubhaprāṇaharemvike ||  
  
agnihotrāgnijaṃ taddhi virajāhomajaṃ śive |  
aupānasa samutpannaṃ samidāgni samudbhavaṃ ||  
  
pacanāgni samudbhūtaṃdāvānala samudbhavaṃ |  
traivarṇikāṇāṃ sarveṣāmagnihotra samudbhavaṃ ||  
  
virajānalajaṃ caiva dhāryaṃ bhasma na gātmaje |  
aupāna sa samutpannaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
p. 71b)  
  
samidagni samutpannaṃ dhāryaṃ vai brahmacāriṇāṃ |  
śūdrāṇāṃ śrotragṛhajaṃ paramāgni samudbhavaṃ ||  
  
anyeṣāmapi sarveṣāṃ dhāryaṃ kavānalodbhavaṃ |  
yadā dvijā bhasmakuryuḥ sadyenānīya gomayaṃ ||  
  
vāmena pātre saṃyojyā ghoramaṃtreṇa nirdahet |  
puruṣeṇa samuddhṛtya īśānena viśodhayet ||  
  
itthaṃ tu saṃskṛtaṃ bhasma agnirityādi maṃtrataḥ |  
tadrudrāyeti yajuṣāmaṃtra vedrudrasaṃjñavā ||  
  
praṇavādyaiścaturmaṃtrairhṛdayaitairnāmabhiḥ priye |  
paṃcavarṇādyakṣarādyairbhālāṃsādarahṛtsu ca ||  
  
tripuṇḍradhāraṇaṃ kuryāt mūrddhni paṃcākṣareṇa ca |  
ebhiścanāmabhirdhāryaṃ punarbhasma dvijādibhiḥ ||  
  
brahmālalāṭe vijñeyo hṛdaye havyavāhanaḥ |  
nābhauskaṃdogalepūṣārudryedakṣiṇavāhuke ||  
  
ādityo vāhumadhye ca śaśī ca maṇivaṃdhake |  
vāmadevo vāmavāhau vāhumadhye prabhaṃjanaḥ ||  
  
maṇibaṃdhe ca vasavaḥ pṛṣṭadeśe hariḥ smṛtaḥ |  
śaṃbhūḥ kakudi saṃproktaḥ paramātmāśirasmṛtaḥ ||  
  
ābrahmaraṃdhrapādāṃtaṃ yogināmāplavaṃ mataṃ |  
nābherūrddhvaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ ca viśeṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
idānīṃ tāṃtrikamataṃ tanmenigaditaṃ śṛṇu |  
kastūryādi susaṃyuktaṃ bhasmaśāktastu dhārayet ||  
  
maṃtritairmūlamaṃtreṇa śivapaṃcākṣareṇa vā |  
anyeṣāmapi sarveṣāṃ vinā maṃtraṃ sureśvarī ||  
  
atha viśeṣastu ||  
  
vibhūtidhāraṇasyāsyamaṃtrasya ca sadāśivaḥ |  
ṛṣistṛṣṭup bhavecchaṃdo rudrodevaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
prāsādavījaṃ vījasyāt śaktiṃ kūrcaṃ ca kīlakaṃ |  
kṣetrapālaṃ sarvapāpakṣayārthe viniyogitā ||  
  
nyāsaṃ ṛṣyādikaṃ kṛtvā mūlena vīkṣaṇaṃ tataḥ |  
saṃsmṛtyetthaṃ dakṣakare vibhūtiṃ vinidhāya hi ||  
  
ācchādya vāmahastena kapotābhi navātmanā |  
vakṣyamāṇena maṃtreṇa trivāramabhimaṃtrayet ||  
  
phaṭkāreṇa trirāvṛtyajalena veṣṭanaṃ caret |  
paṃcavāraṃ mūlamanuṃjaptvā sodhanamācaret ||  
  
tato dakṣakarādvāmakare bhasmanidhāya hi |  
tato mūlena manunājalenālodrayetpriye ||  
  
vartulaṃ maṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā ṣaṭkoṇaṃ tasya madhyagaṃ |  
trikoṇaṃ tasya cāpyaṃtarmūlabījaṃ dvijottamaḥ ||  
  
dakṣakareṇacāchādyamaṃtramenaṃ japet tataḥ |  
prāsādaṃ kūrcabījaṃ ca kṣatrapālaṃ tathāṃkuśaṃ ||  
  
p. 72a)  
  
vibhūtipadamābhāṣya aśeṣaduritāpahe |  
manovākkāyamityuktvā śādhaye dvitayaṃ vade ||   
  
kūrcāstra vahni lalanāyukto maṃtraḥ prakīrtitaḥ |  
atra kaścana viśeṣosti śmaśānabhasmadhāraṇe ||  
  
mūlena vīkṣaṇaṃ kuryāt kūrceṇa veṣṭanaṃ caret |  
tāramaidhatrayākāmakūrcavarmāstrahṛnmanuḥ ||  
  
anena manunā devi saptavāraṃ viśodhya ca |  
paścānmūlamanuṃ japtvā daśavāraṃ sureśvari ||  
  
trivāraṃ saptavāraṃ vā sveṣṭa devyai nivedya ca |  
tadaṃte tilakaṃ kuryāddevatā bhāvasiddhaye ||  
  
tripuṇḍraṃ bhasmanā kuryādiṣṭamaṃtreṇa mānavaḥ |  
tripuṇḍraṃ kārayedbhāle brahmaviṣṇuśivātmakaṃ ||  
  
madhyamānāmikā caiva tarjanyaiva tripuṇḍrakaṃ |  
atisvalpamanādhṛṣyamati dīrghāṃtamakṣayaṃ ||  
  
netrayugmapramāṇena tripuṇḍraṃ dhārayedvijaḥ |  
ṣaḍaṃgula pramāṇaṃ tu brāhmaṇānāṃ tripuṇḍrakaṃ ||  
  
nṛpāṇāṃ caturaṃgulyaṃ vaiśyānāṃ tu triraṃgulaṃ |  
ekāṃgulaṃ tu śūdrāṇāṃ nārīṇāṃ tu visarjanaṃ ||  
  
brahmāviṣṇuścarudraśca tripuṃḍrasyādhidevatāḥ |  
dhyāryaṃ bhasmatripuṇḍraṃ tu gṛhīṇājalasaṃyutaṃ ||  
  
sarvakālaṃ bhave strīṇāṃ yatīnāṃ jalavarjitaṃ |  
evaṃ bhasmadhṛtaṃ yena tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ||  
  
mahāpātakasaṃghāśca tathānye copapātakāḥ |  
naśyaṃti khalu deveśi satyaṃ satyaṃ ca nānyathā ||  
  
vahunoktena kiṃ bhasmadhāraṇaṃ mokṣasādhanaṃ |  
bhūtidā tu vibhūtiḥ syādvidhinā vidhṛtā yadi ||  
  
yathā kathaṃ cidvi dhṛtā bhasmasāt kurute janaṃ |  
dhṛtvā bhasma tu yo mohāt karau prakṣālayadbhuvi ||  
  
sa raurave vasenmartyau yāvadā caṃdratārakaṃ |  
yāvaṃtaḥ patitā bhūmau bhasmanaḥ paramāṇavaḥ ||  
  
tāvadvarṣa sahasrāṇi naro bhavati kilviṣī |  
vibhūtidhāraṇaṃ cādau tilakaṃ caṃdanena tu ||  
  
viśeṣatastu śāktānāṃ dvayamāvaśyakaṃ priye |  
ato nivodha vidhivat tadvaccaṃdanadhāraṇaṃ ||  
  
vāme karatale śvetaṃ sthāpayitvā tu caṃdanaṃ |  
mūlamaṃtraṃ vilikhyātra tato'nāmikayā nanu ||  
  
gṛhītvā prakṣiped bhūmau paṃcamaṃtrāṃ samuccaran |  
tārādyāśca hṛdaṃtyāśca ṅeṃtā api samīritā ||  
  
jñānecche ca kriyāśaktiḥ kāmāḥ sarvakalottarāḥ |  
ācchādya dakṣiṇe naiva tataḥ karatalena tu ||  
  
p. 72b)  
  
gṛṇanmaṃtraṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ kuryāt tilakamīśvari |  
alaṃghayan bhasmarekhāṃ tiryagrekhāṃ vidhānataḥ ||  
  
māyā kāmarūṣaḥ sarvajanamohini voddharet |  
sarvādvaśaṃkarītyuktvānāṃ tato rakṣayugmakaṃ ||  
  
astraṃ śiroyuto maṃtro mayā te parikīrtitaḥ |  
etat taṃtroditaṃ devi proktaṃ tilakadhāraṇaṃ ||  
  
atha saṃdhyā |  
  
ācamya prāṅmukho bhūtvā upaviśya ca maṃtravit |  
vaidikīṃ tāṃtrikīṃ kuryāt tataḥ saṃdhyāṃ samāhitaḥ ||  
  
vakṣyetha tāṃtrikīṃ saṃdhyāṃ mūlenācamanatrayaṃ ||  
  
vidyābhede saṃdhyāsaṃkhyāmāha ||  
  
suṃdaryāstu catuḥkālaṃ saṃdhyāvaṃdanamācaret |  
prātaḥkāle ca madhyāhne sāyāhne hyarddharātrake ||  
  
caturvidhā tu gāyatrī japed yatnena pārvatī |  
prastārā kṛtirūpā ca upasthānābhidhā tathā ||  
  
vāṃchā kalpalatā devi caturthī parikīrtitā |  
ṣaṣṭhī pārāyaṇaṃ prātarmadhyāhne nama saṃjñakaṃ ||  
  
maṃtrapārāyaṇaṃ rātrau niśāyāṃ cakrasaṃjñakaṃ |  
kālikāyāmidaṃ proktamupasthānavivarjitaṃ ||  
  
medhādīkṣādirājñītvāt kālyāṃ saṃdhyāṃ catuṣṭayaṃ |  
saṃdhyā trayaṃ ca tārāyācchinnāyāṃ trividhaṃ bhavet ||  
  
etāsāṃ na hi bhedosti bhedabhāg narakaṃ vrajet |  
śikhāṃ vadhvātha mūlena prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ caret ||  
  
aṃgāni vinyaseddehe karanyāsa purassaraṃ |  
amṛtīkṛtya purato jalaṃ vaṃdhenu mudrayā ||  
  
abhimaṃtrya ca mūlena saptavāraṃ tataḥ paraṃ |  
akārādi kṣakārāṃtairmātṛkārṇaiḥ sa viṃdubhiḥ ||  
  
pratyarṇaṃ prokṣeyenmūrddhni kuśamūlena ca tridhā |  
devaṃ dhyātvātha manuvit bhānumaṇḍala saṃsthitaṃ ||  
  
ādāyatoyamā maṃtryairvījairbhūtātmakaistathā |  
laṃ vaṃ raṃ yaṃ haṃ iti ca tānyetaiḥ saptadhārajaṃ ||  
  
maṃtrayitvā punaḥ saptavāraṃ mūlena maṃtrayet |  
tajjalaṃ vāmahastena dhāryaṃ tatsruta viṃdubhiḥ ||  
  
dakṣahastena saṃprokṣyakaṃ paṭhanmūlamaṃtrakaṃ |  
hastavyabhyāsa nādvāmācārī sevanamācaret ||  
  
nāsāmāśliṣya śiṣṭena tejorūpeṇa tena tu |  
praviśyāṃtargataṃ sarvaṃ malaṃ saṃśodhya nirgataṃ ||  
  
dakṣanāsāpuṭe naitat smṛtvā dakṣiṇahastagaṃ |  
vāmabhāge dakṣaśilāṃ dhyātvāstreṇa ca tatkṣipet ||  
  
prakṣālyahastā vācamya mūlamaṃtreṇa maṃtravit |  
gāyatryāvatha mūlena dadyādarghya trayaṃ tataḥ |  
  
p. 73a)  
  
sūryamaṇḍala vāsinyai devatāyai tataḥ paraṃ |  
arghamaṃjalimādāya gāyatryā ca trirutkṣipet ||  
  
tārāyāṃ tu viśeṣaḥ |  
  
kupītamodra puṣpaṃ ca kulapuṣpaṃ kuśājalaṃ |  
akṣatāśca tathā tāmre kṛtvā cārghyaṃ nivedayet ||  
  
mūlāṃte codyadāditya padānmaṇḍala ityapi |  
vartinyai śivacaitanyamayyai svāheti tanmanuḥ ||  
  
puruṣāṇāṃ viśeṣaḥ ||  
  
ravimaṃḍala saṃsthāya sveṣṭadevāya cārpayet |  
tathā śaktyā japedvidyāṃ gāyatrī tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśatāvṛtyā gāyatrīṃ prajapetsudhīḥ |  
mahāpātaka yuktopi prajaped daśadhā yadi ||  
  
satyaṃ satyaṃ mahādevi mukto bhavati tatkṣaṇāt |  
śaktāśakta prabhedena gāyatrī daśadhā japet ||  
  
jalena mūlamaṃtrāṃtehyamukaṃ tarpayāmi ca |  
uktvā tridhā tarpaṇīyaṃ vāmakaiḥ kāraṇena tu ||  
  
iṣṭadevasya gāyatrīmaṣṭāviṃśati saṃkhyakāṃ |  
japedabhāve brāhmī tu vaidikaṃ matamāśritaḥ ||  
  
tāṃtrikaḥ śivagāyaṃvījapetsāthanirūpyate |  
oṃ tanmaheśāya vidmahe vāgviśuddhāyadhīmahi ||  
  
tannaḥ śivapracodayāt ||  
  
atha gāyatrī dhyānaṃ pūrvāhne ||  
  
udyadāditya saṃkāśāṃ pustakākṣakarāṃ smaret |  
kṛṣṇājīnadharāṃ brāhmīṃ dhyāyettārakitāṃvare ||  
  
madhyāhne ||  
  
śyāmavarṇāṃ caturvāhuṃ śaṃkhacakralasatkarāṃ |  
gadāpadmadharo devī sūryaviṃvakṛtāśrayā ||  
  
sāyāhne ||  
  
sāyāhne varadāṃ devīṃ gāyatrīṃ saṃsmaredvudhaḥ |  
śuklāṃ śuklāṃ varadharāṃ vṛṣāsana kṛtāśrayāṃ ||  
  
trinetrāṃ varadaṃ pāśaṃ śūlaṃ ca nṛkaroṭikāṃ |  
sūryamaṇḍala madhyasthāṃ dhyāyeddevīṃ samabhyaset ||  
  
atha śyāmayā gāyatrī vidhānaṃ ||  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
gāyatrīyā purā proktā devadeva jagatpate |  
ṛṣyādi caivakaṃ dhyānaṃ japapūjādikaṃ tathā ||  
  
sādhanaṃ ca mahādeva kathayasvamayi prabho ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
kathayāmi mahādeva śṛṇuṣva prāṇavallabhe |  
śrīkṛṣṇastu ṛṣistasyāḥ gāyatrī chaṃda eva ca ||  
  
śivaśaktisvarūpā hi devatā parikīrtitāḥ |  
dhyānaṃ caiva vadāmyatra śṛṇuṣva devi bhaktitaḥ ||  
  
p. 73b)  
  
śmaśāne ca mahākālīṃ devīṃ dhyāyeddigaṃvarāṃ |  
daṃṣṭrā karālavadanāṃ muṇḍamālāṃ vibhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
dakṣiṇorddhe dhanudhatte vāme caiva tathā śarān |  
adhaḥ pāśaṃ ca khaḍgaṃ ca tat kramāt parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ dhyātvā mahākālīṃ japellakṣa catuṣṭayaṃ |  
rudhirāktairvilvapatraistaddaśāṃśena homayet ||  
  
sādhanaṃ ca mahādevi pūrvavat samupācaret ||  
  
athādyā gāyatrī yathā ||  
  
kālikāyai padaṃ coktā vidmahe tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
śmaśānavāsinīdreṃtaṃ dhīmahīti tato vadet ||  
  
tannoghore padaṃ procya pravadecca pracodayāt |  
asyāḥ prasādamātreṇa mahāpātakakoṭayaḥ ||  
  
sadyaḥ pralayamāyāṃti sādhakasya na cānyatā |  
rāvaṇasya vadhāccaiva rāmacaṃdro vimohitaḥ ||  
  
mātṛvadhāt parśurāmomocito'syāḥ prasādataḥ |  
surāpānnācca śrīkṛṣṇodattātreyastathaiva ca ||  
  
brahmaṇaśca śiraḥ chedādahaṃ rudrovimocitaḥ |  
evameṣā mahāvidyā gāyatrīdevi suṃdarī ||  
  
mahāpātaka yuktopi prajapeddaśadhāyadi |  
satyaṃ satyaṃ mahādevi mukto bhavati tatkṣaṇāt ||  
  
brahmahatyādayaḥ pāpāḥ khaṃḍaṃ khaṇḍaṃ vrajaṃti hi |  
nānayā sadṛśī vidyānānena sadṛśo japaḥ ||  
  
nānena sadṛśaṃ jñānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati ||  
  
atha tārāyāḥ ||  
  
tārāyai padamābhāṣya vidmahe tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
nahogrāyai padaṃ procya dhīmahīti tataḥ punaḥ ||  
  
tannodevi padaṃ procya vadet paścāt pracodayāt ||  
  
atha chinnāyāḥ ||  
  
vairocanyai vidmahe ca chinnamastāyai ca dhīmahī |  
tanno devipadaṃ coktvā yojanīyaṃ pracodayāt ||  
  
atha tripurasuṃdaryāḥ ||  
  
vāgbhavaṃ tripurādevī vidmahe tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
kāmavījaṃ samuccārya kāmeśvaryai ca dhīmahī ||  
  
tannaḥ klinne padaṃ coktvā vadet paścāt pracodayāt ||  
  
atha bhairavyāḥ ||  
  
tripurā ca tathāṅeṃtaṃ vidmahe padamuddharet |  
bhairavyaiśca tataścoktvā dhīmahīti tato vadet ||  
  
tato devī padaṃ coktvā pracodayāddudīrayet |  
gāyatrī traipurākhyātā vāgbhavādyaṃ samuddharet ||  
  
atha kamalāyāḥ ||  
  
mahālakṣmīpadaṃ procya vidmahe tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
mahāśriyai padaṃ coktvā dhīmahī ca padaṃ vadet ||  
  
tannaḥ śabdācchrīpadaṃ ca tato dadyāt pracodayāt ||  
  
atha bhuvaneśvaryāḥ ||  
  
p. 74a)  
  
māyāvījaṃ samuccārya bhuvaneśvaryai ca vidmahe |  
ādyāyai padamuccārya dhīmahī tadanantaraṃ ||  
  
tannodevī padaṃ procya tato deyaṃ pracodayāt ||  
  
atha mātaṃgī ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi gāyatrī sādhakasya varapradāṃ |  
śukapriyāyai vidmahe śrīkāmeśvarī dhīmahī ||  
  
tannaḥ * * * * * * ? śyāmādevī pracodayāt ||  
  
atha dhūmāvatī ||  
  
dhūmiti vījamuccārya dhūmāvatīti vidmahe |  
vivarṇādevī padato dhīmahī padamuddharet ||  
  
dūmādevyāstu gāyatrī tannoghora pracodayāt ||  
  
atha vagalāmukhī ||  
  
sthiramāyā samuccārya vagalāpadatomukhī |  
vidmahe duṣṭayadataḥ staṃbhinī padamuccaret ||  
  
dhīmahīti padasyāṃte tanno devī pracodayāt |  
vagalāyā maheśāni gāyatrīyaṃ prakīrtitā ||  
  
atha gaṇeśasya ||  
  
tatpuruṣāya vidmahe vakratuṇḍāya dhīmahī |  
tannodaṃtī padaṃ procya vadet paścāt pracodayāt ||  
  
athādityasya ||  
  
saptaturaṃgāya padāt vidmahe padamuddharet |  
sahasrakiraṇaṃ ṅeṃtaṃ dhīmahī padataḥ punaḥ ||  
  
tannoraviḥ padaṃ procya tato jñeyaṃ pracodayāt ||  
  
atha nārāyaṇasya ||  
  
nārāyaṇāya vidmahe vāsudevāya dhīmahī ||  
  
tanno viṣṇuḥ pracodayāt ||  
  
japitvā cārpayeddevastutvā natveṣṭadevatāṃ |  
sūryamaṇḍalato devaṃ vinyaseddhṛdayesvake ||  
  
tato guruṃ ca praṇamediti saṃdhyā tu tāṃtrikī |  
iti saṃdhyā trayaṃ proktaṃ karmiṇāṃ siddhidāyakaṃ ||  
  
trikālamevaṃ kartavyāḥ saṃdhyālopāt phalaṃ na hi |  
saṃdyālopaṃ na kurvīta kadācidapi kutracit ||  
  
prātaḥ saṃdhyā sa nakṣatrāḥ sa sūryāśāpamucyate |  
muhūrta paṃcakādūrddhaṃ viṃśatye vāgyathā yathā ||  
  
āsannābhijitaḥ kālaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhastathā tathā |  
saṃdhyākālasya mukhyasyalope nāḍītrayāṃtare ||  
  
prāyaścittaṃ tvekamarghyamadhikaṃ saṃpradīyate |  
paraḥ saṃdhyākālatorvāgjate kāle tatodhike ||  
  
aṣṭhottaraṃ śataṃ tatra gāyatryā japa iṣyate |  
rājñārurddha gadātervāgīvāvaśyaka karmaṇi ||  
  
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā gāyatryāṣṭottaraṃśataṃ |  
yadā tu tāṃtrikaṃ devī tadā mūlaṃ śataṃ japet ||  
  
prāyaścittāyatāṃ kṛtvā kurvīta samayāgatāṃ ||  
  
atha tarpaṇaṃ ||  
  
vaidikaṃ tarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā tatastāṃtrikamārabhet |  
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā mūlena nyāsamācaret ||  
  
ṛṣyādi tritayasyātha purato dhenumudrayā |  
vaṃ japannamṛtī kṛtyajalaṃ tatra sa cakrakaṃ ||  
  
maṃtrarājaṃ jale dhyātvā tatra devīnnidhāya ca |  
gurupaṃktiṃ ca saṃtarya vaṭukādīśca tarpayet ||  
  
p. 74b)  
  
mūladevīṃ ca saṃtarpya tarpayet parivārākan |  
tarpayed dvārapālādīn tathaivāṃgādi devatāḥ ||  
  
śaṃkhikā suṃdarāṃ paścādaiśyāṃ ca paramaṃ guruṃ |  
agnau parāparaṃ caiva nair-ṛtyāṃ parameṣṭitaṃ ||  
  
vāyavyādīśa paryaṃtaṃ gurupaṃktiṃ ca tarpayet |  
aṅgāni tattatsthāneṣu madhye devīṃ ca tarpayet ||  
  
mūlāṃte cāmukīṃ devīṃ tarpayāmi tataḥ paraṃ |  
vahnijāyāṃtako maṃtro devīnāṃ tarpaṇe smṛtaḥ ||  
  
atha puruṣāṇāṃ ||  
  
tarpayāmi padaṃ yojyaṃ maṃtrāṃte sveṣu nāmasu |  
dvitīyāṃ teṣu cetyevaṃ tarpaṇasya manurmataḥ ||  
  
ekaviṃśati saṃkhyā vā daśadhā vā tridhāpi vā |  
ekaimaṃjaliṃ toyaṃ parivārān pratarpayet ||  
  
devasyāmṛta vudhyā tu tīrthatoyaiḥ pratarpayet |  
tīrthodakaistu paśubhiḥ vāmādyaikāraṇena tu ||  
  
aśaktau mūlamuccārya devīmātraṃ pratarpayet |  
saṃsmṛtya bhairavaṃ devaṃ mārtaṇḍākhyamumāpatiṃ ||  
  
mūlena manunādevaṃ sūryasya manunātha vā |  
māyāvījaṃ samuddhṛtya sohaṃ tu viparītataḥ ||  
  
mārtaṇḍa bhairavaṃ ṅentaṃ prakāśaṃ śakti saṃyutaṃ |  
sūryasya matraḥ saṃproktaḥ stridhā cārghyaṃ prakalpayet ||  
  
yāvannadīyate cārghyaṃ bhāskarāya nivedanaṃ |  
tāvanna pūjayed viṣṇuṃ śaṃkaraṃ vā sureśvarī ||  
  
saṃtarpya devīṃ svahṛditīrthaṃ sūryavisarjayet |  
guruṃ digīśāṃśca khagānnatvā bhāṇḍaṃ kare dadhan ||  
  
jalapūrṇaṃ vrajenmaunī sveṣṭadevaṃ hṛdismaran |  
ekāṃtaṃ nirjanaṃ yāyānmanojñaṃ doṣavarjitaṃ ||  
  
digaṃtaraṃ na vīkṣyeta yāvat prāpnoti vai gṛham ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau prātaḥkṛtyādinirṇayo nāma paṃcadaśaḥ prakāśaḥ ||   
15 ||  
  
atha sarvadhāraṇa nityārcanavidhirlikhyate ||  
  
pūrvajanmapraśamanājjanmamṛtyu nivāraṇāt |  
saṃpūrṇaphaladānācca pūjeti kathitā priye ||  
  
pradakṣiṇaṃ yajñavāṭaṃ kṛtvā pādau ca hastakau |  
prakṣālyācamya pūjāyāḥ gṛhadvārātalesthitaḥ ||  
  
gehe ca dvāradeśesthaḥ praṇamya manasā guruṃ |  
praṇamyediṣṭadevaṃsvaṃ dikpālānapi cetasā ||  
  
yatpūrvamarjitaṃ pāpaṃ taddinenyadinepi vā |  
tatpāpasyāyanodārthaṃ maṃtradvayamudīrayet ||  
  
he deva prākṛtaṃ cittaṃ pāpākrāṃtamidaṃ manaḥ |  
tanniḥ sāraya cittānme pāpaṃ phaṭ phaṭ ca te namaḥ ||  
  
p. 75a)  
  
sūryaḥ somoyamaḥ kālā mahābūtāni paṃca ca |  
ete śubhāśubhasyeha karmaṇo navasākṣiṇaḥ ||  
  
huṃphaḍiti bruvan krodhadṛṣṭyā paśyecca pārśvayoḥ |  
evaṃ kṛte prathamaḥ pāpotsādanakarmaṇi ||  
  
yasmāddṛḍhataraṃ pāpaṃ taddūrecāvatiṣṭhatu |  
atīte pūjanesthāne svaṃprayāṃ tu punaśca tat ||  
  
yasmādalpataraṃ pāpaṃ tannāśamupagacchati |  
pūjanetyakta pāpasya kāmamiṣṭaṃ kṣaṇād bhavet ||  
  
tataḥ prakṣālya pādau ca hastā vācamya yatnataḥ |  
dadyādarghyaṃ dineśāya tatprakāra ihocyate ||  
  
gomayenopaliptāyāṃ bhūmau kṛtvā tu maṇḍalaṃ |  
siṃdūreṇa tataḥ paścādupaviśya nijāsane ||  
  
prāṅmukhaḥ praṇamediṣṭa devatāṃ bhakti tatparaḥ |  
prāṇāyāma trayaṃ kṛtvā sūryamaṃtreṇa maṃtravit ||  
  
hrī& hrī& saḥ iti sūryasya tryakṣaro maṃtra ucyate |  
vinyasya ca tathendrādīn dhyātvā sūryamananyadhīḥ ||  
  
parādvayā bhayavarāndadhataṃ karābjairmāṇikyamaulimaruṇāṃgaruciṃ trinetraṃ   
|  
raktāṃvujāsanamaśeṣaguṇaikasiṃdhuṃbhānuṃ samastajagatāṃmadhiyaṃ   
bhajāmi ||  
  
tatkalpoktavidhānena pūjayedupacārakaiḥ |  
purato maṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā jalena caturasrakaṃ ||  
  
nidhāya tatra sādhāraṃ sajalaṃ tāmrapātrakaṃ |  
gaṃdhapuṣpākṣatān darbhān durvāśarṣapa saṃyutān ||  
  
sa tilānukta puṣpāṇi yavāṃścāpi pravinyaset |  
sūryamaṃtreṇa tatpātraṃ spṛśannaṣṭottaraṃśataṃ ||  
  
abhimaṃtrya ca tatpātraṃ samutthāya karadvayāt |  
mūrddhāṃta sūryamaṃtreṇa dadyādarghyaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
hrī& hrī& saḥ sa graharāśi nakṣatra padamuccaret |  
tataśca yogakaraṇaḥ parivṛttāsaneti ca ||  
  
saṃsthitaḥ śrīsūryāyaiṣaterghasvāhā manuḥ smṛtaḥ |  
catuḥ striṃśadakṣaroyaṃ sūryasyārghaṃ nivedane ||  
  
japet tato yathā śaktyā sūryamaṃtra mananyadhīḥ |  
tadarghāṃvu plutaṃ sūryaṃ dhyāyandeśikasattamaḥ ||  
  
stutvā praṇamya visṛjen maṇḍalātaṃ divākaraṃ |  
tata utthāya vidhivad dvārapūjāṃ samārabhet ||  
  
dvāramarghyāṃvunā prokṣya tanmadhye vighnayaṃ yajet |  
taddakṣiṇe mahālakṣmīṃ vāme cāpi sarasvatīṃ ||  
  
dvāraśriyaṃ ca tanmadhye śākhayordakṣiṇānyayoḥ |  
ūrddhvabhāgāttaraṃ yāvat paṃcapaṃcavibhāgake ||  
  
p. 75b)  
  
nāmasyādyakṣaraṃ viṃduyuktaṃ nāma ca ṅeṃtakaṃ |  
samuccārya hṛtaṃ taṃ ca devānetān prapūjayet ||  
  
gaṇapatiṃ kṣetrapālaṃ tataśca vasuṃdhārayā |  
yuktaṃ śaṃkha nidhiṃ dakṣe vāmeva sumatīyutaṃ ||  
  
pūjayitvā padmanidhiṃ tadadhādakṣavāmataḥ |  
māyāśaktiṃ ca cicchaktiṃ gaṃgā ca yamunāṃ tathā ||  
  
dhatāraṃ ca vidhātāraṃdaṃ dehalyai namastvadhaḥ |  
ādau tu paścimadvāra pūjāve cedyaṃ prakāśitā ||  
  
naṃdī cāpi mahākālīṃ dvārayordakṣa vāmayoḥ |  
saṃpūjyaiva mudagdvāraṃ prāgyāmye ca prapūjayet ||  
  
dvārapālau kramātteṣu gaṇeśavṛṣabhāvapi |  
bhṛṃgirīṭṭistathāskaṃda umācaṃḍeśvarau tathā ||  
  
viṣṇornaṃdaḥ sunaṃdaśca caṇḍaścāpi pracaṃḍakaḥ |  
valaśca pravalaścaiva bhadraścāpi subhadrakaḥ ||  
  
vakratuṇḍaika daṃṣṭrau ca mahodaragajānanau |  
laṃbodaraśca vikaṭo gaṇeśadvārapālakāḥ ||  
  
vighnarājo dhūmravarṇaḥ kramāt paścimadvārataḥ |  
devyāḥ sūryasya yoginyoṣṭāvetā dvārapālakāḥ ||  
  
brāhmī māheśvarī caiva kaumārī vaiṣṇavī tathā |  
vārāhī ca tatheṃdrāṇī cāmuṇḍā ca śriyāsaha ||  
  
atha vakṣye dvāradeva dhyānaṃ taṃtreṣu gopitaṃ |  
devadvāraṃ dvāradevāsvayamudghāṭayaṃṭi yat ||  
  
pāśāṃkuśa phalāṃ bhojapāṇiṃ pāṭala tuṃḍilaṃ |  
vīraṃ vighneśvaraṃ vaṃde gajavaktraṃ trilocanaṃ ||  
  
padmadvaya varābhīti lasatpāṇī catuṣṭayaṃ |  
nirddagdha hemagaurāṃgī mahālakṣmīṃ trilocanāṃ ||  
  
akṣasrak pustakābhīti varahastāṃ trilocanāṃ |  
śvetapadmāsanāṃ śuklāṃ śvetavastrāṃ sarasvatīṃ ||  
  
taptakārtasvarobhāsā divyaratnavibhūṣitā |  
dvāraśrīrūrddhva padmasthāvarābhayakarāṃbujā ||  
  
sitogajāsyaḥ paraśuṃdaṇḍaṃ pāśaṃ triśūlakaṃ |  
bhujaiścaturbhirvibhrāṇo mūṣakoparisaṃsthitaḥ ||  
  
kapālaśūlavibhrāṇāṃ kṛpāluṃ kṛṣṇa vigrahaṃ |  
tryakṣaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ bhāvayāmi kṣetreśaṃ kṣatavidviṣaṃ ||  
  
vasudhārāṃdakṣabhujenāliṃgaṃtaṃ su tuṃḍilaṃ |  
vāme śaṃkhadharaṃ muktānibhaṃ śaṃkhanidhiṃ bhaje ||  
  
āliṃgaṃ taṃ vasumaṃtī lalāṭe padmacihnitaṃ |  
padmanidhiṃ maṇinibhaṃ vāmenotpaladhāriṇaṃ ||  
  
p. 76a)  
  
varāṃkuśābhīti pāśahastāṃ saṃsāramūlikāṃ |  
trinetrāṃ śyāmavarṇāṃtā śyāmāṃ māyāmahaṃbhaje ||  
  
pāśāṃkuśāvarābhītīṃ dadhānāmaruṇa prabhāṃ |  
trinetrāṃ citkalāṃ vaṃde gaurīṃ raktāṃvarojjvalāṃ ||  
  
varābhayakarāṃ saumyāṃ somakoṭi samaprabhāṃ |  
bhaje gaṃgā mahādevīṃ parāṃ deva taraṃgiṇīṃ ||  
  
varābhayakarāṃ vede kāliṃdī kālavigrahāṃ |  
kṛṣṇakacchapamārūḍhāṃ kaṃṭho nīlotpala prabhāṃ ||  
  
kartāraṃ jagatāṃ vaṃde śaṃkhacakragadāṃvujaṃ |  
vibhrāṇaṃ garuḍārūḍhaṃ dhātāraṃ kṛṣṇavigrahaṃ ||  
  
raktaṃ raktāraviṃdasthaṃ varābhaya kamaṇḍaluṃ |  
haṃsārūḍhaṃ vidhātāraṃ vaṃde tryakṣa samanvitaṃ ||  
  
siṃhārūḍhāṃ śyāmavarṇāṃ khaḍgakheṭakadhāriṇīṃ |  
adhasthā dehalī vaṃde paścimasyāṃ sudakṣiṇīṃ ||  
  
paścimadvāramāsādya tālatritaya pūrvakaṃ |  
dvāramudvādyacāstreṇa maṃtritān sarṣapākṣatān ||  
  
puṣpayuktāṃstu vikiren maṇḍapābhyaṃtare vudhaḥ |  
nārā ca mudrayāsanyagastre maṃtreṇa deśikaḥ ||  
  
apakrāmaṃ tu bhūtāni piśācāḥ pretaguhyakāḥ |  
ye cātra nivasatyanye devatā bhuvisaṃsthitāḥ ||  
  
apasarpaṃ tu ye bhūtā ye bhūtā bhuvisaṃsthitāḥ |  
ye bhūtā vighnakartāraste naśyaṃ tu śivājñayā ||  
  
ślokayoraṃ tataścāstraṃ paṭhantārā ca mudrayā |  
kṣiptvā tānmaṇḍapasyāṃ taṃ tato vighnāṃstu nirgatān ||  
  
svavāmāṃgasya saṃkocān mārgaṃ datvāya sārayet |  
astramaṃtraṃ smaran vāmapārṣṇighāta trayeṇa ca ||  
  
bhaumānutsādayettāla tritayeṇāṃtarīkṣagān |  
tiryagdṛṣṭyāvalokena divyān vighnānnivārayet ||  
  
dakṣapādaṃ puraskṛtya praviśeddevamadiraṃ |  
śāktastu vāmapādena dvāramācchādya vāsasā ||  
  
paṃcagavyārghatoyābhyāṃ prokṣayen maṇḍapāṃtaraṃ |  
saṃmārjanopalepādyairdarpaṇodaravat kṛtaṃ ||  
  
vimalaṃ dhūpadīpādi puṣpadāmādiśobhitaṃ |  
paṃcavarṇa rajaścitraṃ sthāna śuddhiriyaṃ matā ||  
  
nair-ṛtyāmarcayedvāstu puruṣaṃ vaṃdanādibhiḥ |  
tatraiva vāstvadhīśāya brahmaṇe nama ityapi ||  
  
raktavarṇaṃ raktavarṇa śaktidvādaśa saṃyutaṃ |  
pūjayitvā dīpanāthaṃ bhairavaṃ prārthayediti ||  
  
p. 76b)  
  
atitīkṣṇa mahākāya kalpāṃta dahanoyamaṃ |  
bhairavāya namastubhyaṃ manujñāṃ dātumarhasi ||  
  
aḥ phaḍiti maṃtreṇa pūjāvedīṃ tato viśet |  
saṃskuryādāsanasthānaṃ caturbhirvīkṣyaṇādibhiḥ ||  
  
saṃskāre tatra saṃpūjyā vedyāṃtāḥ pīṭhadevatāḥ |  
ādhāraśaktimārabhya svāsanaṃ tatra vinyaset ||  
  
pūjāsanamathātmīyaṃ cailājina kuśottaraṃ |  
kaṃvale lohite vāpi kṛṣṇe vā vyāghra carmaṇi ||  
  
sanyāsaṃ brahmacārī tu viśet kṛṣṇasya carmaṇi |  
vyāghrājināṃ sarvasiddhyai jñānasiddhirmṛgājine ||  
  
vastrāsanaṃ rogaharaṃ vetrajaṃ prītivarddhanaṃ |  
kauśeyaṃ puṣṭidaṃ proktaṃ kaṃvalaṃ sarvasiddhidaṃ ||  
  
śuklaṃ vādya divā kṛṣṇaṃ viśeṣādraktakaṃvalaṃ |  
śvete tu kambale dharmaṃ siddhiraktertha siddhayaḥ ||  
  
pīte kāmo dvijānyeṣāṃ mokṣadaḥ kṛṣṇakaṃ valaḥ |  
duḥkhamuktyai raṃjitastu nīlīraṃgo na śobhanaḥ ||  
  
atha niṣiddhāsanaṃ ||  
  
tṛṇapallavakāṣṭhāṇi pāṣāṇaṃ mṛnmayaṃ tathā |  
vaṃśāsanaṃ ca vastraṃ ca kevalaṃ kṣitimāsanaṃ ||  
  
evamaṣṭavidhaṃ devi cāsanaṃ parivarjayet |  
tatropaviśyavidhivatsmaredviṣṇuṃ guruṃmudā ||  
  
merupṛṣṭha ṛṣiḥ proktaḥ sutalaṃ chaṃda īritaṃ |  
pṛthivī devatā proktā viniyogo nijāsane ||  
  
pṛthvī tvayā dhṛtā lokā devitvaṃ viṣṇunā dhṛtā |  
tvaṃ ca dhārayamāṃ devi pavitraṃ kuru cāsanaṃ ||  
  
āsanasya catuṣkoṇe gaṇeśaṃ ca sarasvatīṃ |  
durgāṃ kṣatrapatiṃ cāpi brahmādiṣu samarcayet ||  
  
udaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukho vāsvastikāsanamāsthitaḥ |  
padmāsanagato vāpi ṛjukāyo namaḥ sthiraḥ ||  
  
atha svastika padmāsanayorlakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
jānūrvāraṃtare samyak kṛtvā pādatale ubhe |  
ṛtukāyaḥ samāsīnaḥ svastikaṃ tadudīritaṃ ||  
  
vāmo rūparidakṣiṇaṃ tu caraṇaṃ saṃsthāpya vāmaṃ tathāyāmyorūpari   
paścimena dvividhinā dhṛtvā karābhyāṃ dṛḍhaṃ |  
aṃguṣṭhau hṛdaye nidhāya civukaṃ nāsāgramālokayadetadvyādhi   
vighātakāriyamināṃ padmāsanaṃ procyate ||  
  
sthāpayed dakṣiṇebhāge pūjā dravyāṇi cātmanaḥ |  
suvāsitāṃvu saṃpūrṇaṃ savye kuṃbhaṃ suśobhanaṃ ||  
  
p. 77a)  
  
prakṣālanāya karayoḥ pātraṃ pṛṣṭe niveśayet |  
ghṛtādi jvalitān dīpān sthāpayet paritaḥ śubhān ||  
  
darpaṇaṃ cāmaraṃ chatraṃ tālavṛttaṃ ca pādukāṃ |  
yathāyathaṃ tu saṃsthāpya saṃskuryāttāni cātmavan ||  
  
puṣpanaivedyagaṃdhādīn hā& hī& hra& phaḍiti maṃtrataḥ |  
nārā ca mudrayā dṛṣṭyā samayāṃ ca vilokayet ||  
  
dṛṣṭaṃ vā cātmavijñātaṃ samyak puṣpādidūṣaṇaṃ |  
aspṛśyasparśanaṃ vāpi yadanyā yārjitaṃ ca vā ||  
  
tathā nirmālya saṃspṛṣṭaṃ kīṭādyārohaṇaṃ ca yat |  
tatsarvaṃ nāśamāyāni naivedyāya ca lokanāt ||  
  
tato ramiti maṃtreṇa śikhāṃ dīpasya saṃspṛśet |  
sa tu syācchubhado dīponiṣkravyādaḥ sukhapradaḥ ||  
  
pataṃgakīṭakeśādi dāhāt kravyādasaṃhataḥ |  
vasāmajjādi saṃbhūtairghṛtādyairūpayojitaḥ ||  
  
ajñātarūpaṃ tatsarvaṃ doṣasyarśādvinaśyati |  
kṣroṃvījamuccaranmaṃtrī devatīrthena saṃspṛśet ||  
  
pānīyaṃghva tu madhyasthaṃ dṛṣṭvā samyak ca sādhakaḥ |  
vāmenāpāṇinā dhṛtvā vāmapārśvasthitaṃ ghaṭaṃ ||  
  
pātrādhāreṇa maṃtreṇa saṃskurvan saṃspṛśejjvalaṃ |  
svasaṃjñādyakṣaraṃ viṃdu caṃdrārddha pariyojitaṃ ||  
  
tatpātranāma ṅeṃtaṃ ca hṛdaṃ tanyātra maṃtrakaḥ |  
yadajñānāda medhyādi saṃsṛṣṭiriha saṃgatā ||  
  
yadanyaddūṣaṇaṃ pātretoya cā jñānato bhavet |  
jalāśaya śavaḥ sparśājjalasthānācca saṃgataṃ ||  
  
ityādidūṣaṇaṃ naśyat tatpriye devapūjane |  
tataḥ kṛtāṃjali puṭo vāmadakṣiṇa pārśvayoḥ ||  
  
guruṃ gaṇapatiṃ natvā purataḥ sveṣṭadevatāṃ |  
sugaṃdhapuṣpānādāya caṃdanāktāni maṃtravit ||  
  
hyauṃ maṃtreṇa karayorastramaṃtreṇa marddayet |  
tatpuṣpaṃ vāmahastena samādāya ca mastakaṃ ||  
  
bhrāmayet paritastāraṃ japannāghrāya tatpunaḥ |  
hau& oṃ pūrvapaṭhet ślokamimaṃ sa ca nigadyate ||  
  
te sarve vilayaṃ yāṭu ye māṃhiṃsaṃti hiṃsakāḥ |  
mṛtyuroga bhayakleśāḥ pataṃtu ripumastake ||  
  
astramaṃtreṇa nārā ca sudrayeśadiśi tyajet |  
karaśuddhiṃ tatostreṇa kuryāt tāratrayaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
ūrddhvorddhvamastramaṃtreṇa digvaṃdhamapi tena ca |  
tenasaṃ janitaṃ tejo vahniḥ prākāramudrayā ||  
  
p. 77b)  
  
rakṣedātmani mūlena prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ caret |  
bhūtaśuddhiṃ tataḥ kuryāt tatprakāramathavruve ||  
  
pādato jānuparyaṃt'm caturasraṃ sa vajrakaṃ |  
laṃ yutaṃ pītavarṇaṃ ca bhūsthānaṃ brahmadaivataṃ ||  
  
adhisthitaṃ nivṛtyākhya kalayāsthānamucyate |  
utpattestattujīvānāmekaṃ rūpaṃ viciṃtayet ||  
  
jānvoronābhiparyaṃtamayāṃ sthānaṃ sitaprabhaṃ |  
arddhacaṃdranibhaṃ śṛṃga dvayaṃ tatpadmalāṃchitaṃ ||   
  
ṣaṭkoṇaṃ viṃdubhiḥ ṣaḍbhiryuktaṃ vaṃ vījasaṃyutaṃ |  
pratiṣṭhā kalayā yuktaṃ dhyāyetadviṣṇudaivataṃ ||  
  
nābhyādi kaṇṭhaparyaṃtamāraktaṃ rudradaivataṃ |  
raṃ vījayuktaṃ kalayāyutaṃ vidyākhyayā tathā ||  
  
dīptimatsvastikopetaṃ trikoṇākāratāṃgataṃ |  
mahāpralaya saṃsthānaṃ vahiḥ tatvaṃ viciṃtayet ||  
  
kaṃṭhād bhrūmadhyaparyaṃtaṃ ṣaṭkoṇākāratāṃgataḥ |  
ṣaḍviṃdulāṃchitaṃ vṛttaveṣṭitaṃ kṛṣṇavarṇakaṃ ||  
  
vāyusthānaṃ śāṃtikalādhiṣṭhitaṃ śivadaivataṃ |  
yaṃ vījayuktaṃ sarveṣāṃ prāṇarūpaṃ viciṃtayet ||  
  
bhrūmadhyād brahmaraṃdhrāṃtamākāśasthāna mucyate |  
vṛttākāraṃ dhūmravarṇaṃ mahoccadvajalāṃchitaṃ ||  
  
śāṃtyatītākhya kalayādhiṣṭhitaṃ śivadaivataṃ |  
haṃ vījayuktaṃ dhyātvetthaṃ dehe būtāni vinyaset ||  
  
dharmakaṃda samudbhūtaṃ jñānanāla suśobhitaṃ |  
kṛtvā tatkarṇikāsaṃsthaṃ pradīpakalikānibhaṃ ||  
  
suṣumṇā vartmanā jīvaṃ paramātma niyojayet |  
yogayuktena vidhinā sohaṃ maṃtreṇa sādhakaḥ ||  
  
tatraiva sarvabhūtāni vilīnāni viciṃtayet |  
śarīre vāmakukṣau tu ciṃtayet pāpapūruṣaṃ ||  
  
vāmakukṣisthitaṃ pāpaṃ puruṣaṃ kajjala prabhaṃ |  
brahmahatyāśiraskaṃdhaḥ svarṇasteya bhujadvayaṃ ||  
  
surāpāna hṛdāyuktaṃ gurutalpa kaṭidvayaṃ |  
tatsaṃsarga padadvaṃdvamaṃgapratyaṃgapātakaṃ ||  
  
upapātakaromāṇaṃ raktaśmaśrū vilocanaṃ |  
khaḍgacarmadharaṃ krūraṃ rakṣapāpaṃ viciṃtayet ||  
  
śaivaśākte kremaṇaiva pāparūpaṃ smarecchive |  
śaive dakṣe krameṇaiva śākto vāmakareṇa ca ||  
  
vaiṣṇave tadvayatvena pāpa dhyānaṃ prakīrtitaṃ |  
tathā saṃśoṣayedenaṃ pūrakādi krameṇa vai ||  
  
nābhideśe ca maṅgāraṃ dhūmraṃ vāyu viciṃtayet |  
tena vai śoṣayelliṃgaṃ tanuṃ ṣoḍaśamātrayā ||  
  
p. 78a)  
  
karmātmakaṃ catuḥ ṣaṣṭyā kuṃbhayitvā samācaret |  
dvātriṃśanmātre yodakṣedevamatena vā punaḥ || (?)  
  
raktavarṇaṃ vahnivījaṃ meḍhremūle viciṃtayet |  
malāsanātmakaṃ liṃgaṃ śarīraṃ tena dāhayet ||  
  
pūrvokta kramayogena dakṣanāsā krameṇa tu |  
deśikastu samāsaṃkhyā vā manāsena recayet ||  
  
vaṃkāraṃ vāruṇīvījaṃ ghaṇṭhikāyāṃ vibhāvya ca |  
tenāmṛtaṃ samutpādya sahasradalapaṃkajāt ||  
  
plvāvayet pūrakādīni kṛtvā pādatalāvadhi |  
laṃkāraṃ pṛthivī vījaṃ gudamūle vibhāvayet ||  
  
tenaiva kramayogena dhiyā saṃplāvayedvudhaḥ |  
pāpapuṇya vinirmuktaṃ śarīraṃ śāṃbhavaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
tenaiva pūrvamārgeṇa sarvaṃ saṃpādayet tanuṃ |  
saṃjāte sakale dehe devatopāsane kṣamaḥ ||  
  
ātmalīnāni tatvāni svasthānaṃ prāpayet tataḥ |  
ātmānaṃ hṛdayāṃbhojamānayet paramātmanaḥ ||  
  
haṃsamaṃtreṇa vidhivat tejorūpaṃ kalevaraṃ |  
devo bhuktvā yajeddevaṃ nādevo devamarccayet ||  
  
tasmādiṣṭa svarūpatvaṃ svasmin bhāvyaṃ maheśvarī |  
devatārādhanā yogyamutpannamiti bhāvayet ||  
  
bhūtaśuddhivihīnena kṛtā pūjābhicāravat |  
viparītaphalaṃ dadyādabhaktyā pūjanaṃ yathā ||  
  
bhūtaśuddhiṃ vidhāyaivaṃ prāṇasthāpanamācaret |  
prāṇapratiṣṭhā maṃtrasya munayojeśa padmajāḥ ||  
  
chaṃdo ṛgyajuṣī sāmaprāṇa śaktistudevatāḥ |  
ṛṣiḥ śirasi vaktre tu chaṃdāṃsi hṛdidevatāḥ ||  
  
ā& vījāya namo guhye pade hrī& śaktaye namaḥ |  
nābhau namaḥ krau& kīlakāyanīyogo susthitāviti ||  
  
oṃ ā& hrī& kro& aṃkavargaṃ sānusvāraṃ nabho mukhaṃ |  
paṃcatatva samuccārya ātmane āṃ hṛdinyaset ||  
  
oṃ ā& hrī& kro& iṃ ca vargaṃ tadvacchandādi paṃcakaṃ |  
ātmane ī& samuccārya śirase vahni gehinī ||  
  
tāni vījā uṃ tādṛk ṭavargaṃ śrotrakādi ca |  
proktvā tadātmane ūṃca śikhāyai ca vaṣaḍvadet ||  
  
tāni vījāni e& tuṃ ca vāgādīni tadātmane |  
ai muktā kavacāyeti hru& vadet tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
caturvījaṃ ca pūrvoktaṃ o& pavargaṃ ca tādṛśaṃ |  
vacanādi ca tadvatsyādau netrāya vauṣaṭ tathā ||  
  
p. 78b)  
  
caturvījaṃ ca aṃtādṛgyavargaṃ manuścādi ca |  
tadātmane svaraścāṃtyostrāya phaṭ ceti saṃvadet ||  
  
aṃguṣṭādau hastatalāṃ tanyase devameva hi |  
nābhyaṃ dhaścāpi kaṃthādho mūrddhvādhotha tadaṃtakaṃ ||  
  
ā& drī& kro& kramato nyasya hṛtpadmāṣṭadaleṣu ca |  
pūrvataḥ kramato varṇān karṇikāyāṃ hṛdaṃtakān ||  
  
laṃ raṃ haṃ saṃ vaṃ ca yaṃ ca saṃ śaṃ kṣamiti vargataḥ |  
dikṣu nyaset tato dhyāyet prāṇaśaktiṃ hṛdisthitāṃ ||  
  
raktāṃghriyaṃ tāruṇapadmasaṃsthāṃ pāśāṃkuśā vikṣuśarāsanaṃ ca |  
śūlaṃ kapālaṃ dadhatīṃ karābjairaktāṃ trinetrāṃ praṇamāmi devī ||  
  
hastaṃ nidhāya hṛdaye vāgvījaṃ yādikāṣṭakaṃ |  
haṃsaḥ sohaṃ mamaprāṇāvadedihasthitā iti ||  
  
proktvā tathaiva ca punarmama jīva ihasthitaḥ |  
punastaduktvā mama tu vadet sarveṃdriyāṇi ca ||  
  
punastatho mama tu vāṅmanaścakṣuruccaret |  
śrotraghrāṇapraṇā ihāgatya mukhaṃciraṃ tataḥ ||  
  
tiṣṭhaṃ tu vahnijāyāṃta muktvātāraṃ tato japet |  
vapurjyotimayaṃ dhyāyediti syāt prāṇasaṃsthitiḥ ||  
  
atha prāṇāyāmo yathā ||  
  
prāṇāyāmātṛdhā proktvā stotraṃ vaidikayogikāḥ |  
maṃtrasiddhiḥ pāpanāśo yogasiddhiḥ phalaṃ kramāt ||  
  
mātṛkākhyaśca maṃtrākhyastāṃtriko dvividho mataḥ |  
mātṛkākhyo japāsyādau japāṃte ca kṛto yadi ||  
  
varṇavyatyāsādi doṣā na śeṣān haṃtitaṃ śṛṇu |  
vāmayāpūra yadvāyuṃsvaraiḥ kādyaiśca kuṃbhakaṃ ||  
  
recayedyādibhirdakṣanāsāyāṃ mātṛkādibhiḥ |  
yāvacchakyaṃ niyamyāsūnmanasaiva manuṃ japet ||   
  
kaniṣṭhānāmikāṃguṣṭhairnāsāṃ dhṛtvā tu mātrikaḥ |  
prāṇāyāmastvayaṃ prokto yadanya manasā kṛtaṃ ||  
  
japapūjādikaṃ tasya doṣameva vyapohati |  
gāyatrīṃ śirasā sārddhaṃ saptavyāhṛtipūrvikāṃ ||  
  
pratipraṇava saṃyuktāṃ trirayaṃ vaidikomataḥ |  
madhyāmūlādyāvadagramaṃguṣṭhena nipīḍyate ||  
  
mātrā sā procyate saḍbhiryogebhīṣṭaṃ prayacchati |  
jānuṃ pradakṣiṇī kuryādyāvat kālena hastakaḥ ||  
  
tāvat kālamitāmātrāsva niḥśvāsa samāpi ca |  
jaghanyo ravimātraḥ syājjinamātrastu madhyamaḥ ||  
  
p. 79a)  
  
śreṣṭhaḥ ṣaḍvargamātroyaṃ yogatraya su sādhakaḥ |  
kevale kuṃbhake siddhe siddhiḥ syādrājayogajā ||  
  
vīryāstaṃbhaśca vahvāyurvalīpalitanāśanaṃ |  
pūrake kuṃbhake siddheḥ kriyāyogyasya siddhayaḥ ||  
  
pūrvoktaṃ ca na śītoṣṇa vā dhākṣuttṛdbhavāpi ca |  
pūrakaḥ kuṃbhakoreko yadā tulyaḥ prajāyate ||  
  
haṭhayoga sadāsiddhohyaṇimādyaṣṭasiddhayaḥ |  
īṣat phalaṃ jaghanye tu madhye madhyaparekhile ||  
  
niraṃtarābdatritayābhyāsāt sarvaṃ bhavet phalaṃ |  
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā mātṛkānyāsamācaret ||  
  
ṛṣirgurutvān śirasi varṇatvā chaṃda sā mukhe |  
dhāraṇaṃ procyate cittajñeyāptāddevatā hṛdi ||  
  
ṛgatāviti dhātustu ṛvarṇaḥ prāpakomataḥ |  
yivarṇādhastu vijñānamatastatprāpakastu saḥ ||  
  
chatīti dhāturicchāyāṃdādirdānārthako bhavet |  
ata icchāpradaṃ chaṃdo viśeṣādgaṇavarṇataḥ ||  
  
krīḍārthakāddivo dhātoḥ saṃpūrṇaṃ devatā padaṃ |  
sādhakāya dadānāti devatā parikīrtitāḥ ||  
  
rakṣyamāṇo hṛdātmāyaṃ hṛdayasti cidātmakaḥ |  
tasmāt tatra namaskuryān mukhyāṃguṣṭena saṃspṛśet ||  
  
svāhayā kriyate samyag viṣayā haraṇaṃ yataḥ |  
anāmātarjanībhyāṃ tairākṛṣṭaiḥ keniṣecyate ||  
  
śekhāmahovaṣaṭcāṃgaṃ śikhayātmatanurgrahaḥ |  
yasmāt tasmādvaṣaḍiti krīyaṃteṃgulamadhyayā ||  
  
grahaṇārthaṃ kavacadhāturddhūmahastena gṛhyate |  
śarīretastu kavacaṃ tarjanyā nāmayāpi tat ||  
  
yathārthajñānakadvau ṣaṭnanntretrābhyāṃ prajāyate |  
tasmāduktaṃ tatra vauṣaṭ tarjanyādaistu tat smṛtaṃ ||  
  
ekākṣarāt kuverādi daivateṅeṃtamuccaret |  
bhyāṃtaṃ visṇvādike rudrādau tu ne tantrayātmakaṃ ||  
  
ādhyātmikādi rūpaṃ yatsādhakasya vināśayet |  
avidyājātamastraṃ tat phaṭ tārābhyāṃ prapaṃcyate ||  
  
prāṇāyāmaṃ mātṛkāyāḥ kṛtvānyāsānsamācare |  
te caikaviṃśatiḥ proktā kāmanā bhedatopi ca ||  
  
adhikāri vibhedena nityatvenāpi kecana |  
devatā bhedato vāpi tadrahasyaṃ nirupyate ||  
  
puruṣe devate nityā kevalasvaramātṛkā |  
yannyāsā brahmacaryādyā dharmāḥ siddhyaṃti sādhake ||  
  
ṛṣirbrahmā devatā tu mātṛkākhya sarasvatī |  
halo vījāni gāyatrī chaṃdaḥ śaktiḥ svarāmatāḥ ||  
  
p. 79b)  
  
vyaktiḥ kīlakamuddiṣṭaṃ niyogobhīṣṭa siddhaye |  
dakṣa karatale tasya pṛṣṭe ca karabhe tathā ||  
  
aṃguṣṭhādiṣṭhatho vāme viparyāsena vinyaset |  
viṃdu yuktān krameṇaiva svarānyāsoyamādimaḥ ||  
  
ayaṃ vyatyāsatonyāsa saṃhāranyāsa ucyate |  
pāpaśatrukṣayādyarthe karmaścādau samācaret ||  
  
sa visargaiḥ svarairyastu kevale nyāsavat kṛtaḥ |  
sṛṣṭinyāsaḥ prayogādau kartavyastasya siddhaye ||  
  
vāmā karatalāt tasya kaniṣṭhāṃtaṃ pravinyaset |  
aṣṭau svarān ḷkātadīn tathā dakṣatalādapi ||  
  
akārādyānviṃdu sargayuktonāsoyamīritaḥ |  
sthityākhyo munidevādi prāgvat kāryasthitāvayaṃ ||  
  
kakārādi ṇakārāṃ tān varṇāt paṃcadaśaivahi |  
aṃguṣṭhādi kaniṣṭhāṃtaṃ dakṣahastasya parvasu ||  
  
nyasevinduyutān sarvān vāmepyevaṃ tu tādikān |  
aṃguṣṭhādi kaniṣṭhāṃtaṃ hastayugmopi vinyaset ||  
  
yugayatyādikān paṃcavrūyādvarṇa namoṃtakaṃ |  
tattatsthāne karaṃ datvā karaśuddhi karastvayaṃ ||  
  
aṃ āṃ madhyekavargaḥsyādi īṃ madhye ca vargakaḥ |  
uṃ ūṃ madhye ṭa vargastu e& ai& madhye ta vargakaḥ ||  
  
oṃ auṃ madhye pa vargaḥ syādaṃ aḥ madhya tu yādikāḥ |  
ebhiḥ sa viṃdukairaṃgulyādinyāso hṛdādikaḥ ||  
  
kartavyopyasya ṛṣyādi viniyogosya siddhaye |  
ṣaḍaṃga śuddhe krodhādi jātapāpa nivṛttayaḥ ||  
  
tālatrayaṃ ca digvaṃdhaṃ prakuryādastra maṃtrataḥ |  
tato dhyāyedvarṇapadmaṃ śvetaṃ svaśirasisthitaṃ ||  
  
karṇikāyāṃ nijaṃ maṃtraṃ saṃsmaret keśarāṣṭakaṃ |  
svarayugmaṃ tathā pātreṣvaṣṭasvapi ca kādikān ||  
  
saptavargānaṣṭame tu lakṣāvevaṃ viciṃtayet |  
evaṃ ciṃtayato rogādalpa mṛtyurvinaśyati ||  
  
athāṃtarmātṛkānyāsaṃvakṣyetaḥ śuddhikārakaṃ |  
yaṃ kṛtvā yoginī cittaṃ pātakena pravartate ||  
  
mūlādhāradvaniṃ śrutvā pravuddhā śaktikuṇḍalī |  
jvalatyāvakasaṃkāśāḥ susūkṣmā tejarūpiṇī ||  
  
mūlādhārācchiraḥ padmaṃ spṛśaṃtī vidyudākṛtī |  
jayāspṛṣṭhaśiraḥ padmādamṛtaudyaḥ svarūpiṇaḥ ||  
  
nirgatān mātṛkāvarṇān suṣumṇā vartmanā tanuṃ |  
sthāpayitvā sthitānetānevaṃ dhyātvā pravinyaset ||  
  
kaṇṭhe viśuddhi cakrākhyaṃ padmaṃ ṣoḍaśa patrakaṃ |  
urddhvāsyaṃ prāgdalāttatra saṃsthitāḥ ṣoḍaśaḥ svarā ||  
  
p. 80a)  
  
evaṃ saṃciṃtya tārādi viṃduyuktaṃ namoṃtakaṃ |  
vadet svaraṃ ca sarveṣu varṇeṣvapyeṣu paddhati ||  
  
hṛdayaṃ nāhataṃ cakraṃ dhyāyed dvādaśapatrakaṃ |  
pūrvapatrāttaddaleṣu prāgvatkādin pravinyaset ||  
  
maṇipūraṃ tataścakraṃ ciṃtayennābhimaṇḍale |  
daśapatraṃ tatra ḍādivarṇān prāgvad viciṃtayet ||  
  
svādhisthānaṃ liṃgamūle cakraṃ ṣaḍdalamucyate |  
ciṃtayedvādikāṃstatra ṣaḍvarṇānapi pūrvavat ||  
  
mūlādhārābhidhaṃ cakraṃ padmākṛti caturdalaṃ |  
vaṃ śaṃ ṣaṃ saṃ tatra ciṃtyaṃ pūrvāśādi daleṣu ca ||  
  
ājñākhyaṃ cakraṃ bhrūmadhye dvidalaṃ kamalākṛti |  
haṃ kṣaṃ dhyāyedayaṃ kāryo manasā kevalena tu ||  
  
svadehe vāmayā kāryaḥ puṣpeṇa suramūrtiṣu |  
anādilāna ṛṣyādi brahmavaddhyānamasya tu ||  
  
vahirnyāsamatho vakṣye pūrvokta brahmaraṃdhrake |  
varṇāraviṃde saṃdhyāyen mātṛkākhyāṃ sarasvatīṃ ||  
  
paṃcāśadvarṇabhedairvihitavadanadoḥ pādayukkukṣivakṣodeśāṃbhāsvat   
kapardīkalitaśaśikalāmiṃdu kuṃdā ca dātāṃ |  
akṣasrakkuṃbhacitya likhitavarakarāṃtrīkṣaṇāṃ padmasaṃsthāmacchākalpā   
manucchastanajaṃghanabharāṃ bhāratīṃtāṃ namāmi ||  
  
lalāṭe mukhavṛttekṣi śravornāsā sugaṃḍayoḥ |  
oṣṭayordaṃtapaṃktyośca mūrddhni vaktrenyasetsvarān ||  
  
vāhvoḥ saṃdhiṣu sāgreṣuka ca vargaunyasetsudhīḥ |  
tadavargaupadostadvatpārśvayoḥ pṛṣṭhadeśataḥ ||  
  
nābhau kukṣau pa vargaṃ ca hṛdaṃśakakuṃdaṃ tataḥ |  
nyasyayādi caturvarṇānśādi ṣaṭkaṃ tatonyaset ||  
  
hṛdādikarayoraṃghryorjaṭhare vadane tathā |  
nyāsastvayaṃ varṇamātrāhīnapāṭha prapūrakaḥ ||  
  
atha mātṛkāmudrāmāha ||  
  
lalāṭe nāsikāmadhyenyasecca mukhavṛttake |  
tarjanī madhyamānāmāvinyaseccaiva netrayoḥ ||  
  
tarjanyanāme saṃpūjya nyāset sādhakasattamaḥ |  
aṃguṣṭaṃ karṇayornyasya kaniṣṭhāṃguṣṭakaunasoḥ ||  
  
madhyamāgaṇḍayornyasya madhyamāmoṣṭayornyaset |  
anāmādaṃtayornyasya madhyamāṃ cottamāṃgake ||  
  
mukhenāmāṃ madhyamāṃ ca haste pāde ca pārśvayoḥ |  
kaniṣṭhānāmikāmadhyānnyastavyā pṛṣṭhatastathā ||  
  
sāṃguṣṭhāstānābhi deśe sarvāḥ kukṣau ca vinyaset |  
hṛdaye sādhakaḥ sarvamaṃśayoścaka kutsthale ||  
  
p. 80b)  
  
hapūrvahastapat kukṣimukheṣu talameva ca |  
etāstu mātṛkāmudrāḥ krameṇa parikīrtitāḥ ||  
  
ajñātvā vinyasedyastu nyāsaḥ syāt tasya niṣphalaḥ |  
kṣamārabhya akārāṃto nyāsaścatkriyate yadi ||  
  
saṃhāranyāsanāmāsau viṃdunyāsa itīritaḥ |  
vāmetra dakṣiṇemārge devatādhyānamucyate ||  
  
akṣasrajaṃ hariṇayotamudagraṭaṃkaṃ vidyāṃkarairucirataṃ dadhatīṃ trinetraṃ |  
arddhendu maulimaruṇāmaraviṃdavāsāṃ varṇeśvarīṃ   
praṇamatastanabhāraramrāṃ ||  
  
visargamātṛkānyāso bhavet kevalamātṛvat |  
viśeṣastu visargāṃto varṇoccāro bhavediti ||  
  
viṃdusargayutān ḍādiṭhāṃtān varṇānsthitau nyaset |  
pūrvoktā evamutpādyāḥ ṣaḍaṃgaṃ dhyānamucyate ||  
  
siṃdūrakāṃtimamitābharaṇāṃ trinetrāṃ vidyākṣasūtra mṛgapotavarāṃ   
dadhānāṃ |  
pārśvasthitāṃ bhagavatīmapikāṃvanābhāṃ dhyāyet karābja   
dhṛtapustakavarṇamālāṃ ||  
  
nyāsāḥ kāryāścatuḥ ṣaḍbhiḥsthiti saṃhārasṛṣṭayaḥ |  
saṃhārasṛṣṭiḥ sthitayo gṛhasyastu nyaset kramāt ||  
  
vāṇaprasthāścayatayaḥ sṛṣṭisthitilaya kramāt |  
nyāsān kuryuriti proktaḥ sthitinyāsaḥ savistaraḥ ||  
  
vakṣye kalā mātṛkāyānyāsaṃ tasya ṛṣiḥ smṛtaḥ |  
prajāpatiśca gāyatrī chaṃdanasyāstu devatā ||  
  
sarasvatī mātṛkāsyānniyogobhīṣṭatuṣṭaye |  
tāraiḥ ṣaḍaṃgaṃ kurvīta hrasvadīrghāṃtarasthitaiḥ ||  
  
hastaiḥ padmaṃ rathāṃgaṃ guṇamathahariṇaṃ pustakaṃ varṇamālāṃṭaṃkaṃ
