śubhraṃ kapālaṃdalamamṛtalamaddhvema kuṃbhaṃ vahaṃtīṃ |  
muktā vidyutyayodasphaṭikamaṇijapāvaṃdhuraiḥ paṃcavaktraiḥ   
stryakṣaivakṣojanamrāṃsakalaśaśinibhāṃ śāradāṃtāṃ namāmi ||  
  
dhyātvaivaṃ tārapūrvātāṃ makārādyāṃ ca mātṛkāṃ |  
viṃduyuktā ṅeṃta kalānāmādyāṃ rāmasānvitāṃ ||  
  
pūrvokta śuddhamātrāṇāṃ nyāsasthāneṣu vinyaset |  
nivṛttiśca pratiṣṭā ca viyāśāṃtistathaiṃdhikā ||  
  
dīpikā recikā cāpi bhocikā ca varābhidhā |  
sūkṣmāsūkṣmāmṛtā jñānāmṛtā cāpyāyanītataḥ ||  
  
vyāpinī vyomarūpā ca naṃtāsṛṣṭiḥ samṛddhikā |  
smṛtirmedhā tataḥ kāṃtirlakṣmīrdyatiḥ sthirāsthitiḥ ||  
  
siddhirjarāpālinī vakṣāṃtirīśvarikāratiḥ |  
kāmikā varadācānyāktvādinī prīti saṃyutā ||  
  
dīrghā tīkṣṇā tathā raudrī bhayānidrā ca taṃdrikā |  
kṣudhāsyāt krodhinī paścāt kriyotkārī sa mṛtyukāḥ ||  
  
p. 81a)  
  
pītāśvetāruṇā paścādatśinānaṃ tayānvitā |  
uktākalāmātṛkaivaṃ sthāneḥ kārādike nyaset ||  
  
tannanādātmano jātāḥ svarajāstu sadāśivāt |  
akṣamālā pustakaṃ ca pāśaṃ cāpi kapālakaṃ ||  
  
hastairdadhatyaḥ śvetābhāśvetāṃvaravibhūṣaṇāḥ |  
akārādbrahmaṇo jātāḥ ka ca varga kalādaśa ||  
  
pītā akṣasrajaṃ padmamabhayaṃ ca kamaṇḍaluṃ |  
hastairdadhatyo dhyeyāstāḥ pītagaṃdhānulepanāḥ ||  
  
viṣṇorukārāt saṃjātāḥ ṭatavargakalādaśa |  
śyāmā abhayaśaṃkhāsi varahastāḥ samīritāḥ ||  
  
makārādrudrato jātāḥ payavargakalānava |  
śaraccaṃdranibhā hastairabhayaṃ śūlameva ca ||  
  
kapālaṃ ca varaṃ dhyeyādadhatya iti sādhakaiḥ |  
ṣakārādika paṃcānāmīśvarādviṃtuto bhavet ||  
  
abhayaṃ hariṇaṃ ṭaṃkaṃ valaṃ ca karapallavaiḥ |  
dadhatyo raktavarṇāśca dhyeyānyāse kalāmake ||  
  
keśavādi mātṛkāyāḥ sādhyo nārāyaṇo * * (?) |  
amṛtādyā tu gāyatrī chaṃdo lakṣmīhariḥ suraḥ ||  
  
dviruktaiḥ śakti śrīkāmaiḥ ṣaḍaṃgāni samācaret |  
śaṃkhacakragadāpadmakuṃbhādarśābjapustakaṃ ||  
  
vibhraṃtaṃ megha capalāvarṇaṃ lakṣmīṃ hariṃ bhajet |  
śaktayastu priyāṃkeṣu niṣaṇāḥ sasmitānanāḥ ||  
  
evaṃ dhyātvānyasechaktiḥ śrīkāmapuṭitākṣaraṃ |  
tārādi hṛdayāṃtotha keśavādyāśca śaktayaḥ ||  
  
bhyāṃtā namoṃtā uccāryā sthāne'kārādike nyaset |  
kalāmātrā tu śāktānāṃ nityodyaṃ viṣṇusevināṃ ||  
  
keśavaḥ kīrtisaṃyuktaḥ kāṃtirnārāyaṇānvitā |  
mādhavastuṣṭi saṃyukto goviṃdaḥ puṣṭisaṃyutaḥ ||  
  
viṣṇuśca dhṛti saṃyuktaḥ śāṃtiyugmadhusūdanaḥ |  
trivikramaḥ kriyāyukto * * * * (?) sayānvitaḥ ||  
  
śrīdharo medhayā yukto hṛṣīkeśaśca harṣayā |  
padmanābhayutā śraddhālajjā dāmodarānvitā ||  
  
vāsudevaśca lakṣmīyuktaṃ karṣaṇasarasvatī |  
pradyumnaḥ prītisaṃyukto niruddhorati saṃyutaḥ ||  
  
cakrīgadājayīdurgāśārṅgī tu prabhayānvitaḥ |  
khaḍgī tu satyayāyukto śaṃkhīcaṇḍī samanvitaḥ ||  
  
halīvāṇī samāyukto muśalī ca vilāsinī |  
śūlāṃ ca vijayāyuktaḥpāṇī virajayānvitaḥ ||  
  
aṃkuśī viśvayāyukto mukuṃdo vinadāyutaḥ |  
naṃdajaḥ sunadāyukto naṃdīsmṛtya samanvitaḥ ||  
  
naro ṛddhyānarajitsamṛddhyā śuddhiyuk hariḥ |  
kṛṣṇo vudhyābhūtya satyomati yuktyātvataḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
  
p. 81b)  
  
śaurikṣameśūradamejanārdana umānvitaḥ |  
bhūdharaḥ kledinīyukto viśvamūrtiśca klinnayā ||  
  
vaikuṇṭho vasudhāyukto vasudhā puruṣottamau |  
valī tu parayāyukto valārujaparāyaṇe ||  
  
vālasūkṣmevṛṣaghnastu saṃdhyāyuktarayāvṛṣaḥ |  
haṃsaḥsyād dakṣiṇāmūrti gāyatrī chaṃda īritaḥ ||  
  
arddhādrijāharodevo niyogaḥ sarvasiddhaye |  
halovījāni guhye tu pādayoḥ svaraśaktayaḥ ||  
  
hrasvadīrghāntare kṛtvā prāgvadvargān hasaumasaṃ |  
ṣaḍdīrghasaṃyutān kṛtvā ṣaḍaṃgādinyasettanau ||  
  
vaṃdhūkakāṃcananibhaṃ rucirākṣamālāṃ pāśāṃkuśau ca varadaṃ nija   
vāhudaṇḍaiḥ |  
vibhrāṇamiṃduśakalābharaṇaṃ trinetramarddhāṃvikeśamaniśaṃ   
vapurāśrayāmaḥ ||  
  
hasauṃ te mātṛkā yuktā devā te ca samuccaret |  
ṅeṃtaṃ ṅeṃtāṃ ca tacchaktiṃ namoṃtāṃ mātṛkāsthale ||  
  
tvagasṛṅmāṃsamedocchimajjā śukrāṇyasūn vadet |  
śaktiṃ krodhaṃ tathātmānaṃ ṅeṃtaṃ yādi daśasvapi ||  
  
śrīkaṇṭhapūrṇodaryaucānaṃto virajayānvitaḥ |  
sūkṣmesaḥ śālmalīyukto lolākṣīyuk trimūrtikaḥ ||  
  
amaraśovartulākṣācārvīśodīrghaghoṇayā |  
bhārabhūtirdīrghamukhyātithīśo gomukhiyutaḥ ||  
  
sthāṇvīśo dīrghajihvāyugdharaḥ kuṇḍodarīyutaḥ |  
ūrddhvakeśyāvadgiṇṭhī śobhautiko vikṛtāsyayā ||  
  
sadyo jāto jvālamukhyānugraholkāmukhīyutaḥ |  
akrūre śrīmukhīmahāsane vidyāmukhīyutaḥ ||  
  
krodheśaśca mahākālyā caṇḍaśena sarasvatī |  
paṃcāṃtakaḥ sarvasiddhiḥ gauryāyuktaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
śivottameśo vinyasyo yuktastrailokya vidyayā |  
ekarudromaṃtraśaktyākūrmeśaścāṣṭa śaktiyuk ||  
  
ekanetro bhūmimātrā yuktothaḥ sa varānanaḥ |  
laṃbodaryoyutaḥ proktastvajeśodrāviṇī yutaḥ ||  
  
sarveśo nāgarīyuktaḥ someśaḥ khecarīyutaḥ |  
lāṃgalīśaśca maṃjaryādārukeśena rūpiṇī ||  
  
p. 82a)  
  
vīrīṇyācārddha nārīśohyumākāṃtaḥ punaryutaḥ |  
kākodaryā tathāṣāḍhī pūtanāyukta īritaḥ ||  
  
daṇḍīśo bhadrakālī yugatrīśo yoginīyutaḥ |  
mīneśaḥ śaṃkhinīyuktomeṣeśastarjanīyutaḥ ||  
  
lohitaḥ kālarātryā ca śikhīśaḥ kurddinīyutaḥ |  
chagalaṃḍaḥ kapardinyādviraṇḍeśaśca vajrayā ||  
  
mahākālojayāyukto vālīśaḥ sumukhīyutaḥ |  
bhujagorevatīyukto pinākī mādhavī yutaḥ ||  
  
khaḍgīśo vāruṇīyukto vakeśo vāyavīyutaḥ |  
śvetovakṣovadhāriṇyā bhṛguḥ sahajayā yutaḥ ||  
  
nakulīśālakṣmiyuktaḥ śiveśovyāpinīyutaḥ |  
saṃvartako mahāmāyāyukta etāstumātṛkāḥ ||  
  
śrīkaṇṭhādyāya īśāṃtastatraneśaṃ prayojayet |  
sarve rudrāḥ smṛtā raktādhṛta śūlakapālakāḥ ||  
  
śaktayo rudrapīṭhasthāḥ siṃdūrāruṇavigrahāḥ |  
raktotpala kapālābhyāmalaṃkṛta karāṃvujā ||  
  
yenopāsyā mahāvidyā daśatasyādhikāritā |  
bhuvaneśī vījapūrva mātṛkānyāsanesurāḥ ||  
  
ṛṣiḥ śaktistu gāyatrī chaṃdaḥ syānmātṛkāmayī |  
bhuvaneśī devatātha niyogaḥ sveṣṭasiddhaye ||  
  
hrasvadīrghāṃtaragataiḥ ṣaḍvargairdīrghasaṃyutaiḥ |  
prāgvaddharaiḥ ṣaḍaṃgaṃ syādaṃguṣṭhādi tathaiva ca ||  
  
udyat koṭidivākaraḥ pratibharāttuṃgorūpī na stanīvaddhārdhendu kirīṭahāra rasanā   
maṃjīra saṃśobhitā |  
vibhrājākara paṃkajairjapavaṭīṃpāśau pustakaṃ diśyānnojagadīśvarī   
trinayanāpadmeniyalpāmukhaṃ ||  
  
lajjāvījaṃ pūrvamuktvā mātṛkānyāsa eva hi |  
bhuvaneśī mātṛkāṇāṃ nyāsoktairyatra sādhane ||  
  
śrīvījapūrvakaḥ kāryo lakṣmīkāmairgṛhasthitaiḥ |  
ṛṣirbhṛguścagāyatrī chaṃdo mātṛḥsvarūpiṇī ||  
  
lakṣmīstu devatā proktā harasthāneśarau kuru |  
nyāsārthaṃ tu saḍaṃgāde śeṣaṃ śrīvījapūrvakaṃ ||  
  
vidyuddāma samaprabhāṃ himagiri prakhyaiścaturbhirbhujaiḥ śuṇḍā   
daṃḍasamuddhṛtā mṛtaghaṭairāsiṃcya mānāmimāṃ |  
vibhrāṇāṃ karapaṃkajairjapavaṭīṃ padmadvayaṃ pustakaṃ   
bhāsvadratnasamujvalāṃ kucanatāṃ dhyāyejjagatsvāminīṃ ||  
  
kāmanāmātra siddhyarthaṃ kāmavījādi pūrvakaṃ |  
kuryācca mātṛkānyāsaṃ muniḥ saṃmohanomataḥ ||  
  
p. 82b)  
  
gāyatrīchaṃda uddiṣṭaṃ devatā mātṛkāmayī |  
saṃmohanīnāmadevī pūrvayuktyā ṣaḍaṃgakaṃ ||  
  
vālārkakoṭirucirāṃ sphaṭikākṣamālāṃ kodaṇḍamikṣujanitaṃsmara   
paṃcavāṇān |  
vidyāṃ ca hastakamalairdathatīṃ trinetrāṃ dhyāyet samastajananīṃ   
navacaṃdracūḍāṃ ||  
  
śaktiḥ śrīkāmavījādi mātṛkānyāsato nṛṇāṃ |  
śatrutvādyāmaṃtradoṣo naśyaṃti vahuvarṇatāḥ ||  
  
mahāsaṃmohana ṛṣirgāyatrīchaṃda īritaḥ |  
saṃmohanīnāmadevīnyāsaḥ prāṅmātṛkāsamaḥ ||  
  
dhyāyeyamakṣavalayekṣu śarāśapāśapadmadvayāṃkuśaśarānnavapustakaṃ ca   
|  
āvibhratīṃ nijabhujairaruṇāṃ kurvārtāṃ saṃmohinīṃ trinayanāṃ   
navacaṃdracūḍāṃ ||  
  
sarvavighnanirāsārthamavaśyaṃ nyāsamācaret |  
gaṇeśamātṛkāyāṃturmunirgaṇaka īritaḥ ||  
  
nivadgāyatrikācchaṃdo devaśakti vināyakaḥ |  
smṛtvā dīrghāḍhyayātvaṃgaṃ kṛtvā dhyāyed gajānanaṃ ||  
  
śūlāṃkuśa varābhīti pāṇiṃ raktābjahastayā |  
priyayāliṃgiṃtaṃraktaṃ trinetraṃ gaṇayaṃbhaje ||  
  
evaṃ dhyātvā nyaset svīyavīja pūrvākṣarānvitaṃ |  
vighnohrīṃ samāyukto vighnarājaḥ śriyādyutaḥ ||  
  
vināyakaḥ puṣṭiyuktaḥ śāktiyuktaḥ śivottamaḥ |  
vighnakṛt sṛṣṭisaṃyukto vighnahartā sarasvatī ||  
  
gamāstu svāhayāyukta ekadaṃtastu medhayā |  
dvidaṃtaḥ kāṃti saṃyukto gajavaktreṇakāminī ||  
  
niraṃjano kāminī yukkapardī tu nadīyutaḥ |  
dīrghajihvaḥ pārvatīyuk jvālinyāśaṃkukarṇakaḥ ||  
  
vṛṣadhvajonaṃdayāyuk sudyaśāgaṇanāyakau |  
gajeṃdraḥ kāmarūpiṇyāsūrpakarṇastathomayā ||  
  
trilocanastejovatyālaṃvodarastu satyayā |  
mahānaṃdaśca vighneśyāścaturmūrtiḥ svarūpayā ||  
  
sadāśivaḥ kāmadāyugmādonmadadvijihvayā |  
durmukhobhūti saṃyuktaḥ sumukho bhautikāyutaḥ ||  
  
prabhedaḥ sitayāyukta ekapādoramāyutaḥ |  
dvijihvo mahiṣīyuktaḥ śūlasyāpi bhujaṃginī ||  
  
vīrovikarṇayāyuktaḥ ṣaṇmukho bhṛkuṭīyutaḥ |  
varadorajjayā vāmadevaḥsyāddīrghakoṇayā ||  
  
p. 83a)  
  
dhanurddharācakratuṇḍau dviraṇḍo jāminīyutaḥ |  
senānī rātrisaṃyuktaḥ kāmāṃdhogrāmaṇīyutaḥ ||  
  
mattaḥ śaśiprabhāyukto vimattololalocanā |  
mattavāhana cāṃcalye jaṭīdīptiḥ samanvitaḥ ||  
  
maṃḍī subhagayā yuktaḥ khaḍgīdurbhagayā tathā |  
vareṇyaśca śivāyukto bhagīyugvṛṣaketana ||  
  
bhaktapriyo bhaginyā tu gaṇeśo bhoginīyutaḥ |  
meghanādaḥ subhagayā vyāpī syāt kālarātriyuk ||  
  
gaṇeśvaraḥ kāliketi prokto vighneśamātṛkā |  
tvagādi yogoyādīnāṃ pūrvavat parikīrtitaḥ ||  
  
prapaṃcayoganyāsotha vakṣyate bhuktimuktidaḥ |  
mahāgaṇeśamaṃtreṇa prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ caret ||  
  
ṛṣiḥ prapaṃcayāgasya gaṇakaḥ chaṃda īritaḥ |  
gāyatrī tu nivṛtpūrvā mahāgaṇapatiḥ suraḥ ||  
  
śrīrṣādiṣu nyasettāṃśca gaṃvījaṃ cāpi guhyake |  
svāhāśaktiḥ pādayośca niyogobhīṣṭa siddhaye ||  
  
oṃ śrī& hrī& klī& glau& gamiti pūrvaṃ ṣaḍdīrghayuktakaṃ |  
uccārya kuryādaṃgāni tathāṃguṣṭādiṣu nyaset ||  
  
tālatrayaṃ tathāstreṇa kṛtvā digvaṃdhamācaret |  
tarjanyaṃguṣṭhaśabdena daśadikṣvatha ciṃtayet ||  
  
hastīṃdrānanamiṃdu cūḍamaruṇacchādyaṃ trinetraṃ rasādāśliṣṭaḥ priyayā sa   
padmakarayāsvāṃkasthayāsaṃtataṃ |  
vījāpūragadādhanustriśūlaśirayuk   
cakrābjapāśotpalavrīhyagrasvaviṣāṇaratnakalaśān hastairvahaṃtaṃ bhaje ||  
  
mahāgaṇapatermaṃtraṃ maṣṭavāraṃ japettataḥ |  
gamityakākṣaraṃ vījaṃ gaṇakosya munirmataḥ ||  
  
devo vighneśvaracchaṃdaṃ nivṛdgāya trināyakaṃ |  
prapaṃcākhyasya yāgasya sāṃgatā siddhī hetave ||  
  
catuścatvāriṃśat saṃkhyajapārthe viniyojanaṃ |  
atha ṣaḍdīrghayuktena kuryādaṃgāniena tu ||  
  
taṃtapāśāṃkuśa varakara akṣaṃ caturdalaṃ |  
siṃdūrābhaṃ caṃdramauliṃ sarpabhūṣaṃgalanmadaṃ ||  
  
ekavāraṃ japet paścādgaṇānāṃ tveti vaidikaṃ |  
gaṇeśamālāmaṃtrasya munistu gaṇakaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
  
chaṃdo'mitaṃ gaṇapatirdevatā parikīrtitā |  
hrī& kro& tāro namaḥ sarve ṅeṃtaṃ vidyādhipastataḥ ||  
  
sarvārthasiddhidāyeti sarvaduḥkhapraśeti ca |  
tato gaṇapa ehyehi bhagavat svādayeti ca ||  
  
p. 83b)  
  
staṃbhayeti dvayaṃ hrī& ga& gā& namopyagni gehinī |  
kro& hrī&miti paṃcapaṃcāśadvarṇāmaṃtra ucyate ||  
  
japedidaṃ caturvāraṃ munyādi sahitānyaset |  
nyāsaḥ pūrvaṃ trivāraṃ tu mātṛkā dhyānapūrvakaṃ ||  
  
svarādiḥ sasavargaistu grahānsasamudīritaḥ |  
prapaṃcayāga maṃtrasya munirbrahmā samīritaḥ ||  
  
paramādyā samākhyātā gāyatrī chaṃda uttamaṃ |  
mahaḥ paraṃ samākhyātaṃ devatā cinmayātmakaṃ ||  
  
apyaṃte vodhitaṃ nityaṃ sarvavyāpī niraṃjanaṃ |  
vilomagaiḥ paṃcaparaiḥ prapaṃca manusaṃsthitaiḥ ||  
  
hrasvadīrghāṃtasthakādivargaiḥ pūrvaṃ samanvitaiḥ |  
tāramāyādikairastrairyuktairhariharākṣaraiḥ ||  
  
ṣaḍaṃgāni prakurvīta jātiyuktānideśikaḥ ||  
  
vedādi paṃcamanubhiḥ paricīyamānaṃ mānairagamyamaniśaṃ jagadekamūlaṃ |  
saccitsamastagamanaścaramacyutaṃ tattejaḥ paraṃ bhajatasāṃdra   
kṛpāṃvurāśiṃ ||  
  
vedādimāyayoraṃtekṣakārādyān sa viṃdukān |  
pṛthaguccāryahaṃsaḥ soyaṃ svāheti vadan hṛdi ||  
  
vibhāvayedimān varṇānātma vahnau juhomyahaṃ |  
evaṃ hutvā akārāṃtamakārādyānpunarhunet ||  
  
visargāṃtān kṣakārāṃtaṃ vinyasen mātṛkāsthale |  
evaṃ prapaṃcayāgākhyo mātṛkānyāsa īritaḥ ||  
  
ātmavidyā śivaistatvaistatvanyāsaṃ samācaret |  
pādādinābhiparyaṃtamātmatatvaṃ prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
nābhyādi hṛdayāṃtaṃ hiṃ vidyātatvaṃ prakīrtitaṃ |  
hṛdayāddviṃduparyaṃtaṃ śivatatvaṃ prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
mūlamaṃtra trikhaṇḍāṃte krameṇaiva pravinyaset |  
sarvamaṃtraṃ samuccārya sarvāṃge vyāpakaṃ śive ||  
  
sarvatatvamidaṃ proktaṃ sarvadevatvakārakaṃ |  
tithi tatvāni deveśi ātmatatve bhavaṃti hi ||  
  
paṃcaviṃśati tatvāni vidyātatvaṃ bhavaṃti hi |  
ṣaṭtriṃśacchaivatatvāni śivatatve bhavaṃti hi ||  
  
atha paṃcāśat tatvāni sarvatatve bhavaṃti hi |  
etannyāmāṃtare yogapīṭhākhyaṃ nyāsamācaret ||  
  
tatpūrvamuktaṃ ca tataḥ sveṣṭamaṃtrasya saṃcaret |  
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā mūlamaṃtreṇa sādhakaḥ ||  
  
vinyaset tadṛṣiḥ chaṃdo daivatāni yathāvidhi |  
atha ṛṣyādinyāsa krameṇasthānāni mudrāścāha ||  
  
p. 84a)  
  
ṛṣinyaset mūrddhnideśe chaṃdastu mukhapaṃkaje |  
devatāṃ hṛdaye caiva vījaṃ tu guhyadeśake ||  
  
śaktiṃ ca pādayoścaiva sarvāṃge kīlakaṃ smṛtaṃ |  
ṛṣyādīnvinyaseddevi caturthī hṛdayāṃtakān ||  
  
athāsya mudrā |  
  
ṛṣiḥ chaṃdo devatānāṃ nyāseyyaṃgulaya smṛtāḥ |  
catasroṃguṣṭarahitāḥ śaktyaṃtaṃ vinyaset tataḥ ||  
  
kīlakaṃ vyastahastābhyāṃ sarvāṃge sādhakāgraṇī ||  
  
athavā ||  
  
vināṃguṣṭāmaṃgulibhiḥ saṃyutābhiḥ ṛṣiṃ nyaset |  
vāmāgrābhiḥ punastābhi vinyasenmukhapaṃkaje ||  
  
sarvābhirhṛdaye prāktā gude pāde tathāgrataḥ |  
karābhyāṃ vinyaseddhīmān sarvāṅge cakramādviduḥ |  
  
aghāṃganyāsamudrā ||  
  
kaniṣṭhāṃguṣṭharahitai stribhistu hṛdi vinyaset |  
madhyamā tarjanībhyāṃ tu nyasecchirasi maṃtravit ||  
  
aṃguṣṭhena śikhānyasya daśabhiḥ kavaca nyaset |  
hṛdgatairnetravinyāsaṃ vinyaset parameśvarī ||  
  
tarjanī madhyamābhyāṃ tu tatostraṃ vinyaset priye |  
ṣaḍaṃgaṃ vinyasenmaṃtrī hṛdayāya namo vadet ||  
  
sva sva maṃtraṃ samuccārya śirasya vahni vallabhā |  
skaṃdhamadhye nyaset paścāt śikhāyevaṣaḍityapi ||  
  
kavacāya vāhumūle kūrcavījaṃ samuccaret |  
netra trayebhyo vauṣaḍityaṃtaṃ netra tato nyaset ||  
  
karayorvinyasenmaṃtrī astrāya ca phaḍityapi ||  
  
athāsyārthamāha ||  
  
hṛdayāyeti śabdena hṛstho devaḥ sa vigraha |  
ucyate nama ityasya jñānaṃ tadviṣayaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
śiraḥ śabdo devatāyā utkṛṣṇatvābhidhāyakaḥ |  
svāheti viṣayāḥ sarvedevatāyāṃ samarpitāḥ ||  
  
śikhāyaiva svarūpatvaṃ vaṣaḍapi taducyate |  
devatāyā vyāpakatvaṃ kavacāyābhidhīyate ||  
  
hūmapi vyāpakaṃ tejo devatāyāḥ prakāśyate |  
netra śabdena devasya prakāśyatvaṃ prakāśyate ||  
  
vauṣaḍapita daivoktā maṃtraśabdena vāraṇāṃ |  
aniṣṭasya phaṭ śabdena dāhakaṃ teja ucyate ||  
  
jñātvaiva maṃgamaṃtrārtha maṃganyāsaṃ karoti yaḥ |  
pracayāstasya sarvārthāḥ pūjyate stridaśairapi ||  
  
karāṃganyāsamukhyāstu nyāsānanyān samācaret |  
āgamokto na mārgeṇa nyāsānnityaṃ karoti yaḥ ||  
  
devatābhāvamāpnoti maṃtrasiddhiḥ prajāyate |  
yonyāsaḥ kavacācchaṃdo maṃtraṃ japati yaḥ priye ||  
  
dṛṣṭvā vighnāḥ palāyaṃte siṃhaṃ dṛṣṭvā yathā gajā |  
akṛtvā nyāsajālaṃ yo mūḍhātmā kuruttejayaṃ ||  
  
p. 84b)  
  
vighnaiḥ sa vādhyate nūnaṃ vyāghrairmṛgaśiśuryathā |  
nyāsānāṃ pracuratvena phalānāmapi bhūritā ||  
  
ukta nyāso na hi tyājyaḥ tvadhikaṃ kāmataścaret ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau sādhāraṇanityārcanāyāṃ   
pūjāmaṇḍapapraveśanādinyāsajālāṃtanirṇayo nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ prakāśaḥ || 16 ||  
  
athāṃtarvidhiḥ ||  
  
evaṃ dehamaye pīṭhe ciṃtayediṣṭadevatāṃ |  
dhyānaṃ kuryāttato maṃtrī tattatkalpoktavartmanā ||  
  
tadapi dvividhaṃ proktaṃ sa guṇaṃ nirguṇaṃ tathā |  
ātmano hṛdayāṃbhoje karṇikā keśarojvare ||  
  
praphulle somasūryāgni maṇḍalena virājite |  
svīyeṣṭadevatāṃ tatra yajedāgamavodhitāṃ ||  
  
evaṃ yadvedanaṃ taddhi saguṇaṃ dhyānamucyate |  
athāṃtaryyajanaṃ vakṣye dṛṣṭādṛṣṭa phalapradaṃ ||  
  
yogināṃ yena jāyaṃte adhīrā mānavāḥ sadā ||  
  
śrīdevyuvāca |  
  
vāhyapūjāṃ vinā svāmin kathamaṃtaḥ prapūjanaṃ |  
pūjājñānaṃ yadājātaṃ tadāṃtaḥ pūjanaṃ bhavet ||  
  
sāmagrī jñānahīṃnatvāt kathamaṃtaḥ prapūjanaṃ ||  
  
śrīśiva uvāca ||  
  
satyametanmaheśāni rahasyaṃ śṛṇu yatnataḥ |  
viṣṭhāpūrṇe svādare tu vahiḥ śuddhau tu kiṃ phalaṃ ||  
  
aṃtaḥ śuddhiṃ samāsādya vahiḥ śuddhiṃ samācaret |  
vahiḥ pūjāvidhau devi samāgrīdurmilākalau ||  
  
vyaṃgyatā jāyate satyaṃ sarvatra pūjane śive |  
tatsāṃgatāsiddhihetoraṃtaḥ pūjā prakīrtitā ||  
  
bhāvanāmātragamyevaṃ koṭiratnāni kalpayet |  
aṃtaḥ pūjāvihīnena kṛtaṃ tadaphalaṃ bhavet ||  
  
saṃyogaṃ tu vinā devi yo garbhādhānamicchati |  
savāṃtaḥ pūjanaṃ tyaktvā vahiḥ pūjāṃ sa micchati ||  
  
sadaridrī mahāghorī kathamatra sukhaṃ bhavet |  
aṃtaḥ pūjāṃ samāsādya vahiḥ pūjāṃ samācaret ||  
  
saṃbhāvya pūjanaṃ svāṃte tathaiva racayedvahiḥ ||  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
tathyamuktaṃ tvayādeva saṃśayomesti śaṃkara |  
vahiḥ pūjanamāsādyacāṃtaḥ pūjāṃ samācaret ||  
  
evaṃ krameṇa deveśi pūjā kinna bhaviṣyati ||  
  
śiva uvāca ||  
  
mṛdapakvaṃ samāsādya yathā devi ghaṭodbhavet |  
ghaṭaḥ pakva mṛdādevi pūrvavat kiṃ bhaviṣyati ||  
  
apakvāṃ mṛtsamānīya yathā devi ghaṭo bhavet |  
tataḥ pakvaṃ prakartavyaḥ suṃdaraḥ sa tu jāyate ||  
  
p. 85a)  
  
aṃtarpunarvahiḥ pūrṇaṃ vahiḥ pūrṇatarā bhavet |  
anyonyāśraya saṃyogāt pūjanaṃ sakalaṃ bhavet ||  
  
devo bhūtvā yajeddevaṃ nā devo devamarcayet |  
tasyāddevatvamāsādya cāṃtaḥ pūjādimārgataḥ ||  
  
gurordhyānaṃ prakurvīta yathā pūrvaṃ viśāladhīḥ ||  
  
iti brāhmīmuhūrtakṛtyaṃ ||  
  
snānaṃ budhastataḥ kuryāt saccidānaṃda siddhaye |  
snāyācca vimale tīrthe puṣkare hṛdayāśrite ||  
  
viṃdutīrthe naraḥ snāyāt punarjanma na vidyate ||  
  
iti snānaṃ ||  
  
mūlādhārāt kuṇḍalinīmutthāpya yojayecchive |  
śivaśaktyoḥ samāyogo yasmin kāle prajāyate ||  
  
sā saṃdhyākulaniṣṭānāṃ samādhistaiḥ pragīyate ||  
  
iti saṃdhyā ||  
  
caṃdrārkānalasaṃghaṭṭādgalitaṃ yatparāmṛtaṃ |  
tenāmṛtena divyena tarpayet paradevatāṃ ||  
  
brahmaraṃdhrā dadhobhāge yaccāṃdraṃ pātramuttamaṃ |  
kalāsāreṇa saṃpūrya tarpayettena khecarīṃ ||  
  
iti tarpaṇaṃ ||  
  
ādhāre liṅganābhau hṛdayasarasije tālumūle lalāṭedvepatre ṣoḍaśāre   
dvidaśadaśadale dvādaśārddhe catuṣke |  
vāsāṃte vālamadhye uphakaṭha sahite kaṇṭhamūle   
svarāṃścahakṣaukodaṇḍamadhyenya sa tu vimaladhīnyā sa saṃpatti siddhyai ||  
  
ityaṃtarmātṛkānyāsaḥ ||  
  
athāṃtara ṣaḍaṃganyāsaḥ ||  
  
sahasrāre maṇinibhe sarvavarṇa vibhūṣite |  
akathādi trirekhādyairhalakṣatrayabhūṣite ||  
  
tanmadhye paraviṃduṃ ca sṛṣṭisthitilayātmakaṃ |  
evaṃ samāhitamanādhyāyennyāsoyamāṃtaraḥ ||  
  
mulādi brahmaraṃdhrāṃtaṃ viṃdvaṃ dhyāyaiccidātmakaṃ |  
viṃdusrutasudhāsāraistarpayanmātṛkāṃnyaset ||  
  
ekaikaṃ varṇamuccārya mūlādhārādbhruvāṃtikaṃ |  
namoṃta iti vinnyāsaḥ āṃtaraḥ parikīrtitaḥ ||  
  
hṛdyānmāno hṛdātmāyaṃ hṛdayesyāccidātmakaṃ |  
kriyate tatparatvena hṛnmaṃtreṇa tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
sarvajñādi guṇāttuṃge saccidrūpe parātmani |  
kriyayā viṣayāhāraḥ śiromaṃtreṇa deśikaiḥ ||  
  
hṛcchirorūpaviddhāmalayatā bhāvanādṛṭā |  
kriyate nijadehasya śikhāmaṃtreṇa deśikaiḥ ||  
  
p. 85b)  
  
maṃtrātmakasya dehasya maṃtra vāhye tejasā |  
sarvato varma maṃtreṇa kriyate'hanyasaṃvṛtiḥ ||  
  
yaddadāti paraṃ jñānaṃ saccidrūpe parātmani |  
hṛdayādi mayaṃ tejaḥ syādetannetra saṃjñitaṃ ||  
  
ādhyātmikādi rūpaṃ ca sādhakasya vināśayet |  
avidyājālamastraṃ tatparaṃdhāma samīritaṃ ||  
  
atha dhyānaṃ ||  
  
kiraṇasthaṃ tadagnisthaṃ caṃdrabhāskaramadhyagaṃ |  
mahāśūnyelayaṃ kṛtvā pūrṇaḥ tiṣṭhati yogirāṭ ||  
  
yajjīva brāhmaṇoraikyaṃ sohaṃsyāmiti vedanaṃ |  
tadeva nirguṇaṃ dhyānaṃmiti vedavidoviduḥ ||  
  
iti dhyānaṃ ||  
  
athārccanaṃ ||  
  
arccayedvividhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ tatkṣaṇāttanmayo bhavet |  
nyāsastanmayatāvuddhiḥ sohaṃ bhāvena pūjayet ||  
  
kṣamāyāmanahaṃkāramanāgamamadaṃ tathā |  
amohakaṃmadaṃ daṃbhamadvevākṣomakau tataḥ ||  
  
amātsaryyamalobhaṃ ca daśapuṣpaṃ vidurbudhāḥ |  
ahiṃsā paramaṃ puṣpaṃ puṣpamiṃdriya nigrahaḥ ||  
  
dayāpuṣpaṃ kṣamāpuṣpaṃ jñānapuṣpaṃ ca paṃcamaṃ |  
ityuktairuttamaiḥ puṣpaiḥ pūjayet paradevatāṃ ||  
  
ityārcanaṃ ||  
  
mālāpaṃcāśikī proktā sūtraṃ śaktiśivātmakaṃ |  
grathitā kuṇḍalī śaktiḥ kalāṃte merusaṃsthitiḥ ||  
  
iti japaḥ ||  
  
atha homaḥ ||  
  
mūlādhāragate kuṇḍe devatāgniḥ samujjvale |  
dharmādharmānvite tryasre mūlamaṃtrapuraḥsaraṃ ||  
  
ahaṃ juhomi svāheti pratyekaṃ juhuyāt sudhīḥ |  
ahaṃtā'satyapaiśunya kāmakrodhādikaṃ haviḥ ||  
  
mana eva śrūvaḥ prokta unmanī mugudīritā ||  
  
atha mūlāṃte ||  
  
nābhau caitanya rūpāgnau haviṣā manasā srucā |  
jñānapradīpite nityamakṣavṛttījuhomyahaṃ ||  
  
svāhā iti prathamāhutiḥ ||  
  
mūlāṃte ||  
  
aṃtarniriṃdhana nivaṃdhana medhamāna māyāṃdhakāraparipaṃthini saṃvidagnau   
|  
kasmiṃścidadbhutamarīcivikāśabhūmau viśvaṃ juhomi vasudhādivakhāvasānaṃ   
||  
  
svāhā iti caturthāhutiḥ ||  
  
ityaṃtaryajanaṃ kṛtvā sākṣādbrahmamayo bhavet |  
na tasya pāpapuṇyāni jīvanmukto bhaveddhruvam ||  
  
p. 86a)  
  
ityaṃtaryajanaṃ ||  
  
atha vahiryajanaṃ ||  
  
tatrādāvarghyādi sthāpana ||  
  
mūlamaṃtreṇātha vāmesvasya devāgrataścaret |  
vṛttena veṣṭite samyak trikoṇaṃ caṃdanāṃbhasā ||  
  
tadvahiścaturasraṃ ca vidadhyānmatsyamudrayā |  
saṃpūjya gaṃdhairdevārghyamaṇḍalāya namodhunā ||  
  
aṃgāni caturagnyādi koṇeṣu puratastathā |  
dikṣu cāstraṃ samabhyarcya śaṃkhādhāraṃ pravinyaset ||  
  
ādhāreṇa vinā bhraṃśo na tṛpyaṃti ca mātaraḥ |  
tasmādvidhivadādhāraṃ tripadaṃ vā catuṣpadaṃ ||  
  
padmābhaṃ vā trikoṇaṃ vāyonyābhaṃ vā bhujaṃ tu tat |  
mūlāṃte vāmukādhārapātraṃ saṃsthāpayāmi ca ||  
  
uktvāśaṃkhādikādhāraṃ maṇḍale sthāpayedathamaṃraṃ dharmapradetyuktvā   
vaded daśakalātmakaṃ |  
  
ṅente vahnermaṇḍalaṃ ca deva nāma ca kīrtayet |  
tatorghapātradhārāya namaḥ proktvā prapūjayet ||  
  
vahnerdaśakalāḥ pūjyāstatra ca prokta pradakṣiṇaṃ |  
astramaṃtreṇa ca tataḥ kanadrādi vinirmitaṃ ||  
  
arghadi pātramatha vā śaṃkhamastrānunājalaiḥ |  
prakṣālyāmukadevārghapātraṃ pratisthāpayāmi ||  
  
evamuktvā tadādhāre saṃsthāpyaivaṃ vadet punaḥ |  
arthapradedvādaśeti kalātmane vadet tataḥ ||  
  
sūryamaṇḍalamuccārya ṅeṃtaṃ devasyanāma tu |  
arghapātrāya ca namo manunānena pūjayet ||  
  
tatpātramatha tatraiva bhāvayed bhūmimaṇḍalaṃ |  
ṣaṭkoṇaṃ tatra cāṃgāni pūjayet pūrvavat tataḥ ||  
  
kalādvādaśa sūryasya proktapātre pradakṣiṇaṃ |  
tataḥ sudhāmayaistoyairmūlāṃte mātṛkāpaṭhen ||  
  
vilomāṃ pūrayet tasmin pūjako manunāmunā |  
oṃ śaṃkāmapradet yuktvā ṣoḍaśeti kalātmane ||  
  
namaḥ paṃcadaśārṇoyaṃ maṃtraḥ śaṃkhaḥ prapūraṇe |  
gaṃdhapuṣpākṣatadyava kuśāgratila sarṣapān ||  
  
dūrvā ityarghya pātrasya proktaṃ dravyāṣṭakaṃ surā |  
tatoyaṃ gaṃdhapuṣpādyaiḥ pūjayitvā samarcayet ||  
  
kalā ṣoḍaśakaṃ cāṃdraṃ paścāt sarvakalāsu ca |  
praṇapratikurvīta pūjāṃte sādhakastataḥ ||  
  
prāgvattīrthaṃ samāvāhya mūlamaṃtreṇa tatra tu |  
saṃyojya netramaṃtreṇa puṣpaṇyasya śikhāmunā ||  
  
pradarśyagālinīṃ mudrāṃ mudrayādhenu saṃjñayā |  
amṛtīkṛtya vidhivat sudhāvījena sādhakaḥ ||  
  
dhyātveṣṭa devatāṃ tatra sakalīkaraṇaṃ caret |  
aṃganyāsena vāstreṇa kalayecca diśodaśaḥ ||  
  
p. 86b)  
  
netramaṃtreṇa saṃvīkṣya mudrayā śaṃkhasaṃjñayā |  
avaṣṭabhya tato dīpyamudrayā yonirūpayā ||  
  
gaṃdhapuṣpādibhistatra pūjayediṣṭadevatāṃ |  
ṣaḍaṃgāni ca saṃpūjyamaṃtrayen mūlamaṃtrataḥ ||  
  
aṣṭakṛtvastataścārghyaṃ chādayet matsyamudrayā ||  
  
gālinyādi mudrā yathā ||  
  
kaniṣṭāṃguṣṭhakau saktau karayoritaretaraṃ |  
tarjanī madhyamānāmāsahitābhūgnavarjitāḥ ||  
  
mudraiṣāgālinī proktā śaṃkhasyo paripālitā |  
anyonyābhimukhāśliṣṭākaniṣṭhānāmikā punaḥ ||  
  
tathā ca tarjjanī madhyā dhenumudrā mṛtapradā |  
vāmapuṣpeṃtareṃguṣṭhaṃ niveśyasanarāṃguliḥ ||  
  
dakṣiṇasya karasyaiva vāmāṃguṣṭhena saṃspṛśet |  
śaṃkhamudreyamākhyātā vidvadbhiśca susaṃmatā ||  
  
madhyame kuṭilekārye tarjanyu parisaṃsthite |  
anāmike madhyagate tathaiva ca kaniṣṭhake ||  
  
sarvā ekatra saṃyojya aṃguṣṭha paripīḍitāḥ |  
yonimudrā samākhyātā trailokyotpattimātṛkā ||  
  
dakṣepāṇiḥ pṛṣṭhadeśe vāmapāṇitalaṃ kṣipet |  
aṃguṣṭhau cālayet paścātmudreyaṃ matsyarūpiṇī ||  
  
iti viśeṣārghyavidhiḥ ||  
  
athārghyādi pātrasaṃkhyāmāha ||  
  
arghyasya trīṇipātrāṇi pādyasyāpi trayaṃ bhavet |  
tathā ca mana patrāṇi syuradyekataraṃ bhavet ||  
  
eka pātraṃ na kartavyaṃ yadi sākṣānmaheśvara |  
maṃtrābhyarānmukhāyāṃti āpadaśca pade pade ||  
  
ihaloke ca dāridryaṃ mṛte ca narakaṃ vrajet |  
tataḥ sādhārakaṃ pātraṃ purataḥ sthāpayedbudhaḥ ||  
  
tatpārśve pādyapātraṃ ca tatpārśverghya pradāyakaṃ |  
ācamanīyaṃ ca tatpārśve tadvāme madhuparkakaṃ ||  
  
punarācamanīyaṃ ca snānīyaṃ cakramānnyaset |  
tacchaṃkhasthaṃ jalaṃ kiṃcit kuṃbhato ye viniḥkṣipet ||  
  
ekaikapātraṃ mūlena jyeṣṭhaṃ kṛtvābhi maṃtrayet |  
madhuparkastu sakṣaudraṃ dadhitacca na labhyate ||  
  
dadhidugdhaṃguḍakṣaudreghṛtapratinidhirnahi |  
paramaṃ yatpadaṃ devāmadhusaṃjñaṃ taducyate ||  
  
tadāpyete yena karmatatproktaṃ madhuparkakaṃ |  
kāṃsasya vātha raupyasya śaiveśaṃkha varoharau ||  
  
mahāśaṃkhe vāmamārge sphāṭikaṃ grahanāyake |  
dakṣiṇe prokṣaṇī pātraṃ mādāyābhiḥ prapūrayet ||  
  
p. 87a)  
  
kiṃcidarghaṃ tu saṃgṛhya prokṣaṇyaṃbhasi yojayet |  
punarācamanīyārthaṃ pātraṃ saṃsthāpayet tataḥ ||  
  
pādyaṃ śyāmākadūrvāja viṣṇukrāṃtābhirucyate |  
jātīlaṃvaṃgakaṃ kolaiṣkṛtamācamanīyakaṃ ||  
  
kuśapuṣpayava vrīhi vahumūlatamālakaṃ |  
dāpayet prokṣaṇī pātraṃ bhasitaṃ praṇavena ca ||  
  
śuddhābhiradbhirvihitaṃ punarācamanīyakaṃ |  
dravyābhāve pradātavyāḥ kṣālitāstaṇḍulāḥ śubhāḥ ||  
  
athārghyādi pātrāṇāṃ phalaṃ vakṣye śubhāśubhaṃ |  
sarvakāmapradaṃ svarṇaṃ raupyamāyuḥ sutapradaṃ ||  
  
saubhāgyaṃ tāmrapātreṇa dharmavṛddhistu mṛnmaye |  
nārikeledevatuṣṭidaṃkāca saṃbhavaṃ ||  
  
lakṣmī prāptirvilvapatra brāhmaṇyaṃ brahmavṛkṣaje |  
māraṇoccāṭane lohaṃ staṃbhaḥ pāṣāṇaje bhavet ||  
  
maṃtrasyārādhane kāṣṭaṃ vāmamārge tu tauṃvike |  
ratnādīnāṃ tu pātrāṇi śubharekhāṃkitāni ca ||  
  
arghanaivedyapūjārthavalidāne prakalpayet |  
pātrāṇāmādaraḥ kāryaḥ pātrāṇyavottamāni tu ||  
  
valihoma kriyādyaṃ hi vinā pātraṃ na siddhyati |  
ṣaṭtriṃśadaṃgulaṃ pātraṃ muttamaṃ parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
madhyamaṃ tu tribhāgonaṃ kaniṣṭhaṃ dvādaśāṃgulaṃ |  
vasvaṃgula vihīnaṃ tu na pātraṃ kārayet kvacit ||  
  
nāmīvivararūpāṇi puṇḍarīkā kṛtāni ca |  
śaṃkhanīlotpalābhāni pātrāṇi praikalpayet ||  
  
śvetādītpatiśastāni viprādīnāṃ krameṇa ca |  
secayet prokṣaṇī pātratoyairmūlāstramuccaret ||  
  
ātmānaṃ yāgavastūni pūjādravyāṇi maṇḍale |  
darśayeddhenumudrāṃ ca dravyaśuddhiriyaṃmatā ||  
  
yogapīṭhānyāsa devāttadāsthāneṣu pūjayet |  
maṇipīṭhe bhāvanayā tataḥ pūjyā svadevatāḥ ||  
  
ātmānaṃ devatārūpaṃ dhyāyenmūlena paṃca tu |  
puṣpasyāṃjalayordevāmastake hṛdayegude ||  
  
pādayoḥ sarvagātre ca pūjayeccaṃdanādibhiḥ |  
caturbhirūpavaraiśca naivedyaṃ ca nivedayet ||  
  
gurupadiṣṭa vidhināśeṣamanyat samāpayet |  
prokṣaṇyādbhiḥ prayuṃjītaḥ sarvametatsamāhitaṃ ||  
  
pūjā cakraṃ samabhyukṣya vahiryāgaṃ tataścaret |  
svarṇādi racite pātre kalpoktaṃ yaṃtramālikhet ||  
  
dakṣiṇāvartato lekhaṃ yaṃtraṃ dakṣiṇapūjane |  
vāmakrameṇa kaulādau guptame tatprakāśitaṃ ||  
  
pūjāyaṃtraṃ dakṣamārge tattadgaṃdhāṣṭakena ca |  
likhedvā keśarahimarocanābhissamālikhet ||  
  
vāmamārge likhedādya puṣpeṇa yadi yaṃtrakaṃ |  
yadi tallabhyate devalākṣārasa samanvitaṃ ||  
  
kastūrī kuṃkumāktaṃ ca vaṭī kṛtvā tu gopayet |  
yaṃtrarājaṃ samālikhya pūjayedyadi sādhakaḥ ||  
  
p. 87b)  
  
ṣaṇmāsaṃ pūjanāt tatra tvaritaṃ siddhīmāpnuyāt |  
yuvatyā aprasūtāyā abhāve gṛhyate raja ||  
  
tadabhāve taruṇyāstu nīrogāyā rajomataṃ |  
drāvaṇāṃvutpatiścaiva saṃyogotthātha vā bhavet ||  
  
tadabhāve tu rudhiraṃ mahiṣasya praśasyate |  
tadabhāve tu kusumaṃ grāhye caivā parājitāḥ ||  
  
tasyorddhabhāge niḥkṣipyadyarpitaṃ raktacaṃdanaṃ |  
tadāgataṃ mūlamārgāttena yaṃtraṃ samālikhet ||  
  
tadabhāve tu surayāghṛṣṭaraktakacaṃdanaiḥ |  
yathoktaṃ vilikhedyaṃtraṃ tuṣṭo bhavati devatā ||  
  
navamo na prakāśosti vāmamārge surottamāḥ ||  
  
atha yaṃtrasyāvaśyakatāmāha ||  
  
yaṃtraṃ maṃtramayaṃ proktaṃ yaṃtrātmādevateti ca |  
dehātmanoryathā bhedo yaṃtra daivatayostathā ||  
  
śarīramiva saṃjīvasya dīpasya snehavat priye |  
sarveṣāmapi devānyaṃ tathā yaṃtraṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ ||  
  
ādau likhedyaṃtrarājaṃ devatāyāśca vigrahaḥ |  
kāmakrodhādidoṣottha sarvaduḥkhaniyaṃtraṇāt ||  
  
yaṃtramityāhure tasmin devaḥ prīṇāti tatvataḥ |  
vinā yaṃtreṇa pūjāyāṃ devatā na prasīdati ||  
  
idamapi kaulavāmayoritikeviṃdvadaṃti ||  
  
tathā ca ||  
  
vāme kaule yaṃtrapīṭhe mūrtau pūjā ca dakṣiṇe ||  
  
atha pīṭhapūjāmāha ||  
  
evaṃ pīṭhaṃ vinirmāya pūjayet pīṭhadevatā |  
guruṣaḍbhirudakpūjyā mahāgaṇapateḥ paraṃ ||  
  
pūjayedatalādīni devasyādhastu sapta ca |  
maṇḍūkaścāpi tasyorddhe rudraḥ kālānalastataḥ ||  
  
mūlaprakṛtimādhāraśaktiṃ kūrmamanaṃtakaṃ |  
vārāhaṃ tasya daṃṣṭrāgre pṛthivīmarcayet punaḥ ||  
  
tasyāṃ sudhārṇavaṃ tasmin dvīpaṃ ca navaratnajaṃ |  
svarṇaśailaṃ ca tanmadhye tadūrddhvaṃ naṃdanaṃ vanaṃ ||  
  
tanmadhye kalpavṛkṣāṃśca tanmadhye ratnabhūmikāṃ |  
svarṇaprākāramasyāṃtastanmadhye ratnamaṇḍapaṃ ||  
  
tasyāṃtaḥ svarṇavedīṃ ca ratnasiṃhāsanaṃ punaḥ |  
vedīmadhye bhāvanīyaṃ pūjayeccaṃdanādi vā ||  
  
pūjācakrādhārapīṭhaṃ siṃhāsanamiti smaret |  
tatpādeṣu yajet samyagāgneyādi śivāṃtakaṃ ||  
  
dharmaṃ vṛṣatanuṃ raktaṃ jñānakṛṣṇaṃ ca siṃhavat |  
vairāgyaṃ bhūtavatpītamaiśvaryaṃ kṛṣṇa hastivat ||  
  
adharmādīścitravarṇānpīṭhasyādhaḥ samarccayet |  
māyāvidye ca tanmadhyenaṃtaṃtalyākṛtiṃ yajet ||  
  
p. 88a)  
  
tasya mūrddhni yajet padmamaṣṭa prakṛtipatrakaṃ |  
ānaṃdakaṃdakaṃ saṃvinnālaṃ vikārakesaraṃ ||  
  
karṇikāṃ mātṛkāṃ rūpāṃ tatpatreṣu kramād yajet |  
siddhīnaṣṭau krāmat proktastvaṇimā ca prakāmatā ||  
  
laghimeśitvamahimovaśitvaṃ praptagaurave |  
adhodhaḥ karṇikāyāstu somaḥ sūryastathānalaḥ ||  
  
guṇān satvādikāṃstatra tadvadagnitrayaṃ yajet |  
brahmaviṣṇumaheśāṃśca tato dikṣu ca madhyataḥ ||  
  
jñānamāyā kalāvidyā parapūrvaṃ ca tatvakaṃ |  
keśareṣu tathā madhye pūrvādiṣu yathākramaṃ ||  
  
tattanmaṃtroktapīṭhasya navaśaktīḥ prapūjayet |  
pīṭhamaṃtreṇa gaṃdhādyaiḥ pīṭhamadhye tato'rcayet ||  
  
caturthīnāma saṃyuktaiḥ svaiḥ svairdaivatanāmabhiḥ |  
madhye puṣpāṃjaliṃ dadyāt pīṭhamaṃtreṇa sādhakaḥ ||  
  
mūlamaṃtraṃ samuccārya ṣaṣṭhyātaṃ pīṭhanāma ca |  
mūrtiṃ ca kalpayāmīti mūrtimadhye viniḥkṣipet ||  
  
punarmūlaṃ samuccārya devanāma tataḥ paraṃ |  
mūrtiṃ ca pūjayāmīti tāḥ puṣpeṇa samarcayet ||  
  
atheṣṭa devatā prītyai yajedāyatanānyapi |  
iśeyeneśajaśivāharāvīśeśajenasā ||  
  
ravāvīśeśajājaubhādevyāṃ viśigabhāskarāḥ |  
gaṇeśeyeśabhādevyobhyarcyā īśādi koṇataḥ ||  
  
ekapīṭhe pṛthakpūjāṃ vināyaṃtraṃ karoti yaḥ |  
devatāśāpamāpnoti rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet ||  
  
taṃtreṇa pūjayedyaṃtraṃ sadaivaṃ śāpamāpnuyāt |  
āvāhya devatāmekāmarcayeccānyadevatāṃ ||  
  
anya yaṃtrenya pūjā vā devatā śāpakāriṇī |  
śāligrāmotha vā yaṃtraṃ sthāpya caikatamaṃ śive ||  
  
śālagrāmaṃ tathā yaṃtraṃ dvayamekatra nārcayet |  
paṃcāyatana pakṣīce dvitīyaṃ pūjayet sadā ||  
  
divya cakraṃ yadā prāptaṃ jīvacakraṃ tadā na ca |  
jīvacakraṃ yadā prāptaṃ vāṇaliṃgaṃ na cārcayet ||  
  
vāṇaliṃgaṃ yadā prāptaṃ śālagrāmastadānavai |  
sālagrāmo yadā prāptastadāyaṃtraṃ na pūjayet ||  
  
śālagrāme jīva cakre sarvān devān prapūjayet |  
yo bhāvo yasya vai proktastena bhāvena tiṣṭhati ||  
  
pūjanaṃ vahumūrtīnāmeka pīṭhe bhavedyadi |  
pṛthak caṃdana puṣpāṇi dhūpadīpādi taṃtrataḥ ||  
  
khaṇḍite sphuṭite dagdhe bhraṣṭamāṇa vīvarjjite |  
vyaṃgenahopaśuspṛṣṭhe patite duṣṭabhūmiṣu ||  
  
anya maṃtrārcite caiva patitasparśadūṣitaḥ |  
daśasve teṣu no kuryuḥ sannidhānaṃ divaukasaḥ ||  
  
gaṇeśasūryavisvīśadevīnāṃ pūjanaṃ kramāt |  
daśasthānāni devānāṃ pūjārthaṃ kalpitāni ca ||  
  
p. 88b)  
  
sānnidhyaṃ sarvadevānāmavaśyaṃ yaṃtrato bhavet |  
maṃtrastu jīvavat proktaḥ pratimādyaṃ śarīravat ||  
  
siddhāyamapi sāmagryāṃ vinā maṃtraṃ phalaṃ na hi |  
śivaliṃge maṇau yaṃtre śāligrāme ghaṭeravau ||  
  
sthaṇḍilegnau mūrddhni hṛdisthāneṣṭhe teṣu pūjayet |  
bhūmāvapi kṛtā pūjā putrāyurddha na nāśinī ||  
  
īśvarovāca ||  
  
śāligrāma samutpattiṃ śṛṇvaṃ tu paramādbhutāṃ |  
gaṇḍakyā prāptapastaptaṃ bhavaṃ tu mama devatāḥ ||  
  
sarvaputrāḥ sukhadātuṃ janānāmiti tejadā |  
tasyāstu tapasā hṛṣṭā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ||  
  
varaṃ dātuṃ samudyuktā vraveśā svasya putratāṃ |  
aśaktāstaṃ varaṃ dātuṃ tadāśaptāstayākrudhā ||  
  
pratāraṇaṃ mama surāḥ kṛtaṃ yasmāt punaḥ punaḥ |  
kīṭayonī prapadyethā krudhāstehyaśayaṃkṣutān ||  
  
avicāryavayaṃ sastvayādyattapasādrute |  
tena karma vipākena jaḍākṛṣṇā nadī bhava ||  
  
anyonyaśāpaṃ śrutvetthaṃ mahākolāhalo bhavat |  
prakaṃpitā surāḥ sā ca brahmāṇaṃ tevya jijñiṣuḥ ||  
  
brahmanstrāhi mahāśāpādanyonya patitākruddhā |  
iti devavacaḥ śrutvā brahmāśaṃkaramavravīt ||  
  
śivaḥ provāca dhātāramahaṃ saṃsārakārakaḥ |  
tvaṃ sṛṣṭikartā viṣṇustu pālako buddhimattaraḥ ||  
  
samaṣṭavyo yathā saukhyamubhayoḥ saṃbhavediti |  
iti māheśvaraṃ śrutvā vacanaṃ viṣṇura vravīta ||  
  
śṛṇu brahmanmahādeva śṛṇu devi gajānana |  
madgaṇau brāhmaṇau grāhamātaṃgau śāpatotra tu ||  
  
bhaviṣyati tayormokṣaṃ kariṣyāmi kalevaraṃ |  
śīrṇe bhaviṣyati yadā tanmedomajjasaṃbhavā ||  
  
pāṣāṇīṃtargatāḥ kīṭā vajrākhyāḥ prabhaviṣyatha |  
adyaivaṃ gaṇḍakī puṇyā gaṃgātulyā mahānadī ||  
  
gaṇḍakyāṃgirirājasya dakṣiṇe daśayojanaṃ |  
vistīrṇaṃtan manuṃkṣatraṃ puṇyakṣatraṃ mahītale ||  
  
cakratīrthamitikhyātaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaṃ |  
śālagrāmagatā devādevadvārāvatī gataḥ ||  
  
ubhayoḥ saṃgamo yatra muktistatra na saṃśayaḥ |  
sarvadeva prītikarā bhuktimuktipradāyinī ||  
  
bhavaṃ tvasyāṃ tu pāṣāṇāyetadaṃtargatāḥ surāḥ |  
pārthivāṃśaṃ vinā sarve vajrakīṭā bhavaṃ tviti ||  
  
p. 89a)  
  
anenaiva tu gaṇḍakyāḥ putratvaṃ bhavatāmapi |  
bhaviṣyati tadaṃtaśca cihnaṃ taddevatodbhavaṃ ||  
  
vijñāyayercaviṣyaṃti sā prītā tasya devatā |  
na yaṃtrasya na mūrteśca na vṛkṣasyāpi pūjanāt ||  
  
saṃtoṣo jāyate teṣāṃ gaṇḍakyasyārcarādyathā |  
iti viṣṇu vacaḥ śrutvā brahmāvacanamavravīt ||  
  
kīdṛk pūjyāśilā viṣṇoḥ kiṃ cihnākasya vallabhā |  
kiṃ phalaṃ cādhikārīkaḥ kena mārgeṇa tadvada ||  
  
iti brahmavacaḥ śrutvā viṣṇurvacanama vravīt |  
svīyavarṇā śilāpūjyā brāhmaṇādyaiḥ sukhāptaye ||  
  
snigdhāḥ śilāmaṃtra siddhiṃ rukṣāsiddhiṃ karoti ca |  
pecakā kīrtitā dhautāṃgāravatsāyaśoharā ||  
  
pāṇḍurāyā praśamanī malinā pāpadhīkarā |  
pītā putraphalaṃ dadyādāravarṇāsutān haret ||  
  
nīlāsaṃdiśate lakṣmīṃ dhūmābhāharate matiṃ |  
rogapradā raktavarṇā siṃdūrābhā mahākaliṃ ||  
  
dāridryakāriṇī cakrāsanā sarvārthasādhikā |  
sthūlāni haṃti vai vāyuḥ sūkṣmā svalpamṛtiṃ haret ||  
  
pūjāphalaṃ lāṃchitayā niṣphalaṃ lāṃchinaṃ vinā |  
kapilācitta vaikalpaṃ netrarogaṃ ca karvurā ||  
  
bhagnābhaṃgakarī jñeyā vahucakrā pramāṇitāṃ |  
rakṣaṇāṃtarahīnāvedeka cakrāviyogatāṃ ||  
  
vṛhanmukhī kalataghnīvṛhacakrā sutān haret |  
saṃlagna cakrātva sukhaṃ vaddha vakrāmahāgadaṃ ||  
  
bhagna cakrā tu dāridryaṃ sarvanāśaṃ tvadhomukhī |  
kuṣṭādikaṃ vyālamukhī viṣamā vividhā padaṃ ||  
  
vikṛtāvartanābhiśca vikārān kurute vahūn |  
vaṃśachedo gṛhasthānāṃ nārasiṃhyāṃ prajāyate ||  
  
rekhāvartā duḥkhadātrī yathā sūkṣmā tathā sukhaṃ |  
yathā snigdhā tathā lakṣmīmadvibhedānataḥ śṛṇu ||  
  
lakṣmī hariḥ sa vijñeyo yatra padmaṃ sa cakrakaṃ |  
kevalā vanamālmavā gṛhasthānāmabhīṣṭadaḥ ||  
  
vāsudevaḥ sa vijñeyo yadvāre cakra yugmakaṃ |  
niraṃtaraṃ samaṃ vāpi sa śvetaḥ pāpanāśanaḥ ||  
  
saṃkūrṣaṇaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ prākyaścāccakra yugmakaṃ |  
saṃlagnaṃ pūrvabhāgasthaṃ mahadraktaḥ suśobhanaḥ ||  
  
pradyumnaḥ sūkṣmacakraḥ syācchidraṃ dīrghaṃ vicitritaṃ |  
sukhirāṃtarvahucchidraṃ vīta iṣṭapradāyakaṃ ||  
  
agniruddhastunīlābhovartulaścāti śobhanaḥ |  
rekhādvayaṃ tu tadvārapṛṣṭaṃ padmena lāṃchitaṃ ||  
  
keśavaḥ sa tu vijñeya ekaṃ vā dvayameva vā |  
prāgvāpaścāccakraṃ syāccatuḥkoṇa sa bhāgyakṛt ||  
  
nārāyaṇaḥ śyāmavarṇā nābhau cakraṃ tathānnataṃ |  
dīrgharekhā samāyuktaṃ daikṣiṇe sukhiraṃ pṛthu ||  
  
p. 89b)  
  
harirūpā * * (?) śilāsāsyādyasyā ūrddhvamukhaṃ bhavet |  
harivandṛśyate dvāraṃ bhuktimukti pradātu sā ||  
  
parameṣṭī sa vijñeyaḥ padmacakrānvitastrayaḥ |  
vilvā kṛtiśca śuklābhaḥ pṛṣṭhe ca sukhirāṃ mahān ||  
  
viṣṇustu kṛṣṇavarṇaḥ syāt sthūle cakra suśobhane |  
dvāropari tathā rekhā dṛśyate madhyadeśataḥ ||  
  
narasiṃhastu kapilaḥ pṛthucakro vṛhanmukhaḥ |  
trayo vā paṃcavā tatra viṃdavo gṛhiṇāṃ na sat ||  
  
kapilo narasiṃhastu guḍalākṣānibho bhavet |  
sthūla cakradvayaṃ madhye dvāre rekhā suśobhanā ||  
  
mahānṛsiṃho vijñeyaḥ pūrvoktairlalakṣaṇairyutaḥ |  
rekhāśca keśarākārāmukhaṃ dīrghaṃ bhayānakaṃ ||  
  
lakṣmī nṛsiṃho vijñeyaścatuścakra triviṃdukaḥ |  
pūrvokta lakṣaṇairyukto vanamālā virājitaḥ ||  
  
vārāhosau śaktiliṃge cakre ca viṣame tathā |  
iṃdranīlanibhaḥ sthūla strirekhālāṃchito bhavet ||  
  
pṛthivīvārāhanāmnī sāpāvarāhākṛtiḥ śilā |  
ābhugnā caiva rekhaikāgatarājyapradāyikā ||  
  
matsyākhyā sā śilā jñeyā viṃdutrayavibhūṣitā |  
kāṃsyābhāvāsvarṇanibhā dīrghā sā bhuktimuktidā ||  
  
kūrmākhyā tu śilā pṛṣṭhe vartulāyonnatā bhavet |  
haritaṃ varṇamādhatte kaustubhena ca cihnitā ||  
  
śilākūrmaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ kūrmākārastuyo bhavet |  
cakrāṃkitā tathā vṛttā pūjitā sā padapradā ||  
  
hayagrīvoṃ kuśākārā rekhācakra samīpagā |  
vahuviṃdu samāyuktaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ nīradanīlakaṃ ||  
  
jñeyaḥ saumyahayagrīvāhayagrīvā samāśilā |  
dīrghayā rekhayā yukto rekhā vā tādṛśī bhavet ||  
  
hayaśīrṣaḥ sa vijñeyo mukhaṃ yasya hayākṛtiḥ |  
padmākṛtirbhavedvāpi sākṣamālaṃ śirastathā ||  
  
vaikuṇṭhastilavarṇābhaścakramekaṃ tathā dhvajaṃ |  
hāroparitathā rekhā pūpākārā suśobhanā ||  
  
śrīdharastu tathā devaścihnito varamālayā |  
kadaṃva kusumākāro rekhā paṃcakabhūṣitaḥ ||  
  
vāmanaḥ sa tu vijñeyo yoti hrasvaśca vartulaḥ |  
aṭasīkusumaprakhyo viṃduno pariśobhitā ||  
  
dadhivāmananāmātu ūrddhvādhaścakrasaṃyutaḥ |  
mahādyutiratihrasvaḥ subhikṣakṣemadāyakaḥ ||  
  
sudarśanastathā devaḥ śyāmavarṇo mahādyutiḥ |  
vāmapārśve tathā cakraṃ rekhaikaiva tu dakṣiṇā ||  
  
p. 90a)  
  
sahasrārjuna nāmāsau nānārekhāmayī bhavet |  
cakrākāra yatra paṃktiḥ sa naṣṭadravyadāyakaḥ ||  
  
sthūla dāmodaroyasya madhye cakraṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ |  
dūrvābhaṃ dvāri saṃkīrṇaḥ pītārekhā dhanapradaḥ ||  
  
rādhā dāmodaro jñeya ūrddhvādhaścakramānvilaṃ |  
nātidīrghāmukhaṃ madhye laṃvorekhā sa bhogadaḥ ||  
  
dāmodaraḥ sa vijñeyoyaścakradvayalāṃchitaṃ |  
sūkṣmaṃ bhavecca vivaraṃ pūjitaḥ sukhadaḥ sadā ||  
  
anaṃto vahuvarṇaḥ syānnāga bhogena cihnitaḥ |  
aneka cakra saṃbhinna sarvakāma phalapradaḥ ||  
  
puruṣottama nāmāsau yasya dikṣu vidikṣu ca |  
ūrddhvānyāsyānidṛśyaṃ te puruṣārtha phalapradaḥ ||  
  
yogeśvaraḥ sa vijñeyo liṃgaṃ yasya śirogatam |  
brahmahatyādi pāpānāṃ nāśako yogasiddhidaḥ ||  
  
padmanābhastathāraktaḥ paṃkajaḥ chatrasaṃyutaḥ |  
tulasyā pūjito nityaṃ daridrastvīśvaro bhavet ||  
  
raśmijvālo hiraṇyāsyaścaṃdrābhaḥ sphaṭikopamaḥ |  
athavā jāyate nānāsvarṇarekhābhiranvitaḥ ||  
  
garuḍaḥ sa tu vijñeyo madhya pakṣadvayānvitā |  
sudīrghā dṛśyate rekhā sa sarpyaviṣanāśakaḥ ||  
  
janārdanaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ kevalāni sphuṭāni ca |  
yasyodare tu catvāri cakrāṇi pitṛ tṛptikṛt ||  
  
lakṣmīnārāyaṇo jñeyo vanamālyaṃ kitodaraḥ |  
sūkṣmadvāraścatuścakro bhuktimuktipradāyakaḥ ||  
  
hṛṣīkeśaḥ sa vijñeyoyorddhacaṃdvākṛtirbhavet |  
tamabhyarcyalabhet svarge viṣayāṃśca samīhitān ||  
  
lakṣmīnaraharirjñeyaḥ kṛṣṇavarṇaḥ saviṃdukaṃ |  
vāmapārśve same cakre gṛhasthābhīṣṭadāyakaḥ ||  
  
trivikramastu vijñeyaḥ śyāmavarṇo mahādyutiḥ |  
vāmapārśve cakra yugmamekārekhā tu dakṣiṇe ||  
  
kṛṣṇo jñeyaḥ śilākṛṣṇo sa cakrāvāci cakrikā |  
pradakṣiṇāvarttakṛta vanamālā vibhūṣitā ||  
  
caturmukhaḥ sa vijñeyo dvecakre madhyadeśataḥ |  
catasra pārśvamārekhā vedaśāstrāgamapradaḥ ||  
  
viṣṇorbhedā ime proktā atraivā vā hareddhariṃ |  
visarjayecca pūjāṃte pratiṣṭhāṃ nātra kārayet ||  
  
śāligrāmāḥ samā pūjyāḥ sameṣudvitayaṃ na hi |  
asamānaiva pūjyaṃte ekaḥ pūjyatamottamaḥ ||  
  
p. 90b)  
  
śilādvādaśayonityaṃ bhaktyā saṃpūjayennaraḥ |  
dine dine dharmavṛddhiḥ pāpanāśaḥ prajāyate ||  
  
śālagrāmaśilāyastu bhaktyā saṃpūjayennaraḥ |  
śataṃ dināni yastena kṛtakāmaḥ sa siddhyati ||  
  
śāligrāmāmat svarūpāḥ śṛṇu teṣāṃ tu lakṣaṇaṃ |  
yatsevanādbhavediṣṭamiha loke paratra ca ||  
  
śivanābhaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sa liṃgākāratāṃgataḥ |  
svayaṃbhu liṃgākṛtimānmaṃtra siddhividhāyakaḥ ||  
  
traiyaṃvakaḥ sa vijñeyo yo viṃdutraya bhūṣitaḥ |  
śulākārā tathā rekhāgata puṃstvapradāyakaḥ ||  
  
dhūrjaṭiḥ sa tu vijñeyo yatra rekhā jaṭāsamā |  
tisro yatra pradṛśyaṃte sorcito jñānadāyakaḥ ||  
  
śaktastu pāṇḍuro jñeyo viṃduḥ kṛṣṇastu mastake |  
vilvapramāṇa tejasvī pūjita strīvaśaṃkaraḥ ||  
  
īśvaraḥ sa tu vijñeyo raktaviṃdustu mastake |  
ekacakro dvicakro vābhyaṃtaredhaścagāḥpahaṃ ||  
  
mṛtyuṃjayaḥ savijñeyaḥ svalpamṛtyuvināśakaḥ |  
adhaścakraṃ tadūrddhvaṃ ca śvetārekhā triśūlamān ||  
  
caṃdraśeṣaranāmāsāvarddhacaṃdrākṛtistuke |  
madhyacaṃdra dvayaṃ tasya sevanādroganāśanaṃ ||  
  
rudraḥ sa eva vijñeyaḥ kapilo mūrddhni rukṣataḥ |  
cakraṃ madhye bhavedveṣāmārayedripusaṃtatiṃ ||  
  
śāligrāmānatho vakṣye śaktikīṭasamudbhavān |  
yeṣāṃ pūjanato devī bhavānī suprasīdati ||  
  
śrīvidyā sā tale cakre mūrddhnachatraṃ pradṛśyate |  
vāhyaghaṭāṃkito mūrddhā snigdhā śyāmākhileṣṭadā ||  
  
mahākālī tu sā jñeyā yoni cihna samanvitā |  
rukṣā sthūlā cipiṣṭā ca vāmamārgeṇa pūjayet ||  
  
vārāhī tu varāhasya cihnitāṃtaḥ samanvitā |  
mrāpitā valiraktai sā yadarthaṃ bhakṣayeccataṃ ||  
  
dvichidrādyāḥ sarvaśilā strikoṇe śāṃkitāścayāḥ |  
yadā yudhākṛtiścorddhaṃtāṃ devīṃ tatra nirddiśet ||  
  
devīśilā ca cakrāyā dakṣe mārgenatāṃ yajet |  
sārvitā mārgeṇa lokadvaya sukhāvahāḥ ||  
  
yā cakrarahitā devī śilāṃ tāṃ vāmatorcayet |  
sparśaḥ kāryo na viprāṇāṃ na gavāṃ kṣobha kṛdbhavet ||  
  
p. 91a)  
  
saurīśilādurllabhaiva prāyaḥ kaliyugesurāḥ |  
sphaṭikābhā bhavet sātudyarme muktā vimuṃcati ||  
  
tulasyorddha sthite vahniṃ sābhiṣiktā pravarṣaṇe|  
kurute śapatho mithyā kṛtosyākṛṣṭakārakaḥ ||  
  
gaṇeśaḥ sa tu vijñeyo yaḥ svaśuṇḍāṃkito bhavet |  
śuṇḍākārāśilā vāpi gajānana samāpi vā ||  
  
yasyā madhye mahaccakraṃ sūkṣmacakraṃ ca yaddiśi |  
sā śilā tasyadikyasya sevyā taddiśi rājyadā ||  
  
arddhacaṃdrākṛtiryatra dṛśyate śaṃkaradvayaṃ |  
sā tu caṃdraśilā tryasrayuktā bhaumaśilāmatā ||  
  
vāṇākāreṇa cihnena jñeyā vudhaśilā surāḥ |  
dīrgheṇa caturasreṇa yuktā guruśilā matā ||  
  
paṃcakoṇā tu śukrasya cāpākārāśanermatā |  
sūryākārā tu rāhoḥ syāt ketostu dhvajarūpiṇī ||  
  
prāpte kaliyuge ghore vāmācāre vimiśrite |  
bhaktyā bhakṣya vivārādi rahitā mlecchasaṃkule ||  
  
kāmakrodhādibhirvyāptejanestrībhirvinirjite |  
kvaśiṣyaḥ kvagururmaṃtraḥ kvajapaḥ kva ca siddhayaḥ ||  
  
ayutāvde kaleryāte tyajedviṣṇuśilāṃmahīṃ |  
tadarddhā jāhnavī toyaṃ tadarddhvāddevatāśilāḥ ||  
  
japa evaṃ kalau śreyān śāligrāmārcanaṃ tathā |  
śāligrāme tathā yaṃtre sahasraiva prasīdati ||  
  
śāligrāme tathā yaṃtre vidyamāne maheśvari |  
devaḥ kutravaseddevisthāna dvitayakaṃ bhavet ||  
  
śāligrāmā bhavedyaṃtraṃ śāligrāmo gṛhaṃ bhavet |  
yaṃtraṃ tu gṛhamityuktaṃ gṛhasthā devatāmatā ||  
  
pratimā vā prakartavyo yathoktā śubhalakṣaṇā |  
divyacakre jīvacakre śāligrāme tathaiva ca ||  
  
vāṇaliṃge maheśāni nāvāhana visarjane ||  
  
athāvāhanādikaṃ ||  
  
sūryārghadānasamaye dānaṃ vibhavataḥ paraṃ |  
āvāhanādikaṃ kuryān mūrtyādau navadhā tu tat ||  
  
ādāvā vāhanaṃ kāryaṃ trirjapte mūlamaṃtrakaṃ |  
svalokāt sūkṣmarūpeṇa deva āgatya mūrtiṣu ||  
  
sthita evaṃ bhāvayitvā suṣumṇāvartmanāsudhīḥ |  
ānīya tejaḥ svasyānānnāsikāraṃdhunirgataṃ ||  
  
kare puṣpāṃjalau sthāpyaṃ taddadyādevamūrddhani |  
devasya tejastanmūrtau āvāhinyākhya mudrayā ||  
  
p. 91b)  
  
sthāpayeduccaranmūlametadāvāhanaṃ mataṃ |  
vibhorniveśanaṃ yaṃtre sthāpanaṃ kathitaṃ vudhaiḥ ||  
  
tataḥ saṃsthāpanaṃ kuryādihatiṣṭhehatiṣṭa ca |  
mūlāṃte devatānāma tasyāṃte ca paṭhediti ||  
  
āsthāpanīyamudrāṃ ca darśayitvā vibhāvayet |  
jātaḥ sthirodeva iti paścāt saṃprārthayediti ||  
  
deveśa bhaktisulabha sarvāvaraṇa saṃyutaḥ |  
yāvattvāṃ pūjayiṣyāmitāvattvaṃ susthirobhava ||  
  
evaṃ saṃprārthyate deśaṃ sannidhāpanamācaret |  
pūjāṃ prapūjyamānāṃ tu gṛhītvānu grahādikaṃ ||  
  
kartuṃ sāmarthya tasyāstu tatsānnidhyaṃ pracakṣate |  
mūlamaṃtraṃ samuccārya saṃbudhyaṃ tāṃ ca devatāṃ ||  
  
ihatvaṃ sannidhehīti dviruktvā svasya sannidhau |  
sthitaṃ devatoṣayecca sannidhāpana mudrayā ||  
  
ākarmakāśuparyaṃtaṃ sānnidhyamehibho vadet |  
sannirodha uddiṣṭo bhaktito maṃtravinnaraiḥ ||  
  
sannirodhaṃ tataḥ kuryān mūlamuccārya devatāṃ |  
saṃvudhyatāṃ samuccārya sanniruddho bhaveti ca ||  
  
dviruccaret kṛpāpūrṇāṃ bhaktibhāva nirodhitāṃ |  
pratimāyāṃ sthirījātāṃ devatāmiti ciṃtayet ||  
  
saṃmukhīkaraṇaṃ kuryān mūlamuccārya devatāṃ |  
saṃvudhyatāvadet paścāt saṃmukho bhava ityapi ||  
  
dhyāyet svasaṃmukhaṃ devaṃ suprasannānanāṃvujāṃ |  
saṃmukhīkaraṇīṃ mudrāṃ darśayediti tat smṛtaṃ ||  
  
ānaṃdāyatanaṃ tatvaṃ saccidānaṃdalakṣaṇaṃ |  
tadatra sakalevyāptaṃ dhyeyaṃ syādevaguṇṭhanaṃ ||  
  
tato vaguṇṭhanaṃ kuryān mūlamuccārya devatāṃ |  
saṃvuddhyatāmavaguṇṭhito bhavaṃti pradarśayet ||  
  
avaguṇṭhana mudrāṃ ca darśayecciṃtayediti |  
bhaktyā saṃmohitaṃ deva vismayotphullalocanaṃ ||  
  
sakalīkaraṇaṃ caiva devasya hṛdayādiṣu |  
ṣaḍaṃgamaṃtrānvinyasya mūlamuccārya devatāṃ ||  
  
saṃ * * * * * * * * * * * *   
(?) raṇād bhavet ||  
  
p. 92a)  
  
aṃgānāmaṃgināsārddhaṃ vidadhyādamṛtīkṛtiḥ |  
amṛtīkaraṇaṃ vakṣye pīṭhe saṃsthāpya devatāṃ ||  
  
vadhvā samyagdhenumudrāṃ devamūrdhni pravarṣaṇaṃ |  
jāyate cāmṛtasyeti dhyāyantrarghyodakena ca ||  
  
trisiṃcen mūlamaṃtreṇa dīpinī maṃtratastridhā |  
akārādikṣakārāṃta mātṛkābhistridhā punaḥ ||  
  
atra dīpinī maṃtro yathā ||  
  
vāgbhavaṃ vadayugmaṃ ca vāgvādīni ca vāgbhavaṃ |  
klī& klinnekledinīkledaya mahākṣobhamityapi ||  
  
kuruyugmaṃ kāmavījaṃ saumokṣaṃ kuruyugmakaṃ |  
prāsādaśca parāprāsādaḥ saptatriṃśadakṣaraḥ ||  
  
dīpanāṃ manunākhyā tādeva tejobhivṛddhikṛt |  
mūlaṃ saṃvodhanāṃ taṃ ca devanāmāmṛtīkṛtaḥ ||  
  
bhave hi ca vadedittha mamṛtīkaraṇaṃ smṛtaṃ |  
kṣamātasyāparādhānāṃ vijñeyā paramīkṛtiḥ ||  
  
paramīkaraṇaṃ vakṣye mahāmudrāṃ ca vaṃdhayet |  
uccārya mūlaṃ devaṃ ca pūrvavat paramāmṛtī ||  
  
kṛtā bhaveti ca proktā dhyāyeddevasya mastakeḥ |  
paramāmṛtavṛṣṭiṃ ca devasya hṛdayaṃ spṛśan ||  
  
kuryāt prāṇapratiṣṭhāṃ ca mamasthāne vadet tathā |  
devatānāmaśeṣaṃ tu sarvaṃ prāgvadeva hi ||  
  
atha krameṇāvāhanādi mudrālakṣaṇamāha |  
hastābhyāṃ maṃjaliṃ vadhvā nāmikāmūlaparvaṇoḥ ||  
  
aṃguṣṭāni kṣipet seyaṃ mudrātvā vāhinī matā |  
adhomukhisviyaṃ vai syāt sthāpinīti nigadyate ||  
  
ucchritāṃguṣṭa muṣṭyāstu yogāt saṃdhāpanīmatā |  
aṃtaḥ praveśitāṃguṣṭā saiva saṃrodhanīmatā ||  
  
uttānamuṣṭiyugalā saṃmukhīkaraṇīmatā |  
savyahastakṛtāguṣṭidīrghādhomukhatarjanī ||  
  
avaguṇṭhana mudreyamabhito bhrāmitāsatī |  
devatāṃge ṣaḍaṃgānāṃ nyāsaḥ syāt sakalīkṛtīḥ ||  
  
amṛtīkaraṇaṃ dhenumudrayā soktaiva ||  
  
anyonyagrathitāṃguṣṭhā prasārita parāṃguliḥ |  
mahāmudreyamuditā paramīkaraṇe priye ||  
  
etāḥ prayojayenmudrā devatāhvāna karmaṇi |  
tat taddaivatakalpoktāstato mudrāḥ pradarśayet ||  
  
oṃ klīṃmiti tu vījābhyāṃ mudrayāvaṃdhanaṃ smṛtaṃ |  
darśayenmūlamaṃtreṇa haṃsavījena saṃtyajet ||  
  
p. 92b)  
  
mudaṃ svarūpatvābhābhyāṃ dehadvāreṇa cātmanaḥ |  
yā arpayaṃtyo yatnena mudrāstāḥ śaktayonatā ||  
  
modayaṃti grahādityaḥ pāpaughaṃ drāvayaṃti ca |  
modayaṃ drāvaṇaṃ yasmādato mudrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
yathā vālasyābhinayaṃ dṛṣṭvā hṛṣyaṃti mātaraḥ |  
tathā bhakta kṛtāṃ mudrāṃ dṛṣṭvā hṛṣyaṃti devatāḥ ||  
  
na jātu darśayen mudrāṃ mahājana samāgame |  
kṣubhyaṃti devatāstasya kiṃ phalaṃ tu kṛtaṃ bhavet ||  
  
tataḥ saṃpūjayeddevaṃ śaktyā labhyopacārakaiḥ |  
āsanaṃ svāgataṃ cārghyaṃ pādyamācamanīyakaṃ ||  
  
madhuparkothā ca manaṃ snānaṃ vastramalaṃkṛtiḥ |  
gaṃdhaṃ puṣpāṇi dhūpaśca dīpanaivedyacaṃdanā ||  
  
prayojayedarcanāyāmupacārāṃstu ṣoḍaśaḥ |  
daśopacārā madhyā syāt sā gṛhasthairvidhīyate ||  
  
arghyaṃ pādyaṃ tathā vāmo madhuparkastathācayaḥ |  
gaṃdhādayo nivedyāṃtā upacārā daśasmṛtāḥ ||  
  
gaṃdhādayo nivedyaṃtā pūjāpaṃcopacārikā |  
agṛhasthairgṛhasthairvākartavyākārya tatparaiḥ ||  
  
saparyā trividhā proktātāsāmekatamaṃsrayet |  
upacāreṣu sarveṣu yat kiṃcidurlabhaṃ bhavet ||  
  
tatsarvaṃ manasādhyātvā puṣpakṣepeṇa kalpayet |  
tatra tatra jalaṃ dadyādupacārāṃtarāṃtarā ||  
  
ādau kuryādvaidikastuvada maṃtreṇa pūjanaṃ |  
tataśca tāṃtrikairmaṃtrairvāmīśūdraśca taṃtrataḥ ||  
  
ahaṃ haṃ haṃ ihamidamidaṃ gṛhāṇa ṭhadvayaṃ |  
yojyaḥ sarvopacāreṣu maṃtraḥ paṃcadaśākṣaraḥ ||  
  
paṭhedvā vaidikasyāṃte taṃtramaṃtraṃ tu vaidikaḥ |  
sarvatra vahnijāyāyāḥ sthāna śūdro namaḥ paṭhet ||  
  
athāsanaṃ ||  
  
devasya vāmabhāge tu dadyānmūlena cāsanaṃ |  
pauṣpaṃ dārumayaṃ cāstraṃ cārmakauśaṃ ca tejasaṃ ||  
  
pauṣpaṃ puṣpādi racitaṃ kuśasūtrādi saṃyutaṃ |  
nānāvarṇaṃ sugaṃdhaṃ ca komalaṃ sarvakāmadaṃ ||  
  
yasya yāni niṣiddhāni puṣpāṇyuktānitaiḥ kṛtaṃ |  
kevalairāsanaṃ haṃti sādhakasya manorathān ||  
  
athaiteṣāṃ bhedā ||  
  
yajñadāru samudbhūtaṃ vailvaṃ vā caṃdanodbhavaṃ |  
gaṃbhāryā vā viṣṭaro vā śrīparṇyā vepsitapradaṃ ||  
  
p. 93a)  
  
sakaṃṭakaṃ kṣīrayutaṃ tālasāla vivarjitaṃ |  
caitya śmaśāna saṃbhūtaṃ varjayecca vibhītakaṃ ||  
  
romajaṃ valkalaṃ kośajātaṃ kāryā sa saṃbhavaṃ |  
vāstraṃ caturvidhaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ turyaṃ pūrvamudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
siṃhavyāghratarakṣūṇāṃ chāgasya mahiṣasya ca |  
gajānāṃ turagāṇāṃ ca kṛṣṇaśārasya carmaṇā ||  
  
āsanaṃ nirmitaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ niṣiddhaṃ kharakukkuraṃ |  
śṛgālasya vṛkasyāpi gośaśasya kapestathā ||  
  
kuśaḥkāśaḥśarograṃthoya vā dūrvāśca valkayā |  
gokeśattujaukaṃdaśca pūrvābhāveparaḥ paraḥ ||  
  
yogapīṭhasya sadṛśametemāma saṃsmṛtaṃ |  
pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ śreṣṭhatamaṃ kauśaṃ daśavidhaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
svarṇatārā tāmrasadavaṃgānāṃ tu paraṃ paraṃ |  
hīnaṃ niṣiddhaṃ lohaṃ ca kāṃsyaṃ sīsaṃ ca pittalaṃ ||  
  
atha svāgataṃ ||  
  
sāṃgasāvaraṇaṃ devaṃ pūjārthamihacāgataṃ |  
iti dhyātvā tu mūlāṃte svāgataṃ parikīrtayet ||  
  
athārghyadānaṃ ||  
  
tatorghyaṃ mūrdhni dadyācca kālosya trividhomataḥ |  
āgatāya tathārcāyāṃ snānumāsanagāya ca ||  
  
pūjāṃte gaṃdukāmāyaddevāyārghyaṃ pradāpayet ||  
  
atha pādyadānaṃ ||  
  
arghya dravyadyutaistoyai rūpacāramanuṃpaṭhan |  
āgate snānakāle ca naivedyopakramopi ca ||  
  
trividhaḥ pādyakālaḥ syāt pādyaṃ syāt pādadhāvanaṃ |  
sugaṃdhāmṛttikābhirvāgaṃdhapuṣṭātakairapi ||  
  
samyakkṣālana pūrvaṃ tu śītairvoṣṇajalairbhavet ||  
  
athācamanīyaṃ ||  
  
pādye ca madhuparke ca snāne vastropavītayoḥ |  
bhojanecācamaḥ śuddhetoyaiḥ ṣaṭva prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
atha madhuparkaḥ ||  
  
kṣaudraṃ kṛtvā kāṃsyapātre dadyāddeva mukhāṃvuje |  
divase dadhi saṃyukta mupacāramanuṃ paṭhan ||  
  
atha punarācamanīyaṃ ||  
  
jātīphalalavaṃgailā caṃdrakaṃ kolacūrṇayuk |  
punarācamanīyārthaṃ toyaṃ devamukherpayet ||  
  
atha snānīyaṃ ||  
  
suvarṇa tailairabhyajyasugaṃdhamalakādibhiḥ |  
uddhatanairvidhāyātha snāpayeduṣṇavāriṇā ||  
  
gaṃdhodakaiśca mūlena yathā śaktābhiṣecayet |  
kṣīradadhyājya madhubhiḥ khaṇḍena ca pṛthak pṛthak ||  
  
p. 93b)  
  
nārikelodake nāpi tathā tālaphalāṃvunā |  
gaṃdhadravyaiśca vahunistathāgaṃdhodakena ca ||  
  
ekṣaveṇodakenāpi sa karpūrādi gaṃdhinā |  
kadalīpaṇasāmrotharasenāpi sugaṃdhinā ||  
  
śataṃ sahasramayutaṃ śaktyāṃ cāpyabhiṣecayet |  
śaṃkhaṃ saṃpūryate naiva snāpayettemananyadhīḥ ||  
  
sarveṣāṃ prītidaḥ śaṃkho na sūryāsya kadācana |  
paṃcāmṛtaistīrthatoyairabhiṣiktaḥ śivostudaṃ ||  
  
labhatenānya śaṃkhodaistataḥ śuddhodakena ca |  
snānaṃ puruṣasūktena kāryemūlena vāmibhiḥ ||  
  
atha vastraṃ ||  
  
viṣṇave vagalāmukhyaiḥ pītakauśeyamaṃvaraṃ |  
śivāya ca sarasvatyai pārśvanāthāya śubhrakaṃ ||  
  
raktaṃ śaktyaka vighnānāṃ bhaumasaugatayorapi |  
kṛṣṇaṃ bhairavakālyāderādhādernīlamaṃ varaṃ ||  
  
achidraṃ malahīnaṃ ca sadaśaḥ ṣannadhāritaṃ |  
kāryā sa jaṃvā kauśeyaṃ nārkavaṃ vā viśiṣyate ||  
  
tailādidūṣitādrogaḥ sacchiddhābhyatā bhavet |  
parakīyācca dāridryaṃ jīrṇādāyuḥ kṣayo bhavet ||  
  
dagdhādvipadbhaveddāsyaṃdatte gātrāvalaṃvite |  
śūcīcihnā sphoṭakādi malināt kāṃtihīnatā ||  
  
uptakeśe putranāśaścādhautedīnatā bhavet |  
mithyābhiśāpo bhavati śleṣmamūtrādidūṣite ||  
  
tataḥ pūrvoditaṃ vastraṃ yathā vaibhava kalpitaṃ |  
dadyāddevyāśvabhāvepi kevalaṃ kusumaṃ tathā ||  
  
vastrārpaṇena tu vinā pūjā bhavati niṣphalā |  
ato dadyāt puṣpamapi vastrābhāve sureśvari ||  
  
atha yajñopavīta bhūṣaṇe ||  
  
yajñopavītaṃ datvātha bhūṣaṇāni samarpayet |  
ṅeṃtaṃ namoṃtaṃ tannāma pūjanādau prayojayet ||  
  
tāni nānāvidhānāni syurmukuṭādikabhedataḥ |  
strīṣu prabhedataścāpi vijñeyāni vicakṣaṇaiḥ ||  
  
atha caṃdanaṃ ||  
  
caṃdanaṃ malayotpanna manāghrātaṃ suśītalaṃ |  
karpūrāgurukastūrīhimāṃvukṣoditaṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
cūrṇaghṛṣṭaṃ dhūmasāraḥ saṃmardaprāṇisaṃbhavaḥ |  
gaṃdhaḥ paṃcavidho jñeyo mokṣadaḥ svargavāsināṃ ||  
  
praśastaṃ gaṃdhayuktānāṃ yatra cūrṇāni yāni ca |  
tāni gaṃdhāhvayāni syuścūrṇajaḥ prathamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
  
p. 94a)  
  
ghṛṣṭomalayajogaṃdhaḥ saralo devadāru ca |  
kṛṣṇāguruḥ kadaṃvaśca dvitīyoyaṃ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
śatapatrīrasemagnāccaṃdanā gurukādikāt |  
piṭharīyaṃtrataḥ kācakūpyāṃ siddhastṛtīyakaḥ ||  
  
kṛṣṇāguruścaṃdanadevadāru kālīyakaṃ vālaka bhadramustaṃ |  
śilārasaḥ kuṃdarakokilāścasenaṃtikāketuragāhalīnāḥ ||  
  
mṛtkarpaṭaiḥ saṃyutakā ca kupyāṃ datvā mukhaṃ mudrayalohasūtraiḥ |  
niṣkāsitodhūmarasastu tasyai saugaṃdhikaiḥ kā ca kaṭorakeyaḥ ||  
  
mahāmodanāmāsurāmodakārī tathā bhūtapakṣoragātaṃkakārī |  
jvarārocakachardiśaṃkāpahārī lalāṭesthidoṣāpahārī ||  
  
yathā bhāgamanekāstu sugaṃdhāgaṃdhavāribhiḥ |  
marditā sa caturthastu saṃmarda iti kīrtyate ||  
  
kastūrikā caika bhāgādvaubhāgau mustakasya ca |  
tadarddhailājaṭāmāṃsītvakuṣṭaṃ ca śilārasaḥ ||  
  
caturbhāgaṃ vālakaṃ ca ghṛtabhṛṣṭā tathā nakhāṃ |  
sugaṃdha kokilā lohavāṇo rājavacā tathā ||  
  
aṣṭaubhāgāḥ keśarasya śūlāyāścātha ṣoḍaśaḥ |  
kṛṣṇā guruścākasīraṃ kālīyamathaṣādhayaḥ ||  
  
bhāgāḥ sevaṃtikā kasya caṃdanena vimardayet |  
kāmodanāmāsaṃmarde devatārājatoṣayet ||  
  
kastūrikāyau tu madaḥ prāṇijāta itīryataṃ |  
paṃcamoyaṃ sugaṃdhaśca devadānava toṣayet ||  
  
gaṃdhāṣṭakaṃ ca trividhaṃ śaktiviṣṇuśivātmakaṃ |  
caṃdanā gurukarpūrayora kuṃkumarocanā ||  
  
jaṭāmāṃsī kapiyutā śaktergaṃdhāṣṭakaṃ viduḥ |  
caṃdanāgurūhrīverakuṣṭakuṃkumasevyakāḥ ||  
  
jaṭāmāṃsī suramiti viṣṇorgaṃdhāṣṭakaṃ smṛtaṃ |  
caṃdanā gurukarpūratamālajanakuṃkumaṃ ||  
  
kuśītakuṣṭa saṃyuktaṃ śaivagaṃdhāṣṭakaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
atha puṣpavidhiḥ ||  
  
atha puṣpasya māhātmyaṃ leśamātraṃ dadāmyahaṃ |  
yaṃ jñātvā sādhakaḥ siddhiṃ labhennūnaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
puṇyasaṃvarddhanācāpi pāpaugha parihārakaḥ |  
puṣpa ātmapradānācca puṣpamityabhidhīyate ||  
  
puṣpairdevāḥ prasīdaṃti puṣpe devāśca saṃsthitāḥ |  
kiṃ cāti vahunoktena puṣpasyāti mṛtallikā ||  
  
p. 94b)  
  
paraṃ jyotiḥ puṣpayutaṃ puṣpeṇaiva prasīdati |  
trivargasādhanaṃ puṣpaṃ puṣṭi śrīsvargamokṣakaṃ ||  
  
puṣpamūle vasedbrahmā puṣpamadhye tu keśavaḥ |  
puṣpāgre ca mahādevaḥ sarvedevāsthitādale ||  
  
tasmāt puṣpairyajeddevaṃ nityaṃ bhaktiyuto naraḥ |  
puṣpaṃ paṃcavidhaṃ proktaṃ paraṃ cā parameva ca ||  
  
uttamaṃ madhyamaṃ hīnaṃ teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ |  
paraṃ suvarṇa puṣpaṃ syāt tatsadāyogyameva hi ||  
  
abhyāgata pūrvakaṃ deyamarcanāhraṃ punarbhavet |  
aparaṃ rājataṃ puṣpe tāmraṃ ca parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
sadāyogyaṃ cedamapi trivarṣaṃ caikavarṣakaṃ |  
tulasī ketakī padmaṃ karavījaṃ ca mālatī ||  
  
paṃcaitānnuttamānyāhurmadhyamāni tathā daśa |  
mallikā kuṃdamaṃdāratagarārjuna kiṃ śukāḥ ||  
  
pārijātamaśokaṃ ca vilvaṃ ca paṃkameva ca |  
etadbhinnaṃ suvarṇaṃ ca sugaṃdhaṃ hīnamucyate ||  
  
tattanmaṃtravidhāneṣu vihitāni samarpayet |  
nānopahāravalibhirnnānāpuṣpairmanoramaiḥ ||  
  
apāmārgadalairbhṛṃgaistulasī varjitaḥ śubhaiḥ |  
pūjanīyā sadābhaktyā nṛṇāṃ śīghraphalāptaye ||  
  
sugaṃdhaiḥ śvetalohityaiḥ kusumairarcayet skalaiḥ |  
vilvairmaruvakādyaiśca tulasīvarjitaiḥ śubhaiḥ ||  
  
droṇapuṣpairviśeṣeṇa vajrapuṣpeṇa miśritaiḥ |  
puṣpāṇyapi tathā dadyādraktakṛṣṇāsitāni ca ||  
  
śvetapuṣpaṃ javāpuṣpaṃ karavīraṃ tathāpriye |  
tagaraṃ mālatī jātī sevaṃtī yūthikā tathā ||  
  
dhustūrāśokavakula śvetākṛṣṇāparājitā |  
vakapuṣpaṃ vilvapatraiścaṃpakaṃ nāgakeśaraṃ ||  
  
mallikādgiṇṭhikā kāṃcīraktaṃ yatparikīrtitaṃ |  
arkapuṣpaṃ kokanadaṃ varvaraṃ ca priyāṃvadā ||  
  
āmrajīvūkadaṃvāni kumudāmrātakāni ca |  
sarvadhānyodbhavaṃ puṣpaṃ raṃbhāniṃ ca samudbhavaṃ ||  
  
aṣṭamyāṃ ca viśeṣeṇa tuṣṭā bhavati kālikā |  
padmapuṣpeṇa raktena saṃtuṣṭā sarvadevatā ||  
  
kṛṣṇā vā yadi vā śuklākālikā varadā bhavet |  
śmaśānadhustūreṇaiva tuṣṭā dhūmāvatīya sa ||  
  
vanyaiḥ puṣpaiśca vividhaistuṣṭā bhavati sarvadā |  
āmalakyāstu patreṇa tuṣṭā bhavati pārvatī ||  
  
aparājitā phalaṃ vaktuṃ mayādevi na śakyate |  
aparājitā priyataraṃ priyaṃ devyā na vidyate ||  
  
aparājitāyāṃ sāparṇāsthitā pūrveśaṃtaṃ samā |  
yonirūpeṇa tatrāsau sthitvā nirgacchatāṃ śivā ||  
  
p. 95a)  
  
karavīre liṃgarūpe śivovasati vai sadā |  
śivaśaktyāśca saṃyogāt karavīrā parājitā ||  
  
raktacaṃdana miśreṇa tayoryogena pūjayet |  
tuṣyate parameśāni sā pūjā sa phalā smṛtāḥ ||  
  
puṣpairaraṇya saṃbhūtaiḥ patrairvāgiri saṃbhavaiḥ |  
svārāmodbhavapuṣpairvātrisaṃdhyā śvetalohitaiḥ ||  
  
karavīraḥ paṃcavarṇaḥ kālītārā pragocaraḥ |  
cūḍāmaṇiṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvapuṣpottamottamaṃ ||  
  
cūḍāmaṇirdaśavidho navaratna prabhedataḥ |  
daśamaṃ sarvavarṇādyaṃ puṣpeṃdraḥ saṃjñako bhavet ||  
  
ketakī dvividhā proktā puṃstrī bhedakrameṇa ca |  
puṃbhede vidvidhā proktā pītaśveta prabhedataḥ ||  
  
strībhedepi dvidhā proktā pītaśveta prabhedataḥ |  
puṃbhede kaṭhinaḥ proktaḥ strībhede komalāmatāḥ ||  
  
mallikā vedadhā proktā tat kramaṃ śṛṇu pārvatī |  
śvetādvipuṣpāṣaṭpuṣpāpuṣpagucchā tathā parā ||  
  
navapuṣpo parāproktā raktapuṣpā parā bhavet |  
pītapuṣpānyecakā ca dhūsarā paṃcavarṇajā ||  
  
mālatī paṃcadhā proktā tadbhedān saṃśṛṇu priye |  
gaṃdharājā sarvagaṃdhā tathā śrīkhaṇḍagaṃdhikā ||  
  
kastūrī gaṃdhasaṃyuktā caturthā ketakī matā |  
mālatī svarṇabhājāti śvetāraktaśilāparā ||  
  
raktavarṇā parā jñeyā paṃcavarṇā tathā parā |  
ete bhedā mayā proktā gopitā yāmalādike ||  
  
ḍāmare gopitā devi tava snehādihoditā |  
gopanīyā maheśāni saṃkṣepāde tadeva tu ||  
  
yūthikā mālatī jātī mallikā navamallikā |  
kastūrī gaṃdhikā devi tathaiva vā guru gaṃdhijā ||  
  
nakhagaṃdhāśalākādyā mālatī vedagaṃdhikā |  
svarge tu mālatī proktā raktā pātālagocarā ||  
  
jātīyūthī tathā mallī mṛtyuloke prakīrtitā |  
raktamallīpītamallī varṇapaṃcakarūpiṇī ||  
  
triśaktiloke deveśi sarvadeva prapūjane |  
etadrūpaṃ viciṃtyaivaṃ pūjayeccīnasuṃdarīṃ ||  
  
etadrahasyaṃ saṃproktaṃ puṇyānāṃ nirṇayāmṛtaṃ |  
jātā na tṛpti deveśa viśeṣavada satvaraṃ ||  
  
sālatī rājamallī ca jātī yūthījayaṃtikā |  
mālatī laghuyūthī ca mallīcetikramaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
  
śvetāśrīmālīgaditā jātī raktatalāmatā |  
mālatī dalapatrā ca raktaśvetābhṛśārasā ||  
  
rājamallī maheśāni vahunetrāṇi gaṃdhinī |  
śatapatrā rājamallī kalāpatrā tu mallikā ||  
  
p. 95b)  
  
paṃcapatrā bhavejjātī saptapatrā tu mālatī |  
yūthī sūkṣmā tadvividhā rasagaṃdhāmanoharā ||  
  
mālatī svarṇabhājātī śvetā raktaśilāmatā |  
raktavarṇā paṃcavarṇā pītakṛṣṇā parā smṛtāḥ ||  
  
kastūrī gaṃdhikā devi tathaivā gurugaṃdhikā |  
aśvagaṃdhāmalākākhyā vedayuktā tu mālatī ||  
  
sarvadevavidhau śastā pūjāsāṃgārtha hetave |  
caṃpakaḥ puṣpadānena svarṇaṃ vahuvidhaṃ labhet ||  
  
nāgakeśaradānena rūpavān śubhago bhavet |  
punnāgasya ca puṣpeṇa jvaraśāṃtirbhavet sadā ||  
  
keśarasya pradānena śatruṃ nāśayate dhruvaṃ |  
pārijātaḥ pāribhadradānādāyuḥ pravarddhate ||  
  
kuṃdapuṣpa pradānena kāmānāpnoti vai dhruvaṃ |  
jātī mālati kubjena śīghraṃ tu puṣpaṃti mānataḥ ||  
  
kokilākhya pradānena akālamaraṇaṃ haret |  
odrapuṣpapradānena tuṣyate parameśvarī ||  
  
yathā chāgāni valinā tathā tuṣyati niścitaṃ |  
datte caiva javā puṣpe paṭṭavastra phalaṃ labhet ||  
  
brahmāhatyādikaṃ pāpaṃ kṣaṇānnaśyati niścitaṃ |  
karavīreṇa puṣpeṇa pūjayejjagadīśvarīṃ ||  
  
pratipuṣpeṣu maṃtreṇa yojayitvā niśāsu vai |  
labhate vāṃchitān kāmān ājñā siddhiśca labhyate ||  
  
lohitaṃ vātha raktaṃ vā karavīrastu siddhidaṃ |  
vaṃdhūkasya pradānena paṭṭavastraṃ ca labhyate ||  
  
puṣpamālāṃ cāha ||  
  
ekajātīyakaiḥ puṣpairbhinnajātīyakairapi |  
mālā tathaika varṇaḥ syādbhinnavarṇāpi vā priye ||  
  
sāpurastrividhā jñeyā pariṇāhavaśena tu |  
pateddhṛdaya varjaṃtaṃ yāmalā nityamālinī ||  
  
raikikā sā parijñeyā sarvāvaratayāsthitā |  
adhovastaṃ vilīnābheḥ kausumīyāsragucyate ||  
  
sādhāraṇī parijñeyā madhyamā pūrvatodhikā |  
āgulphasragvinīyā tu pādapadmoparisthitā ||  
  
vanamālati vikhyātā sarvābhyaḥ sragbhyaḥ uttamā |  
kiṃcidviśeṣamatrāpitamapivyāharāmite ||  
  
karavīrairjavāpuṣpairvakairdamanakairapi |  
nīlotpalaiḥ sarasijairllavaṃgairnāgakeśaraiḥ ||  
  
p. 96a)  
  
jātībhirmālatībhiśca mallikācampakādibhiḥ |  
racitāyā bhaveyurhisrajaḥ paramaśobhanā ||  
  
mālābhyo'nyāmya etāṃstu devyāḥ prīti pradāyakaḥ |  
atonyeṣu prasūneṣuttiṣṭhaḥ su varavarṇinī ||  
  
amībhiḥ kusumaistāsāṃgrathane yatnamācaret |  
svadravyaiḥ pūjayed vidyāṃ javāyāvaka siṃdūraiḥ ||  
  
caṃdanaṃ raktasaṃjñaṃ tu śāṇitaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
atha rahasya puṣpaṃ ||  
  
yonipuṣpaṃ maheśāni varjapuṣpaṃ nigadyate |  
āṣoḍaśādanūḍhayā uttamaṃ sarvasiddhidaṃ ||  
  
valātkareṇa ūḍhāyāmadhyamaṃ bhogavarddhanaṃ |  
rajoyogavaśādanyedadhamaṃ sukhadāyakaṃ ||  
  
svayaṃbhūkusumaṃ devi trividhaṃ tu vijāyate |  
savaiḥ puṣpaiḥ sadā pūjyā vihitā vihitairapi ||  
  
kartavyā sarvadevānāṃ bhaktiyogotra kāraṇaṃ |  
na svarṇairnavaratnaiśca na sparśamaṇibhiḥ śubhaiḥ ||  
  
na hi tṛpyati deveśi kālikā bhaktavatsalā |  
tasmādyonibhavaṃ puṣpaṃ pūjārthaṃ saṃgrahecchive ||  
  
rahasyāti rahasyaṃ ca kathyate śṛṇu sāṃprataṃ |  
avīrā paṃcadhā proktā śvetapītāruṇa kramāt ||  
  
śvetapītā pītaraktā raktāśvetā parāmatā |  
evaṃ bhedāṃtare saiva navadhā parikīrtitā ||  
  
avīrā kusume naiva pūjayet sarvadevatā |  
ratipuṣpaṃ kāmapuṣpaṃ devapuṣpakrameṇa ca ||  
  
sevaṃtī vahudhākhyātā tadbhedān śṛṇu pārvatī |  
śvetapītā tathā raktā tritayaṃ tritayaṃ triṣu ||  
  
siṃdūrā divyavarṇā ca hāridrā ca parā bhavet |  
ratipuṣpamidaṃ proktaṃ kāmapuṣpaṃ śṛṇu priye ||  
  
pītaṃ gucchaḥ svarūpaṃ ca raktagucchaḥ svarūpakaṃ |  
pītaṃraktaṃ raktapītaṃ sūkṣmamanyanmaheśvarī ||  
  
ṣaṭbhedāḥ sūkṣmabhede tu atisūkṣmepi ṣaṭbhavet |  
evamaṣṭādaśavidhaṃ kāmapuṣpaṃ maheśvarī ||  
  
devapuṣpaṃ pravakṣyāmi yena devīmayorccanāt |  
śvetaraktaṃ divyarūpaṃ siṃdūrasannibhaṃ tathā ||  
  
aparaṃ śvetapītaṃ ca paṃcavarṇa mathāparaṃ |  
ratipuṣpaṃ paṃcavarṇaṃ suṃdarīlokagocaraṃ ||  
  
kāmapuṣpaṃ paṃcavarṇaṃ kālikānāmagocaraṃ |  
devapuṣpaṃ naṃdavarṇaṃ tāriṇī lokagocaraṃ ||  
  
p. 96b)  
  
anayoḥ graṇoyācāyamāha ||  
  
sūtreṇa paṭṭavastreṇa vīravastreṇa pārvatī |  
kāśmīravastre sūtreṇa paṭṭasūtreṇa pārvatī ||  
  
kastūrī kuṃkumaṃ tatra caṃdanā gurukādikaṃ |  
nānā sugaṃdhikaṃ datvā ekīkṛtvā tu sādhakaḥ ||  
  
aṣṭagaṃdhena vā puṣpaiḥ saṃyuktaṃ puṣpamāharet |  
etenākṣatayogena pūjayet parameśvarīṃ ||  
  
āsanārthe ca pūjārthe homārthe ca kramādviduḥ |  
svayaṃbhu saṃyutaṃ puṣpaṃ siddhapuṣpaṃ vidurvudhāḥ ||  
  
ratimālyāni deveśī na ca paryuṣitāni ca |  
siddhapuṣpāṇi khyātāni gaṃdharva prītidāyi ca ||  
  
suddhāśuddhāni puṣpāṇi navīnāni dinedine |  
etatsarvaṃ samādāya tārāṃ kālīṃ ca pūjayet ||  
  
puṣpadāna phalāt koṭi guṇitaṃ phalamāpnuyāt ||  
  
athāvihitaṃ ||  
  
mārpayedbhūmi patitaṃkārakaṃ kṛmi bhakṣitaṃ |  
aṃgalagnaṃ samāprātaṃ mlānaṃ paryuṣitaṃ tathā ||  
  
ugragaṃdhamagaṃdhaṃ ca kṛmikeśādi dūṣitaṃ |  
aśuddhapātraprāṇyaṃga vā somiḥ kutsitātmabhiḥ ||  
  
ānītaṃ tanniṣiddhaṃ syānmadhyāhnasnānatastathā |  
svayaṃvikāśitaiḥ puṣpaiḥ svayaṃ ca patitaṃ bhuvi ||  
  
bhūgataṃ varjayet puṣpaṃ sephālivakulaṃvinā |  
kalikābhistathātyājyāvināvaṃ pakapadmakaiḥ ||  
  
vilvasya khadirasyaiva tathā dhātrī dalasya ca |  
tamālasya ca patrasya chinnabhinnaṃ na duṣpati ||  
  
viṣṇukrāṃti javā nāgakeśara pallavaṃ |  
vaṃdhūka caiva maṃdārasavṛṃtena samarcayet ||  
  
devīpūjā sadā kāryā jalajaisthalajairapi |  
vihitā vihitairvāpi bhaktiyuktena cetasā ||  
  
patraṃ vā yadi vā puṣpaṃ phalaṃ neṣṭamadhomukhaṃ |  
duḥkhadaṃ tat samākhyātaṃ yathotpannaṃ tathārpaṇaṃ ||  
  
citrapūjāsu sarvāsu na viruddhasya ca dūṣaṇaṃ |  
adhomukhārpaṇaṃ neṣṭaṃ puṣpāṃjalividhau na tat ||  
  
na paryuṣitadoṣosti tulasī vilvacaṃpake |  
jalaje vakulāgastya mālākāra gṛheṣu ca ||  
  
puṣpaiḥ paryuṣitairnnaṣṭaiḥ kṛmikīṭavidāritaiḥ |  
na pūjayeddhomayecca devatāśāpamāpnuyāt ||  
  
p. 97a)  
  
vilvapatraṃ ca tulasī svayaṃ bhūsvarṇapuṣpakaiḥ |  
na paryuṣita rūpatvaṃ nirmālyatvaṃ maheśvarī ||  
  
caturṇāṃ devadeveśi namayākīrtitaṃ bhuvi |  
nṛsiṃhaṃ ca śivaṃ caiva na ketakyā samarcayet ||  
  
śvetakṛṣṇa tulasyā ca kālikāṃ na spṛśet kvacit |  
kamalaṃ daśarātraṃ ca jātī dinatrayaṃ tathā ||  
  
caṃpakaḥ paṃcarātraṃ ca kiṃśuko dina saptakaṃ |  
karavīroṣṭa divasaṃ ketakī daśapaṃca ca ||  
  
kudo netradinaṃ devi munipuṣpaṃ ca dāḍimī |  
japāpuṣpaṃ tato drākhyāṃ  divasa dvayagocarāṃ ||  
  
śatapuṣpaṃ puṣparājo gaṃdharājastathaiva ca |  
bhagapuṣpaṃ maheśāni vedarātraṃ na dūṣyati ||  
  
nāradamate naiva kathyate śṛṇu sāṃprataṃ |  
vilvāyāmārgadhātrī ca tulasī triṃśadāditaḥ ||  
  
vaṣaṭ triṃśa maheśāni na ca paryuṣitāni ca |  
ekena karavīreṇa sahasreṇa śatena ca ||  
  
māṃ ca saṃpūjye deveśi mamarūpo naro bhavet |  
ekena karavīreṇa māṃ ca saṃpūjayet priye ||  
  
tena saṃpūjayeddevi jagatsthāvara jaṃgamaṃ |  
karavīre śaktiviṃdau tatrahaṃ nivasāmyahaṃ ||  
  
ketakī kuṭajeneśaṃ navarvaryākṣatairhariṃ |  
na dūrvāyā yajeddurgāṃ vilvapatrairddivākaraṃ ||  
  
laṃvodaraṃ tulasyā ca vṛṃta hīnaiḥ samarpayet |  
pītākṛṣṇākarautyājyāḥ sūryaśaṃbhau viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
vilvairmaruvakādyaiśca tulasī varjitaiḥ śubhaiḥ |  
tulasīṃ mālatīṃ caiva kālītārā vidhau tyajet ||  
  
vilvaṃ maruvakaṃ caiva vīrakarmaṇi varjite |  
devīnāmarkamaṃdārāvāditye tagaraṃ tathā ||  
  
gaṇeśāya ca sūryāya yastu pūjamati priyaṃ |  
puṣpābhāve pravālairvā tadabhāve ca korakaiḥ ||  
  
tadabhāve ca phalaiḥ patrai tadabhāve ca tṛṇāṃkuraiḥ |  
kadalaṃ dāḍimaṃ kolaṃ jaṃvū ciṃcāmalāmrakaṃ ||  
  
mātuluṃgaṃ ca jaṃvīraṃ paramaṃ śreṣṭhamucyate |  
pūjayet parameśāni puṣpābhāve tu patrakaiḥ ||  
  
patrāṇāmapyalābhe tu drumagulmodbhavādibhiḥ |  
tadbhāvānāma lābhe tu tatphalena prapūjayet ||  
  
p. 97b)  
  
akṣatairvājalairvāpi tadabhāve tu saśarṣapaiḥ |  
sitaisteṣāmalābhe tu mānasaṃ pūjanaṃ caret ||  
  
ataḥ paraṃ puṣpadāna mākarṇaya śucismite |  
yat tatpuṣpasyanāmāpi nama ityakṣaradvayaṃ ||  
  
uccārya dadyāt taddevyaiḥ sarvakāmārtha siddhaye |  
aṃguṣṭha tarjanībhyāṃ ca cakre puṣpaṃ nivedayet ||  
  
puṣpaṃ suśobhanaṃ devi saurabhyena samanvitaṃ |  
mayā niveditaṃ bhaktyā supuṣpaṃ pratigṛhyatāṃ ||  
  
atha puṣpopacārāṃte kuryādāvaraṇārcanaṃ |  
maṃtra saṃpuṭitairvarṇairmātṛkāyāḥ sa viṃdukaiḥ ||  
  
krameṇa gaṃdhapuṣpādyairdevasyāṃge samarcayet |  
layogatvena mātṛṇāṃ sthānāṃgeṣu tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
prathamāvaraṇyaṃ pūjyaṃ tadaṃte devatāṃ yajet |  
punarāvaraṇaṃ ceṣṭvā devatāmarcayet tathā ||  
  
evaṃ samarcya sarvāstā yathoktā vṛttidevatāḥ |  
atha sarvajñatā tṛptiranya divodhasaṃjñīkā ||  
  
svataṃtrātānyā nityāsyādaluptaḥ śaktireva ca |  
ṣaḍaṃga devatāhyetā nāmataḥ parikīrtitāḥ ||  
  
keśareṣvagni koṇādau hṛdayādīni pūjayet |  
netramagre diśāsvastraṃ dhyātavyāścāṃgadevatāḥ ||  
  
tuṣārasphaṭikaḥ śyāmanīlakṛṣṇāruṇārciṣaḥ |  
varadābhayadhāriṇyaḥ pradhānatanavaḥ striyaḥ ||  
  
agnīśāsuravāyavya madhyadikṣu kramāt sthitāḥ |  
vāyavyādiśaṃparyaṃtaṃ gurupaṃktiṃ samarcayet ||  
  
tasmāt sarvatra deveśa saṃkṣepān śṛṇutān gurūn |  
ādau sarvatra deveśa maṃtradaḥ prathamoguruḥ ||  
  
parāpara gurustvaṃ hi parameṣṭītvahaṃ tataḥ |  
sarvamaṃtreṣu vidyā su svayaṃ prakṛtirūpiṇī ||  
  
tataḥ puruṣarūpaṃ ca kathitā guru saṃtatiḥ |  
yeṣu yeṣu ca maṃtreṣu ye ye gurugaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ||  
  
te te pūjyāḥ saparyādau saṃkṣepādgaditaṃ mayā |  
devasya purataḥ prācī jñeyā varaṇapūjane ||  
  
tadādi parivārāṇāṃ prādakṣiṇyena pūjanaṃ |  
aṃgamaṃtrāstu pūjāyāmo namoṃtā hutau tathā ||  
  
svāhāṃtā atha devasyābhi mukhaṃtāḥ samāsthitāḥ |  
tato yajellokapālān svasvadikṣu vyavasthitān ||  
  
āyudhāni tadagre ca teṣāṃ dhyānamathocyate |  
indraḥ surādhipaḥ prītamairāvatagataṃ vibhuṃ ||  
  
p. 98a)  
  
sahasranetraṃ dvibhujaṃ pītavajradharaṃ bhaje |  
agni tejodhipaṃ raktaṃ śvetaśaktikaraṃ prabhuṃ ||  
  
subhūṣaṇaṃ meṣavāhaṃ vaṃde raktāṃtalocanaṃ |  
yamaṃ pretādhipaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ mahiṣo parisaṃsthitaṃ ||  
  
kāladaṃḍadharaṃ krūraṃ vṛttaṃ dūtairbhayānakaiḥ |  
rakṣodhi paṃcanair-ṛtyaṃ śavāsana samāsthitaṃ ||  
  
dhūmābhaṃ khaḍgahastaṃ ca piṃgalaśmaśrukūrcakaṃ |  
makare saṃsthitaṃ vidyunnibhapāśakarāṃvujaṃ ||  
  
śubhrāṃgaṃtaṃḍilaṃ vaṃde varuṇaṃ yādasāṃpatiṃ |  
vāyuṃ prāṇādhipaṃ dhūmraṃ raktāṃkuśakaraṃ paraṃ ||  
  
vātapramīsamārūḍhaṃ dhāvaṃtaṃ vegato bhaje |  
yakṣapatiṃ kuveraṃ ca śuklaṃ śūlagadādharaṃ ||  
  
narasiṃhāsanārūḍhaṃ medalaṃviḥ triṇīyutaṃ |  
vidyādhipaṃ nīlaśūladharaṃ vṛṣabhavāhanaṃ ||  
  
trinetraṃ bhālacaṃdraṃ ca jaṭājūṭadharaṃ mitaṃ |  
gauraṃ nāgādhipaṃ mūrddhniphalāmaṃḍalabhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
pīnottuṃgaṃ cakradharamanaṃtaṃ viśvagaṃ bhaje |  
lokādhipaṃ vidhātāraṃ raktaṃ padmakaraṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
haṃsārūḍhaṃ vedapāṭhakūrvaṃtaṃ tamahaṃ bhaje |  
punarmūlaṃ samuccāryā sāṃgādyaiḥ sa pareti ca ||  
  
vārāyaināmadevyāśca caturthyaṃta mudīrayet |  
nama ityarcayedgaṃdha puṣpādyaiḥ sādhakastriyaḥ ||  
  
atha dhūpadānaṃ ||  
  
dhṛtāśeṣa mahādoṣa pūtigaṃdhaprabhāvataḥ |  
paramānaṃda jananādhūpa ityabhidhīyate ||  
  
dhūpapātraṃ tatostreṇa kṣālayet pūjayet tataḥ |  
hṛdāṇunātha cāstreṇa ghaṇṭhāṃ saṃpūjya vādayet ||  
  
itthaṃ dhūpaṃ prakurvīta tāmrakāsyādinirmite |  
bhājane dvipade bhugnanāle padmākṛtau śubhe ||  
  
sārāṅgāra viniḥkṣiptairgugulvaguruvṛkṣajaiḥ |  
niryāsādyusthitairdhūpaiḥ kuṃdhudravyairathoditaiḥ ||  
  
dhūpaṃ dadedgaṇeśasya priyaḥ proktastu guggulaḥ |  
sarjaṃ devyā maheśasya niryāso devadārujaḥ ||  
  
viṣṇoḥ kṛṣṇāguruḥ śītaṃ bhāskarasya priyaṃ mataṃ |  
jaṭāmāṃsī gugguluṃ ca caṃdanā gurukaistathā ||  
  
caṃdrairajani saṃyuktairmākṣikaissahakuṃkumaiḥ |  
sarpiḥ saṃmiśritairdadyāddevyairdhūpaṃ maheśvari ||  
  
sa guggulva gurūśīraṃsitājya madhucaṃdanaiḥ |  
sārāṅgāra viniḥkṣiptairddhūpaṃ nīcaiḥ pradhūpayet ||  
  
p. 98b)  
  
śakterdaśāṃgaṃ vakṣyāmi śaileyaṃ malayodbhavaim |  
nakhaṃ kuṣṭaṃ sarjarasaṃ mekaikāṃśaṃ prakalpayet ||  
  
śilārasā gurujaṭāmāṃsī bhāgadvayaṃmataṃ |  
ṣaṭmākṣikaṃ sitā cāṣṭau dhūpoyaṃ śaktitohamaḥ ||  
  
harītakīsarjarasamuramāṃsyaḥ kumbhāgikāḥ |  
lākṣātribhā catvāro bhāgāḥ śailajamustayoḥ ||  
  
paṃcabhāgaṃ nakhaṃ proktaṃ ṣaḍbhāgaṃ kuṣṭamucyate |  
dvādaśāṃśo guḍokeśa vighna viṣṇuṃ daśāṃgakaḥ ||  
  
madhumustāghṛtaṃgaṃdho guggulva guruśailajaṃ |  
saralaṃ sihlasiddhārthau śeṣadeva daśāṃgakaḥ ||  
  
gugguluṃ saralaṃ dāruḥputraṃ mayalasaṃbhavaṃ |  
hīveramaguruṃ kuṣṭhaṃ guḍaṃ sarjarasaṃśanaṃ ||  
  
harītakī nakhī lākṣā jaṭāmāṃsī ca śailajaṃ |  
soḍaśāṃgaṃ vidrudhūpaṃ daivapaitre ca karmaṇi ||  
  
athavā'gurukarpūraṃ caṃdanā sahaguggulaṃ |  
madhusarpirjaṭāmāṃsī śailajaṃ kuṃkumaṃ tathā ||  
  
ebhirvimiśritaḥ kāryo dhūpoyaṃ pārvatī priyaḥ |  
lohavāṇau ṣoḍaśāṃgaḥ trividyāyāṃ prakīrtitau ||  
  
kālīvidyāvidhau devi aguruśca daśāṃgakaḥ |  
aṣṭāṃdaśāṃga śrīkhaṃḍaṃ tārāvidyā vidhau smṛtaṃ ||  
  
chinnā vidyā vidhau devi paṃcāṃgaṃ guggulustathā |  
kṛṣṇā guruṃ pītasāro brahmāstu manugocaraṃ ||  
  
rālodya gurucaṃdanaṃ mātaṃgyāṃ parikīrtitaṃ |  
kastūrī caiva karpūramaṣṭagaṃdhaṃ tathaiva ca ||  
  
bhairavyāṃ kīrtitaṃ devī namricaiva śilārasaḥ |  
bhuvaneśyā mayā proktāṃ śrīkhaṃḍaṃ kamalāmatau ||  
  
lākṣāguḍohni dhūmrāyā siddhavidyā vidhau śive |  
madhumustaṃ ghṛtaṃ gaṃdhaṃ gugguluṃ guḍaśailajaṃ ||  
  
caṃdanaṃ sihnasiddhārtha daśāṃgā dhūpa iṣyate |  
sitājya madhusaṃmiśraṃ guggulva gurucaṃdanaṃ ||  
  
ṣaḍaṃgaṃ dhūpametattu sarvadeva priyaṃ sadā |  
astreṇa dhūpadīpādīn saṃpūjya dāpayettataḥ ||  
  
yathāgaṃdhastathā devi dhūpaṃ dadyādvicakṣaṇaḥ |  
vanaspati rasotpannāgaṃdhādyo dhūpanuttamaḥ ||  
  
āghreyaḥ sarvadevānāṃ dhūpoyaṃ pratigṛhyatāṃ |  
vāmataṃ tu tathā dhūpamagrecāna tu dakṣiṇe ||  
  
na dhūpaṃ vitaredbhūmau nāsanena ghaṭe tathā |  
yathā tathā dhāragataṃ kṛtvātaṃ vinivedayet ||  
  
p. 99a)  
  
medomajjāyunāneṣṭā viṣṇavedārasaṃbhavaḥ |  
tataḥ samarpayeddhūpaṃ ghaṃṭāvādanapūrvakaṃ ||  
  
yasyāḥ śabdena vighnāstu yāti sarvediśodaśaḥ |  
vyādhayordurgrahāḥ sarve tathāgrāśca vināyakāḥ ||  
  
duḥsvapnārākṣasā duṣṭāvetālā bhairavāḥ śivā |  
ḍākinyo bhūtasaṃghāśca sarpakarkoṭakādayaḥ ||  
  
valikāmāṃ tu kāmāyā ratikāmān yathā pare |  
ghaṇṭāni nādaśravaṇāddhatavīryabhavaṃti ca ||  
  
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena pūjākāle sadāhanet ||  
  
ghaṇṭāpūjanamaṃtro yathā ||  
  
tāro jayadhvani padaṃ maṃtramātogni gehinī |  
ekādaśākṣaromaṃtro ghaṃṭāyāḥ sarvasiddhidaḥ ||  
  
pūjayitvā svamaṃtreṇa ghaṇṭāṃ tannāda pūrvakaṃ |  
dīpaṃ dadyāttu vibhave nānāvādyapuraḥsaraṃ ||  
  
āvāhanorgha dhūpe ca puṣpanaivedyadīpayoḥ |  
ghaṇṭāṃnādaṃ prakurvīta viśeṣāddhūpadīpayoḥ ||  
  
pūjākālaṃ vinānyatra kuryādasyāḥ pravādanaṃ |  
nonayā ca vinā pūjāṃ kārayet siddhilālasāḥ ||  
  
atha dīpavidhiḥ ||  
  
dīrghājñāna mahādhvāṃtāhaṃkāra parivarjanāt |  
paratatva prakāśācca dīpa ityabhidhīyate ||  
  
ghṛtadīpaḥ prathamatastilataila samudbhavaḥ |  
sārṣapaḥ phalaniryāsa jāto vā vārijodbhavaḥ ||  
  
dadhijaścānnajaścaiva dīvāssapta prakīrtitāḥ |  
padmasūtra bhavāvartirdarbhasūtrabhavāthavā ||  
  
jālājāvādarī vāpi tūlakoṣodbhavāthavā |  
vartikādīpa kṛtyeṣu sadāpaṃcavidhāḥ smṛtāḥ ||  
  
vartiḥśvetā'thavāraktānapītānāsitāpi ca |  
nirvījaṃ vātha kāryā saṃtajjātāstaṃtavotha vā ||  
  
praśastā dīpavartiḥ syāt kadācinnūtanāṃvaraṃ |  
śānaṃvādarajaṃ vāstraṃ jīrṇaṃ malinameva ca ||  
  
upabhuktaṃ tu nādadyādvartikārthaṃ kadācana |  
daśāṃ vivarjayet prājño yadyadvāhatavastrajāṃ ||  
  
taijasaṃ rājasaṃ lauhamārtikyaṃ nārikerajaṃ |  
tṛṇarājodbhavaṃ vāpi dīpapātraṃ praśasyate ||  
  
evaṃ dīpaṃ prakurvīta netraraṃjanakāraṇaṃ |  
dīpaṃ tu yāgaparyaṃta madhomukha prakalpayet ||  
  
labhyate yasya tāyastu dīpasya caturaṃgulāt |  
na sa dīpa ihākhyāta adyavṛdddhistu saṃmṛtaḥ ||  
  
p. 99b)  
  
gosarpiṣā vā tailena vartyā caladyugarbhayā |  
uccaiḥ pradarśayeddīpaṃ navamedādinā kvacit ||  
  
na miśrīkṛtya dadyāttu dipasnehān ghṛtādikān |  
kṛtvā miśrīkṛtaṃ snehaṃtā miśraṃ narakaṃ vrajet ||  
  
dīpasya dhūpavatpātraṃ padmākāra vinirmite |  
pratipatre pradīpaṃ ca tyāgavya ghṛtāktayā ||  
  
atha dhūpadīpapātrayorgrahaṇamāha ||  
  
madhyamānāmikāmadhye aṃguṣṭhāgreṇa dāpayet |  
uttoraṇaṃ tridhākāryaṃ dīpaṃ netrāṃtikaṃ priye ||  
  
dhūmaṃ nāsāgraparyaṃtaṃ darśayet priyavādini |  
pārāvata bhramākāraṃ dīpaṃ netrādi darśayet ||  
  
dakṣiṇe sarpiṣā dīpaṃ tilatailena vāmataḥ |  
sitāvartirdakṣiṇatoraktāvartistu vā mataḥ ||  
  
vṛkṣeṣu dīpo dātavyo na tu bhūmau kadācana |  
sarvaṃ sahāvasumatī sahatena tvidaṃ dvayaṃ ||  
  
akārya pādatvānaṃ ca dīpatāpaṃ tathaiva ca |  
kurvaṃtu pṛthivītāpaṃ yo dīpamutsṛjennaraḥ ||  
  
sa tāpa pāpanarakaṃ prāpnotyevana na saṃśayaḥ |  
naiva nirvāpayeddīpān lakṣmīnāśakarotyataḥ ||  
  
naiva nirvāpayeddīpaṃ devārthamupakalpitaṃ |  
dīpahartābhavedaṃdhakāṇo nirvāpako bhavet ||  
  
aṃguṣṭhāgreṇa deveśi dhṛtvā dīpannivedayet |  
uttoraṇaṃ tathā kuryādgātra tryāmūlayogataḥ ||  
  
pārāvata bhramākāraṃ bhrāmayecca pradarśayet |  
devasya sarvāvayavān ślokamekaṃ tataḥ paṭhet ||  
  
sa prakāśo mahādipa sarvatra timirāpahaṃ |  
sa vāhvābhyaṃtaraṃ jyotirdīpoyaṃ pratigṛhyatāṃ ||  
  
adha naivedyaṃ ||  
  
dakṣiṇe vā purobhāge vāme vā maṇḍalaṃ likhet |  
trikoṇaṃ vṛttabhūvimvamādhāraḥ śaktimarcitaṃ ||  
  
nivedayet purobhāge gaṃdhaṃ puṣpaṃ ca bhūṣaṇaṃ |  
dīpān dakṣiṇato dadyāt purato vāma vāmataḥ ||  
  
vāmatastu tathā dhūpamagrato dānadakṣiṇaḥ |  
naivedyaṃ dakṣiṇe vāme purato na tu pṛṣṭataḥ ||  
  
madirāṃ pṛṣṭhato dadyāccāgrato na kadācana |  
gaṃdhapuṣpaṃ tathā dhūpodīpo naivedyameva ca ||  
  
yasyai yaddīyate vastramalaṃkārādikāṃcanaṃ |  
teṣāṃ daivatamuccārya kṛtvā prokṣaṇapūjane ||  
  
utsṛjya mūlamaṃtreṇa pratimāmnā nivedayet |  
viśeṣārghyodakenaiva copacārān samutsṛjet ||  
  
p. 100a)  
  
anyatoyairyadutsṛjyamarghapātrasthitetaraiḥ |  
na gṛhnāti mahādevī dattaṃ vidhi śatairapi ||  
  
pādyamācamanīyaṃ ca datvā naivedya samarpayet |  
nidhāya svarṇaje pātre sādhāre tacca maṇḍale ||  
  
saṃsthāpya caturasre ca saṃskuryācchāstramārgataḥ |  
astramaṃtreṇa saṃprokṣyaṃ cakra mudrābhirakṣitaṃ ||  
  
hastau tu saṃmukhau kṛtvā saṃlagnau saṃprasāritau |  
kaniṣṭāṃguṣṭha saṃlagnau mudraiṣā cakrasaṃjñikā ||  
  
sparśa dṛṣṭvādi doṣāṃśca vāyuvījena śoṣayet |  
spṛśandakṣa karāgreṇa vahnivījena nirdahet ||  
  
vaṃ vījenāmṛtī kṛtya mūlamaṃtreṇa tatpuraḥ |  
spṛśet karābhyāṃ vidhivada sṛṣṭā cābhi maṃtrayet ||  
  
dhenumudrāṃ pradarśyātha gaṃdhapuṣpaiḥ samarcayet |  
devamabhyarcya kuryācca puṣpāṃjali mananyadhīḥ ||  
  
hemapātrasthitaṃ divyaṃ paramānnaṃ susaṃskṛtaṃ |  
paṃcadhā ṣaḍrasopetaṃ gṛhāṇa mama siddhaye ||  
  
mūlamaṃtraṃ samuccārya svāhāṃtaṃ jalamarpayet |  
karābhyāṃ saṃspṛśan pātraṃ naivedyaṃ te namo vadet ||  
  
devasya dakṣiṇe haste jalaṃ datvā paṭhedidaṃ |  
amṛtopastaraṇamasi svāheti bhavākṣaraḥ ||  
  
darśayedvāmahastena vikalotpalasannibhāṃ |  
darśayitvā grāsamudrāṃ paṃcaprāṇāhutīṃścaret ||  
  
kaniṣṭānāmikāṃguṣṭhaḥ yogaḥ prāṇasya mudrikā |  
tayāgrāsaṃ gṛhītvā prāṇāya svāheti saṃvadet ||  
  
tarjanī madhyamāṃguṣṭhayogenāpānakaṃ vadet |  
ṅentaṃ svāhāṃtamatha ca vyānāya ca tato vadet ||  
  
svāhātha madhyamā nānāṃguṣṭhayogena nirvapet |  
hitvāṃ kaniṣṭāṃ sarvābhirudānāyāgnigehinī ||  
  
sarvābhistu samānāya svāhotkāgrāsanārpayet |  
tataḥ svarṇādije pātre suto yaṃ dhenumudrayā ||  
  
amṛtīkṛtya devāya deyaṃ maṃtramimaṃ paṭhan |  
namaste devadeveśi sarvatṛptikaraṃ varaṃ ||  
  
anyāṃ niveditaṃ śuddhaṃ prakṛtisthaṃ suśītalaṃ |  
paramānaṃda saṃpūrṇaṃ gṛhāṇajalamuttamaṃ ||  
  
uktaivaṃ devatā vāme jalapātraṃ niveśayet |  
tribhirvarṇaiḥ pradātavyaṃ devārthaṃ pākabhojanaṃ ||  
  
ghṛtapakvaṃ dugdhasiddhaṃ sādhitaṃ kevalāgniyā |  
yuktaṃ vaikṣavayaṃ kena tacchūdrasya praśasyate ||  
  
p. 100b)  
  
tataḥ puṣpāṃjali dadyādastramaṃtreṇa vaṃdhanaṃ |  
diśāṃ kṛtvā javanikāṃ devasya parito nyaset ||  
  
amṛtātmaka naivedyaṃ nama ityuccaret punaḥ |  
dhenuṃmudrāṃ pradarśyātha bhujānāṃ devatāṃ smaret ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ japtvā mūlamaṃtraṃ dadejjalaṃ |  
naivedyāṃte cā camanaṃ datvā homa vidhiṃ caret ||  
  
atha ṣoḍaśopacārāṇāṃ krameṇa mudrāmāha |  
  
āsane madmamudrasyāddhastadvayamadhomukhaṃ |  
mudraiṣā kuśalapraśne tadaivorddha mukhaṃ punaḥ ||  
  
mudrāsyāt svāgate cārghyamudrātvaṃjalirūpiṇī |  
anāmāṃguṣṭayoryogātsaivāktāpādyamudrikā ||  
  
uttānaṃ dakṣahastaṃ tu kṛtvā nitaraṃmudhīḥ |  
kaṇiṣṭha hīnā saṃyuktā catasroṃgulya unnataḥ ||  
  
mudraiṣā camane proktādho mukhī sātvatā mayā |  
spṛṣṭāṃguṣṭhā bhavenmudrāṃ madhuparke varānane ||  
  
adhomukhī dakṣahaste kṛtāmuṣṭiḥ kaniṣṭayā |  
vimuktā snānamudraiṣāgaditā parameśvarī ||  
  
uttānaṃdakṣiṇaṃhastaṃ kṛtvā tanmadhyamāpunaḥ |  
aṃguṣṭhena spṛśe devāmudrā vastrasya kīrtitā ||  
  
eṣaivānāmikā sparśān mudrābhūṣaṇa saṃjñakā |  
kaniṣṭhā sparśato hyeṣā upavītasya mudrikā ||  
  
jyeṣṭhāgreṇa kaniṣṭāgraṃ spṛśed gaṃdhasyamudrikā |  
adhomukhaṃ karaṃ kṛtvā tarjanyāgreṇa yojayet ||  
  
aṃguṣṭāgreṇa mudreyaṃ puṣpākhyā parameśvarī |  
aṃguṣṭhāgreṇa tarjanyā spṛśedagraṃ maheśvarī ||  
  
dhūpamudreyamākhyātā sarvadeva priyaṃkarī |  
jyeṣṭhāgreṇa spṛśedagraṃ madhyamāyāsurārcite ||  
  
dīpamudreyamuditā sarvadevāśrayā śubhā |  
anāmāgraṃ spṛśeddevi jyeṣṭāgrena tu deśikaḥ ||  
  
naivdeya mudrā kathitā tatvamudreti kīrtitā ||  
  
atha nitya homavidhiḥ ||  
  
nityahomavidhiṃ vakṣye sarvārthaṃ yena viṃdati |  
saṃkalpa parameśāni nityahomavidhiṃ caret ||  
  
vidhivad  vahnimāniya kravyādīśaṃ parityajet |  
tataśca maṃtramuccārya kuṇḍe vā sthaṇḍile tathā ||  
  
bhūmau vā saṃstaredvahniṃ vyāhṛti tritayena tu |  
āhuti trayamutkṣipya ṣaḍaṃga havanaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
p. 101a)  
  
tato devīṃ samāvāhya mūlenaiva ṣaḍādgatiṃ |  
saṃpūjya mūlamanunā paṃcaviṃśatimāhutiṃ ||  
  
hunedājyena haviṣā tilairvā pāyasaiḥ śubhaiḥ |  
taṇḍulaistilasaṃmiśraiḥ kevalairvātha puṣpakaiḥ ||  
  
aṃgāvaraṇa devānāmekaikāmāhutiṃ hunet |  
udvāsya devaṃ vahniṃ ca pūjāsthānaṃ vrajet tataḥ ||  
  
upaviśyāsane maṃtrī dadyād bhūtavaliṃ tataḥ |  
vāminastūpacārāṃte kuryurmadyena tarpaṇe ||  
  
teṣāmanityo homastu nityaṃ tarpaṇasevanaṃ |  
kṭvāstutvā namaskṛtya visṛjerdvidumaṇḍale ||  
  
atha bhūtavalidānaṃ ||  
  
īśāne maṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā sādhāraṃ tatra niḥkṣipet |  
atra vyaṃjanatoyādyaṃ pātraṃ puṣpādipūritaṃ ||  
  
tatra bhūtāni saṃtyajya tatastebhyo valiṃ haret |  
ye raudrāraudra karmāṇo raudrasthāna nivāsinaḥ ||  
  
yoginyopyugrarūpāśca gaṇānāmadhipāścaye |  
bhūcarākhecarāścaiva ye tiṣṭhaṃtyaṃtarikṣagāḥ ||  
  
sarvete prītimanaso bhūtā gṛhaṃtvimaṃ valiṃ |  
vāmahastena tatpātre jaladhārāṃ samarpayet ||
