puṣpāṃjaliṃ samādāya bhūtāni prārthayediti ||  
  
bhūtāni yānīhavasaṃti bhūtale valiṃ gṛhītvā vivivat prayuktaṃ |  
saṃtoṣamāsādya vrajaṃ tu sarvekṣamaṃ tu tānyatra namostutebhyaḥ ||  
  
datvā puṣpāṃjaliṃ natvā viharaṃ tu yathā sukhaṃ |  
bhūtādīni ca nārā ca mudrayā visṛjettataḥ ||  
  
yathā hastagataṃ cāpaṃ tathā hastaṃ kuru priye |  
vāṇamudrayamākhyātāripuvarga nikṛṃtanī ||  
  
devaṃ tṛptimiti dhyātvā naivedyaṃ gata sārakaṃ |  
saṃciṃtya rakṣodigbhāge pātraṃ tu sthāpayet tataḥ ||  
  
gomayādbhistadastreṇa naivedya sthānaśodhanaṃ |  
devocchiṣṭaṃ gṛhītvā tu nirmālya bhojine namaḥ ||  
  
ityaiśānyāṃ viniḥkṣipyahastaṃ prakṣālayet tataḥ |  
punarācamanaṃ dadyāt karodvartanameva ca ||  
  
śuddhamācamanaṃ datvā sugaṃdhairgaṃdhayetkarau ||  
  
atha tāmbūlaṃ ||  
  
tato dadyāccatāṃvūlaṃ viṣṇave dvādaśāṃgakaṃ |  
khadirailālavaṃgaiṃducūrṇaparṇatamālakaṃ ||  
  
jātīkośadalatvagbhiḥ kastūrīkeśarairyutaṃ |  
pūgīphalamatha proktaṃ daśāṃgaṃ bhāskarasya tu ||  
  
p. 101b)  
  
mṛganābhita mālābhyāṃ hīnaṃ vighneśvarasya tu |  
paṃcāṃgaṃ cūrṇakhadiraḥ parṇapūgī phalendukaṃ ||  
  
śailaṃ devyā jātikośa yutaṃ tacca maheśituḥ |  
tataśca mukuṭādīni dadyādbhūṣaṇakāni ca ||  
  
darśayecca tathā darśaṃ kalpayecchatra cāmare |  
śirasyāropya devasya dūrvākṣata pavitrakaṃ ||  
  
ārātrikaṃ tataḥ kuryāddharmmakāmārtha siddhaye ||  
  
athārātrikaṃ ||  
  
sauvarṇe rājate kāṃsye lokanetra manohare |  
kuṃkumena likhet padmamaṣṭapatraṃ suśobhanaṃ ||  
  
daśadīpairviṃśatibhiḥ paṃcabhirnavabhistu vā |  
aṣṭabhistatva saṃkhyābhiḥ kuryādārātrikaṃ vudhaḥ ||  
  
trikoṇaṃ caiva ṣaṭkoṇa madhye viḍunipātayet |  
tat tadvidyāmayaiḥ patrairviśeṣārghyamayena vā ||  
  
ādau tu bhairavīyaṃtre cakramudrāṃ pradarśayet |  
ārātrikaṃ gṛhāṇemaṃ devatā prītihetave ||  
  
maṃtreṇānena deveśi kuryādārātrikaṃ vudhaḥ |  
māṣaistilaistaṇḍulairvāgodhūmairyavajairapi ||  
  
odanotthāśarkarotthāhāridrāḥ keśarodbhavā |  
aṣṭagaṃdhodbhāvā gauḍādīpā yatnena kārayet ||  
  
dīpānāṃ raktapītānāṃvaśyastaṃbhābhidhaṃ phalaṃ |  
mahādīpaṃ karṇikāyāṃ vasupatreṣṭadīpakān ||  
  
yavagodhūmaracitān śarkarādugdha saṃyutān |  
valayāṃcita śobhābhiḥ śobhitān ghṛta pūritān ||  
  
abhimaṃtrya tato maṃtrī ratneśvaryā na cārṇataḥ |  
śrī& hrī& glū& mlū& mayai prāgvannaśca śrī& hrīmiti kramāt ||  
  
daleśvaryā samuddiṣṭāstato mūlenatāṃ yajet |  
tatastatpātramuddhṛtyamastakāṃtaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ||  
  
navavāraṃ bhrāmayecca cakramudrāṃ pradarśayet |  
devaṃ praṇamya ca tataḥ prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ caret ||  
  
mūlamaṃtreṇātha pūrvanyāsān sarvān samācaret |  
aṣṭottara sahasraṃ tu tadarddhaṃ triśataṃ tu vā ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ vāpi japenmūlamataṃdritaḥ |  
samāpte tu japenmālāṃ nidadhyānmastakopari ||  
  
atha nitya japyarthekaramālāmāha ||  
  
atha vāṃguli mālābhirjapaṃ kuryāt taducyate |  
dvividhatvaṃ ca pratyekaṃ sṛṣṭi saṃhārabhedataḥ ||  
  
anāmā madhyamārabhya anāmūlaparvaṇi |  
triparvaṃ ca kaniṣṭhāyā anāmāgraṃ maheśvarī ||  
  
p. 102a)  
  
madhyamāgrā ca tarjanyā mūlaparvātimaṃ śive |  
śaktimālā tviyaṃ proktā saṃhārādvaiṣṇavī bhavet ||  
  
madhyamā madhyamārabhya tadagrāt parameśvarī |  
anāmā madhyakasyātha pradakṣiṇa manuvrajan ||  
  
tarjanyagrāṃtakaṃ devī ca suparvācchivābhidhā |  
saṃhāra bhairavīmālā tarjanyagrāṃtakaṃ yadi ||  
  
sauramālā tu saṃproktā saṃhārādgāṇapī bhavet |  
anāmāmadhyamārabhya madhyamā madhyataḥ śive ||  
  
agakrameṇa deveśi tarjanyagrāṃtakaṃ śive |  
gāyatrīmālikā proktā saṃhārādvadukābhidhā ||  
  
anāmāmadhyamārabhya madhyamāmadhyamāgataḥ |  
mūlabhāga krameṇaiva pradakṣiṇa manuṃ vrajet ||  
  
cīnamālā tu saṃproktā saṃhārāt kṣetrapālajā |  
madhyamāmadhyamārabhya tarjanīmadhyabhāgataḥ ||  
  
agakrameṇa deveśi tarjanī mūlataḥ śive |  
gāṃdharvamālikā proktā saṃhāradvaṭavāsinaḥ ||  
  
tarjanī mūlamārabhya cāgrabhāga krameṇa ca |  
pradakṣiṇa krameṇaiva madhyamāmūlaparvaṇi ||  
  
maṃjughoṣe mālikā tu saṃhārāt khecarī vidhau |  
kaniṣṭāgraṃ samārabhya mūlāgrāṃtaṃ krameṇa ca ||  
  
tarjanī mūlaparyaṃtaṃ mālā proktā tu sāṃbhavī |  
saṃhārādvāruṇī mālā dhanadasya prakīrtitā ||  
  
kaniṣṭhā mūlamārabhya sarpadaṇḍa krameṇa ca |  
tarjanyagrāṃtagaṃ devī yakṣiṇī mālikāmatā ||  
  
saṃhārāt kinnarīmālāmahāgānakarī parā |  
kaniṣṭhā mūlamārabhya paṃktimārga krameṇa ca ||  
  
kaniṣṭhāyāṃtakaṃ devījainamālā prakīrtitā |  
saṃhārājjainamālāsyādanāmā mūlataḥ śṛṇu ||  
  
pradakṣiṇa krameṇaiva tarjanī madhyamāṃkakaṃ |  
mālācāṃdrī tu saṃproktā saṃhārādvidhimālikā ||  
  
nityaṃ japaṃkare kuryānna tu kāmyaṃ kadācana |  
kāmyamapi kare kuryādyadi mālā na vidyate ||  
  
arghapātrājjalaṃ haste gṛhītvedaṃ paṭhet punaḥ |  
guhyātiguhyagoptātvaṃ gṛhāṇā smṛt kṛtaṃ japaṃ ||  
  
siddhirbhavatume devatvatprasādājjagatpate |  
devyāḥ vāmakaredeyaṃ sadājapaphalaṃ śive ||  
  
devasya dakṣiṇe haste toyaṃ datvā samarpayet |  
japaṃ ca japamālātha sthāpyā rahasiveṣṭhitā ||  
  
tatastu vīrastutibhirghaṃṭhāvādanapurvakaṃ |  
brāhmaṇo vedamaṃtrādyaiḥ kṣatriyaḥ sahitādibhiḥ ||  
  
p. 102b)  
  
paurāṇikādyairvaiśyastu śūdrastu prākṛtādibhiḥ |  
kaulikaiḥ śaktisahitaistaducchiṣṭaṃ ca sevayet ||  
  
mohādvākāmataḥ śūdraḥ purāṇaṃ saṃhitāṃ smṛtāṃ |  
paṭhannarakamāpnoti pitṛbhiḥ sahapāpakṛt ||  
  
yaḥ śūdro vuddhipūrvaṃ tu śṛṇuyāchrāvayedvijaḥ |  
vedaṃtaudvau duḥkhitāvasmin bhavet yatra nārakau ||  
  
adhikāramadādyastu dhanasya madatopi vā |  
śūdrastu śṛṇuyādvedaṃ sa nirvaśaśca nirddhanaṃ ||  
  
ajñānāccecchruto vedaḥ śrāpito cādvijanmanā |  
prājāpatyaṃ trayaṃ kṛtvā taudvau śraddhau bhaviṣyataḥ ||  
  
tatorghya pātramādāya mūlamuccārya maṃtravit |  
sādhu vā sādhu vā karmapadyadā caritaṃ mayā ||  
  
tatsarvaṃ bhagavandeva gṛhāṇārādhanaṃ paraṃ |  
ityarghodakasutsṛjya kiṃciddevasya dakṣiṇe ||  
  
kare samarpyayedvidvān kṛtamārādhanaṃ tataḥ |  
bhaktyā praṇamya deveśaṃ ślokairebhiḥ kṣamāpayet ||  
  
yaddattaṃ bhaktimātreṇa patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ jalaṃ |  
niveditaṃ ca naivedyaṃ tadgṛhāṇānukaṃpayā ||  
  
āvāhanaṃ na jānāmi na jānāmi visarjanaṃ |  
pūjāṃ caiva na jānāmi tvaṃ gatiḥ parameśvaraḥ ||  
  
karmaṇā manasā vācā tvattonānyāgatirmama |  
ataścāreṇa bhūtānāṃ iṣṭātvaṃ parameśvaraḥ ||  
  
nātha yoni sahasreṣu yā suyāsu rvajāmyahaṃ |  
tāsu tāsu sadābhaktiravyayāstu sadātvayi ||  
  
devodātā ca bhoktā ca devaḥ sarvamidaṃ jagat |  
devo jayati sarvatrayo devaḥ sohameva hi ||  
  
atha praṇāma pradakṣiṇe ca ||  
  
namanaṃ māna saṃproktaṃ kāyikaṃ vācikaṃ tathā |  
trividhaṃ ca namaskāre kāyikaṃ cottamaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
paurāṇikairvedikairvā kriyate vācikaṃ punaḥ |  
madhyamo sau namaskāro bhavedvācanikaṃ punaḥ ||  
  
yatsvayaṃ gadyapadyābhyāṃ ghaṭitābhyāṃ namaskṛtiḥ |  
kriyate bhaktiyukto hi vācikastu tataḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
  
jānubhyāmavanīṃ gatvā śirasā spṛśyamedinīṃ |  
kriyate yo namaskāra uttamaḥ kāyikaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
  
puṭīkṛtya karau śīrṣe dīyate pādayostathā |  
spṛṣṭvā ca jānuśīrṣābhyāṃ bhavedanyā namaskṛtaḥ ||  
  
padbhyāṃ karābhyāṃ jānubhyāmurasā śirasādṛśā |  
vacasā manasā ceti praṇāmo'ṣṭāṃga īritaḥ ||  
  
vāhubhyāṃ ca sa jānubhyāṃ śirasā vaca sādṛśā |  
paṃcāṃgoyaṃ praṇāmaḥ syāt pūjāsu pravarāvimau ||  
  
bhūmau niṣatpayaḥ kuryāt kṛṣṇe'ṣṭāṃgama tiṣṭadhīḥ |  
sahasrajanmajaṃ pāpaṃ tyaktvā vaikuṇṭhamāpnuyāt ||  
  
vedavidbhyodharāṃ datvā yatphalaṃ labhate naraḥ |  
tatphalaṃ labhate bhaktyā kṛṣṇe kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ ||  
  
p. 103a)  
  
śaṃkha haste ca sarvatra dakṣiṇaṃ parikīrtitaṃ |  
ekaṃ caṇḍyāṃ ravau saptatrīṇi dadyādvināyake ||  
  
catvāri keśave dadyāt śive cārddhaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ |  
trikoṇākāra sarvatra na tiḥśakteḥ samīritā ||  
  
arddhacaṃdraṃ maheśasya pṛṣṭhataśca samīritā |  
śivapradakṣiṇe maṃtrī arddhacaṃdra krameṇa ca ||  
  
savyāsavya krameṇaiva somasūtraṃ na laṃghayet |  
pradakṣiṇa trayaṃ kṛtvā namaskāraṃ tu paṃcakaṃ ||  
  
punaḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kuryāt punarjanma na vidyate |  
vṛṣasya vṛṣaṇa spṛṣṭvā dakṣāṃgreṃguṣṭatarjanī ||  
  
śṛṃgamadhye śivaṃ dṛṣṭvā punarjanma na vidyate |  
vṛṣaṃ caṇḍaṃ vṛṣaṃ caiva somasūtraṃ punarvṛṣaṃ ||  
  
khaṇḍaṃ ca somasūtraṃ ca punaḥ khaṃḍaṃ punarvṛṣaṃ |  
padepadāṃtaraṃ gacchet kalau śarala varjitaḥ ||  
  
vācāstotraṃ manodhyānaṃ caturaṃgaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ |  
somasūtradvayaṃ yatra yatra vā viṣṇumaṃdiraṃ ||  
  
apasavyaṃ na kurvīta kṛtvā cāṃdrāyaṇaṃ caret |  
prasārya dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ svayaṃ na muśirāpunaḥ ||  
  
darśayed dakṣiṇaṃ pārśvaṃ manasāpi pradakṣiṇaṃ |  
tridhā vaceṣṭayet samyak devatāyāḥ pradakṣiṇe ||  
  
ekahasta pramāṇaṃ tu ekaṃ vāpi pradakṣiṇaṃ |  
akāledarśanaṃ viṣṇorhaṃti puṇyaṃ purākṛtaṃ ||  
  
pradakṣiṇādvāyavīṃ gatvā diśaṃ tasmācca sāṃbhavīṃ |  
tataśca daikṣiṇāṃ datvā namaskāraṃ trikoṇavat ||  
  
brahmārpaṇasya manunā kuryād brahmārpaṇaṃ tataḥ |  
tārāditaḥ pūrvamiti prāṇavuddhīti saṃvadet ||  
  
dehadharmādhikāreti jāgratsvapnasuṣuptya ca |  
sthāsūtkā manasā vācā karmaṇābhyaṃtarastataḥ ||  
  
yacchandoścādareṇeti śiṣṇāyacca smṛtaṃ ca yat |  
uktayecca kṛtaṃ tecca sarvabrahmārpaṇaṃ bhava ||  
  
tursvāheti ca maṃtroyaṃ ṣaṭṣaḍarṇaḥ sa samīritaḥ |  
udvāsayet tato devaṃ parivāragaṇaiḥ saha ||  
  
iti puṣpāṃjaliṃ datvā praṇamya paribhāvayet |  
devasyāṃge vilīnaṃ tadraśmi vṛṃdamaśeṣataḥ ||  
  
tejorūpaṃ śivaṃ dhyātvā kṣamasveti punaḥ punaḥ |  
kṣamāpyāropayetsvīya hṛtaṃ bhoje tu devatāṃ ||  
  
atha saṃhāramudrāmāha ||  
  
spṛṣṭalagnau karau kṛtvā aṃgulyānyonya madhyataḥ |  
parivartya tataḥ kuryāt tarjanyau saralākṛtī ||  
  
p. 103b)  
  
visarjanenigaditāmudrāḥ saṃhārasaṃjñikā |  
gaccha gaccha paraṃ sthānaṃ svasthānaṃ parameśvara ||  
  
ete brahmādayo devā na viduḥ paramaṃ padaṃ |  
viṣṛjyānena maṃtreṇa tataḥ pūrakavāyunā ||  
  
dhyāyaṃśca maṃtreṇānena dhyātvātāṃ sthāpayeddhṛdi |  
tiṣṭha tiṣṭha paresthāne svasthāne parameśvara ||  
  
yatra brahmādayaḥ sarve surā tiṣṭhaṃti me hṛdi |  
iti saṃsthāpya sṃpūjya svātmānaṃ tanmadyaṃ smaret ||  
  
īśānyāṃ maṇḍalaṃ kuryādvāra padmavivarjitam |  
nirmālya bhovjaḥ pūjārthaṃ paṃcāyatana pūjane ||  
  
kartavyāṇi tu paṃcaiva īśādāmadhyamarcayet |  
laṃbodaro gaṇeśasya tejaścaṃḍo vivasvataḥ ||  
  
viśvakteno hareḥ proktaścaṇḍeśvarī maheśi tuḥ |  
caṇḍeśvaro bhavānyāśca maṃtrohaṃ tādṛśaṃ caret ||  
  
lehya coṣyāntapānādi nirmālyaṃ sragvilepanaṃ |  
nirmālya bhojine tubhyaṃ daśamiśrī śivājñayā ||  
  
iti naivedya śeṣaṃ tu datvā natvā visarjayet |  
atha hrī& hrī& saḥ bījaistu sahite nāmunā punaḥ ||  
  
maṃtreṇa bhāskarāyārcāmachidrārthaṃti vedayet |  
namo vivasvate tubhyaṃ sāsvate viṣṇutejase ||  
  
jagatsavitre śucaye savitre karmadāyine |  
tataḥ kṛtyaṃjaliścitte sthirīkṛtya paṭhediti ||  
  
yajñachidraṃ tapaḥ chidraṃ yacchidraṃ pūjane mama |  
sarvaṃ tadachidramastu bhāskarasya prasādataḥ ||  
  
arghyaṃto yena ca tato gaṃdhaṃ pūjāvaśeṣitaṃ |  
āloḍya kiṃcinmūlena maṃtrayedaṣṭadhā punaḥ ||  
  
prokṣayetena toyena svātmānaṃ mūlamaṃtrataḥ |  
nirmālyaṃ mastake dhāryaṃ mūlamaṃtreṇa maṃtriṇā ||  
  
prāśyapādodakaṃ paścānnaivedyaṃ vibhajet punaḥ |  
tadbhaktebhyaḥ svayaṃbhuktvā tanmayo viharetsuya ||  
  
śaivastu śivanirmālya prasādasyādhikāravān |  
anyonirayamāyāti na doṣaḥ paṃcasaṃgame ||  
  
svayaṃbhu liṃgatīrthaṃ vā prasādaṃ vāpi bhaktitaḥ |  
aśaivā vātha vā śaivā mucyaṃte pāparāśitaḥ ||  
  
śūdraḥ saṃsthāpitaṃ liṃgaṃ pūjayedvānameta vā |  
tatsaṃvaṃdhi prasādādi gṛhnannirāyamāpnuyāpnuyāt ||  
  
ayaṃ pūjāvidhirmukhyo yuṣmabhyaḥ saṃprakāśitaḥ ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau sādhāraṇanityārcanāyāṃ   
taryajanādivisarjanāṃtanirṇayo nāma saptadaśaḥ prakāśaḥ || 17 ||  
  
p. 104a)  
  
atha kaulavāminornityārcanamāha ||  
  
tatrādautanmārgotpatimāha |  
  
dakṣayajñe yadā devi tvayā tyaktaṃ kalevaraṃ |  
ahaṃ gṛhītvā tatskaṃdhe citāṃ praveṣṭu mudyataḥ ||  
  
vaḍavāgnergaveṣārthaṃ yatra yatrā bhavet sa tu |  
tatra tatra ca śakreṇa tūrṇaṃ nivrāpito jalaiḥ ||  
  
evaṃ paryaṃṭato varṣaṃ prasvedo me mahāna bhūt |  
tadviṃdu pātra nirdagdhā dharaṇīyaṃ bhaviṣyati ||  
  
tadā saṃprārthito viṣṇurddharaṇī rakṣaṇāya ca |  
tadāśu laghubhirvāṇaistvadaṃgāni samācchinat ||  
  
caturāśīti khaṃḍāni kṛtvāsau pātayadbhuvi |  
vā tena vījitāścāhaṃ prītohamakhilastadā ||  
  
viṣṇuśca prakaṭī bhūyaḥ pādayoḥ parito mama |  
utthāpya ca pariṣṭhaktastavaśokaśca vismṛtaḥ ||  
  
tāvad brahmādikā devānāradādyāmaharṣayaḥ |  
māṃtuṣṭuvustadā vākyaṃ viṣṇuḥ provāca pārvatī ||  
  
jñānadosi maheśatvaṃ kathaṃ mohamupāgataḥ |  
satyāḥ śarīreṇa sahapraveṣṭuṃ havyavāhanam ||  
  
anugacchetpatiṃ nārī na pumānatāṃ ca gacchati |  
iti śāstramanādṛtya kathaṃ deva vimohitaḥ ||  
  
evaṃ vadati deveśa brahmaṇāmāṃ hariṃstathā |  
śleṣālaṃkāra vāhyaiśca tuṣṭuvurvidhinā saha ||  
  
āvābhyāṃ tu tadā proktā yā ca yadhvaṃvaraṃ dvijā |  
tadātairbārhmaṇairuktaṃ jātoyaṃ dharmaviplavaḥ ||  
  
dakṣayajñāśritaiḥ śaivā brāhmaṇyādbhraṃśitā dvijāṃ |  
yajñāgatāśca sarvepi śaivaiḥ śaptādvijātayaḥ ||  
  
viṣṇunākartatairaṃgaiḥ satyāścedaṃ dharātalaṃ |  
sthale sthale śavaḥ sparśād brahmakarma vivarjitam ||  
  
tasmāddharāyāḥ saṃśuddhiṃ viprāṇāṃ cāpi śuddhatāṃ |  
brahmavākyasya satyatvaṃ yathā bhavati tatkuru ||  
  
tato dhyātvā mayā proktaṃ sammatīkṛtya viṣṇunā |  
yatra vedakriyādhvastā tatra taṃtra pravartyatāṃ ||  
  
ye viprāḥ śāpanirdagdhā brahmakarma vivarjitāḥ |  
teṣāṃ tu kauladharmoyaṃ bhuktimuktyestu sādhanaṃ ||  
  
ye viprāḥ pīṭhasaṃjātāḥ śāpanirdagdhavipratāḥ |  
teṣāṃ kuledhikāroyaṃ mārgasyāsya prajāyate ||  
  
tatkule eva pūjyatvāt kauloyaṃ mārga ucyate |  
vāmamārgastato nyūnasteṣāṃ kṣatriya vaiśyakau ||  
  
p. 104b)   
  
yajamānau tayosvatrādhikāraḥ samudāhṛtaḥ |  
siddhāṃtīyustatonyūnastatrāśūdrādhikāritā ||  
  
ye pāraṃparya yajñātvā kauladharme vitite |  
niḥśvāsaṃtatihīnāścarogiṇo nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
kaulajñānehyasiddhoyasta drvayaṃ bhoktamicchati |  
sa mahāpātakī devī sarvakarma vahiḥ kṛtaḥ ||  
  
samayācārahīnasya svairvavṛtterdurātmanaḥ |  
na siddhayaḥ kulabhraṃśestatsaṃsargaṃ na kārayet ||  
  
yaḥ śāstravidhimutsṛjya vartate kāmacārataḥ |  
sa siddhimihamāpnoti paratra ca parāṃ gatiṃ ||  
  
kuladravyāṇi sevaṃta yena darśanamāṣritaḥ |  
tadaṃgaro samaṃkhyātaṃ bhūtayoniṣu jāyate ||  
  
madapraskhalitātmā ca na kiṃcidapi vetti cet |  
na dhyānaṃ na tapaścarcā na dharmaṃ ca na satkriyāṃ ||  
  
na devaṃ na gurunmatmavicāro yadi kaulike |  
kevalaṃ viṣayāsaktaḥ patatyeva na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
śriguroḥ kulaśāstrebhyaḥ samyagvijñāya vāsamom |  
paṃcamudrāṃ niṣeveta cānyathā patito bhavet ||  
  
āvṛttiṃ gurupaṃktiṃ ca vaṭukādīnna pūjyayaḥ |  
vīropyevaṃ vṛthāyāmāddevatā śāpamāpnuyāt ||  
  
atha pūjā prakārastu kathyate kaulavāsinoḥ |  
ātmadāna samudravya devaśuddhiṃ prakalpayet ||  
  
snānasaṃdhyā bhūtaśuddhiḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ pratiṣṭhati |  
prāṇānāṃ mātṛkānyāsādikaiḥ syādātmaśodhanaṃ ||  
  
saṃmārjanānulepādyairdarpaṇodaravat kṛatṃ |  
vitāna dhūpadīpādyaiḥsthāna śuddhiriyaṃmatā ||  
  
grathitā mātṛkāvarṇai mūlamaṃtrākṣarāṇi ca |  
kramotkramatrirāvṛttirmaṃtraśuddhiriyaṃmatā ||  
  
pūjā dravyāṇi saṃprokṣya mūlāstreṇa vidhānavit |  
darśayeddhenu mudrāṃ ca dravyaśuddhiriyaṃmatā ||  
  
pīṭhe devaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya sakalīkṛtya prokṣayet |  
arghyodakena mūlena trirdīpanīṃ pradarśayet ||  
  
devaśuddhirvidhāyetthaṃ paścādyajanamārabhet |  
sā pūjā saphalā jñeyātvanyathā niṣphalā bhavet ||  
  
ādau jalamadhiṣṭāyapādaṃyorkṣālanaṃ tataḥ |  
dvirācamya śikhāṃ vadhvā kuryādvāreśapūjanaṃ ||  
  
p. 105a)  
  
viprānutsārayitvā ca tataḥ puṣpādi śodhanaṃ |  
vīrāsane tathā viśya vijayā bhakṣayet tataḥ ||  
  
śaktiṃ pārśve ca saṃsthāpya nyāsajālaṃ samācaret |  
kuladravyaṃ ca saṃśodhya pātrāṇāṃ sthāpanaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
atha vīrāsanāti ||  
  
mṛdukomalamāsīnaṃ saṃgrāma patitaṃ ca yet |  
jaṃtuvyāpāditaṃ vāpi mṛtaṃ vānaramāsanaṃ ||  
  
garbhacyutaṃ ca tārīṇāmathavā yonijaṃ na vā |  
tvaṃ ca vātaccharīraṃ vā śive kuryāt tatorcanaṃ ||  
  
ṛturaktāktavastraṃ vā āsanāya praklpayet |  
śmaśānakāṣṭhāghaṭitaṃ pīṭha vā yajñadārujaṃ ||  
  
nā dikṣito viśejjātu kṛṣṇasārājine gṛhī |  
ekahastaṃ dvihastaṃ vā caturaṃgulamucchritaṃ ||  
  
viśuddhe āsane kuryāt sthāpanaṃ pūjanaṃ vidhiḥ ||  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
deveśa śrotumicchāmi rahasyāti rahasyakaṃ |  
muṇḍādi vīraparyaṃtaṃ saṃskāraṃ sādhanaṃ vada ||  
  
śrīśiva uvāca ||  
  
rahasyātirahasyaṃ ca na kutrāpi mayeritaṃ |  
tava prītyā maheśāni kathyate śṛṇu sāṃprataṃ ||  
  
mṛdvāsano bhavedādau dvitīyaṃ syādacūḍakaṃ |  
komalaṃ ca tṛtīyaṃ syān muṇḍaproktaṃ caturthakaṃ ||  
  
mṛtāsanaṃ paṃcamaṃ ca ṣaṣṭhaṃ vīrāsanaṃ mataṃ |  
mahāvīrāsanaṃ devī saptamaṃ parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
saptānāṃ sādhayeddevī mālāpātra viśodhanaṃ |  
yaṃtra saṃśodhanaṃ caiva sarvaṃ saṃkathitaṃ purā ||  
  
idānīmāsanānāṃ ca sādhanāṃ śṛṇu pārvatī ||  
  
atha lakṣaṇamāha ||  
  
arvāk ṣaṇmāsatogarbhaḥ cyutamāhurmṛduṃvudhā |  
cūḍopanayanairhīnaimṛtaṃ vā cūḍakaṃ viduḥ ||  
  
nivṛtta cūḍako vālo hīnopanayanaḥ śive |  
yo mṛtaḥ paṃcame varṣe tameva komalaṃ viduḥ ||  
  
sāmānya maraṇaṃ prāptaṃ proktaṃ devi mṛtāsanaṃ |  
vīrarūpeṇa saṃjātaṃ tacca vīrāsanaṃ viduḥ ||  
  
āveśa śūlapāśādi mahāvīrāsanaṃ mataṃ |  
akhaṃḍāṃgaṃśavaṃ devi sa khaṃḍaṃ mastake na yat ||  
  
tanmuṇḍaṃ yatra mālādi pātrakarmaṇi kīrtitaṃ ||  
  
athāsana saṃskāraḥ ||  
  
śavamāniya deveśi garbhajaṃ yadi vāsavaṃ |  
saptamāṣṭāmamāsīnaṃ cūḍakaṃ vāpi komalaṃ ||  
  
sthānaṃ saṃśodhya yatnena vīcaveṣo mudānvitaḥ |  
tataḥ saṃskāramācarya saṃsthāpya vimale sthale ||  
  
p. 105b)  
  
gaṃdhāṣṭakaṃ samādāya prokṣayet prathamaṃ tataḥ |  
paṃcāmṛtaiḥ paṃcamavyaiḥ kalāpaṃca sa maṃtritaiḥ ||  
  
mūlena sthāpayet tatra pīṭhacakredharaṇyadhaḥ |  
trikoṇaṃ viṃdumāyāṃ ca caturasre vikoṇakaṃ ||  
  
trikoṇaṃ tasya vāhye tu padmamaṣṭadalaṃ likhet |  
ṣoḍaśāraṃ ca tadvāhye trivṛttaṃ triguṇānvitaṃ ||  
  
mūladevī ca tanmadhye mūlena paripūjayet |  
vṛttaṃ ca triguṇaṃ caiva ādimādya na yojayet ||  
  
vāṅmāyā kamalāstatra varṇādau sarvakarmasu |  
vahnerdaśakalāstatrakoṇe cāṣṭadale tathā ||  
  
ṣoḍaśāre trivṛtte ca kalā somasya pūjayet |  
tatraiva sthāpayedvīraṃ mṛdvākhyaṃ vā prayatnataḥ ||  
  
svayaṃtraṃ vilikhet tatra sādhāraśaktipūrvakaṃ |  
sudhāsiṃdhuṃmaṇidvīpaṃ ciṃtāmaṇi gṛhaṃ tathā ||  
  
śmaśānaṃ pārijātaṃ ca tanmūle śavavedikāṃ |  
dharmajñānaṃ ca vairāgyamaiśvaryaṃ tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
adharmādi tato maṃtrāpāṇipāde ca yugmakaṃ |  
akārādikṣakārāṃtaṃ mātṛkānyāsa rūpakaṃ ||  
  
tat sthāne pūjayenmaṃtrī hṛdinyāsādi pūjayet |  
karanyāsaṃ tato maṃtrī karābhyāṃ pūjayet tataḥ ||  
  
adhomukhaṃ mṛtaṃ kṛtvā tanmukhe madhuraṃ vadet |  
he vīra paramānaṃda devīparyaṃkaśaṃkaraṃ ||  
  
aṣṭasiddhiṃ ca me dehi mamaśāṃtiḥ sadā kuru |  
etad vrūhi ca vīrendra vasuvarṇaṃ mukhe kṣipet ||  
  
elālavaṃgajātīṃ ca phalatāṃvūla saṃyutaṃ |  
ṣaḍirādrakaṃ ca guḍaṃ karpūraṃ raktataṃtunā ||  
  
mūlena bhāvayet tatrajūṭikāṃ dṛḍhamuṣṭikāṃ |  
arkeṃduśita vāghālanirmitāṃ dīpavartikāṃ ||  
  
nimaṃtrayet tataḥ śāktaḥ sapta * * (?) nanu kramāt |  
vaṃdanāgurupuṣpādyairmūrddhnidevīṃ prapūjayet ||  
  
jīvanyāsaṃ tato maṃtrī prāṇamaṃtreṇa sādhayet |  
gudeliṃge tathānābhau bhūdare guhyadeśake ||  
  
ūrujānu tathā jaṃghā gulphapādatale tathā |  
śire kaṃthe nāsikāyāṃ cakṣuṣoḥ karṇayorapi ||  
  
śikhākavacagaṇḍeṣu ūrddhvādhoṣṭa * (?) ke tathā |  
taṃtayoścaiva jihvāyāṃ śiraḥ pṛṣṭe ca pārśvayoḥ ||  
  
p. 106a)  
  
hṛdādike ca vāhubhyāṃ pādābhyāṃ ca tathaiva ca |  
sarvāṃge vinyase devapīṭhanyāsamanuttamaṃ ||  
  
sūryasyamaṃḍalaṃ tatra tapinyādi kalātmakaṃ |  
mṛtakāyaśavāyātra namaścāṃte padaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
snāpayan mūlamaṃtreṇa pūjayenāṣṭavāriṇā |  
sūryasomātmakaṃ pīṭhamagnirūpaṃ prakalpayet ||  
  
merupṛṣṭa ṛṣiḥ chaṃdaḥ sutalaṃ tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
kūrmodeva tataḥ paścāddharmārtha sādhane tataḥ ||  
  
mokṣe punarmanoścaiva siddhyarthe parikīrtitaṃ |  
kūrmamudrāṃ darśayitvā astrāvaguṃṭhane tataḥ ||  
  
śaktiyonirmatsyamudrāṃ dhenumudrāṃ tataḥ śive |  
pradarśayecchoṭikāyāṃ caturasrāṃ pradarśayet ||  
  
dhṛtvā vimarśayen mūlaṃ pṛthvītvamiti vai kramāt |  
tato vajrodaketyādi manubhiḥ kāmasaṃkhyakaiḥ ||  
  
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuddhṛtya sahasrāra pade tataḥ |  
hū& phaṭ svāhā tadaṃte ca rakṣarakṣa tato vadet ||  
  
mahāpratisare sarve vighnān chedaya yugvadet |  
hūṃ phaḍaṃtaṃ samuddhṛtya vahnijāyāṃ samuccaret ||  
  
dikpāla yajanaṃ kāryamiṃdrodi kramayogataḥ |  
vīrārgalā ghoramaṃtraistathā pāśupatairapi ||  
  
mahāmaṇḍala maṃtrairvādigvaṃdhaṃ tatra kārayet |  
śivā valiṃ tatra dadyādgrahaṇādāvapi priye ||  
  
ādau madhye tathā cāṃte trivāraṃ tu śivā valiḥ |  
muṇḍagrahaṇakāle tu sarvathā tu śivā valiḥ ||  
  
śivāṃ śaktiṃ ca vā pūjyadikpālān vali saṃyutān |  
pūjayet parameśāni sāyudhādi yathākramaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ krameṇa vīrendra sarveṣāṃ valimāharet |  
vāṅmāyāṃ kamalāṃ procya devyāmuka eṣavaidyajuḥ ||  
  
pravartate imaṃ bhāgavaliṃ gṛhnaṃ tu yugmakaṃ || 87 ||  
  
tathā ||  
  
atra tiṣṭha namaḥ procya astute hūṃphaṭ svāhā |  
akārādi kṣakārāṃtaṃ viṃduyuk mātṛkākṣarān ||  
  
śirādi pādaparyaṃtaṃ veṣṭayed dakṣiṇa kramāt |  
sārddhatrivalayairyuktaṃ veṣṭayet sādhakottamaḥ ||  
  
nānāsugaṃdha dravyeṇa raktacaṃdanacaṃdanaiḥ |  
kāśmīrā gurukaṃ datvā pītasūtreṇa veṣṭayet ||  
  
p. 106b)  
  
vaṃdhayedvividhairdravyaiḥ kṣārayukta haridrayā |  
vadhnīyādraktasūtreṇa paṭṭasūtreṇa vāpi vā ||  
  
athādhikāritāmāha ||  
  
nirdvaṃdvo nirahaṃkāraḥ śuddhanāḍīgaṇāvṛtaḥ |  
pākhaṃḍovuddhirahitaḥ sarvabhūta hiterataḥ ||  
  
sarvāvayava saṃśuddhaḥ sarvaśāstra viśāradaḥ |  
kṛtābhiṣekā vidyājño japapūjādi tatparaḥ ||  
  
mṛdvāsane vaset sohitvanyathā narakaṃ vrajet |  
ajñānānmohadaṃbhaiśca dṛṣṭvādṛṣṭaṃ karoti yaḥ ||  
  
sayāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ piśācatva mavāpnuyāt |  
prayāṃti te mahāmūḍhā vyādhiḥ tvaṃ svalpajīvitāṃ ||  
  
viśedvīrastu śāstrajñaḥ samayācāra tatparaḥ |  
maṃtrajñastaṃtradarśī ca yaṃtra maṃtra vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
nigrahānugrahe śaktaścaturvarga vinodakaḥ |  
sasiddhaḥ siddhido lokeśāyānu grahanekṣamaḥ ||  
  
aśaktaḥ kurute yastu mṛtyustasya na saṃśayaḥ |  
mṛdvāsanamidaṃ proktaṃ kimanyachrotu micchasi ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
deveśa śrotumicchāmi acūḍaka viśodhanaṃ |  
acūḍakāsane devī siddhayaḥ sakalāsthitāḥ ||  
  
tamāsanaṃ samādāyamakāra paṃcakānvitaṃ |  
bhaumāṣṭamyāṃ caturdaśyā mamāyāṃ dīpakotsave ||  
  
kulaṛkṣepi deveśi acūḍakāsanaṃ bhavet |  
digvaṃdha bhūtaśuddhādīn kṛtvā yatnena pārvatī ||  
  
vajrodake samārabhya rakṣāṃtakaṃ śive |  
maṃtrānvijñāya yatnena sādhayediṣṭasādhanaṃ ||  
  
anyatsarvaṃ pūrvavat syāt komalepyeva meva tu |  
suṇḍāsanaṃ pravakṣyehaṃ śṛṇu sā vahito bhava ||  
  
bhaumāṣṭamyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ maṃgaleśa nivāsare |  
dīpotsave ca phālguṇyāṃ sāṣṭarātridinepi ca ||  
  
pūrvakṛtyaṃ samāvyāthayāma mātraṃ gate niśi |  
vīraveṣo dayāyukto bhakta bhakto jiteṃdriyaḥ ||  
  
mahāvalo mahābuddhirvijiteṃdriya śāstravit |  
khaḍgahasto muktakeśaḥ siṃdūratilakānvitaḥ ||  
  
validravyāṇi cādāya dṛḍhabhaktau mahāruciḥ |  
vīrasādhanasāmagrī saṃvṛtaḥ sādhakottamaḥ ||  
  
p. 107a)  
  
śivāvaliṃ pradatvā dautadaṃte muṇḍasādhanaṃ |  
śivārūpā svayaṃ devī tatra vighnaharāddhruvaṃ ||  
  
anyathā vighnakartāro devā daityāśca mānavāḥ |  
sarvavighnaṃ vināśārthaṃ siddhyarthaṃ pheravīṃ yajet ||  
  
śmaśāne gahvarenadyāṃ śunyagehepi sādhayet |  
śmaśāne cenmaheśāni vidhistatra śmaśānavat ||  
  
anyatra vīravat kāryaṃ sādhanaṃ sarvasādhanaṃ |  
kādirān kīlakānaṣṭau nikhanenmaṃtramuccaret ||  
  
mahāmaṃḍala maṃtraiśca sarvavighnānvighātayet |  
muṃḍamānīya yatnena paṃcagavyaṃ vinā kṣipet ||  
  
dugdhena snānamācarya tataḥ saṃvijjalena ca |  
tadaṃte surayā snānaṃ kṛtvā yatnena pārvatī ||  
  
tailaṃ lāpya ca tanmuṃḍe siṃdūrekajjalaṃ tathā |  
gaṃdhapuṣpaiśca saṃpūjya khaneddhastārddhamānataḥ ||  
  
tārāyāṃ kālikāyāṃ tu chinnāyāmapi pārvatī |  
muṇḍakādi bhavetpīṭhamādhārādikameva vā ||  
  
tatrāpi daśaśaktau tu tridhā bhinnā maheśvarī |  
ṛṭumatyāṃ tathā śaktau yatkiṃcit pīṭhamarcayet ||  
  
athāsanakālasyāvadhiryathā ||  
  
ṛṭuvastrāsanaṃ devi sūtrāṃ taṃ parikīrtitaṃ |  
muṇḍāsanaṃ tu majjītaṃ tathā śavāsane priye ||  
  
kucāsane japāttaṃ ca suratāsanameva ca |  
mṛdukomalacūḍādi cūrṇāṃtaṃ parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
tathā vīrāsanaṃ devī samādāya prayatnataḥ |  
hṛnmalaṃ dūratastyaktvā hṛdayaṃ śodhayet punaḥ ||  
  
vastrācchannaṃ bhūmayaṃ vā kṛtvā sthitvā japaṃ caret |  
naracarmāsanaṃ tathā ||  
  
vastrāsanaṃ sa bhaṃgāṃtaṃ sa lomāṃtaṃ nṛkeśarī |  
saṃvidrasaṃ sagājākhyaṃ tūrṇākhyaṃ troṭanāṃtakaṃ ||  
  
yonitvagāsanaṃ devī sa lomāṃtaṃ maheśvarī |  
yogyāsanaṃ sa jīvāṃtaṃ pātāṃtaṃ suratāsanaṃ ||  
  
viparītāsanaṃ devī tatpātāṃtaṃ prakīrtitaṃ |  
tadaṃte saṃtyajeddevī yadyanyaṃ cottarottaraṃ ||  
  
viṣarāsanakaṃ devī chedanāṃ taṃ prakīrtitaṃ |  
kramāt siddhiprade devī sarvakāryakaraṃ bhuvi ||  
  
vyāghrāsanaṃ sa lomītaṃ kaḥ cidbhaṃgātamaṃvike |  
iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ kālasaṃkhyāṃ śṛṇu priye ||  
  
p. 107b)  
  
ṛtumatyāsane devī tridināttriguṇā kṛtiḥ |  
ṛtuvastrāsanaṃ devi trisāsrātphaladāyakaṃ ||  
  
muṇḍāsanaṃ tu ṣaṇmāsairdināṃ taṃ tu śavāsanaṃ |  
naracarmāsanaṃ devīmāsāt satphalamucyate ||  
  
kucāsane dvimāsena phalaṃ bhavati suṃdari |  
ratāsane maheśāni pakṣāṃtaṃ tu phalaṃ bhavet ||  
  
mṛdvāsane tu māsane komalaṃ tatvamāsikaṃ |  
phalaṃ bhavaṃ tu deveśi ūrṇākhye daśavarṣataḥ ||  
  
acūḍake viṣṇutatvairvīrepi maṃtra eva ca |  
vastrāsane paṃcavarṣaiḥ siṃhāsanaṃ paṃcamāsakaiḥ ||  
  
mṛgākhye ṣaḍvarṣaścaiva ūrṇākhye daśavarṣataḥ |  
yonitvagāsane devi saptāhe na phalaṃ bhavet ||  
  
yonyāsane sa pakṣāṃte suratākhye dināṣṭakaṃ |  
viparīte ṣaṭdinaiścejjihvāsparśodvivedakaiḥ ||  
  
saptacuṃvanake devī yojayet kālikānnaraḥ |  
tāvatsannārakī jñeyo yāvadā huta saṃplavaṃ ||  
  
atha mṛdvāsanādya bhāve anukalpamāha ||  
  
mṛtābhāvekuśaṃ rūpaṃ viṣṭaraṃ parikalpayet |  
pūjyaṃ pīṭhaṃ viṣṭharākhyaṃ pūjyātā saṃvikāparā ||  
  
śrīdevyāviṣṭarodevidhārāstasyāsphaṭāsti ca |  
viṣṭaraṃ sādhakasyātha kathyate śṛṇu sāṃprataṃ ||  
  
bhūtapatrāṇi yasmin vai sa kuśebhyo vidhīyate ||  
  
haste pāde daśadaśasitādik yugaṃ hṛtsaroje viṃśat saṃkhyā sakalavarade   
mastake kīrtitāśca |  
guhye jihvā vada naradane ghrāṇakarṇastaneṣu liṃge cāṃdre yugaparimitā   
yojanīyākuśāśca ||  
  
ityeṣa viṣṭaraḥ khyātaḥ sarvasiddhi pradāyakaḥ |  
kuśairvā vaṃdhanaṃ kāryaṃ nāḍyāṃ vā parameśvarī ||  
  
raktamiśritasūtreṇa paṭṭasūtreṇa vā punaḥ |  
viṣṭaraṃ parikalpyātha tasyopari japaṃ caret ||  
  
vidhiviṣṭarapadmasya vidhiḥ prokto mayā tava |  
śavarūpaṃ prakalpyātha kavirvāgmī bhavennaraḥ ||  
  
svayaṃbhuvāktaṃ sūtraṃ svakartavyaṃ sarvasiddhaye |  
śavābhāve viṣṭarastu śavarūpaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
sākṣāttu śivarūpo hi viṣṭaraḥ parikīrtitaḥ |  
viṣṭaraḥ śivarūpaḥ syāt svasya śaktitvakalpanā ||  
  
śivaśakti samāyogot kiṃ na siddhyati bhūtale |  
śavavīrottamaṃ vastraṃ dvitīyo viṣṭaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
  
p. 108a)  
  
tṛtīyaṃ śṛṇu deveśi sarvasiddhipradāyakaṃ |  
viṣṭaraṃ śaṃbhurūpaḥ syāt sa śivāśivaviṣṭaraḥ ||  
  
siṃhāsanaṃ ca paryaṃko viṣṭarastu tṛtīyakaḥ |  
catuṣpāde mahādevi brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ |  
  
īśvarastu caturthaḥ syāt tanmadhye tu sadāśivaḥ |  
madhye tu āsanasthānaṃ mahāsamarasātmakaṃ ||  
  
hastau pādau prakalpyātha mastakaṃ hṛdayaṃ tathā |  
sāṃgaṃ sā ca vayaṃ devi śavaṃ vā parikalpya ca ||  
  
sa pāde śatapātreṇa bhūtapatre kuśaiḥ kramāt |  
asthiṃ vā tatra saṃsthāpya śavāṃśaṃ vāpi suṃdari ||  
  
nārī rajonvitaṃ sūtraṃ tena vāgrathanaṃ caret |  
paṭṭasūtreṇa sūtreṇa yathāyogena vā punaḥ ||  
  
jīvanyāsaṃ tatra kṛtvā dhyātvā tārāṃ japaṃ caret |  
anena krame yogena kinnasiddhyati bhūtale ||  
  
sadāśiva pretarūpo viṣṭaraḥ kathito mayā ||  
  
atha viṣṭarasya saṃskāramāha ||  
  
gāyatryātroṭanaṃ  kāryaṃ mūlena grathanaṃ caret |  
yatra noktā tu gāyatrī tat kramaṃ śṛṇu tārike ||  
  
tannāmapada devyaṃ tāṃ gāyatrīśaṃ tu sā matā |  
tannāma karma devyaṃtā gāyatrī tāriṇī mayā ||  
  
kṛtasaṃkalpako maṃtrī komalaṃ vāmapāṇinā |  
kūrcavījena saṃgṛhya astramaṃtreṇa prokṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
praṇavaṃ tu vaneśīṃ ca samuccāryaṃ tu taṃ vadet |  
śavarūpa mahāpreta cāṣṭasiddhiṃ prayacchame ||  
  
iti stutvā tu taṃ samyak kuśamadhye nidhāpayet |  
tasya gehe trikoṇaṃ tu raktacaṃdana vai ||  
  
māyāṃ tanmadhyagāṃ likhya vahirmaṃḍalakaṃ caret |  
praṇavaṃ āḥ sa rerave ca vajrarerave tataḥ ||  
  
kūrca cāstraṃ vahni vadhūmayaṃ ca maṇḍale manūḥ |  
oṃ āṃ kāraṃ ca tato māyāṃ krauṃkāraṃ haṃsa eva ca ||  
  
vahnijāyāṃ samuccārya śavaḥ prāṇāḥ padaṃ vadet |  
iha prāṇāḥ padaṃ proktā śavajīva ihasthitaḥ ||  
  
śavasya sarveṃdriyāṇi punarvāṅmana caks.u ca |  
śrotraghrāṇa ihāgatya sukhaṃ ca virameva ca ||   
  
tiṣṭhaṃ tu svāhayāyukto praṇavaṃ sthāpano manuḥ |  
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuccārya ādhāraśakti padaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
komalāsana padaṃ ṅeṃtaṃ namoṃtena tamarcayet |  
praṇavaṃ kāmapīṭhāya namaḥ śabdānnamaskriyā ||   
  
p. 108b)  
  
svarṇairmāsa trayai paṭṭe kāryā mūrtiḥ śavasya ca |  
saṃsthāpya viṣṭaraḥ syāṃte sarvaṃ pūrvavadācaret ||   
  
samayāśodhanaṃ kṛtvā śaktiśodhanamācaret |  
śaktiḥ saṃśodhanaṃ kṛtvā surāśodhanamācaret ||  
  
surāḥ saṃśodhanaṃ kṛtvā śuddhiśodhanamācaret |  
śuddhiḥ saṃśodhanaṃ kṛtvā mudrāṃ maithunaśodhayet ||   
  
atha dvijayāṃgīkāramāha ||  
  
saṃvidā śavayormadhye saṃviddevīgarīyasī |  
saṃvit prayogasteneha pūjādau sādhakottamaiḥ ||   
  
kartavyā ca mahāpūjā karaṇīyā sumaṃtritaiḥ |  
śuklapuṣpābhavedbrāhmī raktapuṣpā tu kṣatriyā ||  
  
pītapuṣpā bhavedvaiśyā kṛṣṇapuṣpā tu śūdrajā |  
ṛṣirasyā maheśāni ānaṃdabhairavā mataḥ ||  
  
vālāvīja trayeṇaiva vījaṃ śaktiśca kīlakaṃ ||  
  
kramāt kāryaṃ maheśāni viniyogastu śodhane |  
dvidhā tribhistutairvījaiḥ ṣaḍaṃgāni kramādviduḥ ||   
  
atha dhyānaṃ ||  
  
siddhāyāṃ śivavodhinīṃ karalasat pāśāṃkuśo bhairavīṃ bhaktābhīṣṭa   
varapradāna kuśalāṃ saṃsāravaṃdhachidāṃ |  
pīyūṣāṃ vudhimaṃthanodbhavarasāṃ saṃsāravaṃdhachidāṃ   
vīrārādhitapādukāṃ suvijayāṃ dhyāyejjaganmohinīṃ ||  
  
saptābhimaṃtritaṃ kṛtvā pūtaṃ sarvaṃ bhaveddhruvaṃ ||  
  
saṃvide brahmasaṃbhūte brahmaputri sadānaghe |  
bhairavānaṃda dattātvaṃ pavitrā bhavasarvadā ||  
  
oṃ brāhmyai namaḥ svāhā ||  
  
brāhmaṇīṃ śodhayediti ||  
  
siddhimūla kriye devi hīnabodha pravodhinī |  
rājā prajā vaśaṃkarī śatrukaṃṭhanisūdinī ||   
  
ai& kṣatriyāyai namaḥ svāhā ||  
  
śodhayet kṣatriyāṃ tataḥ ||  
  
ajñāneṃdha na dīptāgnerjvālāgnerjñānarūpiṇī |  
ānaṃdasyāgamaṃ prītiṃ samyag jñānaṃ prayacchame ||  
  
hrī& vaiśyāyai namaḥ svāhā ||  
  
śūdrāṃ ca śodhayet tataḥ ||  
  
namasyāmi namasyāmi yogamārga pradarśinī |  
trailokya vijaye mātaḥ samādhi phaladā bhava ||  
  
klī& śūdrāyai namaḥ svāhā ||  
  
kathyate maṃtramuttamaṃ ||  
  
p. 109a)  
  
amṛte amṛtodbhave amṛtavarṣiṇi padaṃ tataḥ |  
amṛtamākarṣayadvaṃdvaṃ siddhiṃ dehi padaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
sarvametha tato vrūyādvaśamānaya tatparaṃ |  
dviṭhāṃtoyaṃ manuḥ proktaścaturṇāmapi śodhane ||   
  
mūlamaṃtraṃ saptavāraṃ tasyopari niyojayet |  
āvāhanādi mudrāśca dhenuyoniṃ tataḥ paraṃ ||   
  
digvaṃdhanaṃ choṭikābhistāratrayapurassaraṃ |  
divyadṛṣṭyā tathā pārṣṇighātairvighnānvighātayet ||   
  
saptadhā tarpayedbrahmaraṃdhre mūlaṃ samuccaran |  
guruṃ padme sahasrāre tathā tatvākhyamudrayā ||   
  
tridhaiva tarpayedbhaktyā sādhakaḥ siddhimānasaḥ |  
ai& vadavadapadaṃ vrūyādvāgvādini padaṃ tataḥ ||   
  
mama jihvāgre sthirībhava sarvaṃ padaṃ tataḥ |  
sarva satvavaśaṃkarī svāhāṃte juhuyānmukhe ||   
  
ānaṃdena yuto devī pūjā kāryā yathāvidhiḥ |  
samayābhakṣitā yena samayāyoṣitā tathā ||   
  
sa śivaḥ sa ca yogī ca sattapasvī satāṃvaraḥ |  
sa bhavenmuktimārgasthaḥ samayā yena bhakṣitā ||   
  
bhakṣayitvā ca samayāyaṃ yaṃ maṃtraṃ japennaraḥ |  
samastaphalamāpnoti satyaṃ satyaṃ varāṇane ||   
  
atha śaktiśodhanaṃ ||  
  
sa śodhanaṃmanāścarya striṣumayeṣu sādhakaḥ |  
kṛtepi siddhihāniḥ syāt kruddhā bhavati caṇḍikā ||   
  
abhiṣekādbhavecchaktirmaṃtrasyoccāraṇāchrutau |  
ratikāla maheśāni dīkṣākāle ca kanyakā ||   
  
kalādvā yatnato vyarthādabhiṣekaṃ samācaret |  
surayā retasā vāpi jalena manunā purā ||  
  
ādau vālāṃ samuccārya tripurāyai samuccaret |  
namaḥ śabdaṃ samuccārya imāṃ śaktiṃ tato vadet ||  
  
pavitrī kuru śabdāṃte mama śaktiṃ kuru priye |  
vahnijāyāṃ samuccārya śuddhimaṃtraḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
anena vidhinā devī abhisiktā striyaḥ sadā |  
ramamāṇotra saṃnityaṃ sarvasiddhimavāpnuyāt ||  
  
ihaloke sukhaṃ bhuktāpare muktimavāpnuyāt |  
asyā karṇebhedavuddhyā māyāvījaṃ samuccaret ||  
  
p. 109b)  
  
tena suddhā bhavennārī pūjā yogyā sadaiva hi ||  
  
atha vāma kaulayorviśeṣanyāsānāha ||  
  
kṣamārabhya akārāṃto nyāsaścetkriyate yadi |  
saṃhāranyāsanāmā syāt viṃdunyā sa itīritaḥ ||  
  
vāmamārge pravṛttānāṃ śaktisevanakāriṇāṃ |  
aṃtarnyāsāt paraṃ viṃdunyāsaiḥ syācchukradhāraṇaṃ ||   
  
yāvat klinnā bhavecchaktistāvadbhogo vidyīyate |  
vāmenna dakṣiṇemārge devatā dhyānamucyate ||  
  
akṣasrajaṃ hariṇapota mudagraṭaṃ.kaṃ vidyāṃkurairavirataṃ dadhatīṃ trinetrāṃ |  
arddhendumaulimaruṇāsaraviṃdavasāṃ varṇeśvarīṃ   
praṇamatastanabhāranamrāṃ ||  
  
śaktermanorathe pūrṇe visarganyā samācaret |  
tato viṃdupatettasmādetau viṃdu visargakau ||  
  
nyāsau proktau yadā śukraṃ vāminaḥ kaulikasya vā |  
śaktaṃ stṛptiṃ vinā sarganyāsenāpi vinācyutaṃ ||   
  
tadāsau nirayaṃ yāṃti yāvaccaṃdra divākarau |  
ihalokepyavaṃśaḥsyādvihīno brahmatejasā ||   
  
bhogamokṣadhiyā vāme patituṃ ye samudyatāḥ |  
vinā maṃtraṃ sarpamaṇiṃ te gṛhītuṃ samudyatāḥ ||  
  
visargamātṛkānyāsobhave kevala mātṛvat |  
viśeṣastu visargāṃto varṇoccāro bhavediti ||  
  
viṃdusargadyutān ḍādivyaṃ tān varṇānsthitau nyaset |  
pūrvoktā eva mutpādyāḥ ṣaḍaṃga dhyānamucyate ||  
  
siṃdūrakāṃti mamitābharaṇāṃ trinetrāṃ vidyākṣasūtra   
mṛgapottavarāndhānāṃ |  
pārśvasthitāṃ bhagavatīmapi kāṃcanābhāṃ dhyāyet karābja   
ghṛtapustakavarṇamālāṃ ||  
  
mātṛkānyāsa saṃsthāne vāme kaulika vartmani |  
prapaṃcayoganāmānaṃ nyāsaṃ kuryāttaducyate ||   
  
śrīprapaṃcedvīpamāye kamalājaladhī tathā |  
giriviṣṇurvallabhe ca yattanaṃ padmadhāriṇī ||  
  
samudratanayā pīṭhe kṣetrayuglokamātṛkā |  
vanaṃ kamalavāsinyau iṃdirācāśramastathā ||  
  
māgṛheturamānadyau padmācatvarakau tathā |  
nārāyaṇapriyodbhijjausvedajāsiddhilakṣmikā ||  
  
aṇḍajaśca mahālakṣmī jarāyurājalakṣmikā |  
svarasthāne ṣoḍaśaiva yugmāni sparśajānyathā ||  
  
āryālavautruṭirmā ca caṇḍikā ca kalānvitā |  
kāṣṭhā durgenimevākhya śivaścāsauhyaparṇikā ||  
  
p. 110a)  
  
aṃvikā ghaṭike caiva muhūrtaśca sanīyutaḥ |  
īśvarī praharaścaiva śāṃbhavī divasānvitā ||  
  
sarvamaṃgalayā yuktā stitinyasya tataḥ paraṃ |  
dākṣāyiṇyo tathā vārāhaimavatyāyutaṃ nyaset ||   
  
nakṣatraṃ ca mahāmāyā yuktaṃ yogenyasettataḥ |  
māheśvaryā ca karaṇaṃ mṛḍānyā pakṣa eva ca ||   
  
rudrāṇī māsasaṃyuktā sarvāṇi rāśi saṃyutā |  
atha tu parameśvaryau kālī cānaya saṃyutā ||   
  
kātyāyaṇāṃvatsarayuk gaurīyuga samanvitā |  
bhavānī pralayau vāthayādi sthāneṣu vinyaset ||  
  
paṃcabhūtayutā brāhmī paṃcatanmātrasaṃyutā |  
vāgīśvarī tato vāṇī paṃcakarmendriyānvitā ||  
  
saṃjñāneṃdriya sāvitrī sā nilāṃ ca sarasvatī |  
gāyatrī guṇayuktā vāk prakaṭaḥ karaṇānvitā ||   
  
avasthāyuk śāradā ca dhātuyuktā ca bhāratī |  
doṣayuktā priyā ceti vyāpakaṃ vidyayā nyaset ||   
  
tritāramūlavidyāṃte mātṛkākṣaṇataḥ paraṃ |  
vadet prapaṃcarūpāyaiśriyai nama iti kramāt ||  
  
prapaṃcādibhirāpohya varṇavyaktiṃ niyojayet |  
mātṛkānyāsa saṃprokta sthāneṣu tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
tritālamūla sakala prapaṃcasya svarūpataḥ |  
āryāvārāṃ vā devyai ca namoktyā vyāpakanyaset ||  
  
prapaṃca nyāsa evaṃ syādbhuvanānyā sa ucyate |  
vinā dravyādhivāsena na smarenna japet tathā ||   
  
ye smaraṃti mahāmūḍhāstesāṃ duḥkhaṃ pade pade |  
nāsavena vināmaṃtraṃ vināmaṃtreṇa nāsavaṃ ||  
  
parasparavirodhitvāt kathaṃ pūjā vidhīyate |  
tatsaṃśaya nivṛttiṃ ca jñātvā gurumukhādyajet ||  
  
vīkṣaṇasparśana dhyānamaṃtra mudrāviśodhanaiḥ |  
dravyaṃ tarpaṇayogyaṃ syāddevatā prītikārakaṃ ||   
  
atha dravyāṃgīkāre adhikāri vivekamāha ||  
  
dravyeṇa sātvike naiva brāhmaṇaḥ pūjayecchivāṃ |  
brāhmaṇo madirāṃ datvā brāhmaṇyādeva hīyate ||   
  
brāhmaṇastvanukalpaṃ ca kṛtvā cāṇḍālatāmiyāt |  
evaṃ dadyātkṣitiṃyopi paiṣṭikīṃno kadācana ||  
  
p. 110b)  
  
nārikelodakaṃ kāṃsyetāmregavyaṃ tathā madhu |  
rājanyavaiśyayordānaṃ na dvijasya kadācana ||  
  
evaṃ pradānamātreṇa hīnāyurbrāhmaṇo bhavet |  
tāmregavyaṃ madhusamaṃdaivayaitrye na duṣyati ||  
  
ata eva maheśāni home tāmre pragṛhyate |  
brāhmaṇena tathā kāryaṃ brāhmaṇyaṃ na vinśyati ||  
  
varṇānu kramabhedena dravyabhedā bhavaṃti ca |  
kṣīreṇa brāhmaṇaistarpyaṃ ghṛtena nṛpavaṃśajaiḥ ||  
  
mākṣikairvaiśyavaryastu āsavaiḥ śūdrajātibhiḥ |  
yatrāvaśyaṃ vinirdiṣṭaṃ madirādānamuttamaṃ ||  
  
brāhmaṇastāmrapātre tu gavyamadyaṃ prakalpayet |  
satyakramāccaturvarṇaiḥ kṣīrājye madhupiṣṭajaiḥ ||  
  
tretāyāṃ pujitā devī ghṛtena sarvajātibhiḥ |  
madhubhiḥ sarvavarṇaiśca pūjitā dvāpareyuge ||  
  
pūjanīyā kalau devī kevalairāsavairniśi |  
brāhmaṇaiśca sadāpeyākṣatriyaiścaraṇāgame ||  
  
vaiśyairddhana prayogaiśca śūdreṇaiva kadācana |  
brāhmaṇasya mukhānmadya vāsanā prabhavedyadi ||  
  
caṇḍālavadvahiḥ kāryo nāsau vā mīnakaulikaḥ |  
brāhmaṇo na spṛśen madyaṃ vaidike vartmani sthitaḥ ||  
  
paṃcalakṣaṇa saṃyukto brāhmaṇaḥ kāla eva sa |  
ahaṃ brahmā tathā viṣṇustadājñāvaśavartinaḥ ||  
  
sa ced vāmapathaṃ prāptaḥ punaḥ śvānobhijāyate |  
caturlakṣaṇa saṃyukto vipro jñeyastu madhyamaḥ ||   
  
tābhyāṃ datto bhāgyavaśāttāṃtrikaḥ kopi cenmanuḥ |  
sadyaḥ phalati vāgyasya kriyayā vāpi tasya tu ||   
  
lakṣaṇa trayayuktoyastasya vaidika tāṃtrike |  
yathoktā caraṇādeva phaladastu na vāmakaḥ ||  
  
lakṣaṇadvayasaṃyuktastasya vāmaśca dakṣiṇaḥ |  
samatulya phalau syātāṃ na kadācana vaidikaḥ ||  
  
ekalakṣaṇa saṃyukto samastaphalapradaḥ |  
sautrāmiṇyāṃ kulācāre brāhmaṇaḥ prapivetsurāṃ ||  
  
anyatra kāmataḥ pītvā prāyaścittī bhavennaraḥ |  
brāhmaṇaiḥ kaulikaiḥ peyaṃ devatā tṛptihetave ||  
  
vāmināṃ kaulikānāṃ ca mukhetiṣṭhaṃti devatāḥ |  
nayaṃtiteṃ tu tadgaṃdhaṃ sa tu vaṃdyo harerapi ||  
  
devatā yasya na mukhe sākṣāccāṇḍāla eva saḥ |  
seveta madhumāṃsāni tṛṣṇayā cet sa pātakī ||   
  
p. 111a)  
  
maṃtrapūtaṃ kuladravyaṃ gurudevārpitaṃ priye |  
ye pivaṃti janāsteṣāṃ stanapānaṃ punarnava ||  
  
vahunoktena kiṃ devi yathā śaktyā dadāti yaḥ |  
kulācāryāya pūjārthaṃ kuladravyaṃ sa dharmavit ||  
  
śaive tu vaiṣṇave śākte saure su gatadarśane |  
vaudve pāśupate sāṃkhye maṃtre kālāmukhe tathā ||  
  
sadakṣa vāmasiddhāṃte vaidikādiṣu pārvatī |  
vinālipisitābhyāṃ tu pūjanaṃ niḥphalaṃ bhavet ||  
  
śṛṇu devī pravakṣyāmi kaulikā caraṇaṃ yathā |  
pāṇerbhrāṃti bhavedyasya ghṛṇāsyādraktaretasoḥ ||  
  
śuddhau cāśuddhitā vudhiḥ pāpaśaṃkā ca maithune |  
sa bhraṣṭaḥ pūjayedevīṃ caṇḍī maṃtraṃ kathaṃ japet ||  
  
atha dravyāṇāmāvaśyakatāmāha ||  
  
vinālivalidānābhyāṃ na prasīdati kālikā |  
madhubhāṃḍa sahasraistumāṃsabhāraśatairapi ||  
  
naiva tuṣṭā bhaveddevī bhagaliṃgāmṛtaṃ ṛte ||  
  
atha kāmarāṇāṃ krameṇa phalamāha ||  
  
yaḥ karoti surāpānaṃ jīvanmuktaḥ sa jāyate |  
māṃsaṃ kādatiyomartyastasya mṛtyubhayaṃ kutaḥ ||  
  
yo bhakṣayati matsyāṃśca sa śivo nātra saṃśayaḥ |  
mudrāṃ bhakṣayatedyastu sa siddhīnāṃ patirbhavet ||   
  
surataṃ yaḥ prakurute trailokya karaṇakṣamaḥ |  
etasya cārtha tritayaṃ sātviko rājasastathā ||  
  
tāmasaśceti tatrādyaurāmādibhyo nirūpataḥ |  
taṃ mārgaṃ ye vijānaṃti te muktā nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
athāśavasyatraividhyamāha ||  
  
madirātri vidhā proktā uttamāmadhyamādhamā |  
uttamā svagṛhotyannāmadhyamācānyagehajā ||  
  
adhamāhaṭṭasaṃkrītā evaṃ sā trividhāmatā ||  
  
śiva uvāca ||  
  
devāsuraiḥ purākalpemathyamāne mahodadhau |  
tatra śyāmā samutpannā surākalaśadhāriṇī ||  
  
gaurāṃgāruṇacailā ca bhāsvaddharitakaṃcukā |  
śvetottarapadādevī trailokyasyāpi mohinī ||  
  
dṛṣṭvātāṃ dānavāḥ sarve śukrācārya valātsurān |  
jitvātāṃ jagṛhustasyāḥ kalaśāccapayuḥ surāṃ ||  
  
devān palāyitān dṛṣṭvā śaktayastatra saṃsthitāḥ |  
payustā apitāṃ puṇyāṃ surāṃ daivatamātaraḥ ||  
  
varānapi vahūn dadyuḥ surāyāḥ suramātaraḥ |  
abhayāsmāttarpayaṃti śeṣaṃ gṛhnaṃti ye narāḥ ||  
  
te smadrūpā na saṃdeho bhuktiktyaikabhājanaṃ |  
surāgaṃgā surāsiṃdhuḥ surādevī sarasvatī ||  
  
p. 111b)  
  
surā godāvarī revāsuraiva paramaṃ padaṃ |  
surāniṃdaṃti ye mūḍhā mūḍhāste janmajanmani ||  
  
gaṃdharvaistūyamānāstā śaktayaste ca dānavā |  
utpattiḥ kathitā devī pānaṃ ca kathayāmyahaṃ ||  
  
jihvāmūlaṃ samārabhya hṛdayaṃ yā ca suṃdarī |  
ṣoḍaśāṃgula vijñeyā sthānā svādomṛtaṃ padaṃ ||  
  
ṣoḍaśaiva kalāyuktaṃ ṣoḍaśāṃgulamāyataṃ |  
pivate daivatairdevi madyamamṛtarūpiṇaṃ ||  
  
prathamaṃ pivate vahni dvitīyaṃ śaśinā pivet |  
viṣṇunā ca tṛtīyaṃ tu caturthaṃ varuṇaḥ pivet ||  
  
kumāraḥ paṃcamaṃ devī ṣaṣṭhaṃ tu vāsavaṃ pivet |  
saptamaṃ ṛṣibhiḥ sarvaiḥ gaṇeśvaroṣṭamaṃ pivet ||  
  
navamaṃ dharmarājena marutairdaśamaṃ pivet |  
ekādaśamasaṃsthāne brahmaputrā pivet priye ||  
  
kaumāra dvādaśaṃ yāti vaināyakyaḥ trayodaśaṃ ||  
  
caturdaśyāṃ paśupatiṃ ||  
  
ete pītvā daśaiḥ paṃcaṣoḍaśaṃ na prakāśayet |  
na pītaṃ mānuṣairbhadre devaiḥ pītvā tu saṃbhavaiḥ ||  
  
pītvā ca kathitairbhadre adhunā devatā śṛṇu |  
yā rasā sā umādevī yo madyaḥ sa maheśvaraḥ ||  
  
yo varṇaḥ sa svayaṃ brahmā yo gaṃdhaḥ sa janārdanaḥ |  
yaḥ svādaḥ sa tu somoyaṃ yo vegaḥ pavanaḥ svayaṃ ||  
  
jñānavijñāna saṃpannaṃ yo madyaṃ citsureśvarī |  
  
atha pākaprakāramāha ||  
  
aṃbhasāṃ dvādaśaprasthaṃ ca taṇḍulā |  
prasthārddhaṃ taṇḍulaṃ proktaṃ tāvanmātrāstadaṃkurān ||  
  
śītādirahite sthāne divasadvayamāsya tat |  
paścāt bhānau samāropya jaṃvāla sadṛśaṃ pacet ||  
  
pādaprasthaṃ daṃḍulāśca tanmātrānaṃ kurākṣipet |  
punardinadvayaṃ sthāpya punarevaṃ prakalpayet ||  
  
arddhaṃ tasya samādāya taṃḍuleṣu viniḥkṣipet |  
kunarevaṃ tridhā kuryāttāṃḍulī sā surā smṛtā ||  
  
ayameva bhavet somaḥ somayāga phalapradaḥ |  
dūtīyāgo bhavedyogaḥ somapānaṃ tu tat smṛtaṃ ||  
  
yāgatiḥ somayajñena kaulikānāmanena sā |  
bhogaḥ svargaśca bhavati vinākaṣṭeṃ na vāmināṃ ||  
  
evaṃ tu yavapiṣṭottho devaṃ soma iti smṛtaḥ |  
yacca taṇḍula yogena śakti somo nigadyate ||  
  
svinnaḥ kuṭṭita godhūmāḥ samakliṣṭe na saṃyutāḥ |  
styāpito dvādaśāhaṃ ca vāruṇyāṃ paripācitāḥ ||  
  
p. 112a)  
  
tanmadyaṃ sūryasaṃjñaṃ syādyoginī sadavarddhanaṃ |  
pītaṃ tacca pūjāṃte vājapeya phalaṃ labhet ||  
  
idameva tridhā yuktaṃ dalaṃ madyaṃ ca sādhikaṃ |  
agnirbhavettasya pānādagnihotra phalaṃ labhet ||  
  
agniryadā saptavāraṃ vāruṇīyaṃtragaḥ kṛtaḥ |  
vaḍavānalamāno sau mahāpātakanāśanaḥ ||  
  
daśaḥprasthaṃ guḍaproktastāvaddhūttūlajātva ca |  
jaṃvutvagdhātakī puṣpaṃ tadarddhaṃ nārikeraja ||  
  
kusumaṃ ca tadarddhaṃ syāt tadarddhaṃ ca harītakī |  
tāvadvibhītakaṃ proktaṃ caturthāṃśaṃ kaṭutrayaṃ ||  
  
tāvacca citrekaṃ tasmādguḍo dvādaśabhāgikaḥ |  
kareṇa bhrāmaye samyak anuloma vilomataḥ ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśatāvṛttyā trisaṃdhyaṃ prativāsaraṃ |  
dvādaśāhena pākaḥ syādvāruṇī yaṃtragaṃ pacet ||  
  
eṣāgauḍīti vikhyātā mahāmadakarī matāḥ |  
śivena nirmitā pūrvaṃ svayaṃ pītā ca bhairavaiḥ ||  
  
dviguṇaṃ makaraṃdākhyaṃ vāri saṃyojayedguḍe |  
ṣoḍaśāhe na pākaḥ syāccheṣamanyatpuroktavat ||  
  
sarvadevapriyāceyaṃ vaśīkaraṇīmadbhutaṃ |  
devānāṃ śaktayovaśyāmānuṣīṇāṃ tu kādrathā ||  
  
harītakī citrakaṃ ca marīcaṃ dhātakī tathā |  
madhūkapuṣpaṃ kṣaudraṃ ca bhāgaikena vivarddhitaṃ ||  
  
aśītiguḍasaṃmiśraṃ śeṣamanyatpuroktavat |  
idaṃ manoharaṃ dravyaṃ yoginī pānamuttamaṃ ||  
  
madyābhāve pravakṣyāmi viṃdumadyādhikaṃ surāḥ |  
māhiṣaṃ dadhisaṃgrāhyaṃ caturdaśaguṇāṃ surāṃ ||  
  
mocā phalasya pakvasya marditasya rasastathā |  
grāhyaṃ dadhi caturthāṃśaṃ tatsaṃmargha ghaṭekṣipet ||  
  
catvāriṃśaddinānyaṣṭau paṃke paṃkaja saṃkule |  
nidhāyoddhṛtya kiraṇaiḥ sauraiḥ samyagviśoṣayet ||  
  
yadā tat kaṭhinī bhāvastathā kuryādvaṃṭī śubhāṃ |  
guṃjābhāṃ jalasaṃpūrṇetāṃ pātre praṇidhāpayet ||  
  
idaṃ surātopyadhikaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ praśasyate |  
gauḍī sādhvī tathā paiṣṭī trividhā tu surā smṛtāḥ ||  
  
śūdrāṇāmucitā ceyaṃ vaṃśā kṣatriya vaiśyayoḥ |  
brahmānaṃda surāyaistu prītā vipraistu kaulikaiḥ ||  
  
na conmādakarī teṣāṃ sureyaṃ vuddhivardhinī |  
sarvasiddhikarī paiṣṭhī gauḍī bhogapradāyinī ||  
  
mādhvī muktikarī jñeyā drākṣā rājyapradāmatā |  
vidyāpradaikṣarīhālā khārjūrī ripunāśinī ||  
  
tālajā staṃbhaneśastāpanasākhā śubhapradā |  
nārikelādbhavā śrīdāniṃvajāroganāśinī ||  
  
madhūkajā jñānakarī vaileyā pāpanāśinī |  
yatsānaṃdaṃ rucikaraṃ sāmodaṃ ca manoharaṃ ||  
  
p. 112b)  
  
madyaṃ taduttamaṃ devā devatā prītikārakaṃ |  
brahmā syāt salile viṣṇurgaṃdhe rudraśca tadruvau ||  
  
paramātmā tadānaṃde tasmāt sevyamidaṃ priye |  
dṛṣṭvā praṇamya prathamaṃ tadrūpāṃ vāruṇī kalāṃ ||  
  
varuṇenārcitā devī vāruṇī iti viśrutā |  
suraistu pivate nityaṃ surānāma iti smṛtā ||  
  
madanenārcitā nityaṃ madireyaṃ prakīrtitā |  
paramārthe tu utpannā parāśaktiḥ prakīrtitā ||  
  
yathāmṛtaṃ tathā madyaṃ proktaḥ kāle niṣevitaṃ |  
amṛtena sahotpannaṃ sthāne madyaṃ sudhāyate ||  
  
viṣeṇāpi sahotpannaṃ tena madyaṃ viṣāyate ||  
  
atha niṣiddhamāha ||  
  
naṣṭaiḥ paryuṣitocchiṣṭai durgaṃdhairgaṃdhavarjitaiḥ |  
hetubhiḥ parapātrasthaistarpaṇaṃ niḥphalaṃ bhavet ||   
  
svapātrasthaṃ ca hetuṃ ca na dadyāt bhairavāya ca |  
datte ca siddhihāniḥ syādityājñā śaṃkaraiḥ kṛtā ||  
  
svādiṣṭaiśca madotsiktairdravyairmṛtasannibhaiḥ |  
manoharaiśca devīnāṃ tarpaṇaṃ saphalaṃ bhavet ||  
  
māṃsaṃ tu trividhaṃ proktaṃ jala khecara bhūcaraṃ |  
jalecarāsyuḥ kūrmādyā khecarāḥ kukkuṭādayaḥ ||   
  
bhūcarā tu mṛgādyāsyuḥ teṣaṃ bhedāṣṭakaṃ bhavet |  
gonarebhāśvamahiṣavarāhājamṛgodbhavaṃ ||  
  
mahāmāṃsāṣṭakaṃ proktaṃ devatā prītikārakaṃ |  
śaśakaṃ śataguṇaṃ proktaṃ godhāyāstaccaturguṇaṃ ||  
  
mayūrapakṣiṇāṃ māṃsaṃ teṣāṃ caivādhikaṃ bhavet |  
kūrmamāhiṣakhaḍgānāṃ puṇyaṃ taccāpyamutra ca ||  
  
hāriṇaṃ tu tato deva puṇyaṃ meṣaṃ tadādhikaṃ |  
meṣāccadviguṇaṃ chāgaṃ chāgādvari caturguṇaṃ ||  
  
hareścāṣṭaguṇo'naḍvānaḍuhāna dviguṇo gajaḥ |  
gajācca ṣaḍguṇācāśva aśvāccalaśunodhikaḥ ||  
  
palāṃḍunārajastulyaṃ viśeṣeṇaiva vidyate |  
matsyaṃ ca trividhaṃ proktamuttamādhamamadhyamaṃ ||  
  
uttamaṃ trividhaṃ devi śālapāṭhī na rohitāḥ |  
prācīśaṃ kaṇṭhakairhīnaṃ tailāktaṃ svādu saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
devyāḥ prītikaraṃ caiva madhyamaṃ tadudāhṛtaṃ |  
kṣudrāṇi tāni sarvāṇi adhamānyādguruttamāḥ ||  
  
vraiheyaṃ maṇḍalākāraṃ caṃdraviṃvanibhaṃ śubhaṃ |  
cāru pakva manohārī śarkarādyaiḥ prapūritaṃ ||  
  
p. 113a)  
  
pūjākāle ca devīnāṃ mudraiyā parikīrtitā |  
bhāgadvayaṃ taṇḍulānāṃ maithikāṃ hiṃgujīrakaṃ ||  
  
lavaṇaṃ ca yathā yogyaṃ surayāmarditaṃ dṛḍhaṃ |  
cakrī kṛtaṃ nāgavallī dalaiśca pariveṣṭitaṃ ||  
  
jalayaṃtre vipakvaṃ tat śaktimudreya mucyate |  
kālekhaṇḍaṃ varkarasya vādyayaṃtra vipācitaṃ ||  
  
māṣāḍhakī masūrāṇāṃ vaṭakānāṃ samanvitaṃ |  
samabhāgena cūrṇena tacca hiṃgvādibhiryutaṃ ||  
  
vaṭakāḥ kaṭutailena pakvāḥ syānmudrikāparā |  
sarvāsāmeva śudrāṇāṃ karaṇe tu jalasthale ||  
  
surādeyātha vā madyamāsavaṃ vāmacetarat |  
godhūmacūrṇaṃmāsaṃ ca pakvaṃ saṃmelaye dṛḍhaṃ ||  
  
dinatrayaṃ jalesthāpyaṃ yāvadamla prajāyate |  
sūkṣmāṇi matsyakhaṃḍāni pakvamaṃtra tu melayet ||  
  
madhye tadroṭikāyāśca datvā paktvā ca roṭikāṃ |  
iyaṃ tu paramāmudrāśaktīnāmati tṛptidā ||  
  
ratimātre vāminātra kartavyā buddhirīdṛśī |  
liṃgaṃ śivobhagaḥ śaktiṃrgāṃgaṃ vārijalaṃ mataṃ ||   
  
iti bhāvanayā vāmīrataṃ kurvannimucyate |  
anyathā strīgamaṃ kurvanniraye paripacyate ||  
  
sadhayārati saṃhūtaṃ kuṇḍamuttamabhūtidaṃ |  
vidhavārati saṃbhūtaṃ golaṃ siddhipradaṃ śuci ||  
  
kuladravyairvinākuryājjapapūjāṃ tathā vrataṃ |  
niṣphalaṃta bhave devi bhasmanā ca hutaṃ yathā ||  
  
atha mukhyābhāve eteṣā manukalpamāha ||  
  
nārikelodakaṃ kāṃsye tāmre vā visṛjen madhu |  
gavyaṃ ca tāmrapātrasthaṃ surātulyaṃ ghṛtaṃ vinā ||  
  
takraṃ kṣīraṃ guḍaṃ kṣaudraṃ dadhyājya tilaśarkarā |  
tailaṃ mārjāravālaṃ ca dravyaṃ daśavidhaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
athavā ||  
  
dravyābhāve tu vaṭakaṃ jale saṃloḍya tarpayet |  
guḍamiśreṇa takreṇa tacca vā madhubhājanaṃ ||  
  
sauvīreṇātha vā kuryāde tatkarma na lopayet ||  
  
vaṭakaṃ yathā ||  
  
madyaṃ māṃsaṃ ca vijayāmaṣṭagaṃdhaiḥ sumiśritāṃ |  
saṃmarghavaṭakaṃ kuryāt tarpaṇārthaṃ ca saṃcayet ||  
  
lavaṇārdrakapiṇyāka palāṃḍuṃ māṃsapaṃcakaṃ |  
laśunaṃ ca mahādevi māṃsa pratinidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||   
  
p. 113b)  
  
matsyābhāve tu kramukaṃ tāṃvūla yadyadāmiṣaṃ |  
mudrābhāve taṃḍulaṃ vā bharjitaṃ ca na kādikaṃ ||  
  
vāmolau saṃlikhed raktacaṃdanena trikoṇakaṃ |  
tanmadhye śaktivījaṃ hi vilekhet sādhakottamaḥ ||  
  
tatra saṃpūjayet kāṃtāṃ maṃtreṇānena pārvatī |  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ vāpi tadardhaṃ vā tadardhakaṃ ||  
  
trikoṇe saṃjapen maṃtrī gāyatryā śakti saṃjñayā |  
śaktau śaktyāṃ prakurvīta karmalopaṃ na kārayet ||  
  
yadi vipro bhavet tatra kulapūjāparāyaṇaḥ |  
tadānena vidhānena kuryāt kularasodbhavaṃ ||  
  
aparāpuṣpagarbhe tu kulasthānaṃ manoharaṃ |  
hayāri kusume devi svayamasti sadāśivaḥ ||  
  
tanmadhyatau tu dhyātyaiva puṣpamadhye tu caṃdanaṃ |  
raktaṃ vā kusumaṃ datvā dhyātvātmānaṃ kulātmakaṃ ||  
  
yojayettaṃ śivaṃ śaktyāmaikyaṃ saṃbhāvayan dhiyā |  
kṣaṇaṃ viciṃtya tatraiva saṃpūjya parameśvarīṃ ||  
  
japtvā tadeva kuṇḍākhyaṃ dravyaṃ paramadurlabhaṃ |  
  
athavā ||  
  
kuṇḍe golodbhavaṃ dravyasyā bhāve śṛṇu suṃdari |  
kathaṃ snānaṃ ca kuryāccadevatātoṣa hetave ||  
  
yasya kasyataroḥ puṣpaṃ gṛhītvāśu prayatnataḥ |  
teṣāṃ madhya dvayaṃ grāhyaṃ hastābhyāṃ manasā tadā ||  
  
ubhayoḥ paṃcamaṃ tatra kurvīta vidhivannaraḥ |  
raktacaṃdana ghṛṣṭena jale caiva kṣipet tadā ||  
  
tajjalena prakurvīta devatā snānamuttamaṃ |  
vāṃchitaṃ phalamāpnoti satyaṃ satyaṃ varānane ||  
  
svayaṃbhū kusumābhāve raktacaṃdanakaṃ kṣipet |  
makāra paṃcā bhāve tu paṃcamaṃkārayet priye ||  
  
abhāve paṃcame devi manasā paṃcamaṃ caret ||  
  
athāṃtarīyemakāramāha ||  
  
āmūlādhāramābrahmaraṃdhragatvā punaḥ punaḥ |  
ciccaṃdrakuṃḍalīśakti mudrayāsyānmukhodayaḥ ||  
  
vyoma paṃkaja niḥsyaṃda sudhāpānarato bhavet |  
madhupānamidaṃ proktamitare madyapāyinaḥ ||   
  
puṇyāpuṇyavaruṃ hatvā jñāna khaḍgena yogavit |  
pare layaṃ nayeccittaṃ palāśī sa nigadyate ||  
  
manasā sveṃdriyagaṇaṃ niyamyātmaniyojayet |  
matsyāśī sa janaḥ proktaḥ śeṣādhīvaravṛttayaḥ ||  
  
p. 114a)  
  
aprabuddhāyaśoḥ śaktiḥ prabuddhā kaulikasya ca |  
śaktiṃ tāṃ sevayedyastu sa bhavecchakti sevakaḥ ||  
  
ityevaṃ paṃcamudrāṇāṃ guptaṃ tatvaṃ mayoditaṃ |  
jñātvā gurumukhāt samyagyaḥ seveta samucyate ||  
  
athaiteṣāṃ saṃskāravaśyakatāmāha ||  
  
asaṃskṛtā sutā pītvā kalahavyādhi duḥkhadā |  
āyuḥ śrīkīrti saubhāgya dharmavidyāvināśinī ||  
  
tasmāt saṃskṛtya vidhivat kuladravyaistatorcayet |  
susaṃskṛtā surā roga duḥkhāpatyayahāriṇī ||  
  
āyuḥ śrīkīrti saubhāgya dharmavidyāvivarddhinī |  
anyathā narakaṃ yāṃti dātā bhoktā na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
yathā surā vahni varṇā mahāpātakanāśinī |  
tathā maṃtra viśuddhā sā divyagniḥ svargamokṣadā ||  
  
dattātreyeṇa muninā śukreṇa ca mahātmanā |  
dhīmatā balabhadreṇa surāḥ pītāstu maṃtritāḥ ||  
  
saṃskāra saṃyute hetau datte tuṣyaṃti devatāḥ |  
maṃtrāṇāṃ smaraṇādeva māhāpātakanāśanaṃ ||  
  
āyuḥ śrīkāṃti saubhāgyaṃ jñānaṃ saṃskṛtayā tataḥ |  
aṣṭaiśvaryaṃ khecaratvaṃ patanaṃ vidhivaryanāt ||  
  
maṃtrairyutaṃ kuladravyaṃ gurudevārpitaṃ priye |  
ye pivaṃti janāsteṣāṃ pāpaleśaṃ na vidyate ||  
  
athaiṣāṃ krameṇa saṃskāramāha ||  
  
tatrādau kulasaṃsthāpanaṃ yathā ||  
  
vāmabhāge maheśāni maṇḍale caturasrake |  
yāti dvayaṃ samālikhya tadaṃtarbrahmaraṃdhrakaṃ ||  
  
vṛttenavettuyitvā tu caturasreṇa veṣṭayet |  
arghyodakena saṃprokṣya tatra saṃsthāpya yaṃtrikāṃ ||  
  
kalābhirdaśabhirvyāptaṃ yajet tatrāgni maṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
atha kalaśasya vyutpatti lakṣaṇaṃ cāha ||  
  
kalāṃ kalāṃ gṛhītvā ca devānāṃ viśvakarmaṇī |  
nirmitoyaṃ surairya smāt kalaśastena ucyate ||  
  
paṃcāśadaṃgula vyāsa ucchrāyo dvādaśāṃgulaḥ |  
kalaśānāṃ pramāṇaṃ tu mukhamaṣṭāṃgulaṃ tathā ||  
  
ādhāre sthāpayan maṃtrī sauvarṇaṃ cātha rājataṃ |  
kāṃśyajaṃ mṛṇmayaṃ vāpi ghaṭaṃ nirvraṇaśālinaṃ ||  
  
sauvarṇaṃ bhogadaṃ proktaṃ rājataṃ mokṣadaṃ smṛtaṃ |  
kāṃśyaṃ śāṃtikaraṃ caiva mṛṇmayaṃ puṣṭidaṃ bhavet ||  
  
ghaṭamūlesthito brahmā ghaṭamadhye ca keśava |  
ghaṭakaṇṭhe nīlakaṇṭho ghaṭāgre śaktidevatā ||  
  
ghaṭasya sthāpane naiva devatā karagā bhavet |  
sarvoktaṃ sarvarūpaṃ ca sarvadevamayaṃ śivaṃ ||  
  
ānaṃdabhairavaṃ paśyat ghaṭhamadhye niraṃtaraṃ |  
tejaḥ svarūpī cākhyāto maṇiḥ kalpalatāmayaḥ ||  
  
p. 114b)  
  
sudhārasamayī vrāṇī amṛtasyaṃdanirbharī ||  
  
devatānāṃ nivedenaṃ ||  
  
svayaṃ karoti deveśi svayaṃ nītvā samoghaṭaḥ |  
tadgehe gamanādeva mūkovadati sāradā ||  
  
sahasra śatadhārī ca sahāśruti dharoddhataḥ |  
ghaṭasiddhiriyaṃ proktā sarvaśāstramayī bhavet ||  
  
sāmānyārghya viśeṣārghyau dvauproktau yatra pārvatī |  
cakṣuḥ prāṇādi rūpatvā ghaṭastvāvaśyakāmataḥ ||  
  
yathā trikoṇaṃ deveśi viṃdunāvarjitaṃ bhavet |  
tathā ghaṭaṃ vinā devi pūjā sarvatra varjitā ||  
  
kṣālayedastramaṃtreṇa kuṃbhaṃ samyak sureśvarī |  
sthāpayet kalaśādhāraṃ kuṃbhaṃ gaṃdhādhikasitaṃ ||  
  
veṣṭitaṃ raktavastreṇa raktamālyena bhūṣitaṃ |  
sthāpayet kalaśaṃ tatra sauvarṇādibhi bhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
kalādvādaśasaṃyuktaṃ bhānuviṃvaṃ yajediha |  
śuddhena hetunā maṃtrī mūlamaṃtreṇa pūrayet ||  
  
kalāṣoḍaśasaṃvyāptamiṃduviṃvaṃ yajediha ||  
  
atha kalānāṃ vījamuktamaṃnyatra ||  
  
maṇḍale kalaśe devyā vahnyekaśaśimaṇḍalaṃ |  
tārabhaṃgaistribhirmaṃtrīviṃva tritayamarcayet ||  
  
rakṣayedastramaṃtreṇa tanutreṇāvaguṇṭhayet |  
vīkṣayenmūlamaṃtreṇa tenaivābhyukṣa sādhakaḥ ||  
  
gaṃdhādinā samabhyarcya bhāvayed devatātmakaṃ |  
anyacca śṛṇu deveśi yathā kulādikarmaṇi ||  
  
hānirna jāyate devi tān vai maṃtrān śrṇu priye |  
ekameva paraṃ brahmasthūla sūkṣmamayaṃ dhruvaṃ ||  
  
kacodbhavāṃ brahmahatyāṃ tena tenāśayāmyahaṃ |  
sūryamaṇḍalasaṃbūte varuṇālayasaṃbhave ||  
  
amāvījamayedevī śukreśāpādvimucyatāṃ |  
vedānāṃ praṇavo vījaṃ brahmānaṃdamayaṃ yadi ||  
  
tena satyena te devi brahmahatyāṃ vyapohatu |  
evaṃ maṃtra trayeṇaiva cābhi maṃtryakulaṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
pradadyāt kālikāyai ca naivedya mudareharet |  
vedādi varuṇāṃtāṃ ca ṣaḍdīrghasvarabheditaṃ ||  
  
śukraśāpavimācitāyai sudhādevyai namostute |  
dvādaśadhā japenmaṃtraṃ śukraśāpa vimuktaye ||  
  
māyayā ramayā vālā saṃvudhyaṃtā trivarṇakā |  
śukraśāpaṃ vimocāya punastadvarṇakāṃtikā ||  
  
p. 115a)  
  
yasyā upāsanā tasyā vījena puṭito manuḥ |  
ṣoḍaśārṇastayākhyāto maṃtritāṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ ||  
   
niḥśāpaṃ kurute sādhyaṃ bhuktimuktyaika bhājanaṃ |  
vedādi vāruṇaṃ vījaṃ ṣaḍdīrghasvarabheditaṃ ||  
  
brahmaśāpavimocitāyai sudhādevyai namostu ca |  
daśakṛtyaṃ japenmaṃtraṃ brahmaśāpa vimuktaye ||  
  
māyāśriyāṃkuśaṃ caiva ṣaḍdīrghaḥ svarabheditaṃ |  
surākṛṣṇa svarūpāṃ te pāpaṃ mocaya tatparaṃ ||  
  
amṛtaṃ śrāvayadvaṃdvaṃ vahnijāyā tataḥ paraṃ |  
anena manunā maṃtrī kṛṣṇaśāpaṃ vimocayet ||  
  
pavamānaḥ parānaṃdaḥ pavamānaḥ parorasaḥ |  
pavamānaṃ paraṃ jñānaṃ tena te plāvayāmyahaṃ ||  
  
ślokānetānpaṭhetpaścāddīpi mṛtaśīmanūn |  
akhaṇḍaika rasānaṃda kalevara sudhātmani ||  
  
svacchaṃdaḥ sphuraṇākāranidhejya mṛtarūpiṇī |  
akulasthāmṛtākāre śuddhijñānakare pare ||  
  
amṛtatvaṃ nidhehya smin vastūniṃ klinnarūpiṇī |  
tadrūpiṇikarasyarśaṃ kṛtvāhyetatsvarūpiṇī ||  
  
bhūtvā mṛtāparākāremapi visphuraṇaṃ kuru |  
athavā mūlamuccārya suṣumṇā mūlavartmanā ||  
  
pāpayitvāṃ kuṇḍalinīṃ dravyaśuddhiriyaṃ punaḥ |  
anenaiva vidhānena vīraśuddhiṃ samācaret ||  
  
dravyamadhye bhairavabhairavyorddhyānaṃ ||  
  
sūryakoṭi pratīkāśaṃ caṃdrakoṭi suśītalaṃ |  
aṣṭādaśabhujaṃ devaṃ paṃcavaktraṃ trilocanaṃ ||  
  
amṛtārṇavamadhyasthaṃ brahmapadmo paristhitaṃ |  
vṛṣārūḍhaṃ nīlakaṃṭhaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
kapālakhaṭvāṃgadharaṃ ghaṇṭhāḍamaruvādinaṃ |  
pāśāṃkuśadharaṃ devaṃ gadā muśaladhāriṇaṃ ||  
  
khaḍgakheṭakapaṭṭīśamudgaraṃ śūlakuṃtakaṃ |  
vicitrakheṭakaṃ muṇḍaṃ varadā bhayapāṇinaṃ ||  
  
lohitaṃ devadeveśaṃ bhāvayet sādhakottamaṃ |  
evaṃ dhyātvā svamaṃtreṇa puṣpāṃjali trayaṃ kṣipet ||  
  
tato ānaṃdabhairavīṃ dhyāyet ||  
  
p. 115b)  
  
tasyotsaṃge surāṃ devīṃ caṃdrakoṭi yutaprabhāṃ |  
himakundendudhavalāṃ paṃcavaktrāṃ trilocanāṃ ||  
  
aṣṭādaśabhujairyuktāṃ sarvānaṃdavarodyatāṃ |  
prahasaṃtīṃ viśālākṣīṃ devadevasya saṃmukhīṃ ||  
  
athavā devadeveśamarddhanārīśvaraṃ smaret |  
evaṃ dhyātvā svamaṃtreṇa pūjayet sādhakottamaḥ ||  
  
śivacaṃdrau mātṛkāṃtaṃ tathā kṣamalavahnayaḥ |  
vāyuśca vāmakarṇena bhūṣito viṃdunā tataḥ ||  
  
vījame tat samuccārya tathā vā naṃdabhairavaṃ |  
ṅentaṃ śikhāmastrayutaṃ pūrvavījaṃ tu saṃlikhet ||  
  
caṃdrahitvādimaṃ kuryāt karṇe vāmākṣi yojayet |  
surādevyai tato vauṣaḍiyamānaṃdabhairavī ||  
  
anena manuyugmena dhyānapūrvaṃ yajeccatau |  
mā&ṣayācādi saṃyuktaṃ vahnimāyedu saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
paramasvāmini prāṃte paramākāśa śunya ca |  
vāhinī caṃdrapādāṃte sūryāgni bhakṣiṇīti ca ||  
  
pātraṃ viśaviśa svāhā daśadhā prajapenmanuṃ |  
vāṅmāyā kamalā prāṃte ānaṃdeśvari vidmahe ||  
  
surādevyaidhīmahīti tannorddhanārīśvarīti |  
pracodayāditi japedgāyatrī daśadhā sudhīḥ ||  
  
tataśca bhāvayeddravyaṃ amṛtaṃ raktabhaṃ priye |  
akathādi tripaṃktyā tu harakṣatrayamaṇḍitaṃ ||  
  
pūrvokta yonimudrāyāṃ śivaśaktyostu saṃgame |  
amṛtaṃ ciṃtayeddravyamaṣṭadhā amṛtāṃ japet ||  
  
amṛtāmaṃtraḥ ||  
  
ai& klī& hrau& ju sa ityuktvā amṛte amṛtodbhave |  
amṛteśvarī amṛtavarṣaṇīti padaṃ vadet ||  
  
amṛtaṃ prāvaya yugaṃ svāhāto dravyaśuddhaye |  
amṛteśī manaḥ proktaḥ paṃcatriṃśadbhirakṣaraiḥ ||  
  
dīpinī maṃtro yathā ||  
  
vāgbhavaṃ vījayugmaṃ ca vāgvādinī vāgbhavaṃ |  
klī& klinnekledinīkledaya mahākṣobhayamityapi ||  
  
kuruyugmaṃ kāmavījaṃ sau mokṣaṃ kuru yugmakaṃ |  
prāsādaḥ parāprāsādaḥ saptatriṃśadaśākṣaraḥ ||  
  
dīpinī manurākhyātaḥ dravyaśuddhirvidhīyate ||  
  
atha prakārāṃtaraśodhanaṃ ||  
  
ghaṭaṃ hetuśca dravyeṇa pūrayedityanuvṛattau |  
tatra yaṃtraṃ vilikhyādau yadyat kulasamudbhavaṃ ||  
  
dhyātveṣṭa devatāṃ tatra japedaṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ |  
dhenuyonī viciṃtyātha prasṛtaṃ tadviciṃtayet ||  
  
dṛṣṭvā mṛtamupāttaṃ vai nṛtyaṃti yoginīgaṇāḥ |  
nṛtyaṃti bhairavāḥ sarve nṛtyaṃti bhairavīgaṇāḥ ||  
  
yadyatkula samudbhūtaṃ tattadyaṃtreṣu pūjayet |  
evaṃ dhyātvā japedvidyā dvayaṃ ca sādhakottamaḥ ||  
  
māyālakṣmī dvayasyāṃte namo bhagavatīti ca |  
maheśvarī svarūpāṃte sarve paśujaneti ca ||  
  
p. 116a)  
  
manaścakṣu tiraskāraṃ kuru dvaṃdvaṃ ca ṭhadvayaṃ |  
tathānya tiraskariṇī lajjāṃ kāmeśvarīṃ tataḥ ||  
  
vāṇīglau tiraskaraṇaṃ sakalajaneti vai tataḥ |  
vāgvādinīti sakala paśu vratajaneti ca ||  
  
manaścakṣu śotra jihvāghrāṇokṣi tiraskaraṇaṃ |  
kuru dvayaṃ ṭhadvayañca sa visargaṃ śiro manuḥ ||  
  
tasyopari svamūlaṃ ca varuṇaṃ saptadhā japet |  
ityanena vidhānena dravyaśuddhiṃ samācaret ||  
  
atha māṃsaśuddhiḥ ||  
  
pretaviṣṇuriti maṃtraṃ sāṃ sa śuddhau niyojayet |  
tryamvakasya tu maṃtreṇa matsya śuddhiṃ samācaret ||  
  
tadviṣṇoriti maṃtreṇa tadviprāso munā tathā |  
mudrāṃ tu śodhayenmaṃtrī devatā prītikārakaṃ ||   
  
viṣṇuryoni manuṃmaṃtraṃ garbhaṃ dhehīti vai tathā |  
kuṇḍagolotthayoḥ śuddhau sādhako viniyojayet ||  
  
māṃsaśuddhiṃ tataḥ kuryāt tena siddhimupālabhet ||  
  
oṃ pratadviṣṇustavatevīryeṇa mṛgo na bhīmaḥ kucarogavighnāḥ ||  
yasyoruṣu triṣu vikramaṇe śuddhi bhavaṃti bhuvanāni viśvā ||  
  
anena manunāmaṃtrī tridhā māṃsaṃ viśodhayet ||  
  
atha matsyaśuddhiḥ ||  
  
oṃ tryaṃvakaṃ yajāmahe sugaṃdhiṃ puṣṭivarddhanaṃ   
ūrvārukamivavaṃdhanānmṛtyormukṣīyamāmṛtāt ||  
  
matsyaśuddhi manenaiva trivāraṃ sādhakaścaret |  
  
atha mdrāśuddhiḥ ||  
  
oṃ tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ sadāpaśyaṃti sūrayaḥ  
divīvacakṣurātataṃ tadviprāso vipannavo jāgṛvāṃsaḥ samiṃdhate ||  
  
viṣṇoryatparamaṃ padaṃ ||  
  
mudrāṇāṃ śodhanaṃ kāryā trivāraṃ manunāmunā ||  
  
atha kuladravyaśodhanam ||  
  
svayaṃbhu kusumādīnāṃ śodhane manu ucyate ||  
  
oṃ viṣṇuryoniṃ kalpayaṃtaḥ tvaṣṭrā rūpāṇipiṃśa tu ||  
  
āsiṃca tu prajāpatirddhātā garbhaṃ dadhātu te |  
grabhaṃdhehisinīvāli garbhaṃdhehi sarasvatī ||  
  
garbhaṃ dhehyaśvinaudevāvādhattāṃ puṣkarasrajau |  
tāraṃ kūrcāstramuddhṛtya śivādi trayaviṃduyuk ||  
  
vahnijāyā ramāmāyā śrīvījaṃ suratapriye |  
tāramāyāramāstraṃ ca vahnijāyāṃ catuṃdiraṃ ||  
  
tato mṛtodbhavāye amṛtavarṣiṇī tatparaṃ |  
priye devi padaṃ yuktaṃ śāpamocaya yugmakaṃ ||  
  
amṛtaṃ ca śrāvayadvaṃdvamamṛtaṃ kuru yugmakaṃ |  
vahnijāyāṃta maṃtreṇa śukraśuddhiṃ samācaret ||  
  
p. 116b)  
  
glū& mlū& plū& nlū& klū& svāhā |  
  
amṛte amṛtodbhave ||  
  
amṛtavarṣiṇi amṛtaṃ śrāvaya śrāvaya svāhā ||  
  
trivṛtyā puṣpaśuddhiṃ ca kārayet sādhakothavā ||  
  
iti vajra puṣpaśodhanaṃ ||  
  
saveṣāṃ śodhane mūlaṃ saptavāraṃ japenmanuṃ |  
anenaiva vidhānena kuryāt paṃcamaśodhanaṃ ||  
  
asādhyaṃ sādhayet sarvaṃ saṃpūjya paradevatām ||  
  
atha pātrāsādanaṃ ||  
  
śrīpātraghaṭayormadhye sarvapātrāṇi sthāpayet |  
ghaṭāte śrīguroḥ pātraṃ bhogapātraṃtadaṃtike ||  
  
tadaṃte śaktipātraṃ ca yogināṃ tadaṃtike |  
tadaṃte vīrapātraṃ ca valeḥ pātraṃ tadaṃtike ||  
  
pādyamācamanīyaṃ ca argheṇa navamaṃ viduḥ |  
uttamaṃ navapātrāṇi saptapātrāṇi madhyamaṃ ||  
  
kecidvadaṃti maṃtrajñā paṃcapātrāṇi madhyaṃ |  
adhamaṃtrīṇi pātrāṇi pātrayugmaṃ tathaiva ca ||  
  
ekapātraṃ na kurvīta yadi sākṣāt kuleśvaraḥ |  
matrāḥ parāṅmukhāyāṃti kruddhā bhavati suṃdarī ||  
  
ihaloke ca dāridryaṃ mṛte ca narakaṃ vrajet |  
śrīgurorbhogapātrāṇi triṣu pātreṣvayaṃvidhiḥ ||  
  
pūjāpātraṃ valeḥ pātraṃ paṃcapātreṣvayaṃvidhiḥ |  
śaktipātraṃ vīrapātraṃ saptapātreṣvayaṃvidhiḥ ||  
  
pādyamānīyaṃ ca navapātreṣṭhayaṃ vidhiḥ |  
pūjāpātraṃ ca vijñeyaṃ yoginīnāṃ ca pūjayet ||  
  
pādyamācamanīyaṃ ca valipātrāt pradāpayet |  
pādyādīni ca sarvāṇi bhogapātrāt pradāpayet ||  
  
pātradvaye maheśāni nirṇayaṃ yatnataḥ śṛṇu |  
bhogapātraṃ śaktipātraṃ vīrapātraṃ ca yoginīṃ ||  
  
valipātraṃ guroḥpātraṃ śrīpātreṇa prakalpayet |  
sāmānyārghyaṃ ca śrīpātramekamavyanmaheśvarī ||  
  
sāmānyārghyeṇa deveśi dravyāṇāṃ prokṣaṇaṃ bhavet |  
śrīpātrena ca pūjā syāt sarvavijñāpitaṃ śivaṃ ||  
  
sāmānyārghye ca dvārārghye viśeṣe tu viśeṣatā |  
sāmānyārghyaṃ tu sāmānyāṃ śrīpātramekameva vā ||  
  
tathāpi devadeveśi ghaṭapātrepyavaśyake |  
kapālaṃ yadi deveśi tadaikapātraṃ mācaret ||  
  
anyatraikaikapātratvaṃ kapāle sarvapātratā |  
kapālapālapātre deveśi kāpālī siddhirasti ca ||  
  
p. 117a)  
  
yadyadvāṃchati kāmāni guṭikāṃjana siddhayaḥ |  
siddhadravyaṃ kāmagatiṃ manorathamayīkalāṃ ||  
  
vāṃchā bhogānnavyamṛṣṭikaraṇaṃ caiva dṛśyatā |  
ciṃtāmaṇiṃ kālamatāṃ yatpātre sarvameva ca ||  
  
kāpālini turyasiddhiḥ kapālasiddhigocarā |  
ekapātraṃ samānīya khaṃḍatritayabhedataḥ ||  
  
atha mānamāhā ||  
  
caturaṃgulamucchrāya māyāme dvādaśāṃgulaṃ |  
aṣṭāṃgulaṃ sa viṣtāridroṇagrāhi jalaṃ yathā ||  
  
tathā pātraṃ pūrṇadīkṣā sūryārghyādau prakīrtitaṃ |  
viśeṣārghyaṃ maheśāni mānasasya parkīrtitaṃ ||  
  
ṣaḍaṃgulaṃ ca vistīrṇaṃ muttānena samākṛti |  
atha vā devadeveśi pātraṃ ca vartulī kṛtaṃ ||  
  
aśvattha patrākāraṃ vā kutayākārameva vā |  
trikoṇākārapātraṃ ca tristriyoni samanvitaṃ ||  
  
madhye viṃduyutaṃ pātraṃ dhvajacihna samanvitaṃ |  
atha vā tu bhagākāraṃ dhvajaviṃduḥ sa keśaraṃ ||  
  
evaṃ pātraṃ samānīya mahācīneśvarīṃ yajet ||  
  
atha pātramāha ||  
  
nārikela svarṇatāmrakā ca śaktiḥ śilodbhavaṃ |  
śaṃkhasaddārukurmotthaṃ kapālājāṃ ca mṛṇmayaṃ ||  
  
uttamaṃ madhyamaṃ hīnaṃ viprādīnāṃ prakīrtitaṃ |  
nāti sthūlaṃ nāti sūkṣmaṃ chinnaṃ vivarjayet ||  
  
tāmrakāṃśyādibhirlohaiḥ pātraṃ naiva tu kārayet |  
sarvasiddhiḥ savarṇesyādudyamastālapātrataḥ ||  
  
śāṃtiḥ śilāyāṃ staṃbhastu mṛṇmayaṃ nārikelaje |  
vaśyādyaṃ kūrmaje jñānaṃ bhuktimukti pradāyinī ||  
  
puṇyavṛkṣajapātraṃ tu pāpaghnaṃ mṛtyunāśakṛt |  
kapāle vīrasaṃsiddhiralāvau yogasiddhayaḥ ||  
  
kāṃsyasyāpyatha rūpyasya śaive śaṃkhacarī harau |  
mahāśaṃkho vāmamārge sphāṭikaṃ grahanāyake ||  
  
viśvāmitre kapālaṃ tu sarvapātrottamottamaṃ |  
brahmahatyādi pāpāni tathā viśvāsaghātakaṃ ||  
  
dṛṣṭvāpātraṃ nārikelaṃ sarvameva praṇaśyati |  
kanyākoṭi pradānāni tathā hema śatāni ca ||  
  
yo dadāti maheśāni rāhudyaste divākare |  
tat phalaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ nārikelārghyapātrataḥ ||  
  
alābhe tasya pātrasya anyapātreṇa pūjayet ||  
  
idamapi mahāśaṃkhetaraparaṃ ||  
  
tathā ca ||  
  
mahāśaṃkhamayaṃ pātraṃ jñeyaṃ sarvottamottamaṃ |  
nārikelābhidhaṃ devi jñeyaṃ cottama madhyamaṃ ||  
  
raktapātraṃ tu suśroṇi jñeyaṃ cottamakalpakaṃ ||  
  
atha mahāpātrādānamāha ||  
  
p. 117b)  
  
ādau muṇḍavidhānaṃ ca proktaṃ tat kathyate śṛṇu |  
sarvamuṇḍe vidhirayaṃ śūlā protādike śṛṇuṃ ||  
  
taruṇaṃ suṃdaraṃ śūraṃ saṃmukhe raṇavartitaṃ |  
parāyaṇa viśūnyaṃ ca kakārāṣṭakavarjitaṃ ||  
  
yaṣṭi prabhṛtyastra viddhaṃ yadāśūlena pātitaṃ |  
cāṇḍālādyabhibhūtaṃ ca śīghraṃ siddhipradāyakaṃ ||  
  
śanibhaumādine vāpi śarīre mṛtasaṃbhave |  
kālarātryāṃ vīrarātryāṃ moharātryāmathāṃvike ||  
  
mahārātryāṃ caturdaśyāmaṣṭamyāṃ pakṣayugmake |  
dīpotsava caturdaśyāṃ grahaṇe saṃkramepi vā ||  
  
vīraveṣaṃ samāsādyaṃ muktakeśo digaṃvaraḥ |  
siṃdūra kūrcatilako surāsaṃvitpradāyakaḥ ||  
  
gatvā śūlasthale devi sarvadravya samanvitaḥ |  
tāṃvūlaṃ vijayā khaḍgaṃ siṃdūraṃ vijayāṃ tathā ||  
  
pāṣāṇamāṃsamadyādi kāraṇādīdhi pārvatī |  
sāmagrīṃ sa kalāṃ kṛtvā sthale gehe viśodhya ca ||  
  
kṛtvā yatnena deveśi śivā pūjāpurassaraṃ |  
śivāmabhyarcya yatnena tato śūraṃ prapūjayet ||  
  
śūlaṃ saṃpūjayeddevi samādānaṃ tataścaret |  
śūlarāja mahākrūra sarvabhūtapriyaṃkaraḥ ||  
  
siddhiṃ saṃkalpitāṃ devi vajraśūla namostute |  
kṛtvā vai jāgṛyādvīraṃ tadaṃte khaḍgapūjanaṃ ||  
  
tacchūlasthaṃ śavaṃ pūjyaṃ dhūpadīpopacārakaiḥ |  
tāṃvūlailālavaṃgādi karpūrāgurusaṃyutaiḥ ||  
  
dravyaiḥ saṃpūjya deveśi khaḍgaṃ pūjya prayatnataḥ |  
kālī khaḍga samudbhūta sarvasiddhi pradāyakaḥ ||  
  
kaviciṃtāmaṇitvaṃ ca khaḍgamuṇḍanamostute |  
vīravīra mahāvīraḥ ṣaṣṭhisiddhiḥ pradarśakaḥ ||  
  
kavikalpalatātvaṃ ca prasanno bhavasatvaraṃ |  
anena mūlamaṃtreṇa prārthyakartanamācaret ||  
  
svayaṃ ca kartayedvīyaṃ brahmāṇḍa valimarpayet |  
paṃcagavyena militaṃ muṇḍamācchādya vā haret ||  
  
gṛhevānīya deveśi hastārddhamānatasthale |  
sarvāḥ sāmagrī kṛtvādau muṇḍaprāṇān pratiṣṭhayet ||  
  
khādirādīn kīlakāṃstaddaśadikṣu nikhātayet |  
tatra sthitvā valiṃ datvā japapūjāparāyaṇaḥ ||   
  
p. 118a)  
  
staddarśanādghoramaṃtrau yathā pāśupatādi ca |  
jayadurgā maheśāni vīrārdanamanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
etairanyaistrayodaśabhiḥsthāna sādhanapūrvakaṃ |  
bhūmau saṃsthāpya deveśi yatra nyāsaḥ samāni ca ||  
  
sthāpya sthitvā japaṃ kṛtvā tatra pūjya maheśvarī |  
divārātri krameṇaiva japellakṣadvayaṃ śive ||  
  
homatarpaṇakaṃ devimārjanaṃ dvijabhojanaṃ |  
kṛtvā saṃsādhitaṃ muṇḍaṃ siddhamuṇḍaṃ bhavecchive ||  
  
evaṃ sādhita muṇḍasya phalaṃ siddhyaṣṭakaṃkare |  
saṃsādhikena muṇḍena mālāpātrādikaṃ caret ||  
  
anyathā kurute yastu tasya siddhirna jāyate |  
mālāyaṃtraṃ tathā pātraṃ tadaṃte siddhimuṇḍataḥ ||  
  
kārayed yat tato devi samayācāra tatparaḥ |  
samiddhaḥ siddhidoloke kalikalpadrumo bhavet ||  
  
sarvaśāstrārtha cettāsyānnātra kāryā vicāraṇā |  
sadyaḥ kṛtaṃ trirātraṃsyaṃ saptarātrasthagaṃ tathā ||  
  
trisaptarātra madhyasya tatravādi kramāchṛṇu |  
uttamaṃ madhyamaṃ caiva hyadhamaṃtvadhamādhamaṃ ||  
  
sadyaḥ kṛtyaṃ trayanmuṇḍamuttamaṃ parikīrtitaṃ |  
ṣaḍrātrottaragaṃ muṇḍamadhyamaṃ parikīrtitaṃ ||   
  
trisaptarātramadhyasthaṃ kīrtitaṃ hyadhamādhamaṃ |  
sadyaḥ kṛttaṃ tu yanmuṇḍaṃ sarvakārye prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
trirātramadhyamaṃ muṇḍamālā yaṃtraḥ prakīrtitaṃ |  
ṣaḍrātrottaragaṃ muṇḍaṃ pātre kāryavinirdiśet ||  
  
atha māhāpātralakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
māhāpātrasya deveśi lakṣaṇaṃ śṛṇu sāṃprataṃ |  
gomukhaṃ gajapṛṣṭaṃ ca gajakuṃbhaṃ tathaiva ca ||  
  
kūrmapṛṣṭo kaṭiścaiva śaktipātraṃ tathaiva ca |  
khaṇḍapadmasamākhyātaṃ lakṣaṇānihyataḥ śṛṇu ||  
  
dīrghākāraṃ tathā pṛṣṭhaṃ agre tīkṣṇaṃ prajāyate |  
gomukhaṃ kathitaṃ devi kapālaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
dīrghaṃ samunnataṃ madhye pārśve naiva susaṃsthitaṃ |  
vistīrṇaṃ ca tathā pṛṣṭhe gajāpṛṣṭhā kṛtiṃ tava ||  
  
madhye samunnataṃ yastu kapāla parimaṇḍalaṃ |  
kūrmapṛṣṭa samākāraṃ kūrmapṛṣṭhaṃ taducyate ||  
  
lalāṭāccaulakaṃ yāvadrekhāsaṃdhyuḥ prajāyate |  
ṣaṭkhaṇḍastu bhavedyastu śaktipātraṃ tu tadviduḥ ||  
  
p. 118b)  
  
samapṛṣṭeṣu yacchṛgaṃ vimnaṃ vāpi tathocchritaṃ |  
madhye caiva samākhyātaṃ padmapātraṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
śṛṣiraṃtargate yastu śikhāyāṃ varavarṇinī |  
ekadvitrīṇi catvāri jātayaḥ syurdvijāditaḥ ||  
  
ekachidraṃ bhavedviprodvikṣidraṃ kṣatriyaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
trichidraṃ vaiśyamityuktaścatuśchidraṃ tu śūdrakaṃ ||  
  
chidrāstu cānyajātiśca kapālāni bhavaṃti hi |  
achidraṃ tu tyajeccaiva kapālaṃ parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
caturvarṇaṃ tu yatpātraṃ tadgrāhyaṃ lakṣaṇānvitaṃ |  
anyajātīni pātrāṇi sādhakaiḥ parivarjayet ||  
  
śyāmavarṇa mahāvyādhiḥ kṛṣṇe ca maraṇaṃ bhavet |  
saṃtāpaṃ raktavarṇena miśravarṇena kiṃcana ||  
  
raktavarṇaṃ tu cāgneyaṃ sphaṭikaṃ sarvato bhavet |  
tadgrāhya sādhakaṃ deśabhuktimukti phalapradaṃ ||  
  
go navanīta saṃkāśaṃ snigdhaḥ chāyā tu muktidaṃ |  
śuklavarṇaṃ hi yadukṣyaṃ mumukṣūṇāṃ prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
vartulaṃ strīkapālaṃ syāt dvipuṭaṃ mokṣadāyakaṃ |  
ekapuṭāni śastāni durlabhāni bhavaṃtyapi ||  
  
dvipuṭāni tu grāhyāṇi lakṣaṇaistu yutāni vai |  
ekakhaṇḍaṃ kapālendraṃ durlabhaṃ tridaśairapi ||  
  
tena hastasthite naiva vidyādhara padaṃ labhet |  
dvikhaṇḍaṃ ca trikhaṃḍaṃ ca bhuktimukti prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
catuḥkhaṃḍaṃ ca yatpātraṃ caturvargapradaṃ tu tat |  
paṃcakhaṃḍaṃ ca ṣaṭkhaṃḍaṃ saptakhaṃḍa manukramāt ||  
  
śatakhaṃḍāṃtakaṃ devi bhāgye naiva tu labhyate ||  
  
atha strīpātrasy sthāpanamāha ||  
  
sādhyasādhakayormadhye ṣaṭtriṃśadaṃgulaṃ bhavet |  
dvādaśāṃgulamūrddhaṃ ca adhobhāge tathāṃgulaṃ ||  
  
dvādaśāṃgulamadhyasthaṃ tatra saṃsthāpayedvudhaḥ |  
svārthaṃ ca dvādaśāṃtyaktvā devārthaṃ dvādaśaṃ tyajet ||  
  
dvādaśāṃgula madhyasthaṃ tatracārghyaṃ nidhāpayet ||  
  
atha maṇḍalānāmāvaśyaka pūrvaka lakṣaṇamāha ||  
  
maṇḍalena vinā pūjā viphalāṃ parikīrtitā |  
tasmāt maṇḍalamālikhya vidhivat tatra pūjayet ||  
  
p. 119a)  
  
akhaṃḍa maṃḍalākāraṃ viśvavyāpya vyavasthitam |  
trailokyaṃ maṇḍitaṃ yena maṇḍalaṃ tat sadāśivaṃ ||  
  
udyānaṃ caturasraṃ syāt kāmarūpaṃ tu vartulaṃ |  
jālaṃdharaṃ cārddhacaṃdraṃ pūrṇaṃ pūrṇagirirmataḥ ||  
  
abhyarcyamaṃḍalaṃ paścādādhāraṃ sthāpayet kramāt ||  
  
atha arghyaṃ dravyamāha ||  
  
surayārghya pradānena yoginīnāṃ bhavet priyaḥ |  
mahāyogī bhaveddevī pīṭhaṃ prakṣyālyatairjalaiḥ ||  
  
atha māhāpātraśodhanaṃ ||  
  
pātrāṇāṃ śodhanaṃ devi śṛṇu yatnena sāṃprataṃ |  
iṃdro tadāditaḥ seṃdurmaṃtreṇānena mārjayet ||  
  
dhruvaṃ maṇḍalamaṃtreṇa bhūgṛhaṃ vṛtta vahniyuk |  
kuryāt tatrādhāraśaktiḥ kūrmītaṃ tān prapūjayet ||   
  
vyomāgni śaktisahita sastume taddhruvādikaṃ |  
anena manunādhāraṃ sthāpayet tatra maṃtravit ||  
  
vahnimaṇḍalametasmin pūjayet tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
krodhavījāstra vījābhyāmādhārekṣālitaṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
mahāśaṃkhaṃ mahāmaṃtrī sthāpayet strīṃ paṭhanaṃ tat |  
śikhāṃ dīrghatrayopetāṃ kālī brahmāramāgnyutāṃ ||  
  
dīrghaḥ śacīpatircāyu hṛdayaṃ manmathāṃtikaṃ |  
dīrghatraya samopetaṃ tāriṇī pūrvavat punaḥ ||  
  
śivaṃ dīrghatrayopetaṃ nīlāśabdāttu pūrvavat |  
māyāṃśarāṃtimaṃ śaṃbhu vāmakarṇeṃdu saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
sarvakāmaḥ kālarātrirdīrghākāya padāt tataḥ |  
sarvādhārāya sarvāya sarvodbhavāya śabdataḥ ||  
  
sarvaśuddhimayā yātha sarvāsurapadāt tataḥ |  
rudhirāruṇāya padāchubhrāya surabhājanaṃ ||  
  
āyadevī kapālāya hṛdayāṃto manurmataḥ |  
ebhiścaturbhirmanubhirmahāśaṃkhaṃ prapūjayet ||  
  
tatrāsāralayaṃ maṃtrī maṇḍalaṃ tigmaroviṣaṃ |  
mūlena pūrayettoyaṃ sudhā vudhyā vidhānavat ||  
  
gaṃdhapuṣpākṣatān kṣiptvā trikhaṃḍāṃ darśayet tataḥ |  
pīyūṣa rocito devi maṇḍalaṃ tatra pūjayet ||  
  
vācaśaktirameśakti manusvarasamanvitaṃ |  
mūletattīya bhairavyāṃ krodhavījaṃ samjjvalaṃ ||  
  
p. 119b)  
  
anena manunāmaṃtrī bhāvayedaṣṭamoṣṭataṃ |  
śaktyā sudhāṃ viniḥkṣipyaśaṃkhaṃ yoniṃ pradarśayet ||  
  
viśeṣārghyokta vidhinā sarvameva puroktavat |  
evaṃ yathoktavidhinā kapālaṃ pātramuttamaṃ ||  
  
anena pātravaryeṇa sādhayediṣṭa sādhanaṃ |  
vāṃchā siddhiṃ khecarīṃ ca parakāya praveśanaṃ ||  
  
manoratho divyadṛṣṭi vetālagutike tathā |  
rasaṃ rasāyanaṃ caiva sādhayediṣṭa sādhanaṃ ||  
  
vāparṇa vījasaṃdi pādukā yakṣiṇīgaṇaṃ |  
khaḍgasiddhiḥ kuṃtasiddhiṃ pāśaṃ vā janameva ca ||  
  
sṛṣṭisiddhirbhairavāṣṭa mahākapālinī śive |  
kapālārghyeṇa deveśi sarvāḥ siddhyaṃti niścitaṃ ||  
  
athārghya sthāpanaṃ ||  
  
tatorghyaṃ sthāpayenmaṃtrī svavāme surasuṃdarī |  
kalaśāddakṣiṇe bhāge trikoṇaṃ vṛttasaṃyutaṃ ||  
  
ṣaṭkoṇaṃ caturasraṃ ca kṛtvā tanmadhyabhāgataḥ |  
vilasaccaṃdra sakalaṃ gaṃdharvaṃ ca samālikhet ||  
  
ojāpūpādikaṃ pīṭhaṃ taccaturdikṣu pūjayet |  
aṃgamaṃtraiśca ṣaṭkoṇe śaktau mūla tribhedataḥ ||  
  
ādhāraśaktiṃ saṃpūjya pūrvavadyaṃ trikāmapi |  
mahāśaṃkhaṃ nārikelaṃ sauvarṇaṃ rājaṃtaṃ tathā ||  
  
tāmraṃ śaktyudbhavaṃ vāpi pātraṃ tatra nidhāpayet |  
samarcya pūrvayanmaṃtrī kuṃbhadravyeṇa pūrayet ||  
  
ādhāraṃ trividhaṃ prāhuḥ ṣaṭpadaṃ vā catuṣpadaṃ |  
atha vā vartulākāraṃ kuryāddevi manoharaṃ ||  
  
padmābhaṃ vā trikoṇaṃ vā yonyābhaṃ dhātujaṃtutaḥ |  
ādhāreṇa vinābhraṃśo na hi tuṣyaṃti devatāḥ ||  
  
tasmādvidhivadādhāraṃ kalpayet kulanāyike |  
dikṣu cāstraṃ samabhyarcya śaṃkhādhāraṃ pravinyaset |  
  
mūlena kṣālitaṃ śaṃkhādhāraṃ saṃsthāpyayāmi ca |  
kālaṃ sa viṃḍukaṃ tadvadbhujaṃ śeśaṃ samuddharet ||  
  
vahnyaṃte maṇḍalāyeti tathā dharmapradeti ca |  
daśakalātmane coktvā namo gaṃdhādibhiryajet ||   
  
śastreṇakṣālitaṃ śaṃkhaṃ tatrasaṃsthāpya pūjayet |  
arghamānaṃ tu prādeśaṃ caturaṃgulamucchritaṃ ||  
  
p. 120a)  
  
arghapātramiti proktaṃ sthāpayāmīti maṃtrataḥ |  
amarkamaṇḍalāyeti vadedvādaśa ityatha ||  
  
kalātmane padaścoktvā arghapātraya hṛnmanuḥ |  
anena śaṃkhamabhyarcyakalāḥ sūryasya pūjayet ||  
  
samarcya pūrvavanmaṃtrī śaṃkhaṃ dravyeṇa pūrayet |  
saṃspṛṣṭvārcanapātraṃ tu pūjayeddhetu mudrayā ||   
  
brahmāṇḍakhaṇḍasaṃbhūtamaśeṣa rasamaṃmitaṃ |  
āpūritaṃ mahāpātraṃ pīyūṣarasamāvahet ||  
  
japan vilomato varṇān mūlamaṃtraḥ samujjvalān |  
saṃpūjya pūrvavat tatra vṛttaṃ ṣaṭkoṇamālikhet ||  
  
akathādi trirekhāṃtaṃ trikoṇaṃ vṛttamadhyataḥ |  
mūlakhaṇḍatrayeṇātha trikoṇaṃ paripūjayet ||  
  
ṣaṭkoṇe ca ṣaḍaṃgāni tatastīrthamayaṃ smaret |  
ānaṃdabhairavaṃ dhyātvā samabhyarcya vidhānataḥ ||  
  
pūjayet paṃcaratnāni kuladravyāṇi niḥkṣipet |  
tatra māṣa pramāṇaṃ tu māṃsamatsyādi niḥkṣipet ||  
  
kulāmṛtaṃ samādāya tatrārghe niḥkṣipedbudhaḥ |  
tataḥ somakalāḥ pūjyā sādhakairnirmalāśayaiḥ ||  
  
racayet pūrvavaccheṣamayamarghavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |  
kulāmṛtā tadānaṃ tu dutaṃ yajane vakṣyāmaḥ ||  
  
bhauvaneśīramarāmā kāmā yoginyanaṃtaraṃ |  
śākinī ca kramāt saptavījāni sthairyabhāṃji hi ||  
  
aṣṭamaṃ tu parijñeyaṃ vījaṃ tribhuvaneśvarī |  
tattallokādimo varṇohyavatṣu pariviṣṭitaḥ ||  
  
gamanaṃ svargamartyau ca pātālaṃ nāga eva ca |  
vigṛhyarala śabdena ṅeṃtena kila hṛtkṣuṣā ||  
  
dhūmrārciruṣmājvalinī jvālinī visphuliṃginī |  
saḥ śrīḥsarūpā kapilāhavyakavya vahetyapi ||  
  
āgneyyāyādi varṇādyā daśadharma pradāḥ kalāḥ |  
tapinī tāpinī dhūmrāmarīci jvālinī ruciḥ ||  
  
suṣumṇā bhogadā viśvāvodhinī dhāriṇī kṣamāḥ |  
kalādyāḥ vasudāḥ saudāḥ phaḍaṃtā dvādaśeritā ||  
  
amṛtāmānadā pūṣā tuṣṭipuṣṭiratirddhṛtiḥ |  
śaśinī caṃdrikā kāṃti jyotsnā śrīḥprītiraṃgadā ||  
  
p. 120b)  
  
pūrṇā pūrṇāmṛtā ceti kathitāḥ kulavāpike |  
saumyāḥ kāmapradāyinyaḥ ṣoḍaśasvarajāḥ kalāḥ ||  
  
prāgvattīrthaṃ samāvāhya tīrthamaṃtreṇa tatra ca |  
saṃyojya netramaṃtreṇa puṣpanyasya śikhāmunā ||  
  
pradarśyagālinī mudrāṃ mudrayā dhenu saṃjñayā |  
amṛtīkṛtya vidhivat sudhāvīje ca sādhakaḥ ||  
  
dhyātveṣṭa devatāṃ tatra sakalī kṛtya sādhakaḥ |  
aṃganyāsasya cāstreṇa kalayecca diśodaśaṃ ||  
  
netramaṃtreṇa saṃvīkṣya mudrayā śaṃkha saṃjñayā |  
gaṃdhapuṣpāṃdibhistatra pūjayediṣṭadevatāṃ ||  
  
ṣaḍaṃgāni ca saṃpūjya maṃtrayen mūlamaṃtrataḥ |  
abhicāreṣu kāryeṣu vilomena japediti ||  
  
aṣṭakṛtva tathā cārghyaṃ chādayen matsyarūpiṇī |  
kaniṣṭhāṃguṣṭhakau yuktaṃ karayoritaretaraṃ ||  
  
tarjanīmadhyamābhyāṃ ca saṃhatābhugnavarjitāḥ |  
mudraiṣāgālinī proktā śaṃkhasyo paricālitā ||  
  
kalaśokta vidhānena sthāpayet pātrasaṃtatiṃ |  
puṣpādinā samuddhṛtya viṃduṃśaṃkhāmṛtasya ca ||  
  
niḥkṣipet sarvapātreṣu sarvaṃ divyaviciṃtayet |  
ekaṃ pātrāṇi saṃsthāpya te naiva tarpaṇaṃ caret ||  
  
atrādau śarīrasthaṃ devatarpaṇaṃ ||  
  
śuddhe dravyeṇa tenāpi gaṃdhapuṣpākṣaṃtairapi |  
nyāsokta sarvamaṃtraiśca svātmānaṃ plāvayet tathā ||  
  
mūrddhni śrīgurupaktiṃ ca mūlādhāre tu pādukāṃ |  
divyaughaṃ tarpayedādau ādināthaḥ sadāśivaḥ ||  
  
īśvaro rudraviṣṇuśca brahmāpatnīyutāstime |  
bhavaṃti dvādaśa ca te siddhau ghaṇṭhān pratarpayet ||  
  
sanakādyāśca catvāraḥ su jātaścārubhūṣitaḥ |  
sanatkumāro vyāsaśca vāmadevaḥ sakastathā ||  
  
dattātreyo raivatako dvādaśaitetha mānavān |  
tarpayet ṣaṭ nṛsiṃhaṃ ca maheśaṃ bhāskaraṃ tathā ||  
  
maheṃdraṃ mādhavaṃ viṣṇuṃ nāmāṃte tu prayojayet |  
mahāśivaṃ ca siddhaughe mānavaughe sadāśivaṃ ||  
  
śivaṃ tu paramaṃ divyaṃ pīṭhapūjāṃ tataścaret ||  
  
ete kaula vāmayoḥ sāmānya guravaḥ ||  
  
brahmaraṃdhre svakemaṃtrī mudrayā tatvasaṃjñayā |  
tarpayed gurupātrīya dravyeṇaugha trayaṃ sudhīḥ ||  
  
p. 121a)  
  
svagurūnapi saṃtarpya trissakṛdvā viśeṣataḥ |  
ātmano hṛdayāṃbhoje parigaṇāvṛtāṃ ||  
  
devī pātrāmṛtenāpi tarpayet kulanāyikāṃ |  
śuddhidravyaṃ samādāya tarpaṇaṃ tatvamudrayā ||  
  
aṃguṣṭha tarjanīmadhye śuddhiṃ saṃgṛhya vāmataḥ |  
vāmena dakṣiṇe vāpi devīṃ saṃtarpayet sudhīḥ ||  
  
atha tatvaśuddhiṃ kuryāt ||  
  
oṃ prāṇāyānavyānodāna samānāse śuddhyaṃtāṃ jyotirahaṃ virajāmi vipāpmā   
bhūyā saṃsvāhā ||  
  
oṃ pṛthivyaptejā vāyvākāśāni me śuddhyaṃtāṃ jyoti ||  
  
oṃ prakṛtya haṃkāra vuddhimanaḥ śrotrāṇi me śuddhyaṃtāṃ ||  
  
oṃ tvak cakṣuḥ śrotrajihvāghrāṇavacāṃsi me śuddhyaṃtāṃ ||  
  
oṃ pāṇipādapādyūpastha śabdā me śuddhyaṃtāṃ ||  
  
oṃ sparśarūparasagaṃdhākāśāni me śuddhyaṃtāṃ ||  
  
oṃ vāyustejaḥ salilabhūmyātmāno me śuddhyaṃtāṃ ||  
  
saptamaṃ trān parāmṛṣya hastābhyāṃ saptadhā punaḥ ||  
sarvāṃgaṃ saṃspṛśenmaṃtrī tatvaśuddhiriyaṃ matā ||  
  
atha vaṭukādi validānaṃ ||  
  
avaśyamādau vāmādau kuryād vaṭukapūjanaṃ |  
mārgesmin vaṭuko mukhyaḥ surādyaṃtenarmitā ||  
  
vinā taṃtu na gṛhnaṃti devāstasmāttadarcanaṃ |  
apūjya vaṭukaṃ yaṃ tu mohāddevaṃ prapūjayet ||  
  
tasya pūjāphalaṃ nāsti vaṭukaśca kupyati |  
sa gaṇaṃ pūjayet tasmādgaṃdhapuṣpā savāmiṣaiḥ ||  
  
tat tanmaṃtrairvidhānena devatā prītimāpnuyāt |  
īśāna vahni nair-ṛtya vāyukoṇeṣu pūrvavat ||  
  
maṇḍalāni vidhāyātha pūrvavat pūjayet priye |  
pūrvavad validānaśca dadyāt sarvasamṛddhaye ||  
  
vaṭukāya maheśāni yoginībhyaśca vallabhe |  
gaṇeśakṣetrapālābhyāṃ pūrvavadvalimutsṛjet ||  
  
dakṣiṇe vaṭuke dadyāduttare yoginī valiṃ |  
sarvabhūta valiṃ dadyāt kṣetrapālāya paścime ||  
  
aṃguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ tu vaṭukāya valirmataḥ |  
kaniṣṭhāṃguṣṭha yogena yoginī valimāharet ||  
  
p. 121b)  
  
aṃguṣṭhā tarjanībhyāṃ ca kṣetrapāla valiṃ haret |  
tāratrayaṃ tato devī putroktvā vaṭuketi ca ||  
  
nātheti kapilajaṭābhārabhāsvarapiṃgala |  
trinetrāgnirjvālāmukha imāṃ pūjāṃ valiṃ vadet ||  
  
gṛhna gṛhna hū& phaṭ svāhā ||  
  
ṣaṭ catvāriṃśaddarśakaḥ ||  
  
maṃtramevaṃ samuccārya tataḥ ślokapaṭhedidaṃ |  
validānena saṃtuṣṭo vaṭukaḥ sarvasiddhidaḥ ||  
  
śāṃtiṃ karotu me nityaṃ bhūtavetālasevitaḥ |  
tāratrayaṃ sarvapūrvettyaḥ saṃtāni vadet kramāt ||  
  
yoginī būtabhūtādhipatītha ca ḍākinī ||  
  
śākinī trailokyavāsinī imāṃ pūjāṃ valiṃ gṛhna gṛhna hū& phaṭ tathā   
svāhā |  
ekapaṃcāśadakṣaraḥ yākācidyoginī raudrā saumyā ghoratarāparā ||  
  
khecarī bhūcarī vyomacārī prītistu me sadā ||  
  
ūrddhvaṃ brahmāṇḍatoyādi gaganatale bhūtale niṣkale pātāle vā'nale vā   
salilapavanayoryatra tatra sthito vā |  
kṣetre pīṭhopapīṭhādiṣu ca kṛtapadāḥ puṣpadhūpādike na prītā devyassadānaḥ   
śubhavali vidhināyāṃ tu deveṃdratulyāḥ ||  
  
etadaṃte maheśāni yāṃ vījaṃ yoginī tataḥ |  
bhyaḥ svāhā sarvavarṇāṃte yogināṃ padamālikhet ||  
  
kavacaṃ cāstramālikhya vahnijāyāṃ punarlikhet |  
anunamanunādevī yoginī valimāharet ||  
  
tālatrayaṃ tathaihye hi devīputra vaṭūkanā |  
thocchiṣṭahāriṇe hū& hū& phaṃ hū& vāṃ radvayaṃ vadet ||  
  
kṣetrapāleti sarveti vighnānnāśaya yugmakaṃ |  
sarvopacāraḥ sahitāmimāṃ pūjāvaliṃ dadet ||  
  
gṛhnagṛhna hūṃ phaṭ svāhā catuḥṣaṣṭhyakṣaro manuḥ |  
kṣetrapālasya saṃproktaḥ sarvasiddhipradāyakaḥ ||  
  
yasmin kṣatranivāsī ca kṣatrapālasya kiṃkaraḥ |  
prītoyaṃ validānena sarvarakṣāṃ karotu me ||  
  
anena manunā devī kṣetrapāla valiṃ haret ||  
  
gā& gī& gū& trayamālikhya ṅentaṃ gaṇapatiṃ vadet |  
varāṃte varadāṃte ca sarvāṃte janamālikhet ||  
  
p. 122a)  
  
mevaśaṃ cānayet yuktvā valiṃ gṛhna dvidhāpadaṃ |  
vahnijāyānvito maṃtrogaṇapasya valiṃ haret ||  
  
vāmabhāge kṛtasyātha maṇḍalasyo parikṣipet |  
ādhāraṃ pūjayet tatra pātraṃ cānnodakānvitaṃ ||  
  
svakāraṇaṃ maṃtrayitvā sarvabhūta valiṃ haret |
