ṣoḍaśārṇena manunā trivāraṃ vīravaṃdite ||  
  
tāraṃ ca bhuvaneśāni sarvavighna padaṃ tataḥ |  
kṛdbhyaśca sarvabhūtebhyo hūṃkāraṃ vahnivallabhāṃ ||  
  
samuccaran valiṃ dadyān mudrayā tatva saṃjñayā |  
tātratrayaṃ vadet sarvabhūtebhyaḥ sarva eva ca ||  
  
paṃcādbhūtapatibhyo hṛduḥ saptadaśākṣaraḥ |  
bhūtā ye vividhākārā divyabhaumāṃtarīkṣagāḥ ||  
  
pātātala saṃsthāśca śivayogena bhāṣitāḥ |  
dhruvādyāḥ satyasaṃdhāśu iṃdrādyāśca vyavasthitāḥ ||  
  
tṛpyaṃtu pretamānaso bhūtā gṛhnaṃ tvimaṃ valiṃ ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau kaulavāmayoḥ sāmānyanityārcanāyāṃ   
tanmārgotpattipūrvaka śrīpātrādisthāpanāṃtanirṇayo nāmāṣṭādaśaḥ   
prakāśaḥ || 18 ||  
atha pūjāmāha ||  
  
paśuvīradivyabhedāt pūjāsthānaṃ tridhā mataṃ |  
gauṇaṃ mukhyaṃ cottamaṃ ca tadidānīṃ nigadyate ||  
  
paśūnāṃ kalpite yaṃtre pūjāgauṇī prakīrtitāṃ |  
vīrāṇāṃ likhite yaṃtre viṃdau śakteśca sthāpanaṃ ||  
  
sveṣṭarūpāṃvatāṃ dhyātvā pūjanāt mukhyatāṃ gatā |  
divyānāṃ divyacakre tu pūjanaṃ cottamaṃ mataṃ ||  
  
jīva cakre maheśāni prasannāsti niraṃtaraṃ |  
jīvacakrasya vijñānī kalau durlabha eva ca ||  
  
vālukāyā bhavettailaṃ vaṃdhyāputraṃ prasūyate |  
khepuṣpamapi jāyaṃte ayonirmanujo pivā ||  
  
jīvackrasya vijñānī kalau kvāpi na bhairavet |  
agrasthānaṃ parityajya bhikṣāmaṭatidurmatiḥ ||  
  
tathā jīvaṃ parityajya paridhāvati dhāvati |  
aho jīvasya vijñānī śivatulyo naro bhavet ||  
  
kalpite vā mahādevī sāṃgāṃ sāvaraṇāṃ yajet |  
saṃpūjya pīṭhapūjāṃtaṃ tasmin siṃhāsanetha vā ||  
  
abhedavudhyā deveśi akṣatāṃ sthāpya pūjayet |  
pīṭhapūjā samācārya paṃcopacāratorcayet ||  
  
p. 122b)  
  
pūjya siṃhāsane sthāpya sudhāsiṃdhau samarcayet |  
tatpīṭhaṃ tu bhavedekaṃ sarvāsāṃ pīṭhamuttamaṃ ||  
  
mukhyaṃ tu devadeveśi yaṃtre pīṭhaṃ samarcayet |  
tadyaṃtraṃ siṃhapīṭhe tu sa pīṭhāṃ sthāpayecchive ||  
  
sā pīṭhā tatra deveśi bhavedā vṛttidevatā |  
pīṭhā vṛttiśca vā kāryā sarveṣāmatamīritaṃ ||  
  
tatra pīṭhe mahāyaṃtraṃ sveṣṭa devātmakaṃ mahat |  
jīvacakretha vā yaṃtraṃ bhāvyaṃ likhyaṃ maheśvarī ||  
  
eteṣāmabhāve pūjāsthānamāha ||  
  
liṃgesthaṃtrilavahyostu phalake mūrddhni maṇḍale |  
mūrtau kuḍye ca hṛdaye pūjā daśa su kīrtitā ||  
  
arūpaṃ rūpiṇaṃ kṛtvā karmakāṃḍaratājanāḥ |  
gavāṃ sarvāṃ gajaṃ kṣīraṃ prasavet stanmukhādyathā ||  
  
tathā sarvamato devaḥ pratimādau virājite |  
ābhimukhyārci viṃvasya pūjāyāśca viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
sādhakasya ca viśvāsāt sānnidhyaṃ devatā labhet |  
gavāṃ sarveśarīrasthaṃ na karotyātmayoṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
sukarma racitaṃ dattaṃ punastāneva poṣayet |  
evaṃ sarvaśarīrasthaḥ sarpicet parameśvaraḥ ||  
  
upāsanā vinā devi na dadāti phalaṃ nṛṇāṃ ||  
  
atha pīṭhapūjā ||  
  
pīṭhapūjā vidhānena pīṭhaṃ saṃpūjayedbudhaḥ ||  
  
tata āvāhayeddevīṃ maṃtrābhyāṃ pūjayet tathā |  
mahāpadmavanāṃtasthe kāraṇānaṃta vigrahe ||  
  
sarvabhūtahite mātarehye hi parameśvarī |  
deveśi bhakti sulabhe sarvāvaraṇa saṃyute ||  
  
yāvattvāṃ pūjayāmīha tāvattvaṃ susthirā bhava |  
dhyātvā mudrāṃ pradarśyātha gaṃdhapuṣpākṣatādibhiḥ ||  
  
cinmayasyā prameyasya nirguṇasyā śarīriṇāḥ |  
sādhakānāṃ hitārthāya brahmaṇorūpakalpanā ||  
  
sakalīkṛtya tatprāṇāṃtadīyānīṃdriyāṇi ca |  
pratiṣṭhāpyārcayeddevānanyathā niḥphalaṃ mataṃ ||  
  
maṃtrahīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ taṃtrahīnaṃ ca yadbhavet |  
yadyat sādhayate sarvaṃ hīnamaṃgaṃ yathā tathā ||  
  
devasya maṃtrarūpasya yaṃtravyāpti sa jānatāṃ |  
kṛtārcanādikaṃ sarvaṃ vyathāṃ bhavati śāṃbhavi ||  
  
ṣoḍaśairupacāraistu sāṃgāṃ sāvaraṇāṃ yajet |  
praṇavādi namoṃ tena tattannāmnāṃ samarcayet ||  
  
atha krameṇa ṣoḍaśopacāramaṃtrāḥ ||  
  
idaṃ tu āsanaṃ dattaṃ mayā suravarārccite |  
bhavaitasminniṣaṇātvaṃ yāvat pūjāṃ karomyahaṃ ||  
  
p. 123a)  
  
pādyagṛhna mahādevi sarvaduḥkhāpahārakaṃ |  
trāyasva varade devi ghorādasmādbhavārṇavāt ||  
  
snāne vastre ca naivedya dadyādā camanīyakaṃ |  
tacca svadhāyadairdadyān madhuparkaṃ tathā priye ||  
  
arghyaṃ svāhā padenaiva sarvamanyantamaḥ yadā |  
dūrvākṣata samāyukte vilvapatra samanvitaṃ ||  
  
śobhanaṃ śaṃkhapātrasthaṃ gṛhāṇārghyaṃ harapriye |  
caṃdrajātī lavaṃgailā kakkola sahitaṃ jalaṃ ||  
  
gṛhāṇā camanīyaṃ tvaṃ mayābhaktyā niveditaṃ |  
madhuparkaṃ maheśāni brahmaṇā parikalpitaṃ ||  
  
mayā niveditaṃ tubhyaṃ gṛhāṇa jagadīśvarī |  
madhuparka pradānāṃte punarācamanīyakaṃ ||  
  
dātavyaṃ prāśanāṃtesya yataducchiṣṭatā bhavet |  
vārīdaṃ himamāmodi prāsastyaṃ madhyameva ca ||  
  
mayā niveditaṃ bhaktyā snāhyanena sureśvarī |  
nānāvarṇa samāyuktaṃ paṭṭasūtrādi nirmitaṃ ||  
  
vāsaḥ śuklaṃ tathā raktaṃ gṛhāṇa tridaśeśvarī |  
dehaśobhākaraṃ pūtaṃ raṃjitaṃ rāgavastubhiḥ ||  
  
paridhatsvajaddhātrī vāso bhaktyā niveditaṃ |  
vāsasaḥ paridhānāṃte punarācamanīyakaṃ ||  
  
dātavyaṃ bhaktibhāvena smṛtyuktatvān manuṣyavat |  
divyaratna samāyuktaṃ vahnibhānu samaprabhaṃ ||  
  
alaṃkārātsvadaṃgāni śobhayaṃ tu sureśvarī |  
alikādhika śobhāyāḥ kārakaṃ nāgasaṃbhavaṃ ||  
  
atirāgi samutyiṃjaṃ siṃdūraṃ parigṛhyatāṃ |  
snigdhamullaṃ hṛdyatamaṃ dṛśāṃ śobhākaraṃ tava ||  
  
gṛhītvā kajjalaṃ sadyo netrāṇyaṃ jayapārvatī |  
tvatpādāṃ bhojana kharadyutikāri manoramaṃ ||  
  
araktakamidaṃ devi mayādattaṃ pragṛhyatāṃ |  
anulepena me tatte mahāsurabhiśītalaṃ ||  
  
mayā niveditaṃ devi gṛhītvā lepayāṃgakaṃ |  
idaṃ kusumamāmodi grāmāraṇya samudbhavaṃ ||  
  
ghrāṇa saṃtarpaṇaṃ hṛdyaṃ mayādattaṃ pragṛhyatāṃ |  
karpūrāgurusaṃmiśrovanaspati rasodbhava ||  
  
mayā nivedito dhūpo devadevi pragṛhyatāṃ |  
tvaṃ sūryaścaṃdrajyotīṣi vidyudagdhnostathaiva ca ||  
  
tvameva jagatāṃ jyotirdīpoyaṃ pratigṛhyatāṃ |  
nānāvidhāni ramyāṇi svādūni rasavaṃti ca ||  
  
mayādattāni gṛhyaṃtaṃ nivedyādi surārcite |  
phalamūlāni sarvāṇi grāmakānajāni hi ||  
  
nānākāra sugaṃdhīni gṛhāṇatvaṃ haripriye |  
caturvidhamidaṃ bhakṣyaṃ devi ṣaḍbhirasaṃyutaṃ ||  
  
sadātṛptakaraṃ ramyaṃmidamannaṃ pragṛhyatāṃ |  
gavyaṃ sarpiḥ payoyuktaṃ nānāmadhuramiśritaṃ ||  
  
p. 123b)  
  
niveditaṃ vedi mayā paramānnaṃ pragṛhyatāṃ |  
amṛtai racitaṃ divyaṃ ghṛtakhaṇḍavinirmitaṃ ||  
  
piṣṭakaṃ vividhaṃ svādu gṛhāṇa haravallabhe |  
modakaṃ svādu ruciraṃ karpūrādibhiranvitaṃ ||  
  
miśraṃ nānāvidhairdravyaiḥ pratigṛhyā śubhujyatāṃ |  
tāmrapātre sthitaṃ sīdhuṃpayogavyamathātra vā ||  
  
nārike rodakaṃ kāṃsye gṛhyaṇa śaṃkara priye |  
pānīyaṃ śītalaṃ svacchaṃ prasannaṃ ghanasārayuk ||  
  
bhojane tṛptikṛddevī kṛpayā parigṛhyatāṃ |  
bhojanāṃte pradātavyaṃ punarācamanīyakaṃ ||  
  
pūrvokte naiva maṃtreṇa sarvatraiva śucismite |  
phalapatraka saṃyuktaṃ karpūrādi suvāsitaṃ ||  
  
mukhakāṃtikaraṃ hṛdyaṃ tāmvūlaṃ pratigṛhyatāṃ ||  
  
athāgamoktamārgeṇa tarpayedali viṃdubhiḥ |  
aṃguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ tu nakhairniḥśabdamutkṣipan ||  
  
tryapātrasyaṃdamuṣṭau ca tarpayeddevatā mukhe |  
sakṛttarpaṇamutsṛjya japtvā mūlaṃ ca pādukāṃ ||  
  
aṃtaḥśakti manusmṛtya tarpayeddeha devatāṃ |  
aṃguṣṭho bhairavasthānaṃ caṇḍikāyāstvanāmikā ||  
  
tasmāttābhyāṃ tarpaṇīyaṃ yatra etat tayoḥ priyaṃ |  
aṃguṣṭha madhyamābhyāṃ ca vaśyakarmaṇi tarpayet ||  
  
tarjanyaṃguṣṭhayogena tarpayedābhicārake |  
kaniṣṭāṃguṣṭhayogena staṃbhakarmaṇi tarpayet ||  
  
evaṃ saṃtarpya devāgre gurupaṃkti prapūjayet ||  
  
karābhyāṃ cinmudrāṃ samudhva nṛkapālaṃ ca dadhatīṃśrita   
svarṇaprakhyātaruṇakusumālepavasanāṃ |  
kṛpāpūrṇāpāṃgī maruṇanayanāvarvarakacāmupetāṃ siddhādyairyajati   
gurupaṃktiḥ kṛtamatiḥ ||  
  
evaṃ svaṃpūjya dhūpaṃ ca dīpaṃ naivedyameva ca |  
āsavaṃ piśitopenaṃ bhakṣyāni vividhāni ca ||  
  
kadalpāni phalānyevaṃ tāṃvūlaṃ ca samarpayet |  
vaṭukādīn samucyaivaṃ kuladīpān pradarśayet ||  
  
īṣat pakvaḥ supiṣṭena kuryādvedāṃgulonnataṃ |  
dīpāṃ ḍamarukākārān trikoṇānati śobhanān ||  
  
karṣāhyagrahiṇaḥ kuryānnavasaptātha paṃca vā |  
aṃtastejo vahisteja ekīkṛtvāmitaḥ prabhān ||  
  
tridhā devyuparibhrāmya kuladīpaṃ nivedayet |  
samastacakra cakreśi yute devi tavāṃtike ||  
  
ārātrikamidaṃ devi gṛhāṇa mamasiddhaye |  
kuladīpān pradarśyātha śaktipūjāṃ samācaret ||  
  
athāśyāvaśyakatāmāha ||  
  
p. 124a)  
  
kaulikāvāpya kaulāvāye caitanmatavartinaḥ |  
teṣā nityā śaktipūjā prāhaivaṃ māṃpuradviṣaḥ ||  
  
kṛtāyāṃ śaktiṃ pūjāyāṃ saphalaṃ nityapūjanaṃ |  
akṛtāyāṃ manuṣyāṃ tu niṣphalaṃ nityapūjanaṃ ||  
  
tasmād yatyena saṃpūjya śaktirnityārcanādanu |  
devīdhiyaiva saṃpūjyā na sāmānya vadhūdhiyā ||  
  
abhyarcya devatā vuddhyā bhogapātraṃ nivedayet |  
tadaṃte kaṇyakāścāpi pramadāśca manoharāḥ ||  
  
saṃpūjya devatā vuddhyā dadyāt pātraṃ pṛthak pṛthak |  
anivedya tu yaḥ śaktyai kuladravyaṃ niṣevate ||  
  
pūjanaṃ niḥphalaṃ tasya devatā na prasīdati |  
maṃtramaṃtra samāyuktā samayācārapālikā ||  
  
kumārī vā vratasthā vā yogamudrādharāpi vā |  
pūjākāle svataḥ prāptā sā pūjyā sahasā vudhaiḥ ||  
  
tatorcanādikaṃ sarvaṃ maṃtrodakapuraḥsaraṃ |  
itaḥ pūrvādi manunāmaṃtrī devyai samarpayet ||  
  
śeṣaṃ dakṣiṇavat kuryāt taducchiṣṭādikaṃ tathā |  
śaktihīnā vṛthā pūjā śivahīnaṃ vṛthārcanaṃ ||  
  
śivaśaktiḥ samāpūjā sā pūjā sarvakāmadā |  
bhaktyābhāve dravyalābhe manaḥ śaktiṃ prapūjayet ||  
  
śeṣikā maṃtrito deyaṃ śeṣikāyai sa kathyate |  
aiṃ hṛducchiṣṭa cāṃḍālini mātaṃgi padaṃ vadet ||  
  
sarvevaśaṃkarī svāhā caika viṃśati varṇakaḥ |  
maṃtreṇānena nirmālyaṃ śeṣikāyai samarpayet ||  
  
devīmucchiṣṭa mātaṃgī dhyāyellokaikamohinīṃ ||  
  
vīṇāvādya vinodgīta niratāṃ nīlāṃśukollāsinīṃ viṃvoṣṭīṃ   
navayāvakārdracaraṇāmākarṇakeśāṃśukāṃ |  
hṛdyāṃgīsitaśaṃkhakuṃdadhavalāṃ māṇikya bhūṣojjvalāṃ mātaṃgīṃ   
praṇatosmisusmitamukhīṃ devīṃ śukaśyāmalāṃ ||  
  
kaulikaiḥ śaktisahitaistaducchiṣṭaṃ ca sevayet |  
svaśaktiṃ vīraśaktiṃ vā dīkṣitāṃ gururūpiṇīṃ ||  
  
pāpayitvā pivenmadhyamiti śāstrasya niścayaḥ |  
tataḥ śrīgururūpāya sākṣāt paraśivātmane ||  
  
karābhyāṃ pātramuddhṛtya sa dvitīyaṃ nivedayet |  
gurorabhāve tatpātraṃ jalamadhye ca niḥkṣipet ||  
  
pūjyaśaktiṃ śaktipātraṃ vīrebhyo vīrapātrakaṃ |  
anyebhyo yoginī pātraṃ svārthe syādbhogapātrakaṃ ||  
  
p. 124b)  
  
kuṇḍalī tarpaṇārthaṃ ca bhogapātraṃ samācaret |  
aṃtaḥśakti manusmṛtya tarpayeddeha devatāṃ ||  
  
atha yena prakāreṇa svīkuryuḥ pātramuttamaṃ |  
tattehaṃ vyāhariṣyāmi yathā rudreṇa bhāṣitaṃ ||  
  
prāṇāyāma vidhāyānu tat tanmaṃtra ṣaḍaṃgakaṃ |  
kurvīta bhaktibhāvena śaktyā vṛkṣādikaṃ tathā ||  
  
tatoghrāya tat tatpātraṃ dakṣahaste niveśayet |  
vāmahastānāmikāyāṃguṣṭhaṃ samabhiyojayet ||  
  
idaṃ hi tarpaṇī mudrā śudrūpā parikīrtitā |  
etayā mudrayā devi saṃhāraḥ kramato khilāt ||  
  
pātrā tu dravyamādāya tarpayeduditakraimaiḥ |  
aṃguṣṭhasyānāmikāyā nakhau yāvat pralimyataḥ ||  
  
vātanniveśanīyā hi mudrā vai kaulikādravaiḥ |  
nimīlya cakṣuṣī dhyāyede tadrūpeṇa kālikā ||  
  
mamāṃtarhṛdayāṃbhojaṃ praviṣṭā siddhidāyinī |  
mūlamaṃtraṃ paṭhan kuryāllalāṭe viṃducitrakaṃ ||  
  
paṃcaprāṇāhutī dadyāt karṣanmāṃsalavaṃ vade |  
ādau tāraḥ śiraḥ śeṣe madhye turyavibhaktigān ||  
  
prāṇāpāna samāno dānavyā nānekarūpiṇaḥ |  
maṃtraṃ paṭhan vakṣyamāṇaṃ niḥśabdaṃ tat piveddravaṃ ||  
  
svātmamūla trikoṇodyat sūryakoṭi samaprabhe |  
kuṇḍalyā kṛti cidrūpe hunedravyaṃ samaṃtrakaṃ ||  
  
anaṃtapātrabharitamidaṃ tat paramāmṛtaṃ |  
parāhaṃtā maye vahnau homasvīkāralakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
idaṃ pavitramamṛtaṃ pivāmi bhavabheṣajaṃ |  
paśupāśa samucchedakāraṇaṃ bhairavoditaṃ ||  
  
anyaṃ maṃtraṃ paṭhintpatra maule yā jagadīśvarī |  
dharmādharma havirdīptamātmāganu manasā śruvā ||  
  
suṣumṇā vartmanā nityamakṣavṛttiṃ juhomyahaṃ |  
kāpālikānāṃ maṃtronyastamapivyāharāmite ||  
  
hṛdaṃ bhojagatāṃ devīṃ snāpayāmi sudhā rasaiḥ |  
tenāyaṃ bhavavaṃdho me vināśamupagacchatu ||  
  
evaṃ maṃtra trayaṃ proktaṃ pātrasvīkārakarmaṇi |  
nirmaṃtraṃ na piveddravyaṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate ||  
  
na kadācit pivenmadyaṃ nirmaṃtraṃ na pivet tathā |  
vinā maṃtraṃ pivenmadyaṃ samurāpo nigadyate ||  
  
pūrṇapātrakare dhṛtvā juhomi sādhakaḥ paṭhet |  
tato vīragaṇāḥ sarvejuṣasveti manuṃ vadet ||  
  
anyonyaṃ caṃdanaṃ kṛtvā pivet tat tadanujñayā |  
yathāvidhi dvitīyena gṛhnīyān maṃtramuccaran ||  
  
piśitaṃ māṣamātraṃ tu madyaṃ culukasaṃmitaṃ |  
svīkāryamādau guruṇā śiṣyebhyaḥ śeṣado bhavet ||  
  
p. 125a)  
  
nissaṃkonirmalo dhīro nirlajjāni kutūhalaḥ |  
nirṇīta vedaśāstrārtho varaṃdā vāruṇīṃ pivet ||  
  
devān pitṝn samabhyarcya vedīśāstroktavartmanā |  
guruṃ smaraṃ pivanmadyaṃ ṣādanmāṃsaṃ na doṣabhāk ||  
  
gurudaivatamaṃtrāṇāṃmaikyaṃ saṃbhāvayandhiyā |  
āgalāṃtaṃ piveddravyaṃ tataśca carvaṇaṃ caret ||  
  
māṃsaṃ matsyaṃ ca mudrāṃ ca maithunaṃ vai kramārcayet |  
svasaṃpradāya saṃyuktairvīraiśca sahapūjayet ||  
  
cittaḥ svātaṃtryasāratvāt tasmānaṃdamayetvataḥ |  
tanmayet vācca bhāvanāṃ bhāvaścāṃtarhite rase ||  
  
svasvātaṃtryavikāśāya surāsastena pīyate |  
tasmādiṣṭā surādevīṃ pūrṇāhaṃtā juhomyahaṃ ||  
  
maṃtreṇānena deveśi mūlamaṃtreṇa maṃtravit |  
anākulamanāḥ kuryān madhupānaṃ śaniḥ śnaiḥ ||  
  
yāvadullā sa paryaṃtamupadaṃśaiḥ pivanmadhuḥ |  
tataḥ pātragataṃ hālāviṃdu bhūmau prapātayet ||  
  
ucchiṣṭaṃ bhairavāyeha dadyān maṃtramanuṃ paṭhan |  
maidhamāyāramāvīje ehyesyucchiṣṭa bhairava ||  
  
visaṃdhi ca valiṃ gṛhya yugaṃ svāhā ca paścime |  
nighṛṣya tadbhūmitale pūrvavaccitrakaṃ caret ||  
  
yenyepi pātraṃ svīkuryusteṣāmapyeṣa hi kramaḥ |  
pānabhedaphalollāsaḥ pramāṇasthiti lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
avijñāya caredyastu ma bhavedā padāṃ padaṃ |  
pānapaṃcavidhaṃ proktaṃ mahādivyādi bhedataḥ ||  
  
mahādivyaṃ tathā divyaṃ vīraścaiva mahāpaśuḥ |  
paśuvaṃdyaḥ śuciśceti paṃcadhā parikīrtitaḥ ||  
  
prāṇāpānau samāhārau pratyāhāramanaḥ sthiraṃ |  
bhānumaṇḍalakaṃ bhītvā iṃdumaṇḍalamadhyagaṃ ||  
  
suṣumṇā vartmanā nityaṃ surādhārā prakarṣaṇī |  
mahādivyamidaṃ proktaṃ śṛṇu divyaṃ maheśvarī ||  
  
divyaṃ devyagrataḥ pānaṃ vīramṛdvāsanottamaṃ |  
tyaktaḥ sarvapāśa mūle vāmanāmala saṃcaye ||  
  
kaulikācāra yogena paṃcatatvena tarpayet |  
ṣaṭcakra kramabhedena huneddravyaṃ sa maṃtrakaṃ ||  
  
dhyānārcana parāvasthāṃ vīrapānamanuttamaṃ |  
udvāsanottaraṃ devi vīrapānaṃ taducyate ||  
  
vīrapānaṃ dvidhā prokta paśupānaṃ śṛṇu priye |  
vīrapāne pūrvadhīro parastu paśurityapi ||  
  
āsakta lolupādaṃbho maṃtrārthe vā prasaṃgakaḥ |  
kārmukaḥ kāryanirdeśe paśupānaṃ taducyate ||  
  
sarvaiḥ kulīnaiḥ sthitvā tu vinā pūjāṃ sa garvitaiḥ |  
yatpānaṃ krīyate devi paśupānaṃ taducyate ||  
  
atopi śṛṇu deveśi paśupāne kramaḥ śive |  
ekākī madyapāpīya ekākī śaktibhukpriye ||  
  
p. 125b)  
  
maheśvarasya saṃsargaṃ na kadāpi karoti cet |  
paśupānamidaṃ proktaṃ mahādāridryadāyakaṃ ||  
  
vinā maṃtraṃ vinā dīkṣāṃ vinā guru mukhātpriye |  
yatpānaṃ kriyate mūrkhaiḥ paśupānaṃ vidurvudhāḥ ||  
  
mahāpaśuriti proktaḥ kaulavāmo śṛṇu priye |  
vāme rāmā manohārī colipātraṃ tu dakṣiṇe ||  
  
pānapātrān maheśāni vāmahastena tarpakaḥ |  
mahākaulo maheśāni bhūmausthāpya pratarpayet ||  
  
hastadvayena ceddevi kaula ityabhidhīyate |  
vāmadakṣavyatpayena vīrakaula prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
alipātraṃ vāmapāṇau dakṣahastena tarpayet |  
kāmagauḍastu saṃproktaḥ caitanyākhyaḥ sa eva tu ||  
  
bhūmau sthāpya maheśāni hastayugmena tarpayet |  
ānaṃdākhyastu saṃproktaḥ vāma ityavidhīyate ||  
  
phalaṃ tu ||  
  
maṃtra saṃskāra saṃśuddho'mṛtapānena pārvatī |  
jāyate devatā bhāvo bhavavaṃdha vimocakaḥ ||  
  
ānaṃda brahmaṇo rūpaṃ tacca mokṣa vyavasthitaṃ |  
tasyābhivyaṃjakaṃ dravyaṃ yogibhistena pīyate ||  
  
divyapānarato vīro devī sāyujya māpnuyāt |  
deśiko vīrapānena devīlokaṃ hi gacchati ||  
  
sādhakaḥ paśupānena rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet |  
āraṃbhastaruṇaścaiva yauvanaḥ prauḍha eva ca ||  
  
tadaṃtaśconmanāsthānāṃvasthāścaiva saptamaḥ ||   
  
athaiṣāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
pātratrayaṃ syādāraṃbhaḥ kathitaḥ kulanāyike |  
tadaṃte taruṇaścaiva taruṇaṃ sukhadaṃ priye ||  
  
yauvanaṃ manasaḥ samyagullāsaḥ kathitaḥ priye |  
skhalanaṃ dṛṅmano vācāṃ prauḍhamitvabhidhīyate ||  
  
svābhīṣṭaveṣṭāvaraṇaṃ prauḍhāṃtaḥ parikīrtitaḥ |  
ūmanāḥ patanotthāna mūrchanācca muhurmuhuḥ ||  
  
deheṃdriyānāmavaśaścā navasthāni gadyate |  
bhojanāṃte viṣaṃ madyaṃ madyāṃte bhojanaṃ viṣaṃ ||  
  
amṛtaṃ tadvijānīyādyadantaṃ surayāsaha |  
carvaṇena yutaṃ madyamamṛtaṃ kathitaṃ sadā ||  
  
carvaṇena vināpānaṃ kevalaṃ viṣabhakṣaṇaṃ |  
tatastutvā namaskṛtya kuryāt saṃbhogamelanaṃ ||  
  
devatāgre tu saṃbhoge devatā prīṇanaṃ bhavet |  
etāsukāṃ vidānīya tataśca yonimaṇḍale ||   
  
pūjayitvā mahādevī tato maithunamācaret |  
dharmādharmahavirdīpte ātmāgnau manasā śruvā ||  
  
p. 126a)  
  
suṣumṇāvartmanā nityamakṣavṛttirjuhomyahaṃ |  
svāhāṃtoyaṃ mahāmaṃtra āraṃbhe parikīrtitaḥ ||  
  
tato japet priyaṃ gacchan devī tribhuvaneśvarīṃ |  
prakāśākāśahastābhyāmavalaṃ vyomanī śruvā ||  
  
dharmādharmakalā snehapūrṇamagnau juhomyahaṃ |  
svāhāṃtoyaṃ mahāmaṃtra śuklatyāge prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
pramādādyadi lupyeta devatā sā prakupyati |  
vinā bhuktvā vinā pītvā vinā kṛtvā tu paṃcamaṃ ||  
  
sa pāpiṣṭhaḥ kathaṃ vrūte kālīmaṃtraṃ japāmyahaṃ |  
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena sādhayet paṃcamaṃ priye ||  
  
yadi cetkriyate naiva tasya duḥkhaṃ pade pade |  
yadi yocinta saṃgastyāttadānu kalpayogataḥ ||  
  
kartavyaṃ karmasāṃgārthaṃ nocedviphalamīritaṃ ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau kaulavāmayoḥ sāmānyanityārcanāyāṃ   
pīṭhapūjādikuladravyaniṣevano nāmaikonaviṃśatitamaḥ prakāśaḥ || 19 ||  
nirgatya pūjāṃ gṛhato viharet svecchayā tataḥ |  
śṛṇu bhojana kālīyaṃ kartavya madhunā priye ||  
  
bhuṃjīta prācyabhimukhaścirakāji jīviṣu |  
yāmyadigvadano devī yaśaḥ kāmaṃ samaśrute ||  
  
paścimābhi mukho bhuṃkte īhamānodhikāṃ śriyaṃ |  
siddhimuktimabhilasadbhakṣayeduttarāmukhaḥ ||  
  
evaṃ sthite dharmapathe viśeṣācchaktyupāsakaḥ |  
sadottarāśābhimukhe'nnamadyāt saṃdhyayordvayoḥ ||  
  
validānaṃ tatra hetu nityāha bhagavācchivaḥ |  
yena kenādhyāsanena yasmin kasmin stathāsane ||  
  
upaviśyānnamaśnīyāttatu bhūmau kadācana |  
ādāvāca manaṃ kṛtvā dakṣe saṃsthā codakaṃ ||  
  
vāca ācamanīya matramaṃtranidadhīta vai |  
rātraupuraḥ pradīpaṃ ca divāgniṃ yaḥ sureśvarī ||  
  
tenāsya jāṭharo vahnirnitya siddho bhavedahe |  
bhūtapreta piśācānāṃ sānnidhyaṃ na ca jāyate ||  
  
rakṣāṃsinovalupyaṃti tadannaṃ taddhavistathā |  
nair-ṛtyāgrāṃ mārutāṃtā rekhāmudakadhārayā ||  
  
rodhaṃrāvāstramuccārya kuryād dakṣiṇapāṇinā |  
vāyavyagrāṃ tatheśānāṃ vasanāṃ tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
p. 126b)  
  
aiśānakoṇādārabhyāgne yāṃtāṃ tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
āgneyāgrāṃ nir-ṛtyaṃ tāṃ sarvaśeṣe vibhāvayet ||  
  
maṇḍalaṃ madhyaviṃdvārgharakṣaḥ koṇe vahirlikhet |  
vajraṃ vāyavyakoṇe ca caṃdrarekhāṃ sa viṃdukāṃ ||  
  
īśānakoṇe vilikhedaṃ kuśaṃ vahnikoṇagaṃ |  
arvācyodīcyagāṃ rekhāṃ madhye kuryāt tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
pratīcī prācyanugatāṃ punastaduparinyaset |  
rekhāgraṃ caṃdrarekhābhiḥ sa viṃdubhirupa spṛśet ||  
  
nirmite maṃḍale vāri dhārayaivaṃ varānane |  
svayaṃ vānyotha vā tatranyasedbhojanabhājanaṃ ||  
  
tadupaskaravastūni cāvaṃtiracitāni hi |  
pṛthak pṛthaktayā tatra vinyasedbhājanāgrataḥ ||  
  
tato dakṣiṇahastena tadannaṃ vāriṇokṣitaṃ |  
śirasyaṃ jalimādhāya praṇavediṣṭa rūpiṇaṃ ||  
  
haviraktaṃ vidhāyādau te manāloḍitaṃ tataḥ |  
gṛhītvā dakṣahastena kiṃcidannaṃ jalānvitaṃ ||  
  
ghanavījaṃ samuccārya paryanyaṃ cabhyasaṃtimaṃ |  
namastasyānu nair-ṛtya koṇe pūrvādike nyaset ||  
  
tārāt prajāpatibhyonu hṛduccāryāni lāhvaye |  
dadyāṃ dannaṃtoya yutaṃ tatra aiśānamaṃḍale ||  
  
kṣudbhyo namastasya vījaṃ pūra uktvā valiṃ nyaset |  
tadvahṛdbhyonamaḥ procya tadvījādyaṃ surārcīte ||  
  
dadyāt sṛṇu pariṣṭānnu sattoyānnaṃ ca dādhakaḥ |  
tataḥ svadakṣe pūrvasyāṃ kuryādvartula maṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
ārabhya pūrvarahito yāvatsyurvidigeśvarāḥ |  
tāvadvādyātsatoyānnaṃ paṭhenmaṃtraṃ pṛthak pṛthak ||  
  
caitanyaṃ praṇavo māyāpāśaḥ kāmaśca śākinī |  
yoginī kamalā ceti vījānyaṣṭau pṛthak pṛthak ||  
  
puṣṭiḥ kāṃtirvalaṃ buddhivīryaṃ jñānaṃ tathaiva ca |  
buddhiḥ siddhiritihyaṣṭau bhinnabhinnapadāni hi ||  
  
dāyai namaśca sarvebhyaḥ krameṇa parikīrtayet |  
ekāstu kālikā devyāḥ śaktirūpāstu mūrtayaḥ ||  
  
parivāratayākhyātā annādhiṣṭādya īritāḥ |  
etāstattat pradāyinyaḥ syurannena prapūjitāḥ ||  
  
tato bhojanapātrāgrecitastimita īritaḥ |  
ṣaṇmaṇḍalāni kurvīta vāriṇākṣallakāni hi ||  
  
p. 127a)  
  
teṣāmadhastāt kramato viṃdustāvat samācaret |  
yāvaddhastenotpatati piṃḍī kartuṃ ca śakyate ||  
  
tāvat tatra puro datvā vāriṇā tat samutsṛjet |  
adhogatistaduparitadaṣṭamanavastataḥ ||  
  
ataḥ paraṃ krameṇaiva maṃtrān dvādaśa tāṃtrikān |  
vakṣyamāṇānmayā devi sāvadhānā niśāmaya ||  
  
tāro māyā carāvaśca kūrcakuṃḍe sa karṇike |  
surasaścāpi phetkārī ghaṭī ceti na caiva hi ||  
  
vījāni purato datvā haṃsārādi trikūṭakaṃ |  
ehyehi saṃbhāṣya tato bhagavatyapi kīrtayet ||  
  
guhyakāli tataḥ procya sarvākhyāya na kāriṇi |  
idamannaṃ visaṃhyutkā gṛhnakhādi yugaṃ yugaṃ ||  
  
balaṃ buddhirmeṃdriyāṇi tato naṃtaramīrayet |  
mayidhehi dvayaṃ cāpi sarvāṃtaryāminīti ca ||  
  
tataḥ sarvamidaṃte ca svedatāṃ tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
prasīda dvitayasyānuroṣāstre śira eva ca ||  
  
maṃtreṇānena devyai tu valyannaṃ vinivedayet |  
annapiṇḍaṃ punaścānyatsaṃparisthāpya maṃḍale ||  
  
udīryamāṇamanunā samutsṛjya nivedayet |  
sārasvataramā kāmaprāsādāṃkuśakālikā ||  
  
ḍākinī preta bhairavyaḥ puro vījāni vai nava |  
kūṭatrayaṃ ca tadanu paiśācaḥ khecarīkulaṃ ||  
  
yoginī ḍākinībhyonunumamannavaliṃ vadet |  
nivedayāmi ca tataḥ saumyā bhuktvā bhavaṃ tu ca ||  
  
siddhiṃ dadatvanu mayi kṛpāṃ dadatu kīrtayet |  
prabhaṃjanādi vījāliṃ tataḥ saptasamullikhet ||  
  
aḍākinī mahārātriṃ roṣamastra trayaṃ śiraḥ |  
idānīma vadhe hitvaṃ vināyaka valiṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
pūrvavanmaṃḍale datvā valyannaṃte manairyutaṃ |  
jalpiṣyamāṇa maṃtreṇa gaṇā'dhipatayepayet ||  
  
vedādi pāśa garuḍayoginī caṃdradakṣiṇāḥ |  
valiḥ padmeśca taṃdrā ca kūṭā siddho prabhānavāḥ ||  
  
mahāgaṇādhipataye vighnarājāya cetyapi |  
imaṃ sopasthala valiṃ daded gṛhnayugaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
bhakṣaya dvitayaṃ cāpi sarvān vighnān tataḥ paraṃ |  
vināśa yadvayaṃ cārumamāriṣṭaṃ dahadvayaṃ ||  
  
vījamāpsarasa caiva māścarya vaiśvadevakaṃ |  
ṛṣabhaṃ ca prayojaṃ ca paṃcaitānī nayet kramāt ||  
  
p. 127b)  
  
astra trayānu svāhā ca tārtīyomaturīritaḥ |  
turyaṃ vaṭukanāthasya maṃtramākarṇaya priye ||  
  
puroktavat piṇḍitānnaṃ maṇḍale vinidhāya vai |  
samuccarantimaṃ maṃtraṃ vaṭukāya samarpayet ||  
  
tāracaitanya pāśahnī bhāruṇḍā kūrcakākinī |  
kālādityai na vaitāni vījāni coccaret punaḥ ||  
  
raudrā naṃdā calākhyātān kūṭāṃ strīṃ stadanaṃtaraṃ |  
ehyehi tadanuprocya mahāvaṭukanātha ca ||  
  
imaṃ vali gṛhīṇānu sarvasiddhi dada dvayaṃ |  
mamaśatruṃ nāśaya dvirdehadvirmāraya dvayaṃ ||  
  
sarvaiśvaryadehi yugmaṃ dāpaya dvitayaṃ tathā |  
sa sauraṃgaṃ carpaṭādi catuṣkaṃ tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
rauṣāstrayostristriruktvā sarvaśeṣe śiro vadet |  
adhunā kṣetrapālasya śṛṇvaṃ tu valimuttamaṃ ||  
  
puro vatsadalaṃ datvā maṃtramenaṃ samuccaret |  
caitanya māyākamalājaṃbha sāhasamekhalau ||  
  
tāṭaṃ kamaṃdasvārṇā ca vījāni purato na ca |  
kūṭatrayaṃ tato brūyān māyāmaṃdāragahvaraṃ ||  
  
hetukādipadaṃ procya bhīṣaṇāṃtebhya ityapi |  
sarvebhyaḥ kṣetrapālebhyaḥ imaṃ valiṃ mitīrayet ||  
  
dade saumyā bhavenmuktvā mamasiddhiṃ samullikhet |  
prayacchaṃ tu tataḥ śatrunnāśayaṃ tu ca kīrtayet ||  
  
hūṃ phaṭ svāhā bhaveccheṣa ityuktvā vāriṇot sṛjet ||  
  
atha ṣaṣṭhavale maṃtraṃ kathayāmi śucismite |  
dīyate parivārebhyoyamuccārya phalārthibhiḥ ||  
  
caitanya tārakamalā pāśaroṣa vadhusmarā |  
tataḥ trāsāda śākinyo purovījāni vai navaḥ ||  
  
bhagamāli kalāmāli vedavatyastataḥ paraṃ |  
ratnakuṃbhaḥ puṣpamālā cūḍākūṭaṃ tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
ekāvalī tato vajrakavacaṃ brahmakarparaṃ |  
jagadā vṛtitvījaṃ ca daśamaṃ parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
mahākalpasthāyi nāma jñeya mekādaśaiva hi |  
pārijātāhvayaṃ kūṭaṃ tadvādaśatamaṃ bhavet ||  
  
ekaviṃśatirevasyāt saṃkhyā vai vījakūṭayoḥ |  
guhyakālī sahacaraṃ yāvadeka padādanu ||  
  
parivārapadaṃ cāpi dvayamevetyasaṃmitaṃ |  
tataḥ saṃdhānasahitamimamannavaliṃ vadet ||  
  
p. 128a)  
  
gṛhna dvayaṃ makṣayadviḥkhāhi dvitayameva ca |  
uktvā kṛtyābhicārāṃśca dahadvirnāśayadvayaṃ ||  
  
sarvasaṃpadamābhāṣya dada dehi dvayaṃ dvayaṃ |  
śatrūn dviḥsaṃhārayoccārya śeṣe kūrcāstrakāni ca ||  
  
valimaṃtrā ṣaḍevaṃte kathitā jagadīśvarī |  
ūrddhvastha maṃḍaleṣvetairutsṛjet sādhakocalīn ||  
  
eṣāmadhastādye proktāḥ viṃdavaḥ ṣaṭpuro mayā |  
taddevāṃstasya maṃtrāṃśca kathayāmyadhunā tava ||  
  
jātavedācāduvaścaśanyagastyau tataḥ paraṃ |  
kālāgni rudrastadanu paṃcamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ||  
  
kalpāṃtakālī ṣaṣṭhī tu vijñeyā tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
turyerkeṣaḍimeśabdāḥ kartavyaḥ suravaṃdite ||  
  
nidheyā kramaśaḥ kiṃtu vedādi hṛdayāṃtaraṃ |  
etairma * (?) bhirutsṛjya tat taddevebhya odanaṃ ||  
  
mūladevyaiḥ sarvamantamutsṛjet tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
uktamaṃtra dvayaṃ tatra vaidikaṃ tāṃtrikaṃ tathā ||  
  
dadyādu bhayamuccārya krama eṣa śivoditaḥ |  
tatrādau vaidikaṃ vacmi vakṣye tadanu tāṃtrikaṃ ||  
  
idamanna prāṇa dhanurddhāraṇā kāraṇaṃ sadā |  
yathā vibhava saṃbhārasaṃbhārita surī kuru ||  
  
tvamevānnaṃ tvamevātrītvaṃ dātrī tvaṃ grahītryapi |  
tvaṃ bhoktrī ca vidhātrī ca saṃhatryaṃpija nitryapi ||  
  
kalpāṃta kālanartaktvai mahāsaṃhāra mūrtaye |  
trilokī grāsakāriṇyai kimannaṃ te pradīyate ||  
  
tathāpi bhaktibhāvena yatta devi niveditaṃ |  
tadannaṃmayi vātsalyāt sādarādbhuṃkṣvakālike ||  
  
nivedyānena maṃtreṇa tāṃtrikaṃ samudīrayet |  
tāromaidhaṃ ca māyā ca prāsādo me ca yoginī ||  
  
pretaḥ paroḍākinī ca phetkārī hārakarṇike |  
saṃhārādi trayaṃ bhokakūṭādyaṃ tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
padaṃ siddhi karālīti siddhito vikarāli ca |  
bhagavatpatha saṃkīrtya guhyakālī tato vadet ||  
  
idamannaṃ visaṃdhyuktvā bhuṃjakhāhi yugaṃ yugaṃ |  
bhakṣaya dvitayaṃ cāpi māṃrakṣayugalaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
lajjā mahācaṃḍayogeśvarīti tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
vajrakāpāli tatra khecarī cakranāyike ||  
  
hasadvayaṃ valgayugaṃ peṣṭiḍiṃḍimadāruṇaḥ |  
roṣasyāstrasya ce tristri svāhāśeṣe vyavasthitaṃ ||  
  
paṭhitvemaṃ manuṃ sarvaṃ kṣipedatvannamūrddhani |  
nimīlya nayane tiṣṭhet kṣaṇaṃ tadanu pārvatī ||  
  
āpośānaṃ tataḥ kuryādimaṃ maṃtramudīrayet |  
imamannaṃ havyaśeṣaṃ devyucchiṣṭhaṃ rasānvitaṃ ||  
  
p. 128b)  
  
asvāmi svargakaṃ valyadharmakāmārtha siddhaye |  
ityuccārya manuṃ namaḥ śiro vāma kaniṣṭhayā ||  
  
gaṇḍūṣaṃ brahmatīrthena spṛśan sthālī caredvudhaḥ |  
tato dakṣakarāṃguṣṭhānāmike yojite caran ||  
  
haviraktaṃ stokamannaṃ gṛhītvā vadane nyaset |  
prāṇāhutībhirjuhuyādanyābhirapi pārvati ||  
  
nānāmatīyāṃtadrīkathayāmyavadhāraya |  
tārāgni jāyayormadhye vibhaktyā turyayānvitā ||  
  
krameṇa vāyavaḥ paṃca teṣāṃ nāmāni vai śṛṇu |  
prāṇāpāna samāno dānavyānāḥ parameśvarī ||  
  
rāṃtyānayābhāṇḍikerojudvatyanyānapi priye |  
nāgaḥ kūrmaśca kṛkaro devadatto dhanaṃjayaḥ ||  
  
etasmādadhikaṃ kiṃcit kuryuḥ kāpālikā kramaṃ |  
yuktiyuktaṃ tamapite kathayāmi varānane ||  
  
tayorevāṃtareśabdau dvau dvau syādaṃtimau sadā |  
kṛtvā vigrahitau pūrvoktarītyā juhuyācchanaiḥ ||  
  
kṣaṭ tṛpau ca śramālasya nidrātaṃdre tathaiva ca |  
kāmakrodhau lobhamohau madamānau tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
rogaśokau janmamṛtyurddharmādharmau kṛtā kṛte |  
puṇyapāpe divārātrau jñānajñāne śubhā'śubhe ||  
  
jāgrat svapnau khaluḥ suṣupti turīyaṃ ca tatonu ca |  
bhāvābhāvau svargamartyau tataḥ satyānṛte priye ||  
  
tasmāt prakṛti puruṣau tanmātreṃdriya ityapi |  
jīvātmā paramātmānau vaṃdhamokṣau tathaiva ca ||  
  
caturviṃśatimau viṃśat prativiṃvau varānane |  
sarvaśeṣe parijñeyaḥ śivaśaktiśca sādhakaiḥ ||  
  
paṃcaviṃśati saṃkhyākametat tatvamudīritaṃ |  
tebhyastvāhuti saṃproktā yāmalādhipaśastutā ||  
  
anityatvena vedādhvapāpināṃ saṃmatātviyaṃ |  
kaulācāravatāṃ kiṃtu nityatvena prakīrtitā ||  
  
paṃcatriṃśāhutiḥ śreṣṭhā daśamadhyādhamātataḥ |  
evaṃ tiṣṭhati siddhāṃte prāṇāhutyāmatāṃtare ||  
  
yāvadyasya bhavecchakyaṃ tāvat tena vidhīyate |  
yāvat prāṇāhutīḥ kuryāt tāvadbhojanabhojane ||  
  
kaniṣṭhā tiṣṭhati tathā maunaṃ cāpi vidhīyate |  
tatastadannaṃ bhuṃjīta yaddevyai viniveditaṃ ||  
  
p. 129a)  
  
na hasan grāsamaśnīyānnāti riktaṃ na vāmanaṃ |  
na sa śabdaṃ pivettoyaṃ nādhikaṃ bhojanāṃtarā ||  
  
nyūnādhike rasānāṃ hi na viṃdyāt kiṃ ca pūjayet |  
naivedya saṃbhṛtau devyai yadyaddravyaṃ niveditaṃ ||  
  
mahāprasādabhūtaṃ tatsarvaṃ bhuṃjīta tatkṣaṇe |  
naikākyadyāt sādhakastu kaulān vālāṃśca vāṃdhavān ||  
  
sahopaveśayet tatra yatra bhuṃkte svayaṃ rahaḥ |  
eṣā mahāvaikaulikyo bhaveyuḥ sthāpitā api ||  
  
bhāgatrayaṃ pūrayīta jaṭharasyā śanaiḥ śanaiḥ |  
eko bhāgovaśoṣyaḥ syāt saṃcāro yonilāṃvunā ||  
  
tiktādyamamlamadhyaṃ hi madhurāṃtaṃ ca bhojanaṃ |  
āyurvedādiṣu prokta mātreyādi maharṣibhiḥ ||  
  
evaṃ nirvātya sakalaṃ bhojanaṃ sādhakaḥ svayaṃ |  
utkṣipya bhājano maṃtramanyatra sthāpayacchanaiḥ ||  
  
avaśiṣṭaṃ kiṃcidannamavaśya bhājane nyaset |  
tadannaṃ piṇḍitaṃ kṛtvā sa jalaṃ dakṣapāṇinā ||  
  
sthālyadho valimādadhyādu bhayatra varānane |  
ucchiṣṭa bhairavāyādau paścimāyāṃdiśi nyaset ||  
  
tathaivocchiṣṭa cāṃḍālyai pūrvasyāmapi ca kramāt |  
etayormaṃtra yugalamidānīmavadhārayet ||  
  
maidhaṃ māyāyoginī carāvarāmāsmarāśaruṭ |  
kulyāyoṭomuṃtālā ca vījānyetāni vai daśa ||  
  
ucchiṣṭa bhairavā yoktvā tathocchiṣṭa valiṃ vadet |  
gṛhna dvayaṃ bhuṃjayugmaṃ hū& phaṭ svāhā ca paścime ||  
  
athāparaṃ śṛṇu manuṃ pūrvasyāṃ yena dīyate |  
maidhaṃ pāśaḥ smarorāvaḥ kūrcaḥ kṣetrapatākinī ||  
  
pūtanāśakti liṃgaṃ ca rāvī ceti daśoddharet |  
ehyehyucchiṣṭa cāṃḍālinyanughaṃsadhi varjitaṃ ||  
  
virūpaveśa uddhṛtya mumukṣūktvā piśācini |  
iyamucchiṣṭa saṃbhāṣya valiṃ gṛhna yugaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
khādadvitayamasyānu mudrāṃ khecaryanaṃtaraṃ |  
yugaṃ prakaṭayaḥ procyaḥ saṃdhyūnamabhicāriṇī ||  
  
sāmarthyaṃ devi yugmaṃ ca piśācinyāstrayaṃ tataḥ |  
atrāpi caramejñeyā pūrvavaccaturakṣarī ||  
  
evaṃ manubhyāmetābhyāṃ datvā valiyugaṃ priye |  
tatraivā ca manaṃ kuryāt saḍaṃgaṃ tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
p. 129b)  
  
prasāda yat tāṃvūlaṃ cāsya vāsanaṃ |  
tāṃvūlaṃ carvayan martyaḥ pavitraṃ śrīkaraṃ paraṃ ||  
  
śubhadaṃ sarvavarṇānāṃ mukhaśuddhiṃ karaṃ paraṃ |  
tāṃvūlaṃ dīpanaṃ rucyaṃ sarvavātaka bhāpadaṃ ||  
  
tyājyaṃ piktva bhrame raktenetroktvaṃ pekṣayepi ca |  
parṇāgraṃ parṇapṛṣṭaṃ ca cūrṇaparṇaṃ vivarjayet ||  
  
parṇamūle bhavedvyādhi parṇāgre pāpavuddhayaḥ |  
cūrṇaparṇaṃ haratyāyuḥ śirāvuddhi vināśinī ||  
  
tarjanyā cūrṇamādāya tāṃvūlaṃ na tu bhakṣayet |  
yadi khedati muḍhātmā rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet ||  
  
pūgo brahmādalaṃ viṣṇuścūrṇa devo maheśvaraḥ |  
kāṣṭhāyaṃ tu bhaveddevī tāṃvūlamatidurlabhaṃ ||  
  
eteṣāṃ saṃpradānena varddhate bhāgyasaṃpadaḥ |  
tāṃvūla samayaṃ devī tatra śṛṇu yathā kramaṃ ||  
  
śataparṇāni deveśi cakravartitarāya ca |  
gurubhyaḥ saṃpradātavyā dvātriṃśatparṇavīṭikā ||  
  
aṣṭāviṃśati bhūpebhyo vāṃdhavebhyo daśāṣṭakaṃ |  
jāmātre pakvaparṇāni vasudvādaśa vā priye ||  
  
paṃcaviṃśati śaktibhyaḥ putrebhyastatva saṃkhyakān |  
ṣaṭparṇāni ca śatrubhyasturīyaṃ dānamuttamaṃ ||  
  
parṇatrayaṃ śatrupakṣe daśaparṇāni vaśyayoḥ |  
vīrebhyaḥ ṣoḍaśa śive divyaughe vasu pīṭhayuk ||  
  
tadarddhaṃ caiva siddhaughe mānavaughe tadarddhakaṃ |  
mānyebhyaḥ saptaparṇāni kanyāyai paṃcaviṃśatiḥ ||  
  
caṃdrayuktaṃ maheśāni pautrebhyo daśapaṃca ca |  
stuṣāyai triṃśati śivedāsye caiva caturdaśaḥ ||  
  
anyebhyaḥ parameśāni viṃśat parṇāni dāpayet |  
paripūtrī tathā dāsī dāsaścaiva caturthakaḥ ||  
  
parivettā pārivettā ṣaṭtāṃvūladāyakāḥ |  
agradānaṃ ca śatrubhyo cakradānaṃ sumitrake ||  
  
tiryagdānaṃ sevakādau yathā yogena yojayet ||  
  
mlecchahastā chatruhastācchaṃki tasya tathaiva ca |  
atha vaidagdha hastasya tāṃvūlaṃ hi niṣidhyati ||  
  
ādyapīkobhiyoktavyo dvitīyalpajyatāṃ sataṃ |  
tṛtīyo gṛhyatāṃvūlāt tṛtayaṃ tṛtayaṃ kramāt ||  
  
patraṃ phalaṃ kādiraṃ ca cūrṇaṃ caiva caturthakaṃ |  
paṃcamaṃ tu sukhaṃ proktaṃ rāgaḥ ṣaṣṭha udāhṛtaḥ ||  
  
ṣaḍaṃgamiti saṃproktaṃ ṣaḍaiśvaryayutāyakaṃ |  
||  
  
p. 130a)  
  
tadgṛhītvā varārohe svecchayā viharet tataḥ |  
atha vā sāyaṃtana bhavaṃ kṛtyaṃ samavadhāraya ||  
  
saṃdhyāhnakālavat saṃdhyāṃ vaidikīṃ samupāsya hi |  
tāṃtrikīmācareddevī trivarṇasthāna cetaraḥ ||  
  
turyastu tāṃtrikīmevano bhāvapyavalājaghanaḥ |  
astaṃgamanavelāyāṃ mārtaṇḍasya niśā su vā ||  
  
atha nitya śivāvalidānaṃ ||  
  
vilvamūle prāṃtare vā śmaśāne vāpi sādhakaḥ |  
sthāpino jayino nityaṃ kāmye caiva kulākule ||  
  
māṃsa pradhāna naivedyaṃ saṃdhyākāle nivedayet |  
kālikālīti vaktavye tadā sā śivarūpiṇī ||  
  
paśurūpadharāyāti parivāragaṇaiḥ saha |  
bhuktvā rauti yadaiśānyāṃ mukhamuttolyasusvaraṃ ||  
  
tadaiva maṃgalaṃ tasya anyathā kuladūṣaṇaṃ |  
avaśyaṃ cānnadānena niyataṃ toṣayecchivāṃ ||  
  
nityaśrāddhaṃ yathā saṃdhyā caṃdanaṃ pitṛtarpaṇaṃ |  
tathaiva kulasevyānāṃ nityatā kulapūjanṃ ||  
  
paśurūpadharāṃ devīṃ yo nārcayati nirjane |  
śivārāveṇa tasyāśu sarvaṃ naśyati niścitaṃ ||  
  
japapūjāvidhānāni yatkiṃcit sukṛtāni ca |  
gṛhītvā śāpamādatte śivārodati nirjane ||  
  
ekayā bhujyate yatra śivayā kulabhairavi |  
tatraiva sarvaśaktīnī prītiḥ paramadurlabhā ||  
  
paśuśaktiḥ pakṣiśaktirnaraśaktiryathā kramāt |  
pūjanād dviguṇaṃ karma saguṇaṃ sādhako yataḥ ||  
  
tena sarvaprayatnena kartavyaṃ pūjanaṃ mahat |  
rājādi bhayamāpanne deśāṃtara bhayādike ||  
  
śubhāśubhāni karmāṇi viciṃtya valimāharet |  
gṛhna devi mahābhāge śive kālāgnirūpiṇī ||  
  
śubhāśubhaphalaṃ vyaktaṃ vrūhi gṛhna valiṃ tava |  
evamuccāryadātavyo valiḥ kulajanai priye ||  
  
tadi no bhujyate devi tadā naiva śubhaṃ bhavet |  
śubhaṃ yadi bhavet tatra bhujyate tadaśeṣataḥ ||  
  
evaṃ jñātvā mahādevi śāṃtiṃ svastyayanaṃ caret ||  
  
iti śivāvalidānam ||  
  
p. 130b)  
  
kṛta śaucastathā cāṃtaḥ punaḥ pūjālayaṃ viśet |  
puṣpasragdhūpanaivedya validīpādi saṃbhṛtiṃ ||  
  
pūjākālī navat kuryāt sādhayaṃtaṃ samarcane |  
ārātrikaṃ vibhavato dīpavṛkṣānapi priye ||  
  
kṣaṇaṃ nimīlya nayane dhyānaṃ pūrvoktavaccaret |  
tato vaddhāṃjaliḥ padmayugalaṃ samudīrayet ||  
  
yoginyo mātaraḥ siddhāḥ kṣetrapālān vināyakāḥ |  
tathā vaṭukanāthaśca cāmuṇḍā bhairavīgaṇāḥ ||  
  
vetālabhūtakuṃbhāṇḍāye cānye kālikānumāḥ |  
iha kurvaṃtu sānnidhyaṃ kurvehaṃ naiśikārcanaṃ ||  
  
paṭhitvetthaṃ tataḥ kuryādṛṣyādidviṣaḍaṃgakaṃ |  
vaktranyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryādāvaśyakatayāpriye ||  
  
anyānapi svecchayaivayāvacchakyān samācaret |  
vaktranyāsasya nityatvamitereṣāṃ ca kāmyataḥ ||  
  
itthaṃ nyāsādikaṃ kṛtvā svecchayā suravaṃdite |  
vaddhāṃjaliḥ punarapi ślokanekaṃ samuccaret ||  
  
he guhyakālī jagadīśvarī viśvamātaścaitanyarūpiṇī sadāśiva jīvatulye |  
dainaṃdina pracitayā pacayāpahatyaisāyaṃtanaṃ smaraṇamamvakaromitehaṃ ||  
  
paṭhitvemaṃ tataḥ puṣpaṃ gṛhītvāṃ jalinā priye |  
trikhaṇḍā mudrayā vāpi dhyānonmīlita dṛk caret ||  
  
atha trikhaṇḍāmudrā yathā ||  
  
parivartyakarau spṛṣṭāvaṃguṣṭhau kārayet samau |  
anāmāṃtargate kṛtvā tarjanyau kuṭilākṛtī ||  
  
kaniṣṭhike niyuṃjīte nijasthāna maheśvarī |  
trikhaṇḍeyaṃ samākhyātā tripurāhvāna karmaṇi ||  
  
pūrvastotrokta padyobhyāṃ na tu dhyāyediti kramaiḥ |  
yāvatvarkakaletekaṃ brahmeṃdreti dvitīyakaṃ ||  
  
śaktau pūrvoktavat kuryādā vāhanapuraḥsarān |  
upacārān ṣoḍaśabhirmaṃtraireva puroditaiḥ ||  
  
aśaktau kusumaiḥ sragbhirddhūpadīpaidirātrikaiḥ |  
naivedyairvalibhistotraiḥ pāṭhairapi japairapi ||  
  
daṇḍavat praṇameccāpi kuryāccāpi pradakṣiṇaṃ |  
kākūktibhiḥ prārthapītaḥ svasyābhīṣṭāni sādhakaḥ ||  
  
yadi vedvidyate devi pratimā yaṃtrameva ca |  
kalpayitvā tadākalpaṃ mṛdvāstaraṇa saṃvṛtaṃ ||  
  
p. 131a)  
  
sthāpayitvopadhānaṃ ca sā japet tatrakālikāṃ |  
naiśārcanopayuktāni syurvaidyāni ca yāni hi ||  
  
avaśyaṃ tāni bhuṃjīta śaktibhiḥ sādhakaiḥ saha |  
gītavādyādi nṛtyaṃtaṃ yathāśaktiṃ tataścaret ||  
  
sāyaṃtanīna sa śanaṃ kuryāt pūrvoktavat tataḥ |  
svayaṃ śayīta tadanusahasvābhiṣṭayāstriyā ||  
  
pracchirā vā dakṣaśirā modak paścimamastakaḥ |  
prāk śireśayane vidyā āyurvittaṃ ca dakṣiṇe ||  
  
paścime pravalā ciṃtāhāni mṛtyustathottare |  
kṛta śaucaḥ karapadairācāṃtaḥ su samāhitaḥ ||  
  
dīpe jvalati nadhvāṃtenā kṛtā pavanāśanaḥ |  
na ca stimitavatpāṇirnanagno nāpi kaṃcukī ||  
  
paṭhendusvapnanāśāya vakṣyamāṇānmarutpriye |  
jaganmātarmahāmāyekālike kālanāśini ||  
  
duḥsvapnaṃ hararudrāṇitvadbhaktaṃ pāhimāṃ sadā |  
bhūtapretapiśācādyāye bhīmādeva mānavaḥ ||  
  
rakṣo dānavadaityāśca ye nidrābhaṃgakārakā |  
duḥsvapnajāścaye doṣā mamahiṃsā karāścaye ||  
  
tetvatsmaraṇadaṃbholi nihitāyāṃ tu saṃkṣayaṃ |  
ye daṃdaśūkā vihagāvṛścikāḥ śūkayonayaḥ ||  
  
yeṣāṃ viṣaṃ vādhateṅgaṃ ye ca śṛṃgaviṣāstathā |  
viṣairvapuryutā kīṭāye codvegapradāyinaḥ ||  
  
śrutvā te kālikānāma vidravaṃ tu diśodaśaḥ |  
kālīkarālī cāmuṇḍā chinnamastā ca bhairavī ||  
  
harasiddhāsiddhilakṣmīrdvāmarī vābhravī tathā |  
mahāmārī tāmasī ca mātaṃgīśavareśvarī ||  
  
carcikā śivadūtī ca mahāmahiṣamardinī |  
ugracaṃḍākubjikā ca phetkārī guhyakālyapi ||  
  
etāste mūrtayo ghorāyāśca saumyāsureśvarī |  
mātaḥ śayānaṃ rakṣaṃ tu duḥsvapnaṃ nāśayaṃ tu ca ||  
  
cakrapāśāsi śūlarṣṭi gadā parighatomarāḥ |  
vajramudgarakuṃteṣu bhuśuṃḍī pāśapaṭṭiśaḥ ||  
  
yānyanyāpi ca deveśi karayorvidhṛtāni te |  
astrāṇi tāni rakṣaṃ tu svayaṃtaṃ māṃ maheśvarī ||  
  
tvadājñayā nārasiṃhī pūrvasyāṃdiśi pātumāṃ |  
vārāhī paścimāyāṃ ca dakṣiṇasyāṃ ca kālikā ||  
  
p. 131b)  
  
uttarasyāṃ ca cāmuṇḍā mahāghoratarāvatu |  
urddhaṃ tathādho digvidiśostvaṃ sarvatraiva pāhimāṃ ||  
  
śaktayoyāścate devi parivāragaṇāścaye |  
sarvatra sarvadā pāṃtu māṃ tvaccaraṇasevakaṃ ||  
  
tvadājñayaiva deveśi nānārūpadharāvubhau |  
devau māmavatāṃ viṣṇurudrau sarvasureśvarau ||  
  
varāho nārasiṃhaśca vāmanonaṃta eva ca |  
trivikramo hayagrīvaḥ ṣaḍaite pāṃtumāṃ sadā ||  
  
mṛtyuṃjayo nīlakaṇṭho dakṣayajña vighātakaḥ |  
tripurapnohariśmaśruḥ pinākī nīlalohitaḥ ||  
  
pramatheśaḥ kīrtivāsā virupākṣo maheśvaraḥ |  
ekādaśaitemāṃ pātu rudrāraudraḥ tanūdharāḥ ||  
  
sadā māmakṛtaṃ bhītiṃ kurustvaṃ guhya kālike |  
evamaṣṭādaśa ślokairakṣāṃ kṛtvān manaḥ priye ||  
  
śayitaściṃtayan kālīṃ nirviśaṃ kena ceta sā |  
sarvā niśāmayogajñogamayatyaiva nidrayā ||  
  
uttiṣṭeccoṣasi punaḥ prātaḥkṛtya cikīrṣayā |  
āhnikaṃ pūrvavat kāryaṃ svasvakalpokta vartmanā ||  
  
atha madhyamānāṃ nityārcanavidhiḥ ||  
  
athānyaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmiyaṃ vināduḥkhamāpnuyāt |  
prātarutthāya gurvādi smṛtvā śaucaṃ samācaret ||  
  
snānasaṃdhyāṃ tarpaṇaṃ ca vaidikaṃ tāṃtrikaṃ tathā |  
āgatya ca gṛhe paścāt prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ caret ||  
  
kuryācca mātṛkānyāsaṃ tathā chaṃdapi devatam |  
tanmaṃtrasya karāṃgākhya nyāsaṃ śaṃkhārgha saṃsthitiḥ ||  
  
maṃtrasnānaṃ devatāyāḥ pūjāpaṃcorikā |  
caṃdanāṃ te tvāvṛtīnāṃ puṣpaireva prapūjanaṃ ||  
  
vaiśva devottaraṃ tatra dadannāhuti paṃcakaṃ |  
mūlena homayet tat prāgjapaścāṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ ||  
  
vaidikākāśavalyaṃte pūjā cocchiṣṭa bhojitaṃ |  
tataḥ saṃprārthayeddevaṃ sāyaṃ saṃdhyā samācaret ||  
  
devāgāraṃ dīpadānaṃ proktaṃ saṃkṣepamāhnikaṃ ||  
  
atha pravāsa kārāgṛhādya śubhasthānāhnikaṃ ||  
  
athāparāhnikaṃ vakṣye tatsthāna daśake bhavet |  
mārge pravāse durge ca nāntaḥ prāptau manobhaye ||  
  
kārāgṛhe śubhesthāne sarpavyāghrādije bhaye |  
paracakrāgame kuryācchau cādyaṃ tu yathā tathā ||  
  
maṃtrasnānādikaṃ ciṃtya kṛtvā mānasapūjanaṃ |  
manasā hṛdayasyāṃtardhyātvā yogākhya pīṭhakaṃ ||  
  
p. 132a)  
  
tatraiva pṛthivīmadhye pūjāṃ devasya cācaret |  
yathā puṣpādibhiḥ pūjā vahirdeśe vidhīyate ||  
  
tathā hṛdyapi kartavyāḥ sarvāstāḥ pratipattaye |  
manasā jaṭhare home etadvipadi cāhnike ||  
  
atha rogiṇāmāhnikaṃ ||  
  
athāturāhnikaṃ vakṣye nityaṃ svāsthyādhikasya tat |  
yadi laṃghanaparyaṃto vyādhirātmani dṛśyate ||  
  
tadā pūjā na kartavyāsthaṇḍilaṃ pratimāsu ca |  
na snānaṃ daṃtakāṣṭhaṃ vā kuryāddho na mathāpi vā ||  
  
ravimaṃḍalamālokya pratimāmatha vā punaḥ |  
mūlamaṃtraṃ sakṛjjaptvā puṣpaṃ sākṣatamutsṛjet ||  
  
śrāṃto vyādhibhiratyugrairjarayā ceṃdriyai śataḥ |  
nijasāmayakairvāpi svakartavyaṃ samāpayet ||  
  
agnivṛttastataḥ kṛtvā pūjayitvāgni devatāḥ |  
guruvidyāṃstadagre ca vākyaṃ ca tadudīrayet ||  
  
etāvat kālavicchinnā pūjāyuṣmat prasādataḥ |  
na doṣostviti saṃprāpya punaḥ pūrvavadācaret ||  
  
yastu rogavaśāddoṣo jātastat kṣālanaṃ caret |  
japena vātha dānena homane dhanatopi vā ||  
  
athāṇau vāhnikaṃ ||  
  
atha sūtakināṃ nityaṃ vaidikaṃ smṛtīritaṃ |  
jātasūtakamādau ca tadaṃte mṛtasūtakaṃ ||  
  
dvijasya sūtake devi na devoccāṭamācaret |  
saṃdhyāṃ ca mānasīṃ kuryāt dhyātvaiva parameśvarī ||  
  
śālagrāmaṃ ca pratimāṃ na spṛśet karhicit priye |  
sparśātpāpī naro bhūyānnā prakāryā vicāraṇāt ||  
  
kṛtvā tāṃtrikapūjādi manasaiva samācaret |  
kāmanārthaṃ prayogaścet tadā pūrvavadācaret ||  
  
mṛtagehaṃ parityajya vāmācāreṇā sūtrakaṃ |  
spṛhāṃ hitvā jñāna pūrvaṃ kulatodharmamāgataṃ ||  
  
yayālabhedvāmadharmaṃ devatāyāṃ sajāyate |  
gurūpadiṣṭaṃ yatkarma bhaktyā vāme karoti yaḥ ||  
  
śāstratatvaṃ devatatvaṃ no vahiḥ sa tu guhyakaḥ |  
jñātvā tamevaṃ bhajate sukhārthā tatra jāyate ||  
  
kṣuṭ tṛṣṇā mohitaḥ pretastasyāddharmaṃ vicārayet |  
saṃtastena na cellasyāvyarghya yātrādi sādhanaṃ ||  
  
p. 132b)  
  
pūjodakena kartvyā toya yannaiva vidyate |  
tadā saṃpūjayeddevaṃ bhāvanā kusumādibhiḥ ||  
  
bhaktiśraddhābhāvanā ca pūjānāṃ jīva ucyate ||  
  
atha jaḍāhnikaṃ ||  
  
jaḍānāmāhnikaṃ vakṣye tathā saṃkṣepa karmaṇi |  
ratnamaṃḍapa dharmādi catuṣkamuragoṃ vrajaṃ ||  
  
mūlamūrtiḥ ṣaḍaṃgāni teṣāṃ pūjā vidhīyate ||  
  
sarveṣāmapi vastūnāma lābhe bhāvanaiva hi |  
nirmalenodake naiva pūjayet sthiramānasaḥ ||  
  
sāmānyatastridhā pūjā cottamā madhyadhamā |  
adhikārī nimittābhyāṃ bhidyate śatadhā punaḥ ||  
  
yā sopakaraṇaiḥ kṛtsnaiḥ krīyamāṇottamāmatāḥ |  
yathā labdhairviniṣpādyairdravyaiḥ pūjā tu madhyamā ||  
  
yatra puṣpāṃvu niṣpādyā pūjā cādhamasaṃjñakāḥ |  
vihitākhila vedāktairbrahmarṣibhirakalmaṣaiḥ ||  
  
kriyamāṇā tu yā pūjā sātvikī sā vimuktidā |  
rājarṣibhistayoniṣṭairbhagavattatvavedibhiḥ ||  
  
yā pūjā krīyate samyagrājasī sā sukhapradā |  
strīvāla vṛddhamūrkhādyairbhaktairakṣudramānasaiḥ ||  
  
yā pūjā krīyate nityaṃ tāmasī sā prakīrtitā ||  
  
araṇye svalpa kāmānāṃ siddhyarthaṃ pūjanaṃ hitaṃ |  
niṣkāmānāṃ gṛhasthānāṃ hitaṃ gehe tu pūjanaṃ ||  
  
kadācidapi ratyājo vedamārgo dvijaiḥ sadā |  
vedacyutānāṃ vipratvaṃ devatvaṃ cāpi durlabhaṃ ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau bhojanādipūjāyāḥ sātvikādibhedāṃtanirṇayo nāma   
viṃśatitamaḥ prakāśaḥ || 20 ||  
sarvasādhāraṇaṃdhīrā uktamevā puro mayā |  
kalpāni daśavidyāyā krameṇa kathayāmi tu ||  
  
atha śyāmā yā viśeṣa kramamāha ||  
  
snānaṃ saṃdhyādikaṃ sarvaṃ pūrvavat samupasya ca |  
avahirmāna sā yogī yāgabhūmiṃ tathā viśet ||  
  
atha sthānamāha ||  
  
ekaliṃge śmaśāne ca śūnyāgāre catuḥpathe |  
tatrasthaḥ sādhayedyogī vidyāṃ tribhavamocinīṃ ||  
  
eteṣāṃ lakṣaṇamāha ||  
  
paṃcakrośāṃtare yatra na liṃgāṃtaramiṣyate |  
tadā kaligamākhyātaṃ tatra siddhiranuttamā ||  
  
p. 133a)  
  
gṛdhragomāyukākādyairmāṃsalubdhairyadāvṛtaṃ ||  
  
tachmaśānamitikhyātaṃ piśāca gaṇasevitaṃ |  
kākādi gṛdhra saṃyuktaṃ kṛmichatrādi saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
nāgarairdūranirmuktaṃ sādhvasodvetakāraṇaṃ |  
saudhasaṃrūḍhadyāsāḍhyaṃ śūnyāgāraṃ taducyate ||  
  
caturṇāṃ patho yatra saṃyogo yugapad bhavet |  
taccatuṣpathamityuktaṃ rajanyāmiṣṭadāyakaṃ ||  
  
pūrvapūrvakamiśastaṃ jaghanyaṃ cottarottaraṃ |  
urjaṭe parvate vāpi nirjane vā catuṣpathe ||  
  
devāgāre devaśūnye vilvamūle nadītaṭe |  
svagṛhe nirjanā rāme tathā cāśvattha sannidhau ||  
  
tadabhāve divyagehe siṃdūrādibhiraṃkite |  
khaḍgaśūlagadākartrī cāmaravyajanādibhiḥ ||  
  
vitāna dhūpasaṃkīrṇe kṛṣṇā guru suvāsite |  
yuvatīnāṃ surāpīnāṃ veśyānāṃlāsya śobhite ||  
  
śaṃkhaghaṃṭhāravākīrṇe dīpāvali virājate |  
evaṃ putragṛhe pūjā kālikāyāḥ suśobhanā ||  
  
atha kālamāha ||  
  
sarva eva śubhaḥ kālo nā śubhaṃ vidyate kvacit |  
na viśeṣo divārātrau saṃdhyāyāmatha vā niśi ||  
  
na viśeṣo divārātrau saṃdhyāyāmatha vā niśi |  
vali pūjādikaṃ sarvaṃ rātrau tu kriyate yadi ||  
  
tattadakṣayatāṃ yāti kālikāyāḥ prasādataḥ |  
gate tu prathameyāme tṛtīya praharāvadhi ||  
  
kulapūjāṃ prakartavyā kulaśāstra viśāradaiḥ |  
jalaśaṃkhaṃ kare kṛtvā gatvā dvāri maheśvarī ||  
  
kṣālayeddhastapādau ca vakṣyamāṇena vartmanā ||  
  
oṃ vajrodake hūṃ phaṭ svāhā maṃtreṇa maṃtravit |  
jalamānīya savyena āsanaṃ śodhayet tataḥ ||  
  
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuddhṛtya jajjāvījaṃ tathaiva ca |  
tato viśuddhāṃte sarve pāpāni śamayaṃ ca ||  
  
aśeṣāṃte viklpaṃ syāda panayeti tataḥ paraṃ |  
tato ācamanaṃ kṛtvā sāmānyārghyaṃ prakalpayet ||  
  
trikoṇavṛttabhūvivaṃ trikoṇa racayet tataḥ |  
ādhāraśaktiṃ saṃpūjya tatrādhāraṃ viniḥkṣipet ||  
  
p. 133b)  
  
astramaṃtreṇa saṃśodhya hṛnmaṃtreṇa prapūrayet |  
niḥkṣipet tīrthamāvāhya gaṃdhādyaṃ praṇavena tu ||  
  
darśayeddhanu mudrā vai sāmānyārghamidaṃ smṛtaṃ |  
sāmānyārgheṇa deveśi pūjayedvārapārśvagān ||  
  
gaṇeśaṃ kṣetrapālaṃ ca vaṭukaṃ yoginīṃ tathā |  
gaṃgāṃ ca yamunāṃ caiva lakṣmīṃ vāṇīṃ tato viśet ||  
  
gāṃ vījādyaṃ gaṇeśānaṃ vā mādyaṃ vaṭukaṃ tathā |  
kṣāmādyaṃ kṣetrapālaṃ ca yāmādyaṃ yoginīṃ tataḥ ||  
  
ūrddhve vāme dakṣiṇe ca adhaścaivaṃ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuddhṛtya sarvavighnāntataḥ paraṃ |  
utsāraya tato hūṃ phaṭ svāhā ca tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
anenaiva ca maṃtreṇa vighnānutsārayetsudhīḥ ||  
  
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuddhṛtya rakṣarakṣa tadaṃtaraṃ |  
hūṃ phaṭ svāheti maṃtreṇa pūjā bhūmiṃ ca śodhayet ||  
  
tataḥ pravṛtta vajrādau praṇavaṃ pūrvamuddharet |  
carmayaṃ ca tataścaiva phaṭ svāhā tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
anenaiva ca maṃtreṇa kuryād bhūmyabhimaṃtraṇaṃ ||  
  
adhiṣṭānepi ca puṣyasya praṇavaṃ pūrvamuddharet |  
ṭhātābhiṣeketi padaṃ ṭhātābhīti tataḥ padaṃ ||  
  
ṣeketi ca padaṃ proktaṃ hūṃ phaṭ svāhā tataḥ paraṃ |  
anena manunā devyāḥ puṣpādhiṣṭhānameva ca ||  
  
praṇavaṃ puṣpaketuśca tathā rājārhate tathā |  
ṭhātāyasasyagityuktvā saṃvuddhāya tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
puṣpe puṣpe mahāpuṣpe supuṣpe puṣpasaṃbhave |  
puṣpe ca yāvakīrṇe hūṃ phaṭ svāhā ca tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
viśuddhaṃ puṣpame tena jalaṃ pūrvavadā haret ||  
  
mṛdumacūḍamāsīnaścānyeṣu komaleṣu vā |  
viṣṭareṣu samāsīraḥ sādhayet siddhamuttamā ||  
  
mṛtāsanaṃ vinā devi yojapet kālikāṃ naraḥ |  
tāvat kālaṃ nārakī syāt yāvadā dūta saṃplavam ||  
  
ṛṣicchaṃdaṃ vidhāyātha kuśāṃ tatraiva dāpayet |  
māyāvījaṃ samuccārya ādhāraśakti pūrvakaṃ ||  
  
kamalāsanamālikhya ṅeṃtamoṃtaḥ prapūjayet |  
ākārāṃtaṃ surekhe ca vajrarekhe tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
hūṃ phaṭ svāheti kūryād vai maṇḍalaṃ tu śavāsane |  
vīrāsanenopaviśyet saṃpūjyāsanameva ca ||  
  
p. 134a)  
  
atha vīrāsanaṃ yathā ||  
  
ekapādamathai kasmin vinyasyoruṇi saṃsthitaḥ |  
itarasminnatho cāruṃ vīrāsana mudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
atha maṃtrācamanamāha ||  
  
upaviśyāsane maṃtrā camanaṃ sarvasiddhidaṃ |  
kālibhistribhiḥ pītvā kālyādibhirūpaspṛśet ||  
  
dvābhyāmoṣṭhau dvirunmṛjya caikena kṣālayet karaṃ |  
āsyaghrāṇe kṣaṇa śrotranābhyuraskaṃ bhujo spṛśet ||  
  
ācamyaivaṃ bhavedyastu vatsarāttāṃ prapaśyati |  
tataḥ ṣoḍaśavarṣīyānnārīmānīya yatnataḥ ||  
  
yuvatīṃ vāmadonmattāṃ suveṣāṃ cāruhāsinīṃ |  
sadā rase sābhilāṣīṃ siṃdūrāṃkitabhālikāṃ ||  
  
sādhake premaśīlāṃtāṃ vāme saṃsthāpayedvudhaḥ ||  
  
vinā hetu kamākhādya kṣobhayukto maheśvarī |  
na pūjānnajapaṃ kuryānnadhyānaṃ nāpi ciṃtanaṃ ||  
  
tasmādbhuktvā ca pītvā ca pūjayet parameśvarīṃ |  
kūrcaṃ viyadviṃduyutaṃ śaktyastrāya phaḍityapi ||  
  
anena manunā kuryād digvaṃdhaṃ choṭikādibhiḥ |  
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuddhṛtya tadanaṃtarameva ca ||  
  
hūṃ phaṭ svāhā manuḥ proktaḥ kāyavāhacittaśodhane |  
rakṣarakṣa hū& phaṭ svāhā maṃtrasyādātmarakṣaṇe ||  
  
tataḥ kṛtāṃjali puṭo vāmadakṣiṇapāśvayoḥ |  
guruṃ gaṇapatiṃ matvā purataḥ sveṣṭa devatāṃ ||  
  
sugaṃdhapuṣpāṇyādāya caṃdanāktāni maṃtravit |  
hyau& maṃtreṇa karayorastra maṃtreṇa mardayet ||  
  
tat puṣpaṃ vāma hastena samādāya ca mastakaṃ |  
bhrāmayet paritastāraṃ japannāghrāya tatpunaḥ ||  
  
hau& oṃ pūrvapaṭhe chlokamimaṃ sa ca nigadyate |  
te sarve vilayaṃ yātuṃ yemāṃ hiṃsaṃti hiṃsakāḥ ||  
  
mṛtyuroga bhayakleśāḥpataṃtu ripumastake |  
astramaṃtreṇa nārā ca mudrayeśa diśi tyajet ||  
  
bhūtaśuddhiṃ tataḥ kuryādātmānaṃ kuṇḍalīyutaṃ |  
jīvaṃ haṃsena saṃyojya śive ca madhyamādyayā ||  
  
pāpaṃ kukṣisthitaṃ krūraṃ vāyvagnimanilākṣaraiḥ |  
śoṣayedāhayedaṃtaḥ prakṣālya recayedvahiḥ ||  
  
sohamaṃtreṇatāmeva yathā sthānaṃ samānayet |  
tataḥ śuddhaśarīro sau jīvanyāsaṃ samācaret ||  
  
athāsyāḥ maṃtrabhūta śuddhimāha ||  
  
bhūtaśuddhiṃ tataḥ kuryāt svamaṃtrākṣarayogataḥ |  
yathā kālī tathā tārā yathā tārā tathonmukhī ||  
  
p. 134b)  
  
bhūtaśudhyādikaṃ sarvaṃ tāriṇīvat samācaret ||  
  
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kuryādvighatayā tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
bhairavosyā ṛṣiḥ prokta uṣṇik chaṃda udāhṛtaḥ |  
devatā kālikā proktā lajjāvījaṃ tu vījakaṃ ||  
  
śaktistu kūrcavījaṃ syāt kīlakaṃ codyavījakaṃ |  
viniyogo maheśāni caturvargasya siddhaye ||  
  
aṃganyā sa karanyāsau yathāvadabhidhīyate |  
ṣaḍdīrghabhājā vījena praṇavādyena kalpayet ||  
  
praṇavaṃ cādyavījaṃ ca ṣaḍdīrghasvarabheditaṃ |  
kuryāt ṣaḍaṃgavinyāsaṃ mūlakhaṃḍatrayeṇa ca ||  
  
varṇanyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryād divyabhāva phalapradaṃ |  
hṛdvāhu pādayugmeṣu sa viṃdūn mātṛkākṣarān ||  
  
paṃktiśo vinyaset paścādvyāpakanyāsamācaret |  
dorbhyāṃ ca vyāpakaṃ kuryān mūlavidyāṃ samuccaran ||  
  
pādādi ca śiro aṃtaṃ śira ādi padāṃtakaṃ |  
sakṛdevaṃ pravinyasya sādhakastanmayo bhavet ||  
  
atha varṇanyāsaḥ ||  
  
hṛdayevinyasedvāpi akārādi daśākṣaraṃ |  
ekārādi daśaccaiva paraṃ tu dakṣiṇe bhuje ||  
  
bhuje vāme pravinyasya ṅakārādi daśākṣaraṃ |  
paraṃ tu dakṣiṇe jaṃgheṇakārādi daśanyaset ||  
  
makārādi kṣakārāṃtaṃ vāmajaṃghe pravinyaset ||  
  
iti varṇanyāsaḥ ||  
  
atha ṣoḍhānyāsaḥ ||  
  
vakṣye ṣoḍhātmakaṃ nyāsaṃ durlabhaṃ bhuvanatraye |  
yaṃ kṛtvā sādhaka śreṣṭho bhavedbhairava sannibhaḥ ||  
  
vinyasen mātṛkāṃ pūrvaṃ nyāsoyaṃ prathamaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
śriyā saṃpuṭitaṃ varṇaṃ varṇa saṃpuṭitāṃ śriyaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ krameṇa vinyasya dvitīyaśca samīritaḥ |  
kāmasaṃpuṭitaṃ lakṣmīṃ lakṣmī saṃpuṭitaṃ ca taṃ ||  
  
vinyasen mātṛkāsthāne tṛtīyoyaṃ samīritaḥ |  
lajjayā saṃpuṭī lakṣmīṃ śriyā saṃpuṭitāṃ hriyaṃ ||  
  
pūrvavad vinyasen maṃtrīnyāsastūrya udāhṛtaḥ |  
mukhavṛtta samārūḍha lajjā dvaṃdvanamodvayaṃ ||  
  
śaśāṃkaśakalārūḍhaṃ kāmaśakrapade sthitaṃ |  
mūlasaṃpuṭitaṃ kṛtvā tatpuṭaṃ ca manuṃ tathā ||  
  
vinyaseduktamārgeṇanyāsoyaṃ paṃcamo bhavet |  
anulomavilomenelipi sthāneṣu kevalaṃ ||  
  
p. 135a)  
  
mūlaṃ vinyasya medhāvī mūlamaṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ |  
saṃjapya vyāpayeddehenyāsaḥ ṣaṣṭhoyamīritaḥ ||  
  
kālikāmaṃtrarājasya ṣoḍhānyāsoyamīritaḥ |  
evaṃ nyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryāt sa maṃtrī bhairavopamaḥ ||  
  
viṣopa mṛtyuharaṇaṃ graharogavināśanaṃ |  
duṣṭāḥ sarvevinaśyaṃti śatravoyāṃti mitratāṃ ||  
  
kavitālaharītasya drākṣārasa paraṃparā |  
aṇimādyaṣṭasiddhistu tasya haste vyavasthitā ||  
  
kāyikaṃ vācikaṃ vāpi mānasaṃ yaccaduṣkṛtaṃ |  
sarvaṃ tasya vināśatvaṃ yāti nyāsasya ciṃtanāt ||  
  
brahmahatyā kṣayaṃ yāṃti yatkiṃcidupapātkaṃ |  
yadrūpaṃ dṛśyate yaistu sa tadrūpaṃ ca gacchati ||  
  
yaṃ namaṃti mahādevi ṣoḍhā puṭitavigrahāḥ |  
alpāyuḥ sa bhavet sadyo devatā kaṃpatebhiyā ||  
  
sa haraḥ sa hariḥ sākṣāt sa devī nātra saṃśayaḥ |  
tārāyāśca tathonmukhyā idaṃ nyāsaṃ samācaret ||  
  
aṇimādyaṣṭa siddhināmīśvaraśca bhavennaraḥ ||  
  
atha guhya ṣoḍhānyāsaḥ ||  
  
īśvara uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devī pravakṣyāmi guhya ṣoḍhāmimāṃ priye |  
na prakāśyamidaṃ kvāpi yadīchedātmano hitaṃ ||  
  
karpūraṃ mātṛkāvarṇaiḥ puṭitaṃ mātṛkā sthale |  
tenaiva puṭitaṃ varṇaṃ nyasedatraiva pārvati ||  
  
kūrcavījayugaṃ devi vinyastavyaṃ prayatnataḥ |  
śaktivījaṃ tathā devī vinyasen mūlamāditaḥ ||  
  
dakṣiṇe kālikebhyāṃ tu pūrvavījatrayaṃ nyaset |  
kūrca vījatrayaṃ devī lajjāvīja dvayaṃ ||  
  
vinyastavyaṃ tathā devimīlitaṃ vahnijā yayā |  
tatastatsakalanyasya vyāpakatvena devate ||  
  
dvāviṃśatpakṣaremaṃtre ṣoḍhānyāsa ihoditaḥ |  
ayaṃ tu siddhido loke tathā devāsureṣu ca ||  
  
avaśyaṃ pratyahaṃ kāryaṃ na pūjā na japastathā |  
kṛtepi sādhakaḥ śreṣṭho mahādeva samo bhavet ||  
  
iti te kathitaṃ kiṃcid rahasyaṃ ghoradakṣiṇe |  
na prakāśyaṃ kadācittu deveṣu ca tathā nari ||  
  
atha tatvanyāsaḥ ||  
  
ātmavidyā śivaistatvaistatvaṃ nyāsaṃ samācaret ||  
  
p. 135b)  
  
atha vījanyāsaḥ ||  
  
atha brahmabhruvormadhye lalāṭe nābhideśake |  
guhye vaktre tu sarvāṃge saptavījāni vinyaset ||  
  
atha maṃtravarṇa nyāsaḥ ||  
  
śirasi nayane bhāle bhrūyugme karṇagaṇḍayoḥ |  
vadane radane jihvāskaṃdhadeśe galeṣu ca ||  
  
bhuja hṛdaya sa pārśve pṛṣṭanābhau ca rudre kaṭi udarakapāde sarvato maṃtra   
varṇān ||  
  
mūlena vyāpakaṃ nyāsaṃ navadhā kārayet priye |  
paṃcadhā navadhā vāpi mūlena saptadhā tathā ||  
  
tataḥ strīveṣadhārī syāt siṃdūrāṃkitabhālakaḥ |  
śṛṃgāro jvalaveśādya tāṃvūlapūritānanaḥ ||  
  
evaṃ veśādikaṃ sarvaṃ vanitāmapi kārayet |  
pīṭhanyāsastataḥ paścādādhāraśakti pūrvakaṃ ||  
  
prakṛtiṃ kajaṭhaṃ caiva śeṣaṃ pṛthvīṃ tathaiva ca |  
sudhāṃvudhiṃ maṇidvīpaṃ ciṃtāmaṇi gṛhaṃ tathā ||  
  
śmaśānaṃ pārijātaṃ ca tanmūle ratnavedikāṃ |  
tasyoparimaṇeḥ pīṭhaṃ nyaset sādhakapuṃgavaḥ ||  
  
caturdikṣu munīn devān śavāṃśca śavamuṇḍakān |  
dharmāṃdīścāpi dharmādīn pādagātra catuṣṭaye ||  
  
hṛdipadme tathā padmaṃ sūryasomau maheśvari |  
vaiśvānaraṃ tathā satvaṃ rajaścaivatamastathā ||  
  
ātmānaṃ caiva vinyasya śakti hṛtpadmake nyaset |  
icchājñāna kriyā caiva kāminī kāmadāyinī ||  
  
ratīratipriyānaṃdā karṇikāyā manonmanī |  
vāgbhavaṃ prathamaṃ coktvā parāyai tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
yai hyau& vācyamataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
sadāśiva mahāpreta ṅeṃtaṃ padmāsanaṃ tataḥ |  
nama ityeva maṃtroyaṃ pīṭha nyāsa udāhṛtaḥ ||  
  
pīṭhapūjāṃ tataḥ kuryāt pradhānaṃ tu svaśaktibhiḥ |  
ugrogra caṇḍā cāmuṇḍā pracaṇḍā vikaṭotkaṭā ||  
  
saṃkaṭā caiva caṇḍogrā tathā maṃgala caṇḍikā ||  
  
atrāṃtaryajanaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ dehamayepīṭhe ciṃtayediṣṭa devatāṃ ||  
  
atha vahiryāyaḥ ||  
  
evaṃ vinyastadehaḥ san yaṃtrarājaṃ samuddharet |  
tāmrapātre kapāle vā śmaśāna kāṣṭhanirmite ||  
  
p. 136a)  
  
śanibhaumadine cāpi śarīre mṛta saṃbhave |  
svarṇe rupye tathā lohe cakramarcyaṃ vidhānataḥ ||  
  
āsurekhe vajrarekhe hū& phaṭ vahnivallabhā |  
maṃtreṇānena vilikhedyaṃtrarājaṃ manoharaṃ ||  
  
svayaṃbhū kusumaṃ kudagolotthaṃ rocanā guruḥ |  
kaśmīra mṛganābhī ca padmaṃ ca malayodbhavaṃ ||  
  
esa gaṃdhaḥ samākhyātaḥ sarvadā caṇḍike priye |  
etena gaṃdhayogena yonicakraṃ samālikhet ||  
  
maṃtrabhedena śrīkālyāḥ yaṃtrāṇi saṃśṛṇu priye |  
ādau śaktiṃ samutpādya śaktīnāṃ tu catuṣṭayaṃ ||  
  
vāhyāvāhya krameṇaiva madhye viṃduṃ likhecchive |  
idaṃ vilikhya deveśi bhūpuraikena saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
kvacid bhūpuraśabdena caturasraṃ prakīrtitaṃ |  
atra bhūpuraśabdena caturdvārātmakaṃ bhavet ||  
  
trikoṇa trayamālikhya ṣaṭkoṇaṃ ca tatopari |  
vṛttāṣṭadalavṛttaṃ ca bhūpureṇa samanvitaṃ ||  
  
viṃdumadhye tu śrīmāyākālī yaṃtraṃ susiddhidaṃ ||  
  
maṃtramanya chṛṇu prājñe yonicakraṃ likhet sudhīḥ |  
yonidvayaṃ tatolikhya ṣaṭkoṇaṃ ca tato bhavet ||  
  
tataścāṣṭadalaṃ padmabhūgṛheṇa samanvitaṃ |  
yaṃtrametan maheśāni mahāsāmrājyadāyakaṃ ||  
  
ādau yoniṃ samālikhya yoniṃ ca tadvahirlikhet |  
yonitrayaṃ tadvahistu tato vṛttaṃ samālikhet ||  
  
tataścāṣṭadalaṃ padmavṛttaṃ caiva tatopari |  
dharaṇī gṛhamālikhya yaṃtrametanmayeritaṃ ||  
  
śaktimādyāṃ samutpādya tataḥ śaktidvayaṃ likhet |  
vahni śaktiṃ samutpādya vāhyaśaktiṃ vibhedayet ||  
  
graṃthibheda krameṇaiva vahniṃ prastārayedadhaḥ |  
agnibheda krameṇaiva śaktyūrddhaṃ cāpi bhedayet ||  
  
ūrddhvaṃ vahni vibhedena adhogniṃ ca vibhedayet |  
trayaṃ yone dvayaṃ vahneḥ kālīyaṃtraṃ susiddhidaṃ ||  
  
ṣaṭkoṇa vṛttāṣṭadalaṃ ṣaḍasraṃ vajralāṃchitaṃ |  
tadvahirbhūpuraṃ yaṃtramāvṛtti trayasaṃyutaṃ ||  
  
śaktyāgnibhyāṃ ca ṣaṭkoṇaṃ tatra yoni trayaṃ bhavet |  
vṛttamaṣṭadalaṃ padmaṃ bhū caturdvārabhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
yaṃtraṃ śrīdakṣiṇākālyāḥ madhye māyā vibhūṣitaṃ |  
maṃtrabhedena vījānāṃ nirṇayaḥ kathyate śṛṇu ||  
  
nādaviṃḍu yutaṃ cetsyāccicchaktiḥ parikīrtitā |  
virādvījaṃ krameṇaiva vījayaṃtre vibhāvayet ||  
  
p. 136b)  
  
pīṭhapūjāṃ tataḥ kuryādādhāraśaktipūrvakāṃ |  
tato hṛdaya padmāṃta sphuraṃtī vidyudā kṛtiṃ ||  
  
deveśītyādi maṃtreṇa viṃdvā vā vāhayet sudhīḥ |  
tataḥ kāmakalādhyānādā vāhyakālikāṃ śivāṃ ||  
  
kūrmākhya mudrayā puṣpaiścakramadhye nidhāpayet ||  
  
kāmakalā dhyānaṃ ||  
  
mukhaṃ viṃduvadākāraṃ tadadhaḥ kucayugmakaṃ |  
sarvavidyāmṛtāpurṇaṃ sarvarogo bhavapradaṃ ||  
  
sarvārthasādhakaṃ sarvajana raṃjanakārakaṃ |  
tadadhaḥ sa parārddhaṃ ca supariskṛtamaṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
sarvadevādi bhūtaṃ ca sarvadeva namaskṛtaṃ |  
sarvāhrādana saṃpūrṇaṃ sarvaraṃjanakārakaṃ ||  
  
sarvārthasādhakaṃ sarvaṃ devavaśya pravartakaṃ |  
etat kāmakalāṃ dhyānaṃ sugopyaṃ sādhakottamaiḥ ||  
  
kūrmamudrā yathā ||  
  
vāmahastātha tarjanyā dakṣiṇasya kaniṣṭhayā |  
tathā dakṣitarjanyā vāmāṃguṣṭhaṃ niyojayet ||  
  
unnataṃ dakṣiṇāṃguṣṭhaṃ vāmasya madhyamādikāḥ |  
aṃgulī yojayet pṛṣṭha dakṣiṇasya karasya ca ||  
  
vāmasya pitṛtīrthena madhyamānāmikā tathā |  
adhomukhe ca te kuryād dakṣiṇasya vahastataḥ ||  
  
evaṃ vidhaḥ sarvasiddhiṃ dadāti karakacchapaḥ |  
kuryā tu hṛdayāsannaṃ nimīlya nayanadvayaṃ ||  
  
samaṃkāya śirogrīvaṃ kṛtvā sthiratarovudhaḥ |  
dhyānaṃ samārabhen maṃtrī sarvapāpa pranāśanaṃ ||  
  
atha dhyānaṃ ||  
  
devyā dhyānamatho vakṣye sarvadevopaśobhitaṃ |  
aṃjanādinibhāṃ devīṃ karālavadanāṃ śivāṃ ||  
  
muṇḍamālā valīkīrṇāṃ muktakeśīṃ smitānanāṃ |  
mahākāla hṛdaṃbhoja sthitāṃ pīnapayodharāṃ ||  
  
viparītaratā saktā ghoradaṃṣṭrāṃ śivena vai |  
nāgayajñopavītaṃ ca caṃdrārddhakṛtaśekharāṃ ||  
  
sarvālaṃkārayuktāṃ ca muktāmaṇi vibhūṣitāṃ |  
mṛtahasta sahasraistu vaddhakāṃcī digaṃvarāṃ ||  
  
śivākoṭi sahasraistu yoginībhirvirājitāṃ |  
raktapūrṇamukhāṃbhojāṃ madyapāna pramattikāṃ ||  
  
vahnyarka śaśinetrāṃ ca raktavisphuritānanāṃ |  
vigatāsu kiśorābhyāṃ kṛtavarṇāvataṃsinīṃ ||  
  
karālavadanāṃ ghorāṃ muktakeśīṃ caturbhujāṃ |  
kālikāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ divyāṃ muṇḍamālāṃ vibhūṣiṇāṃ ||  
  
p. 137a)  
  
sadyaśchinnaḥ śiraḥ khaḍgavāmorddhādhaḥ karāṃvujāṃ |  
abhayaṃ varadaṃ caiva dakṣiṇādhorddhapāṇikāṃ ||  
  
mahāmeghaprabhāṃ śyāmāṃ tathaiva ca digaṃvarāṃ |  
kaṇṭhāvasamuṇḍālīgaladrudhiracarcitāṃ ||  
  
karṇāvataṃ satāṃ nīta śavayugma bhayānakāṃ |  
ghoradaṣṭrāṃ karālāsyāṃ pīnonnata payodharāṃ ||  
  
śavānāṃ karasaṃvyātaiḥ kṛtakāṃcī hasatmukhīṃ |  
sṛkkadvayagaladraktadhārā visphulitānanāṃ ||  
  
ghorarūpāṃ mahāraudrīṃ śmaśānālayavāsinīṃ |  
daṃturāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ divyāṃ muktalaṃvakacoccayāṃ ||  
  
śavarūpa mahādeva hṛdayo parisaṃsthitāṃ |  
śivābhirghoranādādiścaturdikṣu samanvitāṃ ||  
  
mahākālena ca samamupariṣṭaratāturāṃ |  
mukhaprasannanayanāṃ smerānana saroruhāṃ ||  
  
evaṃ saṃciṃtya kālīṃ tu śmaśānālayavāsinīṃ ||  
  
dhyātvā devī samāvāhya yonimudrāṃ ca darśayet |  
khaḍgamuṃḍavarābhīti mahāyoniṃ tu darśayet ||  
  
atha krameṇa khaḍgādi mudrāmāha ||  
  
kaniṣṭhānāmike vaddhvāsyāṃguṣṭhe naiva dakṣataḥ |  
śeṣāṃgulī tu prasṛte saṃspṛṣṭhe khaḍgamudrikāṃ ||  
  
aṃtarāṃguṣṭhamuṣṭhiṃ ca kṛtvā vāmakarasya ca |  
madhyamābhyāṃ dakṣiṇasya tathā laṃvya prayatnataḥ ||  
  
madhyame nātha tarjanyāmaṃguṣṭhāgrāgrimohya tu |  
dakṣiṇaṃ yojayet pāṇiṃ vāmamuṣṭau tu sādhakaḥ ||  
  
darśayed dakṣiṇebhāge muṇḍamudreyamucyate |  
adhaḥ sthito dakṣahastaḥ prasṛto varamudrikā ||  
  
ūrddhvaḥ kṛto vāmahastaḥ prasṛto'bhayamudrikā |  
tarjanyanāmikā madhye kaniṣṭhe cakramādapi ||  
  
karayoryojayeccaiva kaniṣṭhā mūlabhedataḥ |  
aṃguṣṭhāgraṃ tu niḥkṣipya mahāyoniḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
atha viśvasyo bhayātmakatvā chaktiṃ vinā śivasya śivaṃ   
vināśakteścopāsanāyāṃ phalābhāvādubhayoreka daivayajanamāha ||  
  
tathā ca ||  
  
prakṛtyā tu vinā devi na saṃsāraḥ kvacidbhavat |  
puruṣaṃ ca vinā devi na vidyā siddhidāyinī ||  
  
kālikāyāṃ mahākālaḥ suṃdaryāṃ laliteśvaraḥ |  
tārāyāṃ ca tathā kṣobhyaśchinnāyāṃ vikarālakaḥ ||  
  
p. 137b)  
  
bhuvanāyāṃ mahādevo dhūmrāyāṃ kālabhairavaḥ |  
nārāyaṇo mahālakṣmyāṃ bhairavyāṃ vaṭukaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
  
mātaṃgyāṃ tu mataṃgaḥ syādathavā syāt sadāśivaḥ |  
mṛtyuṃjayastu vagalā vidyāyāṃ parikīrtitaḥ ||  
  
tasmāt kāraṇato devī dvitīyaṃ pūjayecchive |  
mahākālaṃ yajet pūrvaṃ paścāddevīṃ prapūjayet ||  
  
mahākālaṃ yajeddevyā dakṣiṇe dhūmravarṇakaṃ |  
vibhrataṃ daṇḍaṣaṭkāṅga daṃṣṭrā bhīmamukhaṃ śiśuṃ ||  
  
vyāghracarmāvṛta kaṭiṃ tuṃdilaṃ raktavāsasaṃ |  
trinetra mūrddhakeśaṃ ca muṇḍamālā vibhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
jaṭābhāslasaccandra khaḍgamugraṃ jvalanniva |  
iti dhyātvā mahākāla maṃtreṇaiva ca prapūjayet ||  
  
kavacaṃ sphau& samuddhṛtya yālārāvāṃ cakrauṃ mataḥ |  
mahākāla bhairaveti sarvavighnāśayeti ca ||  
  
nāśayati punaḥ procya māyāṃ lakṣmīṃ samuddharet |  
phaṭ svāhayā samāyukto maṃtraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ ||  
  
tato deviṃ punarddhyātvā sarvopacārataḥ sudhī |  
pūjayet mūlamuccārya dakṣiṇāṃ kālikāṃvudhaḥ ||  
  
tāṃvūlāṃ te trisaṃtarpya natvā yoniṃ pradarśayet |  
devī vāmorddhādho haste khaḍgaṃ muṃḍaṃ ca pūjayet ||  
  
devyā dakṣahastorddhādhaḥ pūjayeda bhayaṃ varaṃ ||  
  
vijñāpya ca tato devyāḥ parivārāṃstathārcayet |  
tataḥ ṣaḍaṃga pūjāṃte gurupaktiṃ prapūjayet ||  
  
pādyādinā tathā paścāt pūjayedaṃgadevatā |  
sarvamaṃtreṣu purataḥ sarvatra siddhidāyakāḥ ||  
  
divyaughā guravodeva siddhaughā guravastathā |  
mānavaughāḥ samāsena kathayāmita vāgrataḥ ||  
  
tatrāsau kālikādevī tasyāḥ śṛṇu gurukramaṃ |  
mahādevī mahādeva stripurācaiva bhairavaḥ ||  
  
divyaughā guravaḥ proktāḥ siddhaughān kathayāmite |  
brahmānaṃdaśca pūrṇaśca calacittaścalācalaḥ ||  
  
kumāraḥ krodhanaścaiva varadaḥ smaradīpanaḥ |  
māyā māyāvatī caiva mānavaughān śṛṇu priye ||  
  
vimalaḥ kulaścaiva bhīmasenaḥ sudhākaraḥ |  
mīnā gorakṣanāthaśca bhojadevaḥ prajāpatiḥ ||  
  
mūladevoraṃtidevo vighneśo vai hutāśanaḥ |  
samayānaṃda saṃtoṣau kālikā guravaḥ smṛtāḥ ||  
  
p. 138a)  
  
divyā devītike nityaṃ siddhābhūmāvihāyi ca |  
mānavaughā mānaveṣu mamarūpadharāḥ sadā ||  
  
ānaṃdanātha śabdāṃtā guravaḥ sarvasiddhidā |  
striyopi gururūpāścedatvāṃtāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ||  
  
mānavaughāṃtike devī svaguruṃ paripūjayet |  
nijaṃ guruṃ purā dhyātvā tato guru catuṣṭayaṃ ||  
  
pūjayitvā yajeddevaṃ navasaṃkocamācaret |  
guruṃ paramaguruṃ caiva parāpara guruṃ tathā ||  
  
parameṣṭhī guruṃ caiva kathitā guravastava ||  
  
atha guruṇāṃ sthānamāha ||  
  
vidyā pṛṣṭhe maheśāni guravaḥ saṃti sarvadā |  
kalpā tripaṃktimārgeṇa devīpṛṣṭha krameṇa ca ||  
  
divyādi kramayogena tadadhaḥ svagurutrayaṃ |  
dakṣodīcyaḥ pratīcyāṃ ca rekhā tritayakaṃ caret ||  
  
divyaughā devatā pṛṣṭhe tadanyau tu sthale hṛdye |  
vidyāyāḥ bhedabhāge tu svaguruṃ pūjayecchive ||  
  
sarvatvayi maheśāni gurusthānaṃ prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
atha etasyāvaśyakatāmāha ||  
  
gurupūjāṃ vinā vatsadyadi pūjāṃ samārabhet |  
taddoṣaśamane vatsaśaktiṃ pūjāṃ samārabhet ||  
  
viguṇaṃ yatra yadvāsyāt saguṇaṃ kulapūjanāt |  
kulāvalokane caiva syātkva ca proktamārjanaṃ ||  
  
kva snānaṃ kva ca vākśuddhiḥ kva ca māsaviśodhanaṃ |  
dīkṣā prabhuḥ kulīnāścet kulaṃ vā vaṭukeśvaraḥ ||  
  
taddehe gurumānīya kularūpaṃ guruṃ smaret |  
kulaṃ yathā gurustatra na tathā kulasādhakaḥ ||  
  
gurukramaṃ ca kathitaṃ gopanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ |  
yagoragrena caivaiṣāṃ nāmagrāhyaṃ kathaṃcana ||  
  
athāvaraṇa devatāḥ paṃcadaśakoṇeṣu ||  
  
tathā ca ||  
  
tataśca sarvakoṇeṣu devīmāvāhya pūjayet ||  
  
tataḥ pūrvādi koṇeṣu vāmāvartena pūjayet ||  
  
kālī kapālinīṃ hullāṃ prathame tu trikoṇake |  
nīlāṃghanāṃ valākāṃ ca dvitīye tu trikoṇake ||  
  
kurukullā virodhinyau vipravittāṃ tṛtīyake |  
ugrāmugraprabhāṃ dīptāṃ caturthe tu trikoṇake ||  
  
mātrāṃ mudrāṃmitāṃ caiva trikoṇe paṃcamaṃ yajet |  
sarvāḥ śyāmā asikarāmuṇḍamālā vibhūṣaṇā ||  
  
p. 138b)  
  
tarjanī vāmahastena dhārayaṃtyaścasaṃmitāḥ |  
tristriḥ pūjāprakartavyā sarvāsāmapi sādhakaiḥ ||  
  
athāṣṭadale ||  
  
brahmādyāḥ pūjayet patre patrāgre bhairavān yajet |  
lokapālāṃ stato vāhye tadastrāṇi ca tadvahiḥ ||  
  
vahirmaṇḍalataścāpi brāhmī nārāyaṇī tathā |  
māheśvarī ca cāmuṇḍā kaumārī cāparājitā ||  
  
vārāhī ca tathā pūjyā nārasiṃhī tathaiva ca |  
tāraṃ pāśāṃ tathā śrī ca brāhmī śrīpādukāṃ tataḥ ||  
  
pūjayāmita taścaiva dhyāyettāṃ brahmaṇapriyāṃ |  
brahmāṇī haṃsamārūḍhāṃ svarṇavarṇāṃ caturbhujāṃ ||  
  
caturvaktrāṃ trinetrāṃ ca kūrcaṃ ca paṃkajaṃ tathā |  
daṇḍaṃ padmākṣa sūtraṃ ca dadhatīṃ cāruhāsinī ||  
  
jaṭājūṭadharāṃ devīṃ bhāvayet sādhakottamaḥ |  
evaṃ dhyātvā brahmapatnīṃ yathāśaktyāya yatpriye ||  
  
oṃ ismṛtvā nārāyaṇī śrīpādukāṃ tataḥ paraṃ |  
pujayāmīti coddhṛtya dhyāyettāṃ vaiṣṇavī priye ||  
  
nārāyaṇī mahādīptāṃ śyāmāṃ garuḍavāhinīṃ |  
nānālaṃkāra saṃyuktaṃ cārukeśīṃ caturbhujāṃ ||  
  
ghaṇṭhāṃ śaṃkhaṃ kapālaṃ ca cakraṃ saṃdadhatīṃ parāṃ |  
madhumattamadollola dṛṣṭiṃ sarvāṅgasuṃdarīṃ ||  
  
iti dyātvā maheśāni yatnato bhāvayettataḥ |  
pūjayitvā mahādevīṃ māheśvarīṃ yajet punaḥ ||  
  
saviṃduṃ uṃ samuccārya māheśvarīṃ tataḥ priye |  
śrīpādukāṃ tataścoktvā pūjayāmi tataḥ śiraḥ ||  
  
dhyānamasyāvarārohe vravīmite niśāmaya |  
māheśvarīṃ vṛṣārūḍhāṃ śuklāṃ trinayanānvitāṃ ||  
  
kapālaṃ ḍamaruṃ caiva varadā bhayaśūlakaṃ |  
ṭaṃkaṃ ca dadhatīṃ devīṃ nānābharaṇabhuṣitāṃ ||  
  
pūjayecca yathā śaktyā dhyānaṃ kṛtvā maheśvarīṃ ||  
  
ṛṃ vījaṃ cāmuṇḍā muktvā śrīpādukāṃ pūjayāmi |  
pūjayitvā mahādevīṃ tato dhyānaṃ samācaret ||  
  
cāmuṇḍo caṇḍahāsāṃ prakaṭita vadanāṃ bhīmavaktrāṃ trinetrāṃ   
nīlāṃbhojaprabhābhāṃ pramudita vapuṣaṃ nāramuṇḍāli mālāṃ |  
khaḍgaṃ śūlaṃ kapālaṃ naraśiraghaṭitaṃ kheṭakaṃ dhārayaṃtī pretārūḍhāṃ   
pramattāṃ madhumadamuditāṃ bhāvayeccaṃḍarūpāṃ ||  
  
p. 139a)  
  
evaṃ dhyātvā yajeddevīṃ cāmuṇḍāṃ jagadīśvarīṃ |  
ṛṃkāreṇa ca kaumārīṃ saṃpūjya dhyānamācaret ||  
  
kaumārīṃ kuṃkumā bhābhāṃ trinetrāṃ śikhi saṃsthitāṃ |  
caturbhujāṃ śaktipāśāṃmaṃkuśā bhayadāyinīṃ ||  
  
nānālaṃkāra saṃyuktāṃ pramattāṃ prariciṃtayet |  
dhyānaṃ kṛtvā kaumārīṃ ca yathā śaktyā prapūjayet ||  
  
vāgbhavena mahādevīṃ pūjayeda parājitāṃ |  
sarvaṃ pūrveṇa vidhinā tato dhyānaṃ samācaret ||  
  
aparājitāṃ ca pītāhāmakṣamudrā varapradāṃ |  
kamalaṃ mātuliṃgaṃ ca dadhatīṃ pariciṃtayet ||  
  
evaṃ saṃpūjya vidhivat sādhako bhaktito yajet |  
aukāreṇa sureśāni vārāhīṃ pūjayet tadā ||  
  
dhyānamasyānivodhatvaṃ vārāhyāḥ parameśvarī |  
vārāhī dhūmravarṇābhāṃ varāhavadanāṃ śubhāṃ ||  
  
phalakaṃ khaḍgamuśale phalaṃ vedabhujairvṛtāṃ |  
vidhinā pūjayedenāṃ vārāhīṃ parameśvarīṃ ||  
  
visargeṇa nārasiṃhīmarcayet sādhakāgraṇīḥ |  
nārasiṃhī nṛsiṃhasya vibhratī sadṛśaṃ vapuḥ ||  
  
dhyānamasyāḥ pravakṣyāmi devi te tanniśāmaya ||  
  
kopādālolajihvā vivṛta nijamukhāṃ somasūryāgni netrāṃ pādānāṃ   
vābhiraktāmupari hṛditāṃ bhinnadaityeṃdragātrīṃ |  
cakraṃ śaṃkhaṃ ca pāśāṃkuśakuliśagadāvāraṇānuddhṛhaṃtī bhīmāṃ   
tīkṣṇāgradaṃṣṭrāṃ maṇimayamukuṭāṃ nityamīḍe nṛsiṃhīṃ ||  
  
evaṃ dhyātvā pūjayettu yathā śaktyā maheśvarī ||  
  
athāṣṭadalāgre bhairavān bhairavaśca ||  
  
asitāṃ goruruścaṇḍaḥ krodha unmatta bhairavaḥ |  
kapālī bhīṣaṇaścaiva saṃhāraścāṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
  
athaiṣādhyānaṃ ||  
  
dathatāṃ janapuṃjanīlavarṇān varavetāla kapālaśūladaṇḍān |  
laghuduṃdubhi saṃyuktāṃ strinetrān karadaṃḍaiḥkari hastadaṇḍa caṇḍaiḥ ||  
  
gajakṛtti nivarttito turīyān bhrakuṭī saṃghaṭitairlalāṭapaṭṭaiḥ |  
lalitālikulābhakuṃtalāgrān muditāṃtaḥ karaṇān ca yauvanādyān ||  
  
eteṣāṃ maṃtro yathā ||  
  
hrasvārṇā viṃdusaṃyuktāṃ vāṅmāyā pūrvabhūṣitā ||  
  
p. 139b)  
  
atha bhairavāṇāṃ sthāne bhairavyaśca pūjyāḥ ||  
  
bhairavī ca mahāsiṃha dhūmrabhīmādikāṃ catāṃ |  
unmattabhairavīṃ paścād vaśīkaraṇa bhairavīṃ ||  
  
patrāgreṣu yajenmaṃtrī mohanākhyāṃ ca bhairavīṃ |  
tridhā tridhā yajedetā raktamālānu lepanaiḥ ||  
  
atha dhyānamāsāṃ ||  
  
udyadbhānu sahasrakāṃti maruṇakṣaumāṃ śiromālikāṃ raktālipta payodharāṃ   
japavaṭīṃ vidyāmabhītiṃvaraṃ |  
hastābjairdhatīṃ trinetra vilasadvaktrā raviṃdaśriyaṃ deviṃ vaddhahimāṃśu   
ratnamukuṭāṃ vaṃde samaṃdasmitāṃ ||  
  
atha bhūpurasyorddhe lokapālān pūjayet ||  
  
pūrvārabhya īśānāṃtaṃ dikpālān pūjayet sudhīḥ |  
indravījaṃ samuccārya iṃdrāya tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
surādhipataye coktvā sāṃgāya tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
saparivārāya ca tataḥ sāyudhā yata topyanu ||  
  
sa vāhanāya ca tato namaste na prapūjayet ||  
  
la& ra& ya& kṣa& va& ya& śa& ha& a& ka& evaṃ svasva vījādīnāṃ   
dikpālān pūjayet ||  
  
dhyānaṃ tu ||  
  
indraṃ surādhipaṃ pītamairāvatagataṃ vibhuṃ |  
sahasranetraṃ dvibhujaṃ pītaṃ vajradharaṃ bhaje ||  
  
agniṃ tejodhipaṃ raktaṃ śvetaśaktikaraṃ prabhuṃ |  
subhūṣaṇaṃ meṣavāhaṃ vaṃde raktāṃtalocanaṃ ||  
  
yamaṃ pretādhipaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ mahiṣo parisaṃsthitaṃ |  
kāladaṇḍadharaṃ krūraṃ vṛttaṃ dūtairbhayānakaiḥ ||  
  
rakṣodhipaṃ ca nir-ṛtaṃ śavāsanamāsthitaṃ |  
dhūmābhaṃ khaḍgahastaṃ ca piṃgaśmaśruḥ sukūrcakaṃ ||  
  
makare saṃsthitaṃ vidyunnibhapāśakarāṃvujaṃ |  
śubhrāṃgatuṃ dilaṃ vaṃde varuṇaṃ yādasāṃpatiṃ ||  
  
vāyuprāṇādhipaṃ dhūmraṃ raktāṃ kuśakaraṃ paraṃ |  
vātapramī samārūḍhaṃ dhyāvaṃte vegato bhaje ||  
  
yakṣapatiṃ kuveraṃ ca śuklaṃ śūlagadādharaṃ |  
narasiṃhāsanārūḍhaṃ medalaṃ citriṇī yutaṃ ||  
  
vidyādhipaṃ nīlaśūladharaṃ vṛṣabhavāhanaṃ |  
trinetraṃ bhālacaṃdraṃ ca jaṭājūṭadharaṃsitaṃ ||  
  
gauraṃ nāgādhipaṃ mūrddhni phaṇāmaṃḍalabhūṣitaṃ |  
pīnottuṃgaṃ cakradharamanaṃtaṃ visagaṃ bhaje ||  
  
lokādhipaṃ vidhātāraṃ raktaṃ padmakaraṃ śubhaṃ |  
haṃsārūḍhaṃ vedapāṭhaṃ kurvaṃtaṃtamahaṃbhaje ||  
  
tathā ||  
  
p. 140a)  
  
indrokta vidhinā sarvaṃ pūjayet parameśvarī |  
rakṣo varuṇayormadhye śeṣanāgaṃ prapūjayet ||  
  
īśāna śakrayormadhye brahmāṇaṃ pūjayet tataḥ ||  
  
atha lokapālānāṃ mudrā yathā ||  
  
pāṇimūlesu saṃlagne śākhāḥ sarvāḥ prasāritāḥ |  
lokeśānāmiyaṃ mudrā teṣāmarcā sudarśayet ||  
  
atha bhūpurasya vahirdikpālāstrāṇi ||  
  
tadvahirarcaye devi vajraṃ śaktiṃ ca daṇḍakaṃ |  
khaḍgaṃ pāśamaṃkuśaṃ ca gadāṃ triśūlameva ca ||  
  
kuvaro varuṇayormadhye cakraṃ pūjyaṃ tathaiva ca |  
īśānaśakrayormadhye padmaṃ saṃpūjayet tataḥ ||  
  
atha viśeṣābhāve sādhāraṇa maṃtramāha parivārāṇāṃ ||  
  
nāmādya varṇavījāśca ṅeṃtāstāstu namoṃtikāḥ |  
śrīpadaṃ pūrvamuddhṛtya pādukā padamuddharet ||  
  
pūjayāmi namaḥ paścāt pūjayedṅgadevatāḥ |  
tataḥ pūrvokta rūpāṃ tu dhāyaiccaiva hi dakṣiṇāṃ ||  
  
yoginī cakrasahitāṃ mahākāla samanvitāṃ ||  
  
devyāstu dakṣiṇebhāge mahākālaṃ punaryajet |  
pādyābhirmūladevīṃ saṃpūjya tarpayet tataḥ ||  
  
tato devyairdhūpadīpaudadyānnai vedyakaṃ tathā |  
puṣpāṃjali trayaṃ bhaktyā viśeṣārghyodakākṣataiḥ ||  
  
devī vāmorddhādhohaste khaḍgaṃ muṇḍaṃ ca pūjayet |  
devyādakṣahastorddhādhaḥ pūjayeda bhayaṃ varaṃ ||  
  
punarmūlaṃ samuccārya sāṃgāyai sa pareti ca |  
vārāyai nāmadevyāśca caturthyaṃtamudīrayet ||  
  
atha validānaṃ ||  
  
pūjāṃte bhojanādau ca valiṃdadyān maheśvari ||  
  
tatrādau mahākāla validānaṃ tasya maṃtro yathā ||  
  
humaṃte ca mahākālāchmaśānādhipa ityapi |  
imamaṃte sāmiṣānnaṃ valiṃ gṛhnayugaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
gṛhnāpaya padadvaṃdvaṃ vighnanivāraṇaṃ tataḥ |  
kuru siddhiṃ ca me caiva prayaccha svāhayāyutaḥ ||  
  
mahākālāya devāya praṇavādyena dāpayet ||  
  
atha devyā validānaṃ maṃtropi ||  
  
ehyehi jagatāṃ mātarjagatāṃ jananī tathā |  
gṛhna gṛhna imaṃ nityaṃ validāna mataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
siddhiṃ dehi padadvaṃdva tataḥ śatrukṣayaṃ kuru |  
vāyuśabdaṃ samuccārya kūrcayugmaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ||  
  
hṛllekhā dvitayaṃ pūrvamaṃte ca ṭhadvayaṃ punaḥ |  
tadā maṃtra samuddhṛtya phaḍaṃte vahni suṃdarī ||  
  
p. 140b)  
  
validānamidaṃ citraṃ sarvataṃtreṣu gopitaṃ |  
sarvāsu kālī vidyā su yathā nāmnā kṣipedvaliṃ ||  
  
valibhiḥ sādhyate muktirvalibhiḥ sādhyate divaṃ |  
validānena sa tataṃ japecchattra nṛpānnṛpaḥ ||  
  
evaṃ pūjāṃ purā kṛtvā mūle naiva yathā vidhiḥ |  
naivedyādi yathāśaktyā dadyāddaivyai punaḥ punaḥ ||  
  
tato nīrājanaṃ kuryāddaśavāraṃ pradīpakaiḥ |  
tataḥ samāhitaṃ maṃtrī guruṃ natvā śiraḥ sthitaṃ ||  
  
mahākāla mahāmaṃtraṃ japedaṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ ||  
  
śrī-īśvara uvāca ||  
  
kullukāṃ mūrddhni saṃciṃtya hṛdi setuṃ viciṃtayet |  
mahāsetuṃ viśuddhau ca sahasrāre samuddharet ||  
  
maṇipūre tu nirvāṇaṃ mahākuṇḍalinīmataḥ |  
svādhiṣṭhāne kamarājaṃ kākinī mūrddhni saṃsthitāṃ ||  
  
viciṃtya vidhivaddevī mūlādhārāṃtikācchire |  
viśuddhāṃtaṃ smareddevī visataṃtu tanīyasīṃ ||  
  
vedasthānādvijihvāṃtaṃ mūlamaṃtrā vṛtāṃ vibhuḥ ||  
  
atha dīpanī vidyā ||  
  
kāṃtāṃ taṃ jīvanīvījaṃ tripado paribhūṣitaṃ |  
kalāmanusvaropetaṃ vījatrayamudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
tuṃvuruṃ ca tato dadyāt saṃhāraṃ ca tataḥ paraṃ |  
vidyādau yojayeddevī viṃdutraya kalānvitaṃ ||  
  
eṣā tu dīpanī vidyā sarvāmnāyai namaskṛtā |  
tatprabhāpaṭahairjihvāṃ pradīptāṃ ca vibhāvayet ||  
  
ajñātvā dīpanīṃ vidyāṃ yojayet kālikāṃ parāṃ |  
socirānmṛtyumāpnoti mṛte ca narakaṃ vrajet ||  
  
atha maṃtra dhyānam ||  
  
maṃtra dhyānaṃ pravakṣyāmi japāt sārvajñadāyakaṃ |  
maṃtradhyānānmaheśāni siddhyate brahmayataḥ ||  
  
mūlādi brahmaraṃdhrāṃtaṃ sarvāṃ vidyāṃ vibhāvayet |  
sūryakoṭi pratīkāśāṃ yogibhirdṛṣṭa pūrvikāṃ ||  
  
devatā gurumaṃtrāṇāmaikyaṃ saṃbhāvayan dhiyā |  
sa vāsanāṃ japenmaṃtraṃ saṃtuṣṭaḥ sthiramānasaḥ ||  
  
daṃtākṣamālayā caiva rājadaṃte nameruṇā |  
mūlamaṃtreṇātha pūrvanyāsān sarvān samācaret ||  
  
aṣṭottara sahasraṃ tu tadarddhaṃ tridaśaṃ tu vā |  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ vāpi japennitya mananyadhīḥ ||  
  
tejomayaṃ japaphalaṃ devyā haste samarpayet |  
stuvanpradakṣiṇīkṛtya daṇḍavat praṇamedbhuvi ||  
  
p. 141a)  
  
śrījagalanmaṃgalaṃnāma kavacaṃ prapaṭhestataḥ ||  
  
atha dakṣiṇaṃ ||  
  
tato vai śirasi puṣpaṃ datvāṣṭāṃgaṃ praṇamya ca |  
prasāryaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ svayaṃ namrānanaṃ punaḥ ||  
  
darśayed dakṣiṇaṃ pārśvaṃ manasāpi pradakṣiṇaṃ |  
tridhā ca veṣṭayet samyak kālikāyāḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ ||  
  
sa ca pradakṣiṇo jñeyaḥ sarvadevaugha tuṣṭidaḥ |  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ yastu kālikāyāḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ ||  
  
sarvān kāmānavāpnoti paścān mokṣamavāpnuyāt |  
tathaiva manasā proktaṃ vācikaṃ kāyikaṃ tathā ||  
  
sakalaṃ pūrvavat kāryaṃ vāmadakṣiṇabhedataḥ |  
ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ kathitaḥ sāmānyaṃ pūrvamīritaṃ ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau śrīdakṣiṇakālikāyāḥ nityārcananirṇayo   
nāmaikaviṃśatitamaḥ prakāśaḥ || 21 ||  
atha karpūrastavamāha ||  
  
karpūraṃ madhyamāṃtāḥ svarapararahitaṃ seṃduvāmākṣiyuktaṃ vījaṃ te   
vāmātaretattripuraharavadhūtriḥ kṛtaṃ ye japaṃti |  
teṣāṃ gadyāni padyānijamukhakuharādullasaṃtyeva vācaḥ svacchaṃdaṃ   
dhvāṃtadhārādhararucirucire sarvasiddhiṃgatānāṃ ||  
  
īśānaḥ seṃduvāmaśravaṇa parigato vījamanmanmaheśi dvandvāṃte maṃdacetā   
yadi japati janovāramekaṃ kadācit |  
jitvā vācāmadhīśaṃ dhanadamapi ciraṃ mohayannamvujākṣī vṛndaṃ   
caṃdrārddhacūḍe prabhavati samamahāghorarāvāvataṃse ||  
  
īśo vaiśvānarasthaḥ śaśadharavilasadvāmanetreṇayukto vījaṃte   
dvaṃdvamanyadvigalita cikure kālike ye japaṃti |  
dveṣṭāraṃdhraṃtite ca tribhuvanamapitevaśyabhāvaṃ nayaṃti sṛkkadvaṃdvā   
pradhārādvayadharavadane dakṣiṇe tryakṣare ca ||  
  
ūrddhvaṃ vāme kṛpāṇe karakamalatale chinnamuṇḍaṃ tatodhaḥ savyebhītiṃ   
varaṃ ca trijagadyaphaledakṣiṇe kālike ca |  
japtvaitaṃ vāmaye vā tava manu vibhavaṃ bhāvayattastadarthaṃ   
teṣāmaṣṭaukarasthāḥ prakaṭitaradane siddhayastryamvakasya ||  
  
vargādyaṃ vahniyuktaṃ vidhurati lalitaṃ taṃtrayaṃ kūrcayugmaṃ lajjādvaṃdvaṃ   
ca paścāt smitamukhaṃ tadadhaṣṭhadvayaṃ yojayitvā |  
mātaryeye japaṃti smaraharamakhile bhāvayaṃtaḥ svarūpaṃte lakṣmīlākṣya   
līlākamaladaladṛśaḥ kāmarūpā bhavaṃti ||  
  
p. 141b)  
  
pratyekaṃ vā dvayaṃ vā trayamapi ca paraṃ vījamatyaṃtaguptaṃ tvannāmnā   
yojayitvā sakalamapi sadābhāvayaṃtojapaṃti |  
teṣāṃ netrā raviṃ devi rahati kamalāvaktra śubhrāṃ śuvimva vāgdevī   
devimuṇḍasragatiśayalasat kaṃṭhapīnastanāḍhye ||  
  
gatāsūnāṃ vāhu prakarakṛta kāṃcī parilasannitaṃ vāṃ digvastrāṃ tribhuvana   
vidhātriṃ trinayanāṃ |  
śmaśānasthetalyeseva hṛdi mahākālasurataḥ prasaktāṃ tvāṃ dhyāyet janani   
jaḍacetā api kaviḥ ||  
  
śivābhirghorābhiḥ śavanivahamuṇḍāsthinivahaiḥ paraṃ saṃkīrṇāyāṃ prakaṭita   
citāyāṃ haravadhuṃ |  
praviṣṭāṃ saṃtuṣṭāmuparisuratenāti yuvatīṃ sadātvāṃ dhyāyaṃtī kvacidapi na   
teṣāṃ paribhavaḥ ||  
  
vadāmaḥ kiṃvātvāṃ jananivayamuccairjaḍadhiyona dhātānāpīśona harirapite   
vetti paramaṃ |  
tathāpi tvadbhaktirmukharayati cāsmākamasi te tadetatkṣaṃtavyaṃ na khalu   
paśuṃrosaḥ samucitaḥ ||  
  
samaṃtādāpīnastanajaghanadhṛk yauvanavatīratāsakto naktaṃ yadi japati   
bhaktastava manuṃ |  
picāsāstvāṃ dhyāyan galitacikurastasya vaśagāḥ samastāḥ siddhaughā   
bhuvicirataraṃ jīvati kaviḥ ||  
  
samāḥ svasthī bhūtāṃ japati viparītāṃ yadi sadā viciṃtyatvāṃ dhyāyannatiśaya   
mahākālasuratāṃ |  
tadā tasya kṣoṇīṃtala virahamāṇasya viduṣaḥ karāṃbhoje vaśyā haravadhū   
mahāsiddhinivahāḥ ||  
  
prasūteḥ saṃsāraṃ janani bhavatī pālayati yatsamastaṃ kṣityādi pralayasamaye   
saṃharati ca |  
atastvāṃdhātāpi tribhuvanapatiḥ śrīpatiraho maheśopi prāyaḥ sakalamapi   
saṃstauti bhavatīṃ ||  
  
anekāḥ sevaṃte bhavadadhika gīrvāṇani vahān vimūḍhāste mātaḥ kimapi na hi   
jānaṃti paramaṃ ||  
  
samārādhyāmādyāṃ hariharaviriṃcyādi vivudhaiḥ |  
prapannosmi svairaṃratirasa mahānaṃdaniratāṃ ||  
  
dharitrī kīlālaṃ śucirapi samīropi gagaṇaṃ tvamekā kalyāṇī giriśaramaṇīkāli   
sakalaṃ |  
stutiḥ kātemātastavacaraṇayormāmagatikaṃ prasannāstvaṃ   
bhūyādbhavamanurabhūyānmamajanuḥ ||  
  
p. 142a)  
  
śmaśānasthaḥ susthogalita cikurodik paṭadharaḥ sahasraṃ tvarkāṇāṃ   
nijagalitavīryeṇa kusumaṃ |  
japan tvat pratyekaṃ manumapi vidhvāna nirato mahāsālikhairaṃ sa bhavati dharitrī   
paridṛkaḥ ||   
  
gṛhe saṃmārjanyā parigalita vīrya hi cikuraṃ samūlaṃ madhyāhne   
vitaranicitāyāṃkuja dine |  
samuccāra prekṣṇāyanumapi sakṛt kāli sa tataṃ gajāruḍho yāti kṣiti parivṛtaḥ   
satkavivaraḥ ||  
  
svapuṣpairākīrṇaṃ kusumadhanuṣo maṃdiramahāpurodhyāyan yadi japati   
bhaktastava manuṃ |  
sa gaṃdharvaḥ śreṇaīpatiriva kavitvā mṛtanadī nadīnaḥ paryaṃtaṃ   
paramapadalīnaḥ prabhavati ||  
  
tripaṃcāre pīṭhe śavaśivahṛdismesvadanāṃ mahākālenoccairmadana   
rasalāvaṇyaniratāṃ |  
samāyukto naktaṃ svayamapiratānaṃdaniratājanoyodhyāyetvāṃ jananikilasasyāt   
smaraharaḥ ||  
  
sa lomāsthisvairaṃ palalamapi mārjāramapi vā paraṃ mauṣaṃ meṣaṃ   
naramahiṣayośchāgamapi vā |  
valiṃ te pūjāyāṃ mayi viralavaktre vitaraṃtāṃ na kiṃ siddhiḥ sarvāprati   
padamapūrvā prabhavati ||  
  
vaśīlakṣaṃ maṃtraṃ japati haviṣyāśanarato divāmātaryuṣmaccaraṇa   
kamaladhyānanirataḥ |  
paraṃ nakto nagno nidhuvana vinodena ca manuṃjanorlakṣaṃ samyak parahara   
samānaḥ kṣititale ||  
  
idaṃ stotraṃ mātastava manusamuddhāraṇa japasvarūpākhyaṃ pādāṃvuja yugala   
pūjāvidhiyutaṃ |  
niśārddhaṃ vā pūjāsamayamadhivāyastu paṭhati pralāpastasyāpi prasarati   
kavisvāmṛtarasaḥ ||  
  
kuraṃgākṣī vṛṃdaṃta manusarati premataralaṃ vaśastasya kṣoṇīpatirapi kuvera   
pratinidhiḥ |  
ripuḥ kārāgāraṃ kalayati ca tatkeli kalayā ciraṃjīvanmuktaṃ prabhavati subhaktaḥ   
pratijaniḥ ||  
  
iti śrīmahākālakṛtaṃ karpūrastotraṃ samāptaṃ ||  
  
athāsyapuraścaraṇam ||  
  
kapūrākhyamidaṃ stotraṃ yaduktaṃ bhavatā purā |  
ṣaṭkarmasādhanaṃ tasya prayogaṃ vada śaṃkara ||  
  
śrīśiva uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi karpūrastavasādhanaṃ |  
sakṛt kṛtepi deveśi kālī tuṣṭā bhavet sadā ||  
  
p. 142b)  
  
śanibhaumadine devi snātvā prayatamānasaḥ |  
saṃpūjya kālikāṃ devīṃ saṃkalpaṃ samyagā caret ||  
  
kṛtvā ṣoḍhādikaṃ devi paṭhet stotra manuttamaṃ |  
ayutaika pramāṇena taddaśāṃśaṃ hunet sudhīḥ ||  
  
tarpaṇaṃ cābhiṣekaṃ ca brāhmaṇān bhojayet tataḥ |  
paścāt svakārya siddhyarthaṃ prayogānā care tadā ||  
  
prayogamātre deveśi aṣṭottara sahasrakaṃ |  
yojayet sarvakāryārthaṃ kāmanābhedabhāvitaḥ ||  
  
ākarṣaṇe vaśīkāre māraṇoccāṭane tathā |  
rājño bhaye samutpanne durbhikṣe śatrusaṃkaṭe ||  
  
trāsotpanne maheśāni rogaśoka bhaye tathā |  
paṭhet stotraṃ mahākālyāḥ sarvaśāṃtiṃ prayacchati ||  
  
kumārī pūjanaṃ cāṃte kartavyaṃ susamāhitaḥ |  
evaṃ kṛte maheśāni samyak siddhirbhavaddhruvam ||  
  
atha jaganmaṃgalakavacaṃ ||  
  
bhairavyuvāca ||  
  
kālīpūjā śrutānātha vidyāśca vividhāḥ prabho |  
idānīṃ śrotumicchāmi kavacaṃ pūrvasūcitaṃ ||  
  
tvameva śaraṇaṃ nātha trāhimāṃ duḥkhasaṃkaṭāt ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca |  
  
rahasyaṃ śṛṇu vakṣyāmi bhairava prāṇavallabhe |  
śrījaganmaṃgalaṃ nāmakavacaṃ maṃtravigrahaṃ ||  
  
paṭhitvā dhārayitvā ca trailokyaṃ mohayet kṣaṇāt |  
nārāyaṇopiya kṛtvā nārī bhūtvā maheśvaraṃ ||  
  
yogaḥ saṃkṣobhamanayadyaddhṛtvā ca raghūdvahaḥ |  
varadṛptān jaghāneva rāvaṇādīn niśācarān ||  
  
yasya prasādādīśopi trailokyavijayī vibhuḥ |  
dhanādhipaḥ kuveropi sureśo bhucchavīpatiḥ ||  
  
evaṃ hi sa kalā devāḥ sarvasiddhīśvarāḥ priye |  
śrījaganmaṃgalasyāsya kavacasya ṛṣiḥ śivaḥ ||  
  
chaṃdonuṣṭup devatā ca kālikā dakṣiṇeritāḥ |  
jagatāṃ mohaneṃ duṣṭavijaye bhuktimuktiṣu ||  
  
yoṣidākarṣaṇe caiva viniyogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |  
śiro me kālikāpātu krīṃkāraikākṣarīparā ||  
  
krī& krī& krī& me lalāṭaṃ ca kālikā khaḍgadhāriṇī |  
hū& hū& pātu netrayugmaṃ hrī& hrī& pātu śrutī mama ||  
  
p. 143a)
