yaṃtraṃ likhitvādhiṣṭhāya puṣpaśodhanamācaret ||  
  
mṛdvāsanaṃ samāsādya māyāṃ pūrvadale lihket ||  
  
athaiṣāṃ krameṇa maṃtrāmāha ||  
  
praṇavo vahnijāyāṃto manuraṃbha parigrahe ||  
  
tāro vajrodake hū& phaṭ svāhā jalamadhiṣṭhitaṃ |  
tāraṃ lajjā viśuddhāṃte sarve pāpāni caiva hi ||  
  
samayāṃte aśeṣāṃte vikalpa padamuddharet |  
apanayāṃte varma phaṭ svāhā pāda viśuddhayet ||  
  
oṃ māyā vahnijāyā ca smṛta ācamane manuḥ |  
praṇavaṃ maṇidharaṇīni vajriṇī sarvaśabdataḥ ||  
  
vaśaṃkarīti hū& phaṭ svāheti vaṃdhayecchikhāṃ |  
tāraṃ munipadaṃ caiva dharaṇyaṃte ca vajriṇī ||  
  
mahāpratisare rakṣadvaṃdvāṃte māṃ tataśca hū& |  
phaṭ svāhā manunānena rakṣāṃ graṃthiṃ ca kārayet ||  
  
phaḍābhyukṣya hṛdāpūjyā tāreṇa daśamaṃtrayet |  
phaṭkāraiḥ prokṣayeddhāraṃ gaṃdhapuṣpaiḥ prapūjayet ||  
  
dvārorddhagāṃ gaṇeśaṃ ca vāme vāṃ vaṭukaṃ tathā |  
daśamekṣāṃ kṣetrapālamadhoyāṃ yoginīṃ yajet ||  
  
athaiṣāṃ maṃtre viśeṣaśca sarvāte dhruvadīrghāḍhyā ||  
  
śaktivījapuraḥsaraḥ caturthyaṃtā namoṃtāścanāmādya vījasaṃyutāḥ ||  
  
bhūtaśuddhiṃ na vārṇena tataḥ kūrvīta sādhakaḥ ||  
  
oṃ rakṣarakṣa hū& cāstraṃ svāhā maṃtro navākṣaraḥ |  
trayodaśārṇa maṃtreṇa vighnānutsārayet tataḥ ||  
  
oṃ dāraya dāraya hū& phaṭ svāhā vighnadāraṇaṃ ||  
  
oṃ sarvavighnānutsāraya hū& phaṭ vahni gehinī |  
trayodaśārṇakomaṃtraḥ pārṣṇighātena vighnahā ||  
  
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuddhṛtya āḥkāraṃ tadanaṃtaram |  
hū& phaṭ svāhā manuḥ proktaḥ kāyavāk cittaśodhane ||  
  
tatastu devyāḥ pūjārthaṃ maṃtrayet kāśyapīṃ dhruvaṃ |  
pavitra vajra me hū& svāhā maṃtro bhavākṣaraḥ ||  
  
bhūmau trikoṇamālikhyādhāraśaktiḥ prapūjanaṃ |  
māyāvījaṃ samuccārya ādhāraśaktaye tataḥ ||  
  
p. 169a)  
  
kamalāsanamālikhya ṅenamoṃtaśca pūjayet |  
āḥkārāṃte surekhe ca vajrarekhe tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
hū& phaṭ svāheti kuryāsu maṇḍalaṃ vai śavāsane |  
tatra mṛdvāsanaṃ devi pīṭhamaṃtreṇa pūjayet ||  
  
oṃ aiṃ klīṃ kāmapīṭhāya hṛdayāṃ toyamīritaṃ |  
tatra vadhvāsanaṃ vīra ātmānaṃ śodhayet tataḥ ||  
  
caturdaśārṇa manunā kusumāni suśodhayet |  
yathā gatābhiṣeketi samāśrime padaṃ vadet ||  
  
tārādi hū& phaṭ svāhāṃto manukto manuvarṇakaḥ |  
śyāmāvada paraṃ jñeyaṃ puṣpaśodhanakaṃ vudhaḥ ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi bhūtaśuddhiṃ viśeṣataḥ |  
hrī& vījaṃ tu javāpuṣpaṃ nibhaṃ nābhau viciṃtayet ||  
  
tadutthenāgninā dehaṃ dahetsārddhaṃ svayāpmanā |  
strīṃ vījaṃ tu suvarṇābhaṃ ciṃtayeddhṛdi maṃtravit ||  
  
pavanena tadutthena pāpabhasma kṣipedbhuvi |  
hū& vījamiṃdukaṃdābhaṃ bhāle dhyāyecca bhāvataḥ ||  
  
taduttha sudhayā dehaṃ vacayeddevatānibhaṃ |  
anayā bhūtaśuddhyā tu devī sādṛśyamāpnuyāt ||  
  
athāsyā dhyānaṃ ||  
  
bhūtaśuddhiṃ vidhāyetthaṃ śūnyaṃ viśvaṃ viciṃtayet |  
nirlepaṃ nirmalaṃ sūkṣmamātmānaṃ devatāmayaṃ ||  
  
aṃtarīkṣe tato dhyāyedāḥkārād raktapaṃkajaṃ |  
bhūyastasyopari dhyāyeddāṃ kārācchuklapaṃkajaṃ ||  
  
tasyopari tato dhyāyet hū&kāraṃ nīlasaṃnilaṃ |  
tasyopari tato dhyāyet kartṛkāṃ vījabhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
tasyopari mahādevīṃ kharvāṃnīla ghanaprabhāṃ |  
laṃvodarīṃ vyāghracarma samāvṛta nitaṃvinīṃ ||  
  
pīnonnata payobhārāṃ raktavartula locanaṃ |  
piṃgākṣaika jaṭāṃ nīlanāga yajño vibhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
kalotpalalasanmaulīvaddhajūṭāṃ bhayaṃkarīṃ |  
śvetāsthipaṭṭikāyukta kapālaṃ paṃcaśobhitāṃ ||  
  
lalāṭe raktanāgena kṛta karṇāvataṃsinīṃ |  
atiśubhramahānāga kṛtahāra mahojjvalaṃ ||  
  
dūrvādalaśyāmanāgakṛta yajñopavītinīṃ |  
caturbhujāṃ raktamāṃsa khaṃḍamuṇitamuṣṭinā ||  
  
jaṭājūṭena sūtreṇa śobhitāṃ tīkṣṇadhārayā |  
khaḍgena dakṣiṇasyorddhaṃ śobhitāṃ vīranādinīṃ ||  
  
tadadhastādvījarūpa kartṛkālaṃ kṛtāṃ parāṃ |  
vāmārddhe raktanālenavika svaramanoharaṃ ||  
  
p. 169b)  
  
dadhatīṃ nīlapadmaṃ ca tadadhastvāt kapālajaṃ |  
jagatāṃ jāḍyasaṃyuktaṃ dadhatīṃ kuṇḍasannibhāṃ ||  
  
dhūmrābha nāgasaṃdohakṛta keyūra sadbhujāṃ |  
suvarṇa varṇanāgaṃ ca kaṃkaṇo jvalapāṇikāṃ ||  
  
śubhravarṇa mahādeva śavahṛdi samāsanāṃ |  
niryaṃtreṇābhiyā tadvat saṃkoca prapadāṃcalāṃ ||  
  
śavapādahṛyārūḍha vāmapādāṃ hasanmukhīṃ |  
kuṃdābhanāgasaṃśobhi kaṭisūtrāṃ trilocanāṃ ||  
  
īṣadraktena nāgena kṛta nūpura pallavāṃ |  
sadyaśchinnagaladrakta nṛmuṇḍairātmabhūṣaṇaiḥ ||  
  
anyonya keśa grathitaiḥ pādapadma pralaṃvitaiḥ |  
paṃcāśadbhirmahāmālā śobhitāṃ parameśvarīṃ ||  
  
jvalaccitāṃ madhyagatāṃ dvīpi carmottarāṃśukāṃ |  
lākṣābhanāgasaṃvaddha jaṭājūṭāṃ varapradāṃ ||  
  
sāvaiśasmeravadanāṃ lalajihvāṃ varapradāṃ |  
eva dhyātvā paṇḍitohaṃ bhāvayecca mahākaviḥ ||  
  
atha dhyāna rahasyamāha ||  
  
vaśyārthe nīlavarṇā bhāmā kṛṣṭau pītarūpiṇīṃ |  
māraṇoccāṭane dhūmrī kṛṣṇā tu tadapekṣayā ||  
  
ciṃtayet parameśānīṃ dhyātvā preta kṛtāsanāṃ ||  
  
atha maṃtrā ca manamāhā ||  
  
bhūtaśuddhiṃ purā kṛtvā divyamācamanaṃ caret |  
tārābhedaistribhiḥ pītvā māyayā kṣālayetkaraṃ ||  
  
strī& hū& oṣṭaudvirunmṛjya phaṭkāraiḥ kṣālayet karaṃ |  
āsyanāthe kṣaṇaśrotra nābhivakṣaḥ śiro bhujān ||  
  
vairocanādibhiḥ spṛṣṭvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate |  
ācamya bhairavo bhūtvāvatsarāttāṃ prapaśyati ||  
  
atha bhūtaśuddheranaṃtaraṃ kramamāha ||  
  
bhūtaśuddhiṃ vidhāyetthamarghyādi sthāpanaṃ caret |  
prāṇāyāmaṃ tataḥ kuryādṛṣyādinyā samācaret ||  
  
nyāsaiḥ karāṃgayoḥ kuryādātmānaṃ tāriṇīṃ smaret ||  
  
atha āsāmānyārghya sthāpanamāha ||  
  
tataścā camanaṃ kṛtvā sāmānyārghyaṃ prakalpayet |  
trikoṇavṛtta bhūviṃva maṇḍalaṃ racayet tataḥ ||  
  
sādhāraśaktiṃ saṃpūjya tatrādhāraṃ viniḥkṣipet |  
astreṇa pātraṃ saṃśodhya hṛnmaṃtreṇa prapūrayet ||  
  
p. 170a)  
  
niḥkṣipettīrthamāvāhya gaṃdhādīn praṇavena ca |  
darśayeddhenumudrāṃ vai sāmānyārghya vidhirmataḥ ||  
  
nyāsaṃ pravartate devī ṣoḍhānyāsa puraḥsaraṃ ||  
  
athāsyā mahāṣoḍhāmāha ||  
  
tārā ṣoḍhāṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvataṃtreṣu gopitaṃ |  
sarvavighnopaśamanīṃ sarvapāpa vināśinīṃ ||  
  
mahādāridryaśamanīṃ sarvasampratpradāyinīṃ |  
sarvakāmapradāṃ nityāṃ sarvasāmrājyadāyinīṃ ||  
  
śiṣyāya bhaktiyuktāya vinītāya mahātmane |  
vadānyāya kulīnāya śuddhācāraratāya ca ||  
  
evaṃ vidhāya deveśi sādhakāya praveśayet |  
anyathā siddhihāniḥ syādātmājñā śaṃbhunā kṛtā ||  
  
tathā ca ||  
  
nyāsaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ tataḥ kuryāttārāyāḥ sarvasiddhidaṃ |  
tatrādau prathamonyāsaḥ śrīkaṃṭhādiḥpuroditaḥ ||  
  
mātṛkākṣaramuccārya hrī& strī& hū& pūrvakaṃ vadet |  
śrīkaṃṭhādi sapatnīkaṃ namoṃtaṃ mātṛkāsthale ||  
  
vinyasecca caturthyaṃtaṃ nyāsoyaṃ prathamaḥ smṛtaḥ |  
asminnyāse krīyamāṇe devīmevaṃ vidhāṃ smaret ||  
  
śavapīṭhe samāsīnāṃ nīlakāṃtiṃ trilocanāṃ |  
arddheṃdu śekharāṃ nānābhūṣaṇāḍhyāṃ caturbhujāṃ ||  
  
dvitīyaṃ grahanyāsaṃ kuryāttāṃ sa manusmaret |  
trivījapūrvakaścāyaṃ grahanyāsaḥ samīritaḥ ||  
  
svarādikaṃ raviṃ raktaṃ hṛdiyavargapūrvakaṃ |  
somaṃ śvetaṃ bhuvonyasyakavargādyaṃ ca maṃgalaṃ ||  
  
raktaṃ netratrayanyasya ca vargādyaṃ ca vakṣyasi |  
vudhaṃ śyāmaṃ nyaset pītaṃ ṭa vargādyaṃgale guruṃ ||  
  
ta vargādyaṃ śvetavarṇaṃ ghaṭikāyāṃ tu bhārgavaṃ |  
nīlavarṇaṃ pa vargādyaṃ nābhideśeśanaiśvaraṃ ||  
  
śa vargādyaṃ dhūmravarṇaṃ dhyātvā rāhunyasenmukhe |  
lakṣmyādyaṃ dhūmravarṇābhaṃkatuṃ nābhau punarnyaset ||  
  
nyāsaṃ tṛtīyaṃ vakṣyāmi vīja tritayapūrvakaṃ |  
samānavarṇānuccārya prāgiṃdrāya namostute ||  
  
na sisaṃdhyakṣarāṇyuktvācāgneyyāmagnaye namaḥ |  
dakṣiṇeyamāya namaḥ ka vargādyaṃ lalāṭake ||  
  
ca vargādyaṃ ca nair-ṛtyāṃ nair-ṛtyāya namo mukhe |  
ṭa vargādyaṃgale paścādvaruṇāya namastviti |  
  
p. 170b)  
  
nyaseddhṛdi ta vargādyaṃ vāyavyāṃ vāyave namaḥ |  
pa vargādyaṃ kuverāya namoṃtaṃ dakṣiṇe kare ||  
  
vāmahaste ya vargādīśāṇa rudrāya hṛdbhavet |  
śavargādyurddhakāmāya namo nābhau tu vinyaset ||  
  
hū& rakṣādya pṛthivyai hṛdyādayoriti vinyaset |  
śivaśaktyabhidhānyāsaścaturtha kathyatedhunā ||  
  
hrī& strī& hū& pūrvakaḥ kārya iṃdriyādya haraḥ paraṃ |  
brahmāṇaṃ ḍākinīyuktaṃ vādisyaṃ tārṇapūrvakaṃ ||  
  
mūlādhāra pravinyasyeccaturdala samanvitaṃ |  
śrīviṣṇuṃśākinī yuktaṃ vādilāṃ tārṇapūrvakaṃ ||  
  
svādhiṣṭānābhidhe vakre liṃgasthe ṣaṭdale nyaset |  
rudraṃ tu lākinī yuktaṃ ḍādiphāṃtārṇapūrvakaṃ ||  
  
cakre daśadalaṃ nyasyennābhisthe maṇipūrake |  
īśvaraṃkādivātārṇa pūrvakaṃ kākinīyutaṃ ||  
  
vinyased dvādaśadale hṛdayasthetvanāhate |  
sadāśivaṃ śākinīṃ ca ṣoḍaśasvarapūrvakaṃ ||  
  
kaṃṭhasthe ṣoḍaśadale viśuddhākhye pravinyaset |  
ājñācakre paraśivaṃ hākinī saṃyutaṃ nyaset ||  
  
hakṣārṇaṃ bhrūmadhye saṃsthiteti manoharaṃ |  
vakṣyastha paṃcamanyāsaṃ samastāriṣṭanāśanaṃ ||  
  
a& ā& kavarga hrī& strī& hū& tārāyai nama uccaret |  
vinyased brahmaraṃdhretha i& ī& cāpi ca vargakaṃ ||  
  
hrī& strī& hū& nama ugrāyai lalāṭe cāpi vinyaset |  
u& ū& ca varga strī& hrī& hū& mahogrāyai namo vadet ||  
  
vinnyasecca bhruvormadhye kaṇṭha ṛ& ṝ& ṭa vargakaṃ |  
hrī& strī& hū& cāpi vajrāyai namoṃtaṃ sa kaleṣvapi ||  
  
ḷ& ḹ& ta varga hrī& strī& hū& namaḥ kālyai hṛdinyaset |  
e& ai& pa varga hrī& strī& hū& sarasvatyai ca nābhigāṃ ||  
  
oṃ auṃ śa varga hrī& strī& hū& vāmuścarya ca liṃgake |  
a& aḥ rakṣau ca hrī& strī& hū& cāmuṇḍāyai namonyaset ||  
  
mūlādhārenyasetyaścā sveṣṭenyāsaṃ samācaret |  
ādhāre kāmarūpākṣaṃ vīja hrasvā na pūrvakaṃ ||  
  
hṛdi jālaṃdharaṃ pīṭhaṃ dīrghapūrvaṃ tu vinyaset |  
lalāṭe pūrṇagiryākhyaṃ ka vargādyaṃ nyaset sudhīḥ ||  
  
uḍḍīyānaṃ ca vargādyaṃ keśasaṃdhyaiḥ pravinyaset |  
bhuvorvārāṇasīṃ pīṭhaṃ ṭa vargādyaṃ samāhitaṃ ||  
  
p. 171a)  
  
ta varga pūrvakānyasyedavaṃti nayanadvaye |  
pa varga pūrvakaṃ māyāpūripīṭhaṃ mukhanyaset ||  
  
kaṃṭhe tu mathurāpīṭhaṃ ya vargādyaṃ pravinyaset |  
nābhāvayodhyāpīṭhaṃ tu śa vargādyaṃ pravinyaset ||  
  
kaṭaukāṃcīpurīpīṭhaṃ daśamaṃ tu pravinyaset |  
ṣoḍhānyāsastutārāyāḥ proktobhīṣṭapradāyakaḥ ||  
  
atha maṃtraṣoḍhāḥ ||  
  
maṃtreṇāṃtaritāṃ kṛtvā ṣaḍvārāṃ mātṛkāṃ nyaset |  
kramot kramādvarārohe tārā ṣoḍhāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
kṛtesmin nyāsaparye tu sarvapāpaṃ vinaśyati |  
yoginīnāṃ bhavet pūjyaḥ sa devo na tu mānuṣaḥ ||  
  
yaṃ namaṃti maheśāni ṣoḍhāḥ pūtita vigrahāḥ |  
alpāyuḥ sa bhavet sadyo devatā kaṃpate bhayāt ||  
  
na tasya pūrvyolokesmin pitṛmātṛ tu yojanaḥ ||  
  
atha guhya ṣoḍhāmāha ||  
  
na prakāśyamidaṃ kvāpi maṃtriṇaḥ kāyarakṣaṇe |  
praṇavaṃ mātṛkāvarṇaṃ pūtitaṃ mātṛkāsthale ||  
  
tenaiva pūṭitaṃ varṇaṃ nyaset tatraiva pārvati |  
māyāvījaṃ tathā devī vinyastavyaṃ prayatnataḥ ||  
  
vadhūvījaṃ tathā devī vinyasettu samāhitaṃ |  
kūrcavījaṃ tathānyasanīyaṃ maśeṣataḥ ||  
  
astreṃ caiva mathānyastvā sa karaṃ tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
guhya ṣoḍhāhyayaṃ devī na prakāśyā kadācana ||  
  
avaśyaṃ pratyahaṃ kāryaṃ na pūjā na japastathā ||  
  
athāsyāḥ sāmānyaṣoḍhā tu śyāmā prakaraṇepyuktā ||  
  
tārāvidyāvidhau devī kāryaṣoḍhā catuṣṭayī ||  
  
atha nakṣatrakānyāsaḥ ||  
  
akārādi kramatonyasya rohiṇyādi krameṇa tu |  
vyutkrameṇa ca catvāriśeṣaṃ śeṣaṃ na yojayet ||  
  
rohiṇyādi mahānyāsaṃ kṛtvā naravaratsudhīḥ |  
rohiṇī sutavat pṛthvyāmāśocyo bhavati dhruvaṃ ||  
  
akṛtvā tārakānyāsaṃ tāriṇīṃ prayajedyadi |  
śatarakṣa prajaptopi na maṃtraḥ siddhidāyakaḥ ||  
  
atha ṛṣyādinyāsaḥ ||  
  
akṣobhya ṛṣire tasyā vṛhatī chaṃda īritaṃ |  
nīrasarasvatī devī triṣu lokeṣu gopitā ||  
  
hū& vījamatraṃ śaktiḥ syānmāyā strīṃ kīlakaṃ smṛtaṃ |  
vināyogo bhaveddevī caturvarga phalāptaye ||  
  
atha karāṅganyāsaḥ ||  
  
tatrādau sārddha paṃcākṣarai vidyāyā ||  
  
ṣaṭdīrgha māyāvījena ṣaḍaṃga vidhirīritaḥ ||  
  
p. 171b)  
  
atha ṣaḍakṣarī tryavidyayoḥ ||  
  
akhilavāgrūpiṇīṃ procya hṛdayāya namo vadet |  
akhaṇḍa vāgrūpiṇīṃ ca śirase vahnivallabhā ||  
  
brahmavāgrūpiṇīṃ muktvā kavacāya hūṃ muccaret |  
rudravāgrūpiṇī netratrayāya vauṣaḍityapi ||  
  
sarvavāgrūpiṇī muktvā astrāya phaḍiti smaret |  
ṣaḍdīrgha māyayā vījaṃ vījāṃtetā niyojayet ||  
  
atha sārddhavedākṣarī vidyāyāḥ ||  
  
vījāṃte ekajaṭāyai hṛdayaṃ parikīrtitaṃ |  
tāriṇyau śirase tadvadvajrodake śikhā tathā ||  
  
ugra jaṭai ca kavacaṃ mahāparisane tathā |  
piṃgāgraika jaṭe tadvannetrāstre parikīrtite ||  
  
atha vyāpakanyāsaḥ ||  
  
mūlena vyāpakaṃ nyāsaṃ navadhā kārayet priye |  
saptadhā paṃcadhā cāpi tattonūnaṃ ca kārayat ||  
  
atrokta mācaredatra nānyaṃ saṃcārayedbudhaḥ ||  
  
atha yaṃtralikhanamāhā ||  
  
tataḥ kuṃkuma siṃdūraiḥ kāryaṃ yaṃtraṃ tu yoginā |  
sauvarṇe rājate tāmre sphāṭike vaidrume tathā ||  
  
cakre yathokta vidhinā pūjyā devī narottamaiḥ |  
viṃdu trikoṇāṣṭadala bhūpuraṃ vajracihnitaṃ ||  
  
yaṃtra me tanmaheśāni rahasyātirahasyakaṃ |  
viṃdu ṣaṭkoṇa vṛttaṃ ca padmabhūgṛhabhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
yaṃtraṃ proktaṃ mahāprājña bhūpura dvayayugmakaṃ |  
viṃdu trikoṇa ṣaṭkoṇaṃ vṛtta trayamanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
caturasraṃ tato vṛttaṃ dalāṣṭakaṃ tatopari |  
vṛttatrayaṃ samālikhya bhūpuratrayakaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
triśūlatāṃkitaṃ yaṃtraṃ śrīmahātāriṇī manoḥ ||  
  
viṃdu trikoṇa ṣaṭkoṇaṃ vṛttāṣṭadalabhūṣitaṃ |  
ṣoḍaśāraṃ daṃtapadmaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭāṃdalaṃ tathā ||  
  
bhūpuratraya saṃyuktaṃ yaṃtraṃ śrītāriṇī manoḥ ||  
  
atha sa vījayaṃtramāha ||  
  
tataḥ kularase naiva pīṭhaṃ nirmāya yatnataḥ |  
oṃ āḥ surekhe vajrarekhe hū& phaṭ ca vahnivallabhā ||  
  
matreṇānena vilikhettārā yaṃtraṃ manoharaṃ |  
ṣaṭkoṇāṃtargataṃ padmaṃ bhūviṃ vadvitayaṃ punaḥ ||  
  
tanmadhye vilikhenmaṃtrī tārā praṇavameva hi ||  
  
athavā ||  
  
ṣaṭkoṇāṃtargataṃ padmaṃ bhūvimvadyutayaṃ punaḥ |  
māyāpūrvadale caiva dvitayaṃ dakṣiṇe likhet ||  
  
athottare paścime ca hū& phaṭ tāraṃ ca madhyataḥ |  
sa yoniṃ gomayenāṣṭa patramabjaṃ suśobhanaṃ ||  
  
p. 172a)  
  
bhūpuraṃ ca su vajrāḍhyaṃ yaṃtrameka jaṭātmakaṃ |  
māyāṃ pūrvadalenyasya yāmye vījaṃ dvitīyakaṃ ||  
  
tathottere paścime ca phaṭkāre vilikhet tataḥ |  
madhyavījaṃ likhitvā tu bhūtaśuddhiṃ samācaret ||  
  
astrāstravījaniṣanemaptabhedosti ||  
  
kuleśvaramataḥ proktaṃ phottare paścimetuta |  
phaṭ paścimeṭottare ca vikarālamate smṛtaṃ ||  
  
vyomeṃdau rasanārṇa karṇikamacāṃ dvaṃdvaiḥ sphurat keśavaṃ vargollāsiva   
succhadaṃva sumatī gehena saṃveṣṭhitaṃ ||  
  
tārādhīśvara vārivarṇa vilasaddikkoṇa saṃśobhitaṃ |  
yaṃtraṃ nīratanoḥ paraṃ nigaditaṃ sarvārthasiddhipradaṃ ||  
  
śaśūnyaṃ kusumaiḥ kuryācchūnye vighne vinirdiśet |  
hrasvaḥ sākṣī bhayaṃ śveto bhagavānmadanovakaḥ ||  
  
tābhiṣekaṃ tathā coktvā bhṛguḥ kālīmarutpriye |  
kūrcāstraṃ vahnibhāryeti yaṃtre puṣpāṃjaliṃ kṣipet ||  
  
atha pīṭhapūjāmāha ||  
  
mahīgṛhaścaturdikṣu gaṇeśaṃ vaṭukaṃ tathā |  
kṣetrapālaṃ yoginīṃ ca dhyātvā samyak prapūjayet ||  
  
pāśāṃkuśo triśūlaṃ ca kapālaṃ dadhataṃ karaiḥ |  
kṛṣṇaṃ digaṃvaraṃ krūraṃ kṣetrapaṃ paścime jayet ||  
  
kapālaśūlahastābhyāṃ dadhataṃ sarpabhūṣaṇaṃ |  
svayūthaveṣṭitaṃ ramyaṃ vaṭukaṃ dakṣiṇe ca yet ||  
  
ḍamarvaśi triśūlāṃśca kapālaṃ dadhatī karaiḥ |  
raktamālyāṃ raktavastrāṃ yoginīmuttare yajet ||  
  
śmaśānaṃ tatra saṃciṃtya tat tatkāledrumaṃ smaret |  
tanmūle maṇipīṭhaṃ ca nānāmaṇi vibhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
nānāraṃkārabhūṣāḍhyaṃ munidevaiśca bhuṣitaṃ |  
śivābhirvahumāṃsāsthi moḍamānābhiraṃtaraṃ ||  
  
caturdikṣu śavān muṇḍān vitāṃgārāsthi bhūṣitān |  
pīṭhaśaktirathābhyarcyā keśareṣu samaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
varadā dhārīṇyāḥ pīṭhaṃ pīṭhāmunāyajet ||  
  
tāyathā ||  
  
lakṣmī sarasvatī caiva ratiḥ prītistathaiva ca |  
kīrtiḥ śāṃtiśca puṣṭiścatuṣṭirityaṣṭa śaktayaḥ ||  
  
tanmadhye pūjayeddevyā vāhanaṃ śavameva ca ||  
  
atha pīṭhamaṃtramāha ||  
  
viyadbhṛśaṃ samuccārya manu viṃdu kalānvitaṃ |  
mahāpretapadaṃ paścāddhṛdayāṃta mayaṃ manuḥ ||  
  
p. 172b)  
  
athārghya sthāpanaṃ ||  
  
bhūmiṃ pūrvokta maṃtreṇa maṇḍalasya tu maṇḍalaṃ |  
kuryāt tatrādhāraśaktiṃ kūrmaśeṣaṃ ca saṃjapet ||  
  
ādhāraṃ sthāpayet tatra oṃ hrī& phaḍiti maṃtrataḥ |  
ādhāraṃ pūjayet tatrayaṃ vahnimaṇḍalāya ca ||  
  
namoṃte namavārṇena tato narakapālakaṃ |  
hū& phaṭ maṃtreṇa saṃkṣālya strī& vījena niveśayet ||  
  
tatorcayennṛkapālaṃ japenmaṃtraṃ catuṣṭayaṃ ||  
  
kālīkapālāya namo hrī& hrī& hū& purvakaṃ vadet |  
ekādaśākṣaro maṃtro'nena pūjādimāmatā ||  
  
strī& strī& strū& tāriṇītyuktvā kapāloya namoṃtikaḥ |  
dvādarśonena bhavet kapālārcā dvitīyakai ||  
  
hā& hī& hū& procya nīlā kapālāye nama ityayaṃ |  
ekādaśārṇonenoktā kapālārcā tṛtīyakā ||  
  
māyā strī& hū& svargakapālāya sarvāpadaṃ vadet |  
tato dhārāya sarvāya tathā sarvodbhavāya ca ||  
  
sarvaśuddhimayāyeti sarvāsurarudhīti ca |  
devī kapālāya namaścaturtho maṃtra īritaḥ ||  
  
ṣaṭpaṃcāśat kavarṇoyaṃ kapālasya tu pūjane |  
tatastasmin kapāle tu pūjayedarkamaṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
oṃ sūryamaṇḍalāyeti namāṃtoyaṃ navākṣaraṃ |  
sūryamaṇḍalapūjāyāṃ nṛkapāle manurmataḥ ||  
  
mūlamaṃtraṃ paṭhaṃ tasmin sudhāvudhyā sulāṃ kṣipet |  
gaṃdhapuṣpākṣatāḥ kṣiptvā trikhaṇḍākhyāṃ pradarśayet ||  
  
mudrāṃ sā tu kalau vyastāvaṃguṣṭau kārayatsamau |  
anāmāṃtargate kṛtvā tarjanyau kuṭilā kṛtī ||  
  
kaniṣṭhike nijasthāne trikhaṃḍāhvāna karmaṇi |  
tatastasyāṃ surāyāṃ tu pūjayeccaṃdramaṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
ekādaśārṇena tataḥ śaṃkhatoyaṃ tu maṃtrayet ||  
  
hrī& śrī& hrau& oṃ samuccārya hrī& strī& hū& phaṭ samuccaret |  
hyo& humiti vāgvījādi maṃtra ekādaśākṣaraḥ ||  
  
hrī& vījena tato madyaṃ kiṃciccheṣāṃvu niḥkṣipet |  
śaṃkhamudrāṃ yonimudrāṃ śaṃkhatoyāya darśayet ||  
  
tatra vṛttyaṣṭa ṣaṭkoṇaṃ dhyātvā deviṃ viciṃtayet |  
pūrvoktāṃ pūjayitvaināṃ mūle nātha pratarpayet ||  
  
tarjanī madhyamānāmā kaniṣṭhābhi maheśvaraṃ |  
sāṃguṣṭhābhiścaturvāraṃ mahāśaṃkhasthite jale ||  
  
paṃcākṣaroṇunāpaścāttarpya ānaṃdabhairavaḥ |  
tāro hrau& hyau& nama iti paṃcārṇo bhairavo manuḥ ||  
  
p. 173a)  
  
tataste nārghyato yena prokṣet pūjanasādhanaṃ |  
yonimudrāṃ pradarśyātha praṇamedbhavatāriṇīṃ ||  
  
atha pūjāmāha ||  
  
āvāhasthāpayitvā tu dhyātvā mudrāṃ pradarśayet |  
mudrā pradarśya vidhivadupacāraiḥ prapūjayet ||  
  
atha dhyānaṃ ||  
  
pratyālīḍhapadāṃ ghorāṃ muṇḍamālāṃ vibhūṣitāṃ |  
kharvāṃ lamvodarīṃ bhīmāṃ vyāghracarmāvṛtāṃkaṭau ||  
  
navayauvana sampannāṃ paṃcamudrāṃ vibhūṣitāṃ |  
caturbhujāṃ lalajihvāṃ mahābhīmāṃ varapradāṃ ||  
  
khaḍgakartṛdharāṃ savye vāme muṇḍotpalānvitāṃ |  
piṃgāgraikaṃ jaṭāṃ dhyāyenmaulā vakṣobhya bhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
vālārkamaṇḍalākāralocana trayabhūṣitāṃ |  
prajvalat pitṛbhūmadhye gatā daṃṣṭrāṃ karālinīṃ ||  
  
sā vai sasmeravadanāṃ sarpālaṃkārabhuṣitāṃ |  
viśvavyāpakatoyāṃtaḥ śvetapadmoparisthitāṃ ||  
  
atha mudrāmāha ||  
  
tārārcane viśeṣeṇa darśayet paṃcamudrikāṃ |  
yoniśca bhūtinī caiva vījākhyādaityadhūminī ||  
  
lelihā ceti saṃguptāḥ paṃcamudrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |  
yonirmāyādharādhyenurvadhūḥ kūrcaṃ kramādviduḥ ||  
  
vījānyāsāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tu krameṇa kathayāmyahaṃ |  
tarjanya nāmike madhye kaniṣṭhe cakramādapi ||  
  
karayoryojayeccaiva kaniṣṭhā mūlabhedataḥ |  
aṃguṣṭhāgraṃ tu niḥkṣipya mahāyoniḥ prakīrtitā ||  
  
adhomukhīmimāṃ mudrāṃ darśayedvījapūrvikāṃ |  
vaddhvā tu yonimudrāṃ vai madhyame kuṭile kuru ||  
  
aṃguṣṭhe tu tadagre tu mudreyaṃ dhūtinī matā |  
parivartyakarau spṛṣṭvāvaṃguṣṭha tarjanī yugaṃ ||  
  
arddhacaṃdrākṛtirnyāyaṃ yugapat kārayet samaṃ |  
adhaḥ kaniṣṭhāmākṛṣya madhyame vīniyojayet ||  
  
mudraiṣā kathitā devī vījākhyā jñānarūpiṇī |  
parivartyakarau kṛtvā kaniṣṭhā kaṣṭamadhyamāṃ ||  
  
anāmayoryugaṃ cādhastarjanīyugalaṃ pṛthak |  
anyonyaṃ niviḍaṃ vadhvā aṃguṣṭhāgre anāmike ||  
  
daityānāṃ dhūmakatvākhyā mudraiṣā kathitā priye |  
cakraṃ visphāritaṃ kṛtvāpyadho jihvāṃ ca cālayet ||  
  
pārśvestha muṣṭiyugalaṃ lelihāneti kartitā ||  
  
athāsyāḥ pūjāmāha ||  
  
śrīmadekajaṭetyuktvā vajra puṣpaṃ pratīcchava |  
tārādi vahnijāyāṃtamudīrya yajanaṃ caret ||  
  
saṃtarpya paṃcamudrābhirnamaskuryādalakṣitaḥ ||  
  
paṃcamudrā yathā ||  
  
p. 173b)  
  
saṃmukhaṃ caturasraṃ ca vṛttaṃ gomukhameva ca |  
yoni mudreti kathitā mudrāyaṃ ca namaskṛtau ||  
  
athāsāṃ rakṣaṇamāha ||  
  
aṃjaliṃ bhūmau saṃsthāpya tatra datvā śiraḥ punaḥ |  
eṣāmudrā maheśāni khyātā saṃmukhasaṃjñakāḥ ||  
  
uttānaṃ ca vāmakaraṃ bhūmau kṛtvā maheśvarī |  
dakṣaṃ karatalaṃ tatra saṃyojya sādhakottamaḥ ||  
  
karayoraṃgulībhiśca pṛṣṭadeśaṃ parasparaṃ |  
spṛṣṭvā tatra śiroyogānmudrāsyāccatusrikā ||  
  
nidhāya bhūmāvuttānāṃguṣṭha muṣṭidvayaṃ śive |  
mūrddhni yogamaheśāni khyāterya vṛttamudrikā ||  
  
bhūmau karayugaṃ devī saṃpuṭaṃ vistṛtāṃguliṃ |  
kṛtvā tatra śiroyogānmudrā gomukhasaṃjñakā ||  
  
pūrvoktā yonimudrāyā sā bhūmau śirasaṃyutā |  
yoni mudreti kathitā tārā devyā namaskṛtau ||  
  
athāsyāḥ mūrddhni bhairavaṃ yajet ||  
  
tathā ca ||  
  
tataḥ saṃpūjayeddevyā mastake'kṣobhya saṃjñitaṃ |  
munidvādaśavarṇena manunā sa nigadyate ||  
  
akṣobhya vajrapuṣpaṃ ca pratīcchānalavallabhā ||  
  
asyopāsya maṃtradhyānādikamagrevācyaṃ ||  
  
atha saṃpūjayet koṇaṃ ṣaṭke devyāḥ ṣaḍaṃgakaṃ ||  
  
atha divyaughādyā guravaḥ ||  
  
atha tārā gurūn vakṣye dṛṣṭādṛṣṭa phalapradān |  
ūrddhvakeśo vyomakeśo nīlakaṇṭho vṛṣadhvajaḥ ||  
  
divyaughān kathitān vatsa siddhaughān pūjayet tataḥ |  
vaśiṣṭhaḥ kūrmanāthaśca mīnanātho maheśvaraḥ ||  
  
harināthaśca mānaughān śṛṇu vakṣyāmi sadgurūn |  
tārāvatī bhāsvamatī jayā vidyā mahodarī ||  
  
sukhānaṃdaḥ parānaṃdaḥ pārijātaḥ kuleśvaraḥ |  
virūpākṣaḥ pheravī ca kathitaṃ tāriṇī kulaṃ ||  
  
trikoṇa madhye devyagre svaguruṃ pūjayedbudhaḥ |  
kāmeśvaryādikāḥ pūjyā strikoṇe vahnimaṇḍale ||  
  
kāmeśvarī dikkaravāsinī ca caṇḍalāyikā ||  
  
athādho mukhatrikoṇe ||  
  
iṃdrakoṇe lasaddaṇḍakuṇḍikākṣagunābhayāṃ |  
gāyatrīṃ pūjayenmastrīṃ brahmāṇamapi tādṛśaṃ ||  
  
iti ṣaṭkoṇapakṣe trikoṇapakṣetūpaniṣadiviśeṣaḥ ||  
  
p. 174a)  
  
krameṇa koṇatraye vījatrayeṇa brāhmī vaiṣṇavīṃ māheśvarīṃ pūjayediti ||  
  
athāsyāvaraṇārcā vāmāvartenaiva ||  
  
tathā ca ||  
  
vāmāvarte krameṇaiva pūjayedaṃga devatā ||  
  
atha pūrvādyaṣṭadale mūla mahākālpādyāḥ pūjyā |  
tatoṣṭau yoginī vāhye saṃpūjyā dalamūlataḥ ||  
  
mahākālyatha mudrāṇī ugrā bhīmā tathaiva ca |  
ghorā ca bhrāmarī caiva mahārātrīśca saptamī ||  
  
bhairavī cāṣṭamī proktā yoginīstāḥ prapūjayet ||  
  
atha pūrvādi dala catuṣṭaye vai rocanādīn pūjayet ||  
  
vairocanaṃ tathā śaṃkhapāṇḍaraṃ padmanābhakaṃ |  
asitābhaṃ yajenmaṃtrī aindrītaśca caturdale ||  
  
athāgnyādi dala catuṣṭaye nāmakādyāḥ iṣṭyāḥ ||  
  
vidikṣu pūjayet paścādagni koṇāditaḥ kramāt |  
nāmakāṃ nāmakāṃ caiva pāṇḍarāṃtārikāṃ tathā ||  
  
atha vairocanādīnāṃ dhyānamāha ||  
  
vairocanaṃ dvihastaṃ ca yaṣṭi ṭomaradhāriṇaṃ |  
pītaṃ vṛṣāsanagataṃ trinetraṃ raktavatsalaṃ ||  
  
śaṃkhaṃ triśirasaṃ devamasitābhaṃ hiraṇmayaṃ |  
pustakābhīti varadaṃ vimalaṃ śaśavāhanaṃ ||  
  
padmanābhaṃ daṃti vaktuṃ pustakaṃ varadā bhayaṃ |  
pāśaṃ ca vidhṛtaṃ devaṃ trinetraṃ varadaṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
śvetāṃ trinetravaradāṃ pustakābhayadhāriṇīṃ |  
māmakāṃ valadevena saṃyuktena vibhāvitāṃ ||  
  
kṛṣṇāṃ karālavadanāṃ tāmakā navayauvanaṃ |  
godhikāyāṃ samārūḍhāṃ śikhirūḍhāṃ ca tālakāṃ ||  
  
pāṃḍurāṃ śvetavījena caturvāhuḥ samanvitāṃ |  
raktāṃ lamvodarīṃ dhyāyet paṃcapretāsanasthitāṃ ||  
  
atha vairocanādi narakāṃtakāṃ tāyāṃ pūjāyāṃ maṃtra viśeṣamāha ||  
  
ādau praṇavamuccārya nāmādya vījamuccaret |  
saṃvuddhyaṃtaṃvatannāma vajra puṣpaṃ pratīccha ca ||  
  
svāhāṃto manurākhyāto dvādaśānāmayaṃ kramaḥ ||  
  
atha pūrvādyaṣṭa dalāgreṣu brāhmādyaṣṭa mātaraḥ pūjanīyā ||  
  
dalāgre ca maheśāni brāhmādi paripūjayet ||  
  
p. 174b)  
  
atha pūrvādi dvāre catuṣṭaye padmāṃtakādīn jayet ||  
  
dvāre pūrvāditaḥ paścāt padmāntakayarmāttakau |  
vighnāṃtakaṃ samabhyarcya pūjaye narakāṃtakaṃ ||  
  
atha bhūpurasya daśadikṣu digpālān saṃpūjya tadvahyaṣṭadalāni samabhyarcya   
bhūpura pūrvadiśi bhūpurayaṃ kalayoraṃtarāle sūryaṃ saṃpūjya devyottarabhāge   
gurupaṃktyaṃtare vaurddha jayet ||  
  
bhūpure caiva tadvāhye daśadikṣu yathā kramaṃ |  
śakrādīṃścāpi vajrādīn pūjayetadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
bhūviṃvābhyaṃtare sūryaṃ gurupaṃktyuttare tataḥ |  
uttare pūjayedvauddhaṃ punardevī prapūjayet ||  
  
puṣpāṃjali trayaṃ dadyādyathā saṃkhyaṃ japedbudhaḥ ||  
  
atha sarvāvaraṇa sādhāraṇa yajanamastramāha ||  
  
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuccārya nāma saṃvodhanānvitaṃ |  
vajrapuṣpaṃ pratīccheti hū& phaṭ svāheti maṃtritaḥ ||  
  
etanmaṃtreṇyāsamātraṃ bhinnameva na saṃśayaḥ |  
anena manunā sarvān parivārān samarcayet ||  
  
vairocanādiṣu punarnāmādyakṣarapūrvakaṃ ||  
  
atha balidānaṃ ||  
  
tatośca nityā pūjāṃte'nvahaṃ devyai valiṃ haret |  
vāmabhāge trikoṇe ca vṛttaṃ bhūpurameva ca ||  
  
vidhāya rakatamālyādau arcayitvā yathāvidhiḥ ||  
  
śrīmadeka jaṭenīla sarasvatī mahogra ca |  
tārādevī khakhetyuktvā sarvabhūtapiśācarā ||  
  
kṣasān grasagra samamajāḍyaṃ chedaya chedaya ||  
  
śrī& hrī& phaṭ vahni jāyāṃtastāra māyādi ko manuḥ |  
bhaved dvipaṃcaśadaśaḥ pūjaivaṃ pūrṇatāmiyāt ||  
  
atha japamāha ||  
  
tatrādau bhairavasya tataḥ kullukāyāḥ tataḥ sveṣṭadevatāyāśca ||  
  
akṣobhyasya manuṃ tyaktvā devīṃ tārāṃ japedyadi |  
siddhihānirbhavettasya rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet ||  
  
akṣobhyasya manuṃ vipra kavacaṃ sāramuttamaṃ |  
atiguhyaṃ mahādhyānaṃ sarvadhyāneṣu cottamaṃ ||  
  
agre manuṃ pravakṣyāmi dhyānaṃ caiva tataḥ paraṃ |  
kavacaṃ ca tataḥ paścāt kathayāmi krameṇa tu ||  
  
p. 175a)  
  
anuttaraṃ samuddhṛtya prapaṃcama vibhūṣitaṃ |  
akṣobhyeti ca svāhetiramādyaṃtaṃ mahāmanuḥ ||  
  
svayaṃ ṛṣiśca saṃprokto virāṭ chaṃda udīritaḥ |  
akṣobhyo devatā proktastrimūrtirnāgarūpadhṛk ||  
  
viniyogastu niyataṃ puruṣārtha catuṣṭaye ||  
  
atha dhyānaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvasaubhāgyadāyakaṃ |  
sahasrāditya saṃkāśaṃ nāgarūpadharaṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
vidyuṭi samaṃ vaktraṃ vahnibhāsvaralocanaṃ |  
sārddha trivalayopetaṃ jaṭākodyagra saṃsthitaṃ ||  
  
mahārāvaṇya saṃyuktaṃ surāsura namaskṛtaṃ |  
sūrya vidyut samaṃ bhāsvanmahāmaṇi śiropari ||  
  
etadyūyaṃ mahākāyaṃ devīrapi supūjitaṃ ||  
  
śrīśiva uvāca ||  
  
akṣobhya kavacasyāsya brahmaviṣṇuśca rudrakāḥ |  
ṛṣayaśca samākhyātā virāṭ chaṃda udāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
akṣobhya devatā caiva śrīvījaṃ vījameva ca |  
svāhā śaktirviniyogaḥ puruṣārtha catuṣṭaye ||  
  
śrīvījaṃ śirase avyādādi vijiaṃ ca bhārake |  
akāraḥ skaṃdhame avyāt kṣakāro hṛdi rakṣa tu ||  
  
bhakāro nābhi me avyādekāro guhyadeśake |  
maṃtraśaktiśca sarvāṃgaṃ vījaṃ netratraye'vatu ||  
  
sarvabhāvaiśca akṣobhyo vāhu dvaurakṣayet sadā |  
brahmārakṣa tu pādau dvauviṣṇurakṣa tu jānunī ||  
  
mūlādhāraṃ śivomevyāt svādhiṣṭānaṃ vṛṣo'vatu |  
maṇipūre sadā avyāt śivasya gṛhiṇī ca me ||  
  
anāhatāmvujaṃ me'vyādiṃdrādi daśadevatāḥ |  
viśuddhacakreṣṭa tataṃ rakṣāṃ karo me raviḥ ||  
  
maheśvaraḥ sadā rakṣedājñā cakraṃ suśobhanaṃ |  
brahmaśukraṃ ca me rakṣennābhiṃ rakṣa tu bhairavī ||  
  
divyādau gurupaṃktau ca sarvatrākṣobhya ucyate |  
evaṃ kramavidhānena kavacaṃ ca japecchuviḥ ||  
  
trisaṃdhyaṃ yaḥ paṭhennityaṃ śradhābhaktiḥ samanvitaḥ |  
siddhyahānirbhavet tasya nātrakāryā vicāraṇā ||  
  
atha kullukāyāḥ āvaśyakatāmāha ||  
  
ajaptvā kullukāmaṃtrama smṛtvā śrīpatiṃ hariṃ |  
yojayet tāriṇī maṃtra narakeśariṇīyate ||  
  
japitvā kullukāmaṃtramaṣṭottaraśataṃ sudhīḥ |  
prajapettāriṇīṃ paścānnānyathā siddhimāpnuyāt ||  
  
p. 175b)  
  
dhṛtvā tu kullukā haste mahādevīṃ samarcayet |  
athavā mūrddhnī vinyasya pūjayet prajapedapi ||  
  
anitya japasaṃkhyāmāha ||  
  
aṣṭottara sahasraṃ vā aṣṭottara śataṃ ca vā |  
rahasya mālayā maṃtrī japennitya mananyadhīḥ ||  
  
tathā ca ||  
  
sahasraṃ śataṃ viṃśati vā japeṃdrasya mārayeti śrutau |  
rahasya mālayātatā tāriṇī siddhidā bhavet ||  
  
atastayā prajaptavyā mārayā siddhimicchatā |  
mahāśaṃkhamayīmālā paṃcāśanmaṇinirmitā ||  
  
rahasyamālā saṃproktā gopanīyā prayatnataḥ |  
calamālāsthi khaṇḍe naracitā japamālikā ||  
  
mahāśaṃkhamayī jñeyā tadabhāve sphāṭikīmatā ||  
  
atha maṃtradhyānaṃ ||  
  
maṃtradhyānaṃ pravakṣyāmi japā sarvārthasādhakaṃ |  
maṃtradhyānāṃ maheśāni śuddhyate brahmahāyataḥ ||  
  
mūlacakre ca hṛllekhāṃ sūryakoṭiṃ samaprabhāṃ |  
svādhiṣṭāne pītavarṇaṃ dvitīyaṃ ca vibhāvayet ||  
  
sūryakoṭi pratīkāśaṃ kūrcavījaṃ mahāprabhaṃ |  
aṣṭamaṃtraṃ hṛdi dhyāyet kālāgni sadṛśa prabhaṃ ||  
  
mūlādi brahmaraṃdhrāṃtaṃ sarvāṃ vidyāṃ vibhāvayet |  
sūryakoṭi pratīkāśāṃ yogibhirdṛṣṭa pūrvikāṃ ||  
  
jihvāyānyasanādeva mūkopi su kavirbhavet |  
itthaṃ japaṃ samarpyātha ghaṃṭhāvādanapūrvikāṃ ||  
  
stutvā tā stutibhiḥ samyak sādhakobhakti saṃyutaḥ ||  
  
atha stotraṃ yathā ||  
  
svayaṃ līlayāyā paraṃ viṣṇumūrtirvabhau cenna caivaṃ kathaṃ caṃdracūḍaḥ |  
tadaṃghri padmodgatāṃvu pravāhī jagannitya vījaṃ bhajetāṃ trinetrāṃ ||  
  
parāyā na cet kṛṣṇa āsīt kathaṃ sa svavaktrā raviṃdadyuternetrabhaṃgyā |  
smarānervahuvrīhitā kṛchunāmni jagannitya vījaṃ bhajetāṃ trinetrāṃ ||  
  
lasatyā dehastānanākteṣu yasyā madhūnicchurāṃśona paṃcāsyako bhūt |  
atastena labdhvā sadānaṃda saṃjñāṃ jagannitya vījaṃ bhajetāṃ trinetrāṃ ||  
  
yadīyaṃ rasaṃ sannipīyaścareṇa smarīye mukhe cāmṛte caṃdanādau |  
ghṛṇāṃ kiṃ vṛtatyāśita kālakūṭo jagannitya vījaṃ bhajetāṃ trinetrāṃ ||  
  
p. 176a)  
  
vidhātā yadā yā na cāste svayaṃ saḥ svayaṃbhūḥ kathaṃ syāt tadā toti tūrṇaṃ |  
nutārābhidheyo na jātaḥ dyulauleḥ jagannitya vījaṃ bhajetāṃ trinetrāṃ ||  
  
tadaṃśaṃ samāyaṃ dvivījaṃ tataḥ syāt tripādeti vedāṃtinoyāṃ vadaṃti |  
videkāṃkṣaraṃ brahmavījaṃ kūrcaṃ jagannityavījaṃ bhajetāṃ trinetrāṃ ||  
  
tatostraṃ yadā sārddha paṃcākṣarāṃ sā jagattāraṇādugratārā prasiddhā |  
vinā tārakaṃ sā paraikā jaṭāsyājjagannityavījaṃ bhajetāṃ trinetrāṃ ||  
  
vināstraṃ paṃcākṣaraiḥ kullukeyaṃ svayaṃ nīravāṇī paraṃ citsvarūpā |  
smṛtāpyekavālaṃraṃ sadāmukti hetuṃ jagannitya vījaṃ bhajetāṃ trinetrāṃ ||  
  
idaṃ ye janāstotrarājaṃ vivaṃti prasiddhāścate gadyapadya prasaṃge |  
jagadrūpa pāpādi mukto hi tūrṇaṃ śarīrāṃtare yāṃti tārā samīpaṃ ||  
  
vipattau niśārddhe japāṃte prabhāte paṭhedyastu bhaktyā tadarthaṃ viciṃtya |  
bhavennīlavānyādvirephāṃghripadme sajīvastu haṃsaḥ sajīvo na jīvaḥ ||  
  
iti śrīadvaitanirūpaṇemaṃtrārthavivaraṇātmakatātmakastotrarājanāmastotraṃ   
saṃpūrṇaṃ |  
  
atha kavacamāha ||  
  
purā kailāśaśikhare tārāṃ papraccha śaṃkaraḥ |  
guptabhāvena deveśi kathayasva tu sādaraṃ ||  
  
kenopāyena sahasā śarīraṃ sudṛḍhaṃ bhavet |  
kathaṃ vā siddhiratulā tavarmatra vidāṃ priye ||  
  
śrītārovāca ||  
  
asti guhyataraṃ hyetanniḥ sṛtaṃ mukhapaṃkajān |  
idaṃ rahasyaṃ paramaṃ kathayāmitvayi priye ||  
  
śrūyatāṃ sāvadhānena kavacaṃ tanmukhātsṛtaṃ |  
madhukaiṭabhayoryuddhe kathitaṃ padmajanmanā ||  
  
tatprabhāvottu deveśanāśaṃ viṣṇurnagacchati |  
bhavat su kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ tannasmarasi māyayā ||  
  
uddhṛtaṃ sārabhūtānāṃ kavacaṃ yogināṃ sate |  
na kasmaicit pravaktavyaṃ na prakāśyaṃ kathaṃcana ||  
  
śapathaṃ kuru deveśa yadi snehosti sāṃpratī |  
śrūyatāṃ sāvadhānena kavacaṃ sārasaṃgrahaṃ ||  
  
satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ punaḥ |  
kavacena vinā devayonāmarcayati kṣaṇāt ||  
  
tamaśnāmi mahogrāhaṃ yoginībhiḥ suniścitaṃ ||  
  
brahmaviṣṇumaheśānāṃ vījaṃ rakṣa tu mūlakaṃ |  
tadūrddha śaktivījaṃ tu liṃgaṃ rakṣa tu yatnataḥ ||  
  
maṇipūraṃ sadā pātu vadhū vījaṃ viśeṣataḥ |  
anāhataṃ varmavījaṃ pātu me sarvasarvataḥ ||  
  
astrāṇi sarvadā pātu viṣuddhaṃ kaṇṭhabhūṣitaṃ |  
śeṣastu pātu me nityamājñāsthānaṃ dvipatrakaṃ ||  
  
p. 176b)  
  
śīrṣaṃ pātu tathā tārā jaṭāpātu sadānanaṃ |  
nīlasarasvatī pātu hṛdayaṃ me sadāpunaḥ ||  
  
akṣobhyaḥ pātu sarvāgaṃ vṛhatī pātu bhālakaṃ |  
ugratārādevatā me gahvaraṃ pātu sarvadā ||  
  
caraṇai me sadā pātu māyāvījamaśeṣataḥ |  
urūme sarvadā pātu vadhūvījaṃ sadaiva hi ||  
  
stanadvayaṃ sadāpātu kūrcaṃ vighnavighātakaṃ |  
rasanāmasanāpātu lakṣmī devī ca sāsvatī ||  
  
rasāgraṃ sadā pātu sarasvatī prayatnataḥ |  
ratiḥ pātu sadāvījaṃ prītirme vadanaṃ sadā ||  
  
kīrtiḥ kīrtiḥ sadā pātu śāṃtiḥ śāṃtiṃ sadāvatu |  
puṣṭirmeyā tu puṣṭiṃ ca puṣṭituṣṭiḥ sadāvat ||  
  
vairocanaṃ pātu śaṃkhaṃ śaṃkha pūrvastathaiva ca |  
pāṇḍaro me sadāgaṇḍaṃ pātu nityaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ||  
  
padmanābhaḥ sadā pātu nābhirmedaśapatrakaṃ |  
asitābhaḥ pātu liṃgaṃ nāmakaḥ pātu cakṣuṣi ||  
  
māmakoma tathā hastau grīvāṃ me pātu pāṃḍaraḥ |  
tārakaḥ pātu hṛdayaṃ draṣṭiṃ padmāṃtako mama ||  
  
pārśvadvaṃdvaṃ sadā pātu yamāṃtaka narāṃtakau |  
caraṇau me pātu nityaṃ vighnāṃtaka samāhvayaḥ ||  
  
tārā me pātu satatamaṣṭāṃgaṃ parameśvarī |  
idaṃ tu kavacaṃ deva kathitaṃ tanmukhāt sṛtaṃ ||  
  
pramādādyadi deveśa yatra kutra prakāśyate |  
yoginībhistadāhaṃ tu svayaṃ ca vadhakāriṇī ||  
  
yadi bhāgyavaśāllabdhaṃ kenacit sādhakīlavai |  
tadā tasya mahāsiddhirvapuṣā jāyate dhruvaṃ ||  
  
niṣiddhebhyo na dātavyaṃ na prakāśyaṃ kathaṃcana |  
yadi dadyānniṣiddhebhyastadāhaṃ vadhakāriṇī ||  
  
dadyācchāṃtāya śiṣyāya taṃtra maṃtra yutācya ca |  
gurupaṃktipuṭā caiva tadā siddhiranuttamā ||  
  
rahasyaṃ kathitaṃ sarvamanaṃta phaladāyakaṃ |  
gopitavyaṃ tadā deva na prakāśyaṃ kadācana ||  
  
iti śrīyoginītaṃtroktaikajaṭākavacaṃ samāptaṃ ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau tārābhedatritayasādhāraṇanityārcananirṇayo nāma   
caturviṃśatitamaḥ prakāśaḥ || 24 ||  
25th prakāśaḥ not available   
  
atha śrīvairocanīvidyāyāḥ kramollikhyate ||  
  
jalapātraṃ kare kṛtvā pūjāsthānaṃ tato vrajet |  
prakṣālya pādau hastau ca vāsasī paridhāya ca ||  
  
ācamya vidhivaddevī deśikeṃdra sukhāsane |  
prāgāsya mukhagāsyaṃ vā dakṣiṇāsyaṃ viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
svagehādvāmato ramyaṃ devīveśma samācaret |  
praṇavaiścaiva lajjāṃ ca sakāraśca visargavān ||  
  
asurakṣayāya rakṣamāye phaṭ ca dviṭhāṃtikaḥ |  
anenāṃghrī ca prakṣālya jalamīśānatastyajet ||  
  
atha maṃtrācamanaṃ ||  
  
maṃtrairācamanaṃ kuryāddevīṃ dhyāyan hṛdaṃvuje |  
lakṣmīmāyā kūrcavījaistribhiḥ pītvāṃvu sādhakaḥ ||  
  
p. 177a)  
  
lakṣmīmāyā kūrcavījaistribhiḥ pītvāṃvu sādhakaḥ |  
vāgbhavenāṣṭa saṃpūjya māyābhyāṃ vadvirunmṛjet ||  
  
kūrcena kṣālayet pāṇimebhirmaṃtraiśca vinyaset |  
śrīmāyā kūrcavāk kāma tripuṭā bhagavarṇakaiḥ ||  
  
kāmakalāṃ kuśābhyāṃ ca vaktranāsākṣi karṇayoḥ |  
nābhi hṛnmastakaṃ cāṣṭau kṛtvāśasturbhavetkṣaṇāt ||  
  
ācamyaivaṃ chinnamastāṃ vatsarātāṃ prapaśyati |  
puṇyāhaṃ vācayeddhīmānsāmānyārghyaṃ tato diśet ||  
  
dvāramabhyukṣyate naiva dvāradevān prapūjayet |  
dhātāraṃ ca vidhātāraṃ kṣetrapālaṃ tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
vighnarājaṃ maheśāni gaṃgā ca yamunāṃ tataḥ |  
vasudhārāṃ śaṃkhanidhiṃ padmanidhiṃ vasumatīṃ ||  
  
dvāraśriyaṃ namaskṛtya pūjayaṃ kramataḥ sudhīḥ ||  
  
oṃkārādi namoṃtena pūjayeddeśikottamaḥ |  
kiṃcit saṃkucya vāmāṃge vāmapāda puraḥsaraṃ ||  
  
pūjāsthānaṃ viśeddhīmān astrāya phaṭ samuccaran ||  
  
adyapātraṃ vidhāyātha kṣetrapālaṃ namatsudhīḥ |  
ūrddhvaṃ brahmā adhonaṃtaḥ ādhāraḥ śaktiṃ tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
kūrmamanaṃtaṃ pṛthivīṃ kalpavṛkṣaṃ tataḥ paraṃ |  
maṇidevīṃ svarṇa siṃhamaṣṭa śaktistataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
ānaṃdakaṃdaṃ praṇamet saṃvinnālaṃ tataḥ paraṃ |  
tataḥ prakṛti patrāṇi vikāramaya keśaraṃ ||  
  
kamalaṃ sarvatatvaika guṇāḥ satvaṃ rajastamaḥ |  
sūryavimvaṃ caṃdraviṃvaṃhniviṃvaṃ tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
paṃcāśadvījasaṃyuktāṃ karṇikāṃ praṇametsudhīḥ |  
ātmānaṃ paramātmānamaṃtarātmānameva ca ||  
  
vikāraṃ keśaraṃ dhīmān praṇameddaṇḍavadbhuvi |  
divyadṛṣṭyādivyavighnān dūrayet na pūrvakaṃ ||  
  
astrāya * (?) ca maṃtreṇa hū& maṃtreṇāpi suṃdarī |  
ātmānaṃ rakṣayeddhīmān vahniprākārayogataḥ ||  
  
śavaṃ vā gajacarmāṇi naracarma maheśvarī |  
vyāghrājinaṃ kuce laṃvābhūtikāṃgāra saṃbhava ||  
  
śavacailaṃ maheśāni āsane kalpayetsudhīḥ |  
ātmānaṃ nīlacolena nīlayadyatnapūrvakaḥ ||  
  
viśeṣeṇa maheśāni pūjayet sādhakottamaḥ |  
kūrmacakre viśeddhīmān mukhe sarvasamṛddhaye ||  
  
pūjayitvā vidhānena viśeddhīmān tadā śuciḥ |  
uparicāsaneddhīmān śodhayitvā viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
pūjayitvāsanaṃ dhīmānnādhāraḥ śaktiyogataḥ |  
śvetasarṣapamādāya vighnānniḥ sārayetsudhīḥ ||  
  
svargamartya ca pātāle vighnāvighnavināyakāḥ |  
naśyaṃ tu mama kūrmesmin te sarve ca śivājñayā ||  
  
p. 177b)  
  
tāratrayaṃ tato dadyādastrāya phaḍiti smaraṃ |  
vinyasta hastayugalaṃ mūrddhorddha kramayogataḥ ||  
  
dhyātvā guruṃ sahasrāre praṇamyanatimādiśet |  
guruvāmena meddhīmān tatraiva gurupādukāṃ ||  
  
gaṇeśaṃ dakṣiṇe dhyātvā praṇame vighnaśāṃtaye |  
saṃmukhe praṇameddevīṃ chinnamastāṃ vasuṃdharāṃ ||  
  
ratikāmoparisthātāṃ prāṇāyāma tathā caret |  
bhūtaśuddhiṃ tataḥ kuryāddhaṃ sa maṃtreṇa sādhakaṃ ||  
  
oṃkāreṇa purojīva mūrddhamut kṣipya yatnataḥ |  
nirjīvaṃ dehamākārairvahnivījena dāhayet ||  
  
tenaiva vāyuvījena tadbhasmāyagamaṃ bhavet |  
tenaiva megharūpeṇa tatra viṣṭiṃ viciṃtayet ||  
  
tenaivāmṛta vṛṣṭiṃ ca dhyātvā dehanavīkṛtaṃ |  
pūrvokta devatārūpaṃ sarvakalmaṣa varjitaṃ ||  
  
karakacchapikā puṣpaṃ haste mūlena dhārayet |  
itīyaṃ bhūtaśuddhistu lokānāṃ hitakāriṇī ||  
  
bhūtaśuddhiṃ samāsādya mātṛkānya samācaret |  
ṣoḍaśārṇena mūlena prāṇāyāmaṃ samācaret ||  
  
caṃdrāvedāgni saṃkhyābhirmāyayā vā samācaret |  
vikāra vidyā daśanairvidyāsu sakalāṣvapi ||  
  
maṃtranyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryādṛṣyādīn pūrvasūcitām |  
āsāṃ ṛṣirbhairavohaṃ nāmnā tu krodhabhūpatiḥ ||  
  
samrāṭ chaṃdo devatā ca chinnamastāḥ prakīrtitā |  
māyāvījaṃ svāhā śaktiḥ kathitā padmayoginā ||  
  
dharmārtha kāmamokṣeṣu viniyogaḥ prakīrtitāḥ |  
uccaret praṇavaṃ pūrvaṃ ākāraṃ viṃdu saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
khaḍgātha hṛdayāyeti svāhā yuktaṃ kanīyasi |  
ikāraṃ praṇavāddevī caṃdraviṃdu samanvitaṃ ||  
  
sukhadgāyatato vācyaṃ śirase tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
svāhā yuktaṃ tato vācyaṃ pavitrāṃguli saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
ūkāraṃ praṇavāddevī viṃdulāchitamastakaṃ |  
śrīvajrāya samāyuktaṃ śikhāyai ca tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
svāhāṃtaṃ vinyaseddevī madhyamāyāṃ tataḥ paraṃ |  
mātrāṃ dvādaśikāmuktvāpāsāya tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
kavacāya tato vācyaṃ svāhā ca tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
tarjanyāṃ vinyaseddevī saṃbhuvitsu samāhitaṃ ||  
  
p. 178a)  
  
aukāraṃ praṇavāddevī aṃkuśāya tataḥ paraṃ |  
netratrayāya saṃyuktaṃ svāhā ca tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
aṃguṣṭhe vinyaseddevī praṇavādyaṃ tataḥ paraṃ |  
tryaḥkāraṃ ca visargoktaṃ surakṣayāya suṃyutaṃ ||  
  
asurakṣayāya saṃyuktaṃ vinyase karayordvayoḥ |  
hṛdi mūrddhni śikhāyāṃ ca kavace netrayordvayoḥ ||  
  
nyasedastrākhya paryaṃtaṃ digvidikṣu yathākramaṃ ||  
  
atha ṣoḍhānyāsaḥ ||  
  
maṃtraṣoḍhāṃ tataḥ kuryāt trailokyavaśakāriṇīṃ |  
śrīvārātripuṭoyoniḥ prāsādaṃ praṇavastathā ||  
  
kāridhvaṃkuśaiḥ kāmakalā kūrcāstrakaiḥ kramāt |  
ṣoḍaśī maṃtravarṇaiśca pṛthagaṣṭā daśākṣaraiḥ ||  
  
ebhirvījairmātṛkārṇānsveṣusthāneṣu vinyaset |  
eṣā brahmasvarūpā hi vījaṣoḍhāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
anyāścanyasanāt sarvavajradehā bhavaṃti hi |  
sarvaiśvaryayutāste hi jīvanmuktā daśābdataḥ ||  
  
athāsyāḥ yaṃtramāha ||  
  
athāsyāḥ maṇḍalaṃ vakṣye yathā vadavadhārayet |  
dīkṣā karaṃ mahādeviṃ sarvakarma prayojakam ||  
  
sitaṃ kuryāddalaṃ pūrvamāgneyaṃ raktavarṇakaṃ |  
yāmye kṛṣṇaṃ tataḥ pītaṃ śuklaṃ caiva tato'sitaṃ ||  
  
tataḥ pītaṃ prakurvīta karṇikā tasya madhyagā |  
tatra madhye prakurvīta maṇḍalaṃ caṇḍarociṣaṃ ||  
  
rajaḥ satvatamorekhārakta śuklasitāṃ kramāt |  
māyāyugaṃ ca tanmadhye phaḍakṣara samanvitaṃ ||  
  
vāhyāṃtaraṃ ca cakrasya kuryāt tridvāra saṃyutaṃ |  
pūrvaṃ raktaṃ tataḥ pītaṃ śuklaṃ raktaṃ yathā kramaṃ ||  
  
caturdvāra samāyuktaṃ kṣetrapālairadhiṣṭhitaṃ ||  
  
athocyate yaṃtrarājo vairocanyā maheśvarī |  
ṣaṭkoṇa prathamaṃ sakhyamadhyadeśe trikoṇakaṃ ||  
  
sūryavimvaṃ tato dadyāccaturasraṃ tataḥ paraṃ |  
bhūgolaṃ ca tato dadyāccaturasraṃ tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
aṣṭapatraṃ tato dadyādyathā sthānena deśikaḥ |  
caṃdraviṃvaṃ tato dadyād vahniviṃvaṃ tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
bhūgolaṃ ca tato dadyād bhūpura tritayaṃ tataḥ |  
vajraśūlaṃ samāyuktaṃ koṇetaṃkaṇ niyojayet ||  
  
kiṃjalkaṃ keśare dadyān maṃtravarṇāt trikoṇake |  
dūtiḥ kāmopari dhyāyeddevīṃ vairocanīṃ śubhāṃ ||  
  
p. 178b)  
  
bhairavoktaṃ mahaṃ vakṣye yaṃtraṃ samṛddhitaṃ |  
trikoṇaṃ prathamaṃ lekhyaṃ ṣaṭkoṇairvaṣṭayeccataṃ ||  
  
trivimvaṃ ca tato dadyād guṇānāṃ pariṇāmakaṃ |  
bhūpura tritayaṃ kuryād vajraśūlasamanvitaṃ ||  
  
koṇadeśe tato dadyāt ṭaṃkāstraṃ sumanoharaṃ |  
yathāsthāne likheddhīmān kartṛkharparakaṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
ratiḥ kamopari dhyāyeddevīṃ vairocanīṃ śubhāṃ ||  
  
athāsyāḥ yaṃtralikhanāṃnaṃtaramarghyādi sthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ ||  
  
tathā ca ||  
  
arghyapātrādikaṃ kuryān maṇḍalaṃ purataścaret ||  
  
atha pīṭhapūjāmāha ||  
  
ādhāraśaktimārānya paratatvāṃta pūjite |  
pīṭhe jayākhyā vijayājitā cāpi parājitā ||  
  
nityā vilāsinī ṣaṣṭīdogdhī ghorā ca maṃgalā |  
dikṣu madhye ca saṃpūjyā pīṭhavasyena śaktayaḥ ||  
  
atha svanābhimaṇḍalaṃ devīṃ dhyātvā mānasairupacāraiḥ saṃpūjya yathokta   
parityā yonimudrāṃtastha puṣpākṣate samānīya punardhyātvā yaṃtra madhye   
cāvāhya yajet ||  
  
atha dhyānaṃ ||  
  
svanābhau nīrajaṃ dhyāyachuddhaṃ vikaśitaṃśitaṃ |  
tasya keśara madhye tu maṇḍalaṃ caṃḍarociṣaṃ ||  
  
japākusuma saṃkāśaṃ raktavaṃdhūka saṃnnibhaṃ |  
rajaḥ satva tamo rekhā yonimaṇḍalamaṇḍitaṃ ||  
  
viparīta ratiḥsthau ca dhyāyedrati manobhavau |  
ratiḥ kāmopavisthau ca dhyāyeddevīṃ manoharāṃ ||  
  
madhyetāṃ ca mahādevīṃ sūryakoṭiḥ samaprabhāṃ |  
chinnamastāṃkare vāme dhārayaṃtiṃ svamastakaṃ ||  
  
prasārita mukhī bhīmāṃ lelihānogra jihvikāṃ |  
pivaṃtiṃ raktadhārāṃ ca nijakaṇṭha samudbhavāṃ ||  
  
vikīrṇa keśapāśāṃ tāṃ nānāpuṣpa samanvitāṃ |  
dakṣiṇe ca kare kartṛṃ muṇḍamālāṃ vibhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
digaṃvarīṃ mahāghorāṃ pratyālīḍha padasthitāṃ |  
asthimālāṃ dharāṃ devī nāgayajñopavītinīṃ ||  
  
sadā ṣoḍaśavarṣīyāṃ pīnonna tapayodharāṃ |  
ḍākinī varṇinī yuktāṃ vāmadakṣiṇayogataḥ ||  
  
dakṣiṇevarṇinīṃ dhyāyed vāmapārśve tu ḍākinīṃ |  
varṇinīṃ lohitāṃ saumyāṃ muktakeśīṃ digaṃvarāṃ ||  
  
p. 179a)  
  
kapālakartṛkāṃ hastāṃ vāmadakṣiṇa yogataḥ |  
devīgalocchaladraktadhārāpānaṃ prakurvatāṃ ||  
  
asthimālāṃ dharāṃ devīṃ nāgayajñopavītinīṃ |  
ḍākinī vāmapārśve tu kalpāṃta jvalanopamāṃ ||  
  
vidyucchaṭābhanayanāṃ daṃtapaṃktivalākinīṃ |  
daṃṣṭrā karālavadanāṃ pīnonna tapayodharāṃ ||  
  
mahāghorāṃ mahādevīṃ muktakeśīṃ digaṃvarāṃ |  
laṃvodarīṃ kālarātrīṃ nāgayajñopavītinīṃ ||  
  
lelihāna mahājihvāṃ muṇḍamālāṃ vibhūṣitāṃ |  
kapālakartṛkāṃ hastāṃ vāma dakṣiṇayogataḥ ||  
  
devīgalocchaladraktadhārāpānaṃ prakurvatīṃ |  
karasthita kapālena bhīṣaṇenātibhīṣaṇāṃ ||  
  
ābhyāṃ niṣecyamānāṃ tu dhyāyeddevīṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ |  
evaṃ dhyātvā yajeddevī vāmanā bhakti yogataḥ ||  
  
vāhyārcāṃ tu tataḥ kuryāt puṣpaṃ naivedya dhūpakaiḥ ||  
  
atha dhyānāṃtaramāha ||  
  
bhairavoktamahaṃ vakṣye dhyānaṃ sarvasamṛddhidaṃ |  
svanābhau nīrajaṃ dhyāyet samyak vikaśitaṃ sitaṃ ||  
  
pūrvavat saṃkaraṃ dhyātvā ratikaṃ darpasaṃyutaṃ |  
ratikāmoparisthāṃ tu dhyāyeddevīṃ manoharāṃ ||  
  
tanmadhyetāṃ mahādevīṃ makārajaladopamāṃ |  
chinnamastāṃ kare vāme dhārayaṃtiṃ svamastakaṃ ||  
  
prasārita mukhīṃ devīṃ lelihāṃnogra jihvikāṃ |  
pivaṃtīṃ raktadhārāṃ ca nijakaṇṭha samudbhavāṃ ||  
  
vikīrṇa keśapāśāṃtāṃ nānāpuṣpa vibhūṣitāṃ |  
dakṣiṇe ca kare kartṛṃ muṇḍamālāṃ vibhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
śatārddhena nṛmuṇḍena mālāsrak parikalpitāṃ |  
anyonya keśapāśena grathitāṃ sumanoharāṃ ||  
  
digaṃvarāṃ mahārūpāṃ pratyālīḍha padāsthitāṃ |  
asthimālāṃ dharāṃ devīṃ nāgayajñopavītinīṃ ||  
  
sadā ṣoḍaśavarṣīyāṃ pīnonnatapayodharāṃ |  
nānāṃgadā nāgakāṃcīnāganūpurasaṃgatāṃ ||  
  
nāgakuṃḍala saṃyuktāṃ aṣṭanāga samanvitāṃ |  
anaṃto vāsukiścaiva takṣakarkoṭapadmakau ||  
  
mahāpadma tathā śaṃkhaḥ kulikoṣṭau prakīrtitā |  
anaṃtakulikau citrau karṇamūle niyojitau ||  
  
vāsukī śaṃkhapālaśca kṣatriyau pītavarṇakau |  
pratyekaṃ tu phalāsaptaśanasaṃkhyā virājitau ||  
  
p. 179b)  
  
nāgahārāṃ nāgakīṃcī yathāsthāna niyojitāṃ |  
takṣakaśca mahāpadmo vaiśyāvetau udāhṛtau ||  
  
nīlavarṇau phaṇā paṃcaśata yuktau tu sāṃgakau |  
aṃgadaṃ kathitaṃ devyāstābhyāṃ yuktaṃ manoharāṃ ||  
  
padmakarkoṭakau śūdrau raktavarṇāmudāhṛtau |  
phaṇātriṃśatasaṃyuktau nūpurau sumanoharau ||  
  
tābhyāṃ dhṛtāṃ chinnamastāṃ dhyāyedhyāna samādhinā |  
ḍākinīvaṇinīyuktāṃ vāmadakṣiṇa pārśvataḥ ||  
  
dakṣiṇe varṇinīṃ dhyātvā yetṛvāmapārśve tu ḍākinī |  
varṇinī śyāmalāṃ dhyāyet muktakeśīṃ digamvarāṃ ||  
  
kapālakartṛkā hastāṃ vāmadakṣiṇayogataḥ |  
devyā dakṣiṇa nāmāstudhāyapānaṃ prakurvatī ||  
  
muṇḍamālādharāṃ devīṃ nāgayajñopavitinīṃ |  
devyāḥ saṃdṛśa rūpeṇa bhūṣaṇena ca bhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
ḍākinīṃ vāmapārśve tu kalpāṃtajvalanopamāṃ |  
vidyudagni samudbhūtāṃ trinetrāṃ sunoharāṃ ||  
  
dāḍimī vījasadṛśa daṃtapaṃkti virājitāṃ |  
draṣṭrā karālavadanāṃ pīnonna tapayodharāṃ ||  
  
mahādevīṃ muktakeśīṃ mahāghorāṃ digaṃvarāṃ |  
lamvodarīṃ kālarātriṃ nāgayajñopavītinīṃ ||  
  
lelihānāgurasanīṃ muṇḍamālā vibhūṣaṇāṃ |  
kapālakartṛkāhastāṃ vāmadakṣiṇayogataḥ ||  
  
vāmanāḍyoguladraktadhārāpānaṃ prakurvatīṃ |  
karasthita kapālena bhīṣaṇenāti bhīṣaṇāṃ ||  
  
ābhyāṃ niṣevyamānāṃ tu dhyāyeddhyāna samādhinā |  
evaṃ dhyātvā yajeddevīṃ manasā bhaktiyogataḥ ||  
  
vāhyārcāṃ tu tataḥ kuryānnaivedyapuṣpadhūpakaiḥ |  
bhairavoktaṃmidaṃ dhyānaṃ kuryād yatnena deśikaḥ ||  
  
sarvasiddhipradaṃ sākṣyānmahāpātakanāśanaṃ ||  
  
yaḥ smaret prātarutthāya devyāḥ pūjanakepi vā tasya siddhirbhaveddevī   
vāṃchitārtha pradāyinī dhanaṃdhānyaṃ sutaṃ jāyāṃ dvayaṃ hasti na meva ca ||  
  
vasuvaṃdharāṃ mahāvidyāṃmaṣṭasiddhilabhettu saḥ ||  
  
p. 180a)  
  
atha vījaviśeṣādi maṃtrapakṣemāvarṇaviśeṣeṇadhyeyā ||  
  
tathā ca ||  
  
yenaṃ vījena cādyaina yadya dhyānaṃ taducyate |  
kāmādau niśadā dhyāyellajādau lohitāṃ tathā ||  
  
māyādau ca bhavet kṛṣṇāvāgādau vaidyuta prabhā ||  
  
atha yoni mudrāṃ vaddhvā tanmadhye raktacaṃdanākṣatajavāpuṣpaṃnidhāya tatra   
punardhyāyet ||  
  
yonimudrāṃ gataṃ kṛtvā sākṣataṃ raktapuṣpakaṃ |  
dhyāyedevīṃ mahāmāyāṃ sarvakalyāṇakāriṇīṃ ||  
  
sudhāsāgara dvīpe ca smaredudyānamadbhutaṃ |  
tasminnavasarastīreśobhanaṃ raktamaṃḍapaṃ ||  
  
caturdvāra samopetaṃ staṃbharājivirājitaṃ |  
gavākṣamārge daśakavāyuyukta sa kesaraṃ ||  
  
sudhāsaṃvisat tataṃ kalpavṛkṣa catuṣṭayaṃ |  
niviṣṭi ratnastaṃbhe ca saṃsmarennija devatāṃ ||  
  
śavāsanagatāṃ dhyoyet chinnamaṣṭāṃ mahodarīṃ |  
caturbhujāṃ śavārūḍhā raktavastrāṃ trilocanāṃ ||  
  
mukuṭāṭopa saṃpannāṃ dakṣiṇe khaḍgadhāriṇīṃ |  
sotpalāvā mahastena dorbhyāṃ pustakadhāriṇīṃ ||  
  
nikṛtya svaśiraḥ khaḍgaiḥ pivaṃti rudhiraṃ vahu |  
upaddinakarābhāṃ ca caṃdrārddhakṛtaśekharāṃ ||  
  
yogibhiḥ sevyāmaniśaṃ nāgayajñopavītinīṃ ||  
  
athāvāhanamaṃtrastu ||  
  
tatra cāvāhanaṃ kuryānān maṃtreṇānena sādhakaḥ |  
sarvasiddhiprade pūrvamuccaret sādhakottamaḥ ||  
  
varṇanīye tato vācya sarvasiddhiprade tataḥ |  
ḍākinīya tato vācyaṃ devīnāma tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
ehyehīti tato vācya maheti tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
tiṣṭatiṣṭeti vācyaṃ ca māyāyugmaṃ tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
phaḍakṣara samāyuktaṃ svāheti tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
ityāvāhanamuddiṣṭa sthāpanena samanvitaṃ ||  
  
athāsanadāne maṃtraviśeṣamāha ||  
  
athāvāhyāsanaṃ dadyāt maṃtrenānena sādhakaḥ |  
praṇavaṃ prathamaṃ kṛtvā sarvasiddhiprade tataḥ ||  
  
p. 180b)  
  
varṇanīye tato vācyaṃ praṇavaṃ ca tato vadet |  
ḍākinīya tato vācya praṇavaṃ ca tato vadet ||  
  
ihaśabdāstiṣṭatiṣṭamāye phaṭ svāhayāyutaṃ |  
tato dhyātvā yajeddevīṃ yuvatīṃ caṃdrarūpiṇī ||  
  
atha pūjāmāha ||  
  
mūlamaṃtreṇa saṃpūjya maṃḍalaṃsyāmaheśvarī |  
upacāraiḥ prapūjyātha prasūnai raṃjanaistataḥ ||  
  
tadanujāṃ gṛhītvā ca aṃgadevāṃ prapūjayet |  
tato dakṣiṇadeśasthāṃ varṇinīṃ pūjayet tathā ||  
  
praṇavāt sarasvatīvījaṃ prakṛtyai nāmanāmataḥ |  
tataśca vāmapārśvasthāṃ ḍākinīṃ pūjayennaraḥ ||  
  
pūrvavat praṇavādistu ḍākinyai nama ityapi ||  
  
trikoṇe pūjayedādau phaḍanta kavacena tu |  
kālikāṃ bhuvaneśīṃ ca mātaṃgīmīśa deśataḥ ||  
  
uttarādi tataḥ paścāt puṭeṣu ca yathākramaṃ |  
kāmākhyāṃ caiva bheruḍāṃ tathā nīlasarasvatīṃ ||  
  
māyāvījena prayajet mahāvibhava vistaraiḥ |  
bhairavaṃ pūjayeddevaṃ saṃmukhe vidhinā munā ||  
  
samrāṭ chaṃdo dakṣiṇe ca maṃtravarṇān tathauttare |  
vījaśaktī rakṣodiśi pūjayet kramataḥ sudhīḥ ||  
  
mātaraḥ padmamadhye ca brāhmyādyāḥ sarvasiddhidā |  
indrādi lokapālāntāḥ pūjyā astra samanvitāḥ ||  
  
bhūpure pūjayettāṃśca pūrvādi kramayogataḥ |  
pīṭhopari yajedrudraṃ paritaśca manoharaṃ ||  
  
pūrvādiṣu caturdvāre pūjayet sādhakottamaḥ |  
dvāropari mahālakṣmī brahmāṇaṃ cāgrato yajet ||  
  
k.etrapālaṃ karālaṃ ca vikarālaṃ tathā punaḥ |  
praṇavādi namāntena caturthyaṃ tapadena ca ||  
  
pūrvoktamastvanulomenoktaḥ punarasthāpi lomekamāntaramāha ||  
  
p. 181a)  
  
bāhyāvaraṇamārabhya pūjayen pratilomataḥ |  
bhūpurādvāhyabhāgeṣu vajrādīni prapūjayet ||  
  
tadantara surarājādīndvāreṣu dvārayānyajet |  
karāle vikarālaṃ cāti kālaṃ mahākālakaṃ ||  
  
ekaliṃgāṃ yoginīṃ ca ḍākinīṃ bhairavajendrākṣīhyasitāṃgīṃ saṃhāriṇīṃ ||  
  
ṣaḍkoṇeṣu ṣaḍaṃgāni trikoṇe chinnamastakā |  
ḍākinīṃ varṇinīṃ tārāvāgbhyātatpārśvayoryajet ||  
  
evaṃ pūjāprakartavyā validānaṃ tataścaret ||  
  
athādau bhūpurasya vāhye vajrādīni urddhve caṃdrādīn saṃpūjya pūrvādi   
krameṇa dvārapālān pūjayet ||  
  
pūrvadvāre karālaṃ ca vikarālaṃ ca dakṣiṇe |  
paścime cāti kālaṃ ca mahākālaṃ tathottare ||  
  
praṇavādi namontena pūjāmeṣāṃ samācaret ||  
  
athaiteṣāṃ dhyānamāha ||  
  
karālaṃ raktavarṇaṃ ca dvibhujaṃ dvīpasaṃsthitaṃ |  
paścime vikarālaṃ ca nīlanīraja saṃnibhaṃ ||  
  
aṃkuśaṃ puṣṭakaṃ vāme javāpuṣpa chaviṃ smaret |  
garuḍasthaṃ mahākāyaṃ trinetraṃ candraśekharaṃ ||  
  
mahākālaṃ tathā caiva dvibhujaṃ pītavāsasaṃ ||  
  
atha pūrvādi krameṇāṣṭadale caika liṃgādyā bhairavyaḥ pūjyā ||  
  
ekaliṃgāṃ mahādevī ḍhākinī yoginīṃ tathā |  
bhairavīṃ ca mahāpūrvāṃ bhairavīmatha suvrate ||  
  
iṃdrāṣī masitāṃgī ca tataḥ saṃhāriṇī kramāt |  
pūrvādike dale pūjyāḥ śaktayaḥ kramayogataḥ ||  
  
praṇavādi namontena lajjā vījayutena ca ||  
  
athāmākrameṇa dhyānamāha ||  
  
raktāṃ gaurīṃ tathā kṛṣṇā tathā raktāṃ ca piṃgalaṃ |  
pītāṃ muktāṃ ca dhūmrābhāṃ kathayāmi punaḥ kramaṃ ||  
  
p. 181b)  
  
triśūlavaradāmādyāṃ vyāghracarma samanvitāṃ |  
trilocanāṃ ca tanvaṃgī nāgayajñopavītinī ||  
  
dvitīyāṃ suṃdarālokāṃ daṃḍaśaṃkhadharāṃ kare |  
raktavastraparīdhātāṃ raktanāgopavītinīṃ ||  
  
asthimālādharāṃ devīṃ vaddhapadmāsanasthitāṃ |  
tṛtīyāṃ bhīṣaṇākārāṃ lalajihvāṃ mahodarīṃ ||  
  
kapālakartṛkāhastāṃ kṛṣṇanāgopavītinīṃ |  
ghoradaṃṣṭrāṃ mahāghorāmattimatto sudāruṇāṃ ||  
  
caturthī pāvakābhāsāṃ muṇḍamālā vibhūṣitāṃ |  
kapālakartṛkāhastāṃ khaḍgaśūlasamanvitaṃ ||  
  
āpiṃgakeśanicayoṃ pracaṃḍāṭṭāṭṭahāsinī |  
paṃcamīṃ vālasūryābhāṃ ṣaḍbhujāṃ dvipadā tathā ||  
  
trimukhiṃ ca mahogrāṃcca raktapītāsiptānanāṃ |  
kapālakartṛkāhastāṃ khaḍgaśūla samanvitāṃ ||  
  
jaṭājūṭārddha caṃdrāṃ ca prativaktraṃ trilocanāṃ |  
śavoparisthitāṃ devīmānīyasthānamāśritāṃ ||  
  
dvīpi carmaparīdhānāṃ vīraghaṃṭhā samanvitāṃ ||  
  
ṣaṣṭīsuvarṇavarṇābhāṃ sahasranayanojvalāṃ |  
śaṃkha cakra gadā padma vyagrahastāṃ manoharaṃ ||  
  
padmopari samāsīnāṃ kṛta padmāsanasthitā |  
pītavastra parīdhānāṃ snigdhanetrāṃ sudāruṇāṃ ||  
  
aṣṭhamī ca pravakṣyāmi kālajīmūta sannibhāṃ |  
trinetrāṃ ḍākinī devīṃ saṃhārakāriṇīṃ ||  
  
svābhiyuktāṃ sadā dhyāyeddevīṃ trailokyamātaraṃ |  
pūrvādīśānaparyaṃtaṃ pūjayedvidhivatkramāt ||  
  
atha validānaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ pūjāṃ vidhāyātha validānaṃ prakalpayet |  
dadyād valiṃ pāyasaṃ ca kṛśaraṃ madhusaṃyutaṃ ||  
  
sa koṣaṃ madhusaṃyuktaṃ raṃbhā puṣpaṃ tathaiva ca |  
aṃtarāntarato devi paśudānaṃ vidhīyate ||  
  
p. 182a)  
  
samabhyarcya valiṃ pūrvegaṃdha puṣpāṃdinvandanai |  
dhenumudrāṃ pradarśyātha vāmāguṣṭena saṃspṛśet ||  
  
yaṃ mantreśodhanaṃ kṛtvāraṃ maṃtre dāruyettataḥ |  
ṭhaṃ maṃtreṇāmṛtaṃ bhāvyaṃ vaṃ maṃtre plāvayeccata ||  
  
tryaṣṭadhā prajapenmaṃtraṃ mūlaṃ ṅentaṃ nivedayet |  
pradarśya saṃmukhe taṃtu punarācamanaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
atha validānamaṃtra ||  
  
saṃvuddhyaṃta padaṃ vrūyāddehi ehi padaṃ tataḥ |  
gṛhna gṛhna imaṃ vrūyādvali śabdastataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
mamaśabdaṃ samābhāṣya siddhiṃ dehi padadvayaṃ |  
kavaca dvitayaṃ coktvā karālike padaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
phaṭ svāhānto mahāmaṃtro validānaṃ vidhau smṛtaḥ ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ cāpi sahasraṃ vā maheśvari |  
japaṃ samācarenmaṃtrī kullukādyaṃ yathāvidhi ||  
  
japāṃte ca stutiṃ kuryānmālikāṃ śirasi kṣipet |  
japapūjāṃ samāpyaivaṃ stutvā ca kavacaṃ paṭhet ||  
  
tatrādau krodhabhairavasya maṃtro japtavyaḥ ||  
  
stathā ca ||  
  
ādau japtvā bhairavasya krodhasyāsya manuṃ japet |  
asthimālāṃ samādāya vajra vairocanī manu ||  
  
atha krodhabhairavasya maṃtramāha ||  
  
atha krodha manuṃ vakṣye asādhyaṃ yena siddhyati |  
vījaṃ hālāhalaṃ gṛhya krodha vījamataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
bhayaṃkarārṇamābhāṣyāśitāṃgakṣatajasthitaṃ |  
pralayāgnirmahājvālāmābhāṣya manumuddharet ||  
  
evamuccāritaḥ krodhaḥ svayameva prasiddhyati ||  
  
atha ṣaḍaṅganyāsaḥ ||  
  
tatastu krodha maṃtreṇa ṣaḍaṅganyā samācaret |  
viṣaṃ vajrayutaṃ vodhi mahākālaṃ nyased hṛdi ||  
  
p. 182b)  
  
viṣaṃhanayugaṃ vajra kūrcādyaṃ vinyasedvahi |  
hālāhale dehayutaṃ vajrakālanyasecchikhāṃ ||  
  
viṣamaṃtrayutaṃ vajramāyudhaṃ kavacanyaset |  
tāravījayutaṃ vajramāyudhaṃ kavacanyaset ||  
  
tāravījayutaṃ vajramahākālāya netrayo |  
viṣaṃ hanayutaṃ gṛhya daha gṛhya padānvitaṃ ||  
  
krodhaṃ vajrayugaṃ tadvat sarvaduṣṭānathāparaṃ |  
talomāraya varmāstraṃ digvaṃdhāntaṃ ṣaḍagakaṃ ||  
  
atha dhyānamāha ||  
  
tatra madhyenyasedbhīmaṃ taptajvālā samākulaṃ |  
sāṭṭahāsaṃ mahāraudraṃ bhinnāṃjana ca yopamaṃ ||  
  
pratyālīḍhaṃ caturvāhuṃ dakṣiṇe cakradhāriṇa |  
tarjanaṃ vāmahastena tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrākarālinaṃ ||  
  
kapālaratnamukuṭaṃ trailokyasya vināyakaṃ |  
ādityakoṭisaṃkāśa aṣṭhanāga vibhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
aparājita padākrāṃta mudrā vālalaviṣṭitaṃ |  
anāmikā dvayaṃ vadhvā ākuṃcya tarjanīdvayaṃ ||  
  
kaniṣṭhāṃ madhyamā caiva jyeṣṭāṃguṣṭhena ca kramāt |  
eṣa mudrādharaḥ śrīmān trailokyā sādhyasādhakaḥ ||  
  
atha stuti ||  
  
iti pūjārvidhīṃ kṛtvā ca yathā valaṃ ||  
  
vāṃchitārtha prasiddhyarthabhimaṃstavamudīrayet ||  
  
nābhau śuddhasarojamadhyavilasadvandhūka punyāruṇaṃ |  
bhāsvadbhāskaramaṃḍalaṃ tadudaraṃ yadyonicakraṃ mahat ||  
  
tanmadhya viparita maithuna parapradyumna tatkāminī |  
pṛṣṭhasthāṃ taruṇārkakoṭi vilasattejasvarūpāṃ śivāṃ ||  
  
vāme chinnadharāṃ śirottare pāṇau vṛhatkartṛkāṃ |  
pratyālīḍha padāṃ digantavasanomāyuktakeśamrajāṃ ||  
  
p. 183a)  
  
chinnātmīya śiraḥ samucchaladasṛgdhārāṃ pivaṃtīṃ parāvālāditya   
samaprakāśavilasannetra trayodbhāsinīṃ ||  
  
vāmādanyatra nāḍī vahuvahalagaladraktadhārābhiruccaiḥ   
pāyantīmasthibhūṣāṃkarakamalalasat kartṛkāmugrarūpāṃ |  
raktāmāraktakeśīmapagatavasanāṃvarṇinīmātmaśaktiṃ pratyālīḍhogra   
pādāmaruṇitamayanāṃ yoginīṃ yogamudrāṃ ||  
  
digvastrāṃsrastakeśīṃ pralayaghanaghaṭā ghorarūpāṃ pracaṇḍāṃ |  
daṃṣṭrāduḥprekṣyavaktrodaravivaralasallolajihvograbhāsāṃ ||  
  
vidyullola jihvograbhāsāṃ ||   
  
vidyullolākṣigugmāṃ hṛdayataṭalasadbhogibhīmāṃ svamūrtiṃ |  
sadya chinnātmakaṃṭhapragalita rudhirairḍākinīṃ varddhayaṃtīṃ ||  
  
brahmeśānācyutādyaiḥ śirasi vinihitā mandapādāravindāḥ |  
mātmājñeryogimukhyaiḥ patidinamaviśaṃ ciṃtināṃ cityarūpāṃ ||  
  
saṃsāre sārabhūtāṃ tribhuvanajananīṃ chinnamastāṃ praśastā |   
viṣṭāṃtāamiṣṭadātrīṃ kalikaluṣaharāṃ cetasā ciṃtayāmi ||  
  
utpattisthiti saṃhṛtīrghaṭayatuṃ dhatte trirūṣāṃ tanuṃ |  
traiguṇyājjagato yadīya vikṛtirbrahmācyutaṃ bhūlabhṛt ||  
  
mātādyāṃ prakṛtiṃ smarāmi sa tataṃ sarvārtha saṃsiddhaye |  
yasyā smarepadāravindayugalaṃsaṃto bhajente sadā ||  
  
alipiśitapurandhrī yogapūjāparohaṃ vahuvidha kulabhārārambha saṃbhāvitohaṃ ||  
  
paśujanaviratoha bhairavī saṃsthitohaṃ |  
gurucaraṇa parohaṃ bhairavohaṃ śivohaṃ ||  
  
imaṃ stavaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ brahmaṇābhāṣitaṃ purā |  
yaḥ paṭhet prātarutthāya devyāḥ sannihitopi vā ||  
  
tasya siddhirbhaveddevī vāṃchitārtha pradāyinī |  
dhanadhānyaṃ sutaṃ jāyā hayaṃ hasti nameva vā ||  
  
p. 183b)  
  
vasundharāṃ mahāvidyāmaṣṭau siddhirllabheddhruvaṃ ||  
  
iti bhairava prokto devyāḥ stavaḥ samāptaḥ ||  
  
atha kavacaṃ ||  
  
bhairavyuvāca ||  
  
kathitā chinnamastāyādyāyā vidyā sugopitā |  
tvayā nāthena jīvena śrutā ca gaditā mayā ||  
  
idānīṃ śrotumicchāmi kavacaṃ pūrvasūcitaṃ |  
trailokyavijayaṃ nāma kṛpayā kathyatāṃ vibhau ||  
  
bhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu vakṣyāmi deveśi sarvadeva namaskṛte |  
trailokya vijayaṃ nāma kavacaṃ sarvamohanaṃ ||  
  
sarvavidyāmayaṃ sākṣāt surāsura jayapradaṃ |  
dhāraṇāt paṭhanādīśastrailokyavijayīvituḥ ||  
  
brahmānārāyaṇā rudro dhāraṇāt paṭhanādyataḥ |  
kartā pātā ca saṃhartā bhuvanāṃnāṃ sureśvari ||  
  
na deyaṃ paraśiṣyebhyo abhaktebhyo viśeṣataḥ |  
deyaṃ śiṣyāya bhaktāya prāṇebhyopyadhikāya ca ||  
  
devyāśca chinnamastāyāḥ kavacasya ca bhairavaḥ |  
ṛṣiḥ samrāṭ virāṭ chando devatā chinnamastakā ||  
  
trailokya vijaya muktau viniyogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |  
hū&kāro me śiraḥ pātu chinnamastānatvaprabhā ||  
  
hrī& hū& ai& tryakṣarī pātu bhālaṃ raktādigamvarī |  
śrī& hrī& hū& ai& dṛśo pātu muṃḍakartṛdharāpimā ||  
  
sā vidyā praṇavādyaṃtā śruti yugmaṃ sadāvatu |  
vajra vairocanī ye hū& hū& phaṭ svāhā dhruvādikaḥ ||  
  
ghrāṇaṃ pātu chinnamastā svamuṃḍakartṛdhāriṇī |  
śrīmāyā kūrca vāgvīje vajra vairocanīya hū& ||  
  
hū& phaṭ svāhā mahāvidyā ṣoḍaśī brahmarūpiṇī |  
svayādyā dvāramabhyukṣya dakṣiṇa vāma pārśvayoḥ ||  
  
p. 184a)  
  
uparyadhastritārānte svanāmādyarṇa vījataḥ |  
gaṇeśaṃ kṣetrapālaṃ ca tathā dvāraśriyaṃ puna ||  
  
dehalī ca samabhyarcya praviśedyāgamandiraṃ ||  
  
āgneyādiṣu madhye dikṣu yathā kramaṃ |  
tritāranā sa vījānne pūjayedgaṇapādikān ||  
  
gaṇeśa durgā vaṭuka kṣetrapāla catuṣṭayaṃ |  
ratnamaṇḍapamabhyarcya kāmavaṃratiyutaṃ ||  
  
vasaṃtaprīti sahitaṃ tannodevi sarasvatīṃ |  
śriyaṃ paścāt samabhyarca vikiret kusumāṃjali ||  
  
athavā daśadikṣu daśaśakti samabhyarcya madhye vāgīśvarīṃ puṣpāṃjali mā   
dīpanāthaṃ yajet ||  
  
sarasvatīṃ śriyaṃ māyāṃ durgāṃ ca tadanantaraṃ |  
bhadrakāliṃ tathā svastīṃ svāhā caiva śubhaṃkarīṃ ||  
  
gaurīṃ ca lokadhātrīṃ ca tathā vāgīśvarīmapi |  
rakta dvādaśa śaktidbhiḥ sahitaṃ dīpanāthakaṃ ||  
  
tritārayogaḥ sarvatra vijñeyaḥ sādhakottamaiḥ |  
sāmānya kramavatkāryamaparaṃ sādhakottamaiḥ ||  
  
bhūtaśuddhiṃ vidhāyetthaṃ mātṛkānyā samācaret |  
prāṇāyāma trayaṃ kṛtvānyāsānanyān samācaret ||  
  
atha vakṣye maheśāni śrīvidyānyāsamuttamaṃ ||  
  
athādau ṛṣyādinyāsa ||  
  
ṛṣirasya maheśāni dakṣiṇāmūrtiravyayaḥ |  
paṃktiḥ chandaḥ samākhyāto devī tripurasundarī ||  
  
vāgbhavaṃ vījamityuktaṃ śaktistu śaktikūṭakaṃ |  
kāmarājaḥ kīlakaṃ syādriṣyādinyāsa īritaḥ ||  
  
atha karāṅganyāsaḥ ||  
  
a& ā& sau& ritiproktaṃ vījaṃ vividhamuttamaṃ |  
etadvījaṃ dvirāvṛtya madhyamāṃdyaṃgulīṣu ca ||  
  
śuddhiṃ karasya kurvītatalayoḥ pṛṣṭhayorapi |  
caturthīnati saṃyuktānāma maṃtraiḥ pṛthak pṛathak ||  
  
p. 184b)  
  
madhyamānāmikā caiva kanyaṣṭhāṃguṣṭha tarjanī |  
krameṇa nāmavyākhyātamaṃgulīnāṃ maheśvarī ||  
  
athātmarakṣāṃ digvaṃdhanaṃvāha ||  
  
vālīvījaṃ trayaḥ pūrvaṃ tathā tripurasuṃdari |  
ātmānaṃ rakṣarakṣeti kuryādrakṣāṃ hṛdi spṛśan ||  
  
tathaivāstreṇa mudrāyāḥ kuryādigvaṃdhanaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
athāsananyāsaḥ ||  
  
amṛtārṇava śabdapūrva āsanāya tato manuḥ |  
pādayorvinyaset paścādvālāṃta tripureśvarī ||  
  
potāṃvujāsanāyāṃte namojānūvininyaset ||  
  
ai& klī& sau& tripuret yuktvā suṃdarīti padaṃ tataḥ |  
ṅentaṃ devyāsane cāṃtena madduru dvayaṃ nyaset ||  
  
hai& hvrī& hsau&ḥ te& tripuravāsinīti ca ||  
  
cakrāsanā ityamunā sphigadvaya pravinyaset ||  
  
hyai& hstrī& hstrau& * * * * * * * * *   
  
sarvamaṃtrāsanāyāṃte namoguhya pravinyaset |  
hrī& klī& tripuramālinyaṃte tataḥ sādhya padaṃ vadet ||  
  
tatasmiddhāsanaṃ ṅeṃtaṃ nābhideśe pravinyaset |  
hsrai& hśrī& hsrau& maṃtre tripurāmvā padaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
paryaṃka śaktipīṭhāsanāya namo vakṣasi vinyaset |  
trīkūṭavidyā vījāṃte mahātripurabhairavī ||  
  
sadāśiva mahāpreta yadā padmāsanāya ca |  
nama ityamunā brahmaraṃdhrasthāne pravinyaset ||  
  
atha ṣaḍaṃganyāsaḥ ||  
  
sarvajñatā nitya su tṛptitā ca anādi bodhaśca svataṃtratā ca |  
aluptatā śaktimanaṃtatā ca ṣaḍādgaraṃgāni śivayoḥ śivādyāḥ ||  
  
vījāṃte nāma saṃyojya jātiyuktaṃ ṣaḍaṃkaṃ ||  
  
saṃpūrṇāṃ ciṃtayedvidyāṃ brahmaraṃdhreruṇa prabhāṃ |  
sravatsudhāṃ ṣoḍaśārṇāṃ mahāsaubhāgyadāṃ smaret ||  
  
vāmāṃgadeśe saubhāgyadaṇḍinī bhrāmayet tataḥ |  
viśvajihvāgrahammudrāṃ pādānmūlenyaset priye ||  
  
trailokyasyatvahaṃ kartā dhyātvaivaṃ kīlakanyaset |  
saṃpūrṇāmeva vadane veṣṭanatvena vinyaset ||  
  
punaḥ saṃpūrṇaṃ vadane galārddhaṃ vinyasettayā |  
punaḥ saṃpūrṇajā dehe vyāpakatvena vinyaset ||  
  
vyāpakāṃte yonimudrāṃ mukhe kṣiptvābhinaṃdya ca |  
śrīvidyāpūrṇarūpoyaṃ nyāsaḥ saubhāgyavarddhanaḥ ||  
  
p. 185a)  
  
trailokyaṃ kṣobhavetyā śunyāsaṃ sannaddhavigrahaḥ ||  
  
atha daṇḍinīmudrā ||  
  
muṣṭiṃ dhṛtvā caranmaṃtrī tarjanī daṇḍavat tadā |  
saubhāgyadaṇḍinīnāma ripūn daṇḍayate kṣaṇāt ||  
  
atha ripu jihvāgrahāḥ ||  
  
aṃguṣṭaṃ muṣṭigaṃ kuryād ripujihvāgrahā bhavet ||  
  
atha yonimudrā yathā ||  
  
saṃyojya hastau deveśi tarjanyāḥ nāmikāṃ yajet |  
tadvadvāmena saṃsṛjyayonyākāreṇa yojayet ||  
  
paribhrāmyā nāmikāstu murddhānaṃ paritaḥ priye ||  
  
atha saṃmohana nyāsaḥ ||  
  
brahmaraṃdhre jayeddevī maṇivaṃdhe nyaset tataḥ |  
lalāṭe mālikāṃ kuryāt ṣoḍaśārṇāḥ smaredbudhaḥ ||  
  
trailokyamaruṇaṃ dhyāyan śrīvidyāṃ manasi smaret |  
saṃmohanākhyā deveśi nyāsoyaṃ kṣobhakārakaḥ ||  
  
atha saṃhāranyāsaḥ ||  
  
pādayorjaṃghayorjānvoḥ kadyolaṃ dhūnipṛṣṭake |  
nābhau pārśvadvayoścaiva stanayoraṃśayostathā ||  
  
karṇayorbrahmaraṃdhre ca vadane'ndhūni pārvatī |  
tataḥ karmapradeśe tu naraveṣṭanataḥ kramāt ||  
  
saṃhāroyaṃ mahānyāso bījaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ kramāt |  
śrīvidyāyāḥ ṣoḍaśārṇairnyāsairviśveśvaro bhavet ||  
  
sṛṣṭyarthaṃ vinyaseddevī mātṛkāṃ pūrvavat priye ||  
  
atha vasinyādinyāsaḥ ||  
  
mātṛkārṇaḥ svarūpāṃ ca varṇāṣṭaka samanvitāṃ |  
veśinīṃ mātṛkān yasya bījāṣṭaka samanvitāṃ ||  
  
avargāṃte likhedvījaṃ vahni phāṃte samanvitaṃ |  
vāmakarṇe viśobhāḍhyaṃ viṃdunādāṃkitaṃ priye ||  
  
veśinī pūjayed vācāṃ devatāṃ devasuvrate |  
kavarāṃte maheśāni kāmeśī vījamuttamaṃ ||  
  
merubhṛtaṃ samuccārya vāgdevīṃ pūjayet tataḥ |  
ca vargāṃte dhvāṃtarāṃ takṣamāturya svarānvitaṃ ||  
  
mādinīṃ pūjayed vācāṃ devatāṃ tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
ṭa vargāṃte vāyuvījaṃ bhūmisaṃsthaṃ maheśvarī ||  
  
vāmakarṇeṃdu viṃdvādyaṃ vimalāṃ vāgadhīśvarīṃ |  
ta vargāṃte yamakṣmādyaṃ vāmanetraṃ vibhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
biṃdunādāṃkitaṃ vījaṃ vāgdevī manunā yajet |  
pa vargāṃte vyomacaṃdrakṣyātājānila saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
p. 185b)  
  
ūkārasvara saṃyuktaṃ viṃdunāda kalātmakaṃ |  
jayaṃtīṃ pūjayed vācāṃ devatāṃ suravaṃdite ||  
  
ya vargāṃte yāṃtakālarepha vāyusamanvitaṃ |  
vāmakarṇeṃdu viṃdvāḍhyaṃ sarveśīṃ paripūjayet ||  
  
kṣamā vahnigataṃ sūryaṃ vījena pariveṣṭitaṃ |  
viṃdunādakalākrāṃtaṃ kaulinīṃ vācamarcayet ||  
  
śa vargāṃte mahādevīṃ nyaset sarvārthasiddhaye |  
śiro lalāṭe bhrūmadhye karṇahṛnnābhi maṇḍale ||  
  
ādhāradehakaṃ yāvannyaseddevīṃ parā priye ||  
  
atha ṣoḍhānyāsaḥ ||  
  
ṣoḍhānyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryādyena brahmāṇḍarūpa dhṛk |  
virāṭ svarūpa varṇātmā śivaḥ sākṣānna saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
gaṇeśaḥ prathamonyāsaḥ sarvavighnavināśakaḥ |  
taruṇāditya saṃkāśān gajavaktrāṃ trilocanāṃ ||  
  
pāśāṃkuśa varābhīti karālśakti samanvitān |  
etāstu vinyaseddevī mātṛkānyāsavatpriye ||  
  
vighneśvara śriyāmukto vighnanāthaḥ hriyānvitaḥ |  
vināyakastathā tuṣṭiḥ śāṃtiyuktaḥ śivottamaḥ ||  
  
vighnahṛt puṣṭiyuktā ca vighnakartā sarasvatī |  
vighnarāṭ ratiyuktāśca medhā ca gaṇanāyakaḥ ||  
  
ekadaṃtaścakāṃtiśca dvidaṃtaḥkāminīpatiḥ |  
gajavaktro mohanī ca niraṃjana jaṭā tathā ||  
  
kaparddabhṛt tathā tīvrā dīrghavaktra tataḥ priye |  
jvālinī sahitaḥ paścānnaṃdā saṃkarṣaṇastathā ||  
  
vṛṣadhvajaśca surasā gaṇanāthena saṃyutā |  
kāmarūpānikāṃ paścādgajeṃdraśca guhā yutaḥ ||  
  
śūpakarṇastu japinī trinetraḥ satyayā yutaḥ |  
lambodaraśca vighneśi mahānāda svarūpiṇī ||  
  
caturmūrtiḥ kāmadā ca sadāśivayutā tataḥ |  
madavihvalā mahānāda āmodo vijayā tathā ||  
  
durmukhaśca tathā ghūrṇā sumukhā bhūmidā tathā |  
pramodaśca tathā bhūmireka pādastathā satī ||  
  
dvijihvaśca ramāyuktaḥ śūlaśca dhvajinīyutaḥ |  
vīraśca karṇayuktaṃ ca śailāśca makaradhvajā ||  
  
ṣaṇmukhaśca vikarṇaṃ hi varado bhrukuṭī tathā |  
vāmadevastathā lajjā vakratuṇḍastataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
dīrghaghoṇānvitaḥ paścāt dviraṇḍaka dhanurddharau |  
senānīyāminīyukto grāmiṇīrātri saṃyutaḥ ||  
  
p. 186a)  
  
tamaśca caṃdrikāyukto vimaleśca śaśīyutaḥ |  
mattavāhana lolā ca jaṭī ca capalākṣiṇī ||  
  
muṇḍi ṛddhiyutaḥ paścāt khaḍgī ca śubhagāyutaḥ |  
vareṇyaścaiva garbhā ca vṛṣake tu stathā śivā ||  
  
bhaktapriyaḥ satvadā ca meghanādaścakāriṇī |  
gajeśaḥ kālakubjā ca gaṇeśo vighnahāriṇī ||  
  
mātṛkārṇairnyaseddevī grahanyāsastato bhavet |  
raktaṃ śvetaṃ tathā raktaṃ śyāmaṃ pītaṃ tu pāṇḍuraṃ ||  
  
dhūmraṃ kṛṣṇaṃ tathā dhūmraṃ raktadhūmraṃ viciṃtayet |  
ravimukhyān kāmarūpān sarvābharaṇabhūṣitān ||  
  
svarairarkaṃ hṛdīnyasyedyavageṇaśaśītataḥ |  
bhūmadhye ca kavargeṇa bhaumaṃ netraṃ trayanyaset ||  
  
ca vargeṇa budhaḥ kukṣīṭa vargeṇa vṛhaspatiṃ |  
hṛdayoparivinyasyattavargeṇa gale bhṛguṃ ||  
  
pa vargeṇa śaniṃ nābhau rāhuvaktreśavargataḥ |  
lakṣābhyāṃ tu guḍeketuṃ nyasede varānane ||  
  
atha nakṣatra vṛṃdānāṃ nyāsaṃ kuryāt sukhapradaṃ |  
jvalat kālāgnisaṃkāśāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ||  
  
matipāṇyāśvinī mukhyā varadā bhayapāṇayaḥ |  
yugmaṃ yugmaṃ tathā yugmaṃ yugmaṃ yugmena rohiṇī ||  
  
ekamevaṃ tathā dvaṃdvameka puṣpābhamucyate |  
lalāṭe rocane paścād vāmadakṣiṇakarṇayoḥ ||  
  
nāsyādvaye ca deveśi tathā kaṃṭhe nyaset kramāt |  
puṣpābhaṃ tu pravinyasya khagābhyāṃ śleṣmanāmakaṃ ||  
  
dakṣaṃ skaṃdhe ghaḍābhyāṃ tu maghāskaṃdhe dvitīyake |  
cā pūrvaphālguṇī dakṣe kūrparecchaja saṃsthitā ||  
  
uttarā phālguṇīṃ vāme kūrpare vinyaset priye |  
ū ñavarṇasthito hasto maṇivaṃdhe ca dakṣiṇe ||  
  
citrāṭaḍha parātmā ca maṇivaṃdhe nyaset priye |  
ḍa varṇāṃte tathā svātī viśāṣāḍha sa varṇagāḥ ||  
  
vinyaset kramato devī dakṣa vāme stanadvaye |  
tathadasthānurādhāḥ ca nābhau nyaset tu pārvatī ||  
  
dhakāreṇa yutāṃ jyeṣṭāṃ nyased dakṣakaṭau priye |  
na paphadyāṃ tathā mūlāṃ nyased vāmakaṭau priye ||  
  
purvāṣāḍhāṃ vakāreṇa dakṣorau vinyaset tataḥ |  
bhakāreṇottarāṣāḍhāṃ vāmorau tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
makārayuktāṃ śravaṇāṃ dakṣajānuni vinyaset |  
parasthitāṃ dhaniṣṭhāṃ tu vāmajānūni vinyaset ||  
  
lakāreṇa mahādevīnyasecchatabhiṣāṃ priye |  
dakṣajaṃghā gatāṃ paścāt pūrvabhādrapadāṃ tataḥ ||  
  
vaśavarṇaḥ sthitāṃ nyasedvāma jaṃghāgataḥ kramāt |  
ṣasahottara bhādrapadāṃ tathā dakṣiṇapādake ||  
  
p. 186b)  
  
rakṣābhyāṃ viṃdusargābhyāṃ revatīṃ ca tathā priye |  
kṣakāreṇa tato viṃdu visargābhyāṃ ca revatīṃ ||  
  
vāmapāde pravinyasya yoginīnyā samācaret |  
sitāsitāruṇāṃ ca bhruścitrāpītāśca ciṃtayet ||  
  
caturbhujāḥ samairvaktraiḥ sarvābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ |  
ḍāṃḍīṃ vījadvayaṃ coktvā ḍamaravarayetpriye ||  
  
vāmakarṇeṃdu nādāḍhyo ḍākinīṃ nama ityapi |  
svanāṃte tu pravaktavyaṃ cāṃte rakṣapada dvayaṃ ||  
  
tvagatmane kaṇṭhadeśe viśuddhau vinyaset priye |  
kakārādyairākinīṃ tu rakārādyaikṣaraiḥ kramāt ||  
  
pūrvavadvījasaṃyuktairasṛgātmāṃ ca saṃnyaset |  
anāhataṃ nyaset paścāddakārādi phakāragaiḥ ||  
  
rākinī ca tathā devī sāṃsānmāmaṇipūrake |  
varavarṇaiḥ kākinīṃ tu svādhisthāne tathābhidhāṃ ||  
  
madaḥ svarūpāṃ vinyaset ṣasavarṇaiśca kiṃkinīṃ |  
mūlādhāresthi rūpāṃ tu vinyased vīravaṃdite ||  
  
hakṣavarṇaiḥ sitāṃ caiva majjā hākinīkāṃ yajet |  
brahmaraṃdhre maheśāni nyāsoyaṃ yoginī kramāt ||  
  
rāśinyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryāt sarvarakṣākaraṃ sadā |  
raktāśveta haridvarṇaḥ pāṇḍuścitrāsitānyaset ||  
  
piśaṃgaṃ piṃgalau vabhruvarvurāśita dhūmatāṃ |  
akārādi catuḥkena vinyaset suravaṃdite ||  
  
meṣa dakṣiṇa gulphe tu tato dvaṃdvena vai vṛṣaṃ |  
nyasejjānū nivedastu mithunaṃ vṛṣaṇe tataḥ ||  
  
dvābhyāṃ karkaṭa saṃkukṣau dvābhyāṃ skaṃdhe tu siṃhakau |  
anusvāra visargābhyāṃśa vargeṇa ca kanyakāṃ ||  
  
dakṣiṇe tu śorobhāge vinyased vīravaṃdite |  
tathā vāmaśirobhāge kavargeṇa tulānyaset ||  
  
ca vargeṇa tathā skaṃdhe vṛścikaṃ vinyaset priye |  
ṭa vargeṇa tathā saṃdhau dhanvinaṃ vinyaset priye ||  
  
makaraṃ tu ta vargeṇa vṛṣaṇe vinyaset priyet |  
pa vargeṇa tathā kuṃbhe vāmajānūni vinyaset ||  
  
ya vargeṇa kṣakāreṇa mīnaṃ gulphe tulātmake ||  
  
atha pīṭhānividhināvinyaset suravaṃdite |  
sitāsitā'ruṇaḥ śyāmaharityāṃtānyavu kramāt ||  
  
punaḥ punaḥ kramāddevī paṃcāśat pīṭhapaṃktayaḥ |  
pīṭhāni saṃsmarevidvān sarvakāmārthasiddhaye ||   
  
p. 187a)  
  
kāmarūpaṃ mahāpīṭhaṃ vārāṇasīṃ tataḥ |  
nepālaṃ ca tathā pīṭhaṃ tathā vai pauṃḍuvarddhanaṃ ||  
  
puraḥ sthitaṃ tathāpīṭhaṃ carasthitaṃ tataḥ paraṃ |  
pūrṇaśailaṃ mahāpīṭhaṃ narvudaṃ ca tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
āmrāṭakeśvaraṃ pīṭhamekāmaṃ ca tataḥ paraṃ |  
tisrotaṃ pīṭhamanaghaṃ kāmakoṭi mataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
kailāśaṃ bhṛgupīṭhaṃ ca kedāraṃ caṃdrapūrakaṃ |  
śrīpīṭhaṃ ca tathoṅkāraṃ jālaṃdhara mataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
mālavaṃ ca tathā pīṭhaṃ kulāṃtaṃ devakoṭakaṃ |  
gokarṇaṃ ca mahāpīṭhaṃ māruteśvarameva ca ||  
  
aṭṭahāsaṃ ca virajaṃ pīṭhaṃ rājagṛhaṃ tathā |  
mahāpīṭhaṃ kollagiri melāpuramataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
koleśvaraṃ mahāpīṭhaṃ mahāpīṭhaṃ jayaṃtikāṃ |  
pīṭhamarjayinī caiva vicitraṃ kṣīrikābhidhaṃ ||  
  
hastināpūrapīṭhaṃ ca uḍḍīśaṃ ca prayāgakaṃ |  
ṣaṣṭhīśaṃ ca tathā pīṭhaṃ māyuḥpuraṃ jaleśvaraṃ ||  
  
malayaṃ ca mahāpīṭhaṃ śrīśailaṃ merukaṅgiriṃ |  
mahendraṃ vāmanaṃ caiva hiraṇyapurameva ca ||  
  
mahālakṣmīmayaṃ pīṭhaṃ oḍḍīyānamataḥ paraṃ |  
chāyāchatraparaṃ pīṭhaṃ tathaiva parameśvarī ||  
  
pañcāśat pīṭhavinyāsaṃ mātṛkāṃ vinyaset priye ||  
  
gaṇeśaiḥ prathamonyāsaḥ dvitīyastu grahaiḥ smṛtaḥ |  
nakṣatraistu tṛtīyaḥ syādyoginībhiścaturthakaḥ ||  
  
rāśibhiḥ paṃcamo jñeyaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ pīṭhairnigadyate |  
evaṃ tripurasuṃdaryāḥ ṣoḍhānyāsaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
ṣoḍhānyāsaṃ mahādevīnyaset sākṣāt sadāśivaḥ ||  
  
atha tripurānyāsaḥ ||  
  
tripurākhyaṃ tato nyāsaṃ kuryāt kāmārtha siddhaye |  
trivījapūrvā mātṛkādyā ṅenamontā maheśvarī ||  
  
tripurākhyānnyaseddevī mātṛkāyāḥ sthale kramāt |  
asyāstunyāsa mātreṇa jīvanmukto bhavennaraḥ ||  
  
atha kāmaratinyāsaḥ ||  
  
atha kāmānnyaseddevī dāḍimī kusuma prabhān |  
vāmāṅgaśakti sahitān puṣpavāṇekṣukārmukān ||  
  
śaktistu kuṃkumanibhāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ |  
nīlotpalakarādhyeyā trailokyākarṣaṇakṣamāḥ ||  
  
nyaset kāmaṃ ratīṃ paścāt kāmaprītipareśvarī |  
kānteśaḥ kāminī yukto bhrāṃto vai mohinī yutaḥ ||  
  
kāmukaḥ kamalāyuktaḥ kāmacāro vilāsinī |  
karṇakalpalate tadvat komalasyāmale tataḥ ||  
  
kāmavarddhana saṃyuktā vijayā caṃḍavismṛtā |  
tārāstu vidyayā yukto viśālākṣī yuto namaḥ ||  
  
p. 187b)  
  
vimalo lalitāyukto rātrinātha digaṃvare |  
ratipriyaśca rāmāśca ratināthaśca kubjikā ||  
  
malaśca kāṃtayā yukto ramaṇaḥ satyayāyutaḥ |  
niśākaraśca kalyāṇī maṇḍano bhoginī tathā ||  
  
naṃdīśaḥ kāmadāyukto madanaśca sulocana |  
sulāvaṇyāyuto devī tathā naṃdāyitābhidhaḥ ||  
  
niśācaraścamedinyā rahitāṅga tataḥ paraṃ |  
kalahapriyayāyuktaḥ puṣpadhanvācakāṃkṣiṇī ||  
  
mahādhanuśca sumukhī grāmiṇī nalinī yutaḥ |  
bhīmaśca jaṭinī yukto bhrāmaṇe yāminī yutaḥ ||  
  
bhramaṇaḥ śikhinī yuktaḥ śyāmamugdhe tataḥ paraṃ |  
bhrāmaṇī ramayā yukto bhṛgurbhūmī tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
bhrāṃtabhrāmaralolā ca bhrāmāvahasuyaṃcare |  
mohano dīrghajihvā ca sevakaśca tathā satī ||  
  
tathā ca mugdhalolākṣī mohavarṇa na bhṛṅginī |  
mohanaśca ca peṭā ca manmatho nāthayāsaha ||  
  
mataṅgo māriṇī yukto bhṛṃganā paṃka haṃsinī |  
gāyakena samāyukto tathā vai viśvato mukhī ||  
  
gaja nandikayāyukto gītī ca madanaṃtaraṃ |  
nartakaḥ saharaṃjinyā lekhaḥ kāṃtiḥ samanvitaḥ ||  
  
unmatta karakaṇṭhī ca mattaścaiva vṛkodarī |  
meghaḥ śyāmānvito devī vilaṃvinī kramāt priye ||  
  
akārādyairmātṛkāyā sthāneṣu vinyaset priye |  
anena nyāsa yogena trailokya kṣobhako bhavet ||  
  
atha navayo vinyāsaḥ ||  
  
navayonyātmakanyāsaṃvārāvījaistribhiḥ kramāt |  
triṣu triṣu ca sthāneṣu vakṣyamāṇa krameṇa ca ||  
  
karṇayościvuke bhūyo maṇḍapo vedane tathā |  
netrayornāsi vinyasyedaṃśayorjaṭhare punaḥ ||  
  
tataḥ kūrparayoḥ kukṣau jānūnorliṅgamūrddhani |  
pādayorguhyadeśe ca pārśvayorhṛdayāṃbuje ||  
  
stamadvaye kaṇṭhadeśe bījaṃ pratyekakaṃ nyaset |  
navayonyātmakaṃ nyāsaḥ proktoyaṃ parameśvariḥ ||  
  
atha krameṇa pīṭhatatva śrīcakranyāsaḥ ||  
  
punarvālāṃ samuccārya caturasraṃ tu ciṃtayet ||  
  
punarvālāṃ samuccārya golakatvena ciṃtayet |  
golakanyāsa yogena śrīcakraṃ pariciṃtayet yet ||  
  
ṣaṭcakreṣu lalāṭeṣu sīmaṃte ca śirovile |  
navasthāneṣu saṃkalpānyaseddevi tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
p. 188a)  
  
atha śrīvidyāgurunyāsāśca ||  
  
śiro lalāṭa bhruvaktra jihvāyat saṃdhikoṭiṣu |  
ṣoḍaśārṇānyasedvaktre svarasthāneṣu ca kramāt ||  
  
lalāṭagalahṛnnābhi mūlādhāre ca paṃcakaṃ |  
brahmaraṃdhre mukhe svāṃte vījatrayamatho nyaset ||  
  
ādhāra hṛdaye brahmaraṃdhre vījatrayaṃ tataḥ |  
karapādeṣu hṛdayaṃ paṃcavījāni vinyaset ||  
  
vyāpakaṃ pālakaṃ kuryān mahāsaubhāgyahetave |  
śrīvidyāṃ hṛdaye devī saṃpūrṇāṃ vinyasetsudhīḥ ||  
  
śrīvidyāyāṃ brahmaraṃdhreṣu pṛṣṭhato guravaḥ kramāt ||  
  
atha tithi nityānyāsaḥ ||  
  
tithi nityā tato devī mātṛkā svarasaṃyutā |  
mātṛkāvinyasedvaktre sarvasaubhāgyadāyikā ||  
  
atha ṣoḍaśī nityānyāsaḥ ||  
  
prathamā suṃdarī vidyā mahātripurasuṃdarī |  
kāmeśvarī samākhyātā tathaiva bhagamālinī ||  
  
nitya klinnā ca bheruṇḍā tathaiva vahnivāsinī |  
vajreśvarī ca dūtī ca tvaritā kulasuṃdarī ||  
  
nityā nīlapatākā ca vijayā sarvamaṃgalā |  
jvālāmālinī ciṃtrāṃtā paṃcadaśaḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
athaitāsāṃ krameṇa maṃtrānāha ||  
  
śṛṇu devī pravakṣyāmi nityāmaṇḍalamuttamaṃ |  
kāmeśvarī mahāvidyā sarvalokavaśaṃkarī ||  
  
vālāvāgbhava hṛccāṃte kāmeśvarī padaṃ likhet |  
icchāmaphalaprāptāṃte prade sarvapradaṃ likhet ||  
  
tataḥ satvavaśaṃ vrūyāt kali sarvajagatpradaṃ |  
kṣobhanāṃte karaṃ brūyāt hū&kāra tritayaṃ likhet ||  
  
paṃcavāṇān samālikhya vilomena kumārikāṃ |  
eṣā kāmeśvarī vidyā prasaṃgā kathitā priye ||  
  
vāgbhavaṃ bhagaśabdāṃte bhagebhagini cālikhet |  
bhagodarī bhagāṃte ca bhagamāre bhagāvahe  ||  
  
bhagaguhya bhagaprānte yoniprāṃte bhagāṅkite |  
nipātīni ca sarvāṃte tato bhagavaśaṃkarī ||  
  
bhagarūpe tato likhya nīrajāyatalocane |  
nityaklinna bhagaprāṃte svarūpe sarva cālikhet ||  
  
p. 188b)  
  
bhagānimehyānayeti varadetha samālikhet |  
rate surate subhage klinne klinna drave tataḥ ||  
  
kledaye drāvayedve ca sarvasatvān bhageśvarī |  
amoghe bhagavicce cakṣu bhayakṣobha sarva ca ||  
  
satvān bhageśvarī vrūyād vāgbhavaṃ plū& janmādikaṃ |  
bhe& plū& bho& vlū& he& vlū& hai& vlū& klinne caiva tataḥ punaḥ ||  
  
sarvāṇi ce bhagānyaṃte mevaśaṃ cānayeti ca |  
strīvījaṃ cāharaprāṃte balamātmakamakṣaraṃ ||  
  
bhuvaneśīṃ samālikhya vidyeyaṃ bhagamālinī |  
prasaṃgāt kathitā vidyā sarvalokavaśīkarī ||  
  
parāvījaṃ samuccārya nityaklinne madadrave |  
vahnijāyānvitormaṃtro nityaklinneyamīritā ||  
  
sarvasaubhāgyadā nityaṃ sarvaiśvarya pradāyinī ||  
  
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuddhṛtya tathāṃkuśayutaṃ likhet |  
tanmadhye vilikheddevī bhavoyānmakamakṣaraṃ ||  
  
ca vargamaṃtyahīnaṃ tu vilikhed vahnisaṃsthitaṃ |  
caturddaśa svaropetaṃ viṃdunādātmakaṃ pṛthak ||  
  
vahniṃ jāyānvito maṃtro bheruṇḍāyāḥ phalapradaḥ |  
bhuvaneśīṃ samuccārya ṅentā ca vahnivāsinī ||  
  
hṛdatoya manurdevi vidyeyaṃ vahnivāsinī ||  
  
praṇavaṃ bhuvane śāṃtīṃ phalamānmakamakṣaraṃ |  
sa visarga śaśīpaścānnityaklinne madadrave ||  
  
vahnijāyānvitā vidyā sarvaiśvaryapradāyinī |  
mahāvajreśvarī vidyā prasaṃgā ca mayeritā ||  
  
parāvījaṃ samuccārya śivadūtī ca ṅeyutāṃ |  
hṛdaṃte ca manuṃ devī dūtīgrā sarvakāmada ||  
  
oṃkāravījamuccārya parāṃte vahumālikhet |  
khecachekhaṃ samālikhya strīvījaṃ ca samālikhet ||  
  
hū&kāraṃ kṣeparācāstraṃ vidyeyaṃ ṣoḍaśākṣarī ||  
  
athavā ||  
  
khe& ca strī& cai& cha& hū& cai& ca kṣe& visarga samolikhet |  
hū&kāraṃ ca parādevīṃ vidyeyaṃ dvādaśākṣarī ||  
  
tvaritānāma vidyeyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu durlabhā |  
sarvasiṃhāsanamayī vālaiva kulasuṃdarī ||  
  
vālayāpuṭitāṃ kuryāt tathā caitanya bhairavīṃ |  
paṃcavāṇāśca deveśi nityā śakrākṣarī bhavet ||  
  
trailokya vimalā vidyā nityā syāt parameśvarī |  
paṃcākṣaraṃ vāṇavījaṃ nityayena parāpriye ||  
  
p. 189a)  
  
praṇavaṃ bhuvaneśānīṃ phalamātmakamakṣaraṃ |  
sumātrakaṃ dvitīyaśca bhuvaneśyaṃ kuśaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
nityaśabdaṃ samuddhṛtya saṃbuddhyā tu madadrave |  
kavacaṃ cāṃkuśaṃ devī vidyā nīlapatākinī ||  
  
vāṃtaṃ samāyuktaṃ tataḥ śakrasvarānvitaṃ |  
vijayāyai namodevī nityāyaṃ vijayāpriye ||  
  
athavā ||  
  
vāṃte kālāgni vāyuśca tataḥ śakravibhūṣitaḥ |  
nādaviṃdu kalāyuktā vidyeyaṃ vijayā bhavet ||  
  
caṃdraṃ vāruṇasaṃyuktaṃ tāravījaṃ samālikhet |  
tārahṛdbhagavatyaṃte jvālāmālini devi ca ||  
  
dviruccārya ca sarvāṃte bhūtasaṃhārakālike |  
jātavedasi saṃlikhya jvalaṃtī padayugmakaṃ ||  
  
jvāleti prajvala dvaṃdvaṃ hū&kāra dvitayaṃ likhet |  
caturthyāṃ tu tato devī likhecca sarvamaṃgalāṃ ||  
  
hṛdayaṃto manurdevī nityeyaṃ sarvamaṃgalā ||  
  
athavā ||  
  
caṃdraṃ vāruṇa saṃyuktaṃ tāravījaṃ samālikhet |  
caturthyaṃtāṃ tato devī vilikhet sarvamaṃgalāṃ ||  
  
hṛdayaṃto manurdevi nityeyaṃ sarvamaṃgalā |  
vahnivījatrayaṃ hū& ca astraṃ svāhānvito manuḥ ||  
  
iyaṃ nityā mahādevī jvālāmālinikāparā |  
kavargāṃtaṃ svarāṃtaṃ ca śarasvara vibhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
viṃdunādakalākrāṃtaṃ vicitrā parameśvarī |  
akārādiṣu sarvāsu svareṣu kramato yajet ||  
  
viśvamātṛkā ||  
  
svaravadvinyasennityāṃ nīrajāyata locane ||  
  
atha prakaṭayoginīnyāsaḥ ||  
  
ādhārādiṣunādeva nādāṃte brahmarandhreke |  
prakaṭādyānyaset paścānnyāsaḥ prakaṭayoginī ||  
  
atha rahasyayoginīnyāsaḥ ||  
  
śirolalāṭe bhrūmadhye kaṇṭha hṛnnābhiśekhare |  
ādhāravyāpakaṃ yāvadrahasya yoginīṃ nyaset ||  
  
atha sthitinyāsaḥ ||  
  
sthitiṃ nyāsaṃ tataḥ paścācchrī vidyā ṣoḍaśākṣaraiḥ |  
paṃcākṣalīṣu karayorbrahmaraṃdhre mukhe hṛdi ||  
  
evaṃ vinyasyanātyādi pādāṃte caiva madrije |  
galādi nābhiparyaṃtamaparaṃ hi tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
brahmaraṃdhrādi kaṇṭhāṃte mekaṃ vinyasya pādayoḥ |  
aṃgulīṣu ca vinyasya nyāso'yaṃ sthirakārakaḥ ||  
  
p. 189b)  
  
atha sṛṣṭinyāsaḥ ||  
  
sṛṣṭinyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryāt sarvasiddhipradāyakaṃ |  
brahmaraṃdhrāṃtike bhāle ghrāṇe netre śrutauṣṭake ||  
  
daṃtāṃtorddhvaradhodevi jihvāyāṃgala kūcake |  
pṛṣṭhe sarvāṅga hṛdayestana kukṣiṣu liṃgake ||  
  
śrīvidyārṇenyaseddevī maṃtrī sarvasamṛddhaye ||  
  
atha svadehe avyā abhedavudhyā yathokta kāmakalāṃ dhyātvā āyudhanyāsaḥ   
kāryastathā ca ||  
  
evaṃ kāmakalārūpaṃ devatāmayamātmanaḥ |  
vapurviciṃtya śivayoḥ'rāyudhānyā samācaret ||  
  
drā& drī& klī& plū& saḥ ityete kāmavāṇāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |  
yā& rā& lā& vā& mā& idaṃ kāmeśvaryāśca vāṇapaṃcakaṃ ||  
  
drādipaṃcayādi paṃcayaṃ saṃmohanasaptamaḥ |  
ṅeṃtāt kāmeśvaradhanuḥ ṅenamoṃtaṃ samuddharet ||  
  
anena ca śarānādho haste saṃdhārayeddhanuḥ |  
vāmadevyāstathā maṃtrī dhārayedaikṣa vaṃdhanuḥ ||  
  
drādiyādijaṃ jaṃ haṃ netyaṃ kāmeśvari padāṃtike |  
vāṇebhyo nama ityetāṃ dakṣiṇādhaḥ kare nije ||  
  
devyāḥ pravinyasedvāṇānyauṣyātyaṃva ca sādhakaḥ |  
drādiyādīni bhūyopi mukha ātaṃ sa viṃdukaṃ ||  
  
syād vaśīkaraṇāyaṃti kāmeśvaripradaṃ tataḥ |  
pāśāya nama ityaṃtaṃ vāmorddha vinyaset kare ||  
  
yādi drāvīni gagaṇaṃ vahnivāmākṣi viṃdumat |  
syād vaśīkaraṇāyeti tataḥ kāmeśvarīti ca ||  
  
pāśāya nama ityevaṃ vāmorddhva vinyaset kare |  
drādiyādīnikrāṃ sarvastaṃbhanāya padaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
kāmeśvarī padaṃ paścādaṃkuśāya namo likhet |  
dakṣiṇorddhe kare devyā vinyasedaṃ kuśaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
drādiyādīnikroṃ sarvastaṃbhanāya padaṃ tataḥ |  
kāmeśvari padādūrddhvamaṃkuśāya namo likhet ||  
  
dakṣiṇorddhe kare devyā vinyasedaṃkuśaṃ tataḥ |  
mūlena vyāpakaṃ kṛtvā na ca mudrāḥ pradarśayet ||  
  
atha vyāpakanyāsaḥ ||  
  
sarvāṃge vinyased vidyāṃ vyāpakatena suṃdarī ||  
  
atha nyāsa samayamāha ||  
  
prātaḥkāle'thavā pūjāsamaye homakarmaṇi |  
japakālepi vā teṣāṃ viniyogaḥ pṛthak pṛthak ||  
  
p. 190a)  
  
pūjākāle samastaṃ vā kuryāt sādhakasattamaḥ ||  
  
atha navamudrā pradarśayet ||  
  
tathā ca ||  
  
evaṃ vinyastadehaḥ san mudrā saṃdhārayet kramāt |  
anāmābhyāṃ kaniṣṭhābhyāṃ madhyamābhyāṃ kareṇa tu ||  
  
aṃguṣṭāvanujāgnau ca daṃḍavat tarjanī dvayaṃ |  
kṣobhiṇīyaṃ mahāmudrā drāviṇī tu nigadyate ||  
  
etasyā eva vidyāyā madhyame tarjanīyute |  
sarvavidrāviṇīnāma dvitīyā parikīrtitā ||  
  
etasyā eva vidyāyā tarjanī madhyamāyugaṃ |  
aṃkuśākārarūpeṇa yojayet parameśvarī ||  
  
trailokyākarṣaṇī vidyā tṛtīyā parikīrtitā |  
puṭākāraukarau kuryāt tarjanyau cāṃkuśākṛtī ||  
  
paripṛṣṭa krameṇātha madhyame tadadho gate |  
krameṇa tena manuci kaniṣṭhānāmikādvayaṃ ||  
  
saṃyojyagharṣayet sarvāmaṃguṣṭhā cāgradeśagau |  
sarvāvaśakarī mudrā caturthī parameśvarī ||  
  
saṃmukhau tu karau yojyau madhyamāgarbhagenuge |  
tarjanībhyāṃ vahiryukta anāme sarale kuru ||  
  
madhyamānakha deśe tu tatoṃguṣṭhau ca daṃḍavat |  
unmādinīnāma mudrā paṃcamī parikīrtitā ||  
  
krameṇa paṃcavāṇānāṃ manavaḥ parikīrtitā |  
etasyā eva vidyāyāstarjanyau madhyamāvuje ||  
  
kuryānmahāṃkuśākārau mudreyaṃ tu mahāṃkuśā |  
aṃkuśākhyaṃ mahābījaṃ manurasyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
vāmadakṣiṇavāhuṃ tu dakṣiṇaṃ savyahastagaṃ |  
vāhuṃ kuryāt tato devī hastau saṃgharṣayet kramāt ||  
  
kaniṣṭhānāmikā dvaṃdvaṃ madhyamā pṛṣṭagaṃ tataḥ |  
tarjanī madhyamaṃ kuryādubhayatra maheśvarī ||
