श्री& पातु दक्षकर्णं मे त्रिवर्णात्मा महेश्वरी ॥  
  
वामकर्णं सदा पातु ऐं घ्राणं तु मे सदा ।  
ह्री& पातु वदनं देवी ऐं पातु रसना मम ॥  
  
वाक् त्रिपुटा त्रिवर्णात्मा कण्ठं पातु पराम्विकां ।  
श्री& स्कन्धौ पातु नियतं ह्री& पातु भुजौ सर्वदा ॥  
  
क्ली& करौ त्रिपुटेशानी त्रिपुटैश्वर्य दायिनी ।  
आ& पातु हृदयं ह्री& मे मध्यदेशं सदावतु ॥  
  
क्रो& पातु नाभिदेशं सा त्र्यक्षरी भुवनेश्वरी ।  
सर्ववीजं सदा पृष्टे पातु सर्ववशङ्करी ॥  
  
ह्री& पातु गुह्यदेशं मे नमो भगवती कटिं ।  
माहेश्वरी सदा पातु शक्तिनी जानुयुग्मकं ॥  
  
अन्नपूर्णे सदा पातु स्वाहा पातु पदद्वयं ।  
सामां दशाक्षरी पायादन्न पुर्णाखिलं वपुः ॥  
  
तारं माया रसा कामः षोडशार्णा ततः परं ।  
शिरस्थाः सर्वतः पातु विंशत्यन्नास्थिका मुदा ॥  
  
तारदुर्गे युगं रक्ष स्वाहेति च दशाक्षरी ।  
जय दुर्गा घनश्यामा पातु मां सर्वतो मुदा ॥  
  
माया वीजादिका चैषा दशार्णौ च ततः परा ।  
प्रतप्त काञ्चना भासा जयदुर्गाननेव तु ॥  
  
तारं ह्रीं दुं दुर्गायै नमोष्ट वर्णात्मिका परा ।  
शङ्खचक्रधनुर्वाणधरा मां दक्षिणेव तु ॥  
  
महिषमर्दिनी स्वाहा वसुवर्णात्मिका परा ।  
नैर्-ऋत्यां सर्वदा पातु महिषासुरनाशिनी ॥  
  
माया पद्मावती स्वाहा सप्तार्णा परिकीर्तिता ।  
पद्मावती पद्मसंस्था पश्चिमे मां सदावतु ॥  
  
पाशाङ्कुश पुटामायै हि परमेश्वरि स्वाहा ।  
त्रयोदशार्णा ताराद्या साश्वारूढाननेव तु ॥  
  
सरस्वती पञ्चशरो नित्यक्लिन्ने मदद्रवे ।  
स्वाहारत्पक्षरी नित्यामामुत्तरे सदावतु ॥  
  
तारं माया च कवचं खेचर क्षततो वधूः ।  
क्रू& क्षे ह्री फट् महाविद्या द्वादशार्णा खिलप्रदा ॥  
  
अरिष्टोत्वादिभिः पायाच्छिवा कोणे सदा च मां ।  
ऐ& क्ली& सौ&ः सा ततो वाला मामूर्द्धदेशतोवतु ॥  
  
विन्द्वन्तां भैरवी वाला भूमौ मां सर्वदावतु ।  
इति ते कवचं पुण्यं त्रैलोक्यं मङ्गलं परं ॥  
  
प्। २१३ब्)  
  
सारात् सारतरं पुण्यं महाविद्यौघ विग्रहं ।  
अस्यापि पठनात् सद्यः कुवेरोपि धनेश्वरः ॥  
  
इन्द्राद्याः सकलाः देवाधारणात् पठनाद्यतः ।  
सर्वसिद्धीश्वराः सन्तः सर्वैश्वर्यमवाप्नुयुः ॥  
  
पुष्पाञ्जल्यष्टकं दद्यान्मूलेनैव सथक् पृथक् ।  
संवत्सरशतायास्तु पूजायाः फलमाप्नुयात् ॥  
  
प्रीतिमन्योन्यतः कृत्वा कमला निश्चला गृहे ।  
वाणी च निवसेद्वक्त्रे सत्यं सत्यं न संशयः ॥  
  
यो धारयति पुण्यात्मा त्रैलोक्य मङ्गलाभिधं ।  
कवचं परमं पुण्यं सोपि पुण्यवतां वचः ॥  
  
सर्वैश्वर्य युतो भूत्वा त्रैलोक्यविजयी भवेत् ।  
पुरुषो दक्षिणे वाहौ नारी वा मनुजे तथा ॥  
  
वहु पुत्रवती भूत्वा वन्ध्यापि लभते सुतं ।  
ब्रह्मास्त्रादीनि शस्त्राणि नैव दंशन्तितञ्जनं ॥  
  
एतत् कवचम ज्ञात्वा यो भजेद् भुवनेश्वरीं ।  
दारिद्र्यं परमं प्राप्यसो चिरान्मृत्युमाप्नुयात् ॥  
  
इति श्रीरुद्रयामले देवीश्वरसंवादे त्रैलोक्यमङ्गलन्नाम कवचं समाप्तं   
॥  
  
अथ शिवस्य ॥  
  
नमः शिवायेति मन्त्रः पञ्चार्णस्तारापूर्वकः ।  
षडक्षरोयं विप्राणां भुक्तिमुक्ति प्रसाधकः ॥  
  
वामदेवो मुनिः पङ्क्तिश्छन्दो देवः सदाशिवः ।  
षड्वर्णैस्तु षडङ्गानि कल्पयेत् साधकोत्तमः ॥  
  
ततो ध्यायेत गोक्षीर रजताद्रि समप्रभं ।  
चारुचन्द्र कलाराज जटामुकुटमण्डितं ॥  
  
पञ्चवक्त्रधरं शम्भुं पञ्चवक्त्रं त्रिलोचनं ।  
शार्दूल चर्मवसनं रत्नाभरणभूषितं ॥  
  
दक्षोर्द्ध हस्ते टङ्कं च वरं च दधतः करैः ।  
वामोर्द्ध हस्ते हरिणं दधानमभयं पर ॥  
  
सुप्रसन्नमुखाम्भोजं निविष्टङ्कुशविष्टरे ।  
ब्रह्मविष्णुमहेशाद्यं स्तुतं भक्त्या सुरासुरैः ॥  
  
विश्वाद्यं विश्व वपुषं भवभीति हरं भवं ॥  
  
समाप्तश्चायं भुवनेश्वरी क्रमः ॥  
  
अथ धूमावती क्रमः ॥  
  
अथातः सम्प्रवक्ष्यामि धूमावत्या मनुं परं ।  
पिप्पलादो मुनिश्छन्दोनिवृज्ज्येष्ठास्य देवता ॥  
  
षट्दीर्घ विन्दुयुक्तेन धकारेण षडङ्गकं ।  
आद्यवीजद्वयां तस्थैः षड्वर्णैर्न्या समाचरेत् ॥  
  
प्। २१४अ)  
  
अङ्गुष्ठादौ षडङ्गेषु पुनर्देवीं विचिन्तयेत् ।  
विवर्णा चञ्चला कृष्णा दीर्घा च मलिनांवरा ॥  
  
विमुक्त कुण्डला दीर्घा विधवा विरलद्विजा ।  
काकध्वजरथारूढा विलंवित पयोधरा ॥  
  
शूर्यहस्ताति रुक्षाक्षी धूतहस्तात्वरान्विता ।  
प्रवद्धरो मातु भृशं जटिला कुटिलेक्षणा ॥  
  
क्षुत्पिपासार्दिता नित्यं सदा कलह तत्परा ।  
एवं विधां सदा ध्यायेत् ततः कर्म समाचरेत् ॥  
  
पूर्वोक्ते पूजयेत् पीठे ज्येष्ठां शत्रु निवृत्तये ।  
केशरेषु षडङ्गानि पत्रस्था अष्टशक्तयः ॥  
  
क्षुधातृष्णरतिर्निद्रानिर्-ऋतिर्दुर्गातीरुषा ।  
अक्षमेति ततो देवा इन्द्राद्या आयुधान्विताः ॥  
  
एवं ज्येष्ठां समाराध्य सिद्धमन्त्रः प्रजायते ॥  
  
प्। २१४ब्)  
  
अथ धूमावती कवचं ॥  
  
पार्वत्युवाच ॥  
  
देवदेव महादेव भक्तानुग्रहकारकः ।  
धूमावत्यास्तु कवचं ब्रूहि मे करुणानिधे ॥  
  
महादेव उवाच ॥  
  
अस्ति गुह्यतमं लोके कवचं शत्रुनिग्रहं ।  
सर्वेप्सित प्रदं देवि तव स्नेहात् प्रकाश्यते ॥  
  
यच्छ्रुत्वा रामचन्द्रेणसङ्गरे रावणो हतः ।  
भार्गवेणाअपि यच्छ्रुत्वा जितं सर्वं चराचरं ॥  
  
तमेव कवचं वच्मि सावधानावधारय ।  
कवचस्य महादेवि पिप्पलाद ऋषिः स्मृतः ॥  
  
छन्दो विराट् देवता च श्रीमद्धूमावती प्रिये ।  
शत्रूणां मारणे देवी विनियोगः प्रकीर्तितः ॥  
  
ॐ धूमावती सदा पातु शिरो मे शत्रुमर्द्दिणी ।  
चण्डरूपा महादेवी ललाटे पातु मां सदा ॥  
  
क्षुत्कामा नयने पातु पातु भीमा श्रुती मम ।  
काकध्वजा नासिकां मे सर्वशत्रुविनाशिनी ॥  
  
प्रलंवोष्ठी सदा पातु वदनं मुण्डमालिनी ।  
विकृतास्या सदा पातु गलं मे रिपुसूदिनी ॥  
  
धू& वीजाख्या सदा पातु घाटं मे रिष्टतारिणी ।  
स्कन्धौ कङ्कालिनी पातु नृमुण्डस्रग्विभूषणा ॥  
  
शुष्कमांसा सदा पातु भीषणा मे भुजद्धयं ।  
लम्वस्तनी सदा पातु धूमवर्णास्तन द्वयं ॥  
  
सूर्यहस्ता च हृदयं पातु भैरवमादिनी ।  
शत्रु मांसप्रिया पातु पृष्ठं मे रुधिरप्रियां ॥  
  
मदिरा घूर्णनयना पातु पार्श्वे किरीटिनी ।  
करालिनी सदा पातु कुक्षिं मे शववाहिनी ॥  
  
वज्रतुण्डा पातु नित्यं कटिदेशं शिव प्रिया ।  
कराल वदना पातु गुह्यदेशं दिगंवरां ॥  
  
घोराट्टहासिनी पातु जानुनी विरलद्विजा ।  
पादौ मे पातु सततं क्षुत्पिपासा कुला सदा ॥  
  
घोरघण्ठा सदा पातु सर्वाङ्गे शङ्कर प्रिया ।  
इति ते कथितं देवी कवचं रिपु निग्रहं ॥  
  
यस्य प्रपठनाद्देवी सर्वसिद्धिकरे स्थिता ।  
न तस्य शत्रु पीडास्याद्दुष्टपीडा कदापि न ॥  
  
ग्रहपीडा भूतपीडा न भवेत् कुलसुन्दरी ।  
धूमावती समभ्यर्च्य कृष्णपुष्पेण साधकः ॥  
  
मत्स्यमांसा सवैर्देवीं पूजयित्वा यथा विधिं ।  
महामांसस्य धूपेन धूपयेत्तान्त्र मन्त्रवित् ॥  
  
प्। २१५अ)  
  
अष्टोत्तर शतावृत्तिं पठेदेकमनां प्रिये ।  
पक्षमात्रेण देवेशि रिपुंहन्यान्न संशयः ॥  
  
एतत् सर्वं महेशानि मारणेषु नियोजयेत् ।  
कवचस्मरणाद्देवि रिपुर्याति यमालयं ॥  
  
इति श्रीरुद्रयामले धूमावतीकल्पे धूमावतीकवचं ॥  
  
अथाघोरस्य ॥  
  
अथातः सम्प्रवक्ष्यामि सा घोरास्त्राज्ञयं मनुं ।  
माया स्फुरद्वयं चैव प्रस्फुरद्द्वितयं वदेत् ॥  
  
पश्चाद्वदेत्तुरुतुरुरूपां ते च चटद्वयं ।  
प्रचट द्वितयं पश्चात् कहद्वयं वमद्वयं ॥  
  
वन्धद्वयं घातय द्वि हू& हू& फट् शरवर्णकः ।  
मनुः प्रोक्तो घोरमुनिः तिर्ष्टुप्छन्दोस्य देवता ॥  
  
अघोररूपं वं वीजं ह्री& शक्तिः परिकीर्तिता ।  
शरं तु दशदिग्दन्ति दिवाकरमितैर्मनाः ॥  
  
वर्णैः कुर्यात् षडङ्गानि पदन्यासोथ वक्ष्यते ।  
कटौ च वक्त्रगल हृन्माभ्यं धूकरजानुषु ॥  
  
स जङ्घापादयोश्चैवं पदान्ये कादशन्यसेत् ।  
शरं तु नेत्रवस्वद्धिर संवेदाद्धि वेदकैः ॥  
  
रसनेत्रमितैर्वर्णैर्मृत्पदानि भवन्त्युमे ।  
ध्यायेत् ततो मेघकालं भीमदंष्ट्रं त्रिलोचनं ॥  
  
भुजङ्गभूषणं रक्तवसना लेपशोभितं ।  
परशुं करवालं च वाणीस्त्रिशिखमेव च ॥  
  
दधानां दक्षिणैर्हस्तैरुर्द्धादि क्रमतः परैः ।  
डमरुं खेटकं चापं नृकपालं च विभ्रतं ॥  
  
समाप्तश्चायं धूमावती क्रमं ॥  
  
अथ वगलामुखी क्रमः ॥  
  
अथातः सम्प्रवक्ष्यामि स्तम्भनीं वगलामुखीं ।  
नारायणो मुनि स्त्रिष्टुप्छन्दश्च वगलामुखी ॥  
  
देवी वीजं तु हृल्लेखा स्वाहा शक्तिः समीरिता ।  
विनियोगास्य विख्यातः पुरुषार्थश्चतुष्टये ॥  
  
हृल्लेखा हृदयं प्रोक्तं शिवश्च वगलामुखी ।  
शिखा तु सवदुष्टानां ततो वाचं मुखं पदं ॥  
  
स्तम्भयेति च वर्मोक्तं जिह्वां कीलय नेत्रकं ।  
बुद्धिर्विनाशयास्त्रं स्यात् षडङ्गं न्यास ईरितः ॥  
  
मूर्ध्ह्नि भाले भ्रुवोर्मध्ये नेत्रयोः शोत्रयो रसोः ।  
गण्डद्वये तथा चोष्ठे धरास्य चिवुकेषु च ॥  
  
गले च दक्षदोर्मूले तन्मध्ये मणिवन्धके ।  
अङ्गुलीनां तथा मूले हस्ताग्रे चैव मेव हि ॥  
  
प्। २१५ब्)  
  
अन्येद् वामभुजादौ च दक्षोरु मूलके ततः ।  
दक्ष जानुनि गुल्फे चाङ्गुलि मूले पदाग्रतः ॥  
  
गम्भीरा च मदोन्मत्तां तप्तकाञ्चन सन्निभां ।  
चतुर्भुजां त्रिनयनां कमलासन संस्थितां ॥  
  
मुद्गरं दक्षिणे पाशं वामे जिह्वां च वज्रकं ।  
पीतांवरधरा सान्द्र वृत्त पीतपयोधरां ॥  
  
हेमकुण्डलभूषां च पीतचन्द्रार्द्धशेखरां ।  
पीतभूषण भूषां च स्वर्णसिंहासन स्थितां ॥  
  
एवं ध्यात्वा च देवेशीं शत्रूस्तम्भनकारिणीं ।  
भूःप्रदोश मनोरम्ये पुष्पामोद सुधूपिते ॥  
  
गोमयेनाथ संलिप्ते मण्डपेत्वासनं चरेत् ।  
सौवर्णे वाथरौप्ये वा पैत्तरे वाथ भूर्जके ॥  
  
कर्पूरागुरु कस्तूरी श्रीखण्ड कुङ्कुमैरपि ।  
लिपेद्यन्त्रं प्रयत्नेन लेखन्या हेमतारयोः ॥  
  
मध्ये योनिं समालिख्य तद्वाह्ये तु षडस्रकं ।  
तद्वाह्येष्टदलं पद्मं तद्वाह्ये षोडशच्छदं ॥  
  
चतुरस्र त्रयं वाह्ये चतुर्द्वारोपशोभितं ।  
यत्र नोक्तां देवतायाः पीठन्दा पीठशक्तयः ॥  
  
तत्र मायोदितं पीठं ज्ञेयेता एव शक्तयः ।  
तद्वीजेन यजेत् पीठं यद्वा मायामुनाथ वा ॥  
  
तत्रावाह्य यजेद्देवीं सु पीतैरुपचारकैः ।  
यजेदङ्गानि षट्कोणे पूर्वद्वारादिषु क्रमात् ॥  
  
गणेशं वटुकं चापि योगिन्यः क्षेत्रपालकं ।  
ईशानादि निऋत्यन्तं गुरुपङ्क्तिं समर्चयेत् ॥  
  
वगला पूर्वपत्रे तु स्तम्भिनी च ततः परं ।  
जम्भिनी मोहिनी वल्या अचला चञ्चला तथा ॥  
  
दुर्द्धर्षाकल्मषा धीरा कल्पना कालकर्षिणी ।  
भ्रामिका मन्दगमना भोगाख्या चैव योगिका ॥  
  
एताः षोडशपत्रेषु गन्धपुष्पाक्षतैर्यजेत् ।  
षोडश स्वर संयुक्ता सम्प्रदायात् कुलागमे ॥  
  
यजेच्च पत्र मध्येषु कल्पिते चाष्टपत्रके ।  
ब्राह्म्याद्यष्टौ तु पूर्वादौ वाहनायुध संयुताः ॥  
  
लोकेशांश्च तदस्त्राणि पूजयेद् वाह्यतस्तथा ।  
योनिमध्ये मूलदेवीं त्रिपुष्पाञ्जलिभिर्यजेत् ॥  
  
धूपदीपै सु नैवेद्यैर्गन्धतांवूलदीपकैः ।  
नीराज्य विधिवत् पश्चाज्जप सङ्ख्यान्निवेदयेत् ॥  
  
प्। २१६अ)  
  
अथ वगलामुखी स्तोत्रं ॥  
  
ॐ पीतवस्त्रां सु नेत्रां च द्विभुजां दाहद्धोज्वलां ।  
शिलापर्वतहस्तां च स्मरन्ती वगलामुखीं ॥  
  
मध्य सुधाद्धि मणिमण्डप रत्नवेद्यां सिंहासनो परिगतां   
परिपीतवर्णां ।  
पीतांवराभरणमाल्यविभूषिताङ्गी देवी नमामि धृतमुद्गर वैरि जिह्वां ॥  
  
जिह्वाग्रमादाथकरेण देवीं वामेन शत्रुपरिपीडयन्ती ।  
गदाभिघातेन तु दक्षिणेन पीताम्वराढ्यां द्विभुजां नमामि ॥  
  
त्रिशूलधारिणीमम्वी सर्वसौभाग्यदायिनी ।  
सर्वशृङ्गारवेशाढ्यां देवीं ध्यात्वा प्रपूजयेत् ॥  
  
चलत् कनक कुण्डलोल्लसित चारुगण्डस्थलां लसत् कनकचम्पकद्युति विराजित   
चन्द्राननां ।  
गदाहत विपक्षकां कलित लोल जिह्वा चलां स्मरामि वगलामुखीं   
विमुखसन्मुखस्तम्भिनीं ॥  
  
पीयूषो दधिमध्य चारु विलसद्रत्नोज्ज्वले मण्डपे तत् सिंहासन मौलि पाटित   
रिपु प्रेतासनाध्यासिनीं ।  
स्वर्नाभां कलपीडितारि रसनां भ्राम्यद्गवा विभ्रमां यस्त्वां पश्यति   
यान्ति तस्य विलयं सद्योपि सर्वापदः ॥  
  
देवित्वच्चरणाम्वुजे वितनुतेयः पीतपुष्पाञ्जलिं मुद्रां वामकरे निधाय च   
पुनर्मन्त्री मनोज्ञाज्ञाक्षरं ।  
पीतध्यानपरोपि कुम्भक वशाद्वीजे स्मरेत् पार्थिवं तस्या मित्रमुखस्य   
वाघृदयगो स्तम्भो भवेत् तत्क्षणात् ॥  
  
मन्त्रस्थानदलं विपक्षदलने स्तोत्रं पवित्रं च ते यन्त्रं वादि   
निमन्त्रिणां त्रिजगतां यन्त्रं पवित्रं च ते ।  
मातः श्रीवगलेनिनाम ललितं यः स्तूयते ते मुखे तन्नाम ग्रहणेन सम्पदि   
मुखस्तम्भो भवेद्वैरिणां ॥  
  
वादीमूकति शङ्कितः क्षितिपतिर्वैश्वानरः शीततिः क्रोधीशान्ततिदुर्जनः   
सुजनतिः क्षिप्रं मुखं खञ्जति ॥  
  
गर्वी खर्वति सर्व एव जगति त्वद्यन्त्र यन्त्रिताः ।  
श्रीनित्ये वगलामुखि प्रतिदिनं कल्याणि तुभ्यं नमः ॥  
  
दुष्टस्तम्भनकं च विघ्नशमनं दारिद्र्य विध्वंसनं   
भूभृत्सङ्गमनं च यन्मृगदृशां चेतः समाकर्षणं ।  
सौभाग्यैक निकेतनं मम दृशो कारुण्य पूर्णे क्षणं   
मृत्योर्मारणमाविरस्तु परतो मातस्त्वदीयं वपुः ॥  
  
त्वं विद्या परमा त्रिलोक जननी विघ्नौघ सञ्छेदिनी योगाकर्षणकारिणी च सु   
महद्वन्दैक सञ्छेदिनी ।  
दुष्टोच्चाटनकारिणीं जनमनः सम्मोहथ सन्धायिनी जिह्वाकीलन वैभवा   
विजयते ब्रह्मास्त्रस्तु विद्या परा ॥  
  
प्। २१६ब्)  
  
मातः स्तम्भयमद्विपक्षवदनं जिह्वां चलं कीलय ब्राह्मीं   
मुद्रयमुद्रयासुधिषणां वह्नेर्गतिं स्तम्भयः ।  
शत्रूंश्चूर्णयचूर्णयाशुगदया गौराङ्गि पीतांवरे विघ्नौघं वगले   
हर प्रतिदिनं कारुण्य पूर्णेक्षणे ॥  
  
मातर्भैरवि भद्रकालि विजये वाराहि विश्वाश्रये श्रीनित्ये समये महेशि वगले   
कामेशि वामे रमे ।  
मातङ्गी त्रिपुरे परात्परतरे स्वर्गापवर्गप्रदेदासो हंशरणागतं करुणया   
विश्वेश्वरि त्राहिमां ॥  
  
शाङ्कघे चौरसङ्घे प्रहरणसमये वन्धने वारिमध्ये वह्न्यै वादे   
विवादे प्रकुपित्त नृपतौ दिव्य काले निशायां ।  
वाच्यात्वं स्तम्भने वा रिपु वधसमये निर्विपत्तौरणे वा गच्छंस्तिष्ठं   
स्त्रिकालंस्तव पठनमिदङ्कार्य सिद्धिप्रदं च ॥  
  
मातर्यश्चनरः सदास्तवमिदं देव्याः पठेत् साधनं धृत्वा   
यन्त्रमिदं तथैव समये वाहौ करे वा गले ।  
राजानो वरयोषितोपि करणः सर्पामृगेन्द्राः खलाः स्तम्भयान्ति निषीविते   
रिपुगता लक्ष्मीर्यथा सिद्ध्यति ॥  
  
अनुदिनमभिरासं साधकोय स्त्रिकाले पठति त्रिभुवनेशः पूज्यते देववर्गैः ।  
भवति सकलकृत्यं तस्य दृष्ट्वावलोके भवति परमसिद्धौ   
लोकमातस्तथैव ॥  
  
इति श्रीनारदविरचिते पीतां वगलास्तोत्रं सम्पूर्णं ॥  
  
अथ वगलामुखी कवचं ॥  
  
श्रीमहोग्रतारोवाच ॥  
  
राज्ञा मण्डलकादीनां मण्डलो परिसर्पतां ।  
स गर्वाणां महादेव धनैर्विकृत चेतसां ॥  
  
गजसर्पारि जन्तूनां भजनं वद शङ्कर ॥  
  
श्रीभैर उवाच ॥  
  
पुरा कृत युगे देवि वा तक्षोभमुपस्थिते ।  
सप्तार्णवानामेकत्वगमक्षोभं ययुः सुरा ॥  
  
सेन्द्रास्सविष्णवेः सर्वेसुभयान् मामुपस्थिताः ॥  
  
देवा ऊचुः ॥  
  
शिवशङ्कररुद्रेश रक्षास्मान् शरणागतान् ।  
महावातादि विक्षोभ क्षुधानस्मान्महार्णवात् ॥  
  
तच्छ्रुत्वाहं सुरेशानि कवचं पूर्वनिर्मितं ।  
दत्तवान् सर्वदेवेभ्यो महाभय निकृन्तनं ॥  
  
कवचं वगलामुख्याः शिवप्राणप्रदं महत् ।  
पूर्वं भस्मासुरत्रासाद्भयविद्रावितः स्वयं ॥  
  
पठते तच्च मत्प्राणान् रक्षत्वं परमेश्वरी ।  
शिवप्राणप्रदं तस्माद् विश्रुतं रक्षकं परं ॥  
  
षट्त्रीशद्दक्षवामेध्याद् वगला परमाशिरः ।  
सहस्रारे गुरुः पातु शक्त्या परमयोज्ज्वलः ॥  
  
प्। २१७अ)  
  
चिद्रूपा परमाशक्तिर्ललाटं शिवगेहिनी ।  
भूयुगं मे महाकाली नेत्रयुग्मं परेश्वरी ॥  
  
कर्णयुग्मं पीतपुष्पप्रिया मेव्यात् कपोलयोः ।  
चिवुके परमाशक्तिरेष्टयोः परमाकलाः ॥  
  
वदनं सकला पातु परम्ब्रह्मस्वरूपिणी ।  
पीतपुष्पार्चिता कण्ठं स्कन्धौ स्कन्दस्तनप्रदा ॥  
  
पीतांवरा दक्षभुजं वामां वामाङ्गहारिणी ।  
हृदयं स स्तनद्वन्द्वं भानु विंवमुखैकधृक् ॥  
  
पृष्टं चन्द्रधरं मेव्यात् कटिं कन्दर्प्य रूपधृक् ।  
हृत्पङ्कजं सैव शक्तिर्विशुद्धं जीवरूपिणी ॥  
  
आज्ञा चक्रं विन्दुरूपा परम्ब्रह्मकुटुम्बिनी ।  
ब्रह्मरन्ध्र सहस्रारं पङ्कजाख्य स्वरूपधृक् ॥  
  
पातुमां परमाशक्तिश्चामरी कुटिलालका ।  
षट्त्रिंशदक्षराविद्या पीतापीत वपुर्द्धरा ॥  
  
पीतपुष्पार्चिता पीत नैवेद्यादि वलिप्रिया ।  
सर्वाङ्गं मे शुभा पातु वैरि स्तम्भनकारिणी ॥  
  
ब्रह्मरन्ध्रेषु परमासंसारार्णवतारिणी ।  
तारयेन् मां महादेवी मनोवाञ्छितदायिनी ॥  
  
आज्ञा चक्रे गुरौरूपा महाभयनिवाशिनी ।  
सर्वविद्या वरा पातु जिह्वा शास्त्र वपुर्द्धरा ॥  
  
विशुद्धौ षोडशदले जीवेश्वर वपुर्द्धरा ।  
षट्त्रिंशत् तत्वरूपाख्या कण्ठस्था मां सदावतु ॥  
  
हृत्पङ्कजे भवानीशरूपारूप परात्मिका ।  
इन्द्रियादि महाशत्रून् विदारयतु दारुणा ॥  
  
मणिपूरे दशदले महाविष्णु स्वरूपधृक् ।  
दारयन्नखिलान्मोहान् मां माया सा परावतु ॥  
  
प्रजापति स्वरूपेयं स्वाधिस्थाने षड्दले ।  
सृष्टिस्थिता पराविद्या मां मोहाद्वगलावतु ॥  
  
गणेशरूपधृक् पातुत्वाधारे मां चतुर्दले ।  
षोडश स्वररूपेयं पातु मां परमाकला ॥  
  
क& ख& ग& घ& तथा ङ्& च& छ& ज& झ& ञ्& तथा वतु ।  
ट& ठ& ड& ढ& त्वमाकाराणं त& थ& द& तथा वतु ॥  
  
ध& न& प& फ& तु शत्रुभ्यः पातु मां ध्यान तत्परां ।  
व& भ& म& य& विदायार्थ शत्रून् मां वाक्त्वरूपिणी ॥  
  
र& ल& व& श& तथा ष& स& शत्रुजिह्वां विदार्य तु ।  
मे वाचं मे मुखं जिह्वां सदा रक्ष तु शाङ्करी ॥  
  
ह& ल& क्ष& सकलं पातु रक्षन् मे परमं यशः ।  
प्रणवं स्थिरमाया च तृतीयं त्रितयं तथा ॥  
  
य स्तृतीयं स्वराद्युग्मं यादाद्यं स्वरपञ्चमं ।  
का द्वितीयं दक्षनेत्रे सर्वदुष्ट वहु स्मृतं ॥  
  
षष्ठ्यन्तं च तथा वाचं स्तम्भयाथापि जिह्वया ।  
द्वितीयया कालयेति तथा बुद्धिं विनाशय ॥  
  
स्थिर माया तथा तारं चान्ते वह्नि वधूं प्रिये ।  
एषा विद्या महाविद्या शत्रुन्स्तम्भनकारिणी ॥  
  
प्। २१७ब्)  
  
त्रिधा मन्त्रं समुच्चार्य सर्वाङ्गे व्यापकं कुरु ।  
जयत्येव न सन्देहः शत्रून् शूरान्महाहवे ॥  
  
कुलालमृतिकाङ्गृह्य वामहस्तेन दीपकं ।  
कृत्वा प्रज्वाल्य तैलेन वामे स्थाप्य मनुं जपेत् ॥  
  
त्रिरात्रं स्तम्भयत्येव शत्रुसेनां महाहवे ।  
गौरवर्णां पीतपुष्पैर्वालां सम्पूज्य भावतः ॥  
  
न्यासां विधाय देहेन भजन् योगी जपन्मनुं ।  
पीतोपचारैस्तां शक्तिं सन्तोष्य परिवारणां ॥  
  
वशयत्येव लोकेशं किं पुनः क्षुद्रमानुषं ।  
वाचस्तम्भन कारस्तु वीरशक्तिं शुभाननां ॥  
  
षोडशाब्दां सुवर्णां च अलङ्कृत्य यजेत् प्रिये ।  
सहस्र मूलमन्त्रं तु जप्त्वा वाचस्पतेरपि ॥  
  
स्तम्भयत्येव परमां वाचं किं क्षुद्रमानुषं ।  
वशीकरण कामस्तु वद्वापरिकरं दृढं ॥  
  
शक्तिं लिङ्गोपरि स्थाप्य त्रिसहस्रं जपेन्मनुं ।  
इन्द्राणीं वशयत्येव किं पुनः क्षुद्रमानुषीं ॥  
  
मण्डलाधीश वश कृदुत्तराभिमुखं स्थितः ।  
दक्षाननां सुन्दरीं तु सोडशाब्दां शुचिस्मितां ॥  
  
कुचयोस्तु करैर्दत्वा पीताद्यां हसिताननां ।  
लिङ्गे संस्थाप्य सञ्चुवन्मुखं पीता मनुं जपन् ॥  
  
त्रिसहस्रं महाराज वशयत्येव नान्यथा ।  
येन केनाप्युपायेन वगलाभक्ति तत्परः ॥  
  
स्तम्भयेत् सकलांल्लोकान्वशयत्येव शाङ्करी ।  
मारयेच्छत्रु सङ्घातमुच्चाटयति पर्वतान् ॥  
  
देवानां स्थपतिश्चन्द्रः छादयेत् किं परं जनं ।  
अस्य पार्वति माहात्म्यं कवचस्य क्ववर्णितुम् ॥  
  
महाद्रौदारुणे चान्ते प्रलयादावुपस्थिते ।  
स्तम्भितं च तदा देवि वातसङ्घं सकृज्जपात् ॥  
  
एवं सा परमा विद्या महाशत्रुविदारिणी ।  
नास्तिके तस्करे दुष्टेन्मूढे पण्डितमानिनी ॥  
  
न देया हृदया विद्या ददन्वन्धमवाप्नुयात् ।  
सुशीलाय सुदान्ताय गुरुभक्तिपराय च ॥  
  
विशुद्धाय महामन्त्रजापिने देयमुत्तमं ।  
कृत्वा पुरा सुकवचं जपेन्मन्त्रं समाहितः ॥  
  
नान्यथा स्तम्भिनी विद्या सिद्धास्यादिति निश्चयः ॥  
  
इति श्रीएकवीरातन्त्रे महोग्रतारासंवादे वगलामुखीकवचं सम्पूर्णं ॥  
  
प्। २१८अ)  
  
अथ मृत्युञ्जय भैरवस्य ॥  
  
ॐ जू&सः इति मन्त्रस्य प्रोक्तो मृत्युञ्जयाभिधः ।  
ऋषिः कलाहो दैत्यादि गायत्रीछन्द ईरितं ॥  
  
मृत्युञ्जयो महादेवो देवता परिकीर्तितः ।  
षड्दीर्घयु तृगुणा षडङ्गविधिरीरितः ॥  
  
पद्मद्वयस्थितं स्मेरं चन्द्रार्काग्नि विलोचनं ।  
हस्तेषु ज्ञानमुद्रां च पाशमक्षाक्षिमालिके ॥  
  
कर्पूराभं शीर्षचन्द्रः कराद्वामृतधारया ।  
अर्द्धाङ्गं वहुभूषाढ्यं कान्त्या विश्वविमोहनं ॥  
  
समाप्तश्चायं वगलामुखी क्रमः ॥

uttare śuklapītena triśūlaṃ varasuṃdarī |  
śikhāṃśa grahaṇe deviyauṣṭyākarṣaṇa karmaṇi ||  
  
p. 219b)  
  
viṣot kaṭoyaṃ sarvatra ālikhen maṃḍalāni ca ||  
  
gaṇeśvaraṃ vadiṣyāmi adhunā varavarṇini |  
raktasūtreṇa sumitaṃ trihastāyata maṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
karṇikā keśare patre hastamekaṃ tu vāhayet |  
sūrya caṃdra jalasthāne hastamekaṃ tu varṇayet ||  
  
dvārakaṃ hastamālikhya caturasraṃ suśobhanaṃ |  
karṇikā haritā proktā keśaraṃ pītameva ca ||  
  
jalarūpaṃ site naiva sūryaṃ raktena cālikhet |  
caṃdraṃ śvetena darvyeṇa patraṃ rakta suśobhanaṃ ||  
  
dvāraṃ śvetaṃ suśobhāḍhya ma * (?) siṃ pūrvakṛṣṇakaṃ |  
dakṣiṇe śvetanarakaṃ kṛṣṇaśūlaṃ ca paścime ||  
  
uttare haritākāraṃ ḍamaruṃ ca suśobhanaṃ |  
vaśyākarṣaṇa vedheṣu maṃḍalena maheśvarī ||  
  
pratānakaṃ vadiṣyāmi idānīṃ vīramātari |  
gocarmarajjunā bhūmyāṃ pātayet saṃitena ca ||  
  
dvihastamārabhyamitaṃ caturdvāra vibhūṣaṇaṃ |  
karṇikā paṃca aṃgulyā keśaraṃ caturaṃgulaṃ ||  
  
patraṃ ṣoḍaśamaṃgulyā dvihastaṃ jalabhāgataḥ |  
śiraścatvāra maṃgulyā sarvadvārāṇi vāhayet ||  
  
karṇikā haritā bhadre keśaraṃ raktameva ca |  
dalaṃ kṛṣṇena kurvīta dalasaṃdhiṃ jalaṃ tathā ||  
  
raktena tu suśobhāni dhūmena dvāra vāhayet |  
aśiṃ kapālaṃ paraśuṃ triśūlaṃ ca catuṣṭayaṃ ||  
  
caturdvāra samālikhyaṃ yathā śobhāṃ vrajet priye |  
mahāsādhana kāle māraṇe ca viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
pretānakaṃ likhedbhadre maṇḍalaṃ sarvasiddhidaṃ |  
śāṃtikaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ vaśyamāraṇaṃ ca sulocanaṃ ||  
  
viśeṣa maṇḍalaṃ yena jñātvā karmasamārabhet ||  
  
punaranya prakāreṇa pravakṣyāmi viśeṣataḥ |  
sthūlena kalirityāhuḥ kṛṣṇena maraṇaṃ bhavet ||  
  
vakrehāni bhavedghoraṃ chinnerāja bhayāni ca |  
asadṛśaḥ kṛte patre maṃtrasiddhirnna jāyate ||  
  
tasmāt prayatnaṃ kurvīta yadīcchet siddhimuttamaṃ |  
evaṃ karmavibhāgāni jñātvā karma samārabhet ||  
  
kimanyat pṛcchase devī kathitaṃ rajjupātanaṃ ||  
  
p. 220a)  
  
atha pūjā dravyamāha ||  
  
yat sarvaṃ bhakṣapānāni dravyaṃ vittānusārataḥ |  
kalpayitvā tu suśroṇi sarvaṃ dravyaṃ kṣamāpayet ||  
  
caṃdanaṃ ca pavitraṃ ca gaṃdhamālyaṃ ca mohinīṃ |  
āsanaṃ dhūpa siṃdūra sthāpayecca yathā kramaṃ ||  
  
nānāvidhāni māṃsānihyanekā matsyajātayaḥ |  
caturvidhāni bhakṣāṇi upadaṃ śāpadaṃśakāḥ ||  
  
pūrvoktaṃ sakalaṃ dravyaṃ pūrṇamatra prakalpayet ||  
  
atha krameṇa aṣṭakāṣṭakamāha ||  
  
tatrādau vīrādīnāṃ pādaprakṣālana dravyamāha ||  
  
pādaprakṣālanaṃ devi sāṃprataṃ kathayāmi te |  
vacaḥ priyaṃgu surabhī uśīraṃ caṃdanaṃ tathā ||  
  
vālaṃ māṃsi tathā cauraṃ samabhāgāni kārayet |  
piṣṭodakena bhāgena ślakṣṇaṃ kṛtvā yathārthataḥ ||  
  
uṣṇodaka ghaṭe madhye vahisthāne nidhāpayet |  
ekaika vīrapādau ca kṣālayedudakena tu ||  
  
aṭṭahāseva cotpannaṃ caritrāyāṃ priyaṃgukaṃ |  
kolāpuryāṃ tu surabhirjayaṃtyāṃ ca uśīrakaṃ ||  
  
ujjenyāṃ vadanaṃ bhadre prayāge vālameva ca |  
vārāṇasyāṃ ca māṃsī ca karṇamodyāṃ tu caurakaṃ ||  
  
etadaṣṭau samākhyātā aṣṭau kṣetrasya lāṃchanaṃ ||  
  
upahāravidhiṃ vakṣye śṛṇutvaṃ varavarṇini |  
caṃdanaṃ ca pavitraṃ ca gaṃdhamālyaṃ ca mohinī ||  
  
āsanaṃ dhūpa siṃdūraṃ dāpayecca yathā kramaṃ |  
caṃdanaṃ virajaṃ bhadre pavitraṃ merukaṃ tathā ||  
  
hādrāpuraṃ bhavedgaṃdhaṃ mālyamelāpuraṃ smṛtaṃ |  
kāśmīraṃ mohanī jñeyā āsanaṃ merukaṃ tathā ||  
  
tagaraṃ dhūpamityāhuḥ siṃdūraṃ puṇḍravarddhanaṃ |  
etānyaṣṭau bhūṣaṇāni upakṣetrasya lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
yathā krameṇa dātavyamācāryādīn vicakṣaṇaḥ |  
upahāra vidhānaṃ ca saṃkṣepāt kathitaṃ mayā ||  
  
vali saṃsthāpanaṃ bhadre adhunā kathayāmite |  
vṛhadārumaya pātre odanaiḥ paripūrite ||  
  
samucchritaṃ vaijayaṃtyā paṃcaraṃgika kārayet |  
achidra aṃtarmālyena dāpayed valibhājane ||  
  
vicitrapuṣpamālyena yathā śobhāṃ vrajet priye |  
tathā tena prakartavyaṃ devatālaya śobhanaṃ ||  
  
matsyamāṃsāni dhūpāni tilapiṣṭaṃ ca modakaṃ |  
vṛkṣāmlarudhiraṃ bhadre āraktakaṃ tathaiva ca ||  
  
p. 220b)  
  
etadaṣṭau mayākhyātāḥ saṃdoha valikarmaṇi |  
parastīre bhavenmāṃsamatsyaṃ pṛṣṭāpuraṃ tathā ||  
  
kudgaṇḍivo bhaveddhūpaṃ sopānetilaṃ piṣṭakaṃ |  
kṣīrake modakaṃ bhadre māyā puryāmlameva ca ||  
  
āmrātake bhavedraktaṃ gṛharāje alaktakaṃ |  
samudraṃ dārupātraṃ ca odanaṃ merumeva ca ||  
  
ahirājaṃ tu mālāṃ tu sragdānaṃ raktamālyakaṃ |  
brahmāviṣṇuśca rudraśca īśvaraśca sadāśivaṃ ||  
  
paṃcaraṃga patākāṃ ca śuddhā paṃcanivāsinī |  
sāmudramudaraṃ bhadre nābhimeruḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
kuṇḍalākhyā hi rājaṃ vannetra romaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ |  
prāṇo'pānaḥ samānaṃ ca udānavyā nameva ca ||  
  
devatā paṃcakaṃ bhadre śuddhāsana nivāsinī |  
ūrddhvaścāsamadhaḥ śvāsaḥ caṃdrasūryau prakīrtitau ||  
  
trayastriṃśat koṭi devāromakūpe vyavasthitā |  
vali saṃsthāpanaṃ bhadre sa vāhyābhyaṃtarāṇi ca ||  
  
kathitaṃ sarvaśāstrāṇi dagdhāghṛtamivoddhṛtaṃ ||  
  
madyaṃ cāṣṭavidhaṃ proktaṃ mahāmāṃsāṣṭakaṃ tathā |  
aṣṭau ca bhairavāsteṣāṃ sthāne vīrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
bhairavyastu tathā proktastathā cāṣṭau ca mātaraḥ |  
tāsāṃ sthāne śaktayaḥsyure tadvaivāṣṭakāṣṭakaṃ ||  
  
atha pūjāmāha ||  
  
arcācakraṃ svavidyāyāstanmadhye sthāpayedghaṭaṃ |  
madyapūrṇaṃ tatra devī māvāhyārcanamācaret ||  
  
nānāvidhāni māṃsānihyanekā matsya jātayaḥ |  
caturvidhāni bhakṣāṇi upadaṃśopadaṃśakāḥ ||  
  
ete samyak pūjayitvā sāṃgāṃ sāvaraṇāṃ surāṃ |  
śaktayaśca tathā vīrāḥ pūjyāḥ puṣpākṣatādibhiḥ ||  
  
athavā ||  
  
pratyakṣaṃ pūjayeddevī śaktiṃ śaktiḥ svarūpiṇīṃ |  
vīraṃ bhairavarūpeṇa puruṣeṣu prayojayet ||  
  
yāvat pramāṇaṃ yoginyaḥ svacakre paripūjitāḥ |  
yāvat pramāṇaṃ deveśi guravo bhairavādayaḥ ||  
  
dikpālāntā maheśāni puruṣāṃ yaṃtramadhyagāḥ |  
tāvat pramāṇaṃ deveśi nāryaśca puruṣā tathā ||  
  
cakrasthāna vibhāgaiśca tat tadvudhyā niveśeyet |  
madhye viṃdau mayāsārddhaṃ tvāṃ vai yugmātmikāṃ yajet ||  
  
p. 221a)  
  
pūrvoktairmaṃtrarūpaiśca pūjākalpe prakīrtitaiḥ |  
sarvaṃ vivicya vidhivadupacāraiḥ prapūjayet ||  
  
cakre yā devatā saṃkhyāḥ saṃjñācārghāsanāni ca |  
pātrāṇi pūrṇakumbhāśca pratyakṣāṇi nivedayet ||  
  
nānāvidhairalaṃkārairvastrayugmaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak |  
puṣpadhūpākṣataiścaiva sugaṃdhaiśca manoharaiḥ ||  
  
śrīkhaṇḍā gurukarpūrairmṛgamābhi vilepanaiḥ |  
mudrābhiśca namaskārairgītavādyaistathaiva ca ||  
  
vinayena mahādeviṃ toṣayediṣṭadevatāṃ |  
saṃtarpya japahomādi sarvaṃ pūrvavadācaret ||  
  
atha kāmyādau dhyāna viśeṣamāha ||  
  
varadā bhayahastāstu prasannavadanāḥ śubhāḥ |  
śuklāṃ varaparīdhānāḥ śāṃtikarmaṇi ciṃtayet ||  
  
pāśāṃkuśa mahācāpa puṣpavāṇadharāyudhāḥ |  
raktāmvaradharā devyāvaśya karmaṇi ciṃtayet ||  
  
kṛṣṇā kṛṣṇāṃvarā raudrā raudrāyudha parigrahāḥ |  
bhīmakaṃkāladhāriṇyo maṃtra mālāvarā karāḥ ||  
  
kapālakartṛkāhastā pivaṃtyo rudhirāsavaṃ |  
carvaṃtposthīni khādaṃtyo māraṇaivaṃ viciṃtayet ||  
  
pītāṃvara parīdhānā vajrahastā mahābalāḥ |  
staṃbhanekari kuṃbhasthā dhyātavyāḥ śrīkulāṃvike ||  
  
uccāṭane mṛgārūḍhāḥ dhvajahastā su caṃcalāḥ |  
dhūmravarṇā mahādevyoḥ parvatānyā tapaṃ tyapi ||  
  
mohane nīlarūpāśca ākṛṣṭau kapilāruṇau |  
kapotāścaiva vidveṣe citrāroga vivarddhane ||  
  
evaṃ karmānurūpeṇa carkāmnāyamidaṃ priyaṃ |  
yaṣṭyaṃ phalapradaṃ samyak bhaviṣyati na cānyathā ||  
  
pūjā japastathā homaṃ maṃtravidyā gaṇasya ca |  
dhyānaṃ cakroktamārgeṇa śāṃtikādau yathā vidhiḥ ||  
  
atha balidānaṃ ||  
  
pūjā gṛhāduttaratastrikoṇe bhūgṛhāṃtare |  
ucchiṣṭa bhairavaṃ tatra gaṃdha puṣpādibhiryajet ||  
  
ucchiṣṭa doṣo bhavati cakrapūjā mahotsave |  
taddoṣa parihārārthaṃ bhairavaṃ pūjayāmyahaṃ ||  
  
tālatrayaṃ tathocchiṣṭa bhairave hi dvayaṃ tathā |  
valiṃ gṛhṇayugaṃ hū& phaṭ svāhā dvāviṃśadakṣarā ||  
  
anena balidānaṃ tu pūjāṃ tesyāṃ prakalpayet |  
pūjāgāraṃ samāgatya praṇameccakra saṃsthitāṃ ||  
  
paṭhet stotramidaṃ bhadre ekākārasubhāvitaḥ |  
namaste cakravartistu namaste jñānadāyine ||  
  
namaste śivarūpāya namaste bhavatārakaḥ |  
aṣṭāṣṭakāstu yoginyaḥ kṣetrapālāstathaiva ca ||  
  
p. 221b)  
  
bhairavaṃ ca imaṃ cakraṃ ekākāraṃ namāmyahaṃ |  
evaṃ stotraṃ paṭhedādyaṃ niveśya svayamāsane ||  
  
jyeṣṭānu kramataḥ sthāpyaṃ cāsaneṣu yathāvidhiḥ |  
strīṇāmanyatamaṃ sthānaṃ puṃsāmanyatamaṃ pṛthak ||  
  
athavā mithunaṃ kṛtvā kramāt samupaveśayet |  
paṃktyākāreṇa vā samyak cakrākāreṇa vā punaḥ ||  
  
śivaśaktidhiyāḥ sarvān cakramadhye samarcayet ||  
  
gurupātraṃ samādāya madyāmṛtayutaṃ kare |  
pariṣiṃcet sāmayikāṃ nītiṃ śāṃtiṃ svayaṃ paṭhan ||  
  
jayaṃti devyā harapādapaṃkajaṃ prasanna vāmāmṛta mokṣadāyakaṃ |  
anaṃta siddhāṃtamati pravodha kṛnnamāmi sāṣṭāṣṭakayoginīgaṇaṃ ||  
  
yoginī cakramadhyasthaṃ mātṛmaṇḍala veṣṭitaṃ |  
namāmi śirasānāthaṃ bhairavaṃ bhairavīṃ priyaṃ ||  
  
anādi ghorasaṃsāra dhyāṃta vidhvaṃsakāriṇe ||  
  
namaḥ śrīnāthavaidyāya kulauṣadhavidhāyine |  
āpadoduritaṃ rogāḥ samayācāra laṃghanāt ||  
  
yeḥ sarvete vyapohaṃ tu divyacakrasya melanāt |  
āyurārogyamaiśvaryaṃ kīrtirlābhaḥ śubhojayaḥ ||  
  
kāṃtiṃ manorathaścāstu pāṃtu sarvāśca devatāḥ ||  
  
saṃpūjakānāṃ pratipālakānāṃ yatīṃdra yogīṃdra tapodhanānāṃ |  
viśvasya rāṣṭrasya purasya rājñaḥ karotu śāṃtiṃ bhagavān kuleśaḥ ||  
  
naṃdaṃ tu sādhakakulādapi darśakāye sṛṣṭvāghanākhya caturakta   
mahātvayāye |  
naṃdastu sarvakulakaularatāḥ parāyetvanye viśeṣa padabhedaka śāṃbhavāye ||  
  
naṃdaṃ tu siddhaguravastadanukramaughājyeṣṭānujāḥ samayino vaṭukāḥ   
kumāryaḥ |  
ṣaṭyoginī pravaravīra kulaiḥ prasūtānaṃdaṃ tu bhūmipati godvija sādhulokāḥ ||  
  
naṃdaṃ tu nītinipuṇā niravadyaniṣṭhāni matsarā nirūpamā nirūpadravāśca |  
nityaṃ niraṃjanaratā guravo niraṃtāḥ śāṃtograśāṃtamanaso hṛta   
śokaśaṃkāḥ ||  
  
naṃdaṃ tu yoginiratāḥ kulayogayuktā ācārya sāmayika sādhaka putrakāśca |  
bhāvodvijā yuvatayo yatayaḥ kumāryodharme bhavaṃ tu niratā guruśiṣyayuktāḥ ||  
  
naṃdaṃ tu sādhaka kulānyaṇimādyaniṣṭāḥ śāpāḥ pataṃtu samayadyuṣi   
yoginīnāṃ |  
sā śāṃbhavī sphuratu kāpi mamāpyavasthā yasyāṃ guroścaraṇa paṃkajameva   
labhyaṃ ||  
  
p. 222a)  
  
yāścakra krama bhūmikā vasatayo nāḍīṣuyāḥ saṃsthitāyāḥ   
kāyadrumaromakūpanilayāyāḥ saṃsthitā dhātuṣu |  
ucchvāsormimaruttaraṃganilayāniśvāsavāsāśvayāstā devyo ripupakṣabhakṣaṇa   
parāstṛpyaṃ tu kaulārcitāḥ ||  
  
yādivyāḥ kulasaṃbhavāḥ kṣitigatāyā devatāstopagāyā nityaṃ prathitaprabhā   
śikhigatāyā mātaraḥ svāśravyāḥ |  
yo māmamṛtamaṇḍalāmṛtamayāyāḥ sarvagāḥ sarvadātāḥ sarvāḥ   
kulamārgapālanaparāḥ śāṃtiṃ prayacchaṃtu me ||  
  
ūrddhvaṃ brahmāṇḍake vā divigagaṇatale bhūtale niṣkale vā pātāle vā nale vā   
salila pavanayoryatra kutrasthito vā |  
kṣetre pīṭhopapīṭhādiṣu ca kṛtapadā dhūpadīpādi māṃsaiḥ prītādevyaḥ   
sadānaḥ kṛtavalividhināpāṃtu dhīreṃdravaṃghāḥ ||  
  
brahmā śrīśeṣadurgāguhavaṭukagaṇāḥ bhairavāḥ kṣetrapālā vetālāditya rudrā   
grahavasu munayaḥ siddhayo guhyakādyāḥ |  
bhūtā gaṃdharvavidyādharaṛṣipitaraḥ kinnarāyakṣanāgāyogīśāścāranāḥ   
kiṃ puruṣamunisurāścakragāḥ pāṃtu sarve ||  
  
dehasthā khiladevatā gajamukhāḥ kṣetrādhipā bhairavāḥ yoginyo vaṭukāśca   
yakṣapitaro bhūtāḥ piśāgrahāḥ |  
anye bhūcaradikvarāśca khacarā vetālakāśceṭakāstṛptāḥ syuḥ kulaputrakasya   
pivataḥ pānaṃ madīyaṃ carut ||  
  
satyaṃ cedgurudakṣadevapitaro vedāgamā yoginī prītiścet paradevatā yadi   
bhavedvedāḥ pramāṇaṃ hi cet |  
śākteyaṃ yadi darśanaṃ bhavati vedājñāpyamoghāsticetsatpaṃcāpi ca   
kulikāśca yadi cetsyānme jayaḥ sarvadā ||  
  
tṛpyaṃ tu sādhakāḥ sarve sa mudrāḥ sa gaṇādhipāḥ |  
yoginyaḥ kṣetrapālāśca mamadehe vyavasthitāḥ ||  
  
śivādya vaniparyetaṃ brahmādi staṃbha saṃyutaṃ |  
kālājñādi śivāṃtaṃ ca jagadyajñena tṛpyatāṃ ||  
  
paṭhitvebhyarcanāpātraṃ samudvāsya gurustataḥ |  
dadyācchiṣyāya kuṃbhasthaṃ yoginībhyaḥ pṛthak pṛthak ||  
  
pātraṃ tathaiva vīrebhyaścetarebhyaḥ svayaṃ pivet ||  
  
vakṣyetha kaulikācāraṃ lokadvaya phalapradaṃ |  
pātramelāpakaṃ carma procyate kārakaṃ ||  
  
na bhrātā na pitā mitraṃ pātramelāpakādṛte |  
adīkṣitairanācāraira maṃtrajñaira daivataiḥ ||  
  
dūṣitaiḥ samayarduṣṭaiḥ prapaṃca vratadhāribhiḥ |  
strīdviṣṭairgurusaptaiśca bhaktihīnairdurātmabhiḥ ||  
  
p. 222b)  
  
anabhiścairanya pānaiḥ paśubhiḥ kṣudrakarmabhiḥ |  
padavākya pramāṇajñaiḥ śruti smṛtyartha vedibhiḥ ||  
  
strīdviṣṭairguru saptaiśca bhaktihīnairdurātmabhiḥ |  
anabhijñairanyayānaiḥ paśubhiḥ kṣudrakramabhiḥ ||  
  
pādavākya pramāṇajñaiḥ śrutismṛtyarthaḥ vedibhiḥ |  
kulopadeśahīnaiśca vaiṣṇavavratakāribhiḥ ||  
  
brahmatejo mukhaiḥ pātramelanaṃ naiva kārayet |  
tvat pūjā nirataiḥ śāṃtaiḥ paradravya parāṅmukhaiḥ ||  
  
kulopadeśakuśalaiḥ kulamārga pravartakaiḥ |  
strīpriyaiḥ strīstutairddhatyaiḥ suṃdarairmṛduvādibhiḥ ||  
  
kulamārgeti guptaiśca vidyāvadbhiḥ surūpakaiḥ |  
prayogasiddhairdravyādyairbhāgya vadbhiśca kāmukaiḥ ||  
  
brahmabhaktairājamānyairmilitairdevayogataḥ |  
kuryāt pātrasya melāpaṃ saukhya vṛddhirdvayorbhavet ||  
  
ekapātraṃ na kurvīta yadi sākṣāt kuleśvaraḥ |  
maṃtrāḥ parāṅmukhāyāṃti vighnāścaiva pade pade ||  
  
na dadyādbhairavāyāpi svapātrasthita hetukaṃ |  
yadi dadyācca mohena devatāśāpamāpnuyāt ||  
  
āsanaṃ bhojanaṃ pātraṃ manyavraśayanādikaṃ |  
anabhijñairanarhaiśca śaṃkaraṃ naiva kārayet ||  
  
śroto bhedena vā kuryāt kaulikaiḥ pātramelanaṃ |  
pūrvadakṣiṇayoraikyamudakpaścimayostathā ||  
  
yogibhiryoginībhiśca pradattaṃ pūrṇapātrakaṃ |  
svamaṃtra pādukā mūlamaṃtrajaptaṃ pivet tataḥ ||  
  
kvacidyadicchayā prāpta malipātraṃ tu bhaktitaḥ |  
ādāya pūrvavahutvā pivet tacca guruṃ smaret ||  
  
gurubhaktiyutānāṃ ca gurujyeṣṭha kaniṣṭhayoḥ |  
svajyeṣṭhasyāpi cocchiṣṭaṃ khādennānyasya karhicit ||  
  
jyeṣṭhe kanīyase yojyaṃ na punargrāhayet tataḥ |  
śaktyucchiṣṭaṃ pivenmadyaṃ vīrocchiṣṭaṃ tu carvaṇaṃ ||  
  
ātmocchiṣṭaṃ na dātavyaṃ parakīyaṃ na bhakṣayet |  
ucchiṣṭaṃ bhakṣayet strīṇāṃ tābhyāṃ nocchiṣṭamarpayet ||  
  
svasya melāpakasyāpi sthāpayedekamaṇḍale |  
pātraṃ tatorcayeddevīṃ tarpaṇādi samācaret ||  
  
utthāpyānyonya pātre ca dadyādanyonya hastayoḥ |  
dvayoraikyaṃ smaranyeyamiti pātrasya melanam ||  
  
p. 223a)  
  
vālopi dīkṣitaḥ pūrve jyeṣṭasya tu kulāgame |  
dvijopi dīkṣitaḥ paścādantyajaḥ pūrvadīkṣitaḥ ||  
  
dvijaḥ kaniṣṭhaḥ sa jyeṣṭha iti śāstra viniścayaḥ |  
svaśaktiṃ vīraśaktiṃ ca dīkṣitāṃ gururūpiṇīṃ ||  
  
pāyayitvā pivenmadyamiti śāstrasya niścayaḥ |  
tasmāt sulakṣaṇāṃ śaktiṃ gaṃdha puṣpākṣatādibhiḥ ||  
  
abhyarcya devatā vuddhyā bhogapātraṃ nivedayet ||  
  
śrīmadbhairava śeṣa vā mṛtalasaccandrāmṛtaplāvitaṃ kṣetrādhīśvarayoginī   
janagaṇaiḥ siddhaiḥ samārādhitaṃ |  
ānaṃdārṇavakaṃ na cātyakamidaṃ sākṣāt trikhaṇḍāmṛtaṃ vaṃde   
śrīprathamaṃ karāṃvujayutaṃ pātraṃ viśuddhīpradaṃ ||  
  
sarvāmnāya kalakalāpakalitaṃ kautūhala dyotakaṃ caṃdropendra mahendra   
śambhu varuṇa brahmādibhiḥ sevitaṃ |  
dhyātaṃ devagaṇaiḥ paraṃ munigaṇairmokṣārthibhiḥ sarvadā ||  
  
lokānāmativarddhanaṃ sukhakarapātraṃ dvitīyaṃ namaḥ ||  
  
madyaṃ māṃsaka matsyakaṃ harihara brahmādibhiḥ pūritaṃ mudrāmaithuna   
dharmakarma sukhadaṃ kṣārāmlatiktāśrayaṃ |  
ācāryārcitamaṣṭabhairava kalānyāsena saṃśodhitaṃ pāyāt paṃcamakāra   
saṃyutamidaṃ pātraṃ tṛtīyaṃ namaḥ ||  
  
āvirbhūta sa golakuṇḍa sukhadaṃ brahmādi rudrārcitaṃ nārājyaṃ prathamoṃ   
gajātakusumaṃ divyādhi kūṭaṃ paraiḥ |  
machochaumalamuttamottamarasaṃ saṃsevya divyāmṛtaṃ bhūyaḥ paṃcaka   
muktikāmakamidaṃ pātraṃ caturthaṃmude ||  
  
ādhāre bhujagādhirāja valaye pātraṃ mahīmaṇḍalaṃ madyaṃ saptasamudra vāri   
piśitaṃ cāṣṭau ca digdaṃtinaḥ |  
sohaṃ bhairavamarcayan pratidinaṃ tārāgaṇairlakṣitaṃ āditya pramukhaiḥ   
surāsuragaṇairājñākaraiḥ kiṃkaraiḥ ||  
  
chatraṃ cāmara bhadrapīṭha paramānaṃdāyiṃtadāpi rāmārājñya manoharaṃ   
sukhakaraṃ sāyujya sāmrājyadaṃ |  
nānāvyādhibhavāṃdhakāra haraṇaṃ janmāṃtaraṃ nāśanaṃ   
śrīmatsuṃdaritarpaṇendra varadaṃ pātraṃ ca ṣaṣṭaṃ bhajet ||  
  
jāgrat svapnasuṣuptituryapurato caitanya sākṣāt pradaṃ vidyudbhāskara vahnicendra   
dhanuṣajyotiḥ kathābhāṣitaṃ |  
iḍāpiṃgalamadhyagā trivalayā sat kuṇḍalīcorddhagāpātraṃ saptamapūraṇena   
taruṇānaṃdādhikaḥ pātumāṃ ||  
  
p. 223b)  
  
khaḍgaṃ pādukamaṃjanaṃ ca guṭikaṃ sārasvataṃ satyadaṃ   
mṛtyorvaṃcanamugrakāryaṃ grahaṇaṃ dehasthireḥ kāraṇaṃ |  
pāyāt siddhikaraṃ manaḥ sthirakaraṃ vaśyaṃ jagaghoṣitāṃ pātraṃ   
cāṣṭasiddhikaraṇaṃ prauḍhaḥ prasannaṃ sadā ||  
  
sarvānandakaraṃ sadāśivapadaṃ dvaṃdvaika bhaktipradaṃ sāmrājyaṃ sukhadaṃ   
manorathakaraṃ tvaṃ jñānavidhvaṃsanaṃ |  
āyuḥ kīrtiyaśovivarddhanakaraṃ saṃsāra mohachidaṃ pātreyaṃ navanātha śakti   
navakaṃ prauḍha pratāpoditaṃ ||  
  
tripātraṃ paṃcapātraṃ vā saptapātramathāpi vā |  
navapātraṃ pivedvāpi ṣoḍaśārddhaṃ pivenna hi ||  
  
yāvanna calate dṛṣṭiryāvanna calate manaḥ |  
tāvatpānaṃ prakurvīta paśuyāna mataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
pūrṇābhiṣeka yuktānāmānaṃ devi nigadyate |  
karābhyāṃ pātramuddhṛtya smaran mūlaṃ ca pādukāṃ ||  
  
āgalāṃtaṃ pivenmadyaṃ sa mukto nātra saṃśayaḥ |  
pītvā pītvā punaḥ pītvā yāvatyatati bhūtale ||  
  
utthāya ca punaḥ pītvā punarjanma na vidyate |  
ānaṃdāt tṛpyate devī mūrchayā bhairavaḥ svayaṃ ||  
  
camanāt sarvadevāstu tasmāt tritayamācaret ||  
  
brahmājñānī kulācāre surāṃ pītvā sa balanmuhuḥ |  
bhūmau patati tasyāṅgelagaṃti yadi reṇavaḥ ||  
  
tāvat kālaṃ reṇu saṃkhyaṃ brahmaloke samodate |  
pītvā pītvā japitvā ca muktaḥ koṭī kulaiḥ saha ||  
  
brahmaloke vaseddevi satyaṃ satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ |  
tatraiva vyāpti māpnoti na punaḥ prapatediha ||  
  
pītvā ca pūjayitvaiśāmīśatvaṃ labhateddhruvaṃ |  
tatraiva layamāpnoti punarnnaiva nivartate ||  
  
tatra matteṣu vīreṣu kāryākāryaṃ na vidyate |  
tatra yadyat kṛtaṃ karma śubhaṃ vā yadi vā śubhaṃ ||  
  
tatsarvaṃ devatā prītyai jāyate mātra saṃśayaḥ |  
jalpo japaphalaṃ taṃdrā samādhirabhidhīyate ||  
  
vikriyā pūjanaṃ proktaṃ charditaṃ bhairavo valiḥ |  
mūrchāsyācchakti saṃyoga stotraṃ tatkāla bhāṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
nyāsovayava saṃsparśo bhojanaṃ havanakriyā |  
dhyānaṃ vīkṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ śayanaṃ vaṃdanaṃ bhavet ||  
  
tadullā sa kṛtānāṃ ca yā ceṣṭā sā ca satkriyā |  
kāryākāryavikāraṃ tu yaḥ karoti sapātakī ||  
  
etaccakragatā vīrā vijñeyāḥ parayoginaḥ |  
ye nā sruvaṃti manujāḥ sākṣādbhairavarūpatāṃ ||  
  
saṃmoda kopaśamanaṃ patanodgāṇa nartanaṃ |  
veṇuvīṇādivādyaṃ ca kavitā racanādikaṃ ||  
  
rodanaṃ bhāṣaṇaṃ pātaḥ samutthānaṃ vijṛṃbhaṇaṃ |  
gamanaṃ vikriyā devī yoga ityabhidhīyate ||  
  
p. 224a)  
  
vikṛtiṃ manaso hitvā yadollāsaḥ pravartate |  
tadā tu devatā bhāvaṃ bhajaṃte yogapuṃgavāḥ ||  
  
kaulikān bhairavāveśān yo vā niṃdati mūḍhadhīḥ |  
tannāśayaṃtya saṃdeho yoginyo nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
yadvadbhakimadāveśādadmuktaṃ kauliko mataḥ |  
tat tadbhavatya saṃdigdhaṃ śubhaṃ vā yadi vā śubhaṃ ||  
  
tāro namo bhagavati madyamāṃsavihāriṇī |  
rati priye cakradevī vada kaulikavallabhe ||  
  
satyaṃ manogatamedyet yuktvā madyaṃ palānvitaṃ |  
pradadyāt kaulikebhyastattanmattāḥ pravruvaṃtite ||  
  
tatra kaścidakaulaścenna ca sphurati bhāratī ||  
  
na niṃdenna haset drapyeccakre madhumadā kulān |  
etaccakragatāṃ vārtāṃ vahirnaiva prakāśayet ||  
  
tebhyodrohaṃ na kurvīta nāhitaṃ ca samācaret |  
baktyā saṃrakṣayettānnai gopayecca prayatnataḥ ||  
  
cakre ca pramadāṃ dṛṣṭvā ciṃtayed devatādhiyā |  
modate vaṃdate bhaktyā sa gacched yoginī padaṃ ||  
  
pravṛtte bhairavī cakre sarve varṇād vijātayaḥ |  
nivṛtte bhairavī cakre sarve varṇāḥ pṛthak pṛthak ||  
  
striyotha puruṣaḥ paśuścāṇḍālo vā dvijottamaḥ |  
cakra madhye na bhedosti sarve deva samāḥ smṛtāḥ ||  
  
cakramadhye gatāḥ sarve puruṣāḥ śivarūpiṇaḥ |  
striyaḥ sarvāśca pārvatyā tasmādbhedaṃ na kārayet ||  
  
kāmuko na striyaṃ gaccheda nicchaṃti madīkṣitāṃ |  
sadyaḥ saṃskāra saṃśuddhāṃ vihitatvād vrajet striyaṃ ||  
  
sahasracakra pūjātorājyabhraṣṭo nṛpo bhavet |  
paṃcāśadbhiśca putrāptirnīrogodaśabhirbhavet ||  
  
yasya cakrasya pūjāyāṃ ratāt skhalati cāṃganā |  
avaśyaṃ sārvabhaumo sauvarṣamadhye bhaviṣyati ||  
  
yathepsita priyāprāptyai paṃcadhāpūjanaṃ caret ||  
  
atha kaulikārcanaṃ ||  
  
maheśvaraṃ samālokya pūjayedvidhi pūrvakaṃ |  
yathā vibhavarūpeṇa paṃcatatvaṃ navadya ca ||  
  
sadā tuṣṭā bhaveddevī sarvān kāmāṃllabhedapi |  
anyathā naiva siddhiḥ syāt kruddhā bhavati yoginī ||  
  
medinīṃ yastu pūrṇāṃ ca brāhmaṇo vedapārage |  
datvā yatphalamāpnoti tatphalaṃ kaulikārcane ||  
  
aśvamedha sahasrāṇi vājapeya śatāni ca |  
īṣṭvā yat phalamāpnoti tatphalaṃ kaulikārcane ||  
  
p. 224b)  
  
merutulya suvarṇaṃ tu brāhmaṇe vedapārage |  
datvā yatphalamāpnoti tatphalaṃ kaulikārcanāt ||  
  
vāpī kūpa taḍāgidi kṛtvā yatphalamāpnuyāt |  
tatphalāllakṣaguṇitaṃ kaulikānāṃ prapūjanāt ||  
  
kapilāṃ ca gavāṃ datvā yatphalaṃ labhate naraḥ |  
tatphalaṃ koṭi guṇitaṃ kaulikānāṃ prapūjanāt ||  
  
atha dūtīyāgaḥ ||  
  
puruṣeṇa vinā kiṃcit prakṛtyā kriyate nahi |  
tathā śaktiṃ vinā devophalaṃ dātu kṣamo nahi ||  
  
tasmāt puṃśakti saṃyogaṃ kṛtvā maṃtraṃ prasādhayet |  
kaulike vāmamārge ca pumāndevo na siddhyati ||  
  
ātmānaṃ tu śivaṃ dhyāyed devatāṃ śaktirūpiṇīṃ |  
krīḍetyaṃ ca makāraistu suprītā tasya devatā ||  
  
dakṣamārge mātṛbuddhiḥ strībuddhiḥ kaulike pathi |  
yasya tāstā dṛḍhatarātasya tuṣṭāttu devatā ||  
  
etadrahasyamākhyātaṃ gopyaṃ mātari jāravat ||  
  
śaivāḥ smārtā yājñikāśatānna kurvaṃti pārvatī |  
kaulānāmāgamajñānāṃ tāṃtrikācāravartināṃ ||  
  
anukalpapradātṝṇāṃ madhyasthānāṃ tathaiva ca |  
devīti buddhiryositsuyeṣāmatirar caṃcalā ||  
  
teṣāṃ kālī subhaktānāṃ sarvadā niścitātmanāṃ |  
āvaśyakī śaktipūjā pīṭhapūjā vadīśvari ||  
  
kālīvuddhyaiva saṃpūjyā na kāmākulayādhiyā |  
caturthāśramiṇā muktāye kālyarcana tatparāḥ ||  
  
kaulikā vāpya kaulā vāme caitanmatavartinaḥ |  
teṣāṃ nityā śaktipūjāprāhaivaṃ māṃ puradviṣaḥ ||  
  
sā śaktirdvividhā jñeyā svakīyā ca parāṅganā |  
svajātiḥ saṃbhavāyā tu pariṇītā bhavet priye ||  
  
sā svakīyā samuddiṣṭā tathāneyaṃ praśasyate |  
parakīyā paṃcavidhātāḥ krameṇa vravīmyahaṃ ||  
  
saṃjīvadbhartṛkā caikā tādṛgeva mṛtapriyā |  
dāsī veśyā tathā'nūḍhā praśastā cottarottaraṃ ||  
  
ajātavatsā yuvatītā svādyaiva praśasyate |  
kadācijjātavatsāpi sā sarvasadṛśīmatā ||  
  
abhāve pūrvapūrvāyāḥ parāgrāhyā hi sādhakaiḥ |  
sādhikāyāstu kaulāyā evameva pumānapi ||  
  
na sādhakaṃ vinā nāryo na puṃsaḥ sādhikāmṛte |  
maṃtrāḥ siddhyaṃti deveśi kalpakoṭi śatairapi ||  
  
p. 225a)  
  
parastrī saṃgamo madyopaśūnvā prāṇimāraṇaṃ |  
svārthaṃ cennarakāyaiva devyarthaṃ sukṛtāya hi ||  
  
ko hetunnavijānāmi devīprītikarā ityame |  
na pāpa janakaṃ yadvadyajñārthaṃ paśughātanaṃ ||  
  
na kilviṣakarastadvat parastrīsaṃgamādikaḥ ||  
  
atha śaktīnāṃ jātiviśeṣaḥ ||  
  
naṭīkāpālinī veśyā rajakīnāpitāṃgatā |  
brāhmaṇī śūdrakanā ca tathā gopālakanyakā ||  
  
mālākārasya kanyā ca na ca kanyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
nānyūnāṃgyonādhikāṃgyo na sthūlānādhikaṃ kṛśā |  
na chinnanāsāṃgulikā na dīrghā na ca vāmanā ||  
  
na guṇḍitā na kubjāśca mūkāṃdha vadhirā na ca |  
na kekarā na khaṃjāśca bhinnayonirgalātkucā ||  
  
vālāpatyāśca nityebhyo na kāryāḥ śaktayastvimāḥ |  
vadāmi yogyāṃ sādhikyāṃ yābhistuṣpatikālikā ||  
  
gaurāṃgī yuvatī ramyāsmerāsyā cāruvigrahā |  
viśālalola nayanā pīnonnatapayodharā ||  
  
viśālajamanā bhogāvali traya virājitā |  
supārśva tanumadhyā ca susvarā kuṃcitālakā ||  
  
vicitraveśābharaṇā vicitrāṃ varadhāriṇī |  
vicitra sraksamākīrṇā vicitraratidāyikā ||  
  
sadā prasannavadanā devyā bhaktiparāyaṇā |  
kaulikācaraṇajñā ca sādhake bhakti tatparā ||  
  
bhayahīnā smeramukhī sarvadā priyavādinī |  
samayācāra sampannā maṃtrajñā bhayavarjitā ||  
  
vidagdhā cā prasūtā ca dhairya svātaṃtrya saṃyutā |  
evaṃ guṇa samāyuktāḥ pūjayet sarvayoṣitaḥ ||  
  
atha vidyāviśeṣe śaktiviśeṣamāha ||  
  
gaṃdharūpā jātibhedairmahāvidyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |  
tat kramaṃ devadeveśi śṛṇu yatnena sāṃprataṃ ||  
  
rūpagaṃdha krameṇaiva nāmadadyān maheśvarī |  
mātṛ pitṛ kṛtaṃ nāmatyaktvā yatnena pārvatī ||  
  
svayaṃ nāmapradadyādvai yathā yogena pārvatī ||  
  
yā kṛṣṇa nīlakṛṣṇābhā madhupiṃgalalocanā |  
sādhakā kāṃkṣi hṛdayā puṃgaṃdhāniṃdyagaṃdhikā ||  
  
tasyāṃ kālī samāyojyā sā kālī parikīrtitā ||  
  
p. 225b)  
  
madyagaṃdhā tu yā nārī raktanetrāti niṣṭhurā |  
mahogratārā sā proktā mahāpāpa vināśinī ||  
  
sarvadā bhojanāśaktā vahubhojyāti caṃcalā |  
trailokyamohanākārācchinnā vidyāḥ prakīrtitā ||  
  
sarvalakṣaṇa saṃyuktā nānāgaṃdha samākulā |  
suṃdarī cārukeśāṃ ca dīrghanetrā manoharā ||  
  
nānāvilāsakuśalā kulaśāstravicariṇī |  
guruvakṣaḥ sthalākrāṃtā madhyā viraladarśinī ||  
  
suṃdarī sā bhavedgaurī sarvakārya pravartinī ||  
  
yā sā tṛtīyā gaurāṃgī madhugaṃdhānulepanā |  
tripurānāma sā devī svapuṣpa kramasādhinī ||  
  
cārvaṃgī cārunetrā ca kaṃjapadmāsanasthitā |  
pītābharaṇabhūṣāṃgī kamalāḥ parikīrtitā ||  
  
guṃjāhāra vibhūṣādyā śyāmā caṃcalalocanā |  
cāruhāsā tu mātaṃgī vidyākhyātā maheśvarī ||  
  
divyavarṇā kṛśāṃgī ca divyagaṃdhānulepanā |  
bhuvaneśī mayā proktā nānābhūṣaṇabhūṣitā ||  
  
piṃganetrā piṃgakeśā kiṃcidduccāṭihāsinī |  
dhūmāvatī ca sā proktā siddhavidyā śṛṇu priye ||  
  
laṃvavaktrā ca laṃvauṣṭhī pītavarṇāti niścalā |  
bagalā sā maheśāni kīrtitā tava suvrate ||  
  
daśavidyā imākhyātā śaktirūpeṇa pārvatī |  
daśavidyā maheśāni mātṛ strībhaginī kramāt ||  
  
krīḍaṃti satataṃ devi vidyā eva na saṃśayaḥ |  
daśakramo maheśāni daśavidyā su yatnataḥ ||  
  
sarvathā kārayeddevi nānyathā yugakoṭibhiḥ |  
na hi siddhyaṃti deveśi daśapadma japena vaiḥ ||  
  
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena sva sva vidyā kramaṃ caret |  
ātmīyā ca parā caiva śaktimātraṃ maheśvari ||  
  
maṃtrādhi devatā vuddhyā pūjyāḥ sarvopacārakaiḥ |  
vividhaiḥ phalatāṃbūlairvastrālaṃkāra hemabhiḥ ||  
  
saṃpūjya vidhivadbhaktyā vahu hetuṃ pradāpayet |  
saṃbhogavāsanāṃ dhṛtvāyaḥ kuryācchakti pūjanaṃ ||  
  
sa dāridryamavāpnoti nārakī ca bhaveddhruvaṃ ||  
  
p. 226a)  
  
vahubhiḥ kiṃ vaco jālaiḥ samāsāt samayaṃ śṛṇu |  
nirdiśyate śaktipūjā kaulikānāṃ dine dine ||  
  
pratyahaṃ ca surādānaṃ tat svīkāro'nvahaṃ tathā |  
nityatoktastayorddevi kulamārgarateṣu ca ||  
  
heyāheya vicāropi viralaḥ śaktiṣu priye |  
anukalpapradā tṛṇāmapi nityatvameva hi ||  
  
vihāyagarhitā śaktiryogyā eva hi gṛhyate |  
itareṣāṃ śaktipūjākāmyā naimittikī tathā ||   
  
samādhisthita cittānāmitarāsāṃ nirākṛtiḥ |  
vidhānaṃ kalayedāniṃ maṃtrānapi ca pārvatī ||  
  
snātāṃ divyāṃ varadharāṃ nānālaṃkāra maṇḍitāṃ |  
yuvatīṃ pīna vakṣojāṃ tathā cākṛta bhojanāṃ ||  
  
haste gṛhītvā vāmorau sthāpayecchaktimuttamāṃ |  
aśaknuvā * (?) voḍaṃtāṃ devyā vāmetha cāsane ||  
  
vāmabhāge samālikhya trikoṇaṃ padmavartulaṃ |  
śvetarakta samāyuktāṃ nālaṃ siṃdūracarcitaṃ ||  
  
sādhakaḥ prāṅmukho bhūtvā devīṃ pratyuṅmukhīṃ yajet |  
uḍḍiyānaṃ tu tretāyāṃ kṛte pūrṇagiriṃ yajet ||  
  
jālaṃdharaṃ dvāpareṣu kāmapīṭhaṃ kalau yuge |  
tāni catvāri vakṣyāmi guhyādguhyatarāṇi ca ||  
  
ṛṣyādivaṃ caredādau tataḥ śodhanamācaret ||  
  
ṛṣyādikaṃ śṛṇvidānīṃ etasya suravaṃdite |  
śrīśaktipūjanasyāsya gonardda ṛṣirīritaḥ ||  
  
vikṛtiśchaṃda ākhyātaṃ śaktirūpā yadādanu |  
mahākālī devatā ca kāmo vījamudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
śaktirvadhūrbhauvaneśī kīlakaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ |  
śivaśaktiḥ sāmarasya prakāśe viniyogatā ||  
  
saṃsarga paṃcadīrghādyairvadhūvījaiḥṣaḍaṃgakaṃ |  
vidhāyātmaniśaktyaṃgenyāsaṃ vācyamathā caret ||  
  
strīcechakti padasthāne bhairaveti padaṃ vadet |  
yoṣidyoni padasthānesyāliṃga padakalpanā ||  
  
gurupadeśataścāpi svavuddhā vā sureśvari |  
druhaḥ sarvatra kartavyo liṃge tat tatpadeti ca ||  
  
samānaḥ kiṃtu gāyatryā māsamāno bhayatra hi |  
nyāsoddhāramidāniṃ tvaṃ sāvadhānā niśāmaya ||  
  
p. 226b)  
  
trayākāso ramārāvo yoginī roṣayoṣitā |  
ḍākinī pralayohāraḥ phetkārī karṇikāpi ca ||  
  
preto nṛsiṃhaḥ kulikaṃ cichaktiḥ sarvaśeṣagāḥ |  
ekaikaṃ parato dadyād vījaṃ nāmnā surārcite ||  
  
tānyapyādau kaulikī ca bhagamālinyanaṃtaraṃ |  
ratipriyā tathā'naṃgo'kulā samayapālinī ||  
  
madanonmādinī kāmāveśinī tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
vittonmāthinyapi tato mohanyākarṣaṇī tathā ||  
  
smarāturānaṅga rūpānaṅga hṛpramodinyanaṃtaraṃ |  
saṃtāpinī tataḥ saṃkṣobhiṇī ca tridaśārcite ||  
  
sarvaśeṣe parijñeyā sāmarasya svarūpiṇī |  
etāḥ ṣoḍaśa vaikāryā ṅeṃtāḥ pūrvārṇa saṃyutā ||  
  
strīkartṛkatve puṃliṃgā bhairavārcana karmaṇi |  
namaḥ śeṣeṣu sarveṣu sthānāni kalpayādhunā ||  
  
śiraḥ kapolau ca galaḥ skaṃdhau vakṣaḥ kuvau tathā |  
pārśvo kukṣiścanābhiścavastirvaṃkṣaṇa eva ca ||  
  
ūrujānū ca jaṃghe ca pādau yoniśca śekhagau |  
jīvanyāsa vadetasyāḥ sāmarasyamathā caret ||  
  
eta deveti saṃproktaṃ śaktiśodhanamīśvarī |  
kṛtvā prahastu karo datvānu hṛdurojayaoḥ ||  
  
kāmapīṭhetha vā devī nābhau maulīyakīmate |  
manuṃ gṛṇanvakṣyamāṇaṃ vāraikaṃ vā trivārakaṃ ||  
  
jīvanyāsātmakamidaṃ śaktiśodhanamācaret |  
anena śuddhyate śaktirnānyathā maṃtrakoṭibhiḥ ||  
  
māyākāmo vadhūrlakṣmīḥ kūrcaḥ prāsāda eva ca |  
śākinī ḍākinī cāpi vījānyaṣṭaupuraḥ smaret ||  
  
bhogānaṃda kalāśaktirjīvātmā paramātmakāḥ |  
prativiṃvādvaitasaṃjñakātmyanāmalayā'bhidhān ||  
  
daśakūṭān kramāt procya brahma tadviparītakaṃ |  
dvayaṃ daśāṃta uccāryamevamarddhārddhasammitaṃ ||  
  
tato mamānu hṛdayetavānu hṛdaye vadet |  
dadhātu mama vācyuktvāte vācaṃ samudīrayat ||  
  
mameṃdriyeṣu tadanu pravadet kamalānane |  
te iṃdriyāṇi ca saṃbhāṣya mama vācaṃ juṣasva ca ||  
  
tataḥ siddhikarālīti tvāṃ mahyaṃ niyunaktu ca |  
yaivatvaṃ ca sa evāhaṃ ya evāhamitīrayet ||  
  
p. 227a)  
  
saivatvaṃ saṃdhināyuktamubhau tadanukīrtayet |  
śivaśakti samārasya māpannau tadanaṃtaraṃ ||  
  
tadaikamiti saṃkīrtya sādhayāva itīrayet |  
sa saṃdhistāra hṛcchīrṣa maṃtrastadanu suṃdari ||  
  
ayaṃ maṃtraḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ śaktiśodhana karmaṇi |  
aṣṭottaraśatārṇādyona nyūnonāpi cādhikaḥ ||  
  
dhyānaṃ pūrvoditaṃ yatte bhagavatyā mayā tava |  
śaktiṃ ca tādṛgākāraṃ dhyāyedvīkṣyāṅga saṃcayaṃ ||  
  
bhairavadhyānasadṛśa mātmānaṃ ca vibhāvayet |  
tata āvāhayeddevīṃ śaktyaṃge pīṭhasannibhe ||  
  
vakṣyamāṇena maṃtreṇa sādhakoṃjali mudrayā |  
māyākāmavadhūrāva kamalā yoginīruṣaḥ ||  
  
ḍākinī cāpi phetkārī na vaitānyādigānihi |  
ehyehi bhagavatyuktvā mahākālī samīrayet ||  
  
śaktipīṭhe'nusānnidhyamāveśaya samuddharet |  
tatastvāmahamullikhyāvāhayāmi ca kīrtayet ||  
  
sarvaśakti samābhāvya svarūpiṇi tato vadet |  
tāraṃ pratiṣṭha śīrṣaṃ ca śakti mūlamanuṃ śṛṇu ||  
  
māyārāvaḥ smaro nārī śaktaye hṛdayaṃ tataḥ |  
maṃtro navākṣaraḥ proktaḥ śaktipūjana karmaṇi ||  
  
ṛṣyādirnāsti caitanya na chando vījaśaktayaḥ |  
kiṃtu pādyādi sarvopacārādyarpaṇa hetukaḥ ||  
  
japtavyo naiva cāyaṃ hi tripura pravaco yathā |  
sarvopacārānye tena pradadyāt kiṃtu śaktaye ||  
  
pādyadānādi naivedyadānāṃtaṃ yadyadiṣyate |  
na cānyamaṃtro bhinnāsti manmate jagadīśvari ||  
  
kūrcateyaṃtu mauleyā tadamūlaṃ vibhāvyatāṃ |  
śaktipūjā vaśiṣṭaṃ yat puṣpasraganulepanaṃ ||  
  
yadātmane dīyate tat sāmarasyārcanaṃ bhavet |  
tadamaṃtraṃ prakartavyaṃ mevamīśāna śāsanaṃ ||  
  
tato datvā karaṃ śaktiryonipīṭhe japaṃ caret |  
sādhakaḥ śaktigāyatryā śatamarddhārddhameva vā ||  
  
yonipīṭhe japaprakhyo na japaḥ kvāpi vidyate |  
sadyaḥ prabhāvajanako maṃtrāṇāṃ pīṭha uttamaḥ ||  
  
maṃtrāṇāṃ valahīnānāṃ prayoga kṣīṇacetasāṃ |  
anuddhṛtānāṃ śāpebhyo nyūnādhikyārṇatājuṣāṃ ||  
  
gurumliṣṭānāmapi ca pradānonaujasāṃ tathā |  
ajñānavidhi pūjānāma pātrārpaṇabhagināṃ ||  
  
tyaktānāṃ vismṛtānāṃ ca tathā caivā prabhāvināṃ |  
saṃdhukṣaṇārthamubhayaṃ proktaṃ tripuravairiṇā ||  
  
ekaṃ nirvāṇa maṃtreṇa saṃpuṭīṃ kṛtya tajjapaṃ |  
kaulāsane nāparaṃ ca yonipīṭhe japakriyā ||  
  
kaulāsanaṃ yonipīṭhe japaḥ strīṇā manugrahaḥ |  
gurustrī śaktitā cāpi miśrībhūya japedvayoḥ ||  
  
anyaiḥ samindhanaṃ matrairvījādhikya karaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
p. 227b)  
  
athātaḥ śaktigāyatrīṃ śṛṇu devi mahāphalaṃ |  
kāmavījād bhagavatīṃ ṅentāṃpurata īrayet ||  
  
vidmahe yonimālinyai dhīmahīti tataḥ paraṃ |  
tannaḥ śaktiriti procya sarvaśekhe pracodayāt ||  
  
eṣā hi śakti gāyatrī sarvāgama sugopitā |  
etāṃ ni nālaśakyarcāna śaktyarcāṅgiko tapaḥ ||  
  
yathāśakti japitvaināṃ tatsamarpya ca śaktaye |  
vāmorāvupaveśyaiva kuryān mūlajapaṃ priye ||  
  
pūjayenmadanāgāre raktacaṃdanacarcite |  
bhage tadīye vijñeyā nāḍyastisraḥ pravāhikāḥ ||  
  
ekottarāhikā cāṃḍī saurī cānyā tu vāhikāḥ |  
āgneyī cāparājñeyā pūjayettāstu sādhakaḥ ||  
  
aṃbu sravati cāṃḍī sā puṣpaṃ sravati bhānavī |  
vījaṃ sravati cāgneyītāstu nāmabhirarcayet ||  
  
vāgbhavādyairnamoyuktaiḥ pūjayet suprasannadhīḥ |  
dhyānaṃ kuryān maheśāni gahvare makarānane ||  
  
tāmracūḍaśikhākāraṃ gajavaktra samaprabhaṃ |  
tatra sthānaṃ ciṃtayeddevīṃ vidyāṃ bhuvanamohinīṃ ||  
  
bhagamālāmaṃtrastu ||  
  
vāgbhavaṃ bhagaśabdāṃte bhagebhagini cālikhet |  
bhagodari bhagāṃte tu bhagamāle bhagāvahe ||  
  
bhagaguhye bhagaprāṃte yoniprāṃte bhagāṃtake |  
nipātinī ca sarvāṃte tato bhagavaśaṃkarī ||  
  
bhagarūpe tato lekhyaṃ nīrajāyata locane |  
nityaklinne bhagaprāṃte svarūpe sarva cālikhet ||  
  
bhagāni mehyā namoṃte varadetha samālikhet |  
rete svarete bhagavat klinna klinna drave tataḥ ||  
  
kledaya drāvayaścātha sarvasatvān bhageśvari |  
amoghe bhagavīcce cakṣubhaḥ kṣobhaśca sarva ca ||  
  
satvān bhageśvari vrūyādvāgbhavaṃ vrū& japādidaṃ |  
bha& plū& mā& vlū& ca haiṃ klinne tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
sarvāṇi ca bhagānyaṃte meva śañcānayeti ca |  
strīvījaṃ ca haraprāṃte valamātmakamakṣaraṃ ||  
  
bhuvaneśīṃ samālikhya vidyeyaṃ bhagamālinī |  
caturthyaṃtaṃ yajeddevī bhage puṣpaṃ viniḥkṣipet ||  
  
prakṣālya kuladravyeṇa gaṃdhapuṣpaiḥ samarcayet |  
dhūpadīpādikaṃ kṛtvā paścādāvaraṇaṃ yajet ||  
  
ihāpyā vāhanaṃ nāsti jīvanyāsā maheśvarī |  
athaivaṃ ca vidhānenatāḥ ṣoḍaśopacārakaiḥ ||  
  
iṣṭadevīṃ prapūjyātha sarvasiddhīśvarośvaro bhavet ||  
  
p. 228a)  
  
arcayedgaṃdhapuṣpādyaiḥ svaśivaṃ tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
athanyāsaṃ pravakṣyāmi śivātmānaṃ vibhāvayet ||  
  
paṃcavaktraṃ mahādevaṃ kalāyuktaṃ nyaset kramāt |  
īśānassarvavidyānāṃ śaśinī prathamākalā ||  
  
īśvarassarvabhūtānāmaṅgadā tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
brahmādhipati śabdāṃte brahmaṇodhipatiḥ punaḥ ||  
  
brahmeṣṭadā śivomestu marīci saṃpuṭa nyaset |  
sadāśivaḥ samuccārya aṃśumālinyathā parā ||  
  
tatpuruṣāya vidmaheṃ kalāśāṃtiritīritā |  
mahādevāyadhīmahi kalāvidyā tathaiva ca ||  
  
tanno rudraḥ padaṃ paścāt pratiṣṭā kathitā kalā |  
pracodayāt samuccārya nivṛttiḥ syāt tataḥ paraṃ ||  
  
pūrvapaścimayāmyeṣu uttareṣva pāru kramāt |  
hṛdaye vinyaseddevī aghorebhyaḥ stamaḥ kalā ||  
  
atha ghorebhyo mohāṃ ca grīvāyāṃ vinyaset tataḥ |  
ghorāṃte syāt kriyāpaścād dakṣiṇāṃśe pravinyaset ||  
  
namastestu kṣudhāṃ paścāt kalāṃ pṛṣṭhe nyaset kramāt |  
rudrarupebhya ityaṃte tṛṣāntāra namoṃtakāḥ ||  
  
vāmadevāya namoṃte rajāsyād guhyadeśake |  
mukha savye pravinyasya rakṣāṃ jyeṣṭhāyavai namaḥ ||  
  
rudrāya namo ratiṃ paścād vāmamukhaṃ kalāmimāṃ |  
kālāya nama ityaṃte pālinī urudakṣiṇe ||  
  
kalakāmāya deveśi vāme vikaraṇāya ca |  
namaḥ padaṃ samuccārya saṃyamanīndakṣajānuni ||  
  
valakriyā samādiṣṭā vāme vikaraṇāya ca |  
namoṃte vṛddhimuccārya dakṣiṇe sphici vinyaset ||  
  
balapramathanāya namo rātriṃ vāme pravinyaset |  
sarvabhūtadamanāya namonte brāhmaṇīkalā ||  
  
kaṭideśe pravinyasya manau te mohinīṅkalāṃ |  
dakṣiṇe pārśvakenyasya unmanāya namojvalāṃ ||  
  
pādayostana nāsāsu mūrddhni vāhu yugenyaset |  
sadyo jātodbhavāssamyagaṣṭau maṃtrī kalāḥ kramāt ||  
  
sadyojātaṃ prapadyāmi siddhiḥ syāt prathamāḥ kalā |  
sadyo jātāya vai bhūyo namaḥ syādṛddhirīritā ||  
  
bhavedyutistṛtīyāsyāda bhave tadanaṃtaraṃ |  
lakṣmīścaturthī kathitā tato nāti bhave padaṃ ||  
  
medhākhyā paṃcamī proktā kalā bhūyo bhavasvanāṃ |  
prajñā samīritā ṣaṣṭī bhavāṃte syāt prabhā kalā ||  
  
p. 228b)  
  
udbhavāya namaḥ paścāt sudhāsyādaṣṭamī kalā |  
praṇavādyāścaturthyaṃtā namoṃtāśca pravinyaset ||  
  
evanyā sa vidhiṃ kṛtvā svayaṃ śaivaṃ vibhāvayet |  
paṃcākṣaraṃ puraskṛtya rudra dhyānaparāyaṇaḥ ||  
  
sāmarasyamayaṃ kṛtvā rakṣārthaṃ kavacaṃ paṭhet |  
vadhvā tu kṣobhiṇīṃ mudrāṃ yaṃtra madhye viniḥkṣipet ||  
  
bhagaṃ kuṃḍaṃ śruvo liṃgamādyaṃ caiva tu vīryakaṃ |  
sarvatatvaṃ samuccārya sahasraṃ japamācaret ||  
  
dharmādharma havirdīpta ātmāgnau manasā śruvā |  
suṣumṇā vartmanā nityamakṣa vṛttirjuhomyahaṃ ||  
  
svāhāṃ toyaṃ mahāmaṃtra āraṃbhe parikīrtitaḥ |  
śivaśakti samāyogo yoga eva na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
śītkāro maṃtrarūpaṃ ca vacanaṃ stavanaṃ bhavanaṃ bhavet ||  
  
āliṃganaṃ ca kastūrī karpūraṃ cuṃvanaṃ bhavet |  
nakhadaṃṣṭrākṣatādīni puṣpāṇi vividhāni ca ||  
  
mathanaṃ tarpaṇaṃ viddhi vījapāto visarjanaṃ ||  
  
āliṃganaṃ cuṃvanaṃ ca stanayormardanaṃ tathā |  
darśanaṃ sparśanaṃ yonirvikāraṃ liṃgagharṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
praveśaṃ sthāpanaṃ śakternnavapuṣpāṇi pūjayet |  
na dadyāccumbanaṃ yastu daridro jāyate dhruvaṃ ||  
  
āliṃganaṃ vinā devi kuṣṭī bhavati pārvatī |  
vinā daṃtakṣatairdevi loke bhavati niṃditaḥ ||  
  
āliṅgane haredrogān dhanadhānyādi cuṃbane |  
nakhadaṃtakṣatādyaiśca tadā mokṣaḥ prajāyate ||  
  
sāyujyaṃ saṃgame tasyāt satyameva na saṃśayaḥ |  
prakāśākāśahastābyāmavalaṃvyonmanī śrucā ||  
  
dharmādharma kalā snehapūrṇamagnau juhomyahaṃ |  
svāhāṃtoyaṃ mahāmaṃtraḥ śukratyāge prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
śuddha maṃtrauṣadhe naiva yānaistu maṃthanaṃ caret |  
madhyamāne ca tasyā hi jāyate tatvamuttamaṃ ||  
  
gṛhnīyāt tatprayatnena dravyaṃ kuṇḍodbhavaṃ śubhaṃ |  
tenāmṛtena divyena kāilkāṃ tarpayet sadā ||  
  
sānnidhyāt tatkṣaṇādvāpi prītā siddhiṃ prayacchati |  
samasta devatānāṃ tarpaṇaṃ ca sadāmṛtaiḥ ||  
  
guruṇāṃ sādhakānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ tarpaṇaṃ caret |  
te nāmṛtena divyena sarve tuṣṭā bhavaṃti ca ||  
  
yat kāmaṃ kurute maṃtrī tatkṣaṇādeva siddhyati ||  
  
kulāmṛtaṃ samādoya tatrārghe niḥkṣipedbudhaḥ |  
tataḥ somakalāḥ pūjyāḥ sādhakairnirmalāḥśayaiḥ ||  
  
p. 229a)  
  
madhubhāṇḍa sahasraistu māṃsa bhāraśatairapi |  
naiva tuṣṭā bhaveddevi bhagaliṅgāmṛtādṛte ||  
  
kuladravyaṃ ca saṃśodhya śivaśaktimayaṃ priye |  
jīvāmṛtaṃ parabrahmarūpaṃ niḥkṣipyasuṃdari ||  
  
arghyapātrāmṛtairyaṣṭvā nirvikalpaḥ sadānaghaḥ |  
arghadravyaiśca deveśi yonau devīṃ prapūjayet ||  
  
yonipūjāṃ vinā pūjā kṛtā vāpya kṛtā bhavet |  
dutīyāge kṛtaṃ maṃtrī sarvajñāyate dhruvaṃ ||  
  
na tasya punarāvṛttiḥ kalpakoṭi śatairapi |  
yaiḥ kṛtayajanaṃ dūtyāstairiṣṭāḥ kratavo'khilā ||  
  
sarvatīrthamayaḥ proktaḥ sarvadevamayo bhavet |  
puraścaryādi sakalaṃ kṛtaṃ tena na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
aśvamedha sahasrāṇi vājapeya śatāni ca |  
āsamudrā ca dharaṇī dattā tena sa dakṣiṇā ||  
  
merumaṇḍala tulyāni suvarṇānyarpitāni vai |  
go koṭi dānādyat puṇyaṃ tatpuṇyaṃ jāyate priye ||  
  
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena dūtīyāgaṃ samācaret |  
pūjā saṃpūrṇade bhadre sarvāriṣṭa pranāśakaṃ ||  
  
yonipūjāyutā pūjākṛtāmapyakṣayā bhavet |  
āyurārogya vibhavānamitā labhate naraḥ ||  
  
anenaiva vidhānena viṣārtto nirviṣo bhavet |  
putrārthī labhate putraṃ dhanārthī labhate dhanaṃ ||  
  
mātaṃgī śaktimabhyarcya tayāssākaṃ samarcayet |  
mātaṃgī manmathopetāṃ sarvakāmārthasiddhaye ||  
  
śaktyā sākaṃ sadā pujyā mātaṃgī maṃtradevatā |  
sā devī śaktihīnā tu na dadāti manorathaṃ ||  
  
pūrṇābhiṣeka rahito yaḥ śaktiṃ śodhayennaraḥ |  
sodhamaḥ patito rogī paṃcatvaṃ labhate dhruvaṃ ||  
  
iṃdriyāṇāma dhṛṣyatvāt kāmalābhādi saṃbhavāt |  
prāyaḥ kalau kaulikeyaṃ paṃthā naraka hetave ||  
  
uttamā nityapūjāsyān madhyamaṃ parvapūjanaṃ |  
māsapūjādhamā proktā māsādūrddhaṃ paśurbhavet ||  
  
māse vātha trimāse vā ṣaṇmāse vatsarepi vā |  
śrī guruṃ pūjayed bhaktyā prāptai tat strīsutādikān ||  
  
tadabhāve tat kulīnaṃ tacchiṣyaṃ vānyayoginaṃ |  
saṃtoṣayet kuladravyaṃścakrapūjā puraḥsaraṃ ||  
  
atha cakrasya viśeṣācāramāha ||  
  
ucchiṣṭo na spṛśeccakraṃ kuladravyaṃ tathā guruṃ |  
vahiḥ prakṣālya ca karau kuladravyāṇi dāpayet ||  
  
madyabhāṃḍaṃ samuddhṛtya na pātraṃ paripūrayet |  
bhogapātraṃ surākuṃbhaṃ niḥkṣipenna kadācana ||  
  
p. 229b)  
  
cakramadhye suvidhiṃ vā karāsya kṣālanādikaṃ |  
yaḥ karoti hi mūḍhātmā sa bhavedā padāṃ padaṃ ||  
  
niṣṭīvanaṃ malaṃ mūtramadho vāyuvisarjanaṃ |  
śrīcakramadhyeyaḥ kuryāt sa bhavedyoginī paśuḥ ||  
  
cakramadhye ghaṭe bhinne pātre vā skhalite tathā |  
dīpanāśe rāṣṭrapīḍā tacchāṃtyai cakrapūjanaṃ ||  
  
parihāsaṃ pralāpaṃ ca viḍaṃvaṃ vahubhāṣaṇaṃ |  
audāsīnyaṃ bhayaṃ krodhaṃ cakramadhye vivarjayet ||  
  
pātrahastaścakramadhyena bhramet pūrṇapātrakaṃ |  
ciraṃ na sthāpayeddhaste nālapetyotrapāṇikaḥ ||  
  
pādābhyāṃ na spṛśet pātraṃ na ca bhidyāt kadācana |  
naikahastena dātavyaṃ na viṃduṃ pātayedadhaḥ ||  
  
pātraṃ na cālaye sthānānna mudrāvarjitaṃ pivet |  
sa śabdaṃ na pivenmadyaṃ na kuryāt pātrasaṃkaraṃ ||  
  
pātrasyāṃśa dvayaṃ madyapūrṇaṃ tryaṃśaṃ turīyakaṃ |  
nānyonyaṃ tāḍayet pātraṃ na pātraṃ tāḍayedadhaḥ ||  
  
sādhāraṃ noddharet pātramanādhāreṇa niḥkṣipet |  
riktaṃ pātraṃ na kurvīta na pātraṃ laṃghayet tathā ||  
  
prakṣālya gopayet pātraṃ namoṃto vipramīkṣaye ||  
  
śrīcakrasthaṃ kuladravyaṃ dadyādyo vā kule jane |  
phalāni tasya naśyaṃti kruddhā bhavati devatā ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau sakalasādhāraṇacakrārcananirṇayo   
nāmāṣṭāviṃśatitamaḥ prakāśaḥ || 28 ||      
  
atha yaṃtranirmāṇa pratiṣṭhāmāha ||  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
deveśa śrotumicchāmi yaṃtrasthāpana nirṇayam |  
yaṃtraṃ tu gṛhamityuktaṃ yaṃtraṃ pīṭhaṃ prakīrtitaṃ ||  
  
sthirayaṃtre pratikṛtau nāvāhana visarjane |  
pratiṣṭāpya mahāyaṃtraṃ tatadyaṃtraṃ visarjayet ||  
  
yaṃtra pratiṣṭhāmāsādya vidyāṃ tatra vibhāvayet |  
jīvanyāsaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā vidyāṃ tatra vibhāvayet ||  
  
yaṃtraṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ kṛtvādau devaṃ tatra pratiṣṭhayet |  
tadā visarjanaṃ nāsti na cāvāhanameva ca ||  
  
ataḥ kālasya vyatyāsād yaṃtrameva pratiṣṭhayet |  
mūrtiṃ svahṛdgatī tatra dhyātvā pūjya visarjayet ||  
  
p. 230a)  
  
sphāṭikādiṃ svarṇaraupyaṃ yaṃtraṃ ca kārayet priye ||  
  
yāvajjīvaṃ suvarṇesyādraupye dvāviṃśatiṃ priye |  
tāmre dvādaśakaṃ varṣaṃ varṇe'naṃta phala * (?) ka ||  
  
kimvadāmite ||  
  
vidrume racite yaṃtre padmarāgetha vā priye |  
indranīletha vaiḍūrye sphāṭike marakaṭepi vā ||  
  
dhanaṃ putra tathā dārān yaśāṃsi labhate dhruvaṃ |  
suvarṇa racite pīṭhe bhūpālā ca śavartinaḥ ||  
  
rajate na kṛtaṃ yaṃtraṃ āyurārogyakāṃmadaṃ |  
tāmreṇa racite yaṃtraṃ sarvaiśvarya pradaṃ mataṃ ||  
  
yaṃtraṃ tu sphāṭikaṃ svacchaṃ manobhilaṣitapradaṃ |  
māṇikyā racitaṃ yaṃtraṃ rājyadaṃ bhuktimuktidaṃ ||  
  
kṛtaṃ marakaṭe yaṃtraṃ sarvaśatruvināśanaṃ |  
lauha trayodbhavaṃ yaṃtraṃ sarvasiddhikaraṃ mataṃ ||  
  
śrīkhaṇḍaṃ śāṃtidaṃ jñeyaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ raktacaṃdanaṃ |  
śrīparṇī pīṭhamuddiṣṭaṃ pūjārthaṃ dhanarājyadaṃ ||  
  
vaidrumaṃ vahulā saṃpadbhūrjapatre catuḥpadā |  
gaṇḍakī bhavapāṣāṇo bhuktirmuktira dūrataḥ ||  
  
bhūmau siṃdūra rajasā racitaṃ sarvakāmadaṃ |  
sīsakāṃsyādiṣu kṛte saṃpattiṃ saṃtataṃ haret ||  
  
phalakāyāṃ padebhittau sthāpayenna kadācana |  
sthāpitaṃ yadi mohena nāśayet taddhanaṃ kulaṃ ||  
  
teṣāṃ madhye sphāṭikastu sarvasiddhipradaṃ bhavet ||  
  
atha trilohānāṃ saṃkhyāmāha ||  
  
daśabhāgaṃ suvarṇasya tāmrasya dvādaśaṃ tathā |  
ṣoḍaśaṃ rajatasyāpi etallohatrayaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
atha parimāṇamāha ||  
  
arddhāṅgulyena homasya rajatasya tathaiva ca |  
tāmrasya pūrvasaṃkhyau ca māṇikyādau yathecchayāṃ ||  
  
palapramāṇaṃ kartavyamarcā pīṭhaṃ manoharaṃ ||  
  
agniraṃgula vistāra prāk pratyagdakṣiṇottaraṃ |  
parārddhorddhaṃ prakurvīta caturasraṃ samaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
māṇikyādika pīṭhaṃ tu mānanyūnaṃ na doṣakṛt |  
śrīparṇā caṃdanādīnāmadhikaṃ cenna doṣakṛt ||  
  
mahāśaṃkhe śilāyāṃ ca na ca yaṃtravicāraṇā ||  
  
athavā ||  
  
ekatolaṃ dvitolaṃ vā tritolaṃ paṃcatolakaṃ |  
rasatolaṃ vedatolaṃ saptāṣṭatolakaṃ tathā ||  
  
daśatolaṃ sūryatolaṃ kalāsaṃkhyakatolakaṃ |  
radatolaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭhitolakaṃ śatatolakaṃ ||  
  
p. 230b)  
  
yaṃtraṃ manojñaṃ sukhadaṃ surekhaṃ pīṭhamuttamaṃ ||  
  
atha prastāramāha ||  
  
cāturvidhyā hi cakrasya prastārāśca bhavaṃti hi |  
bhūkūrma padmaprastārā meruścāpi tathā vidhaḥ ||  
  
nimnarekhā samāyogo bhūprastāre mayoditeḥ |  
kūrmapadmaka prastāra ūrddhvarekhā mayoditā ||  
  
bhūprastāro dvidhā devi ūrddhva pātālabhedataḥ |  
tribhiḥ kramādunnataṃ syāt kramot kramamathāpi vā ||  
  
dvitrikramādunnatopi dvidvikramamathāpi vā |  
yvāṃtaraṃ yavārddhaṃ vā tilayuktilameva vā ||  
  
taṇḍulārddhaṃ tacca vā syāt tadvaya kramabhedataḥ ||  
  
meruḥ svarge ca kailāśe martyaloke prakīrtitaḥ |  
bhūprastārastu pātāle tritayaṃ kīrtitaṃ mayā ||  
  
kaṃjakūrma ratnagarbhāḥ sarvatrapūjane śubhāḥ |  
śubhāḥ sarvamaheśāni sarvasiddhi pradāyakāḥ ||  
  
ūrddhvarekhābhidheyaṃ tu pūjārthaṃ mṛtyugocaraṃ |  
sthāpanārthaṃ tu pātālarekhā ca kutracinmatā ||  
  
atha yaṃtralikha na karṇikādīnāṃ likhane sthānamāha ||  
  
paṃcavṛttāni saṃlikhya tatra yaṃtraṃ likhedbudhaḥ |  
ādyaṃ syāt karṇikā sthānaṃ keśarāṇāṃ dvitīyakaṃ ||  
  
tṛtīyaṃ dalamadhyasya dalāgrāṇāṃ caturthakaṃ |  
paṃcame būpuraṃ likhyamevaṃ yaṃtravidhau smṛtaṃ ||  
  
keśara dvayayuktaṃ ca dalaṃ proktaṃ maheśvarī |  
daṇḍākāraṃ viṃduvaktraṃ tadvayoktaṃ maheśvari ||  
  
pātālarekhā prastāre keśare mukhyaviṃdunā |  
ūrddhvarekhā vidhau devi rekhā keśaratā matā ||  
  
śrīvidyāyāṃ kālikāyāṃ keśarāṇi kvacicca vā |  
śrīvidyāyāṃ mahādevi keśarāṇi na kārayet ||  
  
yathā dalaṃ keśareṇa viyuktaṃ karmavarjitaṃ |  
tathā trikoṇaṃ deveśi biṃdunāvarjitaṃ bhavet ||  
  
viṃduhīnaṃ tu yadyaṃtraṃśa ca vadbhavet |  
tathaivāṣṭa dalayorddhe vṛttaṃ yatnena kārayet ||  
  
vṛttaṃ vinā cāṣṭadalaṃ garbhabhūṣaṇavarjitaṃ |  
ṛjurekhā bhavellakṣmīrvakrarekhā daridratā ||  
  
na rātrāvaṃkayedyaṃtraṃ sādhakastu kadācana |  
pramādādaṃkite caiva devatāśāpamāpnuyāt ||  
  
yaṃtramātre maheśāni nirṇayaḥ kathito mayā |  
ādhirupācca viṃvasya pūjāyāśca viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
p. 231a)  
  
sādhakasya ca viśvāsāddevaḥ sānnidhyamicchati ||  
  
atha yaṃtrāṇāṃ dhyānamāha ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
pūrve saṃsūcitaṃ nātha yaṃtradhyānaṃ tvayāṃ prabho |  
kathaṃ dhyeyaṃ kiṃ viśiṣṭaṃ kiṃ dhyeyādhyeyameva hi ||  
  
vṛttaṃ mūrtisvarūpaṃ vā mekhalāvat svarūpakaṃ |  
kiṃvā rekhāmayaṃ dhyeya kiṃvā vai bhūsvarūpakaṃ ||  
  
viśvarūpaṃ smaredvāpi tatsarvamapi kathyatāṃ ||  
  
īśvara uvāca ||  
  
dhyānaṃ tu trividhaṃ proktaṃ yaṃtramātre maheśvarī |  
ādau virādviśvarūpaṃ dviścacaṇḍasvarūpiṇaṃ ||  
  
yaṃtraṃ saṃbhāvayeddevi sarvatra kathitaṃ tvidaṃ |  
śrīcakrādau mahādevi virādrūpe tu sāmyatā ||  
  
dvitīyaṃ ca kathaṃ dhyeyaṃ tanmevada maheśvari |  
tejaḥ puṃjanibhārekhā sarvacaitanyarūpiṇī ||  
  
sarvadarpaṇa vadbhāvyaṃ svaprakāśaḥ svarūpiṇaṃ |  
caitanyaṃ bhāvayet sarvaṃ viṃdvādiṃ bhūpurāṃtakaṃ ||  
  
mūlatejaḥ prakāśena abhinnaṃ bhāvayet priye |  
rṛtīyaṃ śṛṇu deveśi merurūpaṃ sanātanaṃ ||  
  
uttarottaramuccaṃ syādviṃdvārabhya vibhāvayet |  
viṃdvadho bhāvayeddevi ekaikottarataḥ śive ||  
  
navottara krameṇaiva bhāvayedvā maheśvari |  
kālīvidyā vidhau devi navaratnaṃ svarūpiṇīṃ ||  
  
rekhāṃ saṃbhāvayeddevi meru prastāravacca vā ||  
  
śrīcakraṃ vījasaṃyuktaṃ niṣphalaṃ parameśvari |  
vījahīnaṃ tu yaccakraṃ nirvījaṃ siddhidaṃ na hi ||  
  
sṛṣṭi cakraṃ bhavedādau sthiticakraṃ dvitīyakaṃ |  
bījasaṃlekhanaṃ devi tridhātragaditaṃ mayā ||  
  
vījaṃ vinā tu nirvījaṃ tadyaṃtraṃ siddhidāyakaṃ |  
dalākāraṃ kalau pūjya nānyathā siddhidaṃ śive ||  
  
maṃtracaitanyakaṃ devi yaṃtracaitanyakaṃ tathā |  
gurucaitanyakaṃ devi svasmitritayabhāvanā ||  
  
na tatra dhyānarūpādi tejo yaṃtraṃ vibhāvanā |  
sa prapaṃce tu saṃsāre durāvārāmṛtaḥ śive ||  
  
bhāvanaiva tu saṃproktā bhāvanā siddhidā matā ||  
  
atha sarvasādhāraṇa yaṃtra saṃskāramāha ||  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
cakrabhedo mahādevatvat prasādānmayāśrutaḥ |  
idānīṃ śrotumicchāmi pratiṣṭhākarma nirṇayam ||  
  
śrī śaṃkara uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi jagatkāriṇi kaulinī |  
tasyodyāpana karmāṃgaṃ sarvavarṇa vinirṇayaṃ ||  
  
lagne śubhagrahopete'nukūle guṇaśālini |  
pratiṣṭhāṃ kārayedeṣāmṛkṣatithyādike kṣaṇe ||  
  
snātvā saṃkalpayenmaṃtrī gurorcana mācaret |  
gururmaṃtreṇa vilikhedyaṃtraṃ svarṇaśalākayā ||  
  
paṃcagavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā śivamaṃtreṇa maṃtritaṃ |  
tatra cakraṃ kṣipenmaṃtrī praṇavena samāhitaḥ ||  
  
p. 231b)  
  
tasmāduddhṛtya taccakraṃ sthāpayet svarṇapaṃkaje |  
paṃcāmṛtena dugdhena śītalena jalena ca ||  
  
snāpayeccaṃdanenāpi kastūrī kuṃkumena ca |  
hāṭakaiḥ kalaśairdevi aṣṭabhirvāri pūritaiḥ ||  
  
kaṣāya jalasaṃpannaiḥ snāpayen maṃtramuccaran |  
sa ta uttolya tadyaṃtraṃ sthāpayeddhema pātrake ||  
  
yaṃtrarājāya vidmahe mahāmaṃtrāya dhīmahī |  
uccaredet tadaṃte tu tanno yaṃtraḥ pracodayāt ||  
  
spṛṣṭvā yaṃtraṃ kuśāgreṇa gāyatryā cābhi maṃtrayet |  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ devī devatā bhāvasiddhaye ||  
  
ātmaśuddhiṃ tataḥ kṛtvā ṣaḍaṃgairdevatāṃ yajet |  
tatrā vāhya yajeddevīṃ jīvanyāsaṃ ca kārayet ||  
  
upacāraiḥ ṣoḍaśabhirmahāmudrādibhiḥ sadā |  
phalatāṃbūla naivedyairdevīṃ tatra samarcayet ||  
  
yadṛ sūtrādikaṃ dadyādvastrālaṃkārameva ca |  
mukuraṃ cāmaraṃ ghaṇṭhāṃ yathāyogyaṃ maheśvarī ||  
  
sarva me tat prayatnena dadyādātma hiterataḥ |  
trirātraṃ pūjayeddevīṃ trisaṃdhyaṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ ||  
  
tato jape sahasraṃ tu sakalepsina siddhaye |  
balidānaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā praṇamedyaṃtra rājakaṃ ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ hutvā saṃpātājyaṃ viniḥkṣipet |  
homakarmaṇya śaktiścedvimuṇaṃ japamācaret ||  
  
dhenumekāṃ samādāya svarṇa śṛṃgādyalaṃkṛtam |  
gurave dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāt tato devyā visarjanaṃ ||  
  
atha kaulikādevi śeṣamāha ||  
  
devyuvāca ||  
  
deveśa śrotumicchāmi rahasyātirahasyakaṃ |  
vāmināṃ caiva kaulānāṃ yaṃtrasaṃskāra karma ca ||  
  
śiva uvāca ||  
  
athocyate mahāyaṃtra saṃskāraḥ sarvasiddhidaḥ |  
śubhehni snānamācarya śubhe lagne śubhe kṣaṇe ||  
  
kṛta nityakriyā maṃtrī prāṅmukho vāyudaṅmukhaḥ ||  
  
pūrvokta dhādu dravyaiśca suṃdaraṃ sumanoharaṃ |  
surekhe śubhadaṃ yaṃtraṃ lekhayitvā vidhānataḥ ||  
  
pratiṣṭhāṃ ca tataḥ kuryād yathā śāstra pramāṇataḥ |  
śubhe lagne puṇyakāle śailādi vihitasthale ||  
  
maṃtrī kalpānusāre tu pūrvedyuradhivāsayet |  
sāyaṃ saṃkalpavidhivadghaṃṭasthāpana pūrvakaṃ ||  
  
p. 232a)  
  
gaṇeśādīn samabhyarcya dikpālān paripūrayet |  
madyaṃ māṃsaṃ tathā matsyaṃ mudrāṃ maithunameva ca ||  
  
yaṃtra saṃskāra karmādau dravya me tanmayeritaṃ |  
yathāśaktyopacārādyaiḥ pūjayen mūladevatām ||  
  
sugaṃdha tailagaṃdhādyairdravyaistamadhi vāsayet |  
caṃdretyādi ca maṃtreṇa japaghoṣa purassaraṃ ||  
  
ityadhi vāsitaṃ kṛtvā saṃyatotiti teṃdriyaḥ |  
prātarnityaṃ vidhāyādau tato yāgasthale viśet ||  
  
patākādhvajasaṃkīrṇe divyamaṇḍalamaṇḍite |  
vitāna cāmaracchatra puṣpamālā virājite ||  
  
maṃgalāṃkura patrādyaiḥ kalaśaiḥ paribhūṣite |  
maṇḍalaṃ sarvato bhadre rekhā sāhasrasaṃyutaṃ ||  
  
sāmānya bhadraṃ vā devi vedyāśco parito likhet ||  
  
athavā dakṣiṇe vāme vakṣye vāruṇamaṇḍalaṃ |  
catusraṃ catuḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ koṣṭhaṃ vidyāṃ niveśayet ||  
  
aṃtyoyāṃtima paṃktyostu dikṣu koṣṭāni mārjayet |  
madhyastha caturakṣīṇi tadvārākhyāni pūrvavat ||  
  
pītaḥ śyāmaḥ śveta haridrajobhiḥ paripūrayet |  
koṇakoṣṭhaṃ vihāyaika paṃcāśatyādasaṃgitāḥ ||  
  
pīṭhasya pāṇḍuro raktaḥpīta kṛṣṇaiḥ prapūrayet |  
āgne pītaḥ koṇakoṣṭānyā raktaharitāsitaiḥ ||  
  
śvetavarṇena catvāri madhye vṛttāni kārayet |  
pūrayedatha tasyorddhaṃ vitānaṃ vaṃdhayed yathā ||  
  
ṣaṭtriṃśadaṃśavyāsārddhaṃ vṛttamādyaṃ tu pītataḥ |  
tat pītaṃ karṇikākāraṃ sitarekhā vṛtaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
dvitīyaṃ dviguṇa vyāsa rūpakeśara saṃyutaṃ |  
pītaraktaḥ śvetavarṇa mūlamadhyāgrakeśaraṃ ||  
  
dvisaptatyaṃśikāśvetāṃ tasyāgre kuru rekhikāṃ |  
tṛtīyaṃ tu tṛtīyāṃśe tulya vyāsaṃ tu vartulaṃ ||  
  
śvetamaṣṭadalaṃ tatra raktāṃ cāṃtaddalāṃtaraṃ |  
śvetaṃ vahiḥ kṛṣṇavarṇā raktāṃgaṃ taddalāṃtare ||  
  
śvetaṃ vahiḥ kṛṣṇā prāgvadrekhāṃ sitāṃ kuru |  
tadvahirvṛtta saṃlagnān ṣoḍaśārān prakalpayet ||  
  
śyāmapītāruṇaḥ śvetai tadaṃtastudya vā kṛtī |  
śitā pītāruṇaḥ śyāmaharitāḥ paṃcarekhikāḥ ||  
  
kāryāḥ su rucirāḥ paṃcasyāṃtarevaṃ prapūrayet |  
vajraśaktirdaṇḍakhaḍgapāśa dhvajagadyaṃ likhet ||  
  
p. 232b)  
  
pūrvatastu tathaiśānyāṃ śūlacakrāṃvujānvitaṃ |  
vāma dakṣiṇayoretanmaṇḍalaṃ vāruṇāhvayaṃ ||  
  
prāṅmukho vāgyato bhūtvā saṃkalpyābhīṣṭasiddhaye |  
paṃcaśuddhiṃ samācarya kurvannakṣata saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
saṃsthāpya maṃḍale tatra yajedādhāraśaktitaḥ |  
pīṭhamaṃtraṃ samāstīrya sthāpayet kalaśaṃ budhaḥ ||  
  
dīkṣākramokta vidhinābhiṣeka kalaśaṃ tathā |  
paṃcagavyaṃ tataḥ kuryācchivamaṃtra vivodhitaṃ ||  
  
tena su snāpayenmaṃtrī yaṃtraṃ ca praṇavaṃ japan |  
paṃcāmṛtena haviṣā dadhnā ca payasā kramāt ||  
  
tata udvartanaṃ kṛtvā jelana sthāpayedapi |  
paṃcagavyaṃ samānīya taṃtra yaṃtraṃ samāhitaḥ ||  
  
japan kṣipet suvarṇādau vedamūla purassaraṃ |  
tata uddhṛtya svarṇādi pātraṃ saṃsthāpya maṃtravit ||  
  
paṃcāmṛtena tīrtheṇa śītalena jalena ca |  
sahasraśīrṣāmaṃtreṇa mūlamaṃtra puraḥsaraṃ ||  
  
susnāpyayāvamānena karpūrāgurunīrataḥ |  
sarvauṣadhi jalairgaṃdhairjalairyatnena mārjanaṃ ||  
  
tataḥ śuddhadukūlena jalamutsārya sādhakaḥ |  
paridhāyadukūledve svarṇanirmitadolayā ||  
  
maṇḍaletaṃ samānīya nṛtyagītairjayasvanaiḥ |  
kuṃkumādyairvilipyātha pūjyaḥ sarvopacārakaiḥ ||  
  
pīṭhapūjāṃ tataḥ kuryāt svasvakalpokta mānataḥ |  
kuśaiḥ kulīnairvā devi śatamaṣṭottaraṃ japet ||  
  
pūrvoktāṃ yaṃtragāyatrīṃ japtvā devatvamāpnuyāt |  
atheṣṭaṃ devatāṃ dhyātvā mudrayā vāhayet tataḥ ||  
  
jīvanyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryāt pūjayediṣṭadevatāṃ |  
nṛtyagītaiśca vāditraiḥ paṃcaghoṣa puraḥ saraṃ ||  
  
tato japediṣṭa maṃtramaṣṭottara sahasrakaṃ |  
kuṇḍe vā sthaṃḍile maṃtrī haviṣā saṃskṛte nale ||  
  
yathāvidhi vidhānena śruco homaṃ samācaret |  
grāsa pramāṇaṃ ca caruṃ mūlenākṛṣya maṃtravit ||  
  
ghṛtaśruvaṃ tato datvā juhuyādagni saṃmukhe |  
paṃcaviṃśati tatvaiśca tatvena tarpaṇaṃ caret ||  
  
p. 233a)  
  
iṃdrādi dikpatibhyaśca dadyāt pūrvoditaṃ valiṃ |  
tata āvṛtti devebhyo ghṛtenāhuti mācaret ||  
  
tadaṃte devi maṃtreṇa hunedaṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ |  
mātṛkā yuktaṃ maṃtraṃ tu japa jaya jayasvanaiḥ ||  
  
gatvā homa samīpe tu datvā pūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ |  
toṣayet svarṇavastrādyaiḥ pradadyād dakṣiṇāmapi ||  
  
kṣakāraiḥ paṃcabhirdevī vīrapūjāṃ samācaret |  
śaktiṃ kumārikāṃ vālā pūjayet paṃcapaṃcakaṃ ||  
  
kuryād daśāṣṭakaṃ vāpi kuladravyaiḥ samastakaiḥ |  
trailokyanātho bhavati yaṃtrapūjanayogataḥ ||  
  
bhūtaśuddhyādikaṃ kṛtvā kalpoktanyā samācaret |  
niśāyāṃ śaktipūjāṃ ca dūtīyāgaṃ ca kaulikā ||  
  
makāraiḥ paṃcabhiryuktaṃ careyurvāminorcanaṃ |  
evaṃ dinatrayaṃ kṛtvā tato nityakramaṃ bhajet ||  
  
sṛṣṭisthiti layatvena suṃdarī yaṃtrapūjanaṃ |  
sṛṣṭisaṃhāramārgeṇa kālikā yaṃtrapūjanaṃ ||  
  
sṛṣṭisaṃhāramārgeṇa tārācchinnā ca pītabhāḥ |  
evaṃ devī pratiṣṭhāyāṃ kramaḥ sānnidhyakārakaḥ ||  
  
strī śūdrāṇāṃ vāmināṃ ca kaulikānāmayaṃ vidhiḥ |  
vidhiyuktaṃ prakartavyaṃ vidhihīnaṃ na kārayet ||  
  
vidhihīnasya vighnāni yāni te kathayāmyahaṃ |  
kalahodvegadvaṃdvaśca vyādhiśūlaṃ jvaraṃ tathā ||  
  
rājopadravahāniśca dravyanāśaṃ rujaṃ tathā |  
cihlākākāśca kākulyo śivo phetkāradāruṇā ||  
  
kapotāśca gṛhe tasya āruhaṃti viśaṃti ca |  
vighnaṃ kurvaṃti vai tasya vidhānaṃ gupta saṃsthitā ||  
  
chidraṃti tasya yoginyo nānāvighnaiḥ pravādhyate |  
sarpavṛścikalūtāśca kīṭāścaiva tu dāruṇāḥ ||  
  
daśaṃti ca mahā ugrā preritāste marīcibhiḥ |  
vṛṣaiścāśvairgajendraiśca meghairvajrāsanistathā ||  
  
upadravaṃti duṣṭāśca jvaro bhūtādayastathā |  
lūtāgardabhāpasmārā abhibhavaṃti nānyathā ||  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau   
yaṃtrakarmaṇādipūrvakapratiṣṭhāṃtanirṇayanāmonatriṃśattamaḥ prakāśaḥ || 29   
||    
  
atha mālāṃ pravakṣyāmi dvividhā sā sthirā calā |  
sthirā tu sthiracittānāṃ caṃcalā calacetasāṃ ||  
  
p. 233b)  
  
tat sādhanaṃ tridhā proktaṃ prathamā varṇamālike |  
dvitīyā japamālā syāt tṛtīyāṃguḷimālikā ||  
  
athācalamālāmāha ||  
  
akārādi kṣakārāṃtairviṃdumanmātṛkākṣaraiḥ |  
anuloma vilomasthai kḷptayā varṇamālayā ||  
  
ekaikaṃ varṇamuccārya varṇanāṃtaritaṃ manuṃ |  
sudhīrevaṃ lakārāṃtaṃ tata āṃtaṃ samānayet ||  
  
kṣakāraṃ merurūpaṃ tu laṃghayenna kadācanā |  
sakṛdevoccaretkṣantu tadaṃte noccarenmanuḥ ||  
  
merūhīnā ca yā mālā merūhīnā ca yā bhavet |  
aśuddhā ca bhavedatra sā mālāniḥ phalā bhavet ||  
  
citriṇī vistaṃtvābhā brahmanāḍīgatā tu yā |  
tayā saṃgrathitā dhyeyāṃ sarvakāma phalapradā ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśate japtetvādau klīvaṃ samuccaret ||  
  
ṛ ṝ ḷ ḹ varṇe catuṣṭāyaṃ klīvaṃ pracakṣate |  
varṇānāmaṣṭamaṃ vāpi kāmyabheda krameṇa tu ||  
  
a ka ca ṭa ta pa yadvā ityevaṃ cāṣṭavargakaṃ ||  
  
kiṃ vā mṛta trayaṃ procya praṇavāṃte ca mātṛkā |  
anuloma vilomātu tvaṣṭottaraśatī bhavet ||  
  
māyā vākkāma śrīyogāt mātṛkā varṇa yogataḥ |  
anuloma vilomābhyāṃ tvaṣṭottaraśatī bhavet ||  
  
trayaṃ gurau trayaṃ devi gāṇape parikīrtitaṃ |  
nyūnātirikte dvitayaṃ śeṣamiṣṭāyayo jayet ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśatīmālā sarvakāryārthasiddhidā |  
nātṛkā varṇarūpatvā prokteyaṃ sthiramālikā ||  
  
akārādi kṣakārāṃtaṃ saiveyaṃ tvakṣamālikā |  
mālā paṃcāśakā proktā sūtraśakti śivātmikā ||  
  
grathanaṃ kuṇḍalī śaktirlaghāṃte merusaṃsthitaḥ |  
etadguptataraṃ kuryādakṣa sūtra śivātmakam ||  
  
prakaṭaṃ naiva kartavyaṃ na meruṃ laṃghayet kvacit |  
suptakīlita saṃmudrāchinnavyā kīrṇayogataḥ ||  
  
dhanairvairī vīryahīna kāṇakhaṃjādayopi ye |  
tepi siddhā bhavaṃtyeva sthiramālā prabhāvataḥ ||  
  
athāsyā dhyānam ||  
  
aṃtarvidruma bhāsamānaṃ bhujagī suptotha varṇojvalāṃ ārohāmavarohikāṃ   
śatamayīṃ vargāṣṭakāṣṭottarāṃ |  
sākṣād brahmamayīṃ kṣameruśikharāṃ śrīmātṛkākṣā valīṃ vidyāṃ   
naumisamastamaṃtrajananīṃ jñānaika dīpāṃkurāṃ ||  
  
p. 234a)  
  
idānīṃ devatābhede mālābhede vadāmyahaṃ |  
daṃtākṣamālā śrīkālyāṃ tārāyāṃ naraśaṃkhajā ||  
  
chinnamastāvidhau śastā narāsthimālikā śubhā |  
raktacaṃdana vījānāṃ mālāsyāt tripurā vidhau ||  
  
svayaṃbhūmālikādevi bhairavyāṃ bālikā vidhau |  
bhujāmālā tu mātaṃgyāṃ dhūmrāyāṃ kharadaṃtajā ||  
  
haridrākṣā tu brahmāstre kapālākṣā tu māvidhau |  
vālāyāṃ bhuvaneśvaryā sphāṭikī parikīrtitā ||  
  
śvetaguṃjā siddhividyā vidhau proktā maheśvari |  
śaṃkhamālā vaiṣṇave ca iṃdrākṣā śaktamātrake ||  
  
bhadrākṣā śarabhe proktā gaṇeśa gajadaṃtajā |  
tripuṭāyāṃ putrajīvī goviṃde tulasī matā ||  
  
ratnasvarṇairaupyamayī tathā tāmramayī śive |  
auḍuṃvaro vījamayī vaṭavījamayī tathā ||  
  
pūgī phalamayī mālājātī phalamayī tathā |  
madhumatyākarṣaṇārthe vīravidyā vidhāvapi ||  
  
pūrvāmnāya sphāṭikajairdakṣiṇe rudranetrajaiḥ |  
pravālairmauktikairdevi paścimāmnāya daivataiḥ ||  
  
uttarāmnāya devānāṃ mahāśaṃkhākhyamālikā |  
ūrddhvāmnāya svayaṃ bhūtthā pātāle ratnasaṃbhavā ||  
  
pravālaiḥ sūryamaṃtre ca mauktikaiḥ śaktimātrake |  
śivaśaktimayīmālā rudrākṣa sphaṭikairyutā ||  
  
rudrākṣa svarṇasaṃyuktā mālā hariharātmikā |  
rudrākṣaraupya saṃyuktā mālāvidhi śivātmikā ||  
  
sarvamaṃtreṣu rudrākṣā śaktimaṃtredivā na hi ||  
  
tathā ca ||  
  
śivaśakti viyogatvānna rudrākṣairdivā japaḥ |  
viyoge pūjitā kālī sahasā na prasīdati ||  
  
rudrākṣaiḥ śaktimaṃtrastu divā yo japati priye |  
sa durgati mavāpnoti japastasya nirarthakaḥ ||  
  
iti śāpa purādattestatkathā kathyate śṛṇu |  
kadācit samaye devi dakṣa yajñaḥ parāyaṇaḥ ||  
  
sakalā ṛṣayo devāyakṣa vidyā dharoragāḥ |  
putrī jāmātṛ saṃbaṃdhādgṛheṇākāritā ca tā ||  
  
p. 234b)  
  
mahādevaḥ satyavatī tena nā kāritā kratau |  
satī ca bhartṛ nikaṭe uktā tatra pragamyate ||  
  
śiva uvāca ||  
  
mamaivā kāraṇaṃ tena na kṛtaṃ prāṇavallabhe |  
tava lajjā kathaṃ nāsti tvayā tatra pragamyate ||  
  
priyo devaḥ priyaḥ prāṇāpriya eva hi bhūṣaṇaṃ |  
māṃ vihāya kathaṃ devi tvayā tatra pragamyate ||  
  
pātivratyamidaṃ kvāsti pratiyogāṃ vihīnataḥ |  
tathāpi tava vāṃchā cet śīghraṃ gaṃtuṃ kṛpāṃ kuru ||  
  
bharturājñāṃ gṛhītvā ca prasthitaṃ yāgamaṇḍape |  
tat siṃhena kṣaṇānnītaṃ brahmaṇo yāgamaṇḍapaṃ ||  
  
tena nādaritā kanyā duḥkhinā dīnamānasā |  
adhomukhī sthitā tatra pārvatī rūpaśā vahan ||  
  
sarve devāścātra saṃti madbhartā nātra dṛśyate |  
mahadduḥkhaṃ mama kṛta me tāvad hṛdayasthitaṃ ||  
  
etasminnaṃtaredevi dakṣaprajāpatiḥ svayaṃ |  
śivaniṃdo paro bhūtvā punarnindārtha mudyataḥ ||  
  
anācārita rūpo bhūdviṣṇunā vāritopi ca |  
muhurnniṃdā paro bhūtvā bhaṃgī vṛṣa bhavāhanaḥ ||  
  
śmaśānavāsī māṃsāśī nagno dhīrataro virāṭ |  
kapālī ca triśūlī ca muṇḍamālā vibhūṣitaḥ ||  
  
bhasmoddhūlita sarvāṃgo vyāghrājina samāsthitaḥ |  
laṃpaṭo lolupaśceti vahuniṃdā paro bhavet ||  
  
duḥkhitā niṃdayā tvaṃ hi maṇḍapādvahirāgatā |  
dūre netrāṃtare gatvā vahni kuṇḍaṃ vidhāya ca ||  
  
satītyaktvā tatra dehaṃ vahni rūpātvatāṃgatā |  
śivohaṃ krodharūpeṇa jvālā bhāsvara maṇḍalaḥ ||  
  
sat krodhena maheśāni bhasmībhūtaṃ jagattrayaṃ |  
majvālayā samutpanno vīrabhadro mahāvibhuḥ ||  
  
koṭikālāṃta dahano duḥsahaḥ sarvajaṃtuṣu |  
dakṣaprajāpateryajñadhvaṃ sā nārthaṃ samudyataḥ ||  
  
triśūla hastī krūraśca yajñadhva.ṃ sa parāyaṇaḥ |  
śavaddhapāṃ śivāṃ devi gṛhītvā skaṃdhagocarām ||  
  
rodanaṃ cakratustasmāt patitāścā śrūviṃdavaḥ |  
tatrā śrūvindavo jātāḥ mahārudrākṣa vṛkṣakāḥ ||  
  
sthāvaratva manuprāpya martyānugrahakāraṇāt |  
phalaṃti sarvakālaṃ hi avicchinna phalapradā ||  
  
śrūyate tena rudrākṣaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaṃ |  
netra trayā samutpannā dhanāśrīkaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
p. 235a)  
  
vāmanetrāt samutpanno moraṃgīyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |  
dhanāśrī koṣṭhadaśa ca pārvatīya manurbhavet ||  
  
ekaviṃśati vaktrāṃtaṃ malākī parikīrtitaḥ |  
evaṃ vaktrāṇi jātāni rudrarodana saṃbhavāt ||  
  
sphuṭavaktre pārvatīye pratiṣṭhā sphuṭameva ca |  
dhanāśrīkeśarākāṃti rekhāyāṃ jāyate prabho ||  
  
malākiye vahnināśastat kālaṃ jalamadhyataḥ |  
jalopari samāyātī sa malākīrtitaḥ ||  
  
tena yat kriyate karma tadanaṃtaphalaṃ bhavet |  
anyamaṃtre siddhirūpā śaktimaṃtre divā na hi ||  
  
iti kāraṇato devi rātrāveva japasmṛtaḥ |  
rātriḥ saṃyogarūpāsyād vidyātvaṃ ca maheśvari ||  
  
vidyogarūpo deveśo maṃtraśāstrai prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
atha rudrākṣa mahātmyaṃ varṇayāmi samāsataḥ |  
rudrākṣa mokṣa kāmastu rudrākṣaṃ śreyasādhanaṃ ||  
  
rudrākṣaṃ harate duḥkhaṃ rudrākṣaṃ pāpanāśanaṃ |  
sarvapāpa kṣayakaraṃ paṭhato śṛṇvatāmapi ||  
  
abhakto vāpi bhakto vā nīco nīcaṃtaropi vā |  
rudrākṣaṃ dhārayedyastu mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ||  
  
rudrākṣadhāraṇaṃ puṇyaṃ kena vā sadṛśaṃ bhavet |  
mahāvratamidaṃ prāhurmunayastatvadarśinaḥ ||  
  
sahasraṃ dhārayedyastu rudrākṣāṇāṃ dhṛtavrataḥ |  
tannamaṃti surāḥ sarve yathā rudrastathaiva saḥ ||  
  
śiromālā tu ṣaṭtriṃśadvātriṃśat kaṃṭhamālikāḥ |  
kūrpare ṣoḍaśa prokto dvātriṃśan maṇibaṃdhayoḥ ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśatairyuktamupavītaṃ vidhīyate |  
tadūrddha suraso mālā śikhāyāmeka ucyate ||  
  
karṇayoścāpi ṣaṭsaṃkhyādhāraṇa kramamīritaṃ |  
saṃkhyā hīnaṃ na kartavyaṃ adhikaṃ naiva duṣpati ||  
  
rudrākṣāṃ dhārayennaiva dehāṃte sa śivo bhavet |  
vahulaṃ labhate puṇyaṃ bhāgyavāniha jāyate ||  
  
snāne dāne jape home vaiśvadeve surārcane |  
prāyaścitte tathā srāddhe dīkṣākāle viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
rudrādhārī bhūtvā ca yat kiṃcit karma vaidikaṃ |  
yo vipraḥ satataṃ kuryāt tatkarma sa phalaṃ bhavet ||  
  
khādanmāṃsaṃ pivanmadyaṃ saṃgacchannaṃtya jātiṣu |  
sadyo bhavati pūtātmā rudrākṣaṃ mūrddhni dhārayan ||  
  
devāṃ pūṣṇaṃti ye devāpaśavaste tu vaidikāḥ |  
tāt pātayaṃti ye kaule teṣāṃ śāstā svayaṃ śivaḥ ||  
  
teṣāṃ saṃrakṣaṇārthāya nānyo rudrākṣato bhuvi |  
rudrākṣāḥ sarvadevānāṃ maṃtrasiddhi vidhāyakāḥ ||  
  
rudrākṣaṃ kaṇṭhamāśritya śunako mriyate yadi |  
sopi rudratvamāpnoti kiṃ punarmānuṣādayaḥ ||  
  
p. 235b)  
  
ucchiṣṭho vā vikarmastho yukto vā sarvapātakaiḥ |  
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo naro rudrākṣa dhāraṇāt ||  
  
rudrākṣamālikāṃ kaṃṭhe dhārayan bhaktivarjitaḥ |  
pāpakarmāpi yo nityaṃ rudraloke mahīyate ||  
  
yo dhārayati rudrātmā rudravatsopi pūjyate |  
muktā pravāla sphaṭikaraupya vaiḍūrya kāṃcanaiḥ ||  
  
samastāddhārayedyastu rudrākṣāt sa śivo bhavet |  
kevalān vāpi rudrākṣān yadyālasyā vibhartayaḥ ||  
  
tanna spṛśaṃti pāpānitamāṃsīva vibhāvasuṃ |  
rudrākṣamālayā japto maṃtronaṃta phalapradaḥ ||  
  
arudro japataḥ puṃsāṃ tāvanmātrā phalapradaḥ |
