yasyāṃge nāsti rudrākṣa ekopi vahu puṇyadaḥ ||  
  
tasya janmanirarthaṃ syān tripuṇḍraṃ rahitasya ca |  
rudrākṣaṃ mastake dhṛtvā śiraḥ snānaṃ karoti yaḥ ||  
  
gaṃgāsnānaphalaṃ tasya jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ |  
rudrākṣaṃ pūjyate yastu vinātoyābhi ṣecanaṃ ||  
  
yatphalaṃ liṃgapūjāyāṃ tadavāpnoti niścitaṃ |  
bhaktyā saṃpūjito nityaṃ rudrākṣaḥ śaṃkarātmakaḥ ||  
  
daridraṃ cāpi kurute rājarāja samaśriyaṃ |  
gaṃgāsnāna samaṃ puṇyaṃ darśanāt phalamāpnuyāt ||  
  
lakṣakoṭi sahasrāṇi lakṣakoṭi śatāni ca |  
rudrākṣadhāraṇādvāpi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ||  
  
ekavaktraḥ śivastasya mālayā japato haret |  
brahmahatyādi pāpāni tathā rājyādikeṣṭadaḥ ||  
  
ekavaktra samāyuktaṃ rudrākṣaṃ yasya tiṣṭhati |  
sa sāmrājya mavāpnoti satyaṃjānāṃ hi pārvati ||  
  
umāśaṃkaranāmākhyodvimukhoyaṃ vyapohati |  
gohatyādika pāpāni grāhasthyādika saukhyadaḥ ||  
  
trimukhastvagni rūpasyāt strīhatyādika pāpahā |  
dharmārthakāmā siddhyaṃti dhāraṇāt tajjapādipe ||  
  
caturmukho bhaved brahmā guruhatyādināśakaḥ |  
sphuraṃti sakalā vidyā vāksiddhiścāpi jāyate ||  
  
paṃcavaktra śivaḥ sākṣāt kālāgnirnāmanāmataḥ |  
śaivagāṇeśa śāktānāṃ drutaṃ siddhistu tajjapāt ||  
  
agamya gamanaṃ caiva abhakṣasyāpi bhakṣaṇaṃ |  
mucyate pātakaṃ ghoraṃ paṃcavaktrasya dhāraṇāt ||  
  
kārtikeyaistu ṣaḍvaktrai skhalate vrata pāpahā |  
bhrūṇahatyādibhiḥ pāpairmucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
p. 236a)  
  
vidhinā dakṣiṇe vāhau dhāraṇāt samare jayaḥ |  
saptavaktro mahānāgonaṃto nāmātha tajjapāt ||  
  
anaṃtāḥ siddhayassarya vibhīṣeścana jāyate |  
suvarṇaiḥ subhagaścaiva daridropīśvaro bhavet ||  
  
gurutalpādibhiḥ pāpairhatvā vahutarāṇyapi |  
mucyate nātra saṃdeho rudrākṣasya tu dhāraṇāt ||  
  
aṣṭavaktro gaṇeśasyāt sarvavighna nivārakaḥ |  
naśyaṃti tajjapāt sarve kāmakrodhādi śatravaḥ ||  
  
pṛṣṭhodarakareṇāpi saṃspṛśedvā gurustriyaṃ |  
evamādīni pāpāni ati pāpāni sarvaśaḥ ||  
  
vighnāstasya naśyaṃti mukto yāṃṭi parāṃ gatiṃ |  
jīvedvarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ mṛtyurnāsti sa śūlabhṛt ||  
  
guṇāḥ hyeteṣu sarveṣu aṣṭavaktrasya dhāraṇāt |  
nava vaktraṃ bhairavaḥ syāt kapilaṃ muktidaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
japo deva prasīdaṃti vāmamārgastha devatāḥ |  
dhārayed vāmahaste ca mamatulya varo bhavet ||  
  
lakṣakoṭi sahasrāṇi brahmahatyāṃ karoti yaḥ |  
tatsarvaṃ dahate kṣipraṃ navavaktrasya dhāraṇāt ||  
  
daśavaktro * * * * * * (?) devo janārdana |  
sahasraiva piśācādyā vetālā brahmarākṣasāḥ ||  
  
ḍākinyo mātaraścaiva tathā vai pretanāyakāḥ |  
pannagāśca vinaśyaṃti daśavaktrasya dhāraṇāt ||  
  
vaktraikādaśa rudrākṣaṃ rudraikādaśakaṃ smṛtaṃ |  
śikhāyāṃ dhārayannityaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ||  
  
aśvamedha sahasrāṇi vājapeya śatāni ca |  
gavāṃ śata sahasrasya samyagdattasya yatphalaṃ ||  
  
sa tu tatphalamāpnoti rudraikādaśadhāraṇāt |  
vaktra dvādaśarudrākṣaṃ bhāskaraṃ dvādaśātmakaṃ ||  
  
dhārayet kaṇṭhadeśe ca japedvāpi samāhitaḥ |  
tejasvī ca pratāpi ca āditya sadṛśo bhavet ||  
  
na pīḍyate mahāghorairādityādi navagrahaiḥ |  
durbhagāḥ subhagāyāṃti rogīrogāt pramucyate ||  
  
gomedha narabhedhādi sarvakratu phalapradaḥ |  
hastyaśva mṛgamārjārān mahiṣān śūkarādikān ||  
  
śvānaṃ śṛṃgālaṣṭakalān vadhvā vahutarāṇyapi |  
mucyate nātra saṃdeho dvādaśāditya dhāraṇāt ||  
  
p. 236b)  
  
vaktraṃ trayodaśaṃ vatsa labdhvā tu yadi dhāraṇāt |  
pūjyate satataṃ devaiḥ prāpyate puṇyamuttamaṃ ||  
  
sarvaṃ phalamavāpnoti saubhāgyaṃ cottamaṃ bhavet |  
rasaṃ rasāyaṇaṃ khaḍgaṃ dhāturvādamanekadhā ||  
  
kāmadhenuśca rudrākṣaṃ icchāsiddhimavāpnuāt |  
siddhyate tena rudrākṣaṃ bhāgyahīnopi yadyasau ||  
  
mātā pitā tathā baṃdhu gurvādapī dahanyate ||  
  
mucyate pātakairghoraistathānyai rūpapātakaiḥ |  
puṇyaiścaturdaśaṃ vaktraṃ rudrākṣaṃ yadi labhyate ||  
  
dhārayet tatprayatnena śikhā yajñopavītake |  
cāmuṇḍā tu svayaṃ vatsa śaktipiṇḍaṃ śivasya tu ||  
  
arcayitvā dhṛte kaṃthe na punarjāyatehyasau |  
siddhyate nātra saṃdeho satyaṃ satyaṃ ca ṣaṇmukhaḥ ||  
  
vicaren martyaloke sau prāsādaśca yathā tathā |  
yogī ca dvicaret sarva sarveṣu ca priyo bhavet ||  
  
paśuśca puruṣo cāpi nagaraṃ cā pavitrakaṃ |  
rasaṃ rasāyaṇaṃ caiva jarāmṛtyu vināśanaṃ ||  
  
labhedvetālakhaḍgaṃ ca aṣṭasiddhiṃ mahādbhutaṃ |  
na puṇya na ca pāpaṃ ca navyādhirna prapīḍitaṃ ||  
  
jīvedvarṣa sahasrāṇi mṛte bhavati śūladhṛk |  
aprārthitāllabhedarthānna cārthasya kṣayo bhavet ||  
  
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo jñānī yajña bhavet phalaṃ |  
caturdaśamukhairjaptaṃ tadānaṃtyāya jāyate ||  
  
pūjyate deva manujairakṣayā labhate gatiṃ |  
yathā hariśca deveṣu sa dehaḥ kṣemamartakaḥ ||  
  
raviryathā grahāṇāṃ ca munīnāṃ kaśyapo yathā |  
nadīnāṃ jāhnavī yadvattīrtheṣu ca yathodadhiḥ ||  
  
āyudhānāṃ dhanuryadvaddhutānāṃ ca caturdaśī |  
kumārāṇīṃstathā skaṃdo devānāṃ ca maheśvaraḥ ||  
  
devīnāṃ ca umādevī airāvata gajeśvaraḥ |  
dhenūnāṃ ca sunaṃdā vai aśvānāṃ haritastathā ||  
  
evaṃ gaṇyeṣu sarveṣu rudrākṣastu viśiṣyate ||  
  
ṣaṇmukhaṃ śirasādhāryaṃ trimukaṃ kaṃthake smṛtaṃ |  
paṃcavaktraṃ mataṃ vāhau caturvaktraṃ kare śubhaṃ ||  
  
dvimukhaṃ dhārayet kaṭhyāṃ ekavaktraṃ ca mūrddhani |  
navavaktraṃ ca rudrākṣaṃ dhārayed vāmavāhunā ||  
  
carurdaśamukhaṃ caiva śikhāyāṃ dhārayedbudhaḥ |  
rudrākṣāṃ dhārayed vipra saṃdhyādiṣu ca karmasu ||  
  
p. 237a)  
  
tatsarvaṃ saphalaṃ proktaṃ lakṣakoṭiguṇaṃ dhruvaṃ |  
liṃgadarśanavat puṇyaṃ bhaved rudrākṣadarśanāt ||  
  
tannu koṭiśataṃ puṇyaṃ labhate dhāraṇānnaraḥ |  
śirasā dhārayet koṭiḥ karṇayordaśakoṭayaḥ ||  
  
gale vadhvā koṭiśataṃ mūrddhni koṭi sahasrakaṃ |  
ayutaṃ copavītaṃ ca lakṣakoṭi bhujadvaye ||  
  
aprameyaṃ phalaṃ haste sa rudrākṣadharo bhavet ||  
  
niśchidrāścaiva pakvaśca rudrākṣā dhāraṇe smṛtā |  
parīkṣā tatra kartavyo rudrākṣasya tu ṣaṇmukha ||  
  
supakvaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ caiva suvedhaṃ susamaṃ smṛtaṃ |  
niśchidraṃ nirvraṇaṃ vai kalpokta phalastayakaṃ ||  
  
pāṇḍaraṃ cādhamaṃ jñeyaṃ madhyamaṃ kṛṣṇavarṇakaṃ |  
uttamaṃ raktavarṇaṃ tu sarvasiddhi pradāyakaṃ ||  
  
vaktraṃ ca khaṇḍitaṃ caiva chidraścaiva viśeṣataḥ |  
kiṃcit kiṃcid bhaved vatsa phalaṃ doṣeṇa hanyate ||  
  
phalaṃ pratyeka meteṣāṃ madhunātvaṃ niśāmaya |  
daṃtākhyamālayādevi ṣaṣṭiḥ siddhīśvaro bhavet ||  
  
akasmādīpsitā siddhirmahāśaṃkhākhyamālayā |  
racitā cāsthi maṇibhiḥ sarvaśatru vināśinī ||  
  
raktacaṃdanajā mālābhoga mokṣapradāmatā |  
svayaṃbhū kusumairdevi sarvavidyeśvaro bhavet ||  
  
guṃjayā mohanaṃ proktaṃ kharadaṃtai ripukṣayaḥ |  
hāridryāstaṃbhanaṃ sastaṃ padmākṣaiḥ puṣṭiruttamā ||  
  
vāksiddhiḥ sphāṭikīyā syāt sarvakāmaphalapradā |  
dhanārthaṃ śvetaguṃjāyā kīrtiḥ śrīśaṃkhajāmatā ||  
  
indrākṣai rājyadā proktā bhadrākṣairbhogasaṃpadāṃ |  
gajadaṃtasya sarvārthaṃ siddhirbhavati sarvadā ||  
  
dhanadhānyasutaḥ prāptirbhavedvai putrajīvakaiḥ |  
tulasyā mokṣamāpnoti ratnairbhogāśca yacchati ||  
  
sauvarṇe rājyalakṣmīḥ syā sarva saukhye tu raupyajā |  
aṃgulī parvabhiḥ sarvasiddhirājyaṃ sa viṃdati ||  
  
auduṃvarairbhūtanāśoplakṣairdāridranāśane |  
vaṭavījairyakṣiṇī syāt kapardībhirmahodayaḥ ||  
  
pravālairvaśyasiddhiḥ syānmauktikāmauktidāmapi |  
kilviṣaugha kṣayakarī kuśagraṃthi vinirmitā ||  
  
vidrumotthāvaśyakarā mohane tāmrajāmatā |  
kucaṃdanaiḥ samākarṣād vidveṣoriṣṭamālayā ||  
  
p. 237b)  
  
maricaihlāsine mālāpivumardairvināśanaṃ |  
arkasyoccāṭanaścaiva māraṇe cāyasīmatā ||  
  
jvalahartrī tu lākṣāyāḥ khaḍgasya pitṛ tṛpti kṛt |  
viṣottāre caṃdanotthāśāṃti kṛcchre tathāṣṭajā ||  
  
padmakāṣṭhodbhavāpuṣpai devadārudbhavairviruk |  
kṛṣṇakāṣṭha samudbhūtaistāmasaṃ karmasiddhyati ||  
  
bhūta staṃbhenivajātā janastaṃbhe samīsavā |  
mahāniṃvena ḍākinyā bhūniṃvai staṃbhanaṃ rujāṃ ||  
  
iṃdrā vṛkṣādvraṇastaṃbhobhicāro vā narāsthitaḥ |  
ṛkṣāsthito vanyasiddhiḥ śārdūlā tasya devatā ||  
  
narāsthyā rākṣasāvaśyā vīrāvaśyā hayāsthibhiḥ |  
rāśabhasthyā kṣudrasiddhirmānyatā bhujagāsthibhiḥ ||  
  
mṛttikābhṛṣṭa maṇijāmālā śāvarasiddhidā |  
śrīphalairjñānamāpnoti rudrākṣaiḥ sarvasiddhidā ||  
  
athātodyathanaṃ vakṣye mālānāṃ tatra vodhanaṃ |  
caturthyāṃ protayenmālāṃ gaṇanāthasya maṃtrakaiḥ ||  
  
madhyāhnārkasya saptamyāṃ ravau vā tasya maṃtrakaiḥ |  
dvādaśyāṃ vaiṣṇavī mālā protavyā viṣṇumaṃtrataḥ ||  
  
trayodaśyāṃ tu saṃdhyāyāṃ tanmaṃtraiḥ śivamālikāṃ |  
aṣṭamyāṃ vā caturdaśyānnavamyāṃ bhūminaṃdane ||  
  
śaktīnāmapi kartavyā bhuktvā rātrau yathā vidhiḥ |  
yena maṃtreṇayā mālā kṛtā taṃtu japet tayā ||  
  
anya maṃtra japācchāpo devatāyāḥ prajāyate ||  
  
athavā mātṛkābhiśca grathanaṃ kārayet priye |  
paṃcāśanmaṇibhirmālākṣakāro merusaṃjñakaḥ ||  
  
anuloma vilomena mālā śatamayī bhavet |  
aṣṭavarge prakalpyātha mālātvaṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ ||  
  
mātṛkāmālayā jāpaḥ sarvamaṃtre praśasyate |  
sarvasiddhimayī mālā druta siddhikarī parā ||  
  
tattanmaṃtramayī devī tatra dhyātvā tu yat kṣaṇe |  
japaṃ kuryāt prayatnena nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ||  
  
sarvasiddhipradā mālā sarvakāryakarī parā ||  
  
dhruveṇa prathamaṃ kāryaṃ pratyekaṃ maṇika kramāt |  
sarvamaṃtramayī mālā sarvasiddhikarī parā ||  
  
tanmaṃtradevatā rūpaṃ dhyātvā tu mālikāṃtaraṃ |  
sarve maṃtrāḥ prajaptavyāḥ sarvakāryārtha siddhaye ||  
  
p. 238a)  
  
śaktimaṃtreṇa saṃgrathya śivamaṃtraṃ japecchive |  
śivamaṃtreṇa saṃgrathya śaktimaṃtraṃ japecchive ||  
  
śivaśaktyora bhedena mālākāryakarī parā ||  
  
yenaiva grathyate devi tameva prajapenmanuṃ |  
ityādyuktaṃ tvayā pūrva kiṃ tvayā vismṛtaṃ prabho ||  
  
idānīmanyathā proktaṃ saṃśayosti mama prabho |  
mātṛkā tārabhinnāni śivaśakti vihīnake ||  
  
mātṛkāyāmidaṃ noktaṃ anyamālāvidhau mataṃ |  
anyaprakāra grathameye naiva grathanaṃ caret ||  
  
tameva prajapanmaṃtraṃ nānyatra japecchive |  
mātṛkādāvapi śive mālāṃ tanmaṃtrarūpiṇī ||  
  
grathitā paṭṭasūtreṇa devyāḥ prityai tu mālikā |  
kārvyāsairvaiṣṇavī mālā padmasūtrairathāpi vā ||  
  
ūrṇābhirvā valkalairvā śaivī kāryā sa sūtrajāḥ |  
kāryā sa dharmakarmādi sādhanaṃ sarvasiddhidaṃ ||  
  
prāyaśaḥ sarvadevānāṃ sūtrotpatī vidhiṃ śṛṇu |  
sūtraṃ dvijeṃdra puṇyastrī nirmitaṃ graṃthivarjitaṃ ||  
  
yā jīvavatsakā nārī suṃdarī pativallabhā |  
tayākartita sūtraṃ ca kumārī kartitaṃ ca vā ||  
  
śvetarakta suvarṇābha kṛṣṇavarṇā dvijāditaḥ |  
sarveṣāmeva varṇānāṃ rakta sarvepsita pradaṃ ||  
  
triguṇaṃ triguṇī kṛtya grāhyaṃ prakṣālya yatnataḥ |  
maru sūtreṇa paṭṭeṇatra sareṇu vinirmitā ||  
  
nirmitā svarṇarajataiḥ svarṇenāpi śubhā matā ||  
  
hāridraṃ sarvathā sūtraṃ grāmakāryā sa saṃbhavaṃ |  
caitra kāryāsajaṃ cātha tyajedgrathanakarmaṇi ||  
  
guruṇā grathitā śreṣṭhā svayaṃ kḷptā tatā'varā |  
śaktyā ca grathitā śreṣṭā na śūdrādibhirīśvari ||  
  
eteṣu brāhmaṇaḥ śreṣṭho jalamālā kṛte bhṛśaṃ |  
alābhe tu dvijātīnāmapi vā sva sva jātayaḥ ||  
  
kalau tu durlabhā viprā yathā viprā svadharmagā ||  
  
athāsyāḥ śodhanaṃ vakṣye samāsāt parameśvarī |  
kulamārgānu sāreṇa smṛtyuktavidhināpi vā ||  
  
kṛta nityakriyaḥ śuddha ukteṣṭhekṣeṣvataṃdriyaḥ |  
upavāsaṃ haviṣyaṃ vā tathaika bhakṣameva vā ||  
  
p. 238b)  
  
vidhāya paṭṭakāryā saḥ śṛtaiḥ sūtraṃ vinirmamet |  
upavāsadine devi tāni sarvāṇi pūjayet ||  
  
dviguṇaṃ triguṇaṃ vāpi tṛccatriguṇamācaret |  
caṃdanākṣatadhūpādyaiḥ kusumairvalidīpakaiḥ ||  
  
kartavyāṇi samāsāni na sthūlāni kṛśāni ca |  
prātastatsūtramādāya kāmanā kāryabhedataḥ ||  
  
śvetaṃ nīlaṃ tathā pītaṃ raktaṃ varṇaṃ ca kārayet ||  
  
rudrākṣa sphāṭikādīnvai samānīya prayatnataḥ |  
ekavaktrairdvivaktraiśca caturvaktraiśca paṃcabhiḥ ||  
  
ṣaḍvaktrairvātha kartavyāmitho miśrāstu varjayet |  
mukhe mukhaṃ tu kartavyaṃ mukhe mūlaṃ tu varjayet ||  
  
mukhaṃ mukhena saṃyojya pṛṣṭhaṃ pṛṣṭeṇa yojayet |  
rudrākṣasyonnataṃ proktaṃ mukhaṃ pucchaṃtu nimnakaṃ ||  
  
dhātṛphalopamaṃ śreṣṭho madhyā vadarasannibhaḥ |  
adhamaśca na kābhaḥ syāt tato hīno vipattikṛt ||  
  
atisthūloti sukṣmaśca sphaṭiko bhaṃguro laghuḥ |  
bhinnaḥ purādhṛto jīrṇo rudrākṣo na śubhaḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
  
na jīrṇāni na kīṭādi viddhāni sunavāni ca |  
ādyaṃ sthūlaṃ tatastasmānyūnaṃ nyūnataraṃ tataḥ ||  
  
eko merustatradeyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ sthūla saṃbhavaḥ |  
asyorddha vaktrayānīyānmerostaṃ naiva laṃghayet ||  
  
maṇimekaikamādāya sūtre saṃpātayet sudhīḥ |  
sarpākārātha vā kāryā gopuccha sadṛśī tathā ||  
  
ekaikaṃ maṇimadhye tu brahmagraṃthiṃ vikalpayet |  
trirāvṛttyātha madhyena cārddha vṛttyāṃ tadeśataḥ ||  
  
graṃthi pradakṣiṇāvartā brahmagraṃthiritīritā ||  
  
athavā graṃthirahitā dṛḍha rajjuḥ samanvitāḥ |  
dṛḍhasūtraṃ niyuṃjīta japetrudyatino yathā ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśataiḥ sarvasiddhiruktā manīṣibhiḥ |  
paścāśadbhiḥ kāmyasiddhiḥ syāt tathā caturuttaraiḥ ||  
  
sarvārthaḥ saptaviṃśatyā paṃcadaśyābhicārake |  
paṃcaviṃśatibhirmokṣaṃ triṃśaḍbhirddhana siddhaye ||  
  
evaṃ nirmāya vai mālāṃ pratiṣṭhāmācaredvudhaḥ |  
apratiṣṭhābhirmālābhirmaṃtraṃ japati yo naraḥ ||  
  
sarvaṃ te niṣphalaṃ vidyāt kruddhā bhavati devatā ||  
  
p. 239a)  
  
atha sāmānya mālāyāḥ saṃskāraṃ pravadāmite ||  
  
tāṃtrikaṃ vaidikaṃ vāpi sadyo jātāhvayaṃ manuṃ |  
paṭhitvā paṃcagavyena snāpayenmālikāṃ puraḥ ||  
  
gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhisarpiḥ kuśodakaṃ |  
paṃcagavyamiti proktaṃ mahāpātakanāśanaṃ ||  
  
dugdhaṃ kāṃcana varṇāyāḥ śvetāyāścaiva gomayaṃ |  
gomūtraṃ tāmravarṇā yā nīlāyāśca bhaved dadhi ||  
  
ghṛtaṃ tu kṛṣṇavarṇāyā evaṃ paṃcāmṛtepi ca |  
gavāṃ varṇāstu sulabhāḥ saṃti deśeṣu tatra ca ||  
  
tatra varṇavibhāgena paṃcagavyāni cāharet |  
varṇā lābhena doṣosti mātrā hīnastu varjayet ||  
  
go śakṛt dviguṇaṃ mūtraṃ sarpidadyāccaturguṇaṃ |  
kṣīramaṣṭaguṇaṃ proktaṃ paṃcagavyaṃ tathā dadhi ||  
  
athavā paṃcagavyānāṃ samāno bhāga ucyate |  
gāyatryādāya gomūtraṃ gaṃdhadvāreti gomayaṃ ||  
  
āpyāyasveti ca kṣīraṃ dadhikrāma tato dadhiḥ |  
tejosi śukramityājyaṃ devasyatvā kuśodakaṃ ||  
  
kṣālayet paṃcagavyādyaiḥ sadyo jāteti maṃtrataḥ |  
caṃdanā guru gaṃdhādyairvāma devena gharṣayet ||  
  
dhūpayedapyaghoreṇa kṛṣṇā guru su guggulaiḥ |  
tat puruṣākhya maṃtreṇa lepayeccaṃdanādibhiḥ ||  
  
īśānaḥ sarvamiti ca pratyekaṃ maṃtrayecchataṃ |  
tenaiva maṃtrayen merumaghoreṇa ca maṃtrayet ||  
  
prāṇapratiṣṭhā me tasyāṃ viśvarūpeṇa cācaret |  
evaṃ saṃskṛtya mālāṃ tāṃ guruhaste samarpayet ||  
  
abhivādya guruṃ mūrddhnā gṛhnīyāt tatkarān svayaṃ |  
etanmaṃtrasya gāyatrīṃ puraḥ paṃcaśataṃ japet ||  
  
tato japenmūlamaṃtramitye tasya viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
athānyamālā saṃskāraṃ vakṣye'śvatthasya patrakaiḥ |  
padmākāreṇa navabhiḥ sthāpitaistatra vinyaset ||  
  
maṇiṃ sūtraṃ ca gaṃdhādyai kṣālayitvātha maṃtrayet ||  
  
oṃ hrīṃ pūrvamātṛkāvarṇaiḥ kramādekaikaśomaṇiṃ |  
sūtraṃ ca tatra vinyasya pūjayitvā hunet tataḥ ||  
  
tilājyaiḥ kevalājyairvā sadyojātābhiḥ pṛthak |  
paṃcamaṃtraiḥ śataṃ cāṣṭāvaṣṭā viṃśatireva vā ||  
  
homābhāve japaḥ proktaḥ pūrvavat kṣālanādikaṃ |  
kaulikādau viśeṣoyaṃ surayāmaṇi tarpaṇaṃ ||  
  
p. 239b)  
  
saṃskṛtyaivaṃ budhomālāṃ tatprāṇāṃstatra sthāpayet |  
mūlamaṃtreṇa deveśi saṃpūjye bhaktibhāvataḥ ||  
  
guruṃ saṃpūjya taddhastād gṛhnīyād dakṣamālikāṃ |  
śūdrārthaṃ ca striyāmarthe mālā saṃskāra ucyate ||  
  
gaṇeśa sūrya viṣṇvīśa durgāḥ saṃpūjya bhaktitaḥ |  
mālāyāmatha tāṃ mālāṃ hasauṃ vījenābhi maṃtritām ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ paṃcagavye tāṃ sthāpayet tryahaṃ |  
caturthe tu samuddhṛtya kṣālayedastra maṃtrataḥ ||  
  
hṛnmaṃtreṇa graṃthayitvā sthaṇḍile tāṃnnidhāpayet |  
tatastu tolyatāṃ mālāṃ sthāpayeddhemapātrake ||  
  
paṃcāmṛtena saṃsnāpya śītalena jalena ca |  
caṃdanena sugaṃdhena kastūrī kuṃkumādibhiḥ ||  
  
abhiṣekaṃ tataḥ kuryāt hyauṃ maṃtreṇa sādhakaḥ |  
navagrahān pūjayi dikpālāṃścāpi pūjayet ||  
  
tilenāmṛte yuktena śaktito homayettata |  
svarṇaṃ tu dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād gurave maṇisaṃkhyakān ||  
  
tanmaṃtrajāpino viprān bhojayedvātha vaidikān |  
oṃ bhāve svarṇapātrasya grāhyamaśvattha patrakaṃ ||  
  
mālāsaṃskāra ityuktvo japaḥ syāt siddhidāyakaḥ ||  
  
athā paraṃ pravakṣyāmi mālā saṃskāra ucyate |  
varṇamānena sā kāryā paṃcagavye tryahaṃ kṣipet ||  
  
sūtraṃ vāpi caturthehni kṣālayedastra maṃtrakaiḥ |  
samānavarṇa sūtreṇa grathayeddhṛdayānunā ||  
  
suvarṇādi guṇairvāpi grathayet sādhakottamaḥ |  
brahmagraṃthiṃ tato dadyān nāgapāśamathāpi vā ||  
  
sārddhaṃ graṃthidvayaṃ devi nāgapāśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |  
sārddhagraṃthi trayaṃ devi brahmagraṃthi prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
brahmagraṃthyā sarvakarma sādhayet parameśvari |  
nāgapāśe krūrakarmadvaividhyaṃ parikīrtitaṃ ||  
  
kavacena ca grathnīān mālā dhyānaparāyaṇaḥ |  
sarvaśeṣe tato meru sūtradvayasamanvitaṃ ||  
  
grathayettāra yogena vadhnīyāt sādhakottamaḥ |  
evaṃ niṣpādya deveśi pratiṣṭhāṃ ca samācaret ||  
  
sthaṇḍile maṇḍale kṛtvā yathā bhāga vidhiḥ kramāt |  
pūjayitvā yathānyāyamiṣṭa deva manukramāt ||  
  
p. 240a)  
  
nyāsapūrvaṃ japenmaṃtramaṣṭottara sahasrakaṃ |  
juhuyācca taddaśāṃśena yasya devasya yatpriyaṃ ||  
  
tato maṇḍala madhye tu tāṃ mālāṃ sthāpayebudhaḥ |  
astramaṃtraṃ tu tonyasya devavat pariciṃtayet ||  
  
advaitarūpamāsādya mālāṃ kuryāt tathātmikāṃ |  
tato valiṃ yathā nyāyaṃ dadyāttaiḥ sādhakottamaiḥ ||  
  
evaṃ pratiṣṭhāmāsādya mālāyāmiṣṭa devatāṃ |  
ācāryaṃ pūjayen maṃtrī śilpinaṃ ca yathāvidhi ||  
  
nānyamaṃtraṃ japet tatra yadīcchet siddhimātmanaḥ ||  
  
atha mālāvidhānaṃ ca kaulikānāṃ ca vāmināṃ |  
kīkasādika mālānāṃ kathyate śṛṇu pārvatī ||  
  
tatrāpi kālikāttārā vidyāyāṃ śavasaṃbhavā |  
mālā vahu vidhā proktā mahāśaṃkhādi bhedataḥ ||  
  
mahāśaṃkhamayī mālā sarvavidyā svarūpiṇī |  
daṃtākhya mālikā devī merustu rājadaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
śaivī brahmāṇḍamālā ca dehadehāṃtarācayaḥ |  
karāsthi mālikā devi tathā yat parvamālikā ||  
  
jaṃghāsthi kīlakāryepi mālāyāmapi siddhikṛt ||  
  
atha govājibhaṣaṇamṛgavā naraśūkaraiḥ |  
bhallūkolūka śārdūla vyāghravāraṇadaṃtajāḥ ||  
  
gavayādi mṛgotthā ca kastūrī mṛgajātijā |  
jīvamātrāsthi saṃbhūtā kharoṣṭravāji daṃtajāḥ ||  
  
daṃtā bhāve pratinidhirmahāśaṃkhe navīnakaṃ |  
viśvāmitra bhavaṃ tacca sarvasatvamayaṃ bhavet ||  
  
śaṃkhamālā daṃtamālā nārikelamayī tathā |  
asthimālā maheśāni vṛddhastrī gomayaṃ vinā ||  
  
mālā tu trividhā proktā uttamādhama madhyamāḥ |  
daṃtākhya mālayā caiva rājadaṃtena meruṇā ||  
  
uttamā mālikā proktā kālikā karṣiṇī parā |  
karṇanetrāṃtarastho yo mahāśaṃkheti kīrtitaḥ ||  
  
mahāśaṃkhamayī mālā paṃcāśanmaṇi nirmitā |  
madhyamā mālikā proktā tārā jāpe prakīrtitā ||  
  
asthibhirvānṛmuṃḍairvā kiṃ vā naralalāṭajā |  
dehadehāṃtarasthairvā mālā proktā kaniṣṭhikā ||  
  
chinnā devyā vidhau devī evaṃ hi trividhā matā |  
saṃmukhau yau ubhau daṃtau rājadaṃtau prakīrtitau ||  
  
p. 240b)  
  
karālāsyā mahākālyā dānavāḥ bhakṣitā purā |  
trailokyagāminau daṃtau rājadaṃtāviti smṛtau ||  
  
rājadaṃteti saṃjñā vai devyāḥ pūrvakṛtā priye |  
yo daitya carvakau daṃtau mama kārya kārāvubhau ||  
  
tasmāt prītena manasā merukārya niyojitau ||  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
sāmānya mālā kathitā viśeṣavada śaṃkara ||  
  
śrīśiva uvāca ||  
  
caṃdramaṇḍalamārabhya karṇāṃtaṃ parameśvari |  
vāmadakṣa yugmake ca mālāsyān merumaṇḍalā ||  
  
merumaṇḍala mālā tu sarvasiddhiḥ parāṃvike |  
dvitīyā sārddhayavakairmālā sāmrājyamohinī ||  
  
eka paṃktiraṃdhra saṃkhyaiḥ kapālaṃ parikīrtitaṃ |  
karṇanetrāṃtarastho yo mahāśaṃkhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
mahāśaṃkhamayī mālā sarvasiddhi pradāyinī |  
karṇanetragalaprāṃtedaṃtāṃtaṃ parameśvari ||  
  
muṇḍaṃ proktaṃ maheśāni pūjāsādhana karmaṇi |  
dakṣabhrūviṃdumārabhya karṇāṃtaṃ parameśvari ||  
  
vāmabhrūviṃdumārabhya vāmaśrutyaṃgaḥ śive |  
mālā tripuṇḍra mārgeṇa śivaśaktimayī ca vā ||  
  
arddha tripuṇḍra mārgeṇa tadadhaḥ śaktimālavat |  
ūrddhvakrameṇa mālā tu sarvamālottamottamā ||  
  
keśakrameṇa deveśi kapālorddhantu mālikā |  
tathaiva maṇayaḥ kāryā śiva eva na cāparaḥ ||  
  
mahāśaṃkhamayī mālā dvitīyā dhruvamaṇḍalā |  
unmanī mālikā devī tṛtīyā parikīrtitā ||  
  
merumālā caturthī syāt paṃcamī merumaṇḍalā |  
daṃtamālā maheśāni merumaṇḍalamālikā ||  
  
rājadaṃtena merustu tena sānmerumaṇḍalā |  
mālā paṃcaka metadvipaṃcatanmātragocaraṃ ||  
  
rājadaṃta dvayaṃ meruniyojya paṃktimārgataḥ |  
ūrddhvamūrddhva krameṇaiva daṃṣṭrā daṃṣṭrā karaṃ śive ||  
  
adharoṣṭha lasatpaṃktihāranāyakaṃ vrajet |  
rājadaṃtastu merustu kṛśāścaturdaśatyajet ||  
  
evaṃ mālā mahāmālā paṃcāśad daṃtagocarā |  
sarvasiddhimayī mālā rājataṃtena meruṇā ||  
  
siddhidā yogadā bhogadā trīrājyaṃ pradātuthā |  
catuḥṣaṣṭhiḥ siddhimate mālā tu paṃcamī smṛtā ||  
  
p. 241a)  
  
brahmāviṣṇuścarudraśca īśvaraśca sadāśivaṃ |  
ete paṃcamahāpretāḥ paṃcamālāmvikāvidhau ||  
  
tārāchinnā tathā kāmakalā kālī ca kālikā |  
śrīvidyādāvapi śive mālikā mālikāmayī ||  
  
pūrvoktānāṃ maṇīnāṃ ca svabhāve parameśvarī |  
gaṃdharūpāśca maṇayo daṃta sphāṭika sannibhāḥ ||  
  
maṇayo yatnataḥ kāryā sarvasiddhimabhīpsubhiḥ |  
mahāśaṃkhepya śaktaścet sphāṭikyā mālayā japet ||  
  
atha mahāmālādhikāriṇamāha ||  
  
sarvāsthimālā saṃśastā adhikāra kramaṃ śṛṇu |  
pūrṇārddhāmnāya bhūṣāḍhyastathā caraṇadīkṣitaḥ ||  
  
ṣaḍanvaya kramāśaktaḥ śrīmedhā saṃyutastathā |  
mahācīnakramāśakto mahānīlakramī ca vā ||  
  
īdṛgvidhaḥ sādhako hi mālā japa parāyaṇaḥ |  
mālādhikāriṇaḥ proktāḥ krameṇa parameśvari ||  
  
rahasyamālārthamuṇḍā dānavidhistu sādhāraṇapūjāprakaraṇeṣuktaḥ ||  
  
atha nirmāṇaprakārastūcyate ||  
  
siddhamuṇḍaṃ purā kṛtvā mālādīn kārayet priye |  
śilpinaṃ pūjayedādau vastra gaṃdhānulepanaiḥ ||  
  
saṃhṛṣṭa kārayen mālāṃ maṃtra pūtaṃ pivanmadhuḥ |  
yathāyogyaṃ vedhavatī mālāṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
daṃtamālā śaṃkhamālā viśvāmitra kapālajā |  
sarvāsthi mālā deveśi jīvamātrāsthi nirmitā ||  
  
aṃguṣṭān mastakāṃtaṃ ca uttarottarataḥ śubhaḥ |  
tatra devī sadā tuṣṭā tatra tiṣṭhati pārvatī ||  
  
etadvidyā vidhau devi pūrvokte ca varāsthi ca |  
paṃcāśanmaṇibhirmālā mātṛkā varṇataḥ kramāt ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśatī cetsā tadāṣṭa varga kalpanaṃ |  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ kṛtvā ṛtubhatyā bhage kṣipet ||  
  
niśāmekāṃ samuddhṛtya kāraṇaiḥ kṣālayet tataḥ |  
śuddhodairmūlamaṃtreṇābhiṣiṃced vijayārasaiḥ ||  
  
prakṣālya dhūpayet paścāt protayediṣṭa sūtrakaiḥ ||  
  
nāḍyā saṃgrathanaṃ kāryaṃ raktena vāsasā priye |  
vāsasā majjayā vāpi nāḍībhirvā śubhāmatā ||  
  
svayaṃbhuvāktāyā nāḍī sā nāḍī sarvatottamāḥ |  
svayaṃbhū kusumāktaistutūlakairvīranāyikā ||  
  
p. 241b)  
  
kumārī kartitaṃ sūtraṃ puṇya strī kartitaṃ ca vā |  
tato dvijeṃdra puṇya strī kartitaṃ graṃthi varjitaṃ ||  
  
veśyā hastabhavaṃ vāpi mātaṃgī hastajaṃ paraṃ |  
rajasvalā hastabhavaṃ sūtraṃ ca kīrtitaṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
kuṇḍāktaṃ cai golāktaṃ svajaṃ vāktaṃ tathaiva ca |  
svayaṃbhuvāktaṃ yat sūtraṃ tat sūtraṃ sarvatottamaṃ ||  
  
sūtraṃ sveṣṭajapennīlaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ māraṇa karmaṇi |  
mohane haritaṃ staṃbhaṃ dhūmābhaṃ dviṣinālabhaṃ ||  
  
śāṃtau pauṣṭau sitaṃ dveṣe raktamuccāṭane bhavet |  
vaśye pītaṃ kaṣāyastu vipakṣakaraṇe mataṃ ||  
  
svayaṃ na kartayedgraṃthiṃ japamālā na guṃphayet ||  
  
atha mālā grathinādhikāriṇamāha ||  
  
mahāmālā daṃtamālā sarvāsthimālikāvidhau |  
krameṇa kathyate devi grathane cādhikāriṇaḥ ||  
  
mātā putrī tathā bhāryā tathāṣṭakanyakā priye |  
ṣaṭtriṃśajjātijāstrīyā svakulāṣṭakajāya vā ||  
  
tārā kulākulaṃ vāpi daśavidyāstriyaiścayāḥ |  
paṃcāśat pīṭhajā vā piveśyā saptakameva vā ||  
  
mālāyā grathane devi śakunāśakunaṃ śṛṇu |  
dadhimāṃsasurāpiṣṭa śaṃkhavāditriveṇavaḥ ||  
  
mṛdaṃgakāhalodgītaṃ duṃdubhirvādyadarśanaṃ |  
gajāśvarathaveśyādi strīṇāṃ pūrṇaghaṭasya vā ||  
  
japasiddherlakṣaṇāni mālāyāṃ parameśvarī |  
rodanaṃ gānanaṃ muṇḍaraṇḍā darśanameva ca ||  
  
kalaho guruniṃdā ca devatā vīraniṃdanaṃ |  
sūtra truṭirathā prāptirmaṇikāsphoṭanaṃ tathā ||  
  
mālāgrathana kāle tu maṇisphuṭati vedyadi |  
putraśoko vinirddiṣṭo duḥkhabhāgī bhaveddhruvaṃ ||  
  
mālāgrathanakāle tu maṇiskhalati cedbhuvi |  
tasya śoko vinirdiṣṭo nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ||  
  
maṇimādāya sūtreṇa grathayen madhyamadhyataḥ |  
brahmagraṃthi vidhāyetthaṃ meruśca graṃthi saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
grathayitvā puro mālāṃ tataḥ saṃskāramārabhet ||  
  
siddhyai vakṣyāmi saṃskāraṃ sarvataṃtreṣu gopitaṃ |  
kṛta nityakriyaḥ śuddhaḥ śuddharkṣeṣu ca maṃtravit ||  
  
cakrapūjāṃ tataḥ kṛtvā sāṣṭottara sahasrakaṃ |  
hunenmadya palābhyāṃ ca mūlamaṃtreṇa sādhakaḥ ||  
  
p. 242a)  
  
tato valiṃ yathā nyāyaṃ mahiṣādeḥ pradāpayet |  
śaktiṃśca sādhakāṃścāpi bhojayen maṇisaṃkhyakān ||  
  
ataḥ paraṃ pṛthak rūpo mālā saṃskāramācaret |  
mālārātrividhiṃ vakṣye śṛṇu sā vahitā bhava ||  
  
sudine śubha ṛkṣādi dine śuddhadine śubhe |  
mahāmālāṃ samādāya vīrapātraṃ samānayet ||  
  
vīrayaṃtraṃ samāsādya vīramālaṃ ca śodhayet |  
devīṃ sāvaraṇāṃ pūjya savalyaṃtaṃ maheśvarī ||  
  
daśaviṃśatyaṃ ca viṃśaddīpāṃ datvā valiṃ caret |  
evaṃ mālāṃ śubhāṃ kṛtvā mahāsaṃskāramācaret ||  
  
śubhe muhūrte saṃlagne mālāṃ vā paṃcagavyake |  
nimaṃtrya paṃcagavyaṃ ca gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ punaḥ ||  
  
dadhisarpiḥ krameṇaiva paṃcagavyaṃ prakīrtitaṃ |  
taduttārya śuddhajalaiḥ saṃkṣālya saṃvidā śavaiḥ ||  
  
mūlamaṃtreṇa saṃkṣālya taddravye sthāpayeddinaṃ |  
tṛtīye dinase devi yakṣa karddamakairyajet ||  
  
sarvagaṃdhairaṣṭagaṃdhairaṇimādyaṣṭakairyajet |  
aṣṭanīrāśca tārāyāstārāṣṭaurocinīmaṇau ||  
  
caturthadivase devi prāṇān sthāpya yajet kramāt |  
rahasya mālāmaṃtrasyāsya ṛṣiḥ parameśvaraḥ ||  
  
śrīmahātāriṇī devī uṣṇikchandaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |  
krī& vījaṃ strī& tathā śaktiḥ hū& maṃtraḥ kīlakaṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
mahāmālā daṃtamālā śodhane viniyojane |  
triśaktyā tu ṣaḍaṃgāni dhyānaṃ maṃtravadā caret ||  
  
dhyātvā saṃkalpa yatnenaṃ maṃtreṇānena pārvati |  
praṇavaṃ ca tathā lajjāśrīlajā kāmakūrcakaiḥ ||  
  
phaṭ svāheti ca maṃtreṇa vasakemālikau kṣipet |  
tatrāvāhanamaṃtrādyaiḥ kālikāṃ kālasāradāṃ ||  
  
sāyudhāṃ parivārāṃśca pūjayet parameśvarī |  
mūlamāvṛttya tārtīyaṃ saṃsmarandhenu mudrayā ||  
  
amṛtī kṛtya kavacenāvaguṇya maheśvari |  
mahāmudrayā samācchādya devī rūpī vibhāvayet ||  
  
dhyāyet tatra kṣipedviṃduṃ tatra maṃtrān śṛṇu priye |  
praṇavaṃ kūrcayugmaṃ ca svāhā praṇavakūrcakau ||  
  
vahnijāyā ca tārāstre vahnijāyā viṣaṃ tathā |  
tārā ca vahnijāyāṃ ca tārā lajjā sa kūrcakau ||  
  
vahnijāyā tatastāraṃ lajjā phaṭ vahnijāyayā |  
dvitriśṛṃkhalikāvyasta samastamaṃtramālayā ||  
  
p. 242b)  
  
śatadhānena maṃtreṇa viṃduprakṣepamācaret |  
kastūrikā keśaraṃ ca caṃdā gurupradhūpakaiḥ ||  
  
puṣpamālāṃ samuttārya vidyayā cābhimaṃtrayet |  
praṇavaṃ ca tathā māyā śrīmahāvajriṇīti ca ||  
  
tato mahāghorarūpe karkaśeti padaṃ vadet |  
mahāsthimaṇḍale procya praviśeti padaṃ tathā ||  
  
sarvasiddhiḥ prayaccheti praṇavaṃ kūrcavījakaṃ |  
māyāvījaṃ vahnijāyā mahākapālinīti ca ||  
  
tato mahāghorarūpe svāhā praṇava māyayā |  
māyā kūrcastri svāhāṃtā vidyoktā cābhimaṃtraṇe ||  
  
durvākṣataiḥ samabhyarcyakāte coddīpanaṃ caret |  
upacāraiḥ samabhyarcya mātṛkāṃ mūlamaṃtrataḥ ||  
  
uddīpanaṃ tataḥ kṛtvāhaṃ kāreṇa tu veṣṭayet |  
valiṃ dadyādanenaiva tāraṃ māyādvayaṃ vadet ||  
  
vāsudevaṃ viṃduyutaṃ kūrceṇa puṭitaṃ vadet |  
kūrcatāre phaṭ ca kūrcaṃ praṇavadvayamuccaret ||  
  
kūrcavījaṃ vahnijāyā praṇavaṃ kūrcavījakaiḥ |  
mahāyogini śabdāṃte tatastribhuvanatāriṇī ||  
  
mahāśaṃkhāsthi mālā ca madhye nivāsa kurvati |  
kuruśabdaṃ sarvasiddhiṃ dehiyuk ca surāpadaṃ ||  
  
māṃsopahāreṇa gṛhneti yuk gṛhnāya padadvayaṃ |  
kullukā phaṭ tataḥ svāhā maṃtreṇānena pārvati ||  
  
yathocitena dravyeṇa valiṃ datvā vidhānataḥ |  
paṃcadravyaiḥ paṃcadinaṃ mālāṃ sthāpya ca paṃcame ||  
  
mālā rātrividhiṃ kuryāt tena siddhyati mālikā |  
nibhṛte sthāpayet mālāṃ rahasyamālikāvidhiḥ ||  
  
daṃtamālāvidhau devi viśeṣaṃ śṛṇu vā paraṃ |  
praṇavaṃ hṛdbhagavatī mānaraṃjini coccaret ||  
  
vicce vicce valocceva haravicce padaṃ vadet |  
mālāvicce tathā mālādhāriṇī haralū& padaṃ ||  
  
hamavrū& mahāśaṃkhāsthidhāriṇīti padaṃ vadet |  
karkaśāsthi mahāmālā vāsinīti padaṃ vadet ||  
  
chinne tāre kālike ca tadaṃte japamālike |  
kullukāṃ phaṭ mahādaṃtamālā madhye padaṃ vadet ||  
  
nivāsaṃ kuru yugmaṃ ca rājeṃdra mālikāṃ tataḥ |  
vāsinīṃ tritayaṃ procya krī& trayaṃ hū& dvayaṃ tahā ||  
  
māyādvayaṃ ca phaṭ svāhā mālāmaṃtreṇa hṛnmanuḥ |  
validāna manuṃ vakṣye śṛṇu sāvahitā bhava ||  
  
p. 243a)  
  
praṇavaṃ karkaśapadaṃ maṃḍaletyaṃvike padaṃ |  
mālinī kaulinī padaṃ gaurāṃ dhāricoccaret ||  
  
girije mālāvati padaṃ kriyāvati padaṃ tataḥ |  
gāyatrī ca gāṇapriye śakrapriye ca śāṃkarī ||  
  
kālīkāpālike kṛṣṇamuṇḍadhāriṇi coddharet |  
aśidhāriṇīti padaṃ tadaṃte jātavedase ||  
  
śrīkālīkāli ca padaṃ mṛḍāṇī rudrāṇi tathā |  
imaṃ valiṃ gṛhnayugmaṃ mālāsiddhiṃ ca cottare ||  
  
dehidāpaya yugmaṃ cakro ṣaṭka sa layāyutaṃ |  
valiṃ dadyādane naiva tadaṃte jāgratī kṛtiḥ ||  
  
kapālakajjalaṃ corapādakajjala yugmakaṃ |  
viśvamohana nāmānaṃ kajjalaṃ viddhi pārvatī ||  
  
tatpādabhasmadeveśi phālguṇot savajaṃparaṃ |  
jagaddhūlīti nāmnā tu vikhyātaṃ śatrunigrahe ||  
  
anena manunā gṛhya udbhrāṃtiṃ dhūlināmikāṃ |  
śatru mūrddhni tathā dehegeṇeśayyāṃ gaṇe jale ||  
  
dāpayet parameśāni udbhrāṃtiṃ dhūlirīritā |  
udbhrāṃta dhūlyā deveśi bhramākrāṃtaṃ jagadvayaṃ ||  
  
yathā grahaṇayugmaṃ ca tathā parvadvayaṃ bhavet |  
nakṣatra rāśi vārādi śuddhā śuddhiṃ na cācaret ||  
  
kāmavījaṃ kṣū& tathā vījaṃ śrī& śrī& phaṭ trayaṃ vadet |  
siddhe jāgraddhūli siddhiṃ dehi svāhā manurmataḥ ||  
  
maṃtreṇānena saṃgṛhya udbhrāṃti dhūlimuttamāṃ |  
mālyāsiddhyā sarvasiddhirbhavatyeva na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
svajāta kusumaṃ devī kuṇḍagolodbhavaṃ tathā |  
anaṃga gaṃdhādeveśi caturthāṃ parikīrtitā ||  
  
evaṃ saṃpādya deveśi jāgratī karaṇaṃ caret |  
siṃdūratilakaṃ bhāle vadane saṃvidā savau ||  
  
vīrāsanī vīraveśī dhūpadīpa pramoditaḥ |  
saṃviddugdharase mālāṃ kṣiptvā dugdhaṃ tato vadet ||  
  
tato rakte kṣipenmālāṃ dhūpenaiva pradhūpayet |  
tato valiṃ pradadyāddhi mālāṃ saṃsiddhaye śive ||  
  
śaktiṃ kumārīṃ mālāṃ vā saṃpūjya siddhibhākkalau |  
balidāna vidhau devi valiṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ ||  
  
ajāgalastha raktena tarpayet tatramālikāṃ |  
raktadhārābhimajjābhiryoni raktairapi priye ||  
  
tarpaṇāt siddhidā mālāyāgadrūpā phalapradā |  
pūrvakrameṇa deveśi āveśokta krameṇa vā ||  
  
p. 243b)  
  
tat taddevī deharūpāmālikā varadā kalau |  
evaṃ kṛtvā varāṃ mālāṃ sādhakaḥ siddhimāpnuyāt ||  
  
aśucirnna spṛśedenāṃ na kadāpi prakāśayet |  
bhūtarākṣasa vetālā siddha gaṃdharvacāraṇāḥ ||  
  
haraṃti prakaṭī yasmāt tasmādguptāṃ samācaret |  
jīrṇasūtraṃ punaḥ sūtraṃ grathayitvā śataṃ japet ||  
  
dvitrimāsaiśca ṣaṇmāsairmālā saṃgrathayecchive |  
ṣaṇmāsottaragaṃ devi jīrṇa sūtrasyamālikā ||  
  
yaḥ sthāpayen maheśāni tasya nāśo bhaviṣyati |  
chinne sūtre bhavenmṛtyustasmādyatnaparo bhavet ||  
  
mahāśaṃkhamayī mālā tathā daṃtākhyamālikā |  
na deyā yasya kasyāpi gopyānu mātṛjāravat ||  
  
athavāṃguli mālābhirjapaṃ kuryāt taducyate |  
anāmā madhyamārabhya kaniṣṭhānu krameṇa tu ||  
  
madhyamā mūlaparyaṃtā karamālā prakīrtitā |  
madhyamā nāmikā madhye parvayugmaṃ prakalpayet ||  
  
meruṃ vā nāmikā mūlāt kaniṣṭhānu krameṇa ca |  
tarjanyagrādito madhyāmūlāṃtaṃ daśasaṃkhyakāḥ ||  
  
athavā kalpayenmeruṃ madhyāmadhyādiparvakaṃ |  
anāmā madhyaparvā tu tarjanī mūlakāvadhi ||  
  
daśasaṃkhyā jape proktā tathā yaṃtrividhomataḥ |  
tatrādau trividho proktaḥ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ śṛṇu ||  
  
anāmā mūlamārabhya prādakṣiṇya krameṇa tu |  
tarjanī mūlaparyaṃtaṃ japenna vasu parvasu ||  
  
madhyamā tritayaṃ grāhyamanāmā mūlameva ca |  
anāmā madhyamaṃ caikaṃ meruṃ kṛtvā na laṃghayet ||  
  
idaṃ ca dvādaśāvṛtyā aṣṭottaraśataṃ bhavet |  
aṃgulyākhyo japaḥ prokto namatennonnatena ca ||  
  
kaniṣṭhikāṃtaścāṃguṣṭo vadhyeyaṃ daśakaṃ bhavet |  
aṃgulīgatarekhābhirjapāllekhā japo bhavet ||  
  
aṃgulirnna viyuṃjīta japamāle kadācanaṃ |  
aṃgulīnāṃ viyogena chidreṣu sravate japaḥ ||  
  
nollaṃghaye ca gaṇanāṃ kiṃcit saṃkocayettalaṃ |  
na darśayet karaṃ no cetphalalaṃ gṛhnaṃti rākṣasāḥ ||  
  
p. 244a)  
  
iti śrītaṃtraciṃtāmaṇau mālābhedādipratiṣṭāṃtanirṇayo nāma triṃśattamaḥ   
prakāśaḥ || 30 ||
